Abhidharmasamuccayabhāṣyam / I lakṣaṇasamuccayo nāma prathamaḥ samuccayaḥ
# # / / rgya gar skad du / / aa bhi dha rmma sarba du tstsha ya bh'a shum / / bod skad du /
oṃ namo ratnatrayāya / kimarthamidaṃ śāstramārabdham / skandhādīnārabhya kati kasmādityevamādiṣu cintāsthāneṣu kauśalyakaraṇārtham
# chos mngon pa kun las btus pa'i bshad pa / / bam po dang po / / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur [dd] pa la phyag 'tshal lo / / ci'i phyir bstan bcos 'di brtsams she na / / phung po la sogs pa las brtsams te / / du dang ci'i phyir zhes bya ba la sogs pa bsam pa'i gnas rnams la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir brtsams so /
tathāhyanena kauśalyena dvividho 'nuśaṃso labhyate manaskārānuśaṃsaṃḥ sāṃkathyaviniścayānuśaṃsaśca / tatra manaskārānuśaṃsaḥ śamathānukūlyādvipaśyanāvṛddhayānukūlyācca veditavyaḥ
# 'di ltar mkhas pa 'dis ni phan yon rnam pa gnyis thob ste / / yid la byed pa'i phan yon dang 'bel ba'i gtam gtan la 'bebs pa'i phan yon no / / de la yid la byed pa'i phan yon ni zhi gnas kyi rjes su mthun pa dang lhag mthong 'phel ba'i rjes su mthun pa rig par bya'o /
śamathānukūlyaṃ punareṣu sthāneṣu kṛtakauśalasya niḥsaṃdehatayā yatheṣṭamālaṃbane aikāgrayayogena sukhaṃ cittasamādhānataḥ
# zhi gnas kyi rjes su mthun pa ni gnas 'di dag la mkhas par byas pas the tshom med pas / / ji ltar rang gi dmigs pa la rtse gcig pa'i tshul gyis bde bar sems mnyam par 'jog pa'i phyir zhi gnas kyi rjes su mthun no /
vipaśyanāvṛddhayānu kūlyaṃ bahubhiḥ prakāraiḥ jñeyaparīkṣayā prajñāprakarṣagamanataḥ
# lhag mthong 'phel ba'i rjes su mthun pa ni rnam pa mang por shes bya yongs su brtags pas shes rab khyad zhugs par 'gro ba'i phyir /
sāṃkathyaviniścayānuśaṃsa eṣu sthāneṣu kuśalasya sarvapraśnavyākaraṇaśaktiyogādvaiśāradyapratilaṃbhato draṣṭavyaḥ
# lhag mthong gi rjes su mthun no / / 'bel ba'i gtam gtan la 'bebs pa'i phan yon ni gnas 'di dag la mkhas pas 'dri ba thams cad lung ston pa'i mthu dang ldan pas mi 'jigs pa thob par blta'o /
pañcākārātmavastūdbhāvanatāmupādāyetyatracaturākāramātmano vastvityātmavastu
# bdag gi gzhi rnam pa lnga brjod pa'i phyir te / / zhes bya ba 'di la rnam pa bzhi ni bdag gi gzhi yin pas bdag gi gzhi'o /
pañcamaṃ tvātmalakṣaṇameva vastvityātmavastviti veditavyam / saparigrahadehagrahaṇena bāhyasyādhyātmikasya ca rūpaskandhasya grahaṇaṃ veditavyam
# lnga pa ni bdag gi mtshan nyid kho na ste / / gzhi yin pas bdag gi gzhir rig par bya'o / / lus yongs su gzung ba dang bcas pa smos pas ni phyi dang nang gi gzugs kyi phung po bsdus so /
vedanādīnāmupabhogāditvaṃ tallakṣaṇanirdeśe jñāpayiṣyate
# tshor ba la sogs pa ni longs spyod la sogs pa nyid de / / de dag gi mtshan nyid bstan pa'i skabs su 'chad do /
tadāśrayātmasvavastu vijñānam teṣāṃ saparigrahadehādīnāmāśrayamātmalakṣaṇaṃ vastvityarthaḥ
# de dag gi gnas ni bdag gi gzhi rnam par shes pa ste / / lus yongs su gzung ba dang bcas pa la sogs pa de dag gi gnas ni bdag gi mtshan nyid de / / gzhi zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tathāhi loke prāyeṇa vijñāne ātmagrāhaḥ śeṣeṣvātmīyagrāha iti / dehaparigrahābhyāmiti cakṣurādī ndriyaṣaṭkena rūpādiviṣayaṣaṭkena ca
# 'di ltar 'jig rten na phal cher rnam par shes pa'i phung po la bdag tu 'dzin lhag ma rnams la ni bdag gir 'dzin to / / lus yongs su gzung ba nyid kyis zhes bya ba la / / mig la sogs pa dbang po drug dang gzugs la sogs pa yul drug gis so /
ṣaḍākāro 'tīto vartamānaścopabhogo vijñānaṣaṭkam tasya dhāraṇamāśrayālaṃbana bhāvataḥ / ityevaṃ taddhā raṇatvena dvādaśānāmindriyaviṣayāṇāṃ dhātutvam / vijñānānāṃ punarupabhogalakṣaṇa dhāraṇatvena dhātutvaṃ veditavyam / yathātītapratyutpannāḥ cakṣurādaya upabhogalakṣaṇadhārakā naivamanāgatāḥ 2 / āyadvāramātratvādindriyārthamātragrahaṇena dvādaśaivāyatanāni vyavasthā pitāni na tūpabhogalakṣaṇaṃ vijñānaṣaṭkamiti
# 'das pa dang da ltar gyi nye bar spyod pa rnam pa drug ni rnam par shes pa drug ste / / de 'dzin pa ni gnas dang dmigs pa'i dang pos 'dzin to / / dbang po dang yul bcu gnyis ni de ltar de 'dzin pa'i phyir khams so / / rnam par shes pa rnams ni nye bar spyod pa'i mtshan nyid 'dzin pas khams nyid du rig par bya'o / / skye ba'i sgo tsam yin pa'i phyir dbang po dang don tsam smos pas skye mched bcu gnyis kho nar rnam par gzhag pa yin te / / nye bar spyod pa'i mtshan nyid rnam par shes pa drug ni rnam par ma gzhag go /
upādānaṃ chando rāgaśca
# nye bar len pa ni 'dun pa dang 'dod chags te /
tatra chando 'bhilāṣaḥ rāgo 'dhyavasānam
# de la 'dun pa ni 'dod pa'o / / 'dod chags ni lhag pa chags pa'o /
chandenānāgatamātmabhāvamabhilāṣamukhenopādatte yenānāgatān skandhānabhinirvarttayati
# 'dun pas ni ma 'ongs pa'i lus 'dod pa'i sgo nas len te / / des ma 'ongs pa'i phung po rnams 'grub po /
rāgena vartamānamātmabhāvamadhyavasānamukhenopādatte yena vartamānān skandhānna parityajati / tasmādetadeva dvayamupādānamityucyate
# 'dod chags kyis ni da ltar gyi lus la lhag par chags pa'i sgo nas len te / / des da ltar gyi phung po rnams yongs su mi gtong ngo / / de bas na 'di gnyi ga yang nye bar len pa zhes bya'o /
tatra skandhavannirdeśa iti / upādānena yuktāstasmātsopādānadharmā iti veditavyam
# de la phung po bzhin du bshad do zhes bya ba ni nye bar len pa dang ldan pa ste / / de'i phyir nye bar len pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams su rig par bya'o /
sparśena rūpāṇāmanyathībhāvo veditavyaḥ
# reg pas gzugs su yod pas ni gzhan du 'gyur bar rig par bya'o /
yā deśe ityabhi mukhapradeśe / idaṃ cedaṃ cetyasthiśaṃkalādikaṃ jñeyavastusabhāgaṃ pratibimbam
# gang yul la zhes bya ba ni mngon du gyur ba'i phyogs la'o / / 'di dang 'di'o zhes bya ba ni keng rus la sogs pa zhes bya ba'i dngos po dang 'dra ba'i gzugs brnyan no /
evaṃ caivaṃ ceti varṇasaṃsthānabhedaiḥ citrīkārateti tathāsaṃjñā / śubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ sukho 'nubhavaḥ phalavipākaḥ / aśubhānāṃ duḥkhaḥ / ubhayeṣāmaduḥkhāsukhaḥ
# 'di lta bu dang 'di lta bu zhes bya ba ni kha dog dang dbyibs kyi bye brag go / / bkra bar 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni de ltar 'du shes pa'o / / las dge ba rnams kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa ni bde ba myong ba'o / / las mi dge ba rnams kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa ni sdug bsngal myong ba'o / / gnyi ga'i 'bras bu rnam par smin pa ni sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa myong ba ste /
tathāhi śubhānāmaśubhānāṃ vā vipāka ālayavijñānaṃ nityamupekṣayaiva saṃprayuktaṃ bhavati / saiva cātropekṣā vipākaḥ / sukhaduḥkhayostu vipākajatvādvipākopacāraḥ / dṛṣṭaśrutatamavijñātānarthāniti dṛṣṭaṃ yacca kṣuṣānubhūtam śrutaṃ yacchrotreṇānubhūtam mataṃ yatsvayamabhyūhitamevaṃ caivaṃ ca bhavitavyamiti vijñātaṃ yatpratyātmamanubhūtamiti
# 'di ltar dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams kyi rnam par smin pa kun gzhi'i rnam par shes pa ni rtag tu btang snyoms nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa yin te / / btang snyoms de nyid rnam par smin pa'o / / bde ba dang sdug bsngal de ni rnam par smin pa las byung ba'i phyir rnam par smin pa zhes nye bar gdags so / / mthong ba dang thos pa dang bye brag phyed pa dang rnam par shes pa'i don rnams la zhes bya ba la / / mthong ba ni gang mig gis myong ba'o / / thos pa ni gang rna bas myong ba'o / / bye brag phyed pa ni gang 'di dang 'di lta bur 'gyur ro zhes bya ba ni bdag nyid kyis mngon par brtags pa'o / / rnam par shes pa ni gang so so rang gis myong ba'o /
vyavaharatītyabhilāpaiḥ prāpayatītyarthaḥ / nānāvasthāsu ceti sukhaduḥkhādyāsu / yena cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭavānityatītavijñānopabhogadhārakatvena dhātutva darśayati
# tha snyad 'dogs pa zhes bya ba ni / / mngon par brjod pa rnams kyis go bar byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / gnas skabs sna tshogs rnams su zhes bya ba ni bde ba dang sdug bsngal la sogs pa rnams su'o / / mig gang gis gzugs rnams mthong bar gyur ba zhes bya ba ni 'das pa'i rnam par shes pa nye bar spyod pa 'dzin pa nyid kyis khams nyid du ston to /
paśyatīti vartamānavijñānopabhogadhārakatvena / yacca tasya cakṣuṣo bījamupacitamālayavijñānaṃ yata āyatyāṃ cakṣunirvartiṣyate vaipākyaṃ ca yato nirvṛttam tadapi dvividhaṃ bījaṃ cakṣurdhāturityucyate cakṣuṣo hetutvāt / yaccakṣurdhātoḥ rūpe ādhipatyamiti rūpīndriyādhipatyena bāhyaviṣayanirvartanāt
# lta ba zhes bya ba ni da ltar gyi rnam par shes pa nye bar spyod pa 'dzin pa nyid kyis khams nyid du ston to / / mig de'i sa bon bsags pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gang yin pa yang khams te / / gang las phyi ma la mig 'grub par 'gyur ba'o / / rnam par smin pa'ang khams te gang las grub zin pa'o / / sa bon rnam pa de gnyi ga yang mig gi rgyu yin pas mig gi khams zhes bya'o / / mig gi khams ni gzugs la dbang byed pa ste / / dbang po'i dbang gis phyi rol gyi yul 'grub pa'i phyir ro / / rang gi rten dang dmigs pa'i bye brag can no /
taddhātuvaddraṣṭavyaṃ tacca yathāyogamiti yena cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi drakṣyati yacca tadbījamityevamādi yojayitavyam / catvāri ca mahābhūtānyupādāyeti / kathamupādāyarūpam
# de ni khams bzhin du blta ste ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyor ro zhes bya ba ni mig gang gis gzugs rnams mthong bar 'gyur ba dang de'i sa bon bsags pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gang yin pa ste / / gang las phyi ma la mig 'grub par 'gyur zhes bya ba dang sbyar ro / / 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa zhes bya ba la rgyur byas pa'i gzugs ji lta bu zhe na /
catvāri mahābhūtānyupādāya jananasaṃniśrayapratiṣṭhopastaṃbhopabṛṃhaṇahetutvena
# 'byung ba chen po bzhi dag rgyur byas pa ni skyed pa dang rten pa dang gnas pa dang ston pa dang 'phel bar byed pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
jananādi hetutvaṃ punarbhūtānāmupādāyarūpe pañcavidhaṃ hetutvamadhikṛtya / utpattihetutvaṃ tairvinā tadanutpatteḥ
# 'byung ba dag rgyur byas pa'i gzugs la rgyu rnam pa lnga'i dbang du byas nas skyed pa la sogs pa'i rgyu nyid yin te / / 'byung ba'i rgyu nyid ni 'di dag med na de mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
vṛttihetutvaṃ bhūtāni pratyākhyāyopādāyarūpasya pṛthagdeśāvaṣṭambhasāmarthyābhāvāt
# 'dug pa'i rgyu nyid ni 'byung ba rnams bsal na rgyur byas pa'i gzugs la sogs shig tu yul gnod pa'i mthu med pa'i phyir ro /
anuvṛttihetutvaṃ bhūtavikāreṇa tatpratiṣṭhitopādāyarūpavikriyāgamanāt
# rjes su 'gyur ba'i rgyu nyid ni 'byung ba gyur na de la gnas pa'i rgyur byas pa'i gzugs kyang 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
sthitihetutvaṃ sadṛśotpattikāle bhūtairupādāyarūpasaṃtānasyānupacchedayogena saṃdhāraṇāt
# gnas par byed pa'i rgyu nyid ni mtshungs par 'byung ba'i dus na 'byung ba rnams kyi rgyur byas pa'i gzugs kyi rgyud rgyun mi 'chad pa'i tshul du 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
upacayahetutvaṃ vṛttikāle bhūtairūpādāyarūpāpyāyanāditi / nīlādīnāṃ pañcaviṃśatīnāṃ rūpāṇāṃ vyavasthānaṃ ṣaḍbhirākārairveditavyam / lakṣaṇataḥ saṃniveśato 'nugrahopaghātataḥ kriyāsaṃniśrayataḥ kriyālakṣaṇataḥ maṇḍanataśca caturṇā daśānāmaṣṭānāmekaikasya ca yathākramam
# 'phel bar byed pa'i rgyu nyid ni 'phel ba'i dus na 'byung ba rnams kyis rgyur byas pa'i gzugs yongs su rgyas par byed pa'i phyir ro / / sngon po la sogs pa gzugs rnam pa nyi shu rtsa lnga ni mtshan nyid dang gnas pa dang phan gnod dang byed pa'i rten dang byed pa'i mtshan nyid dang rgyan dang rnam pa drug gis rnam pa gzhag par rig par bya'o / / bzhi dang bcu dang brgyad dang gcig dang gcig go rims bzhin no /
tatrābhyavakāśastadanyaprativārakaspraṣṭavyarahito yo deśaḥ / nabho yadupariṣṭānnīlaṃ dṛśyate / śabdavyavasthānaṃ lakṣaṇato 'nugrahopaghātataḥ hetuprabhedato deśanāprabhedato vyavahāraprabhedataśca
# de la mngon par skabs yod pa zhes bya ba ni de las gzhan pa zlog par byed pa'i reg bya dang bral ba'i phyogs gang yin pa'o / / nam mkha' zhes bya ba ni / / gang steng na sngon por snang ba'o / / sgra ni mtshan nyid dang phan gnod dang rgyus rab tu dbye ba dang bshad pas rab tu dbye ba dang tha snyad kyis rab tu dbye bas rnam par gzhag go /
lakṣaṇataḥ śrotrendriyagrāhyo yo 'rtha iti / deśanāprabhedato lokaprasiddhādayastrayaḥ
# mtshan nyid ni rna ba'i dbang pos ga zung ba'i don gang yin pa zhes bya ba'o / / bstan pas rab tu dbye ba ni 'jig rten gyi grags pa la sogs pa gsum mo /
śeṣaṃ yathāyogaṃ veditavyam
# lhag ma ni ji ltar mthun mthun du rig par bya'o /
tatropāttamahābhūtahetukastadyathā vākchabdaḥ
# de la zin pa'i 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba ni 'di lta ste / / ngag gi sgra'o /
anupāttamahābhūtahetukastadyathā vṛkṣaśabdaḥ / tadubhayastadyathā hastamṛdaṅgaśabdaḥ
# zin pa ma yin pa'i 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba ni 'di lta ste / / shing la sogs pa'i sgra'o / / de gnyi ga ni 'di lta ste / / lag pa dang rdza rnga la sogs pa'i sgra'o /
lokaprasiddho laukikabhāṣāsaṃgṛhītaḥ
# 'jig rten gyi grag pa ni / / 'jig rten pa'i skad kyis bsdus pa'o /
siddhopanīta āryerdeśitaḥ
# grub pas bstan pa ni 'phags pa rnams kyis bstan pa'o /
parikalpitastīrthyerdeśitaḥ
# kun tu brtags pa ni mu stegs pa can rnams kyis bstan pa'o /
āryānāryavyāvahārikau tudṛṣṭādīnaṣṭau vyavahārānadhikṛtya veditavyau
# 'phags pas tha snyad btags pa dang 'phags pa ma yin pas tha snyad btags pa ni / / mthong ba la sogs pa tha snyad brgyad kyi dbang du byas par rig par bya'o /
gandhavyavasthānaṃ svalakṣaṇato 'nugrahopaghātataḥ prabhedataśca
# dri ni rang gi mtshan nyid dang phan gnod dang gnas skabs kyi sgo nas rab tu dbye bas rnam par gzhag go /
rasavyavasthānamapyevameva veditavyam / tatra sahajo gandhaścandanādonām sāṃyogiko dhūpayuktyadīnām pāriṇāmikaḥ pakvaphalādīnāmiti
# ro yang de bzhin du rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / de la lhan cig skyes pa'i dri ni / / tsan dan la sogs pa'i dri'o / / sbyar ba las byung ba ni bdug spos sbyar ba la sogs pa'i dri'o / / gyur pa las byung ba'i dri ni shing tog smin pa la sogs pa'i dri'o /
spraṣṭavyaikadeśavyavasthānamāmarśanata ātulanataḥ sparśanata āpīḍanataḥ saṃsargato dhātuvaiṣamyasāmyataśca / abvāyusaṃsargācchītam
# reg bya'i phyogs gcig ni kun tu mnabs pa dang kun tu gzhal ba dang reg pa dang kun tu btsir ba dang 'dus pa dang khams snyoms ma snyoms kyi rnam par gzhag go / / chu dang rlung 'dus na grang ngo /
appṛthavīsaṃsargātpicchalam
# chu dang sa 'dus na 'dred do /
viśrāmo balamūrjā ca dhātusāmyāt / ūrjā punarvaiśāradyaṃ veditavyam
# khams snyoms na ngal sos pa dang nyams yod pa dang spungs che bar 'gyur te / / sbungs che ba ni mi 'jigs par rig par bya'o /
tṛptirubhayathā
# tshim pa ni gnyi ga'o /
śeṣā jighatsādayo dhātuvaiṣamyādveditavyāḥ
# bkres pa la sogs pa lhag ma rnam ni khams ma snyoms par rig par bya'o /
ābhisāṃkṣepikaṃ paramāṇurūpam
# bsdus pa las gyur pa ni rdul phra rab kyi gzugs so /
ābhyavakāśikaṃ tadeva yathoktaṃ tadanyaprativārakaspraṣṭavyarahitam
# mngon par skabs yod pa ni de nyid de / / de las gzhan pa thogs par byed pa'i reg bya dang bral ba'o /
sāmādānikamavijñaptirūpam / parikalpitaṃ pratibimbarūpam
# yang dag par blangs pa las byung ba'i rnam par rig byed ma yin pa'i gzugs so / / kun brtags pa ni gzugs brnyan gyi gzugs so /
vaibhūtvikaṃ vimokṣadhyāyigocaraṃ yadrūpam / vedanāskandhavyavasthānamāśrayataḥ svabhāvata āśrayasaṃkalanataḥ saṃkleśavyavadānataśca / tatra rūpāśrayasaṃkalanataḥ kāyikīvedanāvyavasthānam
# dbang 'byor pa ni rnam par thar pa la bsam gtan pa'i spyod yul gyi gzugs gang yin pa'o / / tshor ba'i phung po ni gnas dang ngo bo nyid dang gnas sdom pa dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bas rnam par gzhag go / / de la gzugs kyi gnas sdom pas ni lus kyi tshor ba rnam bar gzhag go /
arūpyāśrayasaṃkalanataścaitasikīvedanāvyavasthānam
# gzugs med pa'i gnas sdom pas ni sems kyi tshor ba rnam par gzhag go /
saṃkleśataḥ sāmiṣādīnām vyavadānato nirāmiṣādīnāṃ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam / tattṛṣṇāviyukteti visaṃyuktā visaṃyogyānukūlā ca veditavyā
# kun nas nyon mongs pas ni zang zing dang bcas pa la sogs pa rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / rnam par byang bas ni zang zing med pa la sogs par rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / de'i srid pa dang mi ldan pa'i zhes bya ba ni mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa dang bral ba'i rjes su mthun par rig par bya'o /
avyavahārakuśalasyāśikṣitabhāṣatayā rūpe saṃjñā bhavati na tu rūpamiti / tasmādanimittasaṃjñetyucyate
# tha snyad la mi mkhas pa ni / / skad ma bslabs pas gzugs la 'du shes ni 'byung na gzugs so snyam pa ni mi shes pa ste / / de'i phyir mtshan ma med pa'i 'du shes zhes bya'o /
animittadhātusamāpannasya rūpādisarvanimittāpagate 'nimitte nirvāṇe saṃjñānimittasaṃjñā
# mtshan ma med pa'i dbyings la snyoms par zhugs pa'i gzugs la sogs pa'i mtshan ma thams cad dang bral ba mtshan ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa la 'du shes pa ni mtshan ma med pa'i 'du shes so /
bhavāgrasamāpannasyāpaṭutvenālaṃbanānimittīkaraṇādanimittasaṃjñā
# srid pa'i rtse mo la snyoms par zhugs pa'i 'du shes ni mi gsal bas dmigs pa la mtshan mar mi byed pa'i phyir mtshan ma med pa'i 'du shes so /
parīttaḥ kāmadhātuḥ nikṛṣṭa tvāt
# chung ngu ni 'dod pa'i khams la ste / / ngan pa'i phyir ro /
mahadgato rūpadhātustata utkṛṣṭatvāt / apramāṇe ākāśa vijñānānantyāyatane 'paryantatvāt
# rgya chen por gyur pa ni gzugs kyi khams la ste de bas mchog tu gyur ba'i phyir ro / / tshad med pa ni nam mkha' dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched la ste / / mtha' yas pa'i phyir ro /
tasmāttadālaṃbanāḥ saṃjñāḥ parīttādisaṃjñā veditavyāḥ / vedanāsaṃjñāvarjyānāṃ sarveṣāṃ caitasikānāṃ cittaviprayuktānāṃ ca saṃskāraskandhalakṣaṇatve cetanāmātrasyaiva tannidaśe grahaṇaṃ tatpūrvakatvāditareṣāmiti kāraṇajñāpanārthamāha yayā kuśalatvāya cetayata ityevamādi
# de bas na de dag la dmigs pa'i 'du shes ni chung ngu la sogs pa'i 'du shes rnams su rig par bya'o / / tshor ba dang 'du shes ma gtogs pa sems las byung ba dang sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa thams cad ni 'du byed kyi phung po'i mtshan nyid kho na yin na / / de bstan pa la sems pa nyi tshe smos pa ni de gzhan dag gi sngon du 'gro ba'i phyir ro / / gtan tshigs bstan pa'i phyir gang gi dge ba'i phyir yang sems par byed ces bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
tatra kuśalā vakṣyamāṇāḥ śraddhādayaḥ
# de la dge ba ni dad pa la sogs pa 'og nas 'byung ba rnams so /
saṃkleśā rāgādayaḥ kleśopakleśāḥ / avasthābhedataḥ cetanāpreritasaṃskārāvasyāsu prajñaptāḥ cittaviprayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ / cetanādīnāṃ caitasikānāṃ lakṣaṇataḥ karmataśca nirdeśo veditavyaḥ / tatra cetanāyāḥ cittābhisaṃskāro manaskarmeti lakṣaṇanirdeśaḥ
# kun nas nyon mongs pa ni 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams so / / gnas skabs kyi bye brag ni sems pas bskyod pa'i 'du byed kyi gnas skabs rnams la btags pa'i sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams so / / sems pa la sogs pa sems las byung ba rnams ni mtshan nyid dang las kyis bstan par rig par bya'o / / de la sems pa ni sems mngon par 'du byed pa yid kyi las te zhes bya ba ni mtshan nyid bstan pa'o /
kuśalākuśalāvyākṛteṣu cittapreraṇakarmiketi karmanirdeśaḥ
# dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams la sems 'jug par byed pa'i las can zhes bya ba ni bstan pa ste /
tathāhi yathābhisaṃskāraṃ kuśalādiṣu dharmeṣu cittasya pravṛttirbhavatīti
# 'di ltar ji ltar mngon par 'du bya ba dge ba la sogs pa'i chos rnams la sems 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
ālaṃbane cittadhāraṇaṃ tatraiva punaḥ punarāvarjanaṃ veditavyam
# dmigs pa la sems 'dzin pa ni de nyid la yang dang yang du gtod bar rig par bya'o /
ata eva samādhilābhī manaḥ saṃskāralābhītyucyate
# de'i phyir yid la byed pa thob pa ni ting nge 'dzin thob pa zhes bya'o /
vijñānotpattāvindriyasya sukhādivedanotpattyanukūlo yo vikārastadākāraḥ sparśo veditavyaḥ / tattadupasaṃhitā kartukāmateti darśanaśravaṇādisarvakriyecchāsaṃgrahārtham
# rnam par shes pa 'byung ba la / / bde ba la sogs pa'i tshor ba 'byung ba dang mthun par dbang po'i 'gyur ba gang yin pa'i rnam pa de ni reg par rig par bya'o / / de dang de la ldan par byed 'dod pa nyid de zhes bya ba ni lta ba dang mnyan pa la sogs pa byed 'dod pa thams cad bsdu ba'i phyir ro /
yathāniścayaṃ dhāraṇā evametannānyathetyadhimuktiḥ / ata eva tatpradhāno 'nyaiḥ saṃhartu na śakyate saṃstutaṃ vastu pūrvānubhūtaṃ veditavyam
# ji ltar nges pa bzhin du 'dzin pa zhes bya ba 'di ni de bzhin te / / gzhan du ma yin no / / zhes du ma yin no zhes smos pa'o / / de'i phyir de gces su byed pa ni gzhan dag gis 'phrogs par mi nus so / / 'dris pa'i dngos po ni sngon myong bar rig par bya'o /
avikṣepakarmikatvaṃ punaḥ smṛterālaṃbanābhilapane sati cittāvikṣepatāmupādāya
# rnam par mi g yeng ba'i las can ni dran pas dmigs pa mngon par brjod par gyur na rnam par g yeng ba med pa'i phyir ro /
cittasyaikāgratāvikṣepaḥ / jñānasaṃniśrayadānaṃ samāhitacittasya yathābhūtajñānāt
# sems rtse gcig pa nyid ces bya ba ni rnam par g yeng ba med pa'o / / shes pa'i rten byed pa ni sems mnyam par gzhag pa na yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du shes pa'i phyir ro /
saṃśayavyāvartanaṃ prajñayā dharmān pravicinvato niścayalābhāt
# som nyi zlog pa ni shes rab kyis chos rnams rab tu rnam par dbye na nges pa rnyed pa'i phyir ro /
astitve 'bhisaṃpratyayākārā śraddhā / guṇatve prasādākārā / śakyatve 'bhilāṣākārā śakyaṃ mayā prāptuṃ niṣpādayituṃ veti
# dad pa ni yod pa nyid la mngon par yid ches pa'i rnam pa dang yon tan can la dad pa'i rnam pa dang nus pa la bdag gi rnam pa thob par byed dam / / sgrub par byed nus so snyam du 'dod pa'i rnam pa'o /
hryādayaḥ sugamatvānna vibhajyante / upapattiprātilambhikaṃ śrutacintāmayaṃ bhāvanāmayaṃ ca yathākramaṃ vipākāgamādhigamarūpaṃ veditavyam / pratisaṃkhyāprajñā dhairyasahitā
# ngo tsha shes pa la sogs pa ni go sla bas yang rnam par ma phye'o / / skye bas thob pa dang thos pa dang bsams pa las byung ba dang bsgoms pa las byung ba ni go rims bzhin du rnam par smin pa dang lung dang rtogs pa'i shes par rig par bya'o / / brtan pa dang bcas pa'i shes rab ni so sor brtags pa'o /
sthāmavānvīryavānutsāhī dṛḍhaparākramo 'nikṣiptadhuraḥ kuśaleṣu dharmeṣvityevamādisūtrapadāni yathākramaṃ saṃnāhādiṣvabhyutsāhavastuṣu yojayitavyāni
# dge ba'i chos rnams la mthu dang ldan pa dang brtson 'grus dang ldan pa dang spro ba dang ldan pa dang brtul ba brtan pa dang brtson pa mi 'dor ba zhes 'byung ba mdo'i tshig 'di rnams ni go cha la sogs pa la mngon par zhen pa spro ba'i dngos po rnams dang go rims bzhin du sbyar ro /
paripūraṇaṃ yathā maulaṃ praveśaḥ
# yongs su rdzogs par byed pa ni / / ji ltar dngos gzhi la 'jug pa lta bu'o /
niṣpādanaṃ tasyaiva suparikarmakṛtatvam
# yongs su bsgrub pa ni de nyid legs par yongs su sbyong ba byas pa'o /
sarvāvaraṇaniṣkarṣaṇaṃ tadvaśenāśrayaparivṛttito draṣṭavyam
# sgrib pa thams cad sel ba ni de'i dbang gis gnas 'gyur bar blta'o /
sarvakuśalabhāvanāyā vīryādipūrvakatvātteṣvapramādaprajñapti / sāsravā dharmā āsravā āsravasthānīyāśca viṣayā iha veditavyāḥ
# dge ba thams cad bsgom pa'i sngon du brtson 'grus la sogs pa bzhi po 'gro bas / / de dag la bag yod par gdags te / / zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams ni 'dir zag pa rnams dang zag pa'i gnas kyi yul rnams su rig par bya'o /
cittasamatādibhirupekṣāyā ādimadhyāvasānāvasthā vyākhyātāḥ
# sems mnyam pa nyid ces bya ba la sogs pas ni btang snyoms kyi thog ma dang tha ma'i gnas skabs bshad de /
tathāhyupekṣayā yuktaṃ cittaṃ layādiveṣamyābhāvādāditaḥ samam
# 'di ltar btang snyoms dang ldan pa'i sems la bying ba la sogs pa'i mi mnyam pa med pas thog mar mnyam pa'o /
tato 'nabhisaṃskāreṇa vahanātpraśaṭham
# de'i 'og tu mngon par bya ba med par rnal du 'dug pa'o /
tataḥ saṃkleśāśaṅkābhāvādanābhogāvasthitamiti
# de'i 'og du kun nas nyon mongs pa'i dogs pa med par lhun gyis grub par gnas so /
a vihiṃsā pyadveṣāvyatirekāt prajñaptisatī veditavyā / duḥkhasaṃjananakarmaka iti tṛṣṇāvaśena pañcopādānaskandha nirvartanāt
# rnam par mi tshe ba ni zhe sdang med pa las gud na med pa'i phyir btags pa'i yod par rig par bya'o / / sdug bsngal bskyed pa'i las can zhes bya ni sred pa'i dbang gi nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga grub pa'i phyir ro /
asparśavihāra āghātacittasya duḥkhavihārāt
# reg par mi gnas pa ni kun nas mnar ba'i sems yod pa sdug bsngal bar gnas pa'i phyir ro /
agauravaṃ guruṣu guṇavatsu ca stabdhatā
# mi gus pa ni bla ma rnams dang yon tan can rnams la 'gying ba'o /
duḥkhotpattiḥ punarbhavotpattirvedi tavyā
# sdug bsngal 'byung ba ni yang srid ba 'byung bar rig par bya'o /
mithyāniścayairviparītaṃ jñānam / vicikitsā saṃśayaḥ
# log par nges pa ni phyin ci log tu shes pa'o / / the tshom ni som nyi'o /
saṃkleśotpattiḥ rāgādikleśasamudācāraḥ / tatsaṃniśrayadānaṃ mūḍhasya sarvakleśapravṛtteriti
# kun nas nyon mongs pa 'byung ba ni 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa kun tu 'byung ba'o / / de'i rten byed pa ni rmongs par 'gyur na nyon mongs pa thams cad 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
ratneṣu vimatirmārgasatye nirodhasatye ca yathāyogam
# bden pa rnams la yid gnyis za ba ni las kyi bden pa dang 'gog pa'i bden pa la ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
tayā kuśalapakṣe 'pravṛttiralabdhaniścayasyānārambhāt
# des dge ba'i phyogs la mi 'jug ste / / nges pa ma rnyed na ma rtsol ba'i phyir ro /
madhyamā pratipacchāśvatocchedagrāhavarjitaṃ pratītyasamutpādajñānam
# dbu ma'i lam zhes bya ba ni / / rtag ba dang chad pa spangs te rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba shes pa'o /
śīlavrataṃ kudṛṣṭipūrvakaṃ veditavyama
# tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs ni lta ba ngan pa sngon du 'gro bar rig par bya'o /
śramavaiphalyaṃ tenāniryāṇāt / nāsti dattaṃ nāstīṣṭaṃ nāsti kṛtaṃ nāsti sucaritaṃ nāsti duścaritamityayaṃ hetvapavādaḥ
# ngal ba 'bras bu med pa ni des nges par mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / sbyin pa med do / / mchod sbyin med do / / sbyin sreg med do / / legs par spyad pa med do / / nyes par spyad pa med do zhes bya ba ni 'di rgyu la skur ba 'debs pa ste /
nāsti duścaritasucaritānāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalavipāka iti phalāpavādaḥ / nāstyayaṃ loko nāsti paraloko nāsti mātā nāsti pitā nāsti sattva upapāduka iti kriyāpavādaḥ lokāntaragamanāgamanakriyāyā bījādhānakriyāyāḥ pratisaṃdhibandhakriyāyāścāpavādāt
# legs par spyad pa dang nyes par spyad pa'i las rnams kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa med do zhes bya ba ni 'bras bu la skur ba 'debs pa'o / / 'jig rten 'di med do / / 'jig rten pha rol med do / / pha med do / / ma med do / / sems can rdzus te 'byung ba med do zhes bya ba ni byed pa la skur ba 'debs pa ste / / 'jig rten gzhan du 'gro ba dang 'ong ba'i byed pa dang sa bon 'debs pa'i byed pa dang nying mtshams sbyor ba'i byed pa la skur ba 'debs pa'i phyir ro /
na santi loke 'rhanta ityevamādi sadvastunāśanam
# 'jig rten na dgra bcom pa med do zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni yod pa'i dngos po 'jig pa'o /
tadanyadyat kiṃcidviparītadarśanaṃ tanmithyāparikalpanaṃ veditavyam
# de las gzhan phyin ci log tu lta ba gang ci yang rung ste / / de dag thams cad ni log par rnam par rtog par rig par bya'o /
kuśalamūlasamucchedo viśiṣṭāyā eva mithyādṛṣṭerna sarvasyāḥ
# dge ba'i rtsa ba gcod pa ni log par lta ba khyad par can las 'byung gi thams cad las ni ma yin no /
pañcaskandhātmake jñeye ātmātmīyasvabhāvasamāropikā satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ
# phung po lnga'i bdag nyid kyis zhes bya ba la bdag dang bdag gi ngo bo nyid du sgro 'dogs pa ni 'jig tshogs la lta ba'o /
ātmanityānityaviśeṣasamāropikāntagrāhadṛṣṭiḥ
# bdag rtag go mi rtag go zhes khyad par du sgro 'dogs pa ni mthar 'dzin par lta ba'o /
kudṛṣṭāvagratā samāropako dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ
# lta ba ngan pa la mchog la sogs par sgro 'dogs pa ni lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
tatraiva śuddhisamāropakaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaḥ / ekā yadbhūyaseti mithyāvikalpikā yā nāvaśyamapavādikatvāt / lakṣaṇato dvābhyāmantagrāhamithyādṛṣṭibhyām saparivārataḥ sarvābhyaḥ
# de nyid la bdag po la sogs par sgro 'dogs pa ni tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa'o / / gcig ni phal cher la zhes bya ba ni log par rnam par rtog pa ni gdon mi za bar skur pa 'debs pa'i phyir ro / / mtshan nyid la brtags na ni mthar 'dzin pa dang log par lta ba gnyis las 'byung ngo / / 'khor dang bcas pa la brtags na ni lnga po thams cad las 'byung ngo /
rūpādayo nātmā tadvilakṣaṇatvāt na hi te ātmalakṣaṇā iti
# gzugs la sogs pa ni bdag ma yin te / / mtshan nyid dang mi mthun pa'i phyir de dag ni bdag gi mtshan nyid ma yin pa'o /
na teṣvātmā anityatādoṣāt / na hyāśrayābhāve āśritaṃ bhavatīti
# de dag la bdag med de / / gnas med na gnas par mi 'gyur bas mi rtag pa nyid kyi nyes par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
na rūpavānātmā asvātantryadoṣaprasaṅgāt / na tebhyo 'nyatrātmā nirdehatādoṣāt / na hi vinā dehenā tmaparikalpa upalabhyata iti / asvātantryatādoṣaḥ teṣvavaśavartanāt / athaivaṃvidhamātmānaṃ kaścitparikalpayet tathāpi nopapadyate 'rūpādika ātmā ayatnato mokṣadoṣāt / dehādibandhanābhāve hi svarasenaiva mokṣaḥ syāditi / rūpāmātmeti samanupaśyati vedanāṃ saṃjñāṃ saṃskārān vijñānamātmeti samanupaśyatītyetāḥ pañcātmadṛṣṭayaḥ
# gzugs ni bdag gi ba ma yin te / / de dag la dbang byed pa med pas rang dbang med pa'i nyes par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / de dag la gzhan na yang bdag med de lus med na bdag kun tu brtags par mi dmigs pas lus med pa'i nyes par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / ci ste la la zhig bdag rnam pa de lta bur yongs su rtog na / / de lta na yang gzugs la sogs pa med pa'i bdag mi 'thad de / / lus la sogs pa'i 'ching ba med na / / rang gi ngang gis grol bar 'gyur bas sgrim mi dgos par thar par 'gyur ba'i nyes par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / gzugs bdag yin par lta ba dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed rnams dang rnam par shes pa bdag yin par lta ba de dag lnga ni bdag tu lta ba'o / / bdag gzugs dang ldan pa zhes bya ba nas bdag rnam par shes pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i bar du lhag ma bco lnga ni bdag gir lta ba'o /
śeṣāḥ pañcadaśātmīyadṛṣṭayaḥ / rūpavān yāvadvijñānavāniti saṃbandhenātmīyatā sā hi tatsaṃvandhāttadvān bhavatīti
# 'brel bas bdag gir gyur ba ni 'di ltar de de dang 'brel bas de dang ldan par 'gyur ro / / gzugs bdag gi yin pa zhes bya ba yin pa nas /
ātmīyaṃ rūpaṃ yāvadvijñānamiti vaśavarttyātmīyatāmupādāya yasya hi yadvaśena vartate dāne viniyoge vā tasya tadātmīyamityucyate
# rnam par shes pa bdag gi yin pa zhes bya ba'i bar ni dbang sgyur bas bdag gir 'gyur ba'i phyir te / / gang zhig sbyin pa'am bskob la gang gi dbang du 'gyur ba de ni de'i bdag gi zhes bya'o / / gzugs la bdag gnas pa zhes bya ba nas /
rūpe yāvadvijñāne ātmetyavinirbhāgavṛttyātmīyatā ayamātmāeṣvanusṛto vistṛtaḥ prakṣipto 'ṅgāṅgānusārigata iti parikalpanāt
# rnam par shes pa la bdag gnas pa zhes bya ba'i bar ni tha dad du mi 'jug pas bdag gir 'gyur ba ste / / bdag 'di ni 'di dag la rjes su zhugs shing rnam par zhugs nas bzhag pa ste / / yan lag can yan lag gi rjes su song bar kun brtags pa'i phyir ro /
anirūpitavastukatvaṃ punā rūpamityevamādilakṣaṇaṃ nirūpayata ātmadṛṣṭeranavakāśāt
# ma dpyad pa'i gzhi can ni gzugs la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid la kun tu dpyad na bdag tu lta ba'i skabs med pa'i phyir te /
tadyathā rajjuṃ sarpato gṛhṇāti kaścit sahasā na punā rajjuriti nirūpayaṃstāṃ sarpato gṛhṇīyāditi
# dper na 'ga' zhig gis ma brtags par thag pa la sprul du 'dzin pa dang 'dra ste / / thag pa yin par dpyad na de la sprul du mi 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
krodhādayaḥ prajñaptisanto veditavyāḥ pratighātādivyatirekeṇābhāvāt
# khro ba la sogs pa ni btags pa'i yod par rig par bya'o / / khong khro ba la sogs pa las gud na med pa'i phyir ro /
tadūrdhvamiti krodhādūrdhvam
# de'i 'og tu zhes bya ba ni khros pa'i 'og tu'o /
akṣāntirapakārāmarṣaṇam / dharmataiṣā yadavadyaṃ praticchādayataḥ kaukṛtyam ataścāsparśavihāra iti
# mi bzod pa zhes bya ba ni gnod pa byed pa la ji mi snyam par mi byed pa'o / / 'di ni chos nyid do / / kha na ma tho ba dang bcas na 'gyod par 'gyur te / / de'i phyir reg par mi gnas pa zhes bya'o /
uccapragāḍhapāruṣyavacanaṃ paramarmaghaṭṭanayogena pratyakṣaravāditā
# tshig rtsub mo brlang zhing drag pa zhes bya ba ni gzhan gyi zher 'debs pa'i tshul gyis ngor lhangs [?] zhes zer ba ni /
asaṃlekho mātsaryeṇānupayujyamānānāmapyupakaraṇānāṃ saṃnicayādveditavyaḥ
# yo byad ma bsnyungs ba zhes bya ba ni ser snas yo byad mi mkho ba rnams kyang ba sogs pa las gyur bar rig par bya'o /
bhūtadoṣavimālanā anyenānyasya pratisaraṇaṃ veditavyam
# nges pa yang dag par skyong ba zhes bya ba ni / / gzhan nas gzhan du sgyur bar rig par bya'o /
samyagavavādalābhaparipanthakarmakatvaṃ yathābhūtamātmānamanāviṣkṛtyāvavādāyogyatvāt
# yang dag pa'i gdams ngag rnyed pa'i bar du gcod pa'i las can zhes bya ba ni bdag gi tshul yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin mi ston na gdams ngag gi 'os ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
dīrghāyuṣkalakṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ tadvikalpanādamaravitarkapūrvakaṃ jīvitamadotpatteḥ
# tshe ring ba'i mtshan ma bzung nas de la rnam par rtog pa'i phyir te / / mi 'chi bar rnam par rtog pa sngon du btang nas srog la rgyags pa skye'o /
anyatamānyatamā sāsravā saṃpattiḥ kulavalarūpamedhābuddhibhogaiśvaryādikā veditavyā / rāgāṃśikaṃ nāndīsaumanasyaṃ saṃkliṣṭo harṣaviśeṣaḥ / śubhanimittamanusarato rāgānukūlaṃ pūrvahasitaramitakrīḍitānusmaraṇāt cittasyānupaśamo veditavyaḥ kausīdyasaṃniśrayadānakarmakatvamaśraddadhānasya prayogacchandābhāvāt
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i phun sum tshogs pa gang yang rung ba zhes bya ba ni rigs dang stobs dang gzugs dang yid gzhungs pa dang blo dang longs spyod dang phyug pa la sogs par rig par bya'o / / dga' ba dang yid bde ba zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi dga' ba'i bye brag go / / sdug pa'i mtshan ma rjes su 'jug pa zhes bya ba ni 'dod chags kyi rjes su mthun pa'o / / sngon dgod dgod pa dang rtse rtse ba la sogs pa rjes su dran nas sems rnam par ma zhi bar rig par bya'o / / le lo'i rten byed pa'i las can zhes bya ba ni ma dad na sbyor ba la 'dun pa med pa'i phyir ro /
asaṃviditā kāyavākcittacaryābhikramapratikramādiṣu samyagapratyavekṣitatayā veditavyā
# lus dang ngag dang sems kyi spyod pa la mi shes bzhin du 'jug pa zhes bya ba ni 'gro ba dang ldog pa la sogs pa la legs par ma brtags par rig par bya'o /
evaṃ hyasya karaṇīyākaraṇīyājñānā dāpattayo bhavantīti
# de ltar na 'di ni bya ba dang bya ba ma yin pa mi shes pas ltung bar 'gyur ro /
svabhāvavikṣepaḥ pañcavijñānakāyāḥ prakṛtyaivādhyātmaṃ samādhātumaśakyatvāt
# ngo bo nyid kyi g yeng ba zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga rnams te / / rang bzhin gyis nang du mnyam par 'jog mi nus pa'i phyir ro /
bahirdhāvikṣepaḥ śrutādikuśale prayuktasya tadālaṃbanādbahiḥ kāmaguṇeṣu cittagamanaṃ veditavyam / adhyātmavikṣepaḥ samādhiprayuktasyaiva taccyutikarau layauddhatyamāsvādanā ca
# phyi rol du g yeng ba zhes bya ba ni thos pa la sogs pa'i dge ba la zhugs pa de la dmigs pa la phyi rol du 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga po dag la sems 'gro bar rig par bya'o / / nang gi g yeng ba zhes bya ba ni ting nge 'dzin du zhugs pa nyid kyi tshe de las nyams par byed pa bying ba dang rgod pa dang ro myong bar byed pa'o /
nimittavikṣepaḥ pare māṃ guṇavattayā saṃbhāvayiṣyantītyetannimittametadartha kuśalaprayuktasya śanaiḥ tatparihāṇito veditavyaḥ
# mtshan ma'i g yeng pa zhes bya ba ni gzhan gyis bdag la yon tan dang ldan par yid ches par bya ba'i phyir te / / de'i mtshan ma ni de'i phyir ro /
dauṣṭhulya vikṣepo 'haṃkārādidauṣṭhulyavaśādutpannotpanneṣu sukhādiṣu vediteṣvahaṃ mama asmīti vā karaṇāt kuśalapakṣāpariśuddhito veditavyaḥ
# dge ba la zhugs pa khad kyis de las nyams par rig par bya'o / / gnas ngan len gyi g yeng ba zhes bya ba ni ngar 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i gnas ngan len gyi dbang gis bde ba la sogs pa'i tshor ba byung ba rnams la nga zhes nga'i zhe 'am nga'o snyam du 'dzin pa'i phyir dge ba'i phyogs yongs su ma dag par rig par bya'o /
āditastathodgrahaṇamudgrahaḥ / vyavakiraṇā tadūrdhvaṃ tena cittasaṃtānasya miśrībhāvaḥ
# 'dzin pa ni thog ma nyid du de ltar 'dzin pa'o / / 'dres pa ni de'i 'og tu de dang sems kyi rgyud 'dres par gyur ba'o /
nimittīkāraḥ tasyaiva veditasya punaḥ punaścitrīkāro veditavyaḥ
# mtshan mar 'dzin pa ni tshor ba de nyid la yang dang yang bkra bar 'dzin par rig par bya'o /
manaskāravikṣepaḥ samāpattyantaraṃ vā samāpadyamānasya dhyānāntaraṃ vā saṃśrayataḥ pūrvasmāddhyutthānato veditavyaḥ
# yid la byed pa'i g yeng ba zhes bya ba ni / / snyoms par 'jug pa gzhan la snyoms par zhugs pa dang theg pa gzhan la brten pa snga ma las langs par rig par bya'o /
vairāgyaparipanthakarmaka ityupakleśātmakaṃ vikṣepamadhikṛtya / middhanimittaṃ tadyathā daurbalyam śramaḥ kāyagauravaḥ andhakāranimittasya manasikaraṇam sarvārambhāṇāmadhyupekṣaṇam punaḥ punastatkālanidrābhyāsaḥ mantrabalena parainidropasaṃhārastathā saṃvāhanādibhirveti
# 'dod chags dang bral ba'i bar du gcod pa'i las can zhes bya ba ni nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i bdag nyid kyi dbang du byas pa'o / / gnyid kyi rgyu zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste nyam chung ba dang ngal ba dang lus lci ba dang mun pa'i mtshan ma yid la byed pa dang rtsom pa thams cad yal bar 'dor ba dang de'i dus na yang dang yang goms pa dang gzhan dag sngags kyi stobs kyis gnyid bro bar byed pa dang de bzhin du lus mnyed pa la sogs pa'o /
mohāṃśika iti samādhito viśeṣaṇārtham / kuśalādibhāvavacanaṃ na tvavaśyaṃ mohātmaka iti kṛtvā
# gti mug gi char gtogs pa zhes bya ba ni ting nge 'dzin las bye brag tu dbye ba'i phyir ro / / dge ba la sogs pa'i dngos po'i tshig ni gdon mi za bar gti mug gi bdag nyid ma yin no /
kāla iti rātryā madhyame yāme
# dus zhes bya ba ni nam gyi gung thun no /
akālastato 'nyaḥ
# dus ma yin pa ni de las gzhan pa'o /
yuktaṃ kāle yathānujñam akāle 'pi glānasya karmaṇyatārtha vā
# rigs pa ni dus su ji ltar gnang ba dang dus yin na yang na ba dang las su rung bar bya ba'i phyir ro /
ayuktastato 'nyaḥ
# mi rigs pa ni de las gzhan pa'o /
kṛtyātipattisaṃniśrayadānamupakleśātmakasya middhasya veditavyaḥ
# bya ba shor ba'i rten byed pa ni nye mongs pa'i bdag nyid kyi dbang du byas par rig par bya'o /
anabhipretaṃ karaṇamabhipretapūrvikā sucaritaduścaritakriyā anabhipretaṃ karaṇaṃ parairbalādavaṣṭabhya kāryamāṇasya kleśābhibhavādvā yathāyogaṃ veditavyam / mohāṃśika ityupakleśasaṃgṛhītaḥ / kāle yāvanna prativiramati akāle tadūrdhvam / yuktaṃ sthāne ayuktamasthāne / cetanāṃ vā niśritya prajñāṃ vetyanabhyūhābhyūhāvasthāyāṃ yathākramam
# bsams pa zhes bya ba ni legs par nyes par spyod pa'i byed pa las mngon par dga' ba sngon du btang ba'o / / ma bsams pa'i bya ba ni gzhan dag gis nan gyis byed du bcug ste byed pa'am / / nyon mongs pas zil gyis mnan pa ste / / ji ltar mthun mthun du rig par bya'o / / gti mug gi char gtogs pa zhes bya ba ni nye ba'i nyon mongs pas bsdus pa'o /
paryeṣaṇākārā manaso 'bhijalpanā vitarkaḥ pratyavekṣaṇākārā manaso 'bhijalpanānuvicāra iti / tāveva vitarkavicārau saṃvadhyete audārikasūkṣmavyavasthānādanayoḥ / tadyathālobhasya lobhaprahāṇam śraddhāyā āśraddhayaprahāṇam / rāgapratipakṣo vairāgyam tasya paripanthakaraṇam tasya tena tadutpattāvantarāyakaraṇāt / evaṃ krodhādīnāmapyupakleśānāṃ maitryādyātmīyaratipakṣāntarāyakaraṇaṃ veditavyam / cittaviprayuktānāṃ saṃskārāṇāmadhiṣṭhānataḥ svabhāvataḥ prajñaptitaśca nirdeśo veditavyaḥ / asaṃjñisamāpattinirodhasamāpattī bhūmito 'pi niḥsaraṇavihārasaṃjñāpūrvakābhyāṃ manaskārābhyāmapi nirdiṣṭe / āsaṃjñikaṃ manaskāravarjyairebhireva / śeṣā adhiṣṭhānādibhistribhireva / tatra kuśalākuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāmityadhiṣṭhānanirdeśaḥ / ācayāpacaya iti svabhāvanirdeśaḥ / tathāhyācaye 'dhimātraiḥ śraddhādibhiḥ samanvāgata ityucyate / apacaye sati mṛdubhiriti / prāptiḥ pratilambhaḥ samāgama iti prajñaptiriti prajñaptinirdeśaḥ / evamanyeṣvapi yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyam / śubhakṛtsnavītarāgasyeti tṛtīyadhyānavītarāgasya
# dus ni ji srid mi spong gi bar du'o / / dus ma yin pa ni de'i 'og tu'o / / rigs pa ni gnas pa'o / / mi rigs pa ni gnas ma yin pa'o / / sems pa'am shes rab la rten zhes bya ba ni mngon par mi rtogs pa dang mngon par rtogs pa'i gnas skabs dang go rims bzhin no / / kun tu tshol ba'i rnam pa yid kyis mngon par brjod pa ni rtog pa'o / / so sor rtog pa'i rnam pa ni spyod pa'o / / sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams ni / / gnas dang ngo bo nyid dang btags pas bshad par rig par bya'o / / de la dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos rnams zhes bya ba ni / / gnas bstan pa'o / / 'phel ba dang 'grib pa zhes bya ba ni rang bzhin bstan pa ste / / 'di ltar 'phel ba yod na dad pa chen po dang ldan pa zhes bya'o / / 'grib pa yod na chung ngu dang ldan pa zhes bya'o / / thob pa dang rnyed pa dang ldan pa zhes gdags so zhes bya ba ni btags pa bstan pa'o / / de bzhin du gzhan dag la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o / / dge rgyas la 'dod chags dang bral ba zhes bya ba ni bsam gtan gsum pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba'o /
uparyavītarāgasyeti caturthadhyānāvītarāgasya
# steng ma'i 'dod chags dang ma bral ba zhes bya ba ni bsam gtan bzhi pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba'o /
niḥsaraṇasaṃjñāpūrvakeṇeti mokṣasaṃjñāpūrvakeṇa
# 'byung ba'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba zhes bya ba ni thar pa'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'o /
asthāvarāṇāmiti pravṛttivijñānasaṅgṛhītānām / nirodha iti samāpatticittakṛtaḥ kālāntaramasthāvaracittacaittasamudācāranirodho āśrayasyāvasthāviśeṣo nirudhyate 'neneti kṛtvā
# brtan pa ma yin pa rnams zhes bya ba ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pas bsdus pa rnams so / / 'gog pa zhes bya ba ni snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems kyis byas pa ste / / dus gzhan na sems dang sems las byung ba brtan pa ma yin pa kun tu 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i gnas skabs kyi bye brag go / / 'dis 'gog par 'gyur bas na 'gog pa'o /
nirodhasamāpattāvuparyavītarāgasyetyavacanai bhavāgravīta rāgasyārhato 'pi tatsaṃbhavāt / tadekatyānāṃ ca sthāvarāṇāmiti kliṣṭamanaḥsaṃgṛhītānām
# 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la ni steng ma'i 'dod chags dang ma bral ba zhes mi brjod de / / de la srid pa'i rtse mo'i 'dod chags dang bral ba'i dgra bcom pa yang yod pa'i phyir ro / / brtan pa de dag las kyang kha cig ces bya ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi yid kyis bsdus pa rnams so /
ete ca samāpattī bhūmitaḥ manaskārato 'dhiṣṭhānataḥ svabhāvataḥ prajñaptitaśca nirdeṣṭe āsaṃjñikaṃ manaskāravarjairebhireva / śeṣā adhiṣṭhānādibhistribhireva / nikāyasabhāga ekajanmikaḥ skandhasaṃtānaḥ
# snyoms par 'jug pa 'di gnyis ni sa dang yid la byed pa dang gnas dang ngo bo nyid dang btags pas bsten to / / 'du shes med pa ni yid la byed pa ma gtogs par gnas la sogs pa de dag gis lhag ma gsum po dag gis bshad do / / ris mthun pa zhes bya ba ni tshe gcig gi phung po'i rgyun no / / gnas pa'i dus nges par zhes bya ba ni ris mthun par 'dis lo brgya'am / / lo stong ngam /
sthitikālaniyama iyantaṃ kālamanenāsmin nikāyasabhāge 'vasthātavyaṃ varṣaśataṃ varṣasahasraṃ veti karmakṛtaḥ sāmarthyaviśeṣaḥ / tasmistasmin sattvanikāya iti devamanuṣyādiṣu sattvajātiṣu / ātmabhāvasadṛśatāyāmityekajātīyatāyām
# dus ji srid cig tu gnas par bya ba ste / / las kyis byas pa'i nus pa'i bye brag go / / sems can gyi ris de dang der zhes bya ba ni lha dang mi la sogs pa'i sems can gyi skye ba rnams su'o / / lus 'dra ba zhes bya ba ni rnam par gcig pa'o /
bāhyasyāpi rūpasya jātimattve nikāyasabhāgamātragrahaṇaṃ sattvasaṃtāne lakṣaṇaprajñaptijñāpanārtham
# phyir rol gyi gzugs kyang skye ba dang ldan pas ris mthun pa tsam smos te sems can gyi rgyud la mtshan nyid gdags par bstan pa'i phyir ro /
bāhyaṃ hi rūpaṃ saṃvarttavivarttaprabhāvitamā dhyātmikāstu jātijarādiprabhāvitā iti / prabandhavināśo maraṇaṃ veditavyam
# phyir rol gyi gzugs ni 'jigs pa dang 'chags pas rab tu phye ba'o / / nang gi 'du byed rnams ni skye ba dang rga ba la sogs pas rab tu phye ba'o / / rgyun 'jig pa ni 'chi bar rig par bya'o /
ete ca jātyādayo na pratikṣaṇaṃ veditavyāḥ kiṃtarhi prabandhāvasthāsviti
# skye ba la sogs pa 'di dag ni skad cig re re la rig par bya ba ni ma yin gyi / / rgyun gyi gnas skabs la bya'o /
svabhāvādhivacanaṃ cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ devo manuṣya ityevamādi
# ngo bo nyid kyi tshig bla dags zhes bya ba ni mig dang rna ba dang lha dang mi zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
viśeṣādhivacanaṃ sarvasaṃskārā anityāḥ sarvasattvā mariṣyantītyevamādi
# khyad par gyi tshig bla dags zhes bya ba ni 'du byed thams cad mi rtag pa'o / / sems can thams cad 'chi bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
tadubhayāśrayeṣvi ti svabhāvaviśeṣādhivacanāśrayeṣvakṣareṣu a i u ityevamādiṣu / etāvacca sarvaṃ yaduta svabhāvo viśeṣastadubhayavyavahāraśca tatsarvamebhiranuvyavahriyata iti
# de gnyi ga'i gnas yi ge rnams la zhes bya ba ni ngo bo nyid dang khyad par gyi tshig bla dags kyi gnas yi ge aa ai au zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / thams cad ni 'di dag tsam du zad de / / 'di ltar ngo bo nyid dang khyad par dang de gnyi gar tha snyad gdags pa'o / / de thams cad ni 'di dag gis tha snyad 'dogs te /
ata ete nāmapadavyañjanakāyā vyavasthāpitāḥ
# de'i phyir ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs 'di dag rnam par gzhag go /
paryāyākṣaraṇatāmupādāyeti yathā cakṣuścakṣurityetasmātparyāyādanyeṣvapi netrākṣinayanalocanādiṣu paryāyāntareṣu kṣarati tairapi tatsaṃjñānāt
# rnam grangs su gtogs pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni dper na mig ni mig ces bya ba'i rnam grangs de la gzhan pa 'dren byed dang gsal byed dang khrid byed dang lta ba la sogs pa rnam grangs su gtogs pa gzhan dag tu'ang 'gyur te / / de dag gis kyang de shes par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
naivaṃ a ityetadakṣaraṃ a ityetaṃ paryāyaṃ mukttvā paryāyāntareṇa śakyate jñāpayitum ataḥ paryāyākṣaraṇādakṣarāaṇi / kṣaraṇaṃ punargamanaṃ veditavyam / prabandhānupacchede pravṛttivyavasthānamekasmin kṣaṇe vyavacchinne vā tadupacārābhāvāt hetuphalanānātvamiṣṭasya phalasya sucaritamaniṣṭasya duścaritamityevamādi
# de bzhin du aa a'i zhes bya ba'i yi ge 'di ni aa a'i zhes bya ba'i rnam grangs 'di ma gtogs par rnam grangs gzhan gyis bstan pa mi nus te / / de'i phyir rnam grangs gzhan du mi 'gyur bas yi ge rnams so / / 'gyur ba ni 'gro bar rig par bya'o / / rgyun ma chad pa la 'jug par rnam par gzhag ste / / skad cig gcig gam rgyun chad pa la de nye bar 'dogs pa med pa'i phyir ro / / rgyu dang 'bras bu tha dad pa zhes bya ba la 'dod pa'i 'bras bu'i rgyu ni legs par spyod pa'o / / mi 'dod pa'i 'bras bu'i rgyu ni nyes par spyod pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste /
phalānāṃ pṛthak pṛthaganyonyahetukatvam
# 'bras bu rnams ni so sor rgyu gzhan dang gzhan las 'byung ba'o /
hetuphalasārūpyamanyatve 'pi yadyasya phalaṃ yujyate
# rgyu dang 'bras bu mthun pa ni gzhan yin du zin kyang / / gang gi 'bras bu gang 'os pa ste /
tadyathā dānasya bhogasaṃpadityevamādi / ekaikasyaiva pravṛttirayugapatpravṛttirveditavyā / hetuphalasya prabandhena pravṛttau satyāṃ yattatra hetuphalamutpannaniruddhaṃ so 'tītaḥ kāla iti prajñapyate yadanutpannaṃ so 'nāgataḥ kālaḥ yadutpannāniruddhaṃ sa pratyutpannaḥ kāla iti
# 'di ltar sbyin pa'i 'bras bu ni longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / re re nas 'byung ba zhes bya ba ni cig car mi 'byung bar rig par bya'o / / rgyu dang 'bras bu rgyun tu 'byung bar gyur pa de la rgyu dang 'bras bu byung zin pa dang 'gags zin pa gang yin pa de ni 'das pa'i dus zhes gdags so / / gang ma byung ba de ni ma 'ongs pa'i dus zhes gdags so / / gang byung ba la ma 'gags pa de ni da ltar byung ba'i dus zhes gdags so /
hetuphalasya digvyāptau deśopacāraḥ / rūpasaṃgṛhītaṃ cātra hetuphalaṃ veditavyamarūpiṇāṃ digvyāpanasāmarthyābhāvāt / pratyekaśo bhede saṃkhyetyabhinnaikātmakatve dvitrisaṃkhyādyanupapatteḥ
# rgyu dang 'bras bus phyogs la khyab pa la yul nye bar gdags ste [*te] / / gzugs can ma yin pa ni phyogs la khyab par byed pa'i mthu med pas rgyu dang 'bras bu ni 'dir gzugs su bsdus par rig par bya'o / / so so tha dad pa la grangs shes bya ba ni tha dad pa ma yin pa'i bdag nyid gcig pa la gnyis gsum zhes bya ba'i grangs la sogs pa mi 'thad pa'i phyir ro /
hetuphalapratyayānāṃ samavadhānaṃ tadyathā vijñānākhyasya hi hetuphalasyendriyāparibhedo vipayābhāsagamanaṃ tajjñānaṃ manaskārapratyupasthānaṃ ceti
# rgyu dang 'bras bu'i rkyen rnams 'dus pa ni 'di lta ste / / rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i rgyu'i 'bras bu'i rkyen ni dbang po ma nyams pa dang yul snang bar gyur ba dang de skyed pa'i yid la byed pa nye bar gnas pa ste /
evamanyatrāpi yojitavyam
# de bzhin du gzhan la yang sbyar bar rig par bya'o /
ityevamete cittaviprayuktāḥ saṃskārāṇāṃ dharmāṇāmavasthāsu prajñapanātsarve prajñaptisanto veditavyāḥ / tatra kuśalākuśalādyācayāpacayāvasthāyāmekaḥ
# de ltar na sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed kyi chos 'di rnams ni gnas skabs dag la gdags pa'i phyir / / thams cad kyang btags pa'i yod par rig par bya'o / / de la dge ba la sogs pa 'phel ba dang sgrib pa'i gnas skabs la ni gcig go /
cittacaitasikāpravṛttyavasthāyāṃ trayaḥ / sthityavasthāyāmekaḥ / sādṛśyāvasthāyāmekaḥ
# sems dang sems las byung ba mi 'byung ba'i gnas skabs la ni gsum mo / / gnas pa'i gnas skabs la ni gcig go / / 'dra ba'i gnas skabs la ni gcig go /
lakṣaṇāvasthāyāṃ catvāraḥ / vyavahārāvasthāyāṃ trayaḥ
# mtshan nyid kyi gnas skabs la ni bzhi'o / / tha snyad kyi gnas skabs la ni gsum mo /
alābhāvasthāyāmekaḥ
# ma thob pa'i gnas skabs la ni gcig go /
hetuphalāvasthāyāṃ śeṣā iti / hetuphalaṃ punaratra sarva saṃskṛtaṃ veditavyam
# rgyu dang 'bras bu'i gnas skabs la ni lhag ma rnams so / / rgyu dang 'bras bu ni 'dus byas thams cad du rig par bya ste /
tato 'nyasyotpādāddhetuḥ / anyatastadutpādāt phalamiti
# de las gzhan 'byung bas rgyu'o / / gzhan las de 'byung bas 'bras bu'o /
skandhādīnāṃ samudācāre tadbījaparipuṣṭirvāsanetyucyate
# phung po la sogs pa kun tu 'byung ba la de'i sa bon yongs su rgyas pa ni bag chags zhes bya'o /
sarvabījakaṃ teṣāmeva skandhādīnāmutpattibījairyuktatvāt
# sa bon thams cad ces bya ba ni phung po la sogs pa de dag nyid 'byung ba'i sa bon dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
ālīyante tasmin dharmā bījataḥ sattvā vātmagrāheṇetyālayavijñānam
# der chos rnams sa bon du 'du ba'am / / bdag tu 'dzin pas sems can du 'du ba'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o /
pūrvakarmanirmitatvāt vipākavijñānam
# sngon gyi las las nges par byung ba'i phyir rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa'o /
punaḥ punaḥ pratisaṃdhibandhe ātmabhāvopādānā dādānavijñānam
# yang dang yang nyid mtshams sbyor bar byed pas len pa'i rnam par shes pa'o /
tatpunaretaccittamityucyate sarvadharmavāsanācittatvāt / tadetadālayavijñānamastīti kathaṃ vijñāyate
# de ni sa zhes kyang bya ste / / chos rnams kyi bdag chags bsags pa'i phyir ro / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa de yod par ji ltar shes she na /
yasmāttena vinā
# 'di ltar de med na /
upāttamādi spaṣṭatvaṃ bījaṃ karma na yujyate
# len dang bzod dang gsal ba dang / / sa bon dang ni las rnams dang /
kāyiko 'nubhavo 'citte samāpattī cyutistathā
# lus kyis myong dang sems med pa'i / / snyoms 'jug de bzhin 'chi mi rung /
etasyāścoddānagāthāyā vibhāgastadyathā viniścayasaṃgrahaṇyāma ṣṭābhirākārairālayavijñānasyāstitā pratyetavyā
# sdom pa'i tshigs su bcad pa'i 'di'i rnam par dbye ba ni 'di lta ste rnam par nges par bsdu ba'i nang du byas so / / rnam pa brgyad kyis kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yod pa nyid du rtogs par bya ste /
tadyathāntareṇālayavijñānaṃ āśrayopādānāsaṃbhavataḥ ādipravṛtyasaṃbhavataḥ spaṣṭapravṛttyasaṃbhavato bījatvāsaṃbhavataḥ karmāsaṃbhavataḥ kāyikānubhavāsaṃbhavatācittakasamāpattyasaṃbhavato vijñānacyutyasaṃbhavataśca
# 'di ltar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na lus nye bar len pa mi srid pa dang gzod ma nas byung ba mi srid pa dang / / gsal bar byung ba mi srid pa dang sa bon mi srid pa dang las mi srid pa dang lus kyis myong ba mi srid pa dang sems med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa mi srid pa dang rnam par shes pa 'chi 'pho ba mi srid pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇenāśrayopādānaṃ na yujyate
# ci'i phyir lus nye bar len pa mi rung zhe na / / smras pa /
āha pañcabhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ
# rnam pa lngas ste [*te] /
tathāhi ālayavijñānaṃ pūrvasaṃskārahetukam / cakṣurādipravṛttivijñānaṃ punarvartamānapratyayahetukam
# 'di ltar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni sngon gyi 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung ba'o / / mig la sogs pa 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni da ltar gyi rkyen gyi rgyu las byung ba ste /
yathoktam indriyaviṣayamanaskāravaśādvijñānānāṃ pravṛttirbhavatīti vistareṇa / idaṃ prathamaṃ kāraṇam / api ca kuśalākuśalāḥ ṣaḍvijñānakāyā upalabhyante / idaṃ dvitīyaṃ kāraṇam
# ji skad du / / dbang po dang yul dang yid la byed pa'i dbang gis rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes rgya cher gsungs pa lta bu ste / / 'di ni gtan tshigs dang po'o / / yang rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug ni dge ba dang mi dge bar dmigs pa ste / / 'di ni gtan tshigs gnyis pa'o /
api ca ṣaṇṇāṃ vijñānakāyānāṃ sā jātirnopalabhyate yāvyākṛtavipākasaṃgṛhītā syāt / idaṃ tṛtīyaṃ kāraṇam
# yang rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po dag la lung du ma bstan par rnam par smin pas bsdus par 'gyur ba gang yin pa'i rnam pa mi dmigs pa ste / / 'di ni gtan tshigs gsum pa'o /
api ca pratiniyatāśrayāḥ ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥ pravartante tatra yena yenāśrayeṇa yadvijñānaṃ pravartate tadeva tenopāttaṃ syādavaśiṣṭasyānupāttateti na yujyate upāttatāpi na yujyate vijñānavirahitatayā / idaṃ caturtha kāraṇam / api ca punaḥ punarāśrayasyopādāna doṣaḥ prasajyate / tathāhi cakṣurvijñānamekadā pravartate ekadā na pravarttate evamavaśiṣṭāni
# yang rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug 'byung ba ni gnas so sor nges pa ste / / gnas gang dang gang las rnam par shes par gang dang gang 'byung ba de dang de ni des zin par 'gyur gyi lhag ma ni ma zin par 'gyur te mi rung ngo / / zin par yang mi rung ste / / rnam par shes pa med pa'i phyir ro / / 'di ni gtan tshigs bzhi pa'o / / yang dang yang lus 'dzin pa'i nyes par yang 'gyur te / / 'di ltar mig gi rnam par shes pa res 'ga' ni 'byung / / res 'ga' ni mi 'byung ngo / / lhag ma rnams kyang de bzhin te /
idaṃ pañcamaṃ kāraṇam / iti pūrvakarmapravarttamānapratyahetuto 'pi kuśalākuśalato 'pi tajjātyanupalaṃbhato 'pi pratiniyatāśrayato 'pi punaḥ punarupādānadoṣato 'pi na yujyate
# 'di ni gtan tshigs lnga pa'o / / 'di ltar sngon gyi las dang da ltar gyi 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung ba dang dge ba dang mi dge ba yin pa dang de'i rnam pa mi dmigs pa dang gnas so sor nges pa dang yang dang yang lus nye bar len pas kyang mi rung ngo /
kena kāraṇenādipravṛttisaṃbhavo na yujyate
# ci'i phyir gzod ma'i 'jug pa 'byung bar mi 'gyur zha na /
sa cetkaścidvadedyadyālaya vijñānamasti tena dvayoḥ vijñānayoḥ yugapatpravṛttirbhaviṣyati
# gal te la la zhig 'di skad du / / ci ste kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yod na de'i phyir rnam par shes pa gnyis cig car 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes zer na de la 'di skad du brjod par bya ste /
sa idaṃ syādvacanīyaḥ adoṣa eva bhavāndoṣasaṃjñī / tathāhi bhavatyeva dvayorvijñānayoryugapatpravṛttiḥ
# nyes pa med pa nyid la khyod nyes par 'du shes par zad kyi / / 'di ltar rnam par shes pa gnyis cig car 'byung ba nyid do /
tatkasya hetoḥ / tathāhyekatyasya yugapadradṣṭukāmasya yāvadvijñātukāmasyādita itaretaravijñānapravṛttirna yujyate
# de ci'i phyir zhe na / / 'di ltar kha cig cig car mthong ba 'dod pa nas / / rnam par shes pa'i bar du 'dod pa la / / thog mar rnam par shes pa gang yang rung ba zhig 'byung ba mi rung ste /
tathāhi tatra manaskāro 'pi nirviśiṣṭa indriyamapi viṣayo 'pi / kena kāraṇenāsatyāṃ yugapadvijñānapravṛttau manovijñānasya cakṣurādivijñānasahānucarasya spaṣṭatvaṃ na saṃbhavati
# 'di ltar de na yid la byed pa dang dbang po dang yul yang yod par bye brag med pa'i phyir ro / / rnam par shes pa cig car 'byung ba med na ci'i phyir mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa dang lhan cig rjes su 'jug pa yid kyi rnam par shes pa gsal bar mi 'gyur zhe na /
tathāhi yasmin samaye 'tītamanubhūtaṃ viṣayaṃ samanusmarati tasmin samaye 'vispaṣṭo manovijñānapracāro bhavati na tu tathā vartamānaviṣayo manaḥpracāro 'vispaṣṭo bhavati / ato 'pi yugapatpravṛttirvā yujyate 'vispaṣṭatvaṃ vā manovijñānasya
# 'di ltar gang gi tshe 'das pa'i yul myong ba rjes su dran pa de'i tshe yid kyi rnam par shes pa rgyu ba ni gsal ba ma yin la / / da ltar gyi yul la rgyu ba'i yid ni de ltar mi gsal ba ma yin te / / de'i phyir yang cig car 'byung ba dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa mi gsal bar yang rung ngo /
kena kāraṇena bījatvaṃ na saṃbhavati ṣaṇṇāṃ vijñānakāyānāmanyonyam / tathāhi kuśalānantaramakuśalamutpadyate akuśalānantaraṃ kuśalam tadubhayānantaramavyākṛtam hīnadhātukānantaraṃ madhyadhātukam madhyadhātukānantaraṃ praṇītadhātukam evaṃ praṇītadhātukānantaraṃ yāvaddhīnadhātukam sāsravānantaramanāsravam anāsravānantaraṃ sāsravam laukikānantaraṃ lokottaram lokottarānantaraṃ laukikam
# ci'i phyir rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug pa dag phan tshun gyi sa bon nyid ma yin zhe na / / 'di ltar dge ba'i 'og tu mi dge ba 'byung la / / mi dge ba'i 'og tu dge ba dang de gnyi ga'i 'og tu lung du ma bstan pa dang khams ngan pa'i 'og tu khams bar ma dang khams bar ma'i 'og tu khams bzang po dang de bzhin du khams bzang po'i 'og tu khams ngan pa dang zag pa dang bcas pa'i 'og tu zag pa med pa dang zag pa med pa'i 'og tu zag pa dang bcas pa dang 'jig rten pa'i 'og tu 'jig rten las 'das pa dang / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i 'og tu 'jig rten pa 'byung ste /
na ca teṣāṃ tathā bījatvaṃ yujyate
# de dag ni de ltar sa bon nyid du mi rung ngo /
dīrghakālasamucchinnāpi ca saṃtatiścireṇa kālena pravartate tasmādapi na yujyate
# rgyud kyi rgyun chad nas yun ring du lon pa yang yun ring zhig na 'byung bas de'i phyir yang mi rung ngo /
kena kāraṇenāsatyāṃ yugapadvijñānapravṛttau karma na saṃbhavati / tathāhi samāsataścaturvidhaṃ karma bhājanavijñaptirāśrayavijñaptirahamiti vijñaptirviṣayavijñaptiśceti
# rnam par shes pa cig car 'byung ba med na ci'i phyir las mi srid ce na / / 'di ltar mdor bsdur na las rnam pa bzhi ste / / snod kyi rnam par rig pa dang gnas kyi rnam par rig pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i rnam par rig pa dang yul gyi rnam par rig pa'o /
etā vijñaptayaḥ kṣaṇe kṣaṇe yugapatpravartamānā upalabhyante
# rnam par rig pa 'di dag ni skad cig gcig la cig car 'byung bar dmigs te /
na caikasya vijñānasyaikasmin kṣaṇe idamevaṃrūpaṃ vyatibhinnaṃ karma yujyate
# rnam par shes pa gcig gis skad cig gcig la ni ngo bo tha dad pa'i las 'di lta bu 'di mi rung ngo /
kena kāraṇenāsatyālayavijñāne kāyiko 'nubhavo na yujyate / tathāhyekatyasya yoniśo vāyoniśo vā cintayato vānuvitarkayato vā samāhitacetaso vāsamāhitacetaso vā ye kāye kāyānubhavā utpadyante 'nekavidhā bahunānāprakārāste na bhaveyurupalabhyante ca / tasmādapyastyālayavijñānam
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na ci'i phyir lus kyi myong ba mi rung zhe na / / 'di ltar 'ga' zhig tshul bzhin nam / / tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i sems sam / / rjes su rnam par rtog gam / / sems mnyam par bzhag gam / / sems mnyam par ma bzhag kyang rung ba ste / / lus kyis myong ba gang dag 'byung ba rnam pa du ma rnam pa sna tshogs mang po de dag 'byung ba dang dmigs par yang mi rung ste / / de'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes par yod do /
kena kāraṇe nāsatyālayavijñāne 'cittā samāpattirna saṃbhavati / tathāhya saṃjñisamāpannasya vā nirodhasamāpannasya vā vijñānameva kāyādapakrāntaṃ syāt
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na ci'i phyir sems med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa mi srid pa dang 'di ltar 'du shes med pa la snyoms par zhugs pa'i rnam par shes pa nyid lus las 'da' bar 'gyur ba'i rigs nam 'das te /
nānapakrāntaṃ tataḥ kālakriyaiva bhavet
# de'i phyir 'chi ba'i dus byed pa nyid du 'gyur ro /
yathoktam bhagavatā "vijñānaṃ cāsya kāyādanapakrāntaṃ bhavatī"ti
# ji skad du / / bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang de'i rnam par shes pa lus dang ma bral ba yin no zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o /
kena kāraṇenāsatyālayavijñāne cyutirapi na yujyate
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na / / ci'i phyir 'chi 'pho ba yang mi rung zhe na /
tathāhi cyavamānasya vijñāna mūrdhvadehaṃ vā śotikurvan vijahāti adhodehaṃ vā / na ca manovijñānaṃ kadācinna pravartate / ato 'pyālayavijñānasyaiva dehopādāna kasya vigamāddehaśītatā upalabhyate dehāpratisaṃvedanā ca
# 'di ltar 'chi ba'i rnam par shes pa lus kyi stod dam smad du drod yal bar byed cing 'dor na yid kyi rnam par shes pa ni nam yang mi 'byung ba ma yin te / / de'i phyir yang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa lus 'dzin pa nyid dang bral ba'i phyir lus drod yal ba dang lus tshor ba med par yang dmigs kyi /
na tu manovijñānasya / ato 'pi na yujyate / mano nirvacanata ālaṃbanataḥ saṃprayogataḥ pravṛttikālataśca nirdiṣṭaṃ veditavyam
# yid kyi rnam par shes pa dang bral bas ni ma yin te / / de'i phyir yang mi rigs so / / yid ni nges pa'i tshig dang dmigs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang 'byung ba'i dus kyis bstan par rig par bya'o /
mārgasaṃmukhībhāve tadabhāvaḥ paramārthajñānasyātmadṛṣṭisamudācāreṇātyantavirodhāt
# las mngon du gyur pa na de med pa ni don dam pa shes pa dang / / bdag tu lta ba kun tu 'byung ba dang shin tu mi mthun pa'i phyir ro /
tadūrdhvamālayavijñānātpravṛttiḥ śaikṣasyāprahīṇatvāt / asaṃjñisamāpattito nirodhasamāpatteḥ śāntataratvaṃ tadasamudācārādeva veditavyam
# slob pas ni ma spangs pa'i phyir de'i 'og tu yang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las byung ngo / / 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bas 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa ches zhi ba'i phyir de kun tu 'byung ba dang mi mthun par rig par bya'o /
samanantaraniruddhaṃ mano 'numatamiti kṛtvānantaraṃ matamityarthaḥ / vijñānasyāśrayata ālaṃbanataḥ svabhāvataśca vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# 'gags ma thag pa yang yid du 'dod pas 'gags ma thag pa'i yid ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / rnam par shes pa ni gnas dang dmigs pa dang ngo bo nyid kyis rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
dhātvāyatanānāṃ nāsti pṛthaglakṣaṇavyavasthānam skandhanirdeśa eva cakṣurādīnāmuktalakṣaṇatvāt
# khams dang skye mched rnams kyi mtshan nyid ni logs shig du rnam par gzhag tu med de / / phung po bstan pa'i skabs su mig la sogs pa nye bar mtshon pa'i phyir te /
tasmātskandhebhya eva niṣkṛṣya dhātavo vyavasthāpyante dhātubhya āyatanāni
# de bas na phung po rnams las dmigs kyis bton te / / khams rnams rnam par gzhag go / / khams rnams las dmigs kyis bton te skye mched rnams rnam par gzhag go /
yattu skandhairasaṃgṛhītamasaṃskṛtaṃ tadaṣṭadhāvyavasthāpya iti / tathatāyāstraividhyamāśrayaprakārabhedānna svabhāvabhedāditi veditavyam
# phung po rnams kyis gang ma bsdus pa 'dus ma byas pa de ni rnam pa brgyad du rnam par gzhag go / / de bzhin nyid rnam pa gsum ni gnas kyi rnam pas tha dad kyi ngo bo nyid kyis tha dad pa ni ma yin par rig par bya'o /
ananyathīma vatā sadaiva bhāvanāṃ nirātmatayā draṣṭavyā
# gzhan du mi 'gyur ba nyid ces bya ba ni rtag tu dngos po rnams kyi bdag med pa nyid du blta bar bya'o /
saṃkleśāpracāratāmupādāyeti tenālabanena saṃkleśavastunaḥ saṃkleśaśūnyīkaraṇāt / yadāpi saṃkliṣṭetyucyate tadāpyāgantukastatropakleśo veditavyaḥ
# kun nas nyon mongs pa mi rgyu ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni de la dmigs pas kun nas nyon mongs pa'i dngos po kun nas nyon mongs pas stongs par byed pa'i phyir ro / / gang gi tshe kun nas nyon mongs pa can zhes bya ba de'i tshe yang de la glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs par rig par bya ste /
katamaḥ punarāgantukastatropakleśaḥ
# chos rnams kyi chos nyid ni rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba'o /
anapoddhṛtagrāhyagrāhakabījasya paratantracittasya dvayākārā pravṛttiḥ / na dharmatā cittasya
# mtshan ma rnams ni gzugs dang tshor ba nas byang chub ces bya ba'i bar du spros pa rnams te /
prakṛtiprabhāsvarā hi sarvadharmāṇāṃ dharmateti
# de la de dag nye bar zhi ba'i phyir mtshan ma med pa'o /
nimittāni rūpaṃ vedanā yāvadbodhiriti prapañcitāni teṣāṃ tatropaśamādanimittam / bhūtaṃ yadaviparītam tasya koṭiḥ paryantaḥ nairātmyātpareṇa tattvāparyepaṇāt / ākāśaṃ rūpābhāva iti rūpasyava viparyayeṇābhāvalakṣaṇo yo dharmo manovijñānaviṣayastadākāśam / manovijñānaviṣayatva punaḥ dharmadhātvadhikāratvena veditavyam
# yang dag pa ni gang phyin ci ma log pa'o / / de'i mtha' ni mur thug pa ste / / bdag med pa las pha rol tu de kho na btsal du med pa'i phyir ro / / nam mkha' ni gzugs med ces bya ba ni gzugs nyid las bzlog pa gzugs med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi chos yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i yul gang yin pa de ni nam mkha'o / / yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i yul ni chos kyi khams kyi skabs yin par rig par bya'o /
rūpasyaivetyavadhāraṇādvedanādisādhāraṇāstathatāpratisaṃkhyāpratisaṃkhyānirodhānityatāḥ paryudāsyante
# gzugs nyid ces bya ba ni rnam pa'i phyir te / / tshor ba la sogs pa dang thun mong ba'i de bzhin nyid dang so sor brtags pa ma yin pa dang so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa dang mi rtag pa nyid sel to /
śaśavipāṇādīnāmatyantamabhāvo na teṣāṃ viparyayeṇa vijñāyate
# ri bong gi rva la sogs pa ni gtan med pa ste / / de dag las bzlog par ni mi shes so /
yasmātta evātyantaṃ na saṃbhavantīti
# de ltar de dag ni gtan nas med pa'i phyir ro /
te 'pi śaśaviṣāṇādayo nāsyaiva vidyamānasya rūpasya viparyayeṇa vedanādisādhāraṇatvāt
# ri bong gi rva la sogs pa de dag ni gzugs yod pa 'di las bzlog pa ma yin te / / tshor ba la sogs pa dang thun mong ba'i phyir ro /
tasmādrūpasyaiva viparyayeṇetyucyate / abhāvalakṣaṇavacanena vedanādonāmarūpiṇāṃ paryudāsaḥ
# de bas na gzugs nyid las bzlog pa zhes bya'o / / gang gzugs ma yin pa zhes brjod par bya ste / / med pa'i mtshan nyid kyi tshig gis tshor ba la sogs pa gzugs can ma yin pa rnams gsal te /
na hi te 'bhāvalakṣaṇā iti
# de dag ni med pa'i mtshan nyid ni ma yin no /
yo nirodho na ca visaṃyoga ityanuśayāsamuddhātāt
# gang 'gog la bral ba ma yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni bag la nyal ma bcom pa'o /
viparyayādvisaṃyogaḥ / dvayamidaṃ prahātavyam kleśāśca tadāśrayabhūtaṃ ca vastu veditam
# bzlog pa ni bral ba'o / / spang par bya ba de ni gnyis te / / nyon mongs pa rnams dang de'i gnas su gyur pa tshor ba'o / / tshor ba de yang rnam pa gnyis te /
tatpunarveditaṃ dvividham vaikārikamavaikārikaṃ ca sukhaduḥkhamaduḥkhāsukhaṃ ca yathākramam / tatra kleśaprahāṇāt pratisaṃkhyānirodhavyavasthānam
# 'gyur bar byed pa dang 'gyur bar mi byed pa ste / / bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang bde ba yang ma yin sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa dang go rims bzhin no / / de la nyon mongs pa spong bas so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa rnam par gzhag go /
dvividhaveditaprahāṇādyathākramamāniñjyasya saṃjñāvedayitanirodhasya ca vyavasthānam / tatra kleśaprahāṇaṃ tatpakṣadauṣṭhulyāpagamādāśrayaparivṛttiḥ veditaprahāṇaṃ tatpratipakṣabhūtāyāḥ samāpatterāvaraṇāpagamādāśrayaparivṛttiḥ
# tshor ba rnam pa gnyis spong bas mi g yo ba dang 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa dang go rims bzhin du rnam par gzhag go / / de la nyon mongs pa spong bas na de'i phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len dang bral ba'i phyir gnas gyur ba'o / / tshor ba spong ba ni de'i gnyen por gyur pa snyoms par 'jug pa'i sgrib pa dang bral ba'i phyir gnas gyur ba'o /
ata eva dvitīye dhyāne duḥkhanirodhasyāsaṃskṛtāvyavasthānam vaikārikasya veditasyāśeṣamaprahāṇāt / rūpaskandhena daśarūpiṇo dhātavaḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ dharmadhātunā sa eva mana āyatanena sapta vijñānadhātava ityevaṃ sarvadharmāstrayo bhavanti
# de'i phyir bsam gtan gnyis par sdug bsngal 'gog pa la 'dus ma byas rnam par mi gzhag ste / / 'gyur bar byed pa'i tshor ba ma lus par ma spangs pa'i phyir ro / / gzugs kyi phung pos ni khams gzugs can bcu bsdus so / / chos kyi khams kyis ni de nyid bsdus so / / yid kyi skye mched kyis ni rnam par shes pa'i khams bdun bsdus te / / de ltar na chos thams cad ni gsum du 'gyur ro /
evaṃ vyavasthāpiteṣu skandhadhātvāyataneṣvānuṣaṃgikametadvayutpādyate
# bam po gnyis pa / / phung po dang khams dang skye mched de ltar rnam par gzhag pa la zhar las 'byung ba de bstan par bya'o /
cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇānāṃ pratyekaṃ dvitve sati kathaṃ dhātūnāṃ naikaviṃśatitvam / yadyapi caiṣāṃ dvitvaṃ na tu dhātvantaratvam lakṣaṇasādharmyeṇobhayoścakṣurlakṣaṇatvāt kṛtyasādharmyeṇobhayoścakṣurvijñānakṛtyatvāt
# mig dang rna ba dang sna rnams so so la yang gnyis gnyis yod na khams nyi shu rtsa gcig tu ji ltar mi 'gyur zhe na / / de dag gnyis gnyis yod du zin kyang / / gnyi ga yang mig gi mtshan nyid yin pas mtshan nyid 'dra ba dang gnyi ga'i bya ba mig gi rnam par shes pa yin par gcig pa'i phyir bya ba mthun pas khams gzhan ma yin no /
evaṃ śrotraghrāṇayoryojyam / dvayordvayostu nirvṛttirāśrayaśobhārtham
# rna ba dang sna la'ang de bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o / / gnyis su grub pa ni gnas mdzes pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ suvibhaktasamobhayapārśva āśrayaḥ śobhano nānyathā / kimekaikameva cakṣurniśritya cakṣurvijñānamutpadyate nityamāhosviddva api
# 'di ltar ngos gnyis shin tu rnam par 'byed na gnas mdzes kyi gzhan du ni ma yin no / / ci mig re re la brten te mig gi rnam par shes pa rtag tu 'byung ba 'on te gnyi ga la yang brten /
dve apītyucyate spaṣṭagrahaṇāt
# smras pa gsal bar 'dzin pa'i phyir /
yathā dvayoścakṣuṣorunmiṣitayoḥ rūpagrahaṇaṃ spaṣṭaṃ bhavati na tathaikasminneveti
# gnyi ga la brten nas 'byung ste / / dper na mig gnyi ga phye na gzugs 'dzin pa la gsal bar 'gyur gyi / / gcig gis ni de lta ma yin no /
tadyathā ekasminnapavarake dvayoḥ pradīpayorekaṃ prabhāpratānaṃ spaṣṭataraṃ dvau pradīpau niśritya varttate
# dper na khang pa gcig tu mar me gnyis bus na / / mar me gnyis la brten nas 'od rgyas pa cig gis shin tu gsal bar 'gyur ro /
tadvadatrāpi nayo draṣṭavyaḥ
# de bzhin du 'dir yang tshul de ltar blta bar bya'o /
ekaikenendriyadvāreṇa vicitraviṣayapratyupasthāne tatprakāreṣu kiṃ krameṇa vijñānānyutpadyante āhosyidyugapadekam
# de'i yul sna tshogs nye bar gnas par gyur na de'i rnam pa rnams la dbang po re re'i sgo nas rnam par shes pa rnams rim gyis 'byung ngam / / 'on te gcig gis cig car 'dzin zhe na /
yugapadekameva vicitrākāraṃ vijñānaṃ veditavyam / jihvāsaṃprāpte kavaḍe jihvākāyavijñānayornityaṃ yugapadutpattirveditavyā
# rnam par shes pa gcig kho nas cig car 'dzin te / / rnam pa ni sna tshogs su rig par bya'o / / lce la kham gyi zas reg na lca dang lus kyi rnam par shes pa rtag tu cig car 'byung bar rig par bya'o /
śabdasyoccheditvānna deśāntareṣvaparāparotpattisaṃtānena deśāntaragamanamasti kiṃtarhi sakṛt / yathā svaprade śamavaṣṭabhya pradīpapratānavat śabdapratānasyotpādo draṣṭavyaḥ / yattvāsannatiraskṛtasya śabdasyāspaṣṭaṃ śravaṇaṃ bhavati tacchabdasya pratighātitvādāvaraṇasauṣiryasvalpoktito veditavyam
# sgra ni rgyun chad pa'i phyir yul gzhan dag tu gcig nas gcig tu brgyud de 'byung ba'i rgyun gyis yul gzhan du 'gro ba med kyi 'di lta ste rang gi yul na 'dug cing thang cig 'byung ste / / mar me'i 'od rgyas pa bzhin du sgra rgyas pa 'byung ba yang de ltar blta'o / / nye yang bar du bcad pa'i sgra gsal bar mi thos pa'i sgra de thogs pa yod pa'i phyir rtsig pa'i gseb nas chung ngu 'byung bar rig par bya'o /
ṣaṇṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ kati vijñānāni savikalpakāni katyavikalpakāni
# rnam par shes pa drug po dag las rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa na du zhig / / rnam par mi rtog pa ni du zhig ce na /
tribhistāvadvikalpaiḥ manovijñānamekaṃ savikalpakam / trayo vikalpāḥsvabhāvavikalpo 'nusmaraṇavikalpo 'bhinirūpaṇāvikalpaśca
# rnam par rtog pa gsum gyis yid kyi rnam par shes pa gcig pu rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa ste / / rnam par rtog pa gsum ni rang bzhin gyi rnam par rtog pa dang rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang mngon par spyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o /
tatra svabhāvavikalpaḥ pratyutpanneṣu saṃskāreṣvanubhūyamāneṣu yaḥ svalakṣaṇākāro vikalpaḥ
# de la rang bzhin gyi rnam par rtog pa ni de ltar 'byung ba'i 'du byed myong ba na gang rang gi mtshan nyid kyi rnam pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o /
anusmaraṇavikalpo yo 'nubhūtapūrvasaṃskārākāraḥ
# rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni / / gang sngon myong ba'i 'du byed kyi rnam par rtog pa'o /
abhinirūpaṇāvikalpo yo 'tītānāga tapratyutpanneṣu viparokṣeṣvabhyūhanākāro vikalpaḥ
# mngon par spyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni gang 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar gyi lkog tu gyur pa rnams la mngon par rtogs pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o /
api khalu sapta vikalpāḥ ālaṃbane svarasavāho vikalpaḥ sanimitto 'nimittaḥ paryeṣakaḥ pratyavekṣakaḥ kliṣṭo 'kliṣṭaśca vikalpaḥ
# yang rnam par rtog pa bdun te / / dmigs pa la rang gi ngang gis 'jug pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang mtshan ma dang bcas pa dang mtshan ma med pa dang kun tu tshol bar byed pa dang so sor rtag pa dang nyon mongs pa can dang nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i rnam pa'i rnam par rtog pa'o /
tatra ādyo vikalpaḥ pañca vijñānakāyāḥ acitrayitvālaṃbanaṃ yathāsvaṃ viṣayeṣu svarasenaiva vahanāt
# de la rnam par rtog pa dang po ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug ste / / dmigs pa la bkra bar ma bzung bar rang gi yul ji lta ba bzhin du rang gi dang gis 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
sanimittaḥ svabhāvānusmaraṇavikalpo vartamānātītaviṣayacitrīkaraṇāt
# mtshan ma dang bcas pa ni rang bzhin dang rjes su dran pa'i rnam par rtog pa ste / / da ltar dang 'das pa'i yul la bkra bar 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
animitto 'nāgataviṣayo manorathākāro vikalpaḥ śeṣā abhinirūpaṇāvikalpasvabhāvā veditavyāḥ
# mtshan ma med pa ni ma 'ongs pa'i yul yid la brnags pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang yin pa'o / / lhag ma rnams ni mngon par spyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i ngo bo nyid du rig par bya ste /
tathāhyekadābhyūhamānaḥ paryeṣate ekadā pratyavekṣate ekadā kliṣṭo bhavati ekadākliṣṭa iti / yadā rūpādiprativijñaptikaṃ vijñānaṃ tatkena kāraṇena cakṣurādivijñānamityucyate na rūpādibhijñānamiti
# 'di ltar res 'ga' ni mngon par rtog cing kun tu tshol lo / / res 'ga' ni so sor rtog go / / res 'ga' ni nyon mongs pa can du 'gyur ro / / res 'ga' ni nyon mongs pa can ma yin no / / gang gi tshe gzugs la sogs pa'i so sor rnam par rig pa'i rnam par shes pa de ci'i phyir mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'i gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes mi bya zhe na /
pañcavidhavigrahopapatteḥ rūpādivacanānupapattiḥ
# tshig rnam par sbyar ba rnam pa lnga 'thad pa dang gzugs la sogs pa'i tshig mi 'thad pa'i phyir ro /
kathamiti / cakṣuṣi vijñānaṃ cakṣurvijñānam āśrayadeśe vijñānotpattitaḥ sati ca tasmistadbhāvāt
# ji lta zhe na / / mig la rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste / / gnas kyi yul la rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / de yod na de'ang yod pa'i phyir te /
tathāhi sati cakṣuṣi cakṣurvijñānamavaśyamutpadyate anandhānāmanandhato 'ndhakārasyāpi darśanāt
# 'di ltar mig yod na long ba ma yin pa rnams kyi mig gi rnam par shes pa 'byung ste / / tha na mun pa na yang mthong ba'i phyir ro /
na rūpe satyavaśyam andhānāmadarśanāditi / cakṣuṣā vijñānaṃ cakṣuvijñānam tadvaśenāvikṛte 'pi rūpe vijñānasya vikriyāgamanatvāt / tadyathā kāmalavyādhyupahatena cakṣuṣā nīlādirūpeṣvapi pītadarśanameva bhavatīti / cakṣuṣo vijñānaṃ cakṣurvijñānam vijñānabījānubandhāccakṣuṣastannirvṛtteḥ
# gzugs yod du zin kyang gdon mi za bar 'byung ba ma yin te / / long ba rnams kyis mi mthong ba'i phyir ro / / mig gi rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste / / gzugs ma gyur kyang de'i dbang gis rnam par shes pa 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / dper na mig ser gyi nad kyis btab na gzugs sngon po la sogs pa la yang mig gis ser po nyid du mthong ba lta bu'o / / mig las rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste / / mig ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i sa bon dang 'brel ba ste / / de las 'grub pa'i phyir ro /
cakṣuṣe vijñānam tasmai hitāhitatvāt / tathāhi vijñānasaṃprayuktenānubhavenendriyasyānugraha upaghāto vā bhavati na viṣayasyeti
# mig gi phyir rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste de la phan pa'i phyir ro / / 'di ltar rnam par shes pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i myong bas dbang po la phan gnod du 'gyur gyi yul la ni ma yin no /
cakṣurvijñānaṃ cakṣurvijñānam ubhayoḥ sattvasaṃkhyātatvāt na tvavaśyaṃ rūpasyeti / kiṃ tāvaccakṣū rūpāṇi paśyatīti veditavyamatha vijñānam
# mig dang mtshungs pa'i rnam par shes pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste / / gnyi ga yang sems can gyi grangs su gtogs pa'i phyir ro / / gzugs ni gdon mi za bar sems can gyi grangs su gtogs pa ma yin no / / ci mig gis gzugs rnams mthong ngam / / 'on te rnam par shes pas mthong zhe na /
naikaṃ nāparaṃ paśyatīti veditavyam nirvyāpāratvāt dharmāṇām / sāmagrayāṃ tu satyāṃ darśanaprajñaptiḥ
# chos rnams ni byed pa med pa'i phyir gcig gis kyang mi mthong la / / cig shos kyis kyang mi mthong bar rig par bya ste / / tshogs par gyur pa las mthong bar gdags so /
api khalu ṣaḍbhirākāraiḥ cakṣuṣo rūpadarśane prādhānyaṃ veditavyaṃ na vijñānasya
# yang rnam pa drug gis ni mig gis gzugs mthong ngo zhes gtso bor rig par bya'o / / rnam par shes pas ni ma yin no /
katamaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ / utpattikāraṇa taḥ cakṣuṣastadutpatteḥ
# rnam pa drug gang zhe na / / 'byung ba'i rgyu'i phyir mig las de 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
tatpadasthānataḥ darśanasya cakṣurāśrayaṇāt / acalavṛttitaḥ cakṣuṣo nityamekajātīyatvāt
# de'i gnas kyi phyir mthong ba'i rten mig yin pa'i phyir ro / / mi g yo bar 'jug pa'i phyir mig ni rtag tu rigs gcig pa'i phyir ro /
svatantravṛttitaḥ pratikṣaṇamutpattipratyayasāmagryanapekṣatvāt
# rang dbang du 'jug pa'i phyir skad cig re re la 'byung ba rkyen tshogs pa la mi ltos pa'i phyir ro /
śobhāvṛttitaḥ tenāśrayaśobhanāt
# mdzes par 'jug pa'i phyir des gnas mdzes pa'i phyir ro /
āgamataḥ "cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭve" ti vacanāt
# lung gi phyir mig gis gzugs rnams mthong ngo zhes gsungs pa'i phyir te /
etacca yathoktaṃ sarva vijñānasya na saṃbhavatīti
# ji skad du bshad pa de thams cad ni rnam par shes pa la mi srid pa'i phyir ro /
calavṛttitvaṃ tvasya bahuprakārotpattito veditavyam / yathā dhātuṣvāyataneṣu cāsaṃskṛtaṃ vyavasthāpitamevaṃ kasmānna skandheṣvapi vyavasthāpitam / skandhārthāsaṃbhavāt
# 'di ni rnam pa mang por 'byung bas g yo bar 'jug pa nyid du rig par bya'o / / ji ltar khams rnams dang skye mched rnams la 'dus ma byas rnam par gzhag pa de bzhin du phung po rnams la ci'i phyir rnam par ma bzhag ce na / / phung po'i don med pa'i phyir ro /
rūpādīnāmatītādiprakārābhisaṃkṣepeṇa rāśyarthaḥ skandhārtho nirdiṣṭaḥ
# gzugs la sogs pa ni 'das pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa dag gis bsdus te / / spungs pa'i don ni phung po'i don du bstan la /
sa ca nityasya na saṃbhavatīti na skandheṣvasaṃskṛtavyavasthānam
# de ni rtag tu yod pa ma yin pas phung po rnams la 'dus ma byas rnam par mi gzhag go /
kena kāraṇena ta eva dharmā skandhadhātvāyatanamukhaiḥ pṛthagdeśitāḥ / vineyānāṃ samāsavyāsanirdeśakauśalyotpādanārtham
# ci'i phyir chos 'di rnams phung po dang khams 'di rnams skye mched kyi sgo nas logs shig tu bshad ce na / / gdul bya rnams bsdus pa dang rgyas par bstan pa la mkhas pa bskyed pa'i phyir te /
tathāhi skandhanirdeśe ye rūpavijñāne samāsena nirdiṣṭe te dhātvāyataneṣvekādaśadhā / saptadhā ca bhittvā vyāsena nirdiṣṭe yathāyogam
# 'di ltar phung po bstan pa la gzugs dang rnam par shes pa gang dag mdor bstan pa de dag khams dang skye mched rnams la rnam pa bcu gcig dang rnam pa bdun du phye nas rgyas par bstan te ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
ye tu tatra vedanādayo vyastāḥ te dhātvāyataneṣu dharmadhātvāyatanatvena samastā iti / api khalu lakṣaṇamātravyavasthānataḥ skandhanirdeśaḥ grāhyagrāhakagrahaṇavyavasthānato dhātunirdeśaḥ grahaṇāya dvārabhūtasya grāhyagrāhakamātrasya vyavasthānata āyatananirdeśo veditavyaḥ
# der tshor ba la sogs pa gang dag rgyas par bstan pa de dag ni khams dang skye mched rnams su chos kyi khams dang skye mched du bsdus te bstan to / / yang mtshan nyid tsam rnam par gzhag pas phung po bstan to / / 'dzin pa dang gzung ba dang 'dzin par byed pa rnam par gzhag pas khams bstan to / / 'dzin par byed pa skye ba'i sgor gyur pa gzung ba dang 'dzin pa tsam rnam par gzhag pas skye mched bstan par rig par bya'o /
samāptamānuṣaṃgikam
# zhar las byung ba rdzogs s+ho /
ataḥ paraṃ mūlagranthasyaivārthanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ
# 'di man chad du ni rtsa ba'i gzhung nyid kyi don bshad par blta'o /
arhataścaramaṃ cakṣuḥ parinirvāṇakāle paścimam / tatra dhātuḥ cakṣurantarasyāhetutvāt / ārūpyopapannasya pṛthagjanasya cakṣurheturiti tataḥ pracyutya rūpiṇi dhātāvupapadyamānasya yasmādālayavijñānasaṃniviṣṭāccakṣurbījācca kṣurnirvartiṣyate na tvāryasya punaranāgamanāditi
# dgra bcom pa tha ma'i mig go zhes bya ba ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i dus tha ma ste / / de ni mig gzhan gyi rgyu yin pas khams ma yin no / / gzugs med par skyes pa'i so so'i skye bo'i mig gi rgyu'o zhes bya ba ni de nas shi 'phos te / / gzugs can gyi khams su skye ba'i mig gi sa bon kun gzhi'i rnam par shes pa la gnas pa las 'di ltar yang mig mngon par 'grub par 'gyur ba ste / / yang phyir mi 'ong bas na 'phags pa rnams kyis ni ma yin no /
kāyadhāturna kāya ārūpyopapannasya pṛthagjanasya yaḥ kāyadhāturityetadatra vaktavyam aṇḍagatādīnāṃ kāyasaṃbhavāt pranaṣṭakāyasya cājīvitasvāditi
# lus kyi khams yin la lus ma yin pa la yang gzugs med par skyes pa'i so so'i skye bo'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba 'dir brjod par bya ste / / sgo nga'i nang na 'dug pa la sogs pa la ni lus yod pa'i phyir ro / / lus zhig pa ni mi 'tsho ba'i phyir ro /
syānmanodhāturna mana ityatrāsaṃjñisamāpanna syāgrahaṇam kliṣṭamanaḥsadbhāvāt
# yid kyi khams yid la yid ma yin pa'ang yod ces bya ba la / / 'dir 'du shes med pa la snyoms par zhugs pa ma smos pa ni nyon mongs pa can gyi yid yod pa'i phyir ro /
jāto bhūtaḥ nirvṛtti vṛddhi cādhikṛtya yathākramam / ārūpyāvacareṇa manasārūpyāvacarān svabhūmikānanāsravāṃśca dharmān vijānātītyāryaśrāvakamadhikṛtya / bāhyakaḥ pṛthagjanaḥ svabhūmikāneva vijānātīti / iha dhārmikastu kaścitpūrvaśrutaparibhāvanāvaśādūrdhvabhūmikānapyālaṃbate tadutpādanārtham / yathā rūpaṃ tathānubhava iti sukhādivedanīyādindriyārthadvayātsukhādivedanotpatteḥ
# byung zhing skyes par gyur zhes bya ba ni 'grub pa dang rgyas par 'gyur ba'i dbang du byas pa ste go rims bzhin no / / gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i yid kyis gzugs med pa na spyod par rang gis pa rnams dang zag pa med pa'i chos rnams kyang shes so zhes bya ba ni 'phags pa nyan thos kyi dbang du byas pa ste / / phyi rol gyi so so'i skye bo ni rang gi sa pa rnams nyid rnam par shes kyi chos 'di pa ni la la sngon thos pas yongs su bsgoms pa'i dbang gis sa gong ma la yang dmigs te bskyed pa'i phyir ro / / gzugs ji lta ba de bzhin du myong ngo zhes bya ba ni bde ba la sogs pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i dbang po dang yul gnyis las bde ba la sogs pa'i 'tshor ba 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
yathā vedayate tathā saṃjānīta iti yathānubhavaṃ nimittodgrahaṇāt
# tshor bar byed pa ji lta ba de bzhin du 'du shes su byed do zhes bya ba ni ji ltar myong ba de bzhin du mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
yathā saṃjānīte tathā cetayati yathāsaṃjñaṃ karmābhisaṃskaraṇāt
# ji ltar 'du shes su byed pa de bzhin du sems par byed do zhes bya ba ni 'du shes ji lta ba de bzhin du mngon par 'du byed pa'i phyir ro /
yathā cetayate tathā vijñānaṃ tatra tatropagaṃ bhavatīti yathābhisaṃskāraṃ viṣayeṣu gatyantareṣu ca vijñānapariṇāmāt
