# sems par byed pa ji lta ba de bzhin du rnam par shes par byed de / / de dang der nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba ni ji ltar mngon par 'dus byas pa'i yul rnams la 'gro ba gzhan rnams su rnam par shes par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
yatra saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate ceti sendriye kāye / yenānubhaveneti sāmiṣanirāmiṣādyena yathākramam
# gang ba kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba zhes bya ba ni dbang po dang bcas pa'i lus la'o / / myong ba gang gis zhes bya ba ni zang zing dang bcas pa dang zang zing med pa la sogs pa dang go rims bzhin no /
yena nimittagrahaṇābhisaṃskāreṇetyayoniśo yoniśaśca pravṛttena
# mtshan mar 'dzin pa dang mngon par 'du byed pa gang gis zhes bya ba ni tshul bzhin ma yin pa dang tshul bzhin du 'jug pas so /
yatsaṃkliśyate vyavadāyate ceti cittadauṣṭhulyādauṣṭhulyopapattitaḥ / ekādaśavidhāttṛṣṇāprakārādrūpādīnāmatītādiprakāravyavasthāna veditavyam / sā punaḥ apekṣātṛṣṇā abhinandanātṛṣṇā adhyavasānatṛṣṇā āmatṛṣṇā viṣayatṛṣṇā kāmatṛṣṇā samāpattitṛṣṇā duścaritaduḥkhatṛṣṇā sucaritasukhatṛṣṇā viprakṛṣṭatṛṣṇā sanikṛṣṭatṛṣṇā ca
# gang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba zhes bya ba ni sems gnas ngan len dang bcas pa dang gnas ngan len med par 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / srid pa rnam pa bcu gcig gi skabs kyi gzugs la sogs pa 'das pa la sogs pa'i rnam pas rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / de yang bltas pa'i srid pa dang mngon par dga' ba'i srid pa dang lhag par chags pa'i sred pa dang bdag la sred pa dang yul la sred pa dang 'dod pa la sred pa dang snyoms par 'jug pa la sred pa dang nyes par spyad pa'i sdug bsngal la sred pa dang lags par spyad pa'i bde ba la sred pa dang ring ba la sred pa dang nye ba la sred pa ste /
asyāḥ tṛṣṇāyā ālaṃbanatvena yathākramamatītādayaḥ prakārā yojitavyāḥ
# sred pa 'di dag gi dmigs pa nyid kyis go rims bzhin du 'das pa la sogs pa'i rnam par sbyor bar bya'o /
aparaḥ paryāyaḥ / utpannānutpannabhedato grāhakagrāhyabhedato bahirmukhāntarmukhabhedataḥ kliṣṭākliṣṭabhedato viprakṛṣṭasaṃnikṛṣṭabhedataśvātītādīni yathāyogaṃ veditavyāni / tatrotpannamatītaṃ pratyutpannaṃ ca
# yang rnam grangs gzhan du na byung ba dang ma byung ba'i bye brag dang 'dzin pa dang gzung ba'i bye brag dang phyi rol du bltas pa dang nang du bltas pa'i bye brag dang nyon mongs pa can dang nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i bye brag dang ring ba dang nye ba'i bye brag dang 'das pa la sogs pa ji ltar mthun mthun du rig par bya'o / / de la byung ba ni 'das pa dang da ltar ro /
anutpannamanāgatam
# ma byung ba ni ma 'ongs pa'o /
vahirmukhamasamāhitabhūmikam / antarmukhaṃ samāhitabhūmikam / śiṣṭaḥ sugamatvānna vibhaktaḥ
# 'dzin pa ni nang gi'o / / gzung ba ni phyi'o / / phyi rol du bltas pa ni mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i sa pa'i'o / / nang du bltas pa ni mnyam par bzhag pa'i sa pa'i'o / / lhag ma ni go sla bas ma bshad do /
duḥkhavaipulyalakṣaṇatāmupādāyeti rūpādisaṃniśrayeṇa jātthādiduḥkhapratānāt
# sdug bsngal ni shin tu rgyas pa'i mtshan nyid kho na'i phyir te zhes bya ba ni gzugs la sogs pa la brten nas skye ba la sogs pa'i sdug bsngal rgyas par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
saṃkleśabhārodvahanaṃ rūpādyāśritatvāt kleśādisaṃkleśasya / tadyathā loke yena śarīrapradeśena bhāra uhyate tatra skandhopacāro dṛṣṭaḥ skandhena bhāramuddhahatīti
# kun nas nyon mongs pa khur khyer ba nyid kyi phyir te zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa la sogs pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa / / gzugs la sogs pa la brten pa'i phyir te / / dper na 'jig rten na phrag pas khur khyer ba'i phyir lus kyi phyogs gang gis khur khyer ba de la phrag pa zhes 'dogs pa mthong ste dang mtshungs so /
sarvadharmabījārtha iti hetvarthamadhikṛtyālayavijñāne / kāryakāraṇabhāvadhāraṇamaṣṭādaśasu dhātuṣu ṣaṇṇāṃ vijñānadhātūnāmindriyārthadhātūnāṃ ca yathākramam
# chos thams cad kyi sa bon gyi don to zhes bya ba ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la rgyu'i dbang du byas pa dang rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin pa'i don to / / 'bras bu dang rgyu'i dngos por 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni khams bco brgyad po dag la rnam par shes pa'i khams drug dang dbang po dang don gyi khams rnam go rims bzhin no /
sarvaprakāradharmasaṃgrahaṇena sūtrāntaranirdiṣṭānāṃ pṛthivīdhātvādīnāmanyeṣāmapi dhātūnāmeṣvevāṣṭādaśasu yathāyogaṃ saṃgrahaṇādveditavyam / bījārthaḥ sarvaprakāradharmasaṃgrahārthaścāyatanārtho 'pi veditavyaḥ
# chos kyi rnam par thams cad bsdus nas 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni mdo sde gzhan dag las sa'i khams la sogs pa dang khams gzhan dag bstan pa dag kyang khams bco brgyad po 'di dag gi nang du ji ltar mthun mthun du bsdu bar rig par bya'o / / sa bon gyi don dang chos kyi rnam pa thams cad bsdus pa'i don ni skye mched kyi don du yang rig par bya'o /
rūpādānāṃ phenapiṇḍo pamatvamasato riktataḥ tucchato 'sārataśca khyānādveditavyam
# gzugs la sogs pa ni dbu ba rdos pa la sogs pa lta bu nyid de / / med pa dang gso ba dang gsog dang snying po med par snang bar rig par bya'o /
eteṣāṃ punaḥ sūtrapadānāmartha ātmaśucisukhanityaviparyāsapratipakṣeṇa yathākramamanātmatāmupādāyetyevamādibhiḥ padarveditavyaḥ / kathaṃ kati kimarthibhiriti praśnatrayavyavasthāpanaṃ lakṣaṇavastusaṃmohayoḥ samāropasya ca prahāṇārtham / tatra kathaṃ dravyasaditi dravyasato lakṣaṇanirdeśena tatsaṃmohaḥ prahīyate / sarvāṇi dravyasantītyanena vastusaṃmohaḥ prahīyate ātmadravyābhiniveśatyājanārthamityanena samāropaḥ prahīyate
# mdo'i tshig 'di rnams kyi don ni bdag dang gtsang ba dang bde ba dang rtag par phyin ci log pa'i gnyen po ste / / bdag med pa nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i tshig rnams go rims bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o / / ji ltar du zhig ci'i phyir zhes 'dri ba gsum rnam par 'jog pa ni mtshan nyid dang dngos po la rmongs pa dang sgro 'dogs pa spong ba'i phyir ro / / de la ji ltar rdzas su yod ces bya ba ni rdzas su yod pa'i mtshan nyid bstan pas de la rmongs pa spong ngo / / thams cad kyang rdzas su yod pa'o zhes bya ba 'dis ni dngos po la rmongs pa spong ba dag la rdzas su mngon par zhen pa spong ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba 'dis ni sgro 'dogs pa spong ngo /
evamanyatrāpi yojyam / abhilāpanirapekṣa indriyagocarastadyathā rūpaṃ vedanetyevamādikaṃ nāmnācitrayitvā yasyārthasya grahaṇaṃ bhavati
# de bzhin du gzhan rnams la'ang sbyor byar bya'o / / dbang po'i spyod yul brjod pa la mi ltos pa ni 'di lta ste gzugs dang tshor ba zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i ming bkra bar mi 'dzin par don gang yin pa 'dzin pa yin no /
tadanyanirapekṣastadyathārthāntaramanapekṣya yatra tadbuddhirbhavati
# de las gzhan pa la mi ltos pa ni 'di lta ste / / don gzhan la mi ltos pa de'i blo 'byung ba ste /
na yathā ghaṭādiṣu rūpādīnapekṣya ghaṭādibuddhiriti
# ji ltar gzugs la sogs pa la ltos nas bum pa la sogs pa la bum pa la sogs pa'i blo 'byung ba lta bu ni ma yin no /
saṃkleśālaṃbanaṃ saṃvṛtisat saṃkleśavṛttyarthena / ātmā saṃkleśasya nimittamityabhiniveśatyājanārtham
# kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba'i dmigs pa ni kun rdzob tu yod pa'o zhes bya ba ni kun nas nyon mongs pa 'phel ba'i phyir ro / / bdag ni kun nas kun nas nyon mongs pa'i rgyu'o snyam du mngon par zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro /
viśuddhaye ālaṃbanaṃ paramārthasat paramajñānagocarārthena
# rnam par dag par 'gyur ba'i dmigs pa ni don dam par yod pa ste / / ye shes dam pa'i spyod yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
sarvāṇi ṣaramārthasantītiti tathatāvyatirekātsarvadharmāṇām / yena saṃkliśyate vyavadāyate ceti rāgādibhiścetasikaiḥ śraddhādibhiśceti veditavyam / yā ca tatrāvastheti rūpacittacetasikāvasthāsu prajñaptāścittaviprayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ / yacca vyavadānamityasaṃskṛtaṃ vyavadānaṃ veditavyam
# thams cad kyang don dam par yod pa'o zhes bya ba ni chos thams cad kyang de bzhin nyid las gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / gang gis kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'o zhes bya ba ni sems las byung ba 'dod chags la sogs pa dang dad pa la sogs par rig par bya'o / / de'i gnas skabs gang yin pa zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sems dang sems las byung ba'i gnas skabs dag la btags pa sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams so / / rnam par byang ba gang yin pa zhes bya ba ni 'dus ma byas te /
tacca yathāyogam
# de ni ci rigs su sbyar ro /
punastrayodaśavidhasya vijñānasya yo viṣayaḥ tajjñeyamanena pradarśitam / tatpunaḥ śrutamayaṃ jñānaṃ cintāmayaṃ jñānaṃ laukikabhāvanāmayaṃ jñānaṃ paramārthajñānaṃ paracittajñānaṃ dharmajñānam anvayajñānaṃ duḥkhajñānaṃ samudayajñānaṃ nirodhajñānaṃ mārgajñānaṃ kṣayānutpādajñānaṃ mahāyānajñānaṃ ca
# yang shes pa rnam pa bcu gsum gyi yul gang yin pa de ni shes bya ste / / de dag ni thos pa las byung ba'i shes pa dang bsams pa las byung ba'i shes pa dang 'jig rten pa'i bsgoms pa las byung ba'i shes pa dang don dam pa shes pa dang gzhan gyi sems shes pa dang chos shes pa dang rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa dang sdug bsngal shes pa dang kun 'byung shes pa dang 'gog pa shes pa dang lam shes pa dang zad pa dang mi skye ba shes pa dang theg pa chen po shes pa ste /
ete 'nye ca yathākramamadhimuktijñānādīni veditavyāni
# de dag ni go rims bzhin du mos pa'i shes pa la sogs par rig par bya'o /
tatra paracittajñānaṃ parātma jñānam parātmacittaviṣayāt
# de la gzhan gyi sems shes pa ni gzhan gyi bdag nyid shes pa ste / / gzhan gyi bdag nyid kyi sems yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
dharmajñānamadharajñānam satyeṣvādita utpādāt
# chos shes pa ni 'og ma shes pa ste / / bden pa rnams la thog mar 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
anvayajñānamūrdhvajñānam dharmajñānādūrdhvamutpādāt / vidūṣaṇāyāsamutthāpanāyānutpāde jñāne niṣṭhāyāṃ mahārtheṣu jñānaṃ tadvidūṣaṇajñānaṃ yāvanmahārthajñānamiti yojayitavyam / mahārthatvaṃ punaḥ svaparārthatvāt
# rjes su rtogs pa'i shes pa ni gong ma shes pa ste / / chos shes pa'i 'og tu 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / rnam par sun 'byin pa'i phyir / / kun nas mi ldang bar bya ba'i phyir / / mi skye ba shes pa la mthar thug pa don chen po la shes pa gang yin pa de ni rnam par sun 'byin pa'i shes pa nas don chen po'i shes pa zhes bya ba'i bar du sbyar bar bya'o / / don chen po ni bdag dang gzhan gyi don gyi phyir ro /
tatra avikalpanataḥ pañcabhirvijñānakāyaiḥ
# rnam par mi rtog pas zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga po dag gis so /
vikalpanataḥ manovijñānena / hetuta ālayavijñānam / pravṛttitastadanyadvijñānam nimittata indriyārthāḥ
# rnam par rtog pas zhes bya ba ni yid kyi rnam par shes pas so / / rgyus zhes bya ba ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pas so / / 'jug pa ni de las gzhan pa'i rnam par shes pa'o / / rgyu mtshan ni dbang po dang don rnams so /
naimittikato vijñānāni / vipakṣapratipakṣataḥ sarāgaṃ vigatarāgaṃ sadveṣaṃ vigatadveṣamityevamādi / sūkṣmaprabhedataḥ saptavidhadurvijñānavijñaptibhedāt / saptavidhādurvijñānā vijñāptistadyathā asaṃviditavijñaptiḥ bhājanavijñaptiḥ sarvakālamaparicchinnākāratvāt citrākāravijñaptirekasyāneka ākāro vicitraśceti durvyavasthāpanādasyāḥ sūkṣmatvam
# rgyu mtshan las byung ba'i rnam par shes pa rnams so / / mi mthun pa dang gnyen po ni 'dod chags dang bcas pa dang 'dod chags dang bral ba dang zhe sdang dang bcas pa dang zhe sdang dang bral ba zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / phra ba'i rab tu phye bas zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes par dka' ba'i rnam par rig pa rnam pa bdun gyi bye brag gis te / / rnam par shes par dka' ba'i rnam par rig pa bdun ni 'di lta ste / / ma rig pa'i rnam par rig pa ni snod kyi rnam par rig pa phra ba ste / / dus thams cad du rnam pa yongs su mchad pa'i phyir ro / / sna tshogs kyi rnam pa'i rnam par rig pa ni gcig gi rnam pa ni gcig dang sna tshogs te / / rnam par gzhag par dka' ba'i phyir 'di ni phra ba nyid do /
sahabhāvavijñaptirekakālotpannāti vijñānāni kathaṃ pṛthagyathāsvaṃ viṣayaṃ paricchindantīti durvyavasthāpanātsūkṣmatvam / sūkṣmatvamiti sarvatrādhikṛtaṃ veditavyam
# lhan cig 'byung ba'i rnam par rig pa ni dus gcig tu 'byung ba'i rnam par shes pa rnams ji ltar so sor rang gi yul ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su gcod pa rnam par gzhag par dka' ba'i phyir ro / / phra ba nyid ces bya ba ni thams cad du sbyar bar rig par bya'o /
vipakṣapratipakṣalaghuparivṛttivijñaptiḥ kathaṃ rāgādisamastabandhanaṃ cittaṃ tanmuhureva sakṛdvītarāgādikaṃ bhavatīti / vāsanāvijñaptiḥ kathaṃ karmabhiḥ samudācaradbhiḥ cittaṃ vāsyate na ca tasmādanyā sā vāsanā nāpi tanmātrameva phaladānaṃ ca prati krameṇa vṛttilābha iti
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs las gnyen po myur du 'byung ba'i rnam par rig pa ni ji ltar 'dod chags la sogs pa'i 'ching ba thams cad dang ldan pa'i sems te / / yud tsam nyid la thang cig tu 'dod chags la sogs pa dang bral bar 'gyur ba'o / / bag chags kyi rnam par rig pa ni ji ltar las kun tu 'byung ba rnams kyis sems la bag chags bsgo bar 'gyur ba ste / / de las bag chags gzhan pa'ang ma yin la de tsam nyid kyang ma yin te /
pratisaṃdhivijñaptiḥ kathamanekaprakārātmabhāvanirvartakakarmaparibhāvitaṃ sadvijñānaṃ tathāpyaparisphuṭāyāṃ maraṇāvasthāyāṃ sahasā prabuddhayānyatarakarmavāsanāmanyatarasyāṃ gatau pratisaṃdhi vadhnānīti
# 'bras bu 'byin pa'ang rim gyis 'byung ba rnyed pa'o / / nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par rig pa ni ji ltar lus rnam pa du mar 'grub pa'i las kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i rnam par shes pa yod pa dang de bzhin du 'chi ba'i dus na shin tu mi gsal ba'i tshe 'phral la las kyi bag chags gang yang rung ba zhig sad cing rgyas nas 'gro ba gang yang rung ba zhig tu nyid mtshams sbyor bar 'gyur ro /
muktavijñaptiḥ kathamarhataścittaṃ paramaṃ niṣprapañcaṃ dharmatāprāptaṃ saṃsārocitasarvaprakārasāśravacaryā samatikrāntamanenākāreṇa vartata iti durvyavasthāpanādasyāḥ sūkṣmatvaṃ veditavyam
# grol ba'i rnam par rig pa ni dgra bcom pa'i sems mchog tu spros pa med pa'i chos nyid thob pa 'khor ba na 'dris pa zag pa dang bcas pa'i spyod pa'i rnam pa thams cad la yang dag par shin tu 'das pa ste / / rnam pa 'dis rnam par gzhag par dka' ba'i phyir 'di phra ba nyid du rig par bya'o /
draṣṭādigrahaṇena draṣṭā śrotā ghrātā svādayitā spraṣṭā vijñātā cetyeṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ veditavyam
# mthong ba po la sogs pa smos pas ni mthong ba po dang nyan pa po dang smon pa po dang myong ba po dang reg pa po dang rnam par shes pa po zhes bya ba 'di dag bsdu bar rig par bya'o /
abhijñeyaṃ ṣaṇṇāmabhijñānāṃ viṣaya
# mngon par shes par bya ba ni mngon par shes pa drug gi yul lo /
gamanaviśeṣaprabhāvitatvādṛddhayabhijñāyāstadviṣayasya saṃkrāntito 'bhijñeyatvam / sarāgādinimittajñānāccaritapraveśāt / atītajanmaparaṃparāgamanajñānādāgatitaḥ / anāgatotpattigamanajñānāt gatitaḥ / traidhātukanirmokṣopāyajñānānnisaraṇataḥ / sarvāṇyabhijñeyānyantyānāṃ tisṛṇāṃ savaṃviṣayatvāt / tatra rūpīti rūpaṃ tasya dharmasyātmasvabhāvastasmādasau rūpī na tu rūpāntareṇa yuktatvāt / yāvaduktaṃ syādrūpasvabhāva iti / bhūtāśrayato 'pīti rūpāntarayogādapi rūpitvamiti darśayati upādāyarūpasya bhūtarūpeṇa yogādbhatarūpāṇāṃ ca parasparamiti / nāndīsamudaya iti nāndyeva yasya samudayastadrūpi na tu yathā vedanādīnāṃ pūrvikā ca nāndo samudayaḥ pratyutpannaśca sparśādiriti
# 'gro ba'i bye brag gis rab tu phye ba'i phyir rdzu 'phrul gyi mngon par shes pa ste / / de'i yul ni kun tu 'gro ba'i phyir mngon par shes par bya ba nyid do / / rna ba'i mngon par shes pas 'gro ba sna tshogs kyi sgra yang yongs su shes pas na rjes su thos pa'o / / spyod pa la 'jug pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'dod chags la sogs pa dang bcas pa'i sems shes pa'i phyir ro / / 'ongs pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'das pa'i tshe rabs gcig nas gcig tu brgyud de 'ongs pa zhes pa'i phyir ro / / 'gro ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni ma 'ongs pa'i skye bar 'gro ba shes pa'i phyir ro / / nges par 'byung ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni khams gsum las nges par thar ba dang thabs shes pa'i phyir ro / / thams cad kyang mngon par shes par bya ba dag go zhes bya ba ni thams cad kyang tha ma gsum gyi yul yin pa'i phyir ro / / gzugs ni chos de'i bdag nyid dang ngo bo nyid yin te / / de'i phyir de gzugs can yin gyi gzugs gzhan dang ldan pa'i phyir ni ma yin te / / gzugs kyi ngo bo nyid ces bya ba'i bar du brjod par 'gyur ro / / 'byung ba rten du gyur pa zhes bya ba ni gzugs gzhan dang ldan pa'i phyir yang gzugs can nyid du ston te / / rgyur byas pa'i gzugs ni 'byung ba'i gzugs dang ldan pa dang 'byung ba'i gzugs rnams kyang nang phan tshun ldan pa'i phyir ro / / dga' ba'i kun 'byung ba zhes bya ba ni dga' ba nyid gang gi kun 'byung ba yin pa de gzugs can yin gyi / / ji ltar tshor ba la sogs pa'i kun 'byung ba ni sngon gyi dga' ba dang da ltar byung ba'i reg pa la sogs pa yang yin pa lta bu ni ma yin no /
sapradeśataḥ sāvayavatvāt / deśavyāptito dikṣu pratyāsparaṇāt / deśopadeśato 'muṣyāṃ diśīti vyavadeṣṭuṃ śakyatvāt deśagocarataḥ kasmiścitpradeśe sthitasyālaṃbanībhāvāt
# phyogs dang bcas pa zhes bya ba ni cha shas dang bcas pa'i phyir ro / / yul la khyab pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni phyogs rnams su lus kyis rgyas pa'i phyir ro / / yul nye bar bstan du rung ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni phyogs che ge mo zhig na'o zhes bstan par nus pa'i phyir ro / / yul spyod yul du gyur pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni phyogs 'ga' zhig na 'dug par dmigs par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
dvayasamagocarataḥ sattvadvayasya kasmiścitpradeśe sthitasyālaṃ vanobhāvāt
# gnyis spyod yul du 'dzin pa mtshungs pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni sems can gnyis mtshungs par dmigs par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / gzugs can ma yin pa ni de lta ma yin te /
dvayasamagocarataḥ sattvadvayasya samamālaṃ vanībhāvānna tvevamarūpiṇo yathātmānubhavaṃ paraiḥ parigrahītumaśakyatvāditi / saṃbandhataścakṣurvijñānā dīnāmapi paryāyeṇa rūpitvam rūpīndriyasaṃbandhāt
# ji ltar bdag gis myong ba bzhin du gzhan dag gis shes par mi nus pa'i phyir ro / / 'brel pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni / / mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa yang brgyud pas gzugs can nyid de / / dbang po gzugs can dang 'brel pa'i phyir ro /
anubandhata ārūpyāṇāṃ pṛthagjanānāṃ rūpabījānubandhāt / prarūpaṇato vitarkavicārāṇāmālaṃbanaprarūpaṇāt
# rjes su 'brel pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni gzugs med par skyes pa'i so so'i skye bo rnams la gzugs kyi sa bon rjes su 'brel ba'i phyir ro / / rab tu rtogs pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni rtogs pa rnams dmigs pa la rab tu rtog pa'i phyir ro /
vyābādhanataḥ pañcānāṃ skandhānāṃ pāṇyādisaṃsparśaiḥ śokādibhiśca yathāyogaṃ rūpaṇāt bādhanādityarthaḥ
# gnod par bya ba yin pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni phung po lnga po dag la lag pa la sogs pas kun tu reg pa dang mya ngan la sogs pas ji ltar mthun mthun du gnod par byar rung ba'i phyir te gnod par bya ba yin zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
saṃprāpaṇato deśanāyā arthanirūpaṇāt
# go bar byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni bstan pas don la rtog pa'i phyir ro /
saṃcayavyavasthānataḥ paramāṇorūrdhvarūpasya sāvayavavyavasthānāt
# bsags pa rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni rdul phra mo las gong ma'i gzugs cha shas dang bcas par rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir ro /
bahirmukhataḥ kāmāvacarasya rūpasya kāmaguṇatṛṣṇāsaṃbhūtatvāt
# phyi rol du bltas pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i gzugs 'dod pa'i yon tan la sred pa las byung ba'i phyir ro /
antarmukhato rūpāvacarasya rūpasya samāpatticittatṛṣṇāsaṃbhūtatvādata evāsya manomayatvaṃ veditavyam
# nang du bltas pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni gzugs na spyod pa'i gzugs de snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems la sred pa las byung ba'i phyir te / / de'i phyir 'di yid las byung ba nyid du rig par bya'o /
āyatataḥ pṛthagjanasya pūrvāntāparāntayoḥ paryantavyavasthānābhāvāt
# yun ring ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni so so'i skye bo'i gzugs sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha'i mu rnam par gnas pa med pa'i phyir ro /
paricchinnataḥ śaikṣasya rūpasya paryantīkṛtasaṃsāratvāt
# yongs su chad pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni slob pa'i gzugs 'khor ba'i mthar phyin par byed pa'i phyir ro /
tatkālato 'śaikṣarūpasya pratyutatpannabhavamātrāvaśeṣāt
# de'i dus kyi phyir zhes bya ba ni mi slob pa'i gzugs da ltar byung ba'i srid pa tsam zhig las pa'i phyir ro /
nidarśanato buddhādirūpasya saṃdarśanamātratvādaniṣpannatāmupādāya
# nges par ston pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni sangs rgyas la sogs pa'i gzugs ni kun tu ston pa tsam du zad kyi grub pa med pa'i phyir ro /
tatra sarvāṇi rūpīṇi vyāvādhanarūpitvena / yathāyogaṃ śeṣairveditavyam
# thams cad kyang gzugs can dag go zhes bya ba ni gnod par bya ba'i gzugs can yin pa'i phyir ro / / lhag ma rnams ni ci rigs su rig par bya'o /
bahirmukhatādayastu ṣaḍ rūpibhedā vedanādisādhāraṇā veditavyāḥ
# phyi rol du bltas pa la sogs pa gzugs can gyi rab tu dbye ba drug ni tshor ba la sogs pa dang thun mong bar rig par bya'o /
śiṣṭasya rūpivat prabheda iti / iti katham / yathā rūvitadātmato 'pīti vistareṇa rūpītyuktaṃ tathā sanidarśanatadātmato 'pi sanidarśanaṃ vistareṇa yojayitavyam / tatra sarvāṇi sanidarśanāni sarvanidarśanasaṃbandhādinārūpiṇāmapi sanidarśanatvāt
# lhag ma'i rab tu dbye ba ni gzugs can bzhin no zhes bya ba ni gzugs de'i bdag nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba rnam pa thams cad do / / thams cad kyang bstan du yod pa dag go zhes bya ba ni bstan du yod pa dang 'brel ba la sogs pas gzugs can ma yin pa rnams kyang bstan du yod pa'i phyir ro / / sgrib par byed pa dang bsgrib par bya ba zhes bya ba la /
āvṛṇotyāvri yata iti gamanapratibandhārthena / āvṛṇotītyetāvati vaktavye āvriyate ceti vacanaṃ prabhādirūpasya sapratighatvavyavasthāpanārtham
# 'gro ba'i gegs byed pa'i phyir sgrib par byed pa zhes de tsam du bstan pas bsgrib par bya ba zhes bya ba'i tshig gis 'od la sogs pa'i gzugs thogs pa dang bcas par rnam par 'jog ste / / de ni bsgrib par bya ba nyid yin gyi / / sgrib par byed pa ni ma yin no /
taddhyāvriyata eva nāvṛṇotītyeṣā tasya jātireṣa svabhāva ityarthaḥ
# 'di ni de'i rigs te / / 'di ni ngo bo nyid ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
paramāṇorūrdhvamityekasya paramāṇorapratighatvāt
# rdul phra rab las gong ma zhes bya ba ni rdul phra rab gcig thogs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
yanna samādhivaśavarti rūpamiti samādhivaśena vartamānasyāpratighatvāt samacittakadevatāvata
# gang ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang gis ma bsgyur pa'i gzugs zhes bya ba ni ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bsgyur ba'i gzugs ni thogs pa med pa'i phyir te / / sems mnyam pa'i lha bzhin no /
prakopapadasthānaṃ yatrāśraya ālaṃbane vā dveṣa utpadyate
# rab tu 'khrug pa'i gzhi'i gnas ni gnas sam dmigs pa gang la zhe sdang skye ba ste /
anena ca sapratighārthena sarvāṇisapratighāni
# thogs pa dang bcas pa'i don 'dis ni thams cad kyang thogs pa dang bcas pa dag go /
yathāyogaṃ veti śeṣaiḥ / āsravatadātmata āsravāṇāṃ sāsravatvamāsravasvabhāvena yuktatvāt / āsravasaṃbandhatastatsahabhuvāṃ citacaittānāṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ cāsravasaṃprayuktatvādāsrava śrayatvācca yathākramam
# yang na ci rigs su sbyar ro zhes bya ba ni lhag ma rnams so / / zag pa de'i bdag nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba ni zag pa rnams zag pa dang bcas pa nyid de / / zag pa'i ngo bo nyid dang ldan pa'i phyir ro / / zag pa dang 'brel ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni de dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams dang mig la sogs pa zag pa dang ldan pa dang gnas yin pa'i phyir te go rims bzhin no /
āsravabandhataḥ kuśalasāsravāṇāṃ tadvaśena punarbhavanirvartanāt / āsravānubandhato 'nyabhūmikānāmapyanyabhūmikāsravadauṣṭhulyāśrayatvāt
# zag pas bcings pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni de'i dbang gis dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa rnams kyang yang srid pa 'grub par byed pa'i phyir ro / / zag pa'i rjes su 'brel ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni sa pa gzhan rnams kyang sa pa gzhan gyi zag pa'i gnas ngan len dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
āsravānukūlyata iti kleśadauṣṭhulyānugatatve 'pi nirvedyabhāgīyānāmanāsravatvavyavasthāpanārtham sarvabhavavaimukhyena tatpratipakṣatvāt
# zag pa'i rjes su mthun pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams nyon mongs pa'i gnas ngan len dang ldan du zin kyang zag pa med pa nyid du rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir te / / srid pa thams cad la rgyab kyis bltas pa'i phyir dang de'i gnyen po la bstan pa'i phyir ro /
āsravānvayato 'rhatāṃ skandhānāṃ paurvajānmikakleśasaṃbhūtatvāt / pañcaskandhāḥ sāsravāḥ
# zag pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni dgra bcom pa rnams kyi phung po rnams tshe rabs snga ma'i nyon mongs pa las byung ba'i phyir ro /
pañcadaśa ghātavo 'ntyāṃstrīn hitvā
# khams bco lnga ni tha ma gsum ma gtogs pa'o /
daśāyatanānyantye dve hitvāḥ
# skye mched bcu ni tha ma gnyis ma gtogs pa'o /
trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ dvayoścāyatanayoḥ pradeśaḥ saparivāramāryamārgamasaṃskṛtaṃ ca hitvā / śastrādānādiraṇahetavo rāgādayo raṇāḥ
# khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs ni 'phags pa'i lam 'khor dang bcas pa dang 'dus ma byas ma gtogs pa'o / / mtshon cha len pa la sogs pa ni 'thab pa ste /
yāvanti sāsravāṇi tāvanti saraṇāṇītyevamādi tadānubaṃdhyārthena veditavyam / punarbhavādhyavasānahetavo rāgādaya āmiṣam / kathaṃ dveṣasya punarbhavādhyavasānahetutvam
# 'dod chags la sogs pa ni rgyu yin pas 'thab pa'o / / zag pa dang bcas pa ji snyed pa 'thab pa dang bcas pa'ang de snyed do zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni de'i rjes su 'brel par rig par bya'o / / yang srid pa la lhag par chags pa'i rgyu nyid de /
vyāvadānikadharmadveṣeṇa punarbhavādhyavasānāt
# rnam par byang ba'i chos la zhe sdang bas srid pa la lhag par chags pa'i phyir ro /
kāmaguṇādhyavasānahetavo rāgādayo gredhaḥ
# 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga la lhag par chags pa'i rgyu yin pas zhe na pa'o /
kīdṛśena dveṣeṇa tadadhyavasānam
# zhe sdang ci 'dra ba zhig gis de la lhag par chags shen /
naiṣkramyadveṣeṇa / kāmakāreṇa saṃmukhībhāvo vimukhībhāvaśca nāsaṃskṛtasya saṃbhavati nityatvāt / naivasaṃskṛtanāsaṃskṛtasya dvayāvyatirekādyaduktam dvayamidaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ cāsaṃskṛtaṃ ceti / tatkathaṃ dvayamevameva bhavatīti
# mngon bar 'byung ba la zhe sdang bas so / / 'dod pa bzhin du byed pas mngon du phyogs pa dang rgyab kyis lta ba ni 'dus ma byas la mi srid de / / rtag pa'i phyir ro / / 'dus byas kyang ma yin 'dus ma byas kyang ma yin pa ni 'di gnyis las gud na med pa'i phyir ro / / 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas zhes bya ba ni 'di gnyis so zhes gang gsungs pa de ji ltar gnyis kho nar 'gyur zhe na /
kāmakārasaṃmukhībhāvārthena saṃskṛtameveti vaktavyam / karmakleśānabhisaṃskṛtatārthenāsaṃskṛtameveti
# 'dod pa bzhin du byed pas mngon du phyogs pa dang rgyab kyis lta ba'i phyir 'dus byas zhes bya'o / / las dang nyon mongs pas mngon par 'dus ma byas pa'i phyir 'dus ma byas zhes bya ste /
na dvayādvayatiricyate
# gnyis las gud na med do /
tatpratibhāsamiti traidhātukaparyāpannākāram tathatādipratibhāsasyaikāntenānucitatvena lokottaratvāt
# de ltar snang ba zhes bya ba ni khams gsum par gtogs pa'i rnam pa'o / / de bzhin nyid la sogs par snang ba ni gcig tu ma 'dris pa'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'o /
skandhānāmekadeśaṃ samyagjñānasaṃgṛhītaṃ lokottarapratibhāsāṃśca pṛṣṭhalabdhān sthāpayitvā
# phung po rnams kyi phyogs gcig ces bya ba ni yang dag pa'i lam gyis bsdus pa dang rjes las thob pa 'jig rten las 'das par snang ba ma gtogs pa'o /
taccāsaṃskṛtaṃ ca sthāpayitvā trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ dvayoścāyatanayoḥ pradeśo draṣṭavyaḥ
# de dag dang 'dus ma byas ma gtogs pa'o / / de dag dang 'dus ma byas ma gtogs ba ni khams gsum dang skye mched gnyis kyi phyogs su blta bar bya'o /
traidhātukapratipakṣa āryamārgaḥ / sa punaḥ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānāṃ nityādicaturvidhaviparyāsapratipakṣatvādaviparyāsanirvikalpatayā nirvikalpaḥ
# khams gsum pa'i gnyen po zhes bya ba ni 'phags pa'i lam mo / / de yang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyis ni rtag pa la sogs pa'i phyin ci log bzhi'i gnyen po yin pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'o / / phyin ci log tu rnam par mi rtog pas rnam par mi rtog pa'o / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ni /
bodhisattvānāṃ rūpādisarvadharmaprapañcapratipakṣatvānniṣprapañcanirvikalpatayā nirvikalpaḥ
# gzugs la sogs pa spros pa'i chos thams cad kyi gnyen po yin pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'o / / spros pa'i rnam par rtog pa med pas rnam par mi rtog pa'o /
asaṃskṛtaṃ tu sarvavikalpāpasthānānnirvikalpaḥ
# 'dus ma byas ni rtog pa thams cad kyi gzhi'i gnas ma yin pas rnam par mi rtog pa'o /
ādyutpannaṃ pratisaṃdhikāle
# dang po byung ba ni nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i dus na'o /
prabandhotpannaṃ tata ūrdhvam
# rgyun gyis byung ba ni de'i phyin chad do /
upacayotpannaṃ caturvidhenopacayena svapnāhārabrahmacaryasamāpattihetukena / āśrayatvotpannamadhyātmakamindriyam
# rgyas pa las byung ba ni nyal ba dang zas dang tshangs par spyod pa dang snyoms par 'jug pa dang rgyas pa rnam pa bzhi'i rgyu las byung ba'o / / rten 'byung ba ni nang gi dbang po'o /
vikārotpannaṃ sukhā divedanotpattau tadanukūla indriyapariṇāmaḥ
# 'gyur ba byung ba ni bde ba la sogs pa'i tshor ba byung ban de dang mthun par dbang po 'gyur ba'o /
paripākotpannaṃ jīrṇāvastham
# yongs su smin par byung ba ni rgas pa'i gnas skabs so /
hānyutpannaṃ sugateścyutvādurgatāvutpadyamānasya
# nyams par byung ba ni bde 'gro nas shi 'phos te ngan 'gror skye ba'o /
viśeṣotpannaṃ viparyayāt
# khyad par du byung ba ni de las bzlog pa'o /
prabhāsvarotpannaṃ krīḍāpramoṣakāṇāṃ manaḥpradūṣakāṇāṃ nirmāṇaratīnāṃ paranirmitavaśavartināṃ rūpārūpyāvacarāṇāṃ ca devānāṃ pramodabāhulyādbhogeṣu vihāre ca svavaśavarttanādyathāyogam
# 'od gsal bar byung ba ni rtse bas rab tu slu ba rnams dang yid rab tu sun 'byin pa rnams dang 'phrul dga' ba rnams dang / / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed pa rnams dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i lha rnams dga' ba mang ba dang longs spyod pa dang gnas la rang gis dbang bsgyur pa'i phyir te ci rigs su sbyor ro /
aprabhāsvarotpannaṃ tadanyat
# 'od gsal ba ma yin par byung ba ni de las gzhan pa'o /
saṃkrāntyutpannaṃ gamanāvasthāyām
# kun tu 'gro bar byung ba ni 'gro ba'i dus na'o /
sabījotpannamarhataścaramān skandhān varjayitvā
# sa bon dang bcas par byung ba ni dgra bcom pa'i tha ma'i phung po ma gtogs pa'o /
abījotpannaṃ caramāḥ skandhāḥ
# sa bon ma yin par byung ba ni phung po tha ma pa rnams so /
pratibimbavibhutvanidarśanotpannaṃ jñeyaṃ vastu sabhāgaṃ vaimokṣikaṃ tāthāgataṃ ca rūpaṃ yathākramam
# gzugs brnyan dang dbang 'byor ba dang nges par bstan pa'i phyir byung ba ni shes bya'i dngos po dang mthun pa dang rnam par thar ba las gyur ba dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzugs te go rims bzhin no /
paraṃparotpannaṃ janmaprabandhe
# gcig nas gcig tu byung ba tshe rabs kyi rgyun no /
kṣaṇabhaṅgotpannaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ lakṣaṇam / saṃyogaviyogotpannaṃ priyāpriyasaṃyogaviyogāvasthāyāṃ cittasya ca sarāgavigatarāgādyavasthāyām
# skad cig gcig nas byung ba ni 'du byed rnams kyi mtshan nyid skad cig so so'i'o / / phrad pa dang bral nas byung ba ni sdug pa dang mi sdug pa dang phrad pa dang bral ba'i dus dang sems 'dod chags dang bcas pa dang 'dod chags dang bral ba'i dus na'o /
avasthāntarotpannaṃ kalalādyavasthāsu vyādhyādyavasthāsu ca
# gnas skabs gzhan du byung ba ni mer mer bo la sogs pa'i gnas skabs rnams dang nad la sogs pa'i gnas skabs rnams su'o /
cyutopapādotpannaṃ sattvalokaḥ
# 'chi 'pho ba dang skye bar byung ba ni sems can gyi 'jig rten no /
saṃvartavivartotpannaṃ bhājanalokaḥ
# 'jig pa dang chags par byung ba ni snod kyi 'jig rten no /
pūrvakālotpannaṃ pūrvakālabhavaḥ
# sngon gyi dus na byung ba ni sngon gyi dus kyi srid pa'o /
maraṇakālotpannaṃ maraṇakālabhavaḥ / antarotpanamantarābhavaḥ
# 'chi ba'i dus na byung ba ni 'chi ba'i srid pa'o / / bar du byung ba ni bar ma do'i srid pa'o /
pratisaṃdhikālotpannamupapattibhavaḥ / rūpasaṃskāraskandhaikadeśa itīndriyalakṣaṇaḥ saṃprayuktalakṣaṇaśca yathākramam
# nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i dus na byung ba ni skye ba'i srid pa'o / / gzugs dang 'du byed kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig ces bya ba ni dbang po'i mtshan nyid dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i mtshan nyid de go rims bzhin no /
dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaḥ saṃprayuktasvabhāvaḥ / bhoktātmā iṣṭāniṣṭānāṃ viṣayāṇāmupalaṃbhārthena veditavyaḥ / aprāptagrāhakaṃ cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ manaśca
# chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni mtshungs par ldan pa'i ngo bo nyid do / / za ba po ni bdag ste 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa'i yul rnams la dmigs par rig par bya'o / / ma phrad par 'dzin pa ni mig dang rna ba dang yid do /
prāptagrāhakaṃ tadanyadindriyam
# phrad nas 'dzin pa ni de las gzhan pa'i dbang po'o /
svalakṣaṇasya vartamānasya pratyekaṃ pratiniyatasya viṣayasya grāhakaṃ pañcendriyajam
# da ltar gyi rang gi mtshan nyid so so ba yul so sor nges pa 'dzin pa ni dbang po lnga las byung ba'o /
svasāmānyalakṣaṇasya sarvakālasya sarvasya viṣayasya grāhakaṃ ṣaṣṭhendriyajam
# rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid dus thams cad pa'i yul thams cad 'dzin pa ni dbang po drug las byung pa'o /
pratyayasāmagrayā vijñānasyotpattimadhikṛtya prajñaptyāṃ grāhakopacāro veditavyaḥ na tu bhūtārthena vyāpāratvād dharmāṇāmiti / yattāvadgrāhakaṃ grāhyamapi tat cakṣurādīnāmapi manovijñānena grāhyatvāt / grāhakagocara evetyavadhāraṇaṃ caitasikavyudāsārtham
# rkyen tshogs nas rnam par shes pa las byung ba'i dbang du byas te btags nas 'dzin pa'i nye bar 'dogs par rig par bya ba'i yang dag pa'i don du na chos rnams byed pa med pa'i phyir ro / / 'dzin pa gang yin pa gzung ba yang de yin no zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pa yang yid kyi rnam par shes pas gzung ba'i phyir ro / / 'dzin pa'i spyod yul nyid ces bsnan pa ni sems dang sems las byung ba bsal ba'i phyir ro /
śrutacintāmayatadanudharmapratipattisaṃgṛhītasyābahirmukhatvam niṣyandadharmahetukatvāt tadvaśena nirvāṇādyālaṃbanato draṣṭavyam
# thos pa las byung ba dang bsam ba las byung ba dang de'i rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pas yongs su bsdus pa ni phyi rol tu bltas pa ma yin pa nyid de / / rgyu mthun pa'i chos kyi rgyu las byung ba'i phyir ro / / de'i dbang gis mya ngan las 'das pa la sogs pa la dmigs par blta'o /
niṣyandadharmaḥ punarbuddhādīnāmadhigamānvayā deśanā veditavyā
# rgyu mthun pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i chos ni sangs rgyas la sogs pas thugs su chud pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i brtan par rig par bya'o /
catvāro dhātavo ghrāṇavijñānadhāturgandhadhāturjihvāvijñānadhātuḥ rasadhātuśca
# khams bzhi ni sna'i rnams par shes pa'i khams dang lce'i rnam par shes pa'i khams dang dri'i khams dang ro'i khams so /
dve āyatane gandharasāyatane tadanyeṣāmekadeśaḥ kāmadhātusaṃgṛhītaḥ / daśānāṃ dhātūnāmiti saptānāṃ vijñānadhātūnāṃ rūpaśabdadharmadhātūnāṃ ca / caturṇāmāyatanānāmiti rūpaśabdamanodharmāyatanānām
# skye mched gnyis ni dri dang ro'i skye mched do / / de las gzhan pa dag gi phyogs gcig ni gang 'dod pa'i khams su bsdus pa'o / / khams bcu zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'i khams bdun dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos kyi khams so / / skye mched bzhi ni gzugs dang sgra dang yid dang chos kyi skye mched do /
hetuphalopayogata ityutpannatvānniruddhatvācca yathākramam
# rgyu dang 'bras bu spyad zin dang zhes bya ba ni skyes zin pa dang 'gags zin pa'i phyir te go rims bzhin no /
saṃkleśavyavadānakāritrasamatikrāntata iti pratyutpannarāgādiśraddhādivaccittasaṃkleśavyavadānasāmarthyābhāvāt
# kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar byed pa yang dag pa shin tu 'das pa zhes bya ba ni da ltar byung ba'i 'dod chags la sogs pa dang dad pa la sogs pa bzhin du sems kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar byed pa'i mthu med pa'i phyir ro /
hetuparigrahavināśato vāsanāṃ sthāpayitvā vinaṣṭatvāt
# rgyu yongs su bzung nas zhig zhes bya ba ni bag chags gzhan nas zhig pa'i phyir ro /
phalasvalakṣaṇabhāvābhāvato vartamāne kāle tadāhitavāsanāsadbhāvāttadādhāyakadravyābhāvācca
# 'bras bu dang rang gi mtshan nyid yod pa dang med pa zhes bya ba na di ltar gyi dus na des bskyed pa'i bag chags yod pa dang de 'jog par byed pa'i rdzas med pa'i phyir ro /
smarasaṃkalpādīnāṃ nimittatvamālaṃbanamātra bhāvādaveditavyam
# dran pa'i kun tu rtog pa'i mtshan ma la sogs pa ni mtshan ma ni dmigs pa tsam du yod par rig par bya'o /
sarveṣāmekadeśo 'nāgatapratyutpannāsaṃskṛtavarjaḥ
# thams cad kyi phyogs gcig ces bya ba ni ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba dang 'dus ma byas ma gtogs pa'o /
hetau satyanutpannata ityasaṃskṛtādviśeṣaṇārtham taddhayanutpannamapi sanna hetumaditi
# rgyu yod kyang ma byung ba zhes bya ba ni 'dus ma byas las bye brag tu dbye ba'i phyir te / / de ni ma byung la rgyu dang ldan pa yang ma yin no /
labdhasvalakṣaṇato 'nirvṛttasvabhāvatvāt / hetuphalānupayogatastadbījasyākṛtakṛtyatvāt tasya cānutpannatvāt
# rang gi mtshan nyid ma thob pa ni / / rang bzhin gyis ma grub pa'i phyir ro / / rgyu dang 'bras bu ma spyad pa ni de'i sa bon gyi bya ba ma byas pa dang de 'ang ma skyes pa'i phyir ro /
hetuphalopayogānupayogataḥ punaranivartyatvādasthitatvācca
# rgyu dang 'bras bu spyad zin pa dang spyad ma zin pa zhes bya ba ni yang mi 'grub pa dang yod pa'i phyir ro /
atītānāgataprabhāvananimittataḥ pratyutpannamadhiṣṭhāyātītānāgataprajñapteḥ
# 'das pa dang ma 'ongs par rab tu gzhag pa'i rgyu zhes bya ba ni da ltar byung ba la brten te / / 'das pa dang ma 'ongs par btags pa'i phyir te /
yattāmavasthāṃ prāpsyati tadanāgatam / yatprāptaṃ tadatītamiti
# gang de'i gnas skabs thob par 'gyur ba de ni ma 'ongs pa'o / / gang thob zin pa de ni 'das pa'o /
kāritrapratyupasthānataścakṣurādīnāṃ vijñānāśrayādibhāvāt
# byed pa nye bar gnas pas kyang zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pa ni rnam par shes pa'i gnas la sogs par yod pa'i phyir ro /
atītanirdeśādhikāreṇedamapi jñāpyate kimartha bhagavatātītādīnyeva trīṇi kathāvastūni vyavasthāpitāni na nirvāṇamiti / nirvāṇasya pratyātmavedanīyatayā nirabhilāpyatāmupādāya kathayitumaśakyatvādityarthaḥ dṛṣṭaśrutamatavijñātavyavahārāṇāṃ bhūtabhavyavartamānādhiṣṭhānatvāt / daśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ vijñānadhātūnāṃ rūpaśabdadharmadhātūnāṃ ca
# 'das pa la sogs pa bshad pa'i skabs kyis 'di'ang ston te / / ci'i phyir bcom ldan 'das kyis 'das pa la sogs pa gsum po nyid gtam gyi gzhir gtam gzhir rnam par gzhag gi mya ngan las 'das pa ni ma yin zhe na / / mya ngan las 'da' ba ni so so rang gi rig par bya ba dang brjod du med pa nyid kyi phyir te / / brjod par mu nus zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / byung ba dang 'byung ba dang da ltar ni mthong ba dang thos pa dang bye brag phyed pa dang rnam par shes pa'i tha snyad rnams kyi gnas ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / khams bcu zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'i khams dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos kyi khams so /
caturṇāmāyatanānāṃ rūpaśabdamanodharmāyatanānām
# skye mched bzhi zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sgra dang yid dang chos kyi skye mched do /
teṣveveti śraddhādiṣu / prakṛtyāpratisaṃkhyāyeti svarasena vinā kalyāṇamitrādibalenetyarthaḥ
# de dag nyid la zhes bya ba ni dad pa la sogs pa'o / / rang bzhin gyis so sor ma brtags par zhes bya ba ni rang gi dang gis te / / dge ba'i bshes gnyen la sogs pa'i stobs kyis ma yin zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ruciḥ saṃtiṣṭhata iti na kevalaṃ rucirevopapattiprātilambhikā kiṃ tarhi saha taiḥ śraddhādibhiriti
# 'dod pa kun tu gnas pa'o zhes bya ba ni skye bas thob pa'i 'dod pa 'ba' zhig ma yin gyi / / dad pa la sogs pa dang lhan cig tu'o /
kuśalasya bhāvanā sarve śrutamayādayaḥ kuśalā dharmāveditavyāḥ / svargāḍhyakulopapattiparigrahābhyāmabhyudayahetuṃ darśyati
# dge ba sgom pa'o zhes bya ba ni thos pa las byung ba la sogs pa thams cad dge ba'i chos rnams su rig par bya'o / / mtho ris dang phyug po'i rigs su skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa gnyis kyis ni mngon par mtho ba'i rgyu ston to /
vyavadānānukalyaparigraheṇa prāptihetumiti / vidūṣaṇāpratipakṣādayaḥ parastānnirdekṣyante / tadanyaḥ kleśopakleśo duścaritasamutthāpaka iti sa punaryaḥ kāmāvacaro 'naiḥsargikaḥ naiḥsargikastu yo duścaritasamutthāpakaḥ so 'kuśalaḥ / tadanyo nivṛtāvyākṛto veditavyaḥ / hiṃsāpūrvakaṃ caityaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati yatrorabhramahiṣādayo hanyante / kudṛṣṭipūrvakaṃ yatrānaśanādibhiḥ puṇyārthino varārthinaśca kliśyanta iti / ākṣepakaṃ vā paripūrakaṃ veti durgatimadhikṛtya / sugatau tu paripūrakameva yenātropapanno dāridrayādikaṃ vyasanaṃ pratyanubhavati / kuśalāntarāyikā dharmā abhīkṣṇaṃ gaṇasaṃnipātādayaḥ / aṣṭau dhātavaścakṣuḥ śrotraghrāṇājihvākāyagandharasaspraṣṭavyadhātavaḥ / aṣṭāvāyatanāni tānyeva / aduṣṭāprasannacitasyeti kuśalākuśalaviparyayaṃ darśayati / taireva parigṛhītā iti tadākāratvena manojalpasukhavṛttatvāt / teṣāmevābhilāpavāsaneti nāma kāyādibhiścitavāsanāyatyāmabhilāpapravṛttaye / tatparigṛhīteścittacaitasikairdharmairyatsamutthāpitamityapraduṣṭāprasannacittasya nāmādyabhilāpākāraiḥ / akliṣṭākuśalacetaso yadyasya na kliṣṭaṃ nāpi kuśalaṃ ceto bhavati tata airyāpathikādyavyākṛtaṃ bhavatyanyathā kuśalākuśalaṃ yathāyogamiti / yathāpi tadapratisaṃkhyāyeti kuśalatvādviśepayati akliṣṭacitta ityakuśalatvāt / pratisaṃkhyāya bhaiṣajyaṃ niṣevate sarvavyādhipratipakṣeṇārogyārtham / adhigamaniṣyandato 'vyākṛtaṃ nirmāṇacittaṃ sahajāmiti yaiścittacaitasikaiḥ vikrīḍanārthaṃ nirmāṇaṃ nirmemīyate / sattvahitārtha tu kuśalaṃ veditavyamiti / nidarśanataḥ kuśalādikaṃ yadbuddhādayo vineyārthavaśātsaṃdarśayanti / akuśalasya kathaṃ saṃdarśanam / corādi nirmāya tadanyasattvabhīṣaṇārtha karacaraṇaśiraśchedādisaṃdarśanāt
# rnam par byang ba'i rjes su mthun pa yongs su 'dzin pas ni mya ngan las 'das pa thob pa'i rgyu ston to / / rnam par sun 'byin pa'i gnyen po zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i ni 'og nas 'chad do / / de dag kyang gang zhe na / / de la rnam par sun 'byin pa'i gnyen po ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i 'dus byas rnams la nyes dmigs su lta ba ste / / des nang dang 'bras la sogs pa'i rnam pas nye bar len pa'i phung po sun 'byin pa'i phyir ro / / spong ba'i gnyen po zhes bya ba ni sbyor ba dang de ma thag pa'i lam ste / / de dag gis nyon mongs pa spong ba'i phyir ro / / gzhi'i gnyen po ni rnam par grol ba'i lam rnams te / / de dag gis spong ba'i thob pa kun tu 'dzin pa'i phyir ro / / thag bsring ba'i gnyen po zhes bya ba ni de'i gong ma'i lam ste / / de sngar spangs pa'i nyon mongs pa thag bsring ba'i phyir ro / / de las gzhan pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang nyes par spyod pa kun nas slong ba'o zhes bya ba ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i rang 'khrungs ma yin pa gang yin pa dang rang 'khrungs las ni nyes par spyod pa kun nas slong ba gang yin pa de mi dge ba'o / / de las gzhan pa ni bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan par rig par bya'o / / 'tshe ba sngon du btang nas gang du lug dang ma he la sogs pa gsod pa dang lta ba ngan pa sngon du btang nas bsod nams 'dod pa dang mchog 'dod pa'i phyir gang du zas mi za ba la sogs pas nyon mongs pa der lha rten byed pa'o / / 'phen pa'am yongs su rdzogs par byed pa zhes bya ba ni ngan 'gro'i dbang du byas pa'o / / bde 'gror ni yongs su rdzogs par byed pa nyid de / / gang gis 'dir skyes nas dbul ba la sogs pa'i sdug bsngal myong ba'o / / dge ba'i bar chad byed pa'i chos zhes bya ba ni rgyun mi 'chad par tshogs kyi nang du 'du ba la sogs pa'o / / khams brgyad ces bya ba ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang dri dang ro dang reg bya'i khams so / / skye mched brgyad ces bya ba ni de dag nyid do / / sdang ba yang ma yin dang ba yang ma yin pa'i sems su gyur pa zhes bya bas ni dge ba dang mi dge ba las bzlog pa ston to / / de dag nyid kyis yongs su zin pa zhes bya ba ni de'i rnam pa yid la brjod pa'i sgo nas 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / de dag nyid brjod pa'i bag chags so / / zhes bya ba ni ming gi tshogs la sogs pas phyi ma la mngon bar brjod pa 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir / / sems la bag chags bsgos pa'o / / de dag gis yongs su zin pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams kyis gang kun nas slong ba'o zhes bya ba ni sdang ba yang ma yin / / dang ba yang ma yin pa'i sems su gyur pa'i ming la sogs pa mngon bar brjod pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis kun nas slong ba'o / / nyon mongs pa can yang ma yin dge ba yang ma yin pa'i sems dang ldan pa zhes bya ba ni / / gal te nyon mongs pa can yang ma yin la / / dge ba yang ma yin pa'i sems su gyur na / / de'i phyir spyod lam la sogs pa lung du ma bstan par 'gyur ro / / gzhan du na dge ba'am mi dge bar 'gyur te ci rigs su sbyar ro / / 'di lta ste so sor brtags pa ma yin pa la zhes bya ba ni dge ba las bye brag tu 'byed do / / nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i sems kyis zhes bya bas ni / / mi dge ba las bye brag tu 'byed do / / yongs su 'dzin pas lung du ma bstan pa zhes bya ba ni bzo'i gnas la goms pa'i bag chags kyis de lta bu'i lus yongs su 'dzin pa'i phyir ro / / so sor ma brtags pas sman bsten ba zhes bya bas ni nad kyi gnyen pos nad med par bya ba'i phyir ro / / rgyu mthun pas lung du ma bstan pa gang zhe na sprul pa'i sems dang lhan cig skyes pa'o zhes bya ba ni sems dang sems las byung ba gang gis rtse ba'i phyir sprul pa sprul pa ste / / sems can la phan pa'i phyir na ni dge bar rig par bya'o / / bstan pas kyang dge ba zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni / / gang sangs rgyas la sogs pas 'dul ba'i don gyi dbang gi phyir kun tu ston pa'o / / mi dge bar ji ltar kun tu ston ce na / / chom rkun la sogs par sprul nas de las gzhan pa'i sems can 'jigs par bya ba'i phyir lag pa dang rkang pa dang mgo gcod pa la sogs pa kun tu ston pa'i phyir ro /
avītarāgasyeti pradeśavairāgyeṇāpyayuktasyāsamādhilābhina ityarthaḥ / itarathā hyanāgamyaṃ kāmapratisaṃyuktaṃ prāpnuyāt
# 'dod chags dang ma 'brel ba zhes bya ba ni / / 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid kyi phyogs tsam dang yang mi ldan pa ste / / ting nge 'dzin ma thob pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / gzhan du na ni mi lcogs pa med pa yang 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan par 'gyur ro /
saha samādhilābhāt prahāṇābhirativipakṣabhūtasya dauṣṭhulyasya prahāṇāt pradeśavairāgyamastīti veditavyam / bāhyaṃ tviha rūpādikamavītarāgakarmādhipatyanirvṛttatvāt kāmapratisaṃyuktam
# ting nge 'dzin thob ma thag tu spong ba la mngon par dga' ba'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur ba'i gnas ngan len spangs ba'i phyir 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid kyi phyogs yod par rig par bya'o / / phyi rol gyi gzugs la sogs pa ni 'dir 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i las kyi dbang gis grub pa'i phyir 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'o /
sarvasattvasādhāraṇakarmādhipatyasaṃbhūtavacanamavītarāgakarmaṇā rūpārūpyāvacareṣvapi vījino 'stitvāt
# sems can thams cad kyi thun mong gi las kyi dbang gis 'byung ba zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa rnams na yang 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i las kyi sa bon yod pa'i phyir ro /
catvāro dhātavo gandharasaghrāṇajihvāvijñānadhātavaḥ
# khams bzhi zhes bya ba ni dri dang ro dang sna dang lce'i rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
dve āyatane gandharasāyatane
# skye mched gnyis zhes bya ba ni dri dang ro'i skye mched do /
tadanyeṣāmekadeśaḥ rūpārūpyāvacarānāsravavarjaḥ / caturo dhātūn dve cāyatane sthāpayitvānantaroktāni / tadanyeṣāṃ skandhadhātvāyatanānāmekadeśaḥ kāmarūpyāvacarānāsravavarjyaḥ / caturṇā skandhānāṃ vedanādīnām
# de las gzhan pa'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa dang zag pa med pa ma gtogs pa'o / / khams bzhi dang skye mched gnyis ma gtogs pa zhes bya ba ni bshad ma thag pa'o / / de las gzhan pa'i phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyi phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni 'dod pa dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa dang zag pa med pa ma gtogs pa'o / / phung po bzhi zhes bya ba ni tshor ba la sogs pa'o /
trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ manodharmamanovijñānadhātūnām
# khams gsum zhes bya ba ni yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam par shes ba'i khams so /
dvayorāyatanayormanodharmāyatanayoḥ
# skye mched gnyis zhes bya ba ni yid dang chos kyi skye mched de /
pradeśaḥ kāmarūpāvacarānāsravavarjyaḥ / ekadeśavairāgyaṃ bhūmimadhikṛtya yāvadaṣṭamasya kleśaprakārasya prahāṇāt
# de dag gi phyogs gcig ni 'dod pa dang gzugs na spyod pa dang zag pa med pa ma gtogs pa'o / / phyogs gcig las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid ces bya ba ni sa'i dbang du byas pa ste / / sa brgyad pa'i bar du nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa spangs pa'i phyir ro /
sakalavairāgyaṃ nava masya prahāṇāt / satkāyavairāgyaṃ vā punaradhikṛtya śaikṣasyaikadeśavairāgyamaśaikṣasya sakalavairāgyaṃ veditavyam
# mtha' dag las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid ces bya ba ni dgu pa spangs pa'i phyir ro / / yang 'jig tshogs las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid kyi dbang du byas nas slob pa ni phyogs gcig las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid do / / mi slob pa ni mtha' dag las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid du rig par bya'o /
prativedhavairāgyaṃ darśanamārgeṇa
# rtog pas 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid ces bya ba ni mthong ba'i lam gyis so /
upaghātavairāgyaṃ laukikena mārgeṇa
# gnod pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid ces bya ba ni 'jig rten pa'i lam gyis so /
samuddhātavairāgyaṃ lokottareṇeti veditavyam / daśavairāgyāṇītyatra prātikūlyārtho vairāgyārtho veditavyo nāvaśyaṃ prahāṇārthaḥ / uccataraṃ sthānaṃ prāptavato nihīnesthāne ityuccataraṃ nagaraśraiṣṭhayādisthānaṃ prāptavato grāmamahattarādisthāne nihīne
# legs par gnon pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid ces bya ba ni 'jig rten la 'das pa'i phyir nyid kyis 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid du rig par bya'o / / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i bcu zhes bya ba 'di la mi 'phrod par 'dzin pa'i don ni 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid kyi don du rig par bya'o / / gdon mi za bar spong ba'i don du ni ma yin no / / thabs shin tu chen po thob pa thabs dma' ba la zhes bya ba ni grong khyer gyi gtso bo la sogs pa dang grong dpon la sogs pa lta bur rig par bya'o /
bālānāṃ nirvāṇa iti tasya śāntatvājñānāt satkāyābhiṣvaṅgācca / pratilabdhadarśanamārgasya traidhātuka iti saṃskāraduḥkhatāṃ parijñātavataḥ sarvasāsravavastunirvedāt / prakṛtyā vairāgyaṃ prakṛtivairāgyaṃ yāvatprahāṇena vairāgyaṃ prahāṇavairāgyamiti padavigrahajātirveditavyā
# byis pa rnams mya ngan las 'das pa la zhes bya ba ni de la zhi ba nyid du mi shes pa dang 'jig tshogs la mngon bar chags pa'i phyir ro / / mthong ba'i lam thob par khams gsum pa la zhes bya ba ni 'du byed sdug bsngal ba nyid du yongs su shes pa dang ldan pa zag pa dang bcas ba'i dngos po thams cad la yid 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
mokṣaprayuktasya kuśalaṃ śaikṣamiti saṃbhṛtasaṃbhārāvasthāyāḥ prabhṛtimokṣārtha prayuktasya veditavyam / saṃbhṛtasaṃbhārāvasthā punarādhigāmikamokṣabhāgīyāvasthā veditavyā
# thar pa la brtson pa'i dge ba ni bslab par blta'o zhes bya ba ni tshogs bsags pa'i gnas skabs nas bzung ste / / thar par bya ba'i phyir brtson par rig par bya'o / / tshogs bsags pa'i gnas skabs ni mngon bar 'gro ba thar pa'i cha dang mthun par rig par bya'o /
daśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ vijñānarūpaśabdadharmadhātūnām
# khams bcu zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'i khams bdun dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos kyi khams rnams so /
caturṇāmāyatanānāṃ rūpaśabdamanodharmāyatanānām
# skye mched bzhi zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sgra dang yid dang chos kyi skye mched rnams so /
śikṣāyāṃ niṣṭhāgatasyetyadhiśīlamadhicittamadhiprajñaṃ ca śikṣāyāṃ niṣṭhāgatasyārhata ityarthaḥ
# bslabs pa'i mthar phyin pa zhes bya ba ni lhag pa'i tshul khrims dang lhag pa'i sems dang lhag pa'i shes rab ni bslab pa'o / / mthar phyin pa ni dgra bcom pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
pṛthagjanasya kuśalādikamiti mokṣaprayuktavarjasya
# so so'i skye bo'i dge ba la sogs pa ni thar pa la brtson pa ma gtogs pa'o /
sa hi śikṣāyāmabhiśikṣaṇācchaikṣa ucyata iti
# de ni bslab pa la slob pas slob pa zhes bya'o /
śaikṣasya kliṣṭāvyākṛtamityatra kliṣṭamakuśalaṃ nivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ ca yathāsaṃbhavam / avyākṛtaṃ punaranivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ veditavyam / parikalpitā kliṣṭā dṛṣṭirasaddharmaśravaṇapūrvikā pañca daṣṭayaḥ / parikalpitagrahaṇaṃ sahajasatkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭivyudāsārtham
# slob pa'i nyon mongs pa can dang lung du ma bstan pa zhes bya ba 'di la nyon mongs pa can ni mi dge ba'o / / lung du ma bstan pa ni bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan pa ste / / ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyor ro / / mi slob pa'i lung du ma bstan pa zhes bya ba ni ma bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan par rig par bya'o / / nyon mongs pa can gyi lta ba kun tu brtags pa rnams zhes bya ba ni dam pa'i chos ma yin pa nyan pa la sogs pa sngon du 'gro ba'i lta ba lnga po dag go / / kun tu brtags pa smos pas ni lhan cig skyes pa'i 'jig tshogs dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba bsal ba'i phyir ro /
antagrāhadṛṣṭiḥ kīdṛśī sahajā
# mthar 'dzin par lta ba lhan cig skyes pa ji lta bu zhe na /
ucchedadṛṣṭiryato 'bhisamayaprayuktasyottrāso bhavatyatha kastarhi me ātmeti
# mngon par rtogs pa la zhugs pa can nga'i bdag gang yin zhes skrag pa gang las byung ba'o /
dṛṣṭisthānaṃ dṛṣṭisahabhuvo dharmāstadvījaṃ ca tathaiva vicikitsāsthānamapi veditavyam
# lta ba'i gnas zhes bya ba ni lta ba dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i chos rnams dang de'i sa bon no / / the tshom gyi gnas kyang de bzhin du rig par bya'o /
ye ca dṛṣṭau vipratipannāḥ kleśopakleśā iti ye dṛṣṭimukhena pravṛttā tadālaṃbanāśca rāgādayaḥ
# lta ba log par zhugs pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa gang yin pa dag ces bya ba ni lta ba'i sgo nas zhugs pa dang de la dmigs pa'i 'dod chags pa gang yin pa'o /
sarveṣāmekadeśo bhāvanāprahātavyānāsravavarjaḥ
# thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni bsgoms pas spang bar bya ba dang zag pa med pa ma gtogs pa'o /
darśanaprahātavyāviparyayeṇa sāsravā iti parikalpitakliṣṭadṛṣṭayādikādanye sāsravā ityarthaḥ / atra punaḥ sāsravagrahaṇena nirvedhabhāgīyānāmapi grahaṇaṃ veditavyaṃ dauṣṭhulyānubandhārthena
# mthong bas spang bar bya ba las bzlog pa zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi lta ba kun tu brtags pa las gzhan pa'i zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / 'dir zag pa dang bcas pa smos pas ni / / des par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams kyang bsdu bar rig par bya ste / / gnas ngan len gyi rjes su 'brel pa yod pa'i phyir ro /
sarveṣāmekadeśaḥ darśanaprahātavyānāsravavarjaḥ
# thams cad kyi phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni mthong bas spang bar bya ba ni zag pa med pa ma gtogs pa'o /
skandhānāmekadeśo 'prahātavyaḥ lokottaro mārgastatpṛṣṭalabdhaśca / daśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ caturṇā cāyatanānām ekadeśa iti sa cā saṃskṛtaṃ ca / kīdṛśo rūpaśabdadhātū na prahātavyau
# phung po rnams kyi phyogs gcig spang bar bya ba ma yin pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam dang de'i rjes la thob pa'o / / khams bcu dang skye mched bzhi zhes bya ba ni de dang 'dus ma byas so / / ci 'dra ba'i gzugs dang sgra'i khams spang bar bya ba ma yin zhe na /
aśaikṣasya kuśala kāyavākkarmasvabhāvau / avidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ityevamādi / tatra asmin satīdaṃ bhavati nirīhapratyayotpattitāmupādāya / sati kevalaṃ pratyaye phalaṃ bhavati na tu phalotpādanaṃ prati pratyayasya kācidīhetyarthaḥ / asyotpādādidamutpadyate anityapratyayotpattitāmupādāya na hyanutpādikāraṇāt kiṃcidutpadyamānaṃ kārya siddhamiti kṛtvā / avidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ityevamādi samarthapratyayotpattitāmupādāya nirīhakatvānityatve 'pi sati na yataḥ kutaścit pratyayāt sarvameva phalamutpadyate kiṃtarhi samarthāt / tadyathāvidyātaḥ saṃskārā yāvajjātito jarāmaraṇamiti
# mi slob pa'i lus dang ngag gi las kyi rang bzhin no / / chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig ma gtogs par zhes bya ba ni 'dus ma byas kyi mtshan nyid do / / bam po gsum pa / / bdag dang chos rgyu med pa dang dbang phyug la sogs pa'i rgyu las byung bar mngon bar zhen pa spang ba'i phyir ro / / bcom ldan 'das kyis rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid gang gsungs pa ni 'di yod pas / / 'di 'byung / / 'di skyes pa'i phyir 'di skye ba ste / / 'di ltar ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so / / de la 'di yod pas 'di 'byung zhes bya ba ni g yo ba med pa'i rkyen las byung ba phyir te / / rkyen yod na 'bras bu 'byung bar zad kyi 'bras bu 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir rkyen la g yo ba ni ci yang med ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / 'di skyes pa'i phyir 'di skye ste zhes bya ba ni mi rtag pa'i rkyen las byung ba'i phyir te / / ma byung ba'i rgyu las 'bras bu 'byung ba ma grub pa'i phyir ro / / ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni nus pa'i rkyen las byung ba'i phyir ro / / g yo ba med cing mi rtag pa yin du zin kyang rkyen gang yang rung ba las 'bras bu thams cad mi 'byung gi nus pa'i rkyen las 'byung ste 'di ltar ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams 'byung ba nas skye ba las rga shi 'byung ba'i bar du'o /
yānyavidyādīni dvādaśāṅgāni vibhaktāni tānyeva punaḥ samasya catvāryaṅgāni bhavantyākṣepā ṅgādīni / etāvacca pravṛttinirdeśe nirdeṣṭavyam yaduta hetukāle yenākṣipyate yaccākṣipyate phalakāle yenābhinirvartyate yaccābhinirvatyate tadetatsarvamebhiraṅgainirdiṣṭaṃ veditavyam / tatra ākṣepakāṅgamavidyāsaṃskārā vijñānaṃ ca anāgatajanmābhinirvṛttaye satyeṣvajñānapūrvakeṇa karmaṇā cittavāsanārthena
# ma rig pa la sogs pa yan lag bcu gnyis rnam par phye ba gang yin pa de dag ni mdor bsdus yan lag bzhir 'gyur te / / 'phen pa'i yan lag la sogs pa'o / / 'byung ba bstan pa la ni 'di dag tsam zhig bstan par bya ste / / 'di ltar rgyu'i dus na gang gi 'phen pa dang gang 'phen pa dang 'bras bu'i dus na gang gis mngon par 'grub par dang gnang mngon par 'grub pa ste / / de dag thams cad ni yan lag 'di rnams kyis bstan par rig par bya'o / / de la 'phen pa'i yan lag ni ma rig pa dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa ste / / ma 'ongs pa'i skye ba mngon par 'grub par 'gyur par bden pa rnams mi shes pa sngon du 'gro ba'i las kyi bag chags sems la bsgo ba'i phyir ro /
ākṣiptāṅgaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā ca tayā cittavāsanayā nāmarūpādīnā māyatyāṃ pūrvotarasaṃniśrayakrameṇābhinirvṛtaye bījapuṣṭitaḥ
# 'phangs pa'i yan lag ni ming dang gzugs dang skye mched drug dang reg pa dang tshor ba ste / / sems kyi bag chags kyi ming dang gzugs la sogs pa snga ma la phyi ma brten nas rim gyis mngon par 'grub par bya ba'i ched du sems kyi bag chags de dag gi sa bon brtas pa'i phyir ro /
abhinirvartakāṅgaṃ tṛṣṇā upādānaṃ bhavaśca aprahīṇakāmādi tṛṣṇādivasena kāmādiṣu sucaritaduścaritaprakāraratipūrvakeṇa chandarāgeṇa sopādāne vijñāne sati maraṇāvasthāyāṃ phaladānaṃ prati chandarāgānurūpyāntarakarmavāsanābhimukhībhāvāt
# mngon par 'grub par byed pa'i yan lag gi sred pa dang len pa dang srid pa ste / / 'dod chags la sogs pa'i srid pa ma spangs pa'i dbang gis 'dod pa la sogs par legs par spyod pa dang nyes par spyod pa'i rnam pa la goms par dga' ba sngon du 'gro ba'i 'dun pa dang 'dod chags kyis nye bar len pa dang bcas pa'i rnam par shes par yod par gyur ba na 'chi ba'i dus na 'bras bu 'byin par bya ba la 'dun pa dang 'dod chags kyi rjes su mthun pa'i las gang yang rung ba'i bag chags mngon du 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
abhinirvṛttyaṅgaṃ jātirjarāmaṇaṃ ca tena prakāreṇa karmāntaravāsanābhimukhye satyanyatarasmin gatiyonyādibhedabhinne nikāyasabhāge yathākṣipte nāmarūpādinirvṛtteḥ / jātijarāmaraṇavacanaṃ saṃskṛtalakṣaṇatrayādhikāreṇodvejanārtham
# mngon par grub pa'i yan lag ni skye ba dang rga shi ste / / rnam pa des de las gzhan gyi bag chags mngon du gyur na ji ltar 'phangs pa bzhin du 'gro ba dang skye gnas la sogs pa'i bye brag tha dad pa'i ris mthun pa gang yang rung bar ming dang gzugs la sogs pa mngon par 'grub pa'i phyir ro / / skye ba dang rga shi smos pa ni 'dus byas kyi mtshan nyid gsum gyi skabs kyis skyo bar bya ba'i phyir ro /
jarāmaraṇasyaikāṅgakaraṇaṃ vināpi jarāṃ maraṇasaṃbhavāt
# rga ba dang 'chi ba yan lag gcig tu bya ba ni rga ba med par yang 'chi ba'i srid pa'i phyir ro /
na tvevaṃ jarāyujāyāṃ yonau vinā nāmarūpādibhiḥ ṣaḍāyatanādīnāṃ saṃbhava ityeṣāṃ pṛthagaṅgīkaraṇaṃ veditavyam / aṅgapratyayatvavyavasthānaṃ caturaḥ pratyayānadhikṛtya / tatra tāvadavidyā saṃskārāṇāṃ pūrvotpannāvāsanato hetupratyayaḥ tatparibhāvitasaṃtānotpannānāṃ karmaṇāṃ punarbhavābhisaṃskaraṇasāmarthyāt tatkālasamudācāriṇī
# mngal nas skye ba'i gnas su ming dang gzugs la sogs pa med par skye mched drug la sogs pa 'byung ba ni de lta ma yin te / / de'i phyir de dag yan lag so sor bya bar rig par bya'o / / yan lag rkyen nyid du rnam par gzhag pa ni rkyen bzhi'i dbang du byas pa ste / / de la ma rig pa ni 'du byed rnams kyi rkyen te / / snga logs su byung ba'i bag chags kyis rgyu'i rkyen to / / des yongs su bsgos pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i las rnams yang srid par mngon bar 'du byed par nus pa'i phyir te / / de'i tshe kun tu 'byung ba'i tshul can no /
āvedhataḥ samanantarapratyayaḥ tadākṣepakaviśeṣeṇa saṃskārasrotānupravṛtteḥ
# shugs kyis zhes bya ba ni de ma thag pa'i rkyen te / / de'i tshe 'phen pa'i bye brag gis 'du byed kyi rgyun gyi rgyun chags par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
manaskārata ālaṃbanapratyayaḥ mūḍhāvasthāyā agratādibhirayoniśomanaskārālaṃbanībhāvāt
# yid la byed pas zhes bya ba ni dmigs pa'i rkyen te / / rmongs pa'i dus na mchog la sogs par tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pas dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
sahabhāvato 'dhipatipratyayaḥ tadādhipatyena tatsaṃprayuktāyāścetanāyā viparītālaṃbanābhisaṃskaraṇāt
# lhan cig byung bas zhes bya ba ni bdag po'i rkyen te / / de'i dbang gis de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems las byung ba rnams dmigs pa la phyin ci log tu mngon bar 'du byed pa'i phyir ro /
avidyā bhave sattvān saṃmohayati tadāvṛtteḥ pūrvāntāparāntamadhyāntānāṃ yathābhūtāparijñānāt
# ma rig pa ni srid pa la sems can rnams rmongs par byed ces bya ba ni des bsgribs pa rnams sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' dang bar gyi mtha' yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su mi shes pa'i phyir te /
yata evaṃ vicikitsati kiṃ nvahamabhūvamatite 'dhvanyāhosvinnābhūvamityevamādi
# 'di ltar ci bdag 'das pa'i dus na byung ba zhig gam / / 'on te ma byung ba zhig snyam pa la sogs pa de ltar the tshom za ba'o /
pratyayaśca bhavati saṃskārāṇām tadvaśena punarbhavikakarmopacayāt
# 'du byed rnams kyi rkyen kyang yin no zhes bya ba ni de'i dbang gis yang srid pa'i las la sogs pa'i phyir ro /
saṃskārā gatiṣu sattvāna vibhajanti karmavaśena sattvānāṃ gatyantaragamanavaicitryāt
# 'du byed rnams ni yang 'gro ba rnams su sems can dag rnam par 'byed ces bya ba ni las kyi dbang gis sems can rnams 'gro ba gzhan du 'gro ba sna tshogs pa'i phyir ro /
pratyayāśca bhavanti vijñānasya vāsanāyāḥ āyatyā nāmarūpābhinirvṛttaye bījapoṣaṇāt
# rnam par shes pa'i bag chags kyi rkyen kyang yin zhes bya ba ni phyi ma la ming dang gzugs la sogs pa 'grub par 'gyur bar sa bon gso bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
vijñānaṃ karmabandhaṃ dhārayati saskārā hitavāsanāsahotpatteḥ / pratyayaśca bhavati nāmarūpasya mātuḥ kukṣau vijñānāvakrāntyā nāmarūpavivṛddhigamanāt
# rnam par shes pa ni sems can rnams kyi las kyi 'ching ba 'dzin pa zhes bya ba ni 'du byed kyis bskyed pa'i bag chags dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / ming dang gzugs kyi rkyen kyang yin zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa ma'i mngal du zhugs na ming dang gzugs kyi lus 'phel bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
nāmarūpamātmabhāvaṃ sattvān grāhayati tannivṛttyā sattvānāṃ nikāyasabhāgāntarabha janāt / nāmarūpādīnāṃ ṣaḍāyatanādipratyayabhāvaḥ pūrvāṅgasaṃniśrayeṇottarāṅganirvṛttito draṣṭavyaḥ
# ming dang gzugs ni sems can rnams lus len du 'jug ces bya ba ni de grub na sems can rnams ris mthun par gzhan la brten pa'i phyir ro / / ming dang gzugs la sogs pa skye mched drug la sogs pa'i rkyen du 'gyur ba ni yan lag snga ma la brten nas yang lag phyi ma 'grub par blta'o /
ṣaḍāyatanamātmabhāvaparipūriṃ ca sattvān grāhayati tannivṛttāvindriyāntarāvaikalyāt / pratyayaśca bhavati sparśasya / sparśo viṣayopabhoge sattvān pravartayati tanmukhena sukhavedanīyāditrividhaviṣayopabhogāt
# skye mched drug ni sems can rnams lus rdzogs par len du 'jug pa zhes bya ba ni de 'grub na dbang po gzhan ma tshang ba med pa'i phyir ro / / reg pa ni yul gyi longs spyod la sems can rnams 'dzud pa zhes bya ba ni de'i sgo nas bde ba myong bar 'gyur ba la sogs pa'i yul rnam pa gsum la longs spyod pa'i phyir ro /
pratyayaśca bhavati vedanāyāḥ / vedanā janmopabhoge ca sattvān pravartayati tadadhiṣṭhāneneṣṭādikarmavipākopabhogāt / pratyayaśca bhavati tṛṣṇāyāḥ tatsaṃprayogādyabhilāṣamukhena tṛṣṇotpatteḥ
# tshor ba ni skye ba'i longs spyod la sems can rnams 'dzud pa zhes bya ba ni de la brten nas 'dod pa la sogs pa'i las kyi rnam par smin pa la nye bar spyod pa'i phyir ro / / srid pa'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes bya ba ni de dang phrad pa la sogs par 'dod pa'i sgo nas sred pa 'byung pa'i phyir ro /
tṛṣṇā janmani sattvānākarṣati tadvaśena janmāntarasroto 'nupacchedāt
# sred pa ni sems can rnams kyi skye ba 'dren pa zhes bya ba ni de'i dbang gis tshe gzhan du brgyud pa rgyun mi 'chad pa'i phyir ro /
pratyayaśca bhavatyupādānasya āsvādaprārthanāmukhena kāmādiṣu chandarāgapravṛtteḥ
# len pa'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes bya ba ni ro myang bar 'dod pa'i sgo nas 'dod pa la sogs ba la 'dun pa dang 'dod chags 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
upādānaṃ punarbhavādānāya sopādānaṃ ca sattvānāṃ vijñānaṃ karoti narakādigativiśiṣṭapunarbhavapratisaṃdhaye karmavāsanāniyamāt
# len pa ni yang srid pa len pa'i phyir sems can rnams kyi rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa dang bcas par byed ces bya ba ni sems can dmyal ba la sogs pa'i 'gro ba bye brag can du yang srid pa'i nying mtshams sbyor bar 'gyur ba'i las kyi bag chags nges par byed pa'i phyir ro /
pratyayaśca bhavati bhavasya tadvaśena saṃskāravāsanayovṛttilābhāt
# srid pa'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes bya ba ni de'i dbang gis 'du byed kyi bag chags 'byung ba rnyed pa'i phyir ro /
bhavaḥ punarbhave sattvānabhimukhīkaroti anantaragatyantarāvāhanāt pratyayaśca bhavati jāteḥ tato nikāyasabhāgāntaranirvṛtteḥ
# srid pa ni yang srid par sems can rnams mngon du phyogs par byed ces bya ba ni de ma thag tu 'gro ba gzhan 'dren pa'i phyir ro / / skye ba'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes bya ba ni de las ris mthun pa gzhan 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
jātirnāmarūpādyānupūrvyā sattvānabhinirvartayati uttarottarāvasthāntarāvāhanāt / pratyayaśca bhavati jarāmaraṇasya jātau satyāṃ tatprabandhasyānyathātvavināśasaṃbhavāt
# skye ba ni ming dang gzugs la sogs pa'i rim gyis sems can mngon par 'grub par byed pa ni phyi ma phyi ma'i gnas skabs gzhan 'dren pa'i phyir ro / / rga shi'i rkyen kyang yin no zhes bya ba ni skye ba yod na de'i rgyus gzhan du 'gyur ba dang 'jig pa srid pa'i phyir ro /
jarāmaraṇaṃ punaḥpunarvayaḥ pariṇāmena jīvitapariṇāmena ca sattvān yojayati yauvanāyuṣovināśena yojanāt / vijñānasya karmasaṃkleśasaṃgrahaṇaṃ saṃskāravāsanāprabhāvitatvādvijñānāṅgasyaḥ
# rga shi ni yang dang yang na tshod 'gyur ba dang srog 'gyur ba la sems can rnams sbyor ba'o zhes bya ba ni dar la bab pa dang tshe rnam par 'jig pa la sbyor ba'o / / rnam par shes pa las kyi kun nas nyon mongs par bsdu ba ni rnam par shes pa'i yan lag 'du byed kyi bag chags kyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
niṣkartṛkārtha īśvarādikartṛrahitatvāt / sahetukārtho 'vidyādihetukatvāt / niḥsatvārthaḥ svayamanātmatvāt / paratantrārthaḥ pratyayādhīnatvāt / nirīhakārthaḥ pratyayānāṃ nirvyāpāratvāt
# byed pa po med pa'i don zhes bya ba ni dbang phyug la spags pa'i byed pa po dang bral ba phyir ro / / rgyu dang bcas pa las byung ba'i don zhes ba ba ni ma rig pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i phyir ro / / sems can med pa'i don zhes bya ba ni rang bzhin gyis bdag med pa'i phyir ro / / gzhan gyi dbang gis don zhes bya ba ni skyen la rag las pa'i phyir ro / / g yo ba med pa'i don zhes bya ba ni rkyen rnams byed pa med pa'i phyir ro /
anityārtho 'śāśvatatvāt / kṣaṇikārtha utpattikālāt pareṇānavasthānāt / hetuphalaprabandhānupacchedārthaḥ kāraṇakṣaṇa nirodhasamakālaṃ kāryakṣaṇotpādāt
# mi rtag pa'i don zhes bya ba ni ther zug ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / skad cig ma'i don zhes bya ba ni skyes pa'i dus las pha rol tu mi gnas pa'i phyir ro / / rgyu dang 'bras bu'i rgyud rgyun mi 'chad pa'i don zhes bya ba ni rgyu'i skad cig 'gag pa dus mnyam du 'bras bu'i skad cig 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
anurūpahetuphalaparigrahārthaḥ sarvataḥ sarvasyāsaṃbhavāt
# rgyu dang 'bras bu mthun ba'i don zhes bya ba ni thams cad las thams cad mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
vicitrahetuphalārtho 'nekaikajātīyātkāraṇādekānekajātīyakāryotpatteḥ
# rgyu dang 'bras bu sna tshogs kyi don zhes bya ba ni rgyu du ma dang gcig gi rnam pa las 'bras bu'i rnam pa gcig dang du ma 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
pratiniyatahetuphalārthaḥ saṃtānāntarāphalanāt / punarebhirevārthaḥ pratītyasamutpādasya pañcavidhaṃ gāmbhīrya veditavyam
# rgyu dang 'bras bu so sor nges pa'i don zhes bya ba ni rgyu gzhan las 'bras bu gzhan mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / yang don 'di dag gis rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba rnams pa ldas zab par rig par bya ste /
hetugāmbhīrya viṣamahetvahetuvādapratipakṣena dvābhyāmarthābhyām
# rgyus zab pa ni mi mthun pa'i rgyud dang rgyu med par smra ba'i gnyen por don gnyis kyis zab bo /
lakṣaṇagāmbhīrya nirātmakatayaikārthena
# mtshan nyid kyis zab pa ni bdag med pa nyid kyis te don gcig gis so /
utpattigāmbhīrya pratyayebhyaḥ phalotpattāvapyatatkṛtatayā dvābhyāmarthābhyām
# skye pas zab ba ni rkyen rnams las 'bras bu 'byung ba yang des ma byas pa'i phyir te / / don gnyis kyis so /
sthitigāmbhīryamavyavasthitānāṃ sthityābhāsanāddvābhyāmarthābhyām
# gnas pas zab pa ni gnas med kyang gnas par snang ba'i phyir te / / don gnyis kyis so /
pravṛttigāmbhīryaṃ hetuphalapravṛttidurvijñānatvāccaturbhirarthairiti / antareṇa eva kartāraṃ karma kriyā cāsti tatphalopabhogaścetyayamatra karmaphalāvipraṇāśo veditavyaḥ
# 'byung bas zab pa ni rgyu las 'bras bu 'byung ba rnam par shes par dka' ba'i phyir te / / don bzhis zab pa'o / / byed pa po med kyang las dang byed pa dang de'i 'bras bu la spyod pa yod de / / 'di ni 'dir las dang 'bras bu chud mi za bar rig par bya'o /
na svayaṃkṛto dharmo 'nutpannasyābhāvādyenāsau kriyeta
# chos ni bdag nyid kyis ma byas pa ste / / gang gis byed pa de ma skyes te med pa'i phyir ro /
na parakṛtaḥ pratyayānāmakartṛkatvāt
# gzhan gyis kyang ma byas te rkyen rnams byed pa po ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
nobhayakṛta etenaiva kāraṇadvayena
# gnyis kas kyang ma byas te / / rgyu de gnyis kyis ma byas pa'i phyir ro /
nāsvayaṃkārāparakārahetusamutpannaḥ hetupratyayānāṃ phalotpattau sāmarthyāt
# rang gis byed pa dang gzhan gyis byed pa dang rgyu med pa las byung ba yang ma yin no zhes bya ba ni rkyen rnams 'bras bu skyed nus pa'i phyir ro /
aparaḥ paryāyaḥ / na svayaṃkṛtaḥ pratyayāpekṣaṇāt
# rnam grangs gzhan du na bdag nyid kyis ma byas pa ni rkyen la ltos pa'i phyir ro /
na parakṛtaḥ satsvapi pratyayeṣu nirvījasyānutpādāt
# gzhan gyis ma byas pa ni rkyen yod du zin kyang sa bon med pa ni mi skye ba'i phyir ro /
nobhayakṛtastadubhayonirīhakatvāt / nāhetusamutpanno bījapratyayānāṃ śaktisadbhāvāditi
# gnyi gas ma byas pa ni de gnyi ga la g yo ba med pa'i phyir ro / / rgyu med pa las byung ba yang ma yin ba ni sa bon dang rkyen rnams la nus pa yod pa'i phyir ro /
bhavati hyapi
# gzhan yang /
svabījatvānna parataḥ na svayaṃ tadapekṣaṇāt
# rang gis bon las te gzhan las min / / de la ltos phyir bdag gis byas ma yin /
niśceṣṭatvānna ca dvābhyāṃ tacchakternāpyahetutaḥ
# g yo ba med phyir gnyis kyis ma byas la / / de ni nus pas rgyu med byung ma yin /
iti / na svayaṃ na parato dvividhakoṭipratikṣepe 'pi gambhīraḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ syāt prāgeva yatra catasro 'pi koṭayaḥ pratikṣipyante tasmādetasya paramagāmbhīrya veditavyam / vijñānotpattiprabhedataścakṣuḥpratītyarūpāṇi cotpadyate cakṣurvijñānamityevamādi
# bdag las ma yin gzhan las ma yin zhes bya bas / / mu rnam pa gnyis spong yang rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zab par 'gyur na / / gang du mu bzhi char spong ba lta smos kyang ci dgos / / de lta bas na 'di mchog tu zab par rig par bya'o / / rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni mig dang gzugs la brten nas mig gi rnam par shes pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
vyutpattiprabhedataḥ satvalokamadhikṛtya avidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ityevamādi
# 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba'i rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni sems can gyi 'jig rten gyi dbang du byas pa ste / / ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
bāhyavasyotpattiprabhedato bījaṃ pratītyāṅkuraḥ aṅkuraṃ pratītya kāṇḍaḥ
# phyi'i lo tog 'byung ba'i rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni sa bon la brten nas myu gu / / myu gu la brten nas sdong bu ste /
tathā nāpatrapuṣpaphalāni yojyāni / saṃvartavivartaprabhedataḥ sarvasattvasādhāraṇakarmādhipatyaṃ pratītya mahāpṛthivyādīnāmutpādāt
# de bzhin du sbu gu dang 'dab ma dang / / me tog dang 'bras bu rnams kyang sbyar bar rig par bya'o / / 'jig pa dang chags pa'i rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni sems can thams cad kyi thun mong gi las kyi dbang la brten nas sa chen po la sogs pa 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
āhāropastambhaprabhedataścatura āhārān pratītya traidhātuke satvānāmavasthānāt
# zas kyis brten pa'i rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni zas bzhi la brten nas sems can rnams khams gsum na gnas pa'i phyir ro /
iṣṭāniṣṭagativibhāgaprabhedataḥ sucaritaduścarite pratītya sugatidurgatigamanāt / viśuddhiprabhedato mokṣabhāgīyāni pratītya nirvedhabhāgīyotpattito yāvaddarśanabhāvanāmārgānupūrvyārhattvaprāptitaḥ parato vā ghoṣaṃ pratītyādhyātmaṃ ca yoniśo manaskāraṃ samyagdṛṣṭistato yāvatsarvāsravakṣaya iti
# 'dod dang mi 'dod pa'i 'gro ba rnam par 'byed pa'i rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni legs par spyad pa dang nyes par spyad pa la brten nas bde 'gro dang ngan 'gror 'gro ba'i phyir ro / / rnam par dag pa'i rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa la brten nas nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa 'byung ba nas mthong ba dang bsgom pa'i lam gyi rim gyis dgra bcom pa thob pa'i bar dang gzhan gyi sgra la brten nas nang du tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang yang dag pa'i lta ba dang gang zag pa thams cad zad pa'i bar du'o /
prabhāvaprabhedato 'dhigamaṃ pratītyābhijñādayo vaiśeṣikā guṇā iti
# mthu stobs kyis rab tu dbye ba zhes bya ba ni thob ba la brten nas mngon par shes pa la sogs pa yon tan khyad par can rnams 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
ebhiḥ prabhedaivistareṇa saṃskārāṇāṃ pratītyasamutpādo 'nusartavyaḥ
# de ltar rab tu dbye ba 'di dag gis 'du byed rnams rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba rgya cher rtogs par bya'o /
saṃkleśānulomapratiloma iti pravṛtyānupūrvīmadhikṛtya avidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ityevamādyanulomanirdeśaḥ / jarāmaraṇaṃjarāmaraṇasamudayo jarāmaraṇanirodho jarāmaraṇanirodhagāminī pratipaditi satyavyavasthānamadhikṛtya pratilomanirdeśo veditavyaḥ
# kun nas nyon mongs pa'i lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mi mthun pa zhes bya ba ni 'byung ba'i rim pa'i dbang du byas pa ste / / ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni lugs dang mthun par ston to / / rga shi dang rga shi kun 'byung ba dang rga shi 'gog pa dang rga shi 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam zhes bya ba ni / / bden pa rnam par gzhag pa'i dbang du byas pa ste /
vyavadānānulomapratilomata iti tadyathāvidyānirodhāt saṃskāranirodha ityevamādi vyavadānānulomanirdeśaḥ
# lugs dang mi mthun pa bstan par rig par bya'o / / de bzhin du ma rig pa 'gags pas 'du byed 'gag ces bya ba la sogs pa ni rnam par byang ba'i lugs dang mthun pa ston to /
kasminnasati na jarāmaraṇaṃ bhavati kasya nirodhājjarāmaraṇanirodha iti pratilomanirdeśataḥ / hetupratyaya ālayavijñānaṃ kuśalavāsanā ca sāsravānāsravāṇāṃ ca saṃskārāṇāṃ yathākramam
# gang med na rga shi mi 'byung ba dang gang 'gags na rga shi 'gags pa zhes bya ba ni lugs dang mi mthun pa ston to / / rgyu'i rkyen gang zhe na / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dang dge ba'i bag chags so zhes bya ba ni zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa'i 'du byed rnams dang go rims bzhin no /
ālayavijñānaṃ punardvividham vaipākikamābhisaṃskārikaṃ ca
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni rnam pa gnyis te / / rnam par smin pa dang mngon par 'du byed pa las byung ba'o /
tatra vaipākikamupapattiprātilambhikānāṃ hetupratyayaḥ
# de la rnam par smin pa ni skye bas 'thob pa rnams kyi rgyu'i rkyan to /
ābhisaṃskārikaṃ prāyogikānāmāyatyāṃ cālayavijñānāntarasya hetupratyayo draṣṭavyaḥ
# mngon par 'du byed pa las byung ba ni sbyor ba las byung ba rnams kyi ste / / phyi ma la kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan gyi rgyu'i rkyen du blta bar bya'o /
ābhisaṃskārikaṃ punarālayavijñānaṃ tajjānmikapravṛttivijñānasamudācāravāsitaṃ veditavyam
# mngon par 'du byed pa las byung pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni / / tshe de'i 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i bag chags bsgos par rig par bya'o /
kuśalavāsanā mokṣabhāgīyānāṃ vāsanā draṣṭavyā
# dge ba'i bag chags ni thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams kyi bag chags su blta bar bya ste /
teṣāṃ lokottarābhyupagamaniṣyandadharmanaimittikatastadvāsanāyā lokottaradharmahetutvaṃ veditavyam / api khalu svabhāvato 'pītyevamādinā ṣaḍḍhetavo hetupratyaya iti darśayati / tatra svabhāvataḥ prabhedataśca kāraṇahetorvyavasthānam
# de dag ni 'jig rten las 'das pa thob pa'i rgyu mthun pa'i chos kyi rgyu las byung ba'i phyir de'i bag chags ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi rgyu nyid du rig par bya'o / / yang ngo bo nyid ces bya ba la sogs pas ni rgyu drug po dag rgyu'i rkyen du ston to / / de la ngo bo nyid dang rab tu dbye ba ni byed pa'i rgyur rnam par gzhag go /
śeṣaiḥ padaiḥ yathākramaṃ sahabhūsaṃprayuktasabhāgasarvatragavipākahetūnāṃ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam / hetusvabhāvamadhikṛtya kāraṇahetuvyavasthānātsarvahetavaḥ kāraṇahetāvantarbhūtā veditavyāḥ
# tshig lhag ma rnams ni go rims bzhin du lhan cig 'byung ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang skal pa mnyam pa dang kun tu 'gro ba dang rnam par smin pa'i rgyu rnams su rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / rgyu'i ngo bo nyid kyi dbang du byas nas byed pa'i rgyu rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir rgyu thams cad ni byed pa'i rgyu'i nang du 'dus par rig par bya'o /
sahāyādiviśeṣaprabhāvanārtha tu pṛthagvyavasthānam
# grogs la sogs pa ni bye brag bstan pa'i phyir so sor rnam par gzhag go / / byed pa'i rgyu'i rab tu dbye ba la /
kāraṇahetuprabhede vijñānasāmagrayādikaṃ yannirdiṣṭamudāharaṇamātraṃ taddraṣṭavyam tayā diśānyasyāpi tajjātīyasyābhyūhanārtham
# rnam par shes pa'i tshogs la sogs gang bstan pa de ni dpe tsam du blta bar bya'o / / phyogs 'dis ni de lta bu'i rang bzhin can gzhan la yang mngon bar brtag par bya ba'i phyir ro /
tatra utpattikāraṇaṃ tataḥ kāryasyābhūtvā prādurbhāvāt
# de la 'byung ba'i byed rgyu ni de las 'bras bu ma byung ba 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
sthitikāraṇamutpannasya prabandhānupacchedāt
# gnas pa'i byed rgyu ni skyes pa'i rgyud rgyun mi 'chad par byed pa'i phyir ro /
dhṛtikāraṇaṃ pātapratibandhāt
# rten pa'i byed rgyu ni ltung ba'i gegs byed pa'i phyir ro /
prakāśanakāraṇamāvṛtasyābhivyañjanāt
# gsal ba'i byed rgyu ni sgrib pa bsal bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
vikārakāraṇaṃ tatsaṃtānasyānyathātvāpādanāt
# 'gyur ba'i byed rgyu ni rgyud gzhan du 'gyur bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
viyogakāraṇaṃ saṃbandhasya dvaidhīkaraṇāt
# 'bral ba'i byed rgyu ni 'brel ba gnyis su gcod pa'i phyir ro /
pariṇatikāraṇaṃ tadavayavānāṃ deśāntarasaṃcaraṇāt
# bsgyur ba'i byed rgyu ni de'i cha shas yul gzhan du 'pho bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
saṃpratyayakāraṇaṃ tena viparokṣānumānāt
# yid ches pa'i byed rgyu ni des lkog tu gyur pa rjes su dpag pa'i phyir ro /
saṃpratyāyanakāraṇaṃ tena samyaṅniścayāt
# yid ches par byed pa'i byed rgyu ni des yang dag par nges par byed pa'i phyir ro /
prāpaṇakāraṇaṃ tenādhigamāt / vyavahārakāraṇaṃ yathānāmadheyaṃ nimittodgrahaṇenābhiniviśyānuvyavaharaṇāt / apekṣākāraṇamanyatrecchotpattinimittatvāt
# thob pa'i byed rgyu ni des thob par byed pa'i rgyu'i phyir ro / / tha snyad kyi byed rgyu ni ming ji lta ba bzhin du mtshan mar 'dzin pas mngon bar zhen nas rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa'i phyir ro / / ltos pa'i byed rgyu ni gzhan du 'dod pa 'byung ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
ākṣepakāraṇaṃ tadanvayāvasthāntaraparāparabhāvina āvedhakatvāt
# 'phen pa'i byed rgyu ni de'i rgyu las byung ba gnas skabs gzhan du gcig nas gcig tu brgyud de 'byung bas 'phen pa'i phyir ro /
ābhinirvṛttikāraṇamanantarabhāvino janakatvāt
# mngon bar 'grub pa'i byed rgyu ni de ma thag tu 'byung ba bskyed pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
parigrahakāraṇaṃ svabījotpādina upodvalatvāt
# yongs su 'dzin pa'i byed rgyu ni rang gi sa bon las byung ba stobs bskyed pa'i phyir ro /
āvāhanakāraṇaṃ tadānukūlyenākarṣaṇāt
# chud par byed pa'i byed rgyu ni de'i rjes su mthun pas 'grub pa'i phyir ro /
pratiniyamakāraṇaṃ bhinnasvabhāvatayānyonyaphalatvāt
# so sor nges pa'i byed rgyu ni rang bzhin tha dad pas 'bras bu gzhan dang gzhan 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
sahakārikāraṇaṃ svakāryanirvartane kāraṇāntarāpekṣaṇāt
# lhan cig byed pa'i byed rgyu ni rang gi 'bras bu 'grub par byed pa la rgyu gzhan la ltos pa'i phyir ro /
virodhikāraṇaṃ vidhnakaraṇāt
# mi mthun pa'i byed rgyu ni gegs byed pa'i phyir ro /
avirodhikāraṇaṃ tadviparyayeṇa veditavyam
# mi mthun pa ma yin pa'i byed rgyu ni de las bzlog par rig par bya'o /
tadyathā bhūtāni bhautikaṃ ceti yathāsaṃbhavaṃ na tvavaśyaṃ sarvatra saṃghāte catvāri mahābhūtāni bhavanti rūpādikaṃ vā bhautikam
# 'di lta ste 'byung ba rnams dang 'byung ba las gyur pa'o zhes bya ba ni ji ltar mthun mthun du snang gyi [*gi] tshogs pa thams cad dang gzugs la sogs pa 'byung ba las gyur pa la 'byung ba chen po bzhi po dag gdon mi za bar 'byung ba ni ma yin no /
ityato yadyatrāsti tattena sahotpadyate nānyonyaṃ vineti
# de'i phyir gang na gang yod pa de ni de dang lhan cig 'byung ste / / gang yang rung ba zhig med na ni ma yin no /
sahāyanaiyamyena sahabhūheturvyavasthāpitaḥ
# de ltar na grogs su nges pas lhan cig 'byung ba'i rgyur rnam par gzhag go /
bhūtāni bhautikaṃ cetyudāharaṇamātrametadveditavyam cittacaitasikānāmanyonyamavinābhāvaniyamāt
# 'byung ba dag dang 'byung ba las gyur pa zhes bya bas de ni dper brjod pa tsam du zad par rig par bya'o / / sems dang sems las byung ba rnams ni gang yang rung ba zhig med na mi 'byung bar nges pa'i phyir ro /
yadyevaṃ saṃprayuktahetoḥ pṛthagvyavasthānaṃ na prāpnoti cittacaitasikānāṃ sahabhūhetāvantarbhāvāt
# gal te de ltar na mtshungs par ldan pa'i rgyu logs shig tu gzhag tu med par 'gyur te / / sems dang sems las byung ba rnams lhan cig 'byung ba'i rgyu'i nang du 'dus pa'i phyir ro /
yadyapyetadevaṃ tathāpyanyenārthena
# de ltar yin du zin kyang don gzhan gyis mtshungs par ldan pa'i rgyur 'gyur te /
ye dharmāḥ sahabhāvenālaṃbanaṃ pratipadyante nānyatama vaikalyena te saṃpratipattitaḥ saṃprayuktakaheturvyavasthāpyate na sahabhāvamātreṇa tadyathā cittai caitasikāśca / pūrvabhāvitānāmiti pūrvābhyastānāṃ pūrvaṃ samudācaritānāmityarthaḥ
# chos gang dag lhan cig 'byung bas dmigs pa mthun par rtogs kyi gang yang rung ba zhig ma tshang na ma yin pa ste / / 'di lta ste sems dang sems las byung ba rnams so / / sngon dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos bsgoms pa rnams zhes bya ba ni sngon goms par byas pa rnams te / / sngon kun tu spyad ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
