yā aparānte uttarottarā puṣṭataratamā pravṛttiriti taiḥ paripoṣitabījānāṃ tadanvayānāmanāgate kāle viśiṣṭotpattito draṣṭavyā
# phyi ma'i mtha' gong nas gong du shin tu rgyas pa dang mchog tu rgyas par 'byung ba gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni de dag gi sa bon yongs su gsos ba rnams te / / de'i rgyu las byung ba rnams ma 'ongs pa'i dus na khyad par can du 'byung bar blta'o /
evamayaṃ sabhāgahetuḥ sadṛśānāṃ puṣṭinimittatvena vyavasthāpitaḥ / sarvatragaheturna kevalaṃ sadṛśasyaiva puṣṭaye kiṃ tarhi yasya kasyacidrāgādeḥ kleśasyābhyāsena sarveṣāṃ dveṣādīnāṃ prabandhapuṣṭayā dṛḍhīkāro bhavatyato vandhanagāḍhīkaraṇānmokṣaprāptiparipanthārthenāsya vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# de ltar na skal ba mnyam pa'i rgyu 'di ni 'dra ba rnams kyi rgyas par byed pa'i rgyur rnam par gzhag go / / kun tu 'gro ba'i rgyu ni 'dra ba rgyas par byed pa 'ba' zhig tu ma zad kyi / / 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa gang yang rung ba goms par byas pas zhe sdang la sogs pa'i rgyun rgyas par bstan par byed par 'gyur te / / de'i phyir dam du 'ching bar byed pas na thar pa thob pa'i bar du gcod pa'i phyir rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
vipākahetuḥ punarāyatyāmekāntavisadṛśasyaivānivṛttāvyākṛtasyātmabhāvasaṃgra hītavyavipākasyākṣepakatvāt parigrahārthena vyavasthāpitaḥ
# rnam par smin pa'i rgyu ni phyi ma la gcig tu mi 'dra ba bsgribs la lung du mi ston pa'i lus su bsdus pa ste / / rnam par smin pa 'phen pa'i phyir yongs su 'dzin pa'i don gyis rnam par gzhag go /
kuśalasāsravagrahaṇamanāsravāṇāṃ janmavirodhitvenānākṣepakatvāt / nairantaryasamanantarato 'pīti nāvaśyaṃ kṣaṇanairantarya kiṃtarhi cittāntaranairantaryamapyatra nairantarya draṣṭavyam
# dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa smos pa ni zag pa med pa rnams kyi skye ba dang mi mthun pas 'phen pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / rgyun mi 'chad par chad med pa zhes bya ba ni gdon mi za bar skad cig gi bar chad med pa ma yin gyi sems gzhan gyi bar chad med pa yang 'dir bar chad med bar blta bar bya ste /
itarathā hyacittikasamāpattau vyutthānacittasya samāpatticittaṃ na samanantarapratyayaḥ syāt / bhavati ca / tasmādekasmin saṃtāne paścimasya cittasya pūrvakaṃ cittaṃ cittāntareṇānantaritaṃ samanantarapratyayaḥ / yathā cittamevaṃ caitasikā api veditavyāḥ / sabhāgavisabhāgacittacaittotpattisamanantarato 'pīti kuśalāḥ cittacettāḥ kuśalānāṃ sabhāgānāmakuśalāvyākṛtānāṃ ca visabhāgānāmanantarotpannānāṃ samanantarapratyayaḥ / evaṃ kuśalāvyākṛtāḥ svānyaprakārāṇāṃ yojayitavyāḥ / tadyathā kāmāvacarā kāmāvacarāṇāṃ rūpārūpyāvacarānāsravāṇāṃ cānantarotpannānāṃ samanantarapratyayaḥ
# gzhan du na snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems ni sems med pa la snyoms par 'jug pa las langs pa'i sems kyi de ma thag pa'i rkyen du ni mi 'gyur ba'i rigs na 'gyur bas de'i phyir rgyud gcig la phyi ma'i sems dang snga ma'i sems kyi bar du sems gzhan gyis bar du ma chod pa ni de ma thag pa'i rkyen to / / sems la ji lta bar sems las byung ba rnams kyang de bzhin du rig par bya'o / / mthun pa dang mi mthun pa las sems dang sems las byung ba 'byung ba'i de ma thag pas kyang zhes bya ba la / / sems dang sems las byung ba'i dge ba rnams ni mthun pa dge ba rnams dang mi mthun pa mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa de ma thag tu 'byung ba rnams kyi de ma thag pa'i rkyen to / / de bzhin tu mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams kyang rang dang gzhan gyi rnam pa rnams dang sbyar bar bya'o / / de bzhin tu 'dod pa na spyod pa rnams ni 'dod pa na spyod pa rnams dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa dang zag pa med pa de ma thag tu 'byung ba rnams kyi de ma thag pa'i rkyen to /
evaṃ rūpāvacarādayo 'pi pṛthagpṛthagrūpāvacarādonāṃ kāmāvacarādīnāṃ cānantarotpannānāmiti yojayitavyam / kiṃ khalu sarvasya cintasyānantaraṃ sarva cittamutpadyate ahosvidasti pratiniyamaḥ
# de bzhin gzugs na spyod pa la sogs pa yang so sor gzugs na spyod pa la sogs pa dang 'dod pa na spyod pa la sogs pa de ma thag tu 'byung ba rnams kyi de ma thag pa'i rkyen to zhes sbyar bar bya'o / / ci sems can thams cad kyi de ma thag tu sems thams cad 'byung ngam /
astītyucyate / avaitasya cittasyānantaramidaṃ cedaṃ ca cittamutpadyata ityucyamāne bahuvaktavyaṃ jāyate
# 'on te nges pa yod ce na / / nges pa yod ces bya ste sems 'di'i 'og tu sems 'di dang 'di 'byung ngo zhes brjod na ni brjod pa mang bar 'gyur ro /
tasmātsāmānyena cittotpattau lakṣaṇamātraṃ vyavasthāpyate
# de lta bas na spyir sems 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid tsam rnam par gzhag go /
tadyathā daśabhirbalaiścittasyotpādo veditavyaḥ paricayabalena chandabalena prayogabalena samāpattibalena ''vedhabalena hetubalena viṣayabalena smṛtibalena manaskārabalena pratisaṃdhibalena ca
# 'di ltar stobs bcus sems 'byung bar rig par bya ste / / 'dris pa'i stobs dang 'dun pa'i stobs dang sbyor ba'i stobs dang snyom par 'jug pa'i stobs dang 'phen pa'i stobs dang rgyu'i stobs dang yul gyi stobs dang dran pa'i stobs dang yid la byed pa'i stobs dang nying mtshams sbyor ba'i stobs kyis so /
paricayabalaṃ punastrividham mṛdu madhyamadhimātraṃ ca
# 'dris pa'i stobs ni rnam pa gsum ste / / chung ngu 'bring dang chen po'o /
samāpattisthitivyutthānanimittānāmanupalakṣitatvānmṛdu
# snyoms par 'jug pa dang gnas pa dang ldang ba'i rgyu rnams mi mngon pa'i phyir chung ngo /
upalakṣitānāṃ svaparicitta tvānmadhyam / suparicitatopalakṣitatvādadhimātram
# mngon par legs par ma 'dris pa'i phyir 'bring ngo / / legs par 'dris pa'i phyir chen po'o /
tatra mṛdunā paricayabalena dhyānārūpyāṇāmanupūrvyasamāpattirveditavyā
# de la 'dris pa chung ngu'i stobs kyis ni bsam gtan dang gzugs med pa rnams la mthar gyis snyoms par 'jug par rig par bya'o /
madhyena vyutkrāntakasamāpattirekāntarikayogena
# 'bring gis ni gcig gis bar du gcod pa'i tshul gyis thod rgal du snyoms par 'jug go /
adhimātreṇa yatheṣṭaṃ sarvāṇi vā vyutkrāmyānulomaṃ pratilomaṃ ca samāpattirveditavyā / chandabalena dvitīyadhyānalābhī prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ samāpanno yadyākāṃkṣati dvitīyadhyānabhūmikaṃ vyutthānacittamāmukhīkarotyatha nā kāṃkṣati kāmāvacaraṃ kuśalamanivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ vā
# chen pos ni ji ltar 'dod pa'am thams cad la thod rgal du zhugs nas lugs dang mthun pa dang lugs dang mi mthun par snyoms par 'jug par rig par bya'o / / 'dun pa'i stobs kyis ni bsam gtan gnyis pa thob pa bsam gtan dang po la snyoms par zhugs la / / gal te 'dod na bsam gtan gnyis pa'i sa pa las ldang ba'i sems mngon du byed do / / gzhan du 'dod na yang 'dod pa na spyod pa dge ba'am ma bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan pa mngon du byed do /
evamanyatrāpi vistareṇa yojyam
# de bzhin du gzhan la'ang rgya cher sbyar bar bya'o /
prayogabalena kāmāvacarasya kuśalasyavānantaraṃ tatprathamato rūpāvacaraṃ cittamutpadyate
# sbyor ba'i stobs kyis ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i dge ba nyid kyi mjug thogs su thog ma kho nar gzugs na spyod pa'i sems 'byung ngo /
anāgamyasya kuśalasyānantaraṃ maulam / maulasya kuśalasyānantaraṃ dvitīyadhyānasamāpannakamityevamādi vistareṇa yāvadbhavāgrāt veditavyam
# mi lcogs pa med pa'i dge ba'i mjug thogs su dngos gzhi'o / / dngos gzhi'i mjug thogs su bsam gtan gnyis pa'i nyer bsdogs zhes bya ba la sogs pa nas rgya cher srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du rig par bya'o /
samāpattibalena śuddhakaṃ samāpannasya kadācicchuddhakamevotpadyate kadācitkliṣṭam
# snyoms par 'jug pa'i stobs kyis ni dag pa la snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems res 'ga' ni dag pa pa gnyis skye'o / / res 'ga' ni nyon mongs pa can no /
āvedhavalena samādhervyutthāya caratastāvatsamāhitabhūmikaṃ cittamasamāhitakṣaṇānantaravyatibhinnamanuvartate yāvattadvirodhikleśasamudācārātparihīṇa iti
# 'phen pa'i stobs kyis ni ting nge 'dzin las langs nas rgyu ba na ji srid du de dang mi mthun pa nyon mongs pa kun tu 'byung bas yongs su nyams par ma gyur ba de srid du mnyam par gzhag pa'i sa pa'i sems dang mnyam par ma bzhag pa'i skad cig 'dren mar rjes su 'jug go /
tadvirodhi kleśasaṃprayuktasya punaścittasya hetvādibhiśca turbhirbalaiḥ samudācāro veditavyaḥ tatra tāvaddhetubalena yadyavaśyaṃ bhūmiparihāṇisaṃvartanīyamāvaraṇaṃ pūrvamupacitaṃ bhavati viṣayabalena yadi rāgādyutpatyanukūlaḥ śubhādinimittaḥ prabhāvotkaṭaviṣaya ābhāsasamāgato bhavati smṛtivalena yadi smaraṇasaṃkalpairatītānviṣayān prapañcayati manaskārabalena yadi mīmāṃsāmanaskāreṇānyatarānyataracchubhanimittaṃ manasikarotīti
# de dang mi mthun pa nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems ni rgyu la sogs pa'i stobs bzhis kun tu 'byung bar rig par bya'o / / de la rgyu'i stobs kyis ni gal te gdon mi za bar yongs su nyams par 'gyur ba'i sgrib pa sngon bsags par gyur pa'o / / yul gyi stobs kyis ni gal te 'dod chags la sos pa 'byung ba dang mthun pa / / sdug pa la sogs pa'i mtshan ma'i stobs shas che ba'i yul snang bar 'gyur ba'o / / dran pa'i stobs kyis ni gal te dran pa'i kun tu rtog pa dag gis 'das pa'i yul la 'pho bar byed pa'o / / yid la byed pa'i stobs kyis ni gal te spyod pa'i yid la byed pas sdug pa'i mtshan ma gang yang rung ba yid la byed pa'o /
pratisaṃdhibalena nava maraṇacittānyātmabhāvatṛṣṇāsaṃprayuktāni triṣu dhātuṣupratyekaṃ kāmarūpārūpyāvacarāṇi / tatra kāmadhātoścyutvā kāmadhātāveva pratisaṃdhi vadhnataḥ kāmāvacaramātmabhāvatṛṣṇāsaṃprayuktaṃ maraṇacittaṃ veditavyam
# nying mtshams sbyor ba'i stobs kyis ni / / 'chi ba'i sems rnam pa dgu ste lus la sred pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa khams gsum du so sor 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa dag go / / de la 'dod pa'i khams nas shi 'phos nas 'dod pa'i khams de nyid du nying mtshams sbyor ba'i 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lus la sred pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa ni 'chi 'pho ba'i sems su rig par bya'o /
rūpārūpyadhātvoḥ pratisaṃdhi badhnato rūpārūpyāvacaram / tathā rūpārūpyadhātubhyāṃ cyutvā tatra vānyatra votpadyamānasya ṣaṭcittāni yojayitavyāni
# gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams su nying mtshams sbyor ba'i sems ni gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i 'chi ba'i sems su rig par bya'o / / de bzhin du gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams nas shi 'phos nas de nyid dang gzhan du skyes pa'i sems kyang drug tu sbyar bar bya'o /
sā punarātmabhāvatṛṣṇā sahajānirūpitālaṃbanānivṛtāvyākṛtā ca / ātmabhāvajātiścāsyāḥ prakārāparicchedenālaṃbanaṃ veditavyam
# lus la sred pa de ni lhan cig skyes pa dang dmigs pa la mi spyod pa dang bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan ba'o / / lus dang lhan cig skyes pa 'di ni dmigs pa ni rnam pa yongs su mi gcod par rig par bya ste /
tadvaśenānantaraṃ pṛthagjanānāmantarābhavapratisaṃdhiḥ
# de'i dbang gis de ma thag tu so so'i skye bo rnams ni bar ma do'i srid par nying mtshams sbyor ro /
āryāṇāmapyavītarāgāṇāṃ maraṇakāle yāvadaspaṣṭasaṃjñāvasthāṃ na gacchati tāvadasau tṛṣṇā samudācarati
# 'phags pa 'dod chags dang ma bral ba rnams ni 'chi ba'i dus na ji tsam du 'du shes mi gsal ba'i gnas skabs su ma gyur pa de srid du sred pa de kun tu 'byung ngo /
te tvenāṃ paricchidya pratipakṣeṇābhinigṛhṇanti
# de dag ni yongs su rtogs nas gnyen pos tshar gcod do /
vītarāgāṇāṃ tvāryāṇāṃ pratipakṣasya valīyastvānnaivāsau samudācaratyaprahīṇāpi satī
# 'phags pa 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams ni ma spongs su zin kyang gnyen po'i stobs che bas de kun tu mi 'byung ngo /
tadanuśayavaśena tu teṣāṃ pratisaṃdhiḥ
# de'i bag la nyal gyi dbang gis ni de dag nying mtshams sbyor ro /
antarābhavapratisaṃdhikṣaṇaḥ punarnityamanivṛtāvyākṛta eva vipākatvāt
# bar ma do'i srid pa'i nying mtshams sbyor ba'i skad cig ni rtag tu ma bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan pa nyid de / / rnam par smin pa'i phyir ro /
tata ūrdhva kuśalo 'pyakuśalo 'pyavyākṛto 'pi yathāsaṃbhavam cyuticittaṃ sthāpayitvā / antarābhavacyuticittaṃ tu nityaṃ kliṣṭaṃ maraṇabhavavat
# de'i 'og tu ni dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar te / / 'chi 'pho ba'i sems ma gtogs so / / bar mdo'i srid pa'i 'chi 'pho ba'i sems ni rtag tu nyon mongs pa can te / / 'chi 'pho ba'i srid pa bzhin no /
upapattipratisaṃdhiḥ punarnityamanivṛtāvyākṛta eveti veditavyam / bodhisattvānāṃ tu praṇidhānabalenopapadyamānānāṃ maraṇacittādikamekāntena sarva kuśalaṃ veditavyam / samāptaḥ samanantara pratyayaprasaṅgaḥ
# skye ba'i nying mtshams sbyor ba ni rtag tu ma bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan pa nyid du rig par bya'o / / byang chub sems dpa' smon lam gyi stobs kyis skye ba rnams kyi 'chi ba'i sems la sogs pa ni thams cad kyang gcig tu dge bar rig par bya'o / / de ma thag pa'i rkyen gyi skabs rdzogs so / / yul yongs su chad pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni /
paricchinnaviṣayālaṃbanataḥ pañcānāṃ vijñānakāyānāmālaṃbanam pratiniyataviṣayatvāt pañcānāṃ vijñānakāyānām / aparicchinnaviṣayālaṃbanataḥ manovijñānasyālaṃbanam sarvadharmaviṣayatvānmanovijñānasya
# rnam par shes pa tshogs lnga po dag gi dmigs pa ste / / rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga po dag gi yul so sor nges pa'i phyir ro / / yul yongs su ma chad pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa ste / / chos thams cad yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
acitrīkāraviṣayālaṃbanato 'vyutpannasaṃjñānāṃ manovijñānasyālaṃbanam nāmato 'kṣarīkartumaśakyatvāt
# yul la bkra bar 'dzin pa med pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni ming lam byang ba rnams kyi yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i dmigs pa ste / / ming dang yi ger byed mi nus pa'i phyir ro /
citrīkāraviṣayālaṃbanatastadviparyayādveditavyam
# yul la bkra bar 'dzin pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni / / de las bzlog par rig par bya'o /
savastukaviṣayālaṃbanato dṛṣṭimasmimānaṃ tatsaṃprayuktāṃśca dharmān sthāpayitvā tadanyeṣāmālaṃbanam
# dngos po dang bcas pa'i yul gyi dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni lta ba dang nga rgyal dang de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i chos rnams ma gtogs par de las gzhan pa dag gi dmigs pa'o /
avastukaviṣayālaṃbanataḥ sthāpitānāmālaṃbanam ātmādhiṣṭhānatvāt
# dngos po med ba'i yul gyi dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni ma gtogs pa rnams kyi dmigs pa ste / / bdag gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro /
vastvālaṃbanato 'nāsravālaṃbanān visabhāgadhātubhūmisarvatragānanivāritavastukāṃścātītānāgatālaṃbanān sthāpayitvā tadanyeṣāmālaṃbanam
# dngos po'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni / / zag pa med pa la dmigs pa dang skal ba mi mnyam pa'i khams dang sa'i kun tu 'gro ba rnams dang ma 'ongs pa'i dmigs pa gzhi gtan la phebs pa med pa ma gtogs par de las gzhan pa dag gi dmigs pa'o /
parikalpālaṃbanataḥ sthāpitānāmālaṃbanam svaparikalpamātrālaṃbanāt
# kun tu brtags pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni ma gtogs pa rnams kyi dmigs pa ste / / rang gi kun brtags pa tsam la dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
viparyastālaṃbanaṃ nityādyākārāṇām / aviparyastālaṃbanamanityādyākārāṇām / savyāghātālaṃbanamaprahīṇajñeyāvaraṇānām / avyāghātālaṃbanaṃ prahīṇajñeyāvaraṇānāmiti / ālaṃbanapratyaye viniścayaḥ lakṣaṇato 'pi prabhedato 'pi sthitito 'pi parijñānato 'pi prahāṇato 'pyālavanavyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# phyin ci log gi dmigs pa zhes bya ni rtag pa la sogs pa'i rnam par byung ba rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / phyin ci ma log pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni mi rtag pa la sogs pa'i rnam par 'byung ba rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / thogs pa dang bcas ba'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni shes bya'i sgrib pa ma spangs pa rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / thogs pa med pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni sgrib pa spong ba rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / dmigs pa'i rkyen gyi rnam par nges pa ni mtshan nyid dang rab tu dbye ba dang; bzhag pa dang yongs su shes pa dang spangs pas kyang dmigs pa rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
kathaṃ lakṣaṇataḥ / yo 'rthastatpratibhāsānāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāmutpattinimittama te cotpannāstadarthābhiniveśavyavahārapratyātmāvagamāya bhavanti tadālaṃbanalakṣaṇam
# mtshan nyid kyis ji lta bu zhe na / / don gang der snang ba'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams 'byung ba'i rgyu dang de dag byung nas kyang don de la mngon par zhen pa dang tha snyad 'dogs pa dang so so rang gis rig par 'gyur ba ni dmigs pa'i mtshan nyid do /
kathaṃ prabhedataḥ / asadālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā viparyastānāṃ cittacaitasikānāmatītānāgatasvapnapratirbibamāyādyālaṃbanaṃ ca
# rab tu dbye bas ji lta bu zhe na / / med pa'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / sems dang sems las byung ba phyin ci log pa rnams kyi dmigs pa dang 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang rmi lam dang gzugs brnyan dang sgyu ma la sogs pa'i dmigs pa'o /
sadālaṃbanaṃ tadanyeṣām / anālaṃbanamālaṃbanaṃ rūpaṃ cittaviprayuktā asaṃskṛtaṃ ca
# yod pa'i dmigs pa ni de las gzhan pa dag gi dmigs pa'o / / dmigs pa med pa'i dmigs pa ni gzugs dang sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa dang 'dus ma byas so /
sālaṃbanamālaṃbanaṃ cittacaitasikā dharmāḥ
# dmigs pa dang bcas pa'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams so /
samyaktvālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā kuśalam / mithyātvālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā kliṣṭam
# yang dag pa nyid kyi dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste dge ba'o / / log pa nyid kyi dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste nyon mongs pa can no /
naivasamyakratvanamithyātvālaṃbanaṃ tadyathānivṛtāvyākṛtam
# yang dag pa nyid kyang ma yin la log pa nyid kyang ma yin pa'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste ma bsgribs pa'i lung du ma bstan pa'o /
yoniśa ālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā kuśalānāṃ cittacaitasikānām
# tshul bzhin gyi dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / sems dang sems las byung ba'i dge ba rnams kyi dmigs pa'o /
ayoniśa ālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā kliṣṭānām / naivayoniśonāyoniśastadvinirmuktānām / sabhāgamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā kuśalādīnāṃ kuśalādīni svabhūmikānāṃ ca svabhūmikaṃ sāsravāṇāṃ ca sāsravamanāsravāṇāṃ cānāsravam / visabhāgamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā kuśalādīnāmakuśalādīnyanyabhūmikānāṃ cānyabhūmikaṃ sāsravānāsravayoścānāsravasāsravam / nānātvamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā savitarkavicārāṇāṃ cittacaitasikānām
# tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / nyon mongs pa can rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / tshul bzhin yang ma yin la tshul bzhin ma yin pa yang ma yin pa'i dmigs pa ni de dag ma gtogs pa rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / 'dra ba'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / dge ba la sogs pa rnams kyi dge ba la sogs pa dang rang gis pa rnams kyi rang gis pa dang zag pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa rnams kyi zag pa med pa'o / / mi mthun pa'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / dge ba la sogs pa rnams kyi mi dge ba la sogs pa dang sa gzhan pa rnams kyi sa gzhan pa dang zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa rnams kyi zag pa med pa dang zag pa dang bcas pa'o / / sna tshogs kyi dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / sems dang sems las byung ba rtog pa dang bcas dpyod pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / gcig bu'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste /
ekatvamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathāvitarkāvicārāṇām / vibhūtyālaṃbanaṃ tadyathāsaṃjñikaprāyogikānāṃ cittacaitasikānāmākāśavijñānānantyāyatanikānāṃ ca
# sems dang sems las byung ba mi rtog mi dpyod pa rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / 'bral ba'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / 'du shes med pa la sogs pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams dang nam mkha' dang rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched kyi dmigs pa'o / / 'bral ba ni med par 'gyur ba'o /
abhisaṃkṣiptaṃ sūkṣmamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathākiṃcanyāyatanikānām / paryantikaṃ sūkṣmamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanikānām
# gzhan du na 'bral ba chen po nyid la bya'o / / bsdus pa phra ba'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / ci yang med pa'i skye mched pa rnams kyi dmigs pa'o / / mthar phyin pa'i phra ba'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched pa rnams kyi dmigs pa'o /
kleśa ālaṃbanaṃ tenālaṃbyata iti kṛtvā
# nyon mongs pa'i dmigs pa ni des dmigs par byed pa'i phyir dmigs pa zhes bya'o /
dharma ālaṃbanaṃ tadyathāryāṇāṃ nāmakāyapadakāyavyañjanakāyāḥ / artha ālaṃbanaṃ tadāśrito 'rthaḥ / parīttamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā śrāvakayānam / vipulamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā mahāyānam / nimittamālavanaṃ tadyathā śamathapragrahopekṣānimittāni
# mdo sde'i tshig la yod pa'i chos kyi dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / gtsug lag rnams kyi ming gi tshogs dang tshig gi tshogs dang yi ge'i tshogs rnams so / / don gyi dmigs pa ni de la brten pa brjod par bya ba'i don gang yin pa'o / / chung ngu'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / nyan thos kyi theg pa'o / / rgya chen po'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / theg pa chen po'o / / mtshan ma'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / zhi gnas dang rab tu 'dzin pa dang btang snyoms kyi mtshan ma rnams so /
animittamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā nirvāṇaṃ bhavāgrayaṃ ca
# mtshan ma med pa'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / mya ngan las 'das pa dang srid pa'i rtse mo'o /
tattvamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā tathatā ṣoḍaśānāṃ cākārāṇāṃ satyāni / vaihārikamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā nirodhasamāpattiḥ
# de kho na'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / de bzhin nyid dang rnam pa bcu drug po dag gi dmigs pa'i bden pa rnams so / / gnas par bya ba'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la sbyor ba sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi dmigs pa'o /
vaśavartyālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā vimokṣādīnāṃ sarvākārajñatāvasānānāṃ guṇānām
# dbang bsgyur ba'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / rnam par thar pa la sogs pa rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mthar thug pa'i yon tan rnams kyi dmigs pa'o /
kṣaṇikamālaṃbanaṃ tadyathāśaikṣāṇāṃ tajjanmikameva / anuvartyālaṃbanaṃ tadyathā buddhabodhisattvānām
# skad cig pa'i dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / mi slob pa rnams kyi tshe de nyid do / / rjes su 'brang ba rnams kyi dmigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dmigs pa'o /
kathaṃ sthititaḥ / ālaṃbanasyāpariniṣpattitastathā vyavasthāpanāt / caturbhiśca kāraṇairapariniṣpannamālaṃbanaṃ veditavyam viruddhavijñānanimittatayā anālaṃbanavijñānopalabdhyā yatnamantareṇāviparyāsaprasaṅgatayā trividhajñānānuvartanatayā ca / tataśca grāhakasyāpyapariniṣpattiḥ
# gzhan pa ji lta bu zhe na / / de bzhin du rnam par gzhag pa'i phyir dmigs pa yongs su ma grub pas so / / rnam pa bzhis yongs su ma grub pa'i dmigs par rig par bya ste / / rnam par shes pa ji mthun pa'i rgyu dang dmigs pa med pa'i rnam par shes pa dmigs pa dang bsgribs pa med par yang phyin ci log med par 'gyur ba dang shes pa gsum gyi rjes su mthun par 'gyur bas so / / de'i phyir 'dzin pa yang yongs su ma grub pa'o /
trividhaṃ jñānaṃ vaśitājñānaṃ vipaśyanājñāna nirvikalpajñānaṃ ca
# shes pa rnam pa gsum ni dbang gi shes pa dang lhag mthong gi shes pa dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i shes pa'o /
tatra caturṇā kāraṇānāmudāharaṇāni
# de la rnam pa bzhi'i dper brjod pa ni /
pretatiryagmanuṣyāṇāṃ devānāṃ ca yathārha taḥ
# yi dgas dud 'gro mi rnam dang / / lha rnams ji ltar rigs rigs su /
tulyavastumanobhedādarthāniṣpattiriṣyate
# dngos gcig yid ni tha dad phyir / / don ma grub par 'dod pa yin /
atītādau tathā svapne pratibiṃbadvaye 'pi ca
# 'das sogs de bzhin rmi lam dang / / gzugs brnyan rnam pa gnyis po yang /
asannālaṃbanatvācca tadālaṃbanayogataḥ
# med phyir dmigs pa med pa'i phyir / / de ni dmigs par rung ma yin /
arthasyārthatvaniṣpattau jñānaṃ na syādakalpakam
# don ni don du grub gyur na / / mi rtog ye shes med par 'gyur / / shes pa rtog pa med mi 'gyur /
tadabhāvācca buddhatvaprāptirnaivopapadyate
# de med pas na sangs rgyas nyid / / thob par 'thad pa ma yin no /
bodhisattve vaśiprāpte 'dhimuktivaśādyataḥ / tathābhāvaḥ pṛthivyādau dhyāyināṃ copalabhyate
# byang chub sems dpa' dbang thob dang / / rnal 'byor pa la 'di ltar yang / / mos pa'i dbang gis sa la sogs / / dngos po de ltar dmigs par 'gyur /
niṣpannavicayasyeha dhīmataḥ samādhilābhinaḥ
# 'di la rnam par 'byed grub dang / / blo ldan zhi ba thob pa yi /
sarvadharmamanaskāre tathārthakhyānato 'pi ca
# chos kun yid la byed pa la / / de ltar don ni snang ba'i phyir /
jñānacāre 'vikalpe hi sarvārthākhyānato 'pi ca
# mi rtog ye shes rgyu ba la / / don kun snang ba med phyir yang /
arthābhāvopagantavyo vijñaptestadabhāvataḥ
# don med khong du chud bar bya / / de med pas na rnam rig med /
kathaṃ parijñānataḥ
# yongs su shes pas ji lta bu zhe na /
lakṣaṇaprabhedasthitīnāṃ yathābhūtajñānataḥ / kathaṃ prahāṇataḥ / śrāvakayānamahāyānābhyāmāśrayaparivṛttitaḥ
# mtshan nyid dang rab tu dbye ba dang gzhag pa rnams yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes pa'i phyir ro / / spong bas ji lta bu zhe na / / nyan thos dang theg pa chen pos gnas gyur pa ste /
śrāvakayānāśrayaparivṛttyā skandhadhātvāyatanālaṃbanebhyo vimokṣo na tu teṣu vibhutvalābhaḥ
# nyan thos kyi theg pas gnas gyur pas ni / / phung po dang khams dang skye mched kyi dmigs pa dag las rnam par thar gyi /
mahāyānāśrayaparivṛttyā tūbhayamiti / samāpta ālaṃbanapratyaye yathāgranthaṃ viniścayaḥ / pratiṣṭhādhipatitaḥ vāyumaṇḍalādīnyammaṇḍalādīnām bhājanalokaḥ sattvalokasya bhūtāni bhautikānām indriyāṇi vijñānānāmityevamādi
# de dag la dbang 'byor pa thob pa ni ma yin no / / theg pa chen pos gnas gyur pa ni gnyis pa'o / / dmigs pa'i rkyen gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par nges pa rdzogs so / / rten la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba la rlung gi dkyil 'khor la sogs pa ni chu'i dkyil 'khor la sogs pa la rten la dbang byed pas bdag po'i rkyen to / / snod kyi 'jig rten ni sems can gyi 'jig rten gyi'o / / 'byung ba rnams ni 'byung ba las gyur pa rnams kyi'o / / dbang po rnams ni rnam par shes pa rnams kyi'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
āvedhādhipatitaḥ sarvasattvasādhāraṇaṃ karma bhājanalokasya paurāṇaṃ sāsravakarma vipākasyetyevamādi sahabhāvādhipatitaḥ cittaṃ caitasānām manaskāraḥ cittasya sparśī vedanāyā ityevamādi / ataḥ paraṃ dvāviśati mindriyāṇyadhikṛtyādhipativyavasthānaṃ veditavyam / tatra viṣayādhipatitaḥ cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanaindriyānām tadādhipatyena rūpādyabhinirvṛtteḥ
# 'phen pa la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba la sems can thams cad kyi thun mong gi las ni snod kyi 'jig rten 'phen pa la dbang byed bas bdag po'i rkyen to / / sngon gyi zag pa dang bcas pa'i las rnams ni rnam par smin pa'i'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / lhan cig 'byung ba la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba la / / sems ni sems las byung ba rnams kyi lhan cig 'byung ba la dbang byed pas bdag po'i rkyen to / / yid la byed pa ni sems kyi'o / / reg pa ni tshor ba'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / 'di man chad ni dbang po nyi shu rtsa gnyis kyi dbang du byas te / / bdag por rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / de la yul la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi dbang po rnams te / / de'i dbang gis gzugs la sogs pa mngon par 'grub ba'i phyir ro /
prasavādhipatitaḥ strīpuruṣendriyayoḥ tadādhipatyena garbhāvakramaṇāt
# skye bar dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni pho dang mo'i dbang po ste / / de'i dbang gis mngal du 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
sthānādhipatito jīvitendriyasya tadvaśena nikāyasabhāgasthānāt
# gnas par dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni srog gi dbang po ste / / de'i dbang gis ris mthun par gnas pa'i phyir ro /
phalopabhogādhipatitaḥ sukhaduḥkhasaumanasyopekṣendriyāṇām tadadhiṣṭhāneneṣṭāniṣṭavipākapratisaṃvedanāt / laukikaviśudhyadhipatitaḥ śraddhāvīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñendriyāṇām taiḥ kleśaviṣkambhaṇāt / lokottaraviśudhyadhipatito 'nājñātamājñāsyāmīndriyasyājñendriyasyājñātāvīndriyasya ca vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam tairanuśayasamudghātāditi
# 'bras bu la nye bar spyod par dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms kyi dbang po rnams te / / de'i dbang gis sdug pa dang mi sdug pa'i rnam par smin pa so sor nyams su myong ba'i phyir ro / / 'jig rten pa'i rnam par dag pa la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni dad pa dang brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi dbang po rnams te / / de dag gis nyon mongs pa rnam par gnon pa'i phyir ro / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rnam par dag pa la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa'i dbang po dang kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po la rnam par gzhag par rig par bya ste / / de dag gis bag la nyal legs par bcom pa'i phyir ro /
vijñānāvirahitatatsādṛśyendriyaviṣayaprabandhotpattitaḥ sabhāgaṃ veditavyam vijñānasahitasya vijñānasādṛśyenendriyasya viṣayeṣu prabandhenotpatteḥ vijñānavṛttisādṛśyārthena tadindriyaṃ sabhāgamityucyate
# rnam par shes pa dang ma bral zhing de dang 'dra ba'i dbang po yul la rgyun du 'byung ba zhes bya ba ni brten pa mtshungs par rig par bya ste / / rnam par shes pa dang ldan zhing rnam par shes pa dang 'dri ba'i dbang po yul rnams la rgyun du 'byung zhing rnam par shes pa 'byung ba dang 'dra ba'i phyir dbang po de ni brten pa dang mtshungs pa zhes bya'o /
vijñānavirahitasvasādṛśyaprabandhotpattitastatsabhāgam vijñānena viprayuktasyendriyasya svātmasādṛśyena prabandhotpattirindriyalakṣaṇasādṛśyārthena tatsabhāgaṃ veditavyam
# rnam par shes pa dang bral zhing rang dang 'dra ba rgyun du 'byung bas zhes bya ba ni de dag dang mtshungs pa ste / / rnam par shes pa dang mi ldan pa'i dbang po bdag nyid dang 'dra ba ni rgyun du 'byung zhing dbang po'i mtshan nyid dang 'dra ba'i phyir de dang mtshungs par rig par bya'o /
rūpaskandhaikadeśaścakṣurādipañcendriyalakṣaṇaḥ / pañca rūpīṇi dhātvāyatanāni cakṣurādīnītyeva / vedanotpattyāśrayarūpata iti yadrūpamāśritya vedanotpadyate tadupāttamityucyate
# gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig ces bya ba ni mig la sogs pa dbang po lnga'i mtshan nyid do / / gzugs can gyi khams dang skye mched lnga'o zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs ba nyid do / / tshor ba 'byung ba'i gnas kyi gzugs kyi zhes bya ba ni gzugs gang la brten nas tshor ba 'byung ba de zin pa zhes bya'o /
rūpaskandhaikadeśaḥ sādhiṣṭhānendriyasaṃgahītaḥ
# gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig ces bya ba ni gnas dang bcas pa'i dbang pos bsdus pa'o /
pañca rūpīṇi dhātvāyatanāni cakṣurādīni / caturṇāṃ caikadeśaḥ rūpagandharasaspraṣṭavyānāmindriyāvinirbhāgī
# khams dang skye mched gzugs can lnga / / zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pa'o / / bzhi'i phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dbang po las gzhan du ma gyur pa'o /
viṣayagrahaṇādhipatitaścakṣurādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām tadādhipatyena rūpādyālaṃbane cittacaitapravṛteḥ
# yul la 'dzin par dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pa drug ste / / de'i dbang gis gzugs la sogs pa'i dmigs pa la sems dang sems las byung ba rnams 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
kulaprabandhādhipatitaḥ strīpuruṣendriyayoḥ tataḥ putrapautrādyanvayapravṛtteḥ
# rigs kyi rgyud la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba ni pho dang mo'i dbang po ste / / de las bu dang tsha bo la sogs pa'i rigs 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
śeṣaṃ yathādhipatipratyaye nirdiṣṭaṃ tathānugantavyam
# lhag ma ni bdag po'i rkyen ji skad bstan pa de bzhin du khong du chud par bya'o /
rūpaskandhaikadeśaścakṣuḥ śrotraghrāṇajihvākāyastrīpuruṣendriyalakṣaṇaḥ
# gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig ces bya ba ni / / mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid dang pho dang mo'i dbang po'i mtshan nyid do /
saṃskāraskandhaikadeśo jīvitaśraddhāvīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñendriyalakṣaṇaḥ
# 'du byed kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig ces bya ba ni srog dang dad ba dang brtson 'grus dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi dbang po'i mtshan nyid do /
dvādaśa dhātava indriyavijñānadhātavaḥ
# khams bcu gnyis zhes bya ba ni dbang po dang rnam par shes pa'i khams rnams so /
ṣaḍāyatanānyādhyātmikāni
# skye mched drug ces bya ba ni nang gi rnams so /
dharmadhātvāyatanaikadeśaśca jīvitendriyaṃ sukhādīni śraddhādāni pañca
# chos kyi khams dang skye mched kyi phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni srog gi dbang po dang bde ba la sogs pa dang dad pa la sogs pa lnga lnga'o /
duḥkhā vedanā duḥkhātmikā satī svenaiva lakṣaṇena duḥkhaduḥkhatāḥ / tadutpattinimittabhūtāstvindriyārthāstatsaṃprayuktāśca duḥkhavedanīyatvādduḥkhaduḥkhatā draṣṭavyā / sukhāyā vedanāyāstadvedanīyānāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ vipariṇāmena daurmanasyotpādāt tadvipariṇatirvipariṇāmaduḥkhatā / tatra cānunayena cittasya vipariṇamanaṃ vipariṇāmaduḥkhatā veditavyā
# sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba ni sdug bsngal gyi bdag nyid yin te / / rang gi mtshan nyid kho nas sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid do / / de las 'byung ba'i rgyur gyur pa dbang po dang don rnams dang de dang mtshungs par ldan pa rnams ni sdug bsngal myong bar byed pa'i phyir sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid du blta'o / / bde ba'i tshor ba dang de myong bar byed pa'i chos rnams 'gyur bas yid mi bde ba 'byung ba'i phyir de 'gyur ba ni 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid do / / de la yang rjes su chags pas sems 'gyur ba ni 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid du rig par bya ste /
yathoktamavadīrṇo vipariṇatena citteneti / aduḥkhāsukhā vedanālayavijñānasaṃprayuktā tadvedanīyāśca saṃskārā duḥkhavipariṇāmaduḥkhatayodauṣṭhulyenānugatatvāttena duḥkhatādvayenāvinirmuktatvādekadā duḥkhāvasthāṃ bhajante ekadā sukhāvasthāṃ na nityakālamaduḥkhāsukhāvasthā eva bhavanti
# ji skad du zhen nas gyur pa'i sems kyis zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'i tshor ba kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang de myong bar byed pa'i 'du byed rnams dang sdug bsngal dang 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid kyi gnas ngan len dang ldan pa dang sdug bsngal de gnyis las rnam par ma grol bas res 'ga' ni bde ba'i gnas skabs la brten / / res 'ga' ni sdug bsngal gyi gnas skabs la brten te / / rtag tu khor mor sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'i gnas skabs su 'gyur ba ni ma yin no /
tasmādanityatānubandhārthenāyogakṣematvātsaṃskāraduḥkhatā veditavyā / skandhānām
# de lta bas na mi rtag pa rjes su bcings pas grub pa dang bde ba ma yin pa'i phyir 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid du rig par bya'o /
trayāṇāṃ dhātūnāṃ manodharmamanovijñānadhātūnām / dvayoścāyatanayormanodharmāyatanayoḥ
# phung po rnams dang khams gsum ni yid dang chos dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams rnams so / / skye mched gnyis ni yid dang chos kyi skye mched do /
ekadeśaṃ sthāpayitvānāsravalakṣaṇam tadanyāni sarvāṇīti
# phyogs gcig ma gtogs pa ni zag pa med pa'i mtshan nyid do / / thams cad do zhes bya ba ni de las gzhan pa dag go /
akuśalasya kuśalasāsravasya cāyatyā sasaṃprayogamālayavijñānaṃ vipākaḥ
# mi dge ba dang dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa'i rnam par smin pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa ni phyi ma la yod de /
atastena vipākena tadubhayaṃ savipākamityucyate / skandhānām / daśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ vijñānarūpaśabdadharma dhātūnām / caturṇā cāyatanānāṃ rūpaśabdamanodharmāyatanānām / ekadeśo 'vyākṛtānāsravavarjaḥ / ālayavijñānāttadanyattu cakṣurādikaṃ ca sukhaduḥkhādikaṃ ca tadvipākrajamityākhyāṃ labhate tato jātamiti kṛtvā / pariṇatitaḥ pāriṇāmikaḥ kavaḍīkāra āhāraḥ pariṇāmakāle indriyamahābhūtapoṣaṇāt / viṣayato vaiṣayikaḥ sparśāhāraḥ iṣṭaviṣayā dhiṣṭhānena sparśenāśrayānugrahaṇāt
# de'i phyir rnam par smin pa des na de gnyis rnam par smin pa dang bcas pa zhes bya'o / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las gzhan pa mig la sogs pa dang bde ba dang sdug bsngal la sogs pa ni rnam par smin pa de las byung ba zhes brjod pa 'thob ste / / de las skyes pa'i phyir ro / / phung po rnams dang khams bcu zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa bdun dang gzugs dang sgra dang chos kyi khams rnams so / / skye mched bzhi zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sgra dang yid dang chos kyi skye mched rnams so / / phyogs gcig go zhes bya ba ni lung du ma bstan pa dang zag pa med pa ma rtogs pa'o / / 'ju bas kyang 'ju ba las gyur pa zhes bya ba ni kham gyi zas 'ju ba'i dus na dbang po'i 'byung ba chen po brtas par byed pa'i phyir ro / / yul gyis kyang yul las gyur pa zhes bya ba ni reg pa'i zas te / / yid du 'ong ba'i yul gyi gnas kyis reg pas lus la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
āśāta āśikaḥ manaḥ saṃcetanāhāraḥ abhipretavastuprativaddhāśāvaśenāśrayānugrahaṇāt
# re bas kyang re ba las gyur pa zhes bya ba ni yid la sems pa'i zas te / / 'dod pa'i dngos po dang 'brel ba'i re ba'i dbang gis lus la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
upādānata aupādānikaḥ vijñānamāhāraḥ ālayavijñānopādānavaśenātmabhā vopasthānāt / tathāhi tadviyukta āśrayaḥ pūtībhavatīti
# len pas kyang len pa las gyur pa zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'i zas te / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa'i dbang gis lus gnas pa'i phyir te / / 'di ltar de dang bral na lus ru la bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
punaścatvāro 'pyāhārāḥ samasya caturbhiḥ prabhedairvyavasthāpyante
# yang zas rnam pa bzhi po dag ni bsdus nas rnam pa bzhis rnam par gzhag go / / 'di lta ste /
tadyathā aśuddhāśrayasthitikaḥ kāmāvacarāṇāṃ pṛthagjanānām sakalabandhanatvāt
# ma dag pa'i lus gnas par byed pa ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i so so'i skye bo rnams kyi ste / / mtha' dag ni 'ching ba dang ldan pa'i phyir ma dag pa'i gnas so /
śuddhāśuddhāśrayasthitikaḥ śaikṣāṇāṃ rūpārūpyāvacarāṇāṃ ca pṛthagjanānām sāvaśeṣavandhanatvāt
# dag pa dang ma dag pa'i lus gnas par byed pa ni slob pa rnams dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa'i so so'i skye bo rnams kyi ste / / 'ching ba'i lhag ma las pa'i phyir ro /
śuddhāśrayasthitiko 'rhatām sarvabandhanavinirmuktatvāt
# dag pa'i lus gnas par byed pa ni dgra bcom pa rnams kyi ste / / 'ching ba thams cad las rnam par grol ba'i phyir ro /
sthitisāṃdarśiko buddhānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ ca mahāprabhāvaprāptānām āhāravaśena sthitiriti saṃdarśanamātratvāt
# gnas par kun tu ston pa ni sangs rgyas rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' mthu chen po thob pa rnams kyi ste / / zas kyi dbang gis gnas par kun tu ston pa tsam gyi phyir ro /
asaṃskṛtaikadeśaḥ niṣpannasvabhāvaḥ sottaramiti nirvāṇaṃ muktvā tasya sarvadharmāgratvādiśuddhāyāśca tathatāyāstallakṣaṇatvāt
# 'dus ma byas kyi phyogs gcig gis kyang gong ma dang bcas pa zhes bya ba ni mya ngan las 'das pa ma gtogs pa ste / / de'i mtshan nyid ni rnam par dag pa'i de bzhin nyid yin pas de ni chos thams cad kyi mchog yin pa'i phyir ro /
samāsataḥ prabhedastrividhaḥ trividhaṃ svabhāvamadhikṛtya pudgalanairātmyanayena veditavyaḥ / tatra parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ skandhādīnyadhiṣṭhāyāvidyamāna ātmādisvabhāvo yaḥ parikalpitaḥ
# bsdus pa'i rab tu dbye ba ni rnam pa gsum ste / / gang zag la bdag med pa'i tshul gyis ngo bo nyid gsum gyi dbang du byas par rig par bya'o / / de la kun tu brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid ni phung po la sogs pa la brten nas med par yang bdag la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid du gang kun tu rtog pa'o /
paratantraḥ svabhāvastānyeva skandhādīni yatrāsāvātmadyabhūtavikalpaḥ pravṛttaḥ
# gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid ni phung po la sogs pa de dag ni gang du yang dag pa ma yin pa bdag la sogs pa'i rnam par rtog pa de 'byung ba'o /
pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvo bhāvābhāvaviyuktalakṣaṇā hi tathatā skandhādiṣvātmādyabhāvanairātmyāstitālakṣaṇatvāt
# yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid ni dngos po dang dngos po med pa dang mi ldan pa'i mtshan nyid de / / phung po la sogs pa la bdag la sogs pa med pa pa dang bdag med pa la sogs pa yod pa nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyi phyir ro /
lakṣaṇaprabhedo dharmāṇāṃ svabhāvamadhikṛtya rūpaṃ vedanetyevamādi
# mtshan nyid kyis rab tu dbye ba ni chos rnams kyi rang bzhin gyi dbang du byas te / / gzugs dang tshor ba la sogs pa'o /
prakāraprabhedo viśeṣamadhikṛtya dravyasantaḥ prajñaptisanta ityevamādi
# rnam pa'i rab tu dbye ba ni khyad par gyi dbang du byas nas rdzas su yod pa dang btags pa'i yod pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
āśrayaprabhedaḥ pratyātmabhāvaṃ skandhādīnāṃ nānātvamadhikṛtya / saṃtatiprabheda ekasminapyātmabhāve skandhādīnāṃ pratilakṣaṇamanyathātvamadhikṛtya
# lus kyi rab tu dbye ba ni so so'i lus te / / phung po la sogs pa tha dad pa'i dbang du byas pa'o / / rgyun gyis rab tu dbye ba ni lus gcig la yang phung po la sogs pa'i skad cig so so gzhan gyi dbang du byas pa'o /
bahirmukhaprabhedo yadbhūyasā kāmāvacara iti bhūyograhaṇaṃ niṣpandadharmahetukaśrutacintāmayavyudāsārtham
# phyi rol tu bltas pas rab tu dbye ba gang zhe na / / phal cher 'dod pa'i khams na spyod pa zhes bya ba ni rgyu mthun pa'i chos kyi rgyu las byung ba'i thos pa dang sems pa las byung ba ma rtogs pa ston pa'i phyir ro /
samāptaḥ prabhedaḥ / lakṣaṇasaṃgraheṇa rūpaskandho rūpaskandhenaiva saṃgṛhīto vistareṇa yāvaddharmāyatanaṃ dharmāyatanenaiva
# bam po bzhi pa / / mtshan nyid kyis bsdus pa ni gzugs kyi phung po nyid kyis gzugs kyi phung po bsdus pa nas / / rgya cher chos kyi skye mched kyis chos kyi skye mched bsdus pa'i bar du'o / / khams kyis bsdus pa gang zhe na /
dhātusaṃgraheṇa sarvāṇi skandhadhātvāyatanānyālayavijñānena saṃgṛhītāni sarveṣāṃ tatra bījato 'stitvāt
# phung po dang khams dang skye mched thams cad kun gzhi rnam par shes pas bsdus pa ste / / de la de dag thams cad kyi sa bon yod pa'i phyir ro /
jātisaṃgraheṇa skandhaiḥ rāśyādyarthayuktā rūpādayaḥ sarve saṃgṛhītā vilakṣaṇā apyanyonyaṃ svalakṣaṇenaikajātīyatvāt / evaṃ dhātubhiścāyatanaiścopabhogadhāraṇārthayuktā āyadvārārthayuktāścakṣurādayaḥ saṃgṛhītā veditavyāḥ
# rigs kyis bsdus pa ni phung po rnams kyis spungs pa la sogs pa'i don dang ldan pa gzugs la sogs pa'o / / rang gi mtshan nyid kyis phan tshun mtshan nyid mi 'dra yang rigs gcig pa'i phyir thams cad bsdus so / / de bzhin du khams rnams dang skye mched rnams kyis kyang nye bar spyod pa 'dzin pa'i don dang ldan pa dang skye ba'i sgo'i don dang ldan pa mig la sogs pa bsdus par rig par bya'o /
avasthāsaṃgraheṇa skandhā ekajātīyā api sukhādyavasthāṃ niyamayya sukhāvasthāḥ sukhāvasthaireva saṃgṛhītā na duḥkhādyavasthaiḥ / evaṃ duḥkhāvasthāduḥkhāsukhāvasthāśca tadavasthaireva saṃgṛhītāḥ
# gnas skabs kyis bsdus pa ni phung po rnams rigs gcig tu zin kyang bde ba la sogs pa'i gnas skabs nges par byas nas bde ba'i gnas skabs ni bde ba'i gnas skabs nyid kyis bsdus kyi / / sdug bsngal gyi gnas skabs kyis ni ma yin no / / de bzhin du sdug bsngal gyi gnas skabs kyang de nyid kyi gnas skabs kyis bsdus so /
yathā skandhā evaṃ dhātava āyatanāni ca
# phung po rnams ji lta bar khams rnams dang skye mched rnams kyang de bzhin no /
sahāyasaṃgraheṇa rūpaskandhaḥ saha tadāśritairvedanādibhiḥ sahāyairgṛhyamāṇaḥ pañcabhiḥ skandhaiḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ
# grogs kyis bsdus pa zhes bya ba la / / gzugs kyi phung po ni sdud pa na de la brten pa tshor ba la sogs pa grogs rnams dang lhan cig tu phung po lnga po dag gis bsdus so /
evaṃ vedanādayāpi pratyekaṃ saparivārā gṛhyamāṇāḥ pañcabhiḥ skandhaiḥ saṃgṛhītā bhavanti / tathā dhātava āyatanāni ca saparivārāṇi pratyekaṃ sarvardhātubhirāyataneśca saṃgṛhītāni veditavyāni
# de bzhin du tshor ba la sogs pa 'khor dang bcas pa rnams kyang sdud pa na so sor phung po lnga po dag gis bsdus par 'gyur ro / / de bzhin du khams rnams dang skye mched 'khor dang bcas pa rnams kyang so sor khams dang skye mched thams cad kyis bsdus par rig par bya'o /
ekadeśasaṃgraheṇa śīlaskandho rūpaskandhaikadeśena saṃgṛhītaḥ
# phyogs gcig gis bsdus pa zhes bya ba la / / tshul khrims kyi phung po ni gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig gis bsdus so /
samādhiprajñāskandhau saṃskāraskandhaikadeśena
# ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi phung po ni 'du byed kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig gis bsdus so /
kāmavyāpādahiṃsādhātavo dharmadhātvekadeśena saṃgṛhītāḥ
# 'dod pa dang gnod sems dang rnam par 'tshe ba'i khams ni chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig gis bsdus so /
ākāśānantyāyatanādīni manodharmāyatanaikadeśena saṃgṛhītāni
# nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la sogs pa ni yid dang chos kyi skye mched kyi phyogs gcig gis bsdus so /
evaṃ kṛtvā yāvanto dharmāḥ skandhadhātvāyatanaiḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ sūtrāntareṣu teṣāmanyatamasaṃgraha ekadeśasaṃgraho veditavyaḥ / sakalasaṃgraheṇa duḥkhaskandhaḥ pañcabhirupādānaskandhaiḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ kāmadhāturaṣṭādaśabhirdhātubhiḥ asaṃjñi sattvāyatanaṃ daśabhirāyatanaṃgandharasāyatanavarjaiḥ saṃgṛhītam / evaṃ kṛtvā yāvanto dharmāḥ skandhadhātvāyatanaṃḥ saṃgṛhītāḥ sūtrāntareṣu teṣāmaśeṣataḥ saṃgrahaḥ sakalasaṃgraho veditavyaḥ
# de ltar byas na mdo sde gzhan dag tu phung po dang khams dang skye mched kyis bsdus pa'i chos ji snyed pa de dag gang yang rung bas bsdus pa ni phyogs gcig gis bsdus par rig par bya'o / / mtha' dag gis bsdus pa zhes bya ba la / / sdug bsngal gyi phung po lnga po nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po dag gis bsdus so / / 'dod pa'i khams ni bco brgyad po dag gis bsdus so / / 'du shes med pa'i sems can gyi skye mched ni dri dang ro'i skye mched ma gtogs pa skye mched bcu po dag gis bsdus pa'o / / de ltar byas na mdo sde gzhan dag tu phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams kyis bsdus pa'i chos ji snyed pa de dag ni mtha' dag gis bsdus par rig par bya'o / / gcig gis gcig bsdus pa zhes bya ba la / / phung po rnams ni so sor khams dang skye mched rnams kyis bsdus te / / ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
itaretarasaṃgraheṇa skandhāḥ pratyekaṃ dhātubhirāyatanaiśca saṃgṛhītāḥ yathāyogamevaṃ dhātavaḥ skandhāyatanarāyatanāni skandhadhātubhiḥ saṃgṛhītāni iti vistareṇāvagantavyam / saṃgrahalakṣaṇaṃ punarlokaprasiddhasaṃgrahānusāreṇa ṣaḍidvadhaṃ draṣṭavyam
# de bzhin du khams rnams kyang phung po dang skye mched rnams kyis bsdus shing / / skye mched rnams kyang phung po dang khams kyis bsdus par rgya cher khong du chud par bya'o / / yang bsdus pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'jig rten gyi grags pas bsdus pa dang mthun par rnam pa drug tu blta ste /
tatpunaḥ katamat / padasthānasaṃgraho yathā jambūdvīpasaṃgṛhītā manuṣyāḥ araṇyasaṃgṛhītā mṛgā iti loke ucyate tathehāpi cakṣurādibhiḥ cakṣurvijñānādīnāṃ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ
# de yang gang zhen / / gzhi'i gnas kyis bsdus pa ni dper na mi 'dzam bu'i gling gis bsdus so / / ri dags rnams ni dgon pas bsdus so zhes 'jig rten na brjod pa de bzhin du 'dir yang mig la sogs pas mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa bsdus par rig par bya'o /
nibandhasaṃgraho yathā rajjvādinā kāṣṭhabhārādikasya tathā kāyena cakṣurādonāmindriyāṇām
# 'ching bas bsdus pa ni dper na thag pa la sogs pas shing khur ba la sogs pa bcings pa de bzhin du lus kyis mig la sogs pa'i dbang po rnams bcings so /
tulyārthasaṃgraho yathā samānasarvaprayojanānāṃ visrambhiṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ parasparaṃ tarthakālaṃbanapravṛttānāṃ saṃprayuktānāmānyonyam / upādānasaṃgraho yathā svāminā ātmīyataḥ parigrahītādīnā dāsādīnāṃ tathālayavijñānenātmabhāvasya
# don mthun pas bsdus pa ni dper na dgos pa thams cad mthun pa'i mi yid gcugs pa rnams phan tshun brten pa de bzhin du dmigs pa gcig la 'byung ba mtshungs par ldan pa rnams kyang gcig gis gcig bsdus so / / nye bar 'dzin pas bsdus pa ni / / dper na jo bos bran la sogs pa bdag gir yongs su bzung ba de bzhin du kun gzhi rnam par shes pas kyang lus bzung ngo /
avisārasaṃgraho yathā ghaṭenodakasya tathā samādhinā tadanyeṣāṃ cittacaitasikānām
# rnam par mi 'phro bas bsdus pa ni dper na bu ma pas chu bzung ba de bzhin du ting nge 'dzin gyis de las gzhan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams bzung ngo /
abhisaṃkṣepasaṃgraho yathā samudreṇa nadīnāṃ tathā rūpaskandhena cakṣurādonāmiti / tadatrābhisakṣapasaṃgrahamadhikṛtyakādaśavidhaḥ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ / paramāṇudeśe sarveṣāṃ deśināmityekaparamāṇuparyāpannānāṃ rūpādīnāmavinirbhāgaḥ samānadeśatvena veditavyaḥ
# mngon bar sdud pas bsdus pa ni / / dper na rgya mtshos 'bab chu rnams bsdus pa de bzhin du gzugs kyi phung pos mig la sogs pa bsdus so / / 'dir mngon par sdud pas bsdus pa'i dbang du byas nas bsdus pa rnam pa bcu gcig tu rig par bya'o / / rdul phra rab kyi phyogs la phyogs can thams cad ces bya ba ni rdul phra rab gcig tu gtogs pa'i gzugs la sogs pa ni phyogs mthun pas tha dad pa med par rig par bya'o /
paramāṇorūrdhva sarveṣāṃ deśināṃ miśrībhāvaḥ tadyathā kaluṣe pānīye appṛthivīparamāṇūnāṃ paramparam
# rdul phra rab las gong ma phyogs can rnams 'dres par gyur pa ni 'di lta ste / / chu rnyog ma can gyi nang na chu dang sa'i rdul phra rab rnams phan tshun du 'dres pa lta bu'o /
deśināmeva samudāyināmanyonyaṃ samavadhānaṃ tadyathā bhittau mṛtpiṇḍena mṛtpiṇḍāntarasya
# phyogs can 'dus pa rnams phan tshun du phrad pa ni 'di lta ste / / rtsig pa la 'jim gong dang 'jim gong gzhan phrad pa lta bu'o /
sahabhāvasaṃprayoga ekātmabhāve kṣaṇikānāṃ skandhādīnām
# lhan cig 'byung bas mtshungs par ldan pa ni lus gcig la phung po la sogs pa skad cig pa rnams so /
kṛtyānuṣṭhānasaṃprayoga ekasmin prayojane prayuktānāmanyonyam
# bya ba grub pas mtshungs par ldan pa ni dgos pa cig la zhugs pa rnams phan tshun du'o /
saṃpratipattisaṃprayogaḥ parabhāvena na svabhāvena tadyathā cittaṃ cittāntareṇa na saṃprayujyate vedanā vedanāntareṇetyavamādi
# mthun par rtogs pas mtshungs par ldan pa ni gzhan gyi dngos po dang yin gyi rang gi dngos po dang ni ma yin pa ste / / 'di ltar sems ni sems gzhan dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin zhing tshor ba yang tshor ba gzhan dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa la sogs pa'o /
na viruddhayostadyathā rāgadveṣayoḥ kuśalākuśalayorvetyevamādi
# mi mthun pa gnyis ma yin pa ni dper na 'dod chags dang zhe sdang gnyis dang dge ba dang mi dge ba gnyis la sogs pa'o /
na visadṛśakālayostadyathā vartamānānāgatayoratītavartamānayorvā
# dus mi 'dra ba gnyis ma yin pa ni 'di lta ste / / da ltar dang ma 'ongs pa gnyis dang 'das pa dang da ltar gnyis so /
na visabhāgadhātubhūmikayostadyathā kāmāvacararūpāvacarayoḥ prathamadvitīyadhyānabhūmikayorvetyevamādi
# mi mthun pa'i khams dang sa pa gnyis ma yin pa ni 'di lta ste / / 'dod pa dang gzugs na spyod pa gnyis dang bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis pa'i sa pa gnyis la sogs pa'o /
sarvatragaḥ saṃpratipattisaṃprayoga vedanādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ sarvāsvavasthāsveṣāṃ vinānyonyamabhāvāt
# mthun par gtogs pas mtshungs par ldan pa tshor ba la sogs pa drug pa 'di dag ni kun tu 'gro ba ste / / gnas skabs thams cad du 'di dag las gang yang rung ba gcig med na med pa'i phyir ro /
ucitastadekatyānāṃ ca śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāmityekāntalaukikānāṃ kuśalānāmakuśalāvyākṛtānāṃ ca yathāsaṃbhavam
# 'dres pa ni slob pa dang mi slob pa dag las kyang kha cig go zhes bya ba ni gcig tu 'jig rten pa'i dge ba rnams dang mi dge ba rnams dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams kyis te / / ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
ādyataduttarāṇāmityapūrvajātīyatvena prathamakṣaṇotpannānāṃ dvitīyādikṣaṇotpannānāṃ ca lokottarāṇāmanucitatvajñāpanārtham
# dang po de dang de'i 'og ma rnams zhes bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa skad cig dang po las byung ba rnams dang skad cig gnyis pa la sogs pa las byung ba rnams kyang sngon gyi rang bzhin ma yin pas ma 'dris pa nyid du bstan pa'i phyir ro / / ldan pa gang zhe na /
samanvāgamo lakṣaṇataḥ pūrvavattadyathā kuśalādīnāṃ dharmāṇāmācayāpacaye prāptiḥ pratilambhaḥ samanvāgama iti prajñaptiḥ
# mtshan nyid kyis ni snga ma bzhin no zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste / / dge ba la sogs pa'i chos rnams kyi 'phel ba dang 'grib pa la 'thob pa dang rnyed pa dang ldan pa gdags so zhes bya'o / / sa bon dang ldan pa gang zhe na /
bījasamanvāgama iti kāmadhātau jātau bhūtastraidhātukaiḥ kleśopakleśaiḥ samanvāgata ityavītarāgaṃ pṛthagjanamadhikṛtyaitadvaiditavyam / vītarāgastu tatrordhvaṃ vā jāto yato bhūmervītarāgastadbhūmikairasamanvāgataḥ samanvāgataśca pratipakṣeṇopahatatvādasamuddhātitatvāccānuśayato yathākramam
# 'dod pa'i khams su skyes par gyur ba ni khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang ldan te / / de ni so so'i skye bo 'dod chags dang ma bral ba'i dbang du byas par rig par bya'o / / 'dod chags dang bral ba ni de 'am / / gong mar skyes kyang rung ste / / sa gong gis 'dod chags dang bral bar sa de pa rnams dang de dag dang mi ldan pa dang ldan pa yang yin te / / gnyen pos gnod par byas pa dang bag la nyal legs par ma bcom pa'i phyir go rims bzhin no /
upapattiprātilambhikaṃśca kuśalariti yatra jātastadbhūmikaireva
# skye bas thob pa'i dge ba rnams zhes bya ba ni gong du skyes pa'i sa pa de'i sa pa rnams nyid dang ldan no /
traidhātukapratipakṣalābhīti lokottaramārgalābhī / yasya yasya prakārasya pratipakṣa utpanna iti bhāvanāprahātavyasyādhimātrādeḥ kleśasya
# khams gsum pa'i gnyen po thob pa zhes bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam thob pa'o / / rnam pa gang dang gang gi gnyen po byung ba zhes bya ba ni bsgoms pas spong bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa chen po la sogs pa'o /
tasya tasya bījasamanvāgamenāsamanvāgato 'nuśayataḥ samuddhātitatvāt
# de dang de'i sa bon dang mi ldan pas ldan pa ma yin zhes bya ba ni / / bag la nyal legs par bcom pa'i phyir ro /
vaśitāsamanvāgamaḥ prāyogikānāṃ kuśalānāmiti śrutamayādīnāṃ satyapi bīje tadabhyāsakṛtāṃ tajjanmikīṃ bījapuṣṭimantareṇa saṃmukhīkartumaśakyatvāt
# dbang dang ldan pa gang zhe na / / sbyor ba las byung ba dge ba'i chos 'jig rten pa rnams zhes bya ba ni thos pa las byung ba la sogs pa'i sa bon yod du zin kyang de goms par ma byas pas tshe de'i sa bon brtas pa med pas mngon du byed mi nus pa'i phyir ro /
tadekatyānāṃ cāvyākṛtānāṃ śaṃlpasthānikanairmāṇikacittaprabhṛtīnām
# de dag las kyang lung du ma bstan pa kha cig ces bya ba ni bzo'i gzas nas sprul pa'i sems la sogs pa'o /
mokṣahetuvaikalyādātyantika eṣāṃ hetvasamanvāgama iti
# thar pa'i rgyu dang mi ldan pa'i phyir / / de dag gtan du rgyu dang mi ldan te /
mokṣaprāptihetvasamanvāgama ityarthaḥ / kaḥ punarmokṣaprāptihetuḥ
# 'jig rten las 'das pa rnams dang thar pa thob pa'i rgyu dang mi ldan pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / thar pa thob pa'i rgyu gang yin zhe na /
yasyaivaṃ tathatāyāṃ kleśadauṣṭhulyaṃ saṃniviṣṭaṃ bhavati tatsati pratipakṣānukūlapratyayalābhe śakyate samuddhātayitum sa bhavyatā rthena heturityucyate
# de bzhin nyid la nyon mongs pa'i gnas ngan len gnas pa yin te / / rgyu gang gnyen po'i rjes su mthun pa'i rkyen rnyed na legs par 'joms nus pa de skal ba dang ldan pa'i phyir rgya zhes bya'o /
viparyayāddhetuvaikalyaṃ veditavyam
# bzlog pa ni rgyu dang mi ldan par rig par bya'o /
II satyaviniścayo nāma dvitīyaḥ samuccayaḥ / tatsattvajanmato janmādhiṣṭhānataśceti yaśca jāyate sattvalokaḥ yatra ca jāyate bhājanaloke tadubhayaṃ duḥkha mityuktaṃ bhavati
# de ni sems can gyi skye ba dang skye ba'i gnas kyis kyang zhes bya ba ni sems can gyi 'jig rten gang skye ba dang snod kyi 'jig rten gang du skye ba de gnyi ga sdug bsngal gyi bden pa zhes bstan pa yin no /
yaśca sattvaloko yaśca bhājanalokaḥ karmakleśajanitaḥ karmakleśādhipateya ityābhyāṃ tayoḥ sattvabhājanalokayorduḥkhatvakāraṇaṃ jñāpayati / api khalu jātirduḥkhamityevamādi pūrvaṃ samasya duḥkhasatyalakṣaṇaṃ vyutpādyādhunā duḥkhasatyamārabhya sūtroktasya nirdeśasyārtha vibhaktumārabhate / jātirduḥkhaṃ saṃvādaduḥkhatāṃ tadanyadukhasvāśrayatāṃ copādāyeti mātuḥ kukṣāvāmapakvāśayayorantarāle āsīnasya niṣkrāmato vā kukṣervividhāśucidravyāsaṃpīḍāṅgasaṃmardaduḥkhānubhavanārthena jātau satyāṃ jarādiduḥkhābhyanuṣaṅgārthena ca yathākramam
# sems can gyi 'jig rten gang yin pa dang snod kyi 'jig rten gang yin ba de las dang nyon mongs pas skyed pa dang las dang nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis byung ba zhes bya ba ni go rims bzhin te / / de gnyis kyis ni sdug bsngal nyid kyi rgyu ston to / / yang skye ba ni sdug bsngal lo zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni sngar mdor bsdus te sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i mtshan nyid bstan nas / / da ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa las brtsams te / / mdo sde las byung ba bstan pa'i don rnam par dbye bar brtsams te / / skye ba'i sdug bsngal ni dog pa'i sdug bsngal nyid dang de las gzhan pa'i sdug bsngal gyi gnas yin pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni ma'i mngal na zhu ba dang ma zhu ba gnyis kyi bar na 'dug pa las 'byung ba dang mngal na mi gtsang ba'i rdzas sna tshogs kyis gzir te / / lus kyi yan lag kun tu btsir ba la sogs pa'i sdug bsngal myong ba'i phyir ro / / btsas nas kyang rga ba la sogs pa'i sdug bsngal zhar la 'byung ba'i phyir te / / go rims bzhin no /
ṣaṭ samānānyaṣṭau bhavanti vipariṇatidukhaṃ tridhā kṛtvā
# brgyad yin yang drug tu 'gyur zhes bya ba ni gsum 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal du byas pa'i phyir ro /
jātyādibhirduḥkhaduḥkhatāparidīpanavacanaṃ duḥkhavedanīyadharmasvalakṣaṇārthena
# skye ba la sogs pas sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid yongs su bstan to zhes bya ba ni sdug bsngal myong bar 'gyur ba'i chos kyi rang gi mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
priyavināmāvādinā vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāparidīpanavacanaṃ prāptāprāptasukhavedanīyadharmavipariṇatisvalakṣaṇārthena
# sdug pa dang bral ba'i dngos po la sogs pas 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid yongs su bstan to zhes bya ba'i tshig ni phrad pa dang ma phrad pas bde pa myong bar 'gyur ba'i chos 'gyur ba'i rang gi mtshan nyid yin ba'i phyir ro /
pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkhamityanena saṃskāraduḥkhatāparidīpanavacanaṃ dvayāvinirmokṣānityetā nubandhayogakṣemārthena
# nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga sdug bsngal lo zhes bya ba 'dis ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyi yongs su bstan to zhes bya ba'i tshig 'di gnyis las rnam par ma grol zhing mi rtag pa nyid rjes su 'brel te grub pa dang bde ba ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
jātirdukhamityevamādi saṃvṛtisatyena dukham laukikajñānaviṣayatvāt / pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkhamiti paramārthasatyena dukham saṃniveśatathatāmukhena lokottarajñānaviṣayatvāt
# skye ba ni sdug bsngal lo zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni kun rdzob kyi bden par sdug bsngal ba ste / / 'jig rten pa'i shes pa'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro / / nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga sdug bsngal lo zhes bya ba ni gnas pa'i de bzhin nyid kyi sgo nas don dam pa'i bden par sdug bsngal ba ste / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes pa'i yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
duḥkhasāmānyalakṣaṇe yairākārairyogine duḥkhasatyaṃ vyavacārayanti tadyathānityato duḥkhataḥ śūnyato 'nātmataśca
# sdug bsngal gyi spyi'i mtshan nyid ni rnal 'byor bas rnam pa gang dag gis sdug bsngal gyi bden par spyad pa ste / / 'di lta ste mi rtag pa nyid dang sdug bsngal ba nyid dang stong pa nyid dang bdag med pa nyid kyis so /
tatra dvādaśavidhena lakṣaṇenānityaṃ duḥkhasatyaṃ veditavyam
# de la mtshan nyid rnam pa bcu gnyis kyis mi rtag pa sdug bsngal gyi bden par rig par bya ste /
tatpuna rasallakṣaṇaṃ yathā nāsti sarvadā duḥkhasatyamātmātmoyasvabhāvamiti yo 'rthaḥ so 'rtho 'nityaṃ duḥkhasatyamiti
# de yang med pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'di lta ste / / bdag dang bdag gi ba'i ngo bo nyid kyi sdug bsngal pa'i bden pa rtag tu med pa'i don gang yin pa'i don de ni mi rtag pa sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'o /
akārasya pratiṣedhārthatvāt nityaśabdasya ca sarvakālārthatvāditi
# mi zhes bya ba ni dgag pa'i don yin pa'i phyir ro / / rtag ces bya ba'i sgra ni dus thams cad pa'i don yin pa'i phyir ro /
vināśalakṣaṇaṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ bhūtvābhāvaḥ
# rnam par 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'du byed rnams byung nas med par 'gyur ba'o /
vipariṇatilakṣaṇaṃ prabandhāsādṛśyena pravṛttiḥ
# 'gyur ba'i mtshan nyid ni rgyu mi 'dra ba nyid du 'byung ba'o /
viyogalakṣaṇaṃ tadavastheṣveva vastuṣu svabhāvavaśitvabhraṃśaḥ kvacitparaiḥ svīkaraṇamapi veditavyam / saṃnihitalakṣaṇaṃ yattadānīmevānubhūyamānānityatā
# 'bral ba'i mtshan nyid ni dngos po'i gnas skabs de dag nyid la rang bzhin gyi dbang nyams pa dang kha cig tu ni gzhan dag gis bdag gir byas par yang rig par bya'o / / nye ba'i mtshan nyid kyi tshe na mi rtag pa nyid myong ba gang yin pa'o /
dharmatālakṣaṇaṃ yāmavaśyamanubhaviṣyati / kṣaṇalakṣaṇamātmalābhānantaramavaśyavināśitā
# chos kyi mtshan nyid ni gang gdon mi za bar myong bar 'gyur ba'o / / skad cig gi mtshan nyid ni bdag nyid rnyed nas de ma thag tu gdon mi za bar rnam par 'jig pa nyid do /
prabandhalakṣaṇamanādimati saṃsāre ājavaṃjavībhāvena vṛttiḥ / vyādhijarāmaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ dhātuvaiṣamyaṃ khalityādikaṃ sthitikālāvedhopayogaśca / cittacittākāravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ vipakṣapratipakṣāvasthānāvasthitatvam
# rgyun gyi mtshan nyid ni thog ma med pa can gyi 'khor ba nas 'ong ba dang 'gro bar 'gyur bas 'byung ba'o / / na ba dang rga ba dang 'chi ba'i mtshan nyid ni khams ma snyoms pa dang spyi cer du gyur pa dang gnas pa'i dus kyi 'phen pa zad pa'o / / sems sna tshogs kyi rnam par 'gyur ba'i mtshan nyid ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang gnyen po'i gnas la gnas pa'o /
bhogasaṃpattilakṣaṇaṃ sarvalaukikasamṛddho nāmanātyantikatayā durantatvam
# longs spyod 'byor pa rgud pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'jig rten pa'i 'byor ba thams cad gtan du 'dug pa ma yin pas mthar nyes pa nyid do /
bhājanasaṃvartavivartalakṣaṇaṃ mahāpṛthivyādināmagnyādibhiḥ punaḥ punarvināśata utpādataśca agnyambuvāyusaṃvartanībhirdahanakledanaśoṣaṇātmikābhiryathākramam / prathamadvitīyatṛtīyadhyānasthānāvasāne lokasaṃniveśe saṃvṛtte tadūrdhvaṃ yānyavaśiṣyante dvitīyatṛtīyacaturthadhyānasyānāntarāṇi tāni tāsāṃ śīrṣāṇi veditavyāni
# snod 'jig pa dang chags pa'i mtshan nyid ni sa chen po la sogs pa me la sogs pas yang dang yang 'jig pa dang 'byung ba ste / / me dang chu dang rlung 'tshig par byed pa dang rul bar byed pa dang skam par byed pa'i bdag nyid kyi 'jig pa rnams dang go rims bzhin du bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis pa dang gsum pa'i gnas kyi mthar thug par 'jig rten gnas pa 'jig go / / de'i gong ma lhag ma lus pa bsam gtan gnyis pa dang gsum pa dang bzhi pa'i gnas gzhan gang yin pa de dag ni de dag gis bsdus bar rig par bya'o /
caturthadhyānabhūmikānāṃ tarhi vimānānāṃ kena saṃvartavivartaḥ
# bsam gtan bzhi pa rnams kyi gzhal med khang rnams gang gis 'jig cing chags she na /
na kena cidbāhyena taireva tu sarvairjāyamānaiḥ saha tāni vimānāni nirvartante cyavamānaiḥ saha tāni nirudhyanta iti / sa eva teṣāṃ saṃvartavivarto veditavyaḥ
# phyi rol gang gis kyang ma yin gyi gzhal med khang de dag ni sems can de dag nyid skye ba dang lhan cig tu 'grub cing 'chi ba dang lhan cig tu 'gag ste / / de nyid de dag gi 'jig pa dang chags par rig par bya'o /
yaiḥ kalpasya niryāṇaṃ bhavatīti parisamāptirbhavatītyarthaḥ
# de dag gis bskal ba tshar phyin par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba ni yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
eko 'ntarakalpo 'pakarṣaḥ vivartakāle ekānnaviṃśatitamaḥ / aṣṭādaśa utkarṣāpakarṣāḥ
# chags pa'i dus na mar 'bri ba bar gyi bskal pa gcig dang yar 'phel ba dang mar 'bri ba bco brgyad de bcu dgu'o /
tata ūrdhvameka utkarṣaḥ paścimaḥ
# de'i 'og tu tha mar yar skye ba gcig go /
āyukṣayānmaraṇaṃ kālacyutimadhikṛtya yāvadākṣepamāyuṣaḥ parisamāptatvāt
# tshe zang ces bya ba ni 'chi ba ste / / tshe'i 'phen pa ji tsam yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir dus su 'chi ba'i dbang du byas pa'o /
puṇyakṣayādakālacyutimadhikṛtya samāpattyāsvādanatayā tadāyurākṣepakakarmabhāvanopadhātāt
# bsod nams zad ces bya ba ni dus ma yin par 'chi ba'i dbang du byas pa ste / / snyoms par 'jug pa'i ro myong bar byed pas de'i tshe 'phen par byed pa'i las bsgos pa las gnod pa'i phyir ro /
karmakṣayātprabandhacyutimadhikṛtya tasminnāyatane upapadyāparaparyāyavedanīyakarmaṇa upayuktatvādabhāvādvā tatra bhūyo 'nutpattito veditavyam
# las kyang zad nas zhes bya ba ni rgyun chad nas 'chi ba'i dbang du byas pa ste / / gnas der skyes nas myong bar 'gyur ba dang lan grangs gzhan la myong bar 'gyur ba'i las spyad zin pa'i phyir ram / / med pa'i phyir der yang mi skye bar rig par bya'o /
aṣṭākāraṃ vā duḥkhamiti saṃbādhaduḥkhatādi
# sdug bsngal rnam pa brgyad ces bya ba ni dog pa'i sdug bsngal nyid la sogs pa'o /
utpādāṃśikī anityatā abhūtvā bhāvaḥ sa ca duḥkhapakṣyāṇāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ bādhanātmakaḥ
# skye ba'i char gtogs pa'i mi rtag pa nyid ni ma byung ba las 'byung ba ste / / de ni sdug bsngal gyi phyogs kyi 'du byed rnams la gnod pa'i bdag nyid do /
iti tāmanityatāṃ pratītya duḥkhaduḥkhatā prajñāyate
# mi rtag pa nyid de la brten nas sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid rab tu shes so /
vyayāṃśikī bhūtvābhāvaḥ sa ca sukhapakṣyāṇāṃ saṃskārāṇāmanabhipretaḥ
# 'jig pa'i char gtogs pa na byung nas med par 'gyur ba ste / / de ni bde ba'i phyogs kyi 'du byed rnams kyi mi 'dod pa'o /
iti tāṃ pratītya vipariṇāmaduḥkhatā prajñāyate
# de la brten nas 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid rab tu shes so /
sadauṣṭhulyānāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ prabandhenodayo 'pyanabhipretaḥ vyayo 'pīti tadubhayāṃśikīmanityatāṃ pratītya saṃskāraduḥkhatā prajñāyate / saṃskārānityatāṃ saṃskāravipariṇāmatāṃ ca saṃdhāyoktam mayā yatkiṃcidveditamidamatra duḥkhasyetyayamaduḥkhāsukhasya sukhasya ca veditasya duḥkha vacane 'bhisaṃdhirveditavyaḥ / duḥkhasya tu veditasya duḥkhatvena prasiddhatvālloke na tatra punarabhisaṃdhirucyata iti
# gnas ngan len dang bcas pa'i 'du byed rnams kyi rgyun du 'byung ba dang 'jig pa yang 'dod pa ma yin te / / de gnyi ga'i char gtogs pa'i mi rtag pa nyid la brten nas 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid rab tu shes so / / ngas 'du byed mi rtag pa nyid dang 'du byed 'gyur ba nyid la dgongs nas gang ci tshor yang rung 'di ni 'dir sdug bsngal du gsungs so zhes bya ba ni 'dir sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang bde ba myong ba ni sdug bsngal nyid kyi tshig tu dgongs par rig par bya'o / / sdug bsngal myong ba ni sdug bsngal nyid du 'jig rten na grags pa'i phyir der yang dgongs pa brjod mi dgos so /
yeṣu cānityeṣu saṃskāreṣu jātyādikaṃ prajñāyate teṣām anityatvāt duḥkhamityabhisaṃdhirveditavyaḥ / anyathā mārgo 'pyanityatvādduḥkhaṃ syāditi
# 'du byed mi rtag pa gang dag la skye ba la sogs par snang ba de dag ni mi rtag pa nyid kyi phyir sdug bsngal du dgongs par rig par bya'o / / gzhan du na ni lam yang mi rtag pa'i phyir sdug bsngal du 'gyur ro /
śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ nityādilakṣaṇasyātmanaḥ saṃskārebhyo 'rthāntarabhūtasya teṣvabhāvaḥ
# stong ba'i mtshan nyid ni rtag pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi bdag 'du byed rnams las don gzhan du gyur ba ste / / de dag la med pa'o /
teṣāṃ ca saṃskārāṇāṃ nityakālaṃ tadrahitaprakṛtikalakṣaṇasya nairātmyasya bhāvastadubhayaṃ śūnyatetyucyate
# 'du byed de dag ni rtag tu de dang bral ba'i rang bzhin gyi mtshan nyid kyi bdag med pa'i ngo bo nyid yin te / / 'di gnyi ga yang stong pa nyid ces bya'o /
svabhāvaśūnyatā parikalpitaṃ svabhāvamupādāya tasya svalakṣaṇenaivābhāvāt
# ngo bo nyid kyis stong pa nyid ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid nye bar bzung ba ste / / rang gi mtshan nyid kho nas med pa'i phyir ro /
tathābhāvaśūnyatā paratantraṃ svabhāvamupādāya tasya yena yena prakāreṇa parikalpyate tena tena prakāreṇābhāvāt
# de bzhin du yod pa ma yin pa'i stong pa nyid ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid nye bar bzung ba ste / / de ni rnam pa gang dang gang kun tu brtag par bya ba'i rnam pa de dang de med pa'i phyir ro /
prakṛtiśūnyatā pariniṣpannaṃ svabhāvamupādāya tasya śūnyatāprakṛtikatvāt
# rang bzhin gyis stong pa nyid ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid nye bar bzung ba ste / / de ni stong pa nyid kyi rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro /
anātmalakṣaṇaṃ punasteṣāmeva saṃskārāṇāmātmavādibhiḥ parikalpitenātmalakṣaṇenānātmalakṣaṇatā
# bdag med pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'du byed de dag nyid bdag tu smra ba rnams kyis kun tu brtags pa'i bdag gi mtshan nyid ma yin pa nyid do /
vināśādilakṣaṇānityatā prasiddhā kṣaṇikalakṣaṇā tu na prasiddhā sarvasaṃskārāṇāmataḥ sā prasādhayitavyā
# 'du byed thams cad 'jig pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid mi rtag pa nyid du ni grags la / / skad cig pa'i mtshan nyid du ni ma grags te / / de'i phyir de bsgrub par bya'o /
tatra cittacaitasikānāṃ kṣaṇikatvaṃ loke prasiddhamataḥ tenāprasiddhaṃ rūpasya kṣaṇikatvaṃ prasādhyate
# de la sems dang sems las byung ba rnams la ni skad cig pa nyid du 'jig rten du grags te / / de'i phyir des ma grub pa'i gzugs kyi skad cig pa nyid bsgrub bo /
kathamiti
# ji ltar zhe na /
cittopāttatāmupādāya kṣaṇikena hi cittena kāya upātta
# sems kyis zin pa zhes bya ba ni sems skad cig pas lus zin pa'o / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
kenārthena / cittaikayogakṣematāmupādāya tathāhi kāyaḥ savijñānaka eva samudāgacchati vijñānāpakrāntyā ca pūtībhavati / tasmāccittenaikayogakṣematvāttadivāsya kṣaṇikatvaṃ veditavyam / kiṃ ca cittāśrayatāmupādāya cittasya hi vikāreṇa kāyasya vikāro dṛśyate sukhaduḥkharāgadveṣādyavasthāsu
# grub pa dang bde ba gcig pa'i phyir te / / 'di ltar rnam par shes pa dang bcas pa nyid kyi lus ni yang dag par 'grub kyi / / rnam par shes pa dang bral ba ni rul bar 'gyur ro / / de lta bas na sems dang grub pa dang bde ba gcig pa'i phyir de bzhin du 'di yang skad cig pa nyid du rig par bya'o / / sems gyur na de 'gyur ba'i phyir zhes bya ba ni bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang 'dod chags dang zhe sdang la sogs pa'i gnas skabs na sems 'gyur bas lus 'gyur bar snang ste /
ataḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ vikāriṇaścetaso 'nuvidhānāt kāyasya kṣaṇikatvaṃ siddham
# de'i phyir skad cig re re la 'gyur ba'i sems kyi rjes su 'gyur bas lus skad cig pa nyid du grub bo / / sems kyi gnas yin pa'i phyir zhes bya ba la /
cittādhipatyasaṃbhūtatāmupādāya cittasya hi sendriyaḥ kāya āśrayaḥ prasiddhaḥ yasya ca ya utpatyāśrayo nāsau svavināśamantareṇa tasyāśrayībhavandṛṣṭaḥ
# dbang po dang bcas pa'i lus ni sems kyi gnas su rab tu grub pa ste / / gang zhig gang gi skye ba'i gnas yin pa de bdag 'jig pa med par de'i gnas su 'gyur bar mi snang ste /
tadyathāgnyaṃkurādīnāmindhanabījādikaḥ
# dper na me dang myu gu la sogs pa'i shing dang sa bon la sogs pa bzhin no /
tasmātpratikṣaṇaṃ cittasyāśrayabhāvātpratikṣaṇameva vinaśyatīti siddham
# de bas na skad cig re re la sems kyi gnas su gyur pas skad cig re re kho na la rnam par 'jig pa grub bo /
cittasyādhipatyasaṃbhūtatāmupādāya sarvaṃ hyādhyātmikabāhyaṃ rūpaṃ cittasyādhipatyena saṃbhavati
# sems kyi dbang gis 'byung ba'i phyir zhes bya ba la nang dang phyi'i gzugs thams cad ni sems kyi dbang gis byung ba ste / / de bas na rgyu skad cig pa yin pa'i phyir / / 'bras bu yang skad cig pa nyid du rig par bya ste /
ataḥ kāraṇasya kṣaṇikatvātkāryasya kṣaṇikatvaṃ veditavyam ye hetavo ye pratyayāḥ rūpasyātpādāya te 'pyanityāḥ anityān khalu hetupratyayān pratītyotpannaṃ rūpaṃ kuto nityaṃ bhaviṣyatīti sūtrapadānusāreṇa
# gzugs 'byung ba'i rgyu gang dag yin pa dang rkyen gang dag yin pa de dag ni mi rtag pa yin na / / rgyu rkyen mi rtag pa la brten nas 'byung ba'i gzugs rtag par ga las 'gyur zhes mdo las byung ba'i tshig gi tshul du rig par bya'o /
cittavaśavarttitāṃ copādāya prabhāvaviśiṣṭasya ca cittasya rūpaṃ vaśe vartate tena yatheṣṭaṃ pariṇāmāt / ataḥ pratikṣaṇamanyathādhimokṣe satyanyathotpādātkṣaṇikatvasiddhiḥ
# sems dbang bsgyur ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni mthu khyad par du 'phags pa'i sems gzugs la dbang bsgyur ba ste / / de ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du bsgyur ba'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir skad cig re re la rnam pa gzhan du mos na rnam pa gzhan 'byung bas skad cig pa nyid du grub po /
api khalu ante vikāropalabdhitāmupādāya na hi pratikṣaṇaprakṛtivikāritāmantareṇākasmiko rūpasyānte vikāro yuktaḥ sa copalabhyate
# yang mthar 'gyur bar dmigs pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni / / skad cig re re la rang bzhin gyis 'gyur ba med par glo bur du gzugs kyi tha mar 'gyur ba'i mi rigs na zhes dpe gzhan las 'byung ngo /
tasmātsvāsāṃtānikapratikṣaṇavikārābhivṛddhihetukatvādantyasya rūpavikārasya kṣaṇikaṃ rūpamiti siddham
# mtha' mi 'gyur ba'i rigs na / / de yang dmigs pa de bas na mtha' ma'i gzugs kyi 'gyur ba'i rang gi rgyud kyi skad cig re re 'gyur ba 'phel ba'i rgyu las byung ba'i phyir gzugs skad cig par grub bo /
utpannasya cānapekṣya pratyayaṃ svarasavināśitāmupādāya sarvasyotpannasya vināśaḥ pratyayamanapekṣya svarasenaiva bhavati
# skyes nas kyang rkyen la mi ltos par rang gi ngang gis rnam par 'jig pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni skyes pa thams cad ni rkyen la mi ltos par rang gi ngang nyid kyis 'jig par 'gyur ro / / de'i phyir rkyen gzhan la mi ltos par gdon mi za bar 'jig ste /
ataḥ pratyayāntaranirapekṣo 'vaśyaṃbhāvī vināśa utpannamātrasyaiva bhāvasya na bhavati paścādbhatīti na kiṃcidviśeṣaṇamasti / tasmātsarveṇa vināśinotpannamātreṇa vinaṣṭamiti siddhaṃ kṣaṇikatvam
# dngos po skyes pa tsam nyid kyis 'jig pa ma yin la / / phyis 'jig go zhes bya bar ni bye brag cung zad kyang med do / / de lta bas na rnam par 'jig pa'i tshul can thams cad ni skyes pa tsam gyis 'jig par 'gyur bas skad cig pa nyid du grub bo /
ekapradeśāśrayibhāvārtha upādāyārthaḥ bhūtadeśanirapekṣasya pṛthak svatantravṛttitāsāmārthyābhāvāt
# phyogs gcig la brten pa'i dngos po'i don ni rgyur byas pa'i don to zhes bya ba ni 'byung ba'i phyogs la mi ltos par 'byung bar gyur pa logs shig tu rang dbang du 'byung ba'i mthu med pa'i phyir ro /
asti samudāya ekabhautikastadyathā śuṣko mṛtpiṇḍaḥ / asti dvibhūtikaḥ sa evārdraḥ
# 'byung ba gcig las gyur ba'i 'dus pa yang yod de / / 'di lta ste sa rdog skam po lta bu'o / / 'byung ba gnyis las gyur pa yang yod de / / de nyid gsher ba'o /
asti tribhūtikaḥ sa evoṣṇaḥ
# 'byung ba gsum las gyur pa yang yod de de nyid dro ba'o /
asti sarvabhūtikaḥ sa evārdra uṣṇaśca mṛtpiṇḍo gamanāvasthāyāmiti
# 'byung ba thams cad las gyur pa yang yod de / / sa rdog de nyid gsher ba dang dro ba dang 'dril zhing 'gro ba'i tshe'o /
asti samudāya ekopādāyarūpikastadyathā prabhā
# 'dus pa rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gcig pa yang yod de / / 'di lta ste 'od lta bu'o /
dvyupādāyarūpikastadyathā śabdagandho vāyuḥ / tryupādāyarūpikastadyathā dhūmaḥ tasya rūpagandhaspraṣṭavyaviśeṣaprabhāvitatvāt / spraṣṭavyaviśeṣaḥ punaratra laghutvaṃ veditavyam / caturupādāyarūpikastadyathā guḍapiṇḍaḥ / pañcopādāyarūpikastadyathā sa eva saśabdaḥ / ityanyatrāpi yadyatropalabhyate bhūtaṃ bhautikaṃ vā tatra tadastīti veditavyaṃ nānyatra / niḥśarīraḥ paramāṇuriti niḥsvabhāvo vyavasthānamātramityarthaḥ apakarṣamaryādābhāvāt
# rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gnyis dang ldan pa yang yod de 'di lta ste sgra dang dri dang bcas pa'i rlung lta bu'o / / rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gsum dang ldan pa yang yod de / / 'di lta ste / / du ba lta bu'o / / de ni gzugs dang dri dang reg bya'i bye brag gis rab tu phye ba'i phyir te / / reg bya'i bye brag ni 'dir yang pa nyid du rig par bya'o / / yang rgyur byas pa'i gzugs gsum dang ldan pa yang yod de / / dri rnam pa med pa'i nor bu'i snod kyi nang na yod pa'i chu la gzugs dang ro dang reg bya yod pa'o / / rgyur byas pa'i gzugs bzhi dang ldan pa yang yod de / / 'di lta ste / / bu ram gyi ling lta bu'o / / rgyur byas pa'i gzugs lnga dang ldan pa yang yod de / / 'di lta ste / / de nyid sgra dang bcas pa'o / / de ltar gzhan la yang 'byung ba'am 'byung ba las gyur ba gang na gang dmigs pa de na yod par rig par bya ste / / gzhan du na ni ma yin no / / rdul phra rab lus med pa zhes bya ba ni rang gi ngo bo nyid med pa ste / / rnam par gzhag pa tsam du zad do zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
buddhyā paryantabhedatastu paramāṇuvyavasthānaṃ buddhyā yāvānavayapāpakarṣaparyantaḥ śakyate prabhettuṃ tāvatā paramāṇuvyavasthānaṃ kriyate
# bshig na mu thug pa med pa'i phyir ro / / blos mthar rab tu phye nas rdul phra rab tu rnam par gzhag ces bya ba ni blos ji tsam du cha shas kyis bshig pa'i mthar rab tu dbye bar nus pa de tsam du rdul phra rab tu rnam par 'jog par byed pa'o /
kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ yadevaṃ niḥśarīro 'pi paramāṇurvyavasthāpyate
# ci'i phyir de ltar lus med kyang rdul phra rab tu rnam par 'jog ce na / / ril po'i 'du shes rnam par bshig pa'i phyir te /
piṇḍasaṃjñāvibhāvanatāmupādāya avayavaśo hi buddhyā bhidyamāne rūpe sarvametadekaṃ rūpamiti piṇḍasaṃjñā vigacchati yataḥ pudgalanairātmyapraveśasyānukūlyaṃ bhavatīti / rūpadravyāpariniṣpattipraveśatāṃ copādāya evaṃ hi buddhyā bhidyamānaṃ rūpaṃ na kiṃcidbhavatīti matvā rūpadravyasyāpariniṣpattiṃ praviśati yato vijñaptimātrāvatāreṇa dharmanairātmyapraveśasyānukūlyaṃ bhavatīti / vipuladuḥkhamasaṃlikhitaṃ kāmāvacaramanupacitakuśalamūlānām sarvaduḥkhatāgatiyoniprabhāvitatvāt kāmadhātoranupacittakuśalamūlatvenānāvṛtaṃ sarvagatigamanatvācca yathākramaṃ tadvipulamasaṃlikhitaṃ ca veditavyam saṃlikhitaṃ tadevotpannamokṣabhāgīyānām avaśyaṃ parinirvāṇaniyamāt
# gzugs la blos cha shas kyis bshig na 'di thams cad ni gzugs gcig go zhes ril por 'du shes pa dang bral bar 'gyur te / / 'di ltar gang zag la bdag med par 'jug pa'i rjes su mthun par 'gyur ro / / gzugs la rdzas su yongs su grub pa med par 'jug par bya ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni / / de ltar blos rab tu phye na gzugs ci yang med par rtogs nas gzugs la rdzas su yongs su grub pa med par 'jug ste / / 'di ltar rnam par rig pa tsam du 'jug pas chos la bdag med pa la 'jug pa'i rjes su mthun par 'gyur ro / / blo'i dbye ba dang rdzas kyi dbye bas rdul phra rab rnam par gzhag par shes par bya ste / / tshig gnyis dang go rims bzhin no / / sdug bsngal shin tu rgyas la ma bsrabs pa ni 'dod pa'i khams na spyod pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bsags pa rnams kyi ste / / 'dod pa'i khams ni sdug bsngal nyid thams cad dang 'gro ba dang skye gnas kyis rab tu phye ba dang dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bsags pas na / / thogs pa med par 'gro ba thams cad du 'gro ba'i phyir te / / go rims bzhin du de ni shin tu rgyas la ma bsrabs par rig par bya'o / / bsrabs pa ni de nyid thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa skye pa rnams kyi ste / / gdon mi za bar yongs su mya ngan las 'das par nges par bya ba'i phyir ro /
saṃlikhitāsaṃlikhitaṃ tadeva kāmāvacaraṃ duḥkhaṃ laukikavairāgyāvaropitakuśalamūlānām duḥkhaduḥkhatādisamatikramaniyamitatvādanātyantikatvācca yathākramam
# bsrabs pa'ang ma yin la ma bsrabs pa'ang ma yin pa ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i sdug bsngal de nyid 'jig rten pas 'dod chags dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa rnams kyi ste / / sdug bsngal gyi sdug bsngal nyid la sogs pa las yang dag par shin tu 'da' bar nges par byas pa dang gtan du ma yin pa'i phyir te / / go rims bzhin no /
evaṃ madhyāsaṃlikhitādīni yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyāni
# bar ma bsrabs pa la sogs pa yang de bzhin du ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o /
mahāsaṃlekhapratyupasthānamanekasattvasaṃtānikaduḥkhāpanayanapratyupasthānāt
# bsrabs pa chen pos nye bar gnas pa zhes bya ba ni sems can du ma'i rgyud la yod pa'i sdug bsngal bsal bar nye bar gnas pa'i phyir ro /
kuśalādicittasya maraṇamityātmasnehasaṃprayuktāccyuticittāpavargāvasthāmadhikṛtya veditavyam
# dge ba la sogs pa'i sems yod pa la 'chi ba zhes bya ba ni bdag la chags pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i 'chi 'pho ba'i sems kyi snga rol gyi gnas skabs kyi dbang du byas par rig par bya'o /
manomaya upapādukatvena cittamātrahetukatvāt / gandharvo gandhenārvaṇāt gandhānusāreṇo papattideśagamanādityarthaḥ
# yid las byung ba zhes bya ba ni rdzus te skye ba nyid de / / sems tsam gyi rgyu las byung ba'i phyir ro / / dri za zhes bya ba ni dris 'gro ba'i phyir te / / dri dang mthun par skye ba'i yul du 'gro ba'i phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
paraṃ saptāhaṃ tiṣṭhatyantareṇa ca cyavate yadyupapattipratyayān labhate
# de ltar thogs na zhag bdun gnas te / / de tshun chad kyis 'chi 'pho'o zhes bya ba ni gal te skye ba'i rkyen rnyed na'o /
atha na labhate saptāhātpareṇa cyutvā punarantarābhava eva nivartate
# ci ste ma rnyed na zhag bdun gyi 'og tu shi 'phos nas yang bar do'i srid pa nyid 'grub bo /
evaṃ yāvat saptakṛtvaḥ tataḥ pareṇa ekadā ca vyāvartate yadi tadavasthā syādyatropapattipratyaya / balavanta āmukhībhūtā bhavanti caturthadhyānalābhino 'rhattvābhimānino bhikṣostadbhūmikāntarābhavābhinirvṛttau mokṣāpavādi kamithyādṛṣṭipratilambhānnārakāntarābhavābhinirvṛttivat
# de ltar lan bdun gyi bar du byas nas ci ste na ldog go zhes bya ba ni gal te gnas skabs de na gzhan du skye ba'i rkyen stobs dang ldan pa zhig mngon du gyur na ste / / bsam gtan bzhi pa thob pa'i dge slong dgra bcom pa'o snyam pa'i mngon pa'i nga rgyal can sa de pa'i bar mdo'i srid pa mngon par grub pa na thar pa la skur ba 'debs pa log par lta ba rnyed nas sems can dmyal ba'i bar mdo'i srid pa mngon par 'grub pa bzhin no /
tatrasthaśca karmopacinoti pūrvāvedhavaśena kuśalādicetanāsamudācārāt
# de na gnas pa yang las bsogs so zhes pa ni sngon gyi 'phen pa'i dbang gis dge ba la sogs pa'i sems kun tu 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
sabhāgāṃśca sattvānpaśyati yaiḥ saha pūrva tatkuśalamakuśalaṃ vā caritaṃ bhavati taiḥ saha vartamānamātmānaṃ svapna iva saṃjānīte / yatra cāsāvupapanno tatpūrvakālabhavākṛtirnirvartate
# skal ba mnyam pa'i sems can rnams kyang mthong zhes bya ba ni gang dag dang lhan cig tu sngon dge ba'am / / mi dge ba kun tu spyod par gyur pa de dag dang bdag lhan cig tu 'dug par rmi lam tsam gyi tshod du shes so / / gang du skye bar 'gyur ba de'i sngon logs kyi srid pa'i byad gzugs grub bo /
tata ūrdhvamindriyābhinirvṛttiryathā pratītyasamutpāda iti nāmarūpādyānupūrvyā / yathoktam
# de'i 'og tu dbang po rnams mngon par 'grub ste / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba las ji skad du 'byung ba de bzhin zhes bya ba ni ming dang gzugs la sogs pa'i rim pas so / / ji skad du /
kalalaṃ prathamaṃ bhavati kalalājjāyate 'rbudam
# thog ma nyid du nur nur 'gyur / / nur nur po las mer mer 'gyur /
arbudājjāyate peśī peśīto jāyate dhanam
# mer mer po las nar nar 'gyur / / nar nar po las gor gor 'gyur /
ghanātpraśākhā jāyante keśalomanakhādayaḥ
# gor gor po las rkang lag 'gyus / / skra spu sen mo la sogs 'byung /
indriyāṇi ca rūpīṇi vyañjanādyanupūrvaśaḥ / samudayasatyaṃ yato duḥkhaṃ samudeti
# dbang po gzugs can rnams dang ni / / mtshan rnams mthar gyis 'byung bar 'gyur / / zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / kun 'byung gi bden pa ni gang las sdug bsngal kun 'byung ba ste /
tatpunaḥ katamat
# de yang gang zhe na /
kleśāḥ kleśādhipateyaṃ ca karma iti sāsravamityarthaḥ / yadyevaṃ kimartha bhagavatā tṛṣṇaiva samudayanirdeśe nirdiṣṭā
# nyon mongs pa dang nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis 'byung ba'i las te / / zag pa dang bcas pa'i zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / gal te de lta ma yin na kun 'byung ba zhes bstan pa la ci'i phyir bcom ldan 'das kyis sred pa nyid bstan ce na /
sarvatragatvena prādhānyāt
# thams cad du 'gro bas gtso bor gyur ba'i phyir te /
tṛṣṇā vastusarvatragā prāptāprāptasarvātmabhāvaviṣayavastuvyāpanāt
# ji ltar sred pa dngos po thams cad du 'gro ba ni thob pa dang ma thob pa'i yul dang yul gyi dngos po thams cad la khyab pa'i phyir ro /
prāpte ātmabhāve tṛṣṇā aprāpte paunarbhavikī
# de la lus thob pa ni sred pa'o / / ma thob pa ni yang 'byung ba'o /
prāpteṣu viṣayeṣu nandīrāgasahagatā
# thob pa'i yul rnams ni dga' ba'i 'dod chags dang ldan pa'o /
aprāpteṣu viṣayeṣu tatratatrābhinandinī veditavyā
# ma thob pa'i yul rnams ni / / de dang de la mngon par dga' bar rig par bya'o /
avasthāsarvatragā duḥkhaduḥkhatāditryavastheṣu saṃskāreṣvanugatatvāt
# gnas skabs thams cad du 'gro ba ni / / 'du byed rnams kyi sdug bsngal la sogs pa gnas skabs gsum po dag dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
tatra duḥkhaduḥkhatāvastheṣu prāpteṣu viyogatṛṣṇā aprāpteṣvasaṃyogatṛṣṇā
# de la sdug bsngal nyid yi gnas skabs thob pa la ni 'bral bar srid do / / ma thob pa la ni mi phrad par srid do /
vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāvastheṣu aviyogatṛṣṇā saṃyogatṛṣṇā ca prāptāprāptabhedāt / saṃskāraduḥkhatāvastheṣu saṃmohatṛṣṇā kleśadauṣṭhulyaprabhāvitatvādaduḥkhāsukhavedanāprabhāvitatvācca
# 'gyur ba'i sdig bsngal nyid kyi gnas skabs la ni thob pa dang ma thob pa'i bye brag gis mi 'bral ba'i srid pa dang phrad pa'i sred pa'o / / 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyi gnas skabs la ni gti mug gi sred pa ste / / nyon mongs pa'i gnas ngan len gyis rab tu phye ba dang / / sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa bde ba yang ma yin pa'i tshor bas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
