ālayavijñānaṃ viśeṣeṇa saṃskāraduḥkhatāvasthaṃ tatra cātmasaṃmohasukhena tṛṣṇā pravṛttā veditavyā / adhvasarvatragā triṣvapyadhvasvanugatatvāt
# bye brag tu ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyi gnas skabs te / / de la bdag tu rmongs pa'i sgo nas srid pa 'byung bar rig par bya'o / / dus thams cad du 'gro ba ni dus gsum po dag ni rjes su 'gro ba'i phyir ro / / 'das pa'i dus la ni bltas pa'i rnam pas rjes su 'gro'o /
atīte tāvadadhvanyapekṣākāreṇānugatā anāgate abhinandanākāreṇa pratyutpanne adhyavasānākāreṇa
# ma 'ongs pa la ni mngon par dga' ba'i rnam pas rjes su 'gro'o / / da ltar byung ba la ni lhag par chags pas rjes su 'gro'o /
dhātusarvatrikā traidhātukaspharaṇātkāmarūpārūpyatṛṣṇābhiḥ
# khams thams cad du 'gro ba ni 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa dag gi sred pa dag gis khams gsum khyab pa'i phyir ro /
eṣaṇāsarvatrikā tayā kāmabhavamithyābrahmacaryaiṣaṇāt / kāmaiṣaṇayā kāmadhātoraparimucyamānastatraiva duḥkhaṃ nirvartayati
# tshor ba thams cad du 'gro ba ni des 'dod pa dang sred pa dang log pas tshangs par spyod pa tshol ba'i phyir ro / / 'dod pa'i tshol bas ni 'dod pa'i khams las yongs su ma grol ba de nyid du sdug bsngal 'grub par byed do /
tathā bhavaiṣaṇayā rūpārūpyadhātvoḥ dukhaṃ nirvartayati / mithyābrahmacaryaiṣaṇayā saṃsārādaparimucyamānastatra saṃsaratīti / prakārasarvatrikā śāśvatocchedaprakārānugatatvādbhavavibhava tṛṣṇābhyām
# de bzhin du srid pa tshol bas ni gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams su sdug bsngal 'grub par byed do / / log pas tshangs par spyod pa tshol bas ni 'khor ba las yongs su ma grol bar der 'khor ro / / rnam pa thams cad du 'gro ba ni 'byung ba dang 'jig pa'i sred pas rtag pa dang chad pa'i rnam pa dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
dṛṣṭeḥ prañcākāro bhedaḥ satkāyadṛṣṭirantagrāhadṛṣṭimithyādṛṣṭiḥ dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśa iti
# lta ba rnam pa lnga'i bye brag ni 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang log par lta ba dang lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
apraśāntalakṣaṇatā kleśānāṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ veditavyam
# rab tu ma zhi ba'i mtshan nyid ni nyon mongs pa rnams kyi spyi'i mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o /
sā punaḥ ṣaḍākārā tadyathā vikṣepāpraśāntatā viparyāsāpraśāntatā auddhatyāpraśāntatā styānamiddhāpraśāntatā pramādāpraśāntatālajjāpraśāntatā ca
# de la rnam pa drug ste / / 'di ltar g yeng bas rab tu ma zhi ba dang phyin ci log gis rab tu ma zhi ba dang rgod pas rab tu ma zhi ba dang rmugs pas rab tu ma zhi ba dang bag med pas rab tu ma zhi ba dang 'dzem pa med pas rab tu ma zhi ba'o /
kleśānuśayaścāprahīṇo bhavatīti tatpakṣasya dauṣṭhulyasyāsamudghāti tatvāt
# nyon mongs pa'i bag la nyal ma spangs par gyur pa zhes bya ba ni de'i phyogs dang mthun pa'i gnas ngan len legs par ma bcom pa'i phyir ro /
kleśasthānīyaśca dharma ābhāsagato bhavati raṃjanīyādiḥ
# nyon mongs pa'i gnas kyi chos snang bar gyur pa zhes bya ba ni chags par 'gyur ba la sogs pa'o /
tatra cāyo niśomanaskāraḥ pratyavasthito bhavatīti tasminviṣaye śubhanimittādyudgrāhako rāgādyutpattyanukūlaḥ / avidyā dṛṣṭivicikitsā ūrdhvabhūmyālaṃbanā api santi na punarāsāṃ sā bhūmiḥ sākṣādālaṃbanaṃ veditavyaṃ yathā svabhūmiḥ tatparikalpamukhapravṛttatvāt tu tadālaṃbanavyavasthānaṃ veditavyam / tatrāvidyā ūrdhvabhūmyālaṃbanā yā dṛṣṭisaṃprayuktā
# de la yang tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa nye bar gnas pa yin zhes bya ba ni yul de la sdug pa'i mtshan ma la sogs pa 'dzin pa ste / / 'dod chags la sogs pa 'byung ba dang mthun pa'o / / ma rig pa dang lta ba dang the tshom sa gong ma pa la dmigs pa yang yod mod kyi / / de dag ni ji ltar rang gi sa pa la dmigs pa bzhin dus de mngon sum du dmigs pa ni ma yin par rig par bya ste / / de la kun tu brtags pa'i sgo nas zhugs pa'i phyir / / de la dmigs par rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / de la ma rig pas gong ma pa la dmigs pa ni gang lta ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa'o /
dṛṣṭiḥ satkāyadṛṣṭi sthāpayitvā na hi parabhūmikān saṃskārānahamityabhiniviśamāno dṛṣṭa iti
# lta ba ni 'jig tshogs la lta ba ma gtogs te / / gzhan gyi sa pa'i 'du byed la nga'o snyam du mngon par zhen pa ni ma mthong ngo /
ūrdhvabhūmikasya tu kleśasyādhobhūmirālaṃbanaṃ na bhavati tato vītarāgatvāt
# sa gong ma'i nyon mongs pa ni sa 'og ma dmigs pa ma yin no zhes bya ba ni de las 'dod chags dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
nirodhamārgālaṃbanasya tau nālaṃbanam lokottareṇa jñānena tatpṛṣṭhalabdhena vā pratyātmavedanīyatvāt
# 'gog pa dang lam la dmigs pa ni de gnyis la dmigs pa ma yin te / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes dang de'i rjes la thob pa so so rang rang gis rig par bya ba yin pa'i phyir ro /
tat parikalpitaṃ tvasyālaṃbanamiti vaktavye tatparikalpastvasyālaṃbanamiti vacanam tadavyatirekātparikalpitasya
# de'i dmigs pa ni des yongs su rtogs pa'o zhes bya ba ni de'i dmigs pa ni des yongs su brtags pa'o zhes brjod par bya ste / / de'i dmigs pa ni des yongs su rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i tshig de las yongs su brtags pa gud na med do /
rāgaḥ pratidhena na saṃprayujyate ekāntaviruddhayorekatra vṛttyayogāt
# 'dod chags ni khong khro dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no zhes bya ba ni shin tu mi mthun pa gnyis gcig tu 'byung ba mi rigs pa'i phyir ro /
vicikitsayāpi na saṃprayujyate na hi vicikitsāvyavasthitabuddhiradhyavasyatīti
# the tshom dang yang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa ni / / the tshom du gyur na blo gnas pa med pas chags par 'gyur ba med pa'i phyir ro /
śiṣṭaistvasya mānādibhiraviruddhatvātsaṃprayogo veditavyaḥ
# lhag ma ni de dang zhes bya ba ni nga rgyal la sogs pa dang mi mthun pa med pa'i phyir mtshungs par ldan par rig par bya'o /
pratigho mānena dṛṣṭyā ca na saṃprayujyate na hi yo yatra vastuni pratihatastena sa unnatiṃ gacchati tadvā saṃtīrayituṃ śaknotīti evamanyadapi yojayitavyam
# khong khro ba yang nga rgyal dang lta ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin no zhes bya ba ni su zhig dngos po gang la zhe 'gras par gyur pa des de khengs par mi 'gyur ro / / der yang rtog par mi nus so /
krodhādaya anyonyaṃ na saṃprayujyanta iti viruddhā viruddhairna saṃprayujyante
# de bzhin du gzhan la yang sbyar bar bya'o / / khong khro ba la sogs pa phan tshun mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa zhes bya ba ni mi mthun pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin te /
tadyathā rāgāṃśikāḥ pratighāṃsikaiḥ / aviruddhāstu kleśavadeva saṃprayujyanta iti veditavyam
# dper na 'dod chags kyi char gtogs pa rnams zhe sdang gi char gtogs pa dag dang ma yin pa bzhin no / / mi mthun pa med pa dag ni nyon mongs pa bzhin du mtshungs par ldan par rig par bya'o /
āhrīkyānapatrāpyaṃ sarvatrākuśale saṃprayujyate svaparanirapekṣatāmantareṇākuśalasatsamudācārā saṃbhavāt
# ngo tsha med pa dang khrel med pa ni mi dge ba thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan no zhes bya ba ni bdag dang gzhan la mi lta ba med par kun tu 'byung ba med pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ styānādayaḥ sarvatra kliṣṭe yojayitavyāḥ akarmaṇyādikamantareṇa kliṣṭatvā saṃbhavāditi
# de bzhin du rmugs pa la sogs pa yang nyon mongs pa can thams cad dang sbyar bar bya ste / / las su mi rung ba nyid la sogs pa med par nyon mongs pa can mi srid pa'i phyir ro /
yadyena prakāreṇa yasmin vastuni saṃprayojayati tannirdeśena saṃyojananirdeśo veditavyaḥ
# gang zhig rnam pa gang gi dngos po gang la kun tu sbyor ba de bstan pas kun tu sbyor ba bstan par rig par bya'o /
kiṃ saṃyojayati
# kun tu sbyor ba ci zhe na /
anunayasaṃyojanaṃ tāvattraidhātukarāgasvabhāvaṃ saṃyojayati / kena prakāreṇa saṃyojayati
# rjes su chags pa'i kun tu sbyor ba ni khams gsum pa'i 'dod chags kyi ngo bo nyid de kun tu sbyor bar byed do / / rnam pa gang gis kun tu sbyor zhe na /
tadvataḥ traidhātukānudvege satyakuśalasamudācarataḥ kuśalāsamudācarataśca
# de dang ldan pa khams gsum pa la yid mi 'byung ba ni mi dge ba kun tu spyod cing dge ba mi spyod pas so /
kasmin saṃyojayati / āyatyāṃ duḥkhābhinirvṛttau
# gang kun tu sbyor zhe na / / phyi ma la sdug bsngal mngon par 'grub par ro /
evaṃ pratighasaṃyojanādiṣu yojayitavyaḥ
# de bzhin du khong khro'i kun tu sbyor ba la yang sbyar bar bya'o /
avidyāsaṃyojanena saṃprayukto duḥkhadharmān samudayadharmānnādhyavasyati phalahetubhūtānsāsravānsaṃskārāstadādīnavāparijñānāt / dṛṣṭisaṃyojanena saṃprayukto mithyāni saraṇaṃ paryeṣata ityaha mokṣo mama mokṣo muktaśca nityo bhaviṣyāsyucchetsyāmi veti na ca bauddhānāmasti mokṣa iti
# mi rig pa'i kun tu spyod pa dang ldan pa ni sdug bsngal gyi chos rnams dang kun 'byung ba'i chos rnams la lhag par chags te 'bras bu dang rgyur gyur pa zag pa dang bcas pa'i 'du byed rnams dang de'i nyes dmigs yongs su mi shes pa'i phyir ro / / lta ba'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni log pas nges par 'byung ba kun tu tshol te bdag grol bar 'gyur ro / / bdag grol lo / / grol nas kyang rtag par 'gyur ro snyam pa dang chad par 'gyur te / / sangs rgyas pa la thar pa med do snyam pa'o /
parāmarśasaṃyojanena saṃprayukto mithyāniḥsaraṇopāyaṃ kalpayatyabhiniviśate āryāṣṭāṅgaṃ mārgaṃ hitvā satkāyadṛṣṭayā tatpūrvakeṇa ca śīlavratena śuddhipratyayanāt
# mchog tu 'dzin pa'i kun tu sbyor ba dang ldan pa ni log pas nges par 'byung ba'i thabs la rtog ste / / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa por nas 'jig tshogs la lta ba la sogs pa dang de sngon du 'gro ba'i tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs kyis lhag par yid ches pa'i phyir ro /
rāgādibandhanaivipariṇāmaduḥkhatādibandhanavacanaṃ sukhādivedanānuśayitatvāt / bāhyena hi bandhanena baddho dvayaṃ na labhate gantuṃ ca na labhate āsīno 'pi yatheṣṭamabhipretaceṣṭāyāṃ kāmakāraṃ na labhate / tatsādharmyeṇādhyātmikaṃ rāgādibandhanaṃ veditavyam
# 'dod chags la sogs pa'i 'ching bas 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal nyid la sogs pa la 'ching bar bstan pa ni 'dod chags la sogs pa ni bde ba la sogs pa'i tshor ba la phra rgyas su 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / phyi rol gyi 'ching bas bcings pa ni gnyis mi 'thob ste / / 'gro ba mi thob pa dang 'dug kyang ji ltar 'dod pa dang bsam pa dang spyod pa dang 'dod pa bzhin du byed pa mi thob pa'o / / nang gi 'dod chags la sogs pa'i 'ching ba yang de dang 'dra bar rig par bya'o /
kāmaiṣaṇāyā aviratasya kāmarāgapratighānuśayāvanuśayā te tanmukhena tayoḥ puṣṭigamanāt / mithyā mokṣaṃ mokṣopāyaṃ ca santīrayantīti yathākramaṃ tisṛbhirdṛṣṭibhirdvābhyāṃ ca parāmarśābhyāṃ yathā saṃyojaneṣūktamiti
# 'dod pa 'tshol ba ma spangs pa'i 'dod pa la 'dod chags dang khong khro ba'i bag la nyal phra rgyas su 'gyur te / / de'i sgo nas de gnyis rgyas par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / log par thar pa dang thar pa'i thabs la rtog par byed do zhes bya ba ni kun tu sbyor ba'i nang du lta ba gsum dang mchog tu 'dzin pa gnyis ji skad du bshad pa dang go rims bzhin no /
ṣaḍ rāgādīn kleśān sthāpayitvā tadanyaḥ kliṣṭaścaitasikaḥ saṃskāraskandhaḥ krodhādiko veditavyaḥ
# gang 'dod chags la sogs pa nyon mongs pa rnams ma gtogs par de las gzhan pa sems las byung ba'i 'du byed kyi phung po nyon mongs pa can no zhes bya ba ni khro ba la sogs par rig par bya'o /
kuśalapakṣāntarāyāya yogināṃ punaḥpunarudvegena cittaṃ paryavanahyantīti paryavasthānāni / kuśalapakṣaḥ punaryathākālaṃ śamathapragrahopekṣānimittabhāvanā tatsaṃniśrayaśca brahmacaryādiśuddhisaṃgṛhītaṃ śīlam
# rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi dge ba'i phyogs kyi bar chad bya ba'i phyir yang dang yang shas cher sems la kun nas 'khril bar byed pas kun nas dkris pa dag go / / dge ba'i phyogs ni zhi gnas dang rab tu 'dzin pa dang btang snyoms kyi rgyu mtshan bsgom pa ste / / dus ji lta ba bzhin no / / de dag gi gzhi ni tshangs par spyod pa la sogs pa dag pas bsdus pa'i tshul khrims so /
tatra śamathakāle styānamiddhamantarāyaṃ karoti ādhyātmaṃ saṃkṣepāvāhanāt
# de la zhi gnas kyi dus ni rmugs pa dang gnyid par chad byed de / / nang du zhum par byed pa'i phyir ro /
pragrahakāle auddhatyakaukṛtyam bahirdhā vikṣepāvāhanāt / upekṣākāle īrṣyāmātsaryam tadvataḥ parātmasaṃpattyamarśagrahamukhena muhurmuhuścittakaṃpanāt / śīlaviśuddhikāle āhvīkyānapatrāpyam tadubhayavataḥ sarvathāpattisthāneṣvalajjanāditi / saṃkleśavyavadānaguṇavaiguṇyārthena yathākramamoghayogavyavasthānaṃ veditavyam / āśritāśrayasaṃbandhayogeneti dṛṣṭayaugha āśritaḥ avidyaugha āśrayaḥ saṃmohe sati mokṣatadupāyaviparītaṃ saṃtīraṇāt
# rab tu 'dzin pa'i dus na ni rgod pa dang 'gyod pa ste / / phyi rol du rnam par g yeng bar byed pa'i phyir ro / / btang snyoms kyi dus na ni / / phrag dog dang ser sna ste / / de dang ldan na gzhan dang bdag gi phun sum tshogs pa la mi bzod pa dang kun tu 'dzin pa'i sgo nas yang dang yang sems g yo ba'i phyir ro / / tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i dus na ni / / ngo tsha med pa dang khrel med pa ste / / de gnyi ga dang ldan na rnam pa thams cad du ltung ba'i gnas kyis mi 'dzem pa'i phyir ro / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i rjes su mthun pa dang mi mthun pa'i phyir chu bo dang sbyor ba go rims bzhin du rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / gnas pa dang gnas 'brel ba'i tshul gyis so zhes bya ba la / / lta ba'i chu bo ni gnas pa'o / / ma rig pa'i chu bo ni gnas te / / rmongs par gyur na thar pa dang de'i thabs la log par rtog pa'i phyir ro /
dṛṣṭiśīlavratopādānābhyāṃ tīrthyā anyonyaṃ vivadanti tatrānekamatyāt
# lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs kyi nye bar len pa gnyis kyis mu stegs can rnams nang rtsod de / / de la blo du mar gyur pa'i phyir ro /
ātmavādopādānena tvanyonyaṃ na vivadanti ātmano 'stitvaṃ prati sarveṣāṃ matasāmyāt
# bdag tu smra ba'i nye bar len pas ni nang mi rtsod de; thams cad kyang bdag yod pa nyid du blo mthun pa'i phyir ro /
ātmavādopādānena tīrthyāihadhārmikaiḥ sārddhaṃ vivadanti eṣāṃ nairātmyavāditvāt / abhidhyādayaḥ kāyagranthā iti na rūpakāyasyaite granthā veditavyāḥ kiṃtarhi samāhitacittasvabhāvasya kāyasya parigranthārthena granthāḥ
# chos 'di pa rnams dang ni rtsod de / / bdag med par smra ba'i phyir ro / / brnab sems la sogs pa lus kyi mdud pa zhes bya ba ni de dag gzugs kyi lus kyi mdud pa ma yin par rig par bya ste / / mnyam par gzhag pa'i sems kyi rang bzhin gyi lus kyi bar du bcod pas mdud pa dag go /
pṛthagdṛṣṭisaṃniśrayeṇedameva satyaṃ moghamanyadityabhiniviśya jñeyaṃ saṃtīrayatāmayoniśo jñeyasaṃtīraṇahetoḥ cittaṃ vikṣipyate
# so so'i lta ba la brten nas 'di nyid bden gyi gzhan ni don med pa'o zhes mngon par zhen nas shes bya la kun tu rtog pas tshul bzhin ma yin par shes bya la log par rtog pa'i rgyus sems rnam par g yeng bar byed do /
kuto vikṣipyate / samāhitacittasya yathābhūtajñānadarśanataḥ
# gang las rnam par g yeng bar byed ce na / / mnyam par gzhag pa'i sems yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes pa mthong ba la sogs /
kuśalapakṣasyāsaṃprakhyānāya cittaṃ nivṛṇvantīti nivaraṇāni kuśalapravṛtterantarāyaṃ kurvantītyarthaḥ / kāmacchandaṃ pravrajyābhiraterantarāyaṃ karoti viṣayopabhogābhilāṣamukhena tatra tatrābhiramaṇāt
# dge ba'i phyogs mi rtogs par 'gyur bar sems la sgrib par byed pas sgrib pa rnams te / / dge ba la 'jug pa'i bar chad byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de la 'dod pa la 'dun pa ni rab tu 'byung ba la mngon par dga' ba'i bar chad byed de / / yul la nye bar spyod par 'dod pa'i sgo nas / / de la mngon par mi dga' ba'i phyir ro /
vyāpādaścodanāyāṃ samyakpratipatteḥ sabrahmacāribhiḥ śikṣāsthāneṣu codyamānasya vyāpannacittatayāsamyakśaikṣaṇāt
# gnod sems ni bskul ba'i dus na ste / / tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa rnams kyis yang dag par bsgrub pa'i bslab pa'i gnas la bskul nas gnod sems kyi sems kyis yang dag par mi slob pa'i phyir ro /
styānamiddhamoddhatyakaukṛtyaṃ ca śamathapragrahayoḥ pūrvavatsaṃkṣepavikṣepāvāhanādibhiḥ
# rmugs pa dang gnyid dang rgod pa dang 'gyod pa ni zhi gnas dang rab tu 'dzin pa gnyis snga ma bzhin du zhum pa dang rnam par g yeng bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
vicikitsā upekṣāyām niścaya mantareṇābhyupekṣitumaśakyatvāt
# the tshom ni btang snyoms kyi dus na ste / / gtan la phebs pa med par btang snyoms su byed mi nus pa'i phyir ro /
pratipakṣalāṃgarlaidurbhedārthena khilavyavasthānaṃ veditavyam janmāntarābhyāsena khilībhūtatvāt / dauḥśīlyāśucisaṃbhāvanānimittatvānmalāḥ / punaḥ punaḥ saṃsāre jātijarāmaraṇayogena nidhnantīti nighāḥ
# gnyen po thong gshol gyis rlog par dka' ba'i phyir tha bar rnam par gzhag par rig par bya ste / / tshe rabs gzhan na goms par byas pas spyod pas tha bar gyur pa'i phyir ro / / 'chal pa'i tshul khrims mi gtsang bar yid ches pa'i rgyu yin pas dri ma rnams so / / yang dang yang 'khor bar skye ba dang 'chi ba'i tshul gyis gnod par byed pas sdig pa rnams so /
bhavabhogeṣu ratneṣu ca tṛṣṇāvicikatsāmukhenānupraviśya todanācchalyāḥ
# srid pa dang srid pa'i yo byad rnams dang dkon mchog rnams la sred pa dang the tshom gyi sgo nas zhugs pas gnod pa'i phyir zug rdu rnams so /
bahūpakaraṇaparigraheṇa sakiṃcanaṃ kṛtvā bhayādibhiryojanāt kiṃcanāḥ
# yo byad mang po yongs su 'dzin pas lci yang dang bcas par byas nas 'jig pa la sogs pa dang sbyor ba'i phyir lci yang rnams so /
prāṇātipātādyakuśalacaryāvāhanādduścaritāni
# srog gcod pa la sogs pa'i mi dge ba spyod pa 'dres pas nyes par spyod pa rnams so /
lobhadveṣamohānāmevākuśalamūlatvena vyavasthānam ebhirmukhaiḥ sattvānāṃ duścaritacaraṇāt
# chags pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug nyid mi dge ba'i rtsa bar rnam par gzhag ste / / de dag gi sgo nas sems can rnams nyes par spyad pa spyod pa'i phyir ro /
tatrāmiṣakiṃcitkahetoḥ bhogārthino lobhena duścaritaṃ caranti
# de la zang zing cung zad tsam gyi rgyus sems can longs spyod don du gnyer ba rnams chags pas nyes par spyad pa spyod do /
apakāranimittaparikalpahetoḥ parāparādhāmarṣiṇo dveṣeṇa mithyādharmābhiniveśahetoḥ viparītadarśino mohena duścaritaṃ caranti yājñikādaya iti
# gnod par byas pa'i rgyu la yongs su rtog pa'i rgyus gzhan gyi nyes pa mi bzod pa rnams zhe sdang gis nyes par spyad pa spyod do / / chos log pa la mngon par zhen pa'i rgyus phyin ci log tu lta ba la mchod sbyin la sogs pa dag gti mug gis nyes par spyad pa spyod do /
cittavisāraṃ srutaṃ kurvantītyāsravāḥ / kāyikacaitasikavighātakaratvādvighātāḥ
# sems rnam par 'phro bar zag par byed pa'i phyir zag pa rnams so / / lus dang sems la phongs par byed pas phongs pa rnams so /
ayoniśonimittamanuvyañjanaṃ ca grāhayitvā kāyaṃ cittaṃ ca paridahantīti paridāhāḥ
# tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i mtshan ma dang mngon rtags 'dzin du bcug nas lus dang sems la yongs su gdung bar byed pas yongs su gdung ba rnams so /
rūpādike vastuni ratyadhyavasānaṃ kārayitvā tadvipariṇāme śokādibhiḥ sattvānāyāsantītyu pāyāsāḥ
# gzugs la sogs pa'i dngos po la dga' ba'am lhag par chags par byed du bcug nas de rnam par gyur na mya ngan la sogs pas sems can rnams nyon mongs par byed pa'i phyir 'khrug ba rnams so /
raṇayanti śastrādānādibhiriti raṇāḥ
# mtshon cha len pa la sogs pas 'thab par byed pas 'thab pa rnams so /
adharmarāgādimahāparidāhakaratvāt jvarā iva jvarā veditavyāḥ
# chos ma yin pa la 'dod chags la sogs pa ni yongs su gdung ba chen po byed pas rims nad dang 'dra bas na rims nad rnams su rig par bya'o /
tatrādharmarāgaḥ yo 'kuśaleṣu karmapatheṇānurāgaḥ
# de la chos ma yin pa la 'dod chags ni gang mi dge ba'i las kyi lam rnams la rjes su chags pa'o /
viṣamalobho 'nyāyenādharmeṇa viṣayaparyaṣṭiḥ
# mi mthun pas chags pa ni mi rigs pa'i chos ma yin pas yul kun tu 'tshol ba'o /
mithyādharmo durākhyāto dharmavinayo veditavyaḥ
# chos log pa ni nyes par bshad pa'i chos 'dul bar rig par bya'o /
jātimūlaka saṃskārataruvanaṃ saṃjānayantīti vanasāḥ
# skye ba'i rtsa ba 'du byed kyi shing gi nags tshal la chags par byed pas nags sbyor rnams so /
kāyasāpekṣāditayā kuśalaprayogavibandhanādvibandhāḥ
# lus la lta ba la sogs pa dang bcas pas dge ba la sbyor ba'i gegs byed pas gegs rnams so /
kāyasāpekṣatādīni punaḥ pañca cetovinibandhānadhikṛtya / rāgo viṣaye dṛṣṭau ca vipratipanna iti bhāvanāprahātavyo darśanaprahātavyaśca yathākramam
# lus la lta ba la sogs pa dang bcas pa ni sems kyi gegs lnga'i dbang du byas pa'o / / 'dod chags ni yul dang lta ba la sogs par rtog pa'o zhes bya ba ni bsgoms pas spang bar bya ba dang mthong bas spang bar bya ba dang go rims bzhin te /
śubhatāmātrālaṃbanatvādrāgasya yo 'pi sattveṣu rāgaḥ so 'pi viṣayamukhenaiva vipratipanno veditavyaḥ
# 'dod chags ni sdug pa tsam du dmigs pa'i phyir ro / / gang yang sems can la 'dod chags pa de ni yul gyi sgo nyid nas log par rtog par rig par bya'o /
evaṃ pratikūlamātrālaṃbanatvāt pratighasya sattveṣvapi pravartamāno viṣayamukhenaiva vipratipanno veditavyaḥ
# de bzhin du khong khro ba ni mi mthun pa'i rgyu tsam du dmigs pa'i phyir ro / / sems can rnams la 'byung ba ni yul gyi sgo nyid nas log par rtog par rig par bya'o /
mānaḥ sattveṣu dṛṣṭau ca vipratipannaḥ hīnādasmi śreyānityevamādyākārapravṛttatvātsatveṣu vipratipanno veditavyaḥ
# nga rgyal ni sems can rnams dang lta ba log par rtog pa'o zhes bya ba ni chung du bas bdag che'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir sems can rnams la log par rtog par rig par bya'o /
satkāyāntagrāhamithyādṛṣṭayo jñeye vipratipannāḥ samāropāpavādamukhena yathāyogam
# 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang log par lta ba ni shes bya la log par rtog pa'o zhes bya ba ni sgro 'dogs pa dang skur ba'i sgo nas ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
śīlavrataparāmarśādiḥ dṛṣṭau vipratipannaḥ dṛṣṭidoṣeṇaiva śīlavratasya śuddhitaḥ parāmarśanāt
# tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa ni lta ba la log par rtog pa'o zhes bya ba ni lta ba'i nyes pa nyid kyis tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs la lhag par mchog tu 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
vicikitsā pratipakṣe vipratipannā satyeṣu buddhirdvaghāpādanāt / te duḥkhasamudayayordaśāpi kleśā nidānaṃ bhavanti
# the tshom ni gnyen po la log par rtog pa'o zhes bya ba ni bden pa rnams la blo rnam pa gnyis su 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / nyon mongs pa bcu char yang sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i rgyu yin la /
tau ca teṣāṃ padasthānam
# de gnyis kyang de dag gi gzhi'i gnas yin no /
ataste tannidānapadasthānato vipratipannā ityucyante
# de'i phyir de'i rgyu dang gzhi'i gnas kyis log par rtog pa rnams zhes bya'o /
nirodhe mārge cottrāsasaṃjananato vipratipannāḥ kleśavaśātsaṃsāre 'bhiratasya vyavadānataḥ prapātasaṃjñātrāsāt / viparītakalpanataśca nirodhe mārge ca vipratipannā draṣṭavyāḥ tīrthyairanyathā parikalpya tatra vipratipatteḥ
# 'gog pa dang lam la yang skrag pa skyes pas log par zhugs pa'o zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis 'khor ba la mngon bar dga' ba dang rnam par byang ba la g yeng bar 'du shes nas skrag pa dang phyin ci log tu rtog pas 'gog pa dang lam la log par rtog par blta bar bya'o / / mu stegs can rnams kyis ni rnam pa gzhan du kun du brtags nas de la log par rtog pa'i phyir ro /
kāmāvacaro rāgaḥ pañcavijñānakāyikaḥ sukhena saṃprayujyate
# 'dod pa na spyod pa'i 'dod chags rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga dang ldan pa ni bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan no /
manovijñānakāyikaḥ saumanasyena / sarva upekṣayāprabandhoparatikāle / duḥkhadaurmanasyābhyāṃ tu na saṃprayujyate harṣākārapravṛttatvāt
# yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i tshogs dang ldan pa ni yid bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan no / / 'dod chags thams cad ni rgyun chad pa'i dus na btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan no / / sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba gnyis dang mi mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin te / / dga' ba'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
pratigho duḥkhena saṃprayujyate pañcavijñānakāyikaḥ ṣaṣṭho daurmanasyena sarva upekṣayā pūrvavat sukhasaumanasyābhyāṃ na saṃprayujyate dainyākārapravṛttatvāt / mānaḥ kāmadhatau sukhena na saṃprayujyate pañcavijñānakāyikābhāvāt
# rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga dang ldan pa'i khong khro ba ni sdug bsngal dang mtshungs par ldan no / / drug pa yid kyi sa pa ni yid bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan no / / thams cad ni btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan te snga ma bzhin no / / bde ba dang yid bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ni ma yin te / / dman pa'i rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / nga rgyal ni 'dod pa'i khams na bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin te / / rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga dang mtshungs par ldan pa med pa'i phyir ro /
prathamadvitīyayostarhi dhyānayoḥ kathaṃ sukhena saṃprayujyate
# bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis par bde ba dang ji ltar ldan zhe na /
manobhūmikena sukhena / kathaṃ tatra manobhūmikaṃ sukham
# yid kyi sa pa'i bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan no / / de ni yid kyi sa pa'i bde ba ji lta bu zhe na /
yattaducyate prītisukhamiti yathoktam "prītiḥ katamā
# dga' ba dang bde ba zhes gang 'byung ba ste / / ji skad du dga' ba gang zhe na /
yā parivṛttāśrayasya parivṛttivijñānāśritā cittatuṣṭiḥ cittaudvilyaṃ cittaharṣaḥ cittakalpatā sātaṃ veditaṃ vedanāgatam
# gang gnas gyur pa'i 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa la brten pa'i sems tshim pa dang sems shin tu dga' ba dang sems rangs pa dang sems dga' ba dang bde ba myong ba ste /
sukhaṃ katamat
# tshor bar gtogs pa'o /
yatparivṛttāśrayasyālayavijñānāśrita āśrayānugrahata āśrayahlādaḥ sātaṃ veditaṃ vedanāgatamiti
# bde ba gang zhe na gang gnas gyur pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la brten pa'i gnas la phan pa dang gnas kyi tshim pa dang bde ba myong ba ste / / tshor bar gtogs pa'o zhes bshad pa lta bu'o /
" tadetaduktaṃ bhavati / sukhā vedanā prathamadvitīyayordhyānayorutpadyamānā yena cittacaitakalāpena saṃprayujyate taṃ ca harṣākāreṇa prīṇayati āśrayaṃ cālayavijñānasvabhāvaṃ prasrabdhisukhena hlādayati
# de ni 'di skad du bstan to / / 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa la brten pa zhes bya ba ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa la brten pa yin te / / gzhan la mnyam par gzhag pa med pa'i phyir ro / / bde ba'i tshor ba bsam gtan dang po dang gnyis pa la 'byung ba na / / sems dang sems las byung ba'i tshogs gang yang mtshungs par ldan pa de dga' ba'i rnam pas tshim par byed pa dang gnas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i ngo bo nyid shin tu sbyongs pa'i bde bas tshim par byed pa ste /
atastadubhayakṛtyakaratvādubhayathaivāsyā vyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ prītiḥ sukhaṃ ceti
# de lta bas na de gnyis ka'i bya ba byed pa'i phyir 'di ni dga' ba dang bde ba zhes bya ba rnam pa gnyi gar rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
tasmāttayā saṃprayujyamāno mānaḥ sukhena saumanasyena ca saṃprayujyata ityucyate
# de bas na de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i nga rgyal ni bde ba dang yid bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa zhes bya'o /
mithyādṛṣṭiḥ kāmadhātau daurmanasyena saumanasyena ca saṃprayujyate sukṛtaduṣkṛtakāriṇāṃ tadvaiphalyadarśanenādhṛtiharṣotpādāt
# log par lta ba ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa zhes bya ste / / legs par bya ba dang nyes par bya ba byed pa rnams kyi de'i 'bras bu med par mthong nas mi mos pa dang dga' ba skye ba'i phyir ro /
sukhaduḥkhābhyāṃ na saṃprayujyate manobhūmikatvāt sarvasyā dṛṣṭeḥ
# bde ba dang sdug bsngal ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ni ma yin te / / lta ba thams cad ni yid kyi sa pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
vicikitsā kāmadhātau saumanasyena na saṃprayujyate aniścitacittasya nairvṛttyamantareṇa saumanasyābhāvāt
# the tshom ni 'dod pa'i khams na yid bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin te / / sems gtan la phab pa med pa ni mos pa med pas yid bde ba med pa'i phyir ro /
rūpadhātau vicikitsottaradhyāyināmapi prītisukhaṃ samādhivalādhānenānuvartata eveti tatra sukhasaumanasyābhyāmapi saṃprayujyate
# gzugs kyi khams na ni the tshom gyi shas che ba'i bsam gtan pa rnams kyi dga' ba dang bde ba ni ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs bskyed pa'i rjes su 'gro ba nyid de / / de na bde ba dang yid bde ba dang yang mtshungs par ldan no /
āveṇikāyā apyavidyāyā eṣa eva nayo draṣṭavyaḥ sukhasaumanasyābhyāṃ saṃprayogāsaṃprayogamārabhya
# ma rig pa ma 'dres pa yang bde ba dang yid bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa las brtsams te tshul 'di 'dra bar blta bar bya'o /
sarvakleśā upekṣayā saṃprayujyante audāsīnyamāgamyāstagamanatāmupādāyeti kleśapravandhasya mandataratamatāgamanenoparatavegasyoparamaṇādante 'vaśyamaudāsīnyamukhenopekṣāyāḥ saṃprayogo veditavyaḥ
# ci'i phyir nyon mongs pa thams cad btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan zhe na / / tha mal par 'dug pa la brten nas nub par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa'i rgyun je chung je chung du 'gro bas rgyun chad pa'i shugs kyis rgyun chad pa'i phyir tha mar gdon mi za bar tha mal par 'jug pa'i sgo nas btang snyoms dang mtshungs par ldan par rig par bya'o /
rūpadhātau caturvijñānakāyikastatra ghrāṇajihvāvijñānābhāvāt
# gzugs kyi khams na ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs bzhi dang mtshungs par ldan te / / de na sna dang lce'i rnam par shes pa med pa'i phyir ro /
mānādayo manovijñānakāyikā eva paritulanatāmukhapravṛttitvāt
# nga rgyal la sogs pa ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i tshogs dang ldan pa nyid de / / yongs su 'jal ba'i sgo nas 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
mānasyaikadeśapravṛttitvaṃ kenacidevāṃśenonnatigamanāt / kāmadhatau daśa dukhadarśanaprahātavyā iti ye tatra tannidānapadasthānato vipratipannāḥ
# nga rgyal ni phyogs gcig la 'jug pa nyid de / / gang yang rung ba'i yan lag gis khengs par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / 'dod pa'i khams na sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba dag ni bcu'o zhes bya ba ni de na gang dag de'i rgyu dang gzhi'i gnas kyis kyang log par rtog pa dag go /
evaṃ samudayādiṣu yathāyogaṃ vipratipannāstaddarśanaprahātavyā iti veditavyāḥ
# de bzhin du kun 'byung ba la sogs pa yang ji ltar mthun mthun du log par rtog pa dag ste / / de ni mthong bas spang bar bya bar rig par bya'o /
kiṃ khalu ye yadālaṃbanāste tatra vipratipannā iti veditavyāḥ
# ci'i phyir gang dag gang gi tshe dmigs pa de dag de la ci log par rtog par rig par bya zhe na /
nāvaśyam anāsravālaṃbanānāṃ sāsrave vastunyanuśayāditi
# zag pa med pa'i dmigs pa dag ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i dngos po nyid gdon mi za bar phra rgyas su byed pa ma yin no /
rūpadhātau pratidhābhāvānnava eva duḥkhādidarśanaprahātavyā veditavyāḥ
# gzugs kyi khams na ni khong khro ba med pas sdug bsngal la sogs pa mthong bas spang bar bya ba dag ni dgu'o /
evamārūpyadhātau / sahajā satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ kā bhāvanāprahātavyā
# gzugs med pa'i khams na'ang de bzhin no / / 'jig tshogs la lta ba lhan cig skyes pa ni bsgoms pas spang bar bya ba ste /
yāmadhiṣṭhāyotpannadarśanamārgasyāpyāryaśrāvakasyāsmimānaḥ samudācarati
# mthong ba'i lam skyes su zin yang gang la brten nas 'phags pa nyan thos la nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal kun tu 'byung ba'o /
yathoktam "nāhamāyuṣmandāsakemān pañcopādānaskandhānātmata ātmīyato vā samanupaśyāmyapi tvasti me eṣu pañcasūpādānaskandheṣvasmīti māno 'smīti chando 'smītyanuśayo 'prahīṇo 'parijñāto 'nirodhito 'vāntīkṛta iti / " yathā kliṣṭasya dhātrīcailasyoṣādibhiḥ sudhautasya nirmalasyāpi satastadadhivāsanākṛtaṃ gandhamātramanuvartate yattatsugandhadravyaparibhāvanayā bhūyo 'pyapanetavyaṃ bhavatyevameva darśanamārgeṇa prahīṇaparikalpitasatkāyadṛṣṭimalasyāpyāryaśrāvakasya pūrvābhiniveśābhyāsakṛtamaparicchinnavastukamātmadarśanamanuvartate yattatpunarmārgabhāvanayā prahātavyaṃ bhavatīti / antagrāhadṛṣṭiḥ sahajocchedadṛṣṭisaṃgṛhītā veditavyā yayā nirvāṇāt pratyudāvartate mānasaṃ paritrasanamupādāyātha kastarhi me ātmeti
# ji skad du tshe dang ldan pa bran can kho bos ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po 'di dag la bdag gam bdag gir rjes su mi mthong mod kyi / / 'on kyang nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po 'di dag la nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang nga'o snyam pa'i 'dun pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i bag la nyal ma spangs pa'o / / yongs su ma shes so / / ma bkag go / / mtha' med par ma byas so zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / dper na ma ma'i gos dri ma can du gyur pa bul tog la sogs pas legs par bkrus te dri ma med par gyur kyang de zhen par gos pas dri ma nam pa'i bag yod de / / de spos dri zhim po bsgo bas yang bsal bar bya dgos pa de bzhin du mthong ba'i lam gyis 'jig tshogs la lta ba kun tu brtags pa'i dri ma spangs pa'i 'phags pa nyan thos la yang sngon mngon par zhen te goms par byas pa dngos po ma gtogs pa'i bdag tu lta ba rjes su 'brang ste / / de ni lam bsgoms pas spang bar bya dgos pa yin no / / mthar 'dzin par lta ba lhan cig skyes pa ni chad par lta bas bsdus par rig par bya ste / / des bdag gi bdag gang yin zhes yongs su mi chad pa'i phyir mya ngan las 'das pa la yid phyir ldog par byed do /
rāgādayo bhāvanāprahātavyā dṛṣṭipakṣān muktvā
# lta ba'i phyogs dang mthun pa ma gtogs par 'dod chags la sogs pa ni bsgoms pas spang bar bya ba dag go /
tannidānavastuparijñānaṃ kleśānuśayaścāprahīṇo bhavatyevamādi pūrvavat
# de'i gzhi'i dngos po yongs su shes pa zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa'i bag la nyal ma spangs pa yin te zhes bya ba la sogs pa snga ma bzhin no /
svabhāvaparijñānaṃ kleśa eṣa utpannaḥ cittasaṃkleśātmaka iti / ādīnavaparijñānamātmāvyāvādhāya saṃvartate paravyābādhāyobhayavyābādhāya dṛṣṭadhāmikamavadyaṃ prasavati sāṃparāyikaṃ dṛṣṭadharmasāṃparāyikamavadyaṃ prasavati tajjaṃ caitasikaṃ duḥkhadaurmanasyaṃ pratisaṃvedayata ityevaṃ tribhiḥ prakāraiḥ parijñāyotpannaḥ kleśo 'nadhivāsanayogena parivarjyate / anutpannasya tvanutpādāya mārgo bhāvyate
# ngo bo nyid yongs su shes pa zhes bya ba ni sems kun nas nyon mongs par byed pa'i bdag nyid kyi nyon mongs pa ni 'byung po zhes bya'o / / nyes dmigs yongs su shes pa zhes bya ba ni bdag la gnod pa dang gzhan la gnod pa dang / / gnyi ga la gnod par 'gyur ba dang / / mthong ba'i chos kyi kha na ma thob ba bskyed pa rnams dang / / tshe phyi'i ma'i kha na ma thob pa bskyed pa dang de las byung ba'i sems las byung ba sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba myong bar byed pa'o / / de ltar rnam pa gsum gyis yongs su shes nas nyon mongs pa 'byung bar 'gyur ba dbang du mi len pa'i tshul gyis yongs su spang ngo / / ma skyes pa mi bskyed pa'i phyir lam bsgom mo /
asaṃbhinnālaṃbanena manaskāreṇeti miśrālaṃbanena sarvadharmasāmānya lakṣaṇākāreṇetyarthaḥ
# 'dres pa la dmigs pas yid la byed pas zhes bya ba ni tha dad pa la dmigs pa ste / / chos thams cad kyi spyi'i mtshan nyid kyi rnam par zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
yadi sarvadharmā anātmana iti nairātmyajñānenaiva kleśaprahāṇaṃ bhavatyanityādyākārāḥ kimarthamupadiśyante
# gal te chos thams cad bdag med do zhes bdag med par shes pa nyid kyis nyon mongs pa spong bar 'gyur na / / mi rtag pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa ci'i phyir bstan zhe na /
na te kleśaprahāṇārthaṃ kiṃtarhyanātmākāraparikarmārtham
# de dag ni nyon mongs pa spong ba ma yin gyi bdag med pa'i rnam par yongs su sbyang bar bya ba'i phyir te /
anityākāraṃ hi niḥsṛtyānātmākāraḥ / yathoktam "yadanityaṃ taddukhaṃ yaddukhaṃ tadanātmeti" / ata evānātmākārasyānuttaryavyavasthānam / ānuttaryāṇyārabhya trīṇyānuttaryāṇi jñānānuttaryaṃ pratipadānuttaryaṃ vimuktyānuttaryaṃ ca
# mi rtag pa'i rnam pa la brten nas sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa 'thob bo / / sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa la brten nas bdag med pa'i rnam pa 'thob ste / / ji skad du gang mi rtag pa de sdug bsngal ba'o / / de bdag med pa'o zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / de bas na bdag med pa'i rnam pa ni bla na med pa nyid du rnam par gzhag go / / bla na med pa nyid las brtsams nas bla na med pa nyid gsum ste / / shes pa bla na med pa nyid dang / / lam bla na med pa nyid dang / / rnam par grol ba bla na med pa nyid do /
tatra jñānānuttaryaṃ nairātmyajñānam tataḥ pareṇa jñānāntarāparyeṣaṇāt
# de la shes pa bla na med pa nyid ni bdag med pa'i shes pa nyid de / / de'i pha rol du shes pa gzhan btsal du med pa'i phyir ro /
pratipadānuttarya sukhā kṣiprābhijñā tasyāḥ sarvapratipadagratvāt
# lam bla na med pa nyid ni sla la mngon par shes pa myur ba ste / / de ni lam thams cad kyi mchog yin pa'i phyir ro /
vimuktyānuttarya maśaikṣākopyā ca vimuktiḥ sarvavimuktiprativiśiṣṭatvāt / etāni ca trīṇyānuttaryāṇi yathākramaṃ darśanabhāvanāniṣṭhāmārgānadhikṛtya veditavyāni
# rnam par grol ba bla na med pa nyid ni mi slob pa mi 'khrugs pa'i rnam par grol ba ste / / rnam par grol ba thams cad las khyad par du 'phags pa'i phyir ro / / bla na med pa nyid rnam pa gsum po 'di dag ni go rims bzhin du mthong ba dang bsgoms pa dang mthar phyin pa'i lam gyi dbang du byas par rig par bya'o /
upalabdhikarma cakṣurādīnāṃ rūpadarśanādi
# bam po lnga pa / / dmigs pa'i las zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pa'i ste /
kāritrakarma pṛthivyādīnāṃ dhāraṇādi yadvā yasya svalakṣaṇakṛtyam / tadyathā rūpaṇā rūpasyetyevamādi / vyavasāyakarmābhisaṃdhipūrvakaṃ kāyādikarma
# gzugs la lta ba la sogs pa'o / / byed pa'i las ni sa la sogs pa'i ste / / rten pa la sogs pa'o / / yang na gang gi mtshan nyid kyi byed pa gang yin pa ste / / 'di lta ste gzugs kyi ni gzugs su yod pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa lta bu'o / / rtsol ba'i las ni bsam pa sngon du btang ba'i lus la sogs pa'i las so /
pariṇatikarma suvarṇakārādīnāmalaṃkārādi
# bsgyur ba'i las ni gser mgar la sogs pa'i ste / / rgyan la sogs pa'o /
prāptikarmāryamārgādīnāṃ nirvāṇādhigamādi / asmiṃstvarthe yadbhūyasyā vyavasā karmābhipretamiti prāptikāritrakarmaṇorapi saṃbhavāt / kāyādikarma karmapathā iti sūtrānusāreṇa yathāpradhānaṃ nirdeśo veditavyaḥ tatprayogādīnāpi kāyādikarmāntarbhāvāt / trayaścatvārastrayaśca karmapathā yathākramaṃ kāyavāṅmanaḥkarmalakṣaṇā veditavyāḥ
# 'thob pa'i las ni 'phags pa'i lam la sogs pa ste / / mya ngan las 'das pa 'thob pa la sogs pa'o / / skabs 'dir ni phal cher rtsol ba'i las su 'dod do zhes bya ba ni 'thob par byed pa'i las kyang yod pa'i phyir ro / / lus la sogs pa'i las la las kyi lam zhes bya ba ni mdo sde dang mthun par ji ltar gtso bo bstan par rig par bya ste / / de la sbyor ba la sogs pa yang lus la sogs pa'i las kyi nang du 'dus pa'i phyir ro / / las kyi lam gsum dang bzhi dang gsum ni go rims bzhin du lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las kyi mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o /
prāṇātipātādīnāṃ vastu sattvasaṃkhyātamasattvasaṃkhyātaṃ vā yathāyogaṃ yadadhiṣṭhāya prāṇātipātādayaḥ pravartante
# srog gcod pa la sogs pa'i gzhi ni sems can gyi grangs su gtogs pa dang / / sems can gyi grangs su ma gtogs pa ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar te / / gang la brten nas srog gcod pa la sogs pa 'byung ba'o /
āśayastatra vastuni tatsaṃjñāśayastatkarmapathakriyecchāśayaśca
# bsam pa ni gzhi de la der 'du shes pa'i bsam pa dang / / las kyi lam de byed par 'dod pa'i bsam pa'o /
prayogastatkriyāyai svayaṃ parairvā kāyavāṅmanobhirārambhaḥ
# sbyor ba ni de bya ba'i phyir bdag gam gzhan gyi lus dang ngag dang yid kyi rtsom pa'o /
kleśaḥ lobhadveṣamohā yathāyogaṃ samastavyastāḥ / niṣṭhāgamanaṃ tena tena prayogeṇa tasya tasya karmaṇaḥ paripūraṇaṃ tatkālamūrdhvakālaṃ vā / tatra prāṇātipātasya vastu sattvaḥ / āśayastatra tatsaṃjñino vadhābhiprāyaḥ
# nyon mongs pa ni 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug 'dus pa dang so so ba ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro / / zin par byas pa ni sbyor ba de dang de'i dus sam / / phyis las de dang des yongs su rdzogs pa'o / / de la srog gcod pa'i gzhi ni sems can no / / bsam pa ni de la der 'du shes shing bsad pa'i bsam pa'o /
prayogo vadho yatpraharaṇādibhiḥ
# sbyor ba ni bsad par bsams pa'i mtshon cha la sogs pa'o /
kleśo lobhādikaḥ / niṣṭhāgamanaṃ tasya prāṇinastena prayogeṇānantaraṃ praścādvā maraṇam
# nyon mongs pa ni 'dod chags la sogs pa'o / / zin par byas pa ni sbyor ba des de ma thag tu 'am phyis shi ba'o /
adattādānādonāṃ vastu ca niṣṭhāgamanaṃ ca nirdhekṣyāmaḥ
# ma byin par len pa la sogs pa'i gzhi dang zin par byas pa bshad par bya'o /
śeṣaṃ yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyam
# lhag ma ni ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o /
adattādānasya vastu paraparigṛhītaṃ sattvasaṃkhyātamasattvasaṃkhyātaṃ vā
# ma byin par len pa'i gzhi ni gzhan gyis yongs su gzung ba sems can gyi grangs su gtogs pa'am sems can gyi grangs su ma gtogs pa'o /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ tatsvīkaraṇam
# zin par byas pa ni bdag gir byas pa'o /
kāmamithyācārasya vastvagamyā strī gamyā vānaṅgādeśākāle vamātrāyuktābhyāṃ ca sarvaśca pumānnapuṃsakaṃ ca
# 'dod pas log par g yem ba'i gzhi ni spyod yul ma yin pa'i bud med dang spyod yul yin yang yan lag ma yin pa dang yul ma yin pa dang dus ma yin pa dang tshod ma zin pa dang rigs ma yin pa dang pho dang ma ning thams cad do /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ dvayadvayasamāpattiḥ
# zin par byas pa ni gnyis kyis gnyis sprad pa'o /
mṛṣāvādasya vastu dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mataṃ vijñātamadṛṣṭamaśrutamamatamavijñātaṃ ca / āśayo 'nyathāvatkukāmatā
# brdzun du smra ba'i gzhi ni mthong ba dang thos pa dang bye brag phyed pa dang rnam par shes pa dang ma mthong ba dang ma thos pa dang bye brag mi phyed pa dang rnam par ma shes ba'o / / bsam pa ni gzhan du 'du shes la gzhan du smra bar 'dod pa'o /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ parṣatprativādivijñāpanam / paiśunyasya vastu samagravyagrāḥ sattvāḥ / āśayasteṣāmeva bhedāpratisaṃdhānābhiprāyaḥ
# zin par byas pa ni 'khor dang phyir rgol bas go bar byed pa'o / / phra ma'i gzhi ni sems can 'dum pa dang mi 'dum pa dag go / / bsam pa ni dbye ba dang sdum mi byed par sems pa'o /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ bhedyavijñāpanam
# zin par byas pa ni phye bar shes par byed pa'o /
pāruṣyasya vastvāghātanimittabhūtāḥ sattvāḥ
# ngag rtsub po'i gzhi ni kun nas mnar sems kyi gzhir gyur pa'i sems can rnams so /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ pārūṣāṇām / saṃbhinnapralāpasya vastvanarthopasaṃgṛhītārthaḥ
# zin par byas pa ni ngag rtsub po smras pa'o / / tshig kyal pa'i gzhi ni don med pa dang ldan pa'i don no /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ tasya bhāṣaṇam / abhidhyāyā vastu parakīyaṃ vittopakaraṇam / āśayastatra tatsaṃjñinastathāruciḥ
# zin par byas pa ni de smras pa'o / / brnab sems kyi gzhi ni gzhan gyi nor dang yo byad do / / bsam pa ni de la der 'du shes shing de bzhin du 'dod pa'o /
prayogastatsvīkaraṇasaṃpradhāraṇam
# sbyor ba ni de bdag gir bya bar sems pa'o /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ tatsvīkaraṇaniścayaḥ
# zin par byas pa ni bdag gir bya bar nges pa'o /
vyāpādasya vastvāghātanimittabhūtāḥ sattvāḥ
# gnod sems kyi gzhi ni kun nas mnar sems kyi rgyur gyur pa'i sems can rnams so /
niṣṭhāgamanaṃ prahanananiścayaḥ / mithyādṛṣṭervastu sannarthaḥ
# zin par byas pa ni bsad pa la sogs par nges pa'o / / log par lta ba'i gzhi ni don yod pa'o /
āśayaḥ satyatatsaṃjñinastathāruciḥ / niṣṭhāgamanamapavādaniścayaḥ
# bsam pa ni yod pa la med par 'du shes shing de bzhin du 'dod pa'o /
parājñaptisaṃcetanīyatā yathā kaścidanicchannapi parairbalādājñāpyamano 'bhisaṃghāyākuśalamācarati / parasaṃjñaptisaṃcetanīyatā yathā kaścidanicchanniva paraiḥ saṃjñāpyamānaḥ samādāpyamāno hitametaditi grāhyamāṇo 'bhisaṃghāyā kuśalamācarati / avijñāya saṃcetanīyatā yathā kaścidguṇadoṣānabhijño 'nabhiniviṣṭaḥ yadṛcchayābhisaṃdhāyākuśalamācarati / mūlābhiniveśasaṃceta nīyatā yathā kaścidkuśalamūlaiḥ lobhādibhirabhibhūta āviṣṭacittastīvreṇābhiniveśenābhisaṃghāyākuśalamācarati / viparyāsasaṃcetanīyatā yathā kaściddharmakāmo viṣamahetudṛṣṭirāyatyāmiṣṭaphalārthamabhisaṃdhāyākuśalamācarati / tatra pūrvikābhistisṛbhiḥ saṃcetanīyatābhiḥ kṛtamapi karma naivopacīyate yato 'sya nāvaśyaṃ vipākaḥ pratisaṃvedanīyaḥ / paścimābhyāṃ tu saṃcetanīyābhyāṃ yadi kṛtaṃ bhavatyupacitaṃ cāvaśyamevāsya vipākaḥ pratisaṃvedyate
# zin par byas pa ni skur ba 'debs par nges pa'o / / gzhan gyis bsgo ba sems pa las gyur pa ni 'di la ste / / 'ga' zhig mi 'dod pa bzhin du gzhan dag gis nan gyis bsgos nas bsams te / / mi dge ba spyod pa'o / / gzhan gyis gsol ba btab pa sems pa las gyur pa ni 'di lta ste / / 'ga' zhig mi 'dod bzhin du gzhan dag gis gsol ba btab nas 'di ni phan pa'o zhes yang dag pa 'dzin du bcug cing len du bcu gnas bsams te mi dge ba spyod pa'o / / mi shes pa'i sems pa la gyur pa ni 'di lta ste / / kha cig yon tan dang nyes pa mngon par mi shes shing / / mngon par zhen pa med la / / 'dod dgar bsams nas mi dge ba spyod pa'o / / rtsa ba la mngon par zhen pa'i sems las gyur pa ni 'di lta ste / / 'ga' zhig mi dge ba'i rtsa ba la chags pa la sogs pas zil gyis non cing sems non nas mngon par zhe na pa drag pos bsams te mi dge ba la spyod pa'o /
upacayo vāsanāvṛddhirityālayavijñāne vipākabīja paripoṣaṇaṃ veditavyam / karmakriyāniyamaḥ pūrvakarmabhireva niyamya vipākasaṃtatirāviddhā bhavati / yadasmin janmanyanenedaṃ karma karaṇīyamiti sa tamavadhimalaṃghayitvā tatkarma karoti yasyākaraṇāya pratibandhaṃ buddhā api bhagavanto na samarthāḥ kartum yathāhetuniyamanaṃ phalasaṃtānapariṇāmāditi / vipākapratisaṃvedanāniyamaḥ saṃcetanīyasya karmaṇaḥ pūrvavat / avasthāniyame dṛṣṭadharmavedanīyādibhiravasthāpi niyamitā bhavatīti / yathānena vipākena dṛṣṭe dharme bhavitavyamanenopapadyānenāparasmin paryāya iti / akuśalānāṃ karmapathānāṃ mṛdumadhyādhi mātrāṇāṃ vipākaphalaṃ tiryakpretanarakeṣu veditavyam / niṣyandaphalamapāyebhyaścyutvā manuṣyeṣūpapannānaṃ pratyekaṃ prāṇātipātādattādānādyānurūpyeṇātmabhāvaparigrahayorvipattiḥ / tadyathālpāyuṣkatā dāridrayamityevamādi yathāyogam
# phyin ci log gi sems pa las gyur pa ni 'di lta ste / / 'ga' zhig chos 'dod kyang mi mthun pa'i rgyu la lta ste / / phyi ma la yid du 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i don du bsams nas mi dge ba spyod pa'o / / de la sems pa las gyur pa dang po gsum ni las byas su zin kyang stsogs pa nyid du mi 'gyur te / / de'i phyir 'di'i rnam par smin pa gdon mi za bar myong bar 'gyur ba ma yin no / / sems pa las gyur ba tha ma gnyis ni gal te byas par gyur na bsags pa yin te / / de'i rnam par smin pa gdon mi za bar myong bar 'gyur ro / / stsogs pa ni bag chags 'phel ba'o zhes bya ba ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la rnam par smin pa'i sa bon yongs su gsos par rig par bya'o / / las byed par nges pa ni sngon gyi las rnams kyis rnam par smin pa'i rgyud nges par byas nas 'phangs par gyur ba ste / / gang gi tshe de la 'dis las 'di byed par nges par de dang mi 'gal bar las de byed /
adhipatiphalaṃ pratyekaṃ tadānurūpyeṇaiva bāhyānāṃ bhāvānāṃ sasyādīnāṃ vipattiḥ / tadyathā prāṇātipātasyādhipatyenālpaujaso bhavantyevamādi
# de'i rgyu'i nges pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'bras bu'i rgyur gyur ba'i phyir de mi bya bar bzlog pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis kyang mdzad mi spyod do /
yathāsūtram "sarvairdaśabhirakuśalaiḥ karmapathairāsevitairbhāvitairbahulīkṛtairnarakeṣūpapadyate / tadeṣāṃ vipākaphalam / sa cedicchatvamāgacchati manuṣyāṇāṃ sabhāgatām prāṇātipātenālpāyurbhavati adattādānena bhogavyasanī bhavati / kāmamithyācāreṇa sasapatnadāraḥ / mṛṣāvādenābhyākhyānabahulaḥ / paiśūnyena mitrabhedo 'sya bhavati / pāruṣyeṇāmanojñaśabdaśravaṇaṃ bhavati / saṃbhinnapralāpenānādeyavākyaḥ / abhidhyayā tīvrarāgaḥ / vyāpādena tīvradveṣaḥ / mithyādṛṣṭyā tīvramohaḥ tasyā mohabhūyastvāt / idameṣāṃ niṣyandaphalam / prāṇātipātenātyāsevitena bāhyābhāvā alpaujaso bhavanti / adattādānenāśanirajobahulāḥ
# rnam par smin pa myong bar nges pa ni / / sems pa las gyur pa'i las kyi ste snga ma bzhin no / / dus nges pa ni mthong ba'i chos la myong bar 'gyur ba la sogs pa'i las rnams kyi dus kyang nges par byas pa yin te / / ji ltar rnam par smin pa 'dis ni mthong ba'i chos la rnam par smin par byed do / / 'dis ni skyes nas so / / 'dis ni lan grangs gzhan la'o zhes bya'o / / mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam rnams kyi rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ni dud 'gro dang yi dgas dang sems can dmyal ba rnams su rig par bya'o / / rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu ni ngan song rnams nas shi 'phos nas mir skyes pa rnams kyi srog gcod pa dang ma byin bar len pa la sogs ba so so dang mthun pa'i lus dang yongs su gzung ba mi 'byor ba ste /
kāmamithyācāreṇa rajo 'vakīrṇāḥ / mṛṣāvādena dugandhāḥ / paśūnyenotkūlanikūlāḥ
# 'di ltar tshe thung ba dang dbul ba la sogs pa ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
pārūṣyeṇoṣarajaṅgalāḥ pratikrusṭāḥ pāpabhūmayaḥ / saṃbhinnapralāpena viṣamartupariṇāmāḥ / abhidhyayā sūkṣmaphalāḥ / vyāpādena kaṭukaphalāḥ / mithyādṛṣṭayālpaphalā aphalā vā / idameṣāmadhipatiphalam / daśānāṃ kuśalānāṃ karmapathānāṃ vipākaphalaṃ devamanuṣyeṣu / niṣyandaphalaṃ teṣveva pratyekamānurūpyeṇātmabhāvaparigrahasaṃpattiḥ / yathākuśalānāṃ karmapathānāṃ vipākaphalādi triphalā vasthānaṃ kṛtam evaṃ kuśalādīnāṃ karmapathānāṃ sāsravāṇāṃ devamanuṣyeṣu trīṇi phalāni yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyāni / ekena karmaṇā ekamātmabhāvamākṣipati ekena karmakṣaṇenaikajanmikasyaiva vipākasya bījapoṣaṇāt / ekenānekamākṣipati tenaivānekajanmikavipākabījapoṣaṇāt / anekenaikamākṣipati bahubhiḥ karmakṣaṇaiḥ tasyaivaikasya punaḥ punaḥ bījapoṣaṇāt / anekenānekamākṣipati bahubhiranyonyāpekṣayā janmaparaṃparābījapoṣaṇāditi
# bdag po'i 'bras bu ni so so dang mthun pa nyid du phyi'i dngos po lo tog la sogs pa mi 'byor ba ste / / 'di ltar srog gcod pa'i dbang gis ni byin chung bar 'gyur zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / de bzhin du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam zag pa dang bcas pa rnams kyi 'bras bu dag kyang lta dang mi rnams kyi nang du gsum gsum du 'gyur ba ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o / / las gcig gis lus gcig 'phen pa ni las kyi skad cig gcig gis tshe gcig kho na'i rnam par smin pa'i sa bon gsos pa'i phyir ro / / gcig gis du ma 'phen pa ni / / de nyid kyis tshe rabs du ma'i rnam pa smin pa'i sa bon gsos pa'i phyir ro / / du mas gcig 'phen pa ni las kyi skad cig mang pos gcig po de nyid kyi sa bon dang yang gsos pa'i phyir ro / / du mas du ma 'phen pa ni mang po dag phan tshun ltos nas tshe rabs gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i sa bon gsos pa'i phyir ro /
kena kāraṇena rūpārūpyapratisaṃyuktaṃ kuśalamānijyamityucyate
# ci'i phyir gzugs dang gzugs med pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i dge ba la mi g yo ba zhes bya zhe na /
yathā kāmāvacaramanyagatikamapi paripūrakaṃ kuśalamūlamanyatra vipākaṃ prayacchati naivaṃ rūpyārūpyāvacaram bhūminaiyamyena phaladānāt
# ji ltar 'dod pa na spyod pa'i 'gro ba gzhan gyi yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i dge ba ni gzhan du rnam par smin pa 'byin pa byed pa de bzhin du / / gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa ni de lta ma yin te /
ato vipākadānaṃ pratyakampanārthenānijyamuktaṃ samāhitabhūmikatvāccākampanārtheneti
# sa'i nges pas 'bras bu 'byin pa'i phyir ro / / de bas na rnam par smin pa 'byin par g yo ba med pa dang mnyam par gzhag pa'i sa pa yin pas mi g yo ba'i phyir mi g yo ba zhes bshad do /
phalavipākasaṃmūḍhasyāpuṇyāḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃbhavanti teṣāmekāntakliṣṭatvenāvidyāsāṃnidhye sati phalavipākābhisaṃpratyayākārāyāḥ samyagdṛṣṭeranavakāśāt
# 'bras bu rnam par smin pa la rmongs pa ni mi dge ba'i 'du byed rnams 'byung ngo zhes bya ba ni de dag gi ni gcig tu nyon mongs pa can yin pas ma rig pa yod par 'gyur na 'bras bu rnam par smin pa la mngon par yid ces pa'i rnam pa'i yang dag pa'i lta ba'i skabs med pa'i phyir ro /
tattvārthasaṃmūḍhasya puṇyāniṃjyāstattvārtha ucyate catvāryāryasatyāni / tatra saṃmohaḥ kuśalacittānāmapyadṛṣṭasatyānāmanuśayato 'nubuddho bhavati yadvaśena te duḥkhatastraidhātukasya yathābhūtamaparijñānāt punarbhavahetubhūtān puṇyānijyasaṃskārānutthāpayanti / na tvevaṃ dṛṣṭasatyāstattvārthasaṃmohābhāvāt
# de kho na'i don la rmongs pa ni bsod nams dang ye shes mi g yo ba rnam so zhes bya ba de kho na'i don zhes bya ba ni 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag go / / de la rmongs na dge ba'i sems yod du zin kyang bden pa ma mthong ba nams la bag la nyal gyi rjes su 'brel par 'gyur ro / / de'i dbang gis de dag khams gsum pa sdug bsngal nyid du yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su ma shes pa'i phyir yang srid pa'i rgyur gyur pa'i bsod nams dang mi g yo ba'i 'du byed rnams slong bar byed do / / bden pa mthong ba rnams ni de lta ma yin te / / de kho na'i don la rmongs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
ataste taddhetukā ityucyante
# de bas na de dag ni de'i rgyu las byung ba rnams zhes bya'o /
prāṇātipātasya lobhena prayogo māṃsikādīnām
# srog gcod pa la yang shal sogs pa 'dod pa rnams ni chags pas sbyor ro /
dveṣeṇaiva vairaniryātanakāmānām
# sha glon par 'dod pa rnams ni zhe sdang gis sbyor ro /
mohena yājñikādīnām / dveṣeṇaiva niṣṭhā nirghṛṇatāmantareṇa parasattvavipādanāsaṃbhavāt
# mchod sbyin la sogs pa gti mug gis sbyor ro / / zhe sdang nyid kyis ni mthar phyin par byed de / / snying rje med pa ma yin par sems can gsod mi srid pa'i phyir ro /
evaṃ pāruṣyādīnāṃ yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyam
# ngag rtsub po la sogs pa la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o /
abhidhyādīnāṃ kathaṃ lobhādibhiḥ prayogaḥ
# brnab sems la sogs pa la ji ltar chags pa la sogs pas sbyor zhe na /
tatrābhidhyākarmapathaḥ paravittopakaraṇasvīkaraṇaniścaya ityuktam / tadyadi tenaiva vittopakaraṇenārthī bhavati tatsvīkaraṇāyābhisaṃskarotyato 'sya lobhena prayogo vyavasthāpyate / atha maivāsya bhūdityevaṃ dveṣeṇa
# de la brnab sems kyi las kyi lam ni gal te gzhan gyi nor dang yo byad bdag gir byed par nges pa'o zhes bstan pa de la gal te gzhan gyi nor dang yo byad de nyid 'dod par gyur na / / de bdag gir bya ba'i phyir mngon par 'du byed de / / de'i phyir chags pas sbyor bar rnam par gzhag go / / ci ste 'di yi ra ma gyur cig ce na / / de ltar na ni zhe sdang gis sbyor ro /
atha parasvīkaraṇe na kaściddoṣa iti mohena prayogo veditavyaḥ
# ci ste gzhan gyis bdag gir byas kyang nyes pa ci yang med do snyam na gti mug gis sbyor bar rig par bya'o /
evamanyadapi yojayitavyam
# gzhan la yang de bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o /
anyonyādhipateyamapi karma sādhāraṇaṃ veditavyaṃ yadvaśātsattvā anyonyaṃ citacaittapariṇāmanimittaṃ bhavantīti
# phan tshun gyi dbang gis byung ba yang thun mong ba'i las su rig par bya ste / / de'i dbang gis sems can rnams phan tshun du sems dang sems las byung ba 'byung ba'i rgyur 'gyur ro /
vaipakṣikāt karmaṇaḥ prātipakṣikai karma balavaddraṣṭavyam pratipakṣabalenākṣiptasyāpi vipakṣaphalasyānyathātvāpādanāt
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi las ni gnyen po'i las stobs dang ldan par blta ste / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyis 'bras bu 'phangs su zin kyang gnyen po'i stobs kyis gzhan du bsgyur ba'i phyir ro /
sarvaṃ ca kuśalaṃ karma saṃcetanīyaṃ pratipakṣabalikasyākuśalād balavaddraṣṭavyam / pratipakṣabaladurbalasya tvakuśalaṃ kuśalādbalavat
# gnyen po'i stobs can gyi dge ba'i las sems pa las gyur pa ni / / mi dge bas stobs dang ldan par blta'o / / gnyen po'i mthu chung ba'i mi dge ba ni dge ba bas stobs dang ldan no /
sarvaṃ cāviśeṣeṇa kuśalākuśalaṃ niyatavipākamārya mārgeṇāprahīṇaṃ balavadityucyate
# dge ba dang mi dge ba rnam par smin par nges pa 'phags pa'i lam gyis ma spangs ba thams cad ni bye brag med par stobs dang ldan pa zhes bya'o /
kāmapratisaṃyuktamakuśalaṃ prakṛtyā balavat kleśopakleśādibahuparivāratvāt
# 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i mi dge ba ni rang bzhin gyis stobs dang ldan pa ste / / nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa la sogs pa'i 'khor mang ba'i phyir ro /
yadyapi pūrvābhyastaṃ tadapi balavat saṃtatestena bhāvitatvāt
# gang sngon gyi goms par byas ba de yang stobs dang ldan pa ste / / des rgyud la bsgos pa'i phyir ro /
yadapi padasthaṃ paripūrṇavayasām tīvrābhiniveśaprasādakaraṇāt
# gang gnas la gnas pa ni nar son pa rnams kyi ste / / mngon par zhen pa dang dad pa drag pos byed pa'i phyir ro /
yadapyasādhyamaparinirvāṇadharmakāṇām pratipakṣeṇānuddhāryatvāt
# yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can rnams kyi lam sgrub tu med pa gang yin pa de ni gnyen pos byung du med pa'i phyir ro /
kṣetrato 'pi mātṛbadhādikam
# zhing ni ma gsod pa la sogs pa'o /
cittābhisaṃskārato 'pi mahābodhipraṇidhānādikaṃ balavatkarma veditavyam
# sems kyi mngon par 'du byed pa ni byang chub sems por smon lam btab pa la sogs pa ste / / stobs dang ldan pa'i las su rig par bya'o /
punarnavabhirākārairbalavatkarma veditavyam / tadyathā kṣetrato yadi guṇavaddakṣiṇīyaṃ kṣetraṃ bhavati
# yang rnam pa dgus stobs dang ldan pa'i las su rig par bya ste 'di lta ste / / zhing ni gal te yon tan dang ldan pa'i sbyin gnas zhing du gyur pa'o /
vastuno yadi praṇītaṃ prabhūtaṃ deyavastu bhavati
# dngos po ni gal te sbyin pa'i dngos po gya nom zhing mang por gyur pa'o /
svabhāvato dānācchīlaṃ śīlādbhāvanetyevamādiḥ / āśrayataḥ puṇyānāṃ kartā yadi vītarāgo bhavati / manaskārato yadi tīvraprasādasahagato manaskāro bhavati
# ngo bo nyid ni sbyin ba bas tshul khrims stobs dang ldan no / / tshul khrims pas bsgom pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / gzhi ni bsod nams byed pa gal te 'dod chags dang bral bar gyur pa'o / / yid la byed pa ni gal te yid la byed pa dang ba drag po dang ldan par 'gyur ba'o /
āśayato yadi nirvāṇāśayo bhavati / sahāyato yadi tadanyapuṇyakriyāvastuparigṛhītaṃ bhavati
# bsam ba ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i bsam pa dang ldan par gyur pa'o / / grogs ni de las gzhan pa'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos pos yongs su zin par 'gyur ba'o /
bahulīkārataḥ yadi paunaḥ punyena kṛtaṃ bhavatyanuvitarkitaṃ vā
# lan mang du byed pa ni yang dang yang du byas par gyur ba'am / / rjes su rnam par brtags pa'o /
bāhujanyato yadi svayaṃ ca kṛtaṃ bhavatyanyaiśca kāritamiti / ya evaṃ vadet yathā yathāyaṃ puruṣapudgalaḥ karma karotyupacinoti tathā tathā vipākaṃ pratisaṃvedayata ityevaṃ sati brahmacaryavāso na bhavatyavakāśaśca na prajñāyate samyagduḥkhakṣayāya duḥkhasyāntakriyāyai
# skye bo mang pos kyang zhes bya ba ni bdag gis kyang byas par gyur la gzhan dang kyang byed du bcug pa'o / / su zhig 'di skad du skyes bu gang zag 'di ji ltar las byed cing stsogs pa de lta de ltar rnam par smin pa myong ba gyur na / / de ltar na tshangs par spyod pas gnas par mi 'gyur zhing yang dag par sdug bsngal zad pa dang sdug bsngal mthar dbyung ba'i skabs kyang mi snang ngo zhes zer zhes bya ba la /
kathaṃ kṛtvā brahmacaryavāso na bhavati
# ji ltar byas na tshangs par spyod pas gnas par mi 'gyur zhe na /
tīvrakleśasya pratisaṃkhyāya sahaduḥkhena sahadaurmanasyena śīlaparipālanāt / yadi tadvipākastathaiva sahaduḥkhena sahadaurmanasyenānubhūyeta vṛthā tatparipālanaṃ syāt / pāradārikaprabhṛtīnāṃ ca sahasukhena sahasaumanasyena dauḥśīlyakaraṇādyadi tadvipākastathaivānubhūyeta vṛthā tadviratiḥ syādityevaṃ kṛtvā brahmacaryavāso na bhavati / kathamavakāśaśca na prajñāyate samyagduḥkhakṣayāya duḥkhasyāntakriyāyai
# nyon mongs pa drag po dang ldan pas so sor brtags na sdug bsngal dang bcas par tshul khrims yongs su bsrungs ba'i phyir gal te de'i rnam par smin pa yang de bzhin du sdug bsngal dang bcas shing yid mi bde ba dang bcas pa myong na ni de yongs su srung ba don med par 'gyur ro / / gzhan gyi chung ma la sogs pa la bde ba dang bcas shing yid bde ba dang bcas par tshul khrims 'chal bar byas pa'i phyir gal te de'i rnam par smin pa de bzhin du myong na ni de spong ba don med par 'gyur te / / de ltar byas na tshangs par spyod pas gnas par mi 'gyur ro / / ji ltar na yang dag par sdug bsngal zad pa dang sdug bsngal mthar dbyung ba'i skabs kyi kyang mi snang zhe na /
ata eva tadupaniṣadbhatasya brahmacaryavāsasya duḥkhavipākatvāditi / evaṃ ca kṛtvā sukhasahagatasya karmaṇaḥ sukhasahagata eva vipāko duḥkhasahagatasya duḥkhasahagato 'duḥkhāsukhasahagatasya tatsahagata eveti niyamaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ / atra yastvevaṃ yathāvedanīyaṃ yathāvedanīyamityevamādinā sukhasahagatasya kuśalākuśalasya yathāyogamāyatyāṃ sukhaduḥkhāduḥkhāsukhavedanīyasya sukhādiko vipāko 'nujñātaḥ / evaṃ duḥkhāduḥkhāsukhasahagatasya sukhādivedanīyasya sukhādiko vipāko 'nujñāyata iti
# de'i phyir de'i rgyur gyur ba tshangs pa spyod pas gnas pa'i rnam par smin pa sdug bsngal ba'i phyir ro / / de ltar byas na bde ba dang bcas pa'i las kyi rnam par smin pa ni bde ba dang bcas pa nyid du 'gyur / / sdug bsngal dang bcas pa'i rnam par smin pa ni sdug bsngal nyid du 'gyur / / sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang bcas pa'i ni / / sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa dang bcas pa nyid du 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i nges pa ni 'dir bcom ldan 'das kyis bkag go / / yongs su zhig 'di skad du / / skyes bu gang zag 'di ji ltar myong bar 'gyur ba ji ltar myang bar 'gyur zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni bde ba dang ldan pa'i dge ba dang mi dge ba phyi ma la ji ltar mthun mthun du bde ba dang sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal yang ma yin pa bde ba yang ma yin par myong bar 'gyur ba'i bde ba la sogs pa'i rnam par smin pa ni gnang ngo /
pravrajitasya saṃvaraḥ pañcavidho bhikṣusaṃvaro yāvacchāmaṇerīsaṃvara iti / sa duścaritavivekacaritaṃ kāmavivekacaritaṃ ca pudgalamadhikṛtya vyavasthāpitaḥ
# rab tu byung ba'i sdom pa ni rnam pa lnga ste / / dge slong gi sdom pa nas dge tshul ma'i sdom pa'i bar du'o / / nyes par spyod pa las dben par spyod pa dang 'dod pa las dben par spyod pa zhes bya ba ni gang zag gi dbang du byas nas rnam par gzhag pa ste /
tathāhi sa tādṛśaḥ śaknoti yāvajjīvaṃ prāṇātipātāda brahmacaryācca virantumiti
# 'di ltar de 'dra ba de ni ji srid 'tsho'i bar du srog gcad pa la sogs pa nyes par spyod pa dang mi tshangs par spyod pa spang bar nus so /
upāsakopāsikāsaṃvaro duścaritaviveka caritamadhikṛtya no tu kāmavivekacaritam
# dge bsnyen dang dge bsnyen ma'i sdom pa ni nyes par spyod pa las dben par spyod pa'i dbang du byas pa ste / / 'dod pa las dben par spyod pa ni ma yin no /
ataḥ evāsya yāvajjīvaṃ kāmamithyā cāraviratirvyavasthāpyate nābrahmacaryaviratiriti / upavāsasaṃvaro naiva duścaritavivekacaritaṃ na kāmavivekacaritam
# de bas na 'di'i sdom pa ni ji srid 'tsho'i bar du 'dod pa la log par g yem pa spang bar rnam par gzhag gi / / mi tshangs par spyod pa spong ba ni ma yin no / / bsnyen gnas pa'i sdom pa ni nyes par spyod pa las dben par spyod pa yang ma yin 'dod pa las dben par spyod pa yang ma yin pa ste /
ata evāsyāhorātrika upavāsasaṃvaraḥ prajñaptaḥ śanaistadubhayābhyasanārthamiti
# de'i phyir de'i sdom pa na nyin zhag gcig pa la bsnyen gnas pa'i sdom pa brtags te / / rims kyis de gnyi ga goms par bya ba'i phyir ro /
yathā paṇḍapaṇḍakānāṃ bhikṣubhikṣuṇī pakṣopāsanāyogyatvādupāsakatvapratiṣedhaḥ evamubhayavyañjanānāmapi strīpuruṣakleśasamudācāreṇobhayapakṣopāsanāyogyateti na te pṛthaguktāḥ
# ji ltar tha ma dang ma ning rnams la ni dge slong dang dge slong ma'i phyogs gnyis la bsnyen bkur bya ba'i 'os ma yin pa'i phyir dge bsnyen nyid ni bkag pa bzhin du mtshan gnyis pa rnams kyang de bzhin du ste / / skyes pa dang bud med kyi nyon mongs pa kun tu spyod pas phyogs gnyi ga la bsnyen bkur bya ba'i 'os ma yin pa'i phyir de dag logs shig tu ma bshad do /
dhyānasaṃvaro dauḥśīlyasamutthāpakānāṃ lobhādīnāṃ kāmāvacarāṇāṃ kleśopakleśānāṃ viṣkambhaṇapratipakṣeṇa bījopaghāte sati pradeśavairāgyeṇāpi kāmebhyo vītarāgasya yā tasmādauḥśīlyādviratiḥ
# bsam gtan gyi sdom pa ni 'chal ba'i tshul khrims kun nas slong ba dag gi chags pa la sogs pa 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams rnam par gnon pa'i gnyen pos sa bon bcom pas phyogs gcig pa las 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid du zad de 'dod pa dag las 'dod chags dang bral ba'i 'chal ba'i tshul khrims te /
yāvattṛtīyadhyānavītarāgasya dūrībhāvapratipakṣeṇa teṣāmeva dauḥśīlyasamutthāpakānāṃ sutarāṃ bījopaghāto veditavyaḥ
# spong ba gang yin pa'o / / bsam gtan gsum pa'i bar las 'dod chags dang bral ba'i ring du byed pa'i gnyen pos 'chal ba'i tshul khrims kyi kun nas slong ba de dag nyid kyi sa bon shin tu 'joms par rig par bya'o /
caturthadhyānavītarāgasya tvārūpyeṣu rūpābhāvāccholasaṃvarāvyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# bsam gtan bzhi ba la 'dod chags dang bral ba ni gzugs med pa rnams ni gzugs med pa'i phyir tshul khrims kyi sdom pa rnam par gzhag pa med par rig par bya'o /
aurabhrikā ye paśūn hatvā tadvikrayeṇa jīvikāṃ kalpayanti
# shan pa ni gang dag phyugs rnams bsad nas de 'tshong bas 'tsho bar byed pa rnams so /
evaṃ kaukkuṭikādayo yathāsaṃbhavaṃ yojayitavyāḥ
# bya gag gsod pa la sogs pa la yang de bzhin du ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyor bar bya'o /
nāgabandhakā araṇyāt hastino vaddhvā damayanti
# glang po che 'dzin pa ni gang dag nags nas glang po che bzung nas 'dul bar byed pa rnams so; /
nāgamaṇḍalikā ye sarpānādāya tatkrīḍanairjīvanti
# sprul gyis 'tsho ba ni gang dag sprul bzung nas rtse bas 'tsho bar byed pa rnams so /
mūtrakā ye parān paiśunyenopahatva jīvanti
# nyan rna ba ni gang dag gzhan dag la phra mas gnod par byas nas 'tsho bar byed pa rnams so /
abhijanmato vā tatkarmasamādānato veti tatkulīnasyānyakulīnasya ca yathākramam
# de dag gi las skyes pas sam yang dag par blangs pa ste zhes bya ba ni de'i rigs sam / / gzhan gyi rigs kyi go rims bzhin no /
kāyavākprayogapūrvakaḥ tatkarmādhyācāraniścayo 'saṃvara ityucyate / yathoktasaṃvarāsaṃvaravinirmuktasya dānapriyavacanādikaṃ khaṭacapeṭādikaṃ ca karma navasaṃvaronāsaṃvara ityucyate
# de dag gi las spyad par nges par byas pa ni lus dang dag gi sbyor ba sngon du btang ba ste / / sdom pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o / / ji skad bshad pa'i sngom pa dang sdom pa ma yin pa dang mi ldan pa'i sbyin pa dang ngag snyan pa la sogs pa dang khu tshur dang thal lcag la sogs pa'i las ni sdom pa yang ma yin /
dṛṣṭadharmavedanīyaṃ karma yatra janmani kṛtaṃ tatraiva yadvipacyate / upapadyavedanīyaṃ yadanantare janmani tadyathā pañcānantaryāṇi karmāṇi
# sdom pa ma yin pa yang ma yin ba zhes bya'o / / mthong ba'i chos la myong bar 'gyur ba'i las ni tshe gang la byas pa de nyid la gang rnam par smin par 'gyur ba'o / / skyes nas myong bar 'gyur ba'i las ni gang de ma thag tu 'byung ba'i tshe la myong bar 'gyur ba ste / / 'di ltar mtshams med pa lnga'i las rnams so /
yasya tāvadekamevānantarya tasya tadvipāko 'nantaraṃ yuktaḥ yasyedānīṃ saṃbahulāni tasya kathaṃ tadvipākapratisaṃvedanā
# gang gi mtshams med pa gcig nyid ni de'i rnam par smin pa de de ma thag par rigs na / / de gang gi mang po gang yin pa de'i de dag gi rnam par smin pa ji ltar myong bar 'gyur zhe na /
sarveṣāṃ yugapadvipākaḥ pratisaṃvidyate tathāhyanekānantaryakāriṇa āśrayaḥ sukumārataro nirvartate kāraṇāśca bahutīvravicitrā yadvaśādbhūyasīṃ vedanāṃ pratyanubhavati
# thams cad kyi rnam par smin pa gcig car myong bar 'gyur te / / 'di ltar mtshams med pa du ma byed pa'i lus shin tu gzhon par mngon par 'grub la / / chad pa yang mang zhing mi zad pa sna tshogs 'byung ste / / de'i dbang gis tshor ba shin tu mang po 'byung bar 'gyur ro /
ārambhaṃ ca pratyetāni dṛṣṭadharmavedanīyādīni vyavasthāpyante na tanmātravedanīyatāmadhikṛtya / yasya tatraiva janmani vipāko vipaktumārabhate taddṛṣṭadharmavedanīyam
# rtsom pa'i dbang du byas nas mthong ba'i chos la myong bar 'gyur ba la sogs pa 'di dag rnam par gzhag gi / / de tsam la myong bar 'gyur ba'i dbang du byas pa ni ma yin no / / tshe de nyid la gang gis rnam par smin pa rnam par smin par rtsom pa de ni mthong ba'i chos la myong bar 'gyur ba'o /
yasyānantare janmanyārabhate tadupapadyavedanīyam
# gang de ma thag ba'i tshe la rtsom pa de ni skyes nas myong bar 'gyur ba'o /
yasyānantaraṃ janma laghayitvārabhate tadaparaparyāyavedanīyamityevaṃ ca kṛtvā hācittāvadāne "ānantaryasya karmaṇo narake punaḥpunaścyutyupapādena vipākapratisaṃvedanam" anulomitaṃ bhavatīti
# gang de ma thag tu 'byung ba'i tshe thal nas rtsom pa de ni lan grangs gzhan la myong bar 'gyur ba ste / / de ltar byas na kyi hud sems zhes bya ba'i rtogs pa brjod pa las mtshams med pa'i las kyi rnams par smin pas sems can dmyal bar yang dang yang 'chi 'pho zhing skye bas rnam par smin pas myong ngo zhes 'byung ba dang mthun par byas pa yin no /
kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇavipākaṃ karmākuśalam kliṣṭatvādaniṣṭavipākatvācca
# gnag la rnam par smin pa gnag pa'i las ni mi dge ba ste / / nyon mongs pa can dang rnam par smin pa mi 'dod pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
viparyayācchuklaṃ śuklavipākaṃ traidhātukaṃ kuśalam
# bzlog pa ni dkar la rnam par smin pa dkar ba ste / / khams gsum pa'i dge ba'o /
kṛṣṇaśuklaṃ kṛṣṇaśuklavipākaṃ yatkāmapratisaṃyuktaṃ vipākaṃ vyāmiśraṃ kuśalākuśalamityarthaḥ
# dkar gnag tu gyur la rnam par smin pa dkar gnag tu gyur pa ni gang 'dod pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i 'dres ma ste / / dge mi dge zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
kathamekaṃ kuśalaṃ bhavatyakuśalaṃ ca
# gcig na ci ltar dge bar yang 'gyur la mi dge bar 'gyur zhe na /
nātra pravṛttikṣaṇanaiyamyenocyate tadevobhayamityapi tu sahāśayaprayogeṇaikaṃ karmetyayamatrābhi saṃdhirvedivyaḥ / tayośca kṛṣṇaśuklatāṃ pratyanyonyāsādṛśye satyekaṃ karma kṛṣṇaśuklaṃ vyavasthāpyate
# di la 'jug pa'i skad cig nges par de gnyi ga brjod pa ni ma yin gyi / / bsam pa dang ldan cig pa'i sbyor ba las gcig ces bya ste / / 'di ni 'dir dgongs pa yin par rig par bya'o / / de gnyis nag po dang dkar po nyid du phan tshun 'dra bar gyur pas nag po dang dkar po las gcig tu rnam par gzhag go /
tatrāśayataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ prayogataḥ śuklaṃ yathāpi kaścitparān vañcayitukāmasteṣāṃ saṃpratyayananimittaṃ bhāvena dānāni dadāti yāvatpravrajatyapi
# de la bsam pa gnag la sbyor ba dkar ba ni dper na 'ga' zhig gzhan dag la slu bar 'dod nas de dag yid ches par bya ba'i mtshan mar bsam pas sbyin pa rnams sbyin pa nas rab tu 'byung ba'i bar du'o /
prayogataḥ kṛṣṇamāśayataḥ śuklaṃ yathāpi kaścitputraṃ vā śiṣyaṃ vāhitānnivārayitukāmo hite ca niyojayitukāmo 'nukampācittaḥ kāyena vācā vā paruṣayā tasminkāle saṃkliśyate
# sbyor ba gnag la bsam pa dkar ba ni dper na 'ga' zhig bu 'am slob ma la mi phan pa bzlog par 'dod cing phan pa la sbyor bar 'dod nas / / snying brtse ba'i sems kyis lus dang ngag gis drag tu byed pa de'i tshe / / kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ro / / mi gnag cig dkar la rnam par smin par mi 'gyur zhing las zad par 'gyur ba'i las gang zhe na /
akṛṣṇaśuklāvipākaṃ karma karmakṣayāya saṃvartate prayogānantaryamārgeṣvanāsravaṃ karmaprayogamārgānantaryamārgāṇāṃ prahāṇapratipakṣatvāt
# sbyor ba dang ba chad med pa'i lam rnams la zag pa med pa'i las zhes bya ba la / / sbyor ba dang bar chad med pa'i lam rnams ni spong ba'i gnyen po yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatrākṛṣṇaṃ kleśamalābhāvāt
# de la mi gnag pa ni nyon mongs pa'i dri ma med pa'i phyir ro /
śuklamekāntavyavadānatvāt
# dkar ba ni gcig tu rnam pa byang ba'i phyir ro /
avipākaṃ saṃsāravirodhitvāt
# rnam par smin par mi 'gyur ba ni /
karmakṣayāya saṃvartate 'syaiva kṛṣṇādikasya trividhasya sāsravasya karmaṇastenānāsraveṇa karmaṇā vipākadānavāsanāsamudghātāt / aviśeṣeṇa ca sarvasyānāsravasya karmaṇaḥ paripanthamānukūlyaṃ svabhāvamadhikṛtya vaṃkadoṣakaṣāyāṇāṃ śauceyānāṃ mauneyānāṃ ca yathākramaṃ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam / tatra vaṃkamṛjukamārgasyāṣṭāṅgasyotpattyāvaraṇabhūtaṃ kāyavāṅmanaḥkarma
# 'khor ba dang mi mthun pa'i phyir ro / / las zad par 'gyur ba ni nag po la sogs pa zag pa dang bcas pa'i las rnam pa gsum po 'di nyid zag pa med pa'i lam des rnam par smin pa 'byin pa'i bag chags legs par bcom pa'i phyir ro / / bye brag med par zag pa med pa'i las 'di thams cad kyi bar du gcod pa dang rjes su mthun pa dang ngo bo nyid kyi dbang du byas nas yon po dang nyes pa dang rnyog pa dang btsang ba dang thub pa rnams go rims bzhin du rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o / / de la yon po ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las drang po'i lam 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa 'byung ba'i sgrib par gyur pa'o /
doṣo yena kāyādikarmaṇā dūṣite saṃtāne tattādṛśamāvaraṇabhūtaṃ karmotpadyate
# nyes pa ni lus la sogs pa'i las gang gis rnam par sun phyung ba'i sems kyi rgyud la de dang 'dra ba'i sgrib par gyur pa'i las 'byung ngo /
kaṣāyāḥ tīrthikadṛṣṭisaṃniśritaṃ kāyādi karma buddhaśāsanaprasādavipakṣeṇāśraddhyakāluṣyaparigṛhītatvāt / aparaḥ paryāyaḥ śāśvatocchedānupatitaṃ madhyamāpratipadvirodhārthena vaṃkam
# rnyog pa ni mu stegs can gyi lta ba la brten pa'i lus la sogs pa'i las gang yin pa ste / / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la dad pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma dad pa'i rnyog pas yongs su zin pa'i phyir ro / / rnams grangs gzhan du na / / rtag pa dang chad pa'i mthar lhung ba ste / / dbu ma'i lam dang mi mthun pa'i phyir yon po'o /
apavādadṛṣṭiparigṛhītaṃ vyavadānavyavasthānapradveṣārthena doṣaḥ
# skur ba'i lta bas yongs su bzung ste rnam par byang ba rnam par gzhag pa la rab tu zhe sdang ba'i phyir nyes pa'o /
satkāyadṛṣṭiparigṛhītaṃ nairātmyatattvadarśanaprativaddhārthena kaṣāya iti
# 'jig tshogs la lta bas yongs su bzung ste / / bdag med pa'i de kho na la lta ba'i bar du gcod pa'i phyir rnyog pa zhes bya'o /
śauceyāni suviśuddhaśīlasaṃgṛhītamṛjudṛṣṭisaṃgṛhītaṃ ca yatkāyavāṅmanaḥkarma śīladṛṣṭivipattimalavarjitatvāt
# gtsang ba ni shin tu rnam par dag pa'i tshul khrims kyis yongs su zin pa dang lta ba drang pos yongs su zin pa'i lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las gang yin pa ste / / tshul khrims dang lta ba la log par zhugs pa'i dri ma spangs pa'i phyir ro /
mauneyāni śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ yadanāsravaṃ kāyavāṅmanaḥkarma munīnāṃ tatkarmeti kṛtvā
# thub pa ba ni gang slob pa dang mi slob pa rnams kyi lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las zag pa med pa ste / / de thub pa rnams kyi las yin pa'i phyir ro /
dānasaṃpadamadhikṛtya dānaṃ dātā bhaviṣyatītyanenābhīkṣṇadānatāṃ darśayati tacchīlatayā punaḥ punardānāt / śramaṇebhyo brāhmaṇebhya ityevamādināpakṣapātadānatām aviśeṣeṇa sarvārthibhyo dānāta
# sbyin pa phun sum tshogs pa'i dbang du byas nas sbyin pa por 'gyur ro zhes bya ba 'dis ni phyir zhing sbyin pa ston te / / de'i dang tshul can du gyur pas yang dang yang sbyin ba'i phyir ro / / dge sbyong rnams dang bram ze rnams la zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni phyogs mi 'byed par sbyin pa ston te / / 'dod pa thams cad la bye brag med par sbyin pa'i phyir ro / / bza' ba dang btung ba zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni /
annapānamityevamādinecchāparipūraṇadānatām yathābhiprāyaṃ sarvopakaraṇavastuparityāgāt
# 'dod pa yongs su rdzogs par sbyin pa ston te / / bsam ba ji lta ba bzhin du yo byad kyi dngos po thams cad yongs su gtong ba'i phyir ro /
muktatyāgaḥ pratatapāṇirvyavasargarato yāyajūkastyāgasaṃpanno dānasaṃvibhāgarata ityebhiḥ padairyathākramamaniśritadānatādayo veditavyāḥ
# lhug par gtong ba dang lag brkyang ba dang gtong ba la dga' ba dang mchod sbyin byed pa'i dang tshul can dang gtong ba phun sum tshogs pa dang sbyin pa legs par 'ged pa la dga' ba zhes bya'i tshig 'di dag ni mi gnas par sbyin pa la sogs pa dang go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o /
aniśritadānatā punarbhavabhogāpariṇāmitatvena veditavyā
# mi gnas pa'i sbyin pa ni srid pa dang longs spyod kyi phyir yongs su mi bsngo ba nyid du rig par bya'o /
deyasaṃpadamadhikṛtyotthānavīryādhigatairityanenānabhidrugdhadeyavastutāṃ darśayati
# sbyin par bya ba phun sum tshogs pa'i dbang du byas nas ldang ba'i brtson 'grus kyis thob pa zhes bya ba 'dis ni sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po gnod pas grub pa ma yin pa ston te /
abhidrugdhaṃ hyanutthānabīryādhigataṃ bhavati svasthāne sthitvā paranikṣepāpalapanena pratilabdhatvāt
# gnod pas grub pa ni ldang ba'i brtson 'grus kyis thob pa ma yin te / / rang gi gnas na 'dug cing gzhan gyis bcol ba bsnyon pas thob pa'i phyir ro /
bāhubalopārjitairityanenāparāpahṛtadeyavastutām / parebhyo hyapahṛtaṃ na bāhubalopārjitaṃ bhavati taiḥ kṛcchreṇa vividhairūpāyairarjitasyāpaharaṇāt
# lag dar ba'i mthus bsgrubs pa zhes bya ba 'dis ni sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po gzhan las phrogs pa ma yin pa ston to / / gzhan las phrogs pa ni lag dar ba'i mthus bsgrubs pa ma yin te / / de dag gi sha thang bar thabs sna tshogs kyis bsgrubs pa phrogs pa'i phyir ro /
svedamalāpakṣiptairityanenākuthitavimaladeyavastutām svedamalābhyāmapakṣiptatvādujjhitatvādityarthaḥ
# rdul dang dri mas ma phog pa zhes bya ba 'dis ni sbyin par bya ba'i dngos pa ma rul cing dri ma med pa ston te / / rdul dang dri mas mas ma phog pa zhes bya ba ni spangs zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
dhārmikairityanena kalpikadeyavastutām śastraviṣamadyādyakalpikavastuvivarjitatvāt
# chos dang mthun pa zhes bya ba 'dis ni sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po rung ba ston te / / mtshon dang dug dang chang la sogs pa rung ba ma yin pa'i dngos po yongs su spangs pa'i phyir /
dharmalabdhairityanena dharmārjitadeyavastutāṃ darśayati tulākūlādimithyājīva parivarjanenopārjitatvāt
# chos kyis thob pa zhes bya ba 'dis ni sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po chos kyis bsgrub pa ston te / / gzhal bal g yo 'jug pa la sogs pa dang log pas 'tsho ba la sogs pa yongs su spangs nas bsgrubs pa'i phyir ro /
śīlaṃ samādāyākhaṇḍanena tadyogācchīlavān bhavati
# tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas ma nyams pas de dang ldan pa'i phyir tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin no /
mokṣaṃ prati yaḥ saṃvaraḥ sa prātimokṣasaṃvaraḥ
# thar pa'i phyir sdom pa gang yin pa de ni so sor thar pa'i sdom pa ste /
sa hi saṃsārānniryāṇāya bhavati
# de ni 'khor ba las 'byung bar 'gyur pa yin no /
ācārasaṃpannaḥ sadbhiragarhiteryāpathāditvāt
# cho ga phun sum tshogs pa ni spyod lam la sogs pa dam pa rnams kyis ma smad pa'i phyir ro /
gocarasaṃpannaḥ pañcāgocaraparivarjanāt
# spyod yul phun sum tshogs pa ni spyod yul ma yin pa lnga spangs pa'i phyir te /
pañca bhikṣoragocarāḥ ghoṣo veśaḥ pānāgāraṃ rājakulaṃ caṇḍālakaṭhinameva pañcamam
# dge slong gi spyod yul ma yin pa lnga ni gsod pa'i sa dang smad 'tshong gi gnas dang chang 'tshong gi khyim dang rgyal po'i pho brang dang gdol ba'i khyim ste lnga pa'o /
prajñaptisāvadyeṣvapi prakṛtisāvadyeṣviva tīvreṇa gauraveṇa śikṣaṇādaṇumātreṣvavadyeṣu bhayadarśī bhavati
# bcas pa'i kha na ma tho ba rnams dang rang bzhin gyi kha na mtho ba rnams la yang bsam pha drag pos bslab pas kha na ma thob chung du tsam rnams la yang 'jigs par lta ba yin no /
samantāt paripūrṇa śikṣāmādāya śikṣate śikṣāpadeṣvityucyate
# kun nas yongs su rdzogs par bslab pa rnams blangs nas slob pa'i phyir yang dag par blangs te bslab pa'i gzhi rnams la slob ces bya'o /
ataḥ paraṃ śīlamārabhya yadbhagavatā sūtrāntareṣu nirdiṣṭaṃ kāyena saṃvṛto bhavatītyevamādi tasyārtha ucyate
# 'di man chad du ni tshul khrims las brtsams nas / / bcom ldan 'das kyis mdo sde gzhan dag las lus dang ngag bsdams pa yin no zhes bya ba la sogs pa gang bstan ba de'i don brjod par bya'o /
tatra kāyena vācā saṃvṛto bhavati saṃprajanyaparigṛhītatayā yathanujñātamabhikramapratikramādiṣu buddhipūrvaṃ samyagvartanāt
# de la lus dang ngag gi bsdams pa yin pa ni shes bzhin gyis yongs su zin pa'i yin pa'i phyir te / / ji ltar bka' stsal pa bzhin du 'gro ba dang ldog pa la sogs pa la blo sngon du btang nas legs par bsgrubs pa'i phyir ro /
kāyavāksaṃpattyā saṃpannaḥ āpattyanadhyāpannatayā śīlāvipādanāt
# lus dang ngag phun sum tshogs pas phun sum tshogs pa ni ltung ba mi byed pa'i phyir te / / tshul khrims chud mi gson pa'i phyir ro /
pariśuddhakāyavākasamudācāraḥ samādhisaṃniśrayatayā samādhibalena dauḥśīlyamaladūrīkaraṇāt
# lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa yongs su dag pa ni ting nge 'dzin la gnas pa'i phyir te / / ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs kyis 'tshal ba'i tshul khrims kyi dri ma thag bsring pa'i phyir te /
kuśalakāyavāksamudācāraḥ kliṣṭavitarkāvyavakīrṇatayaikāntaśubhatvāt
# lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa dge ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi rtog pa dang ma 'dres pa'i phyir te / / gcig tu dge ba'i phyir ro /
anavadyakāyavāksamudācāro bhavabhogāpariṇāmitatvena sadbhiḥ praśastatvāt
# lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa kha na ma tho ba med pa ni srid pa dang longs spyod kyi phyir yongs su mi bsngo bas dam pa rnams kyis bsngags pa'i phyir ro /
avyābadhyakāyavāksamudācāra ātmotkarṣaṇādibhiḥ pareṣāmavajñāduḥkhasaṃvāsenāghaṭṭanāt
# lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa gnod pa med pa ni bdag la bstod pa la sogs pas gzhan dag khyad du gsod cing 'grogs na mi bde bas zher 'debs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
ānulomikakāyavāksamudācāro nirvāṇānuprāptyanukūlatayāryamārgāvāhanāt / anucchavikakāyavāksamudācāraḥ svadoṣaguṇāviṣkambhaṇachādanārtham / aupayikakāyavāksamudācāraḥ sabrahmacāryupagrahaṇaśīlatayopagamanārhatvāt
# lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa rjes su mthun pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa thob par byed pa dang mthun pa'i phyir te / / 'phags pa'i lam 'dren pa'i phyir ro / / lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa rjes su 'byor ba ni rang gi nyes pa dang yon tan sgrogs pa dang mi spyoms pa'i phyir ro / / lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa thabs dang ldan pa ni tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa nye bar sdud pa'i tshul khrims yin pa'i phyir te / / nye bar 'gro bar bya ba'i 'os yin pa'i phyir ro /
pratirūpakāyavāksamudācāro guruṣu gurusthānīyeṣu ca nihitamānatayā yathārhamupacaraṇāt
# lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa 'tsham ba ni bla ma rnams dang bla ma dang 'dra ba rnams la nga rgyal bcag pa'i phyir te / / ci rigs su bsnyen bkur byed pa'i phyir ro /
pradakṣiṇakāyavāksamudācāro 'vavāde pradakṣiṇagrāhitayāsvayaṃdṛṣṭiparāmarśatvāt / ataptakāyavāksamudācāraḥ kaṣṭatapolūhādhimuktivivarjitatayānātmatapatvāt
# lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa mthun pa ni gdams ngag la mthun par 'dzin pa'i phyir te / / rang gi lta ba la mchog tu 'dzin pa med pa'i phyir ro / / lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa gdung ba med pa ni dka' thub drag po dang ngan don la mos pa spangs pa'i phyir te /
ananutāpyakāyavāksamudācāraḥ samutsṛṣṭān bhogān karmāntāṃścārabhyāvipratisāritayā paścāttāpābhāvāt / avipratisārakāyavāksamudācāraḥ kuśalapakṣamārabhyālpamātreṇāsaṃtuṣṭasyā vipratisāritayā yāvacchakyaṃ saṃpādanāt
# bdag la gdung bar mi byed pa'i phyir ro / / lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa phyis 'gyod pa med pa ni longs spyod pa rnams dang las kyi mtha' rnams spang pa la brtsams nas 'gyod pa med pa'i phyir te / / phyis 'gyod pa med pa'i phyir ro / / lus dang ngag gi kun tu spyod pa yid la gcags pa med pa ni dge ba'i phyogs la brtsams nas cung zad tsam gyis chog par mi 'dzin pa'i yid la gcags pa med ba'i phyir te / / bsgrub nus pa'i bar du'o /
karma svakameṣāṃ ta ime karmasvakāḥ
# 'di dag gi las ni bdag gir bya ba yin pas 'di dag ni las bdag gir bya ba dag go /
kathaṃ punasteṣāṃ karma svakaṃ bhavati
# de dag gi las bdag gir bya ba ji lta bu yin zhe na /
svayaṃkṛtakarmavipākapratisaṃvedanatāmupādāya taddhi nāma svakamityucyate yatparairasādhāraṇamiti
# rang gis byas pa'i las kyi rnam par smin pa myong ba'i phyir te / / gang gzhan dag dang thun mong ma yin pa de ni bdag gi zhes bya'o /
karmāṇi dāyāya eṣāṃ ta ime karmadāyādāḥ / kathaṃ karmaṇāṃ dāyādatvam
# 'di dag ni las kyi bgo skal la spyod pa yin pas 'di dag ni las kyi bsgo skal la spyod pa dag go / / ji ltar na las kyi bgo skal la spyod pa nyid yin zhe na /
tasyāṃ svayaṃkṛtavipākapratisaṃvedanāyāṃ kuśalākuśalānāṃ karmaṇāmanyonyadāyādatāmupādāya yathāsvamiṣṭāniṣṭaphalasaṃvibhajanāt
# rang gis byas pa'i las kyi rnams par smin pa myong ba de la dge ba dang mi dge ba so so'i bgo skal la spyod pa'i phyir te / / 'di lta ste /
te punaḥ svakṛtakarmeṣṭāniṣṭavipākapratisaṃvedinaḥ sattvāḥ kuta āditaḥ saṃbhūtāḥ kimahetukā āhosvit prakṛtīśvarādihetukā ityāha karmayonīyāḥ / karmeveṣāmahetuviṣamahetuvarjito yoniḥ sattvānāṃ saṃbhavāyetyarthaḥ / evaṃ tāvatpravṛttimārabhya nivṛttimapyārabhya karmapratisaraṇāḥ sāsravakarmaprahāṇāyānāsravakarmasaṃśrayaṇāt karmaivaiṣāṃ pratisaraṇaṃ bhavatīti
