# rang rang gi 'bras bu 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa 'ged pa'i phyir ro / / rang gis byas pa'i las la 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa dag gi rnam par smin pa myong ba'i sems can de dag thog ma ga las byung / / ci rgyu med pa las byung ba zhig gam / / 'on te rang bzhin dang dbang phyug la sogs pa'i rgyu las byung ba zhig ce na / / smras pa / / las kyi skyes gnas la dgag go / / 'di dag gi las nyid rgyu med pa dang mi mthun pa'i rgyu rnams par spangs pa'i skyes gnas te / / sems can rnams 'byung ba'i phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de ltar 'jug pa las kyang brtsams ldog pa las kyang brtsams nas las bstan par bya ba dag ste / / zag pa dang bcas pa'i las spang ba'i phyir zag pa med pa'i las rten yin pas / / 'di dag gi brten par bya ba ni las nyid yin no /
yaduktamacintyaḥ sattvānāṃ karmavipāka iti na sarvaiḥ prakāraiḥ a sāvacintyo veditavyaḥ
# sems can rnams kyi las kyi rnam par smin pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o zhes gang gsungs pa de ni rnam pa thams cad du bsam gyis mi khyab pa yin par rig par bya'o /
kathaṃ tarhi cintyaḥ kathamacintyaḥ
# bsam gyis mi khyab pa ni ji lta bu zhe na /
kuśalākuśalasyeṣṭāniṣṭo vipākaḥ sugatidurgatyoriti cintyaḥ śakyatvāt samyagdṛṣṭyādiguṇāvāhanācca
# dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rnam par smin pa bde 'gro dang ngan 'gror 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa zhes bya ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa ste / / nus pa dang yang dag pa'i lta ba la sogs pa'i yon tan khyad par can 'dren pa'i phyir ro /
anena karmaṇā sattvānāmātmabhāvasya varṇasaṃsthānādiprakārabhedavaicitryamityacintyaḥ aśakyatvāt sarvajñādanyasyonmādādidoṣābāhanācca
# las 'dis sems can rnams kyi lus kyi kha dog dang dbyibs la sogs pa rnams pa tha dad pa sna tshogs zhes bya ba ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa ste / / mi nus pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid las gzhan pa mgo rmongs pa la sogs pa'i nyes pa 'dren pa'i phyir ro /
tadeva karmasthānādibhiracintyam / tatra sthānaṃ yatra pradeśe sthitvā yatkarma kṛtvā grāme vā nagare vetyādi / vastu yadadhiṣṭhānaṃ sattvasaṃkhyātamasattvasaṃkhyātaṃ vā
# dge ba la sogs pa'i las de nyid gnas la sogs pa'i rab tu dbye bas ni bsam gyis mi khyab bo / / de la gnas ni grong ngam grong khyer gyi phyogs gang du gnas nas las de byas zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / dngos po ni sems can gyi grangs su gtogs pa'am / / sems can ma yin pa'i grongs su gtogs pa gang la brten te byas pa'o /
hetuḥ kuśalākuśalādeḥ kuśalākuśalamūlāniyathāyogam / vipākastadevātmabhāvavaicitryam
# rgyu ni dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams te / / ji ltar mthun mthun sbyar ro / / rnam par smin pa ni lus sna tshogs pa de nyid do /
bāhyabhāvavaicitryābhinirvartakaṃ karmācintyam kīdṛśena khalu karmaṇā kaṇṭakādīnāṃ taikṣṇādikaṃ kṛtamiti lokacintā nantarbhūtatvāt / maṇimantrauṣadhimuṣṭiyogapratisaṃyuktaṃ karmācintyam / tatra maṇipratisaṃyuktaṃ candrakāntādīnāmudakakṣaraṇādi
# sna tshogs mngon par 'grub par byed pa'i las bsam gyis mi khyab pa ni las ci 'dra bas tsher ma la sogs pa'i rno ba la sogs pa byas pa ste / / 'jig rten gyis bsam par gtogs pa'i phyir ro / / nor bu dang sngas dang sman dang mkhyud spyod dang ldan pa'i las bsam gyis mi khyab ste / / de la nor bu dang ldan pa ni chu shel la sogs pa las chu 'byung ba la sogs pa'o /
mantrapratisaṃyuktaṃ tadabhimantritānāmadāhādi
# sngags dang ldan pa ni sngags de dag gis btab pa mi 'tshig pa la sogs pa'o /
auṣadhipratisaṃyuktaṃ tayā gṛhītayānturdhātādi
# sman dang ldan pa ni des zin na mi snang bar 'gyur ba la sogs pa'o /
muṣṭiyogapratisaṃyuktaṃ tena tena muṣṭiyogena jvarāpagamādi
# mkhyud spyad dang ldan pa ni mkhyud spyad de dang des rims nad dang 'bral bar 'gyur ba la sogs pa'o /
sarva ca yogināṃ prabhāvakarmācintyam / katham
# rnal 'byor pa thams cad kyi mthu'i las bsam gyis mi khyab pa ji lta bu zhe na /
te cittaprabhāvena mahāpṛthivī kampayantyākāśena votpatantītyevamādi
# de dag gi sems kyi mthus sa chen po g yo bar byed pa'am / / nam mkha' la 'phur ba la sogs pa'o /
bodhisattvānāṃ vaśitābhiryat kriyate karma tadacintyam / tadyathā āyurvaśitayā bodhisattvā āyuḥsaṃskārānadhiṣṭhā ya yāvadicchanti tiṣṭhanti
# byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang gi las la sogs pas las gang byed pa de bsam gyis mi khyab pa ni 'di lta ste / / tshe la dbang ba sa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs nas ji srid 'dod pa de srid du gnas so /
cittavaśitayā yathecchaṃ samādhīn samāpadyante pariṣkāravaśitayāprameyamanardheyamupakaraṇavarṣa sattvānāṃ varṣanti / karmavaśitayānyadhātu bhūmigatiyonyavasthāvedanīyāni karmāṇyanyathā pariṇāmayanti / upapattivaśitayā dhyānairapi vihṛtyāparihīṇā eva kāmadhātāvupapadyante
# sems la dbang ni ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par 'jug go / / yo byang la dbang bas ni sems can thams cad la yo byad rin che ba dang dpag tu med pa'i char 'bebs so / / las la dbang bas ni khams dang sa dang 'gro ba dang skye gnas dang gnas skabs gzhan na myang bar 'gyur ba'i las rnams gzhan du bsgyur ro / / skye ba la dbang bas ni bsam gtan la gnas shing yongs su ma nyams bzhin du 'dod pa'i khams su skye'o /
adhimuktivaśitayā pṛthavyādīnavāditvenādhimucyante
# mos pa la dbang bas ni sa la sogs par chu la sogs par mos so /
praṇidhānavaśitayā yatheṣṭaṃ svaparārthasaṃpattikarāṇyasaṃkhyeyāni mahāpraṇidhānānyabhinirharanti
# smon lam la dbang bas ni ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du bdag dang gzhan gyi don phun sum tshogs par byed pa'i smon lam rgya chen po grangs med pa mngon par sgrub bo /
ṛddhivaśitayā sattvānāmāvaja nārthamaprameyamṛddhipratihārya saṃdarśayanti
# rdzu 'phrul la dbang bas ni sems can rnams 'dun par bya ba'i phyir rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul dpag tu med pa kun tu ston ston to /
jñānavaśitayā dharmārthaniruktipratibhānānāṃ prakarṣaparyantaṃ gacchanti
# ye shes la dbang bas ni chos dang don dang nges pa'i tshig dang spobs pa rnams kyis rab kyi mthar phyin par 'gro'o /
dharmavaśitayā yathārhaṃ yāvat sarvasatvānāmanyānyairnāmapadavyaṃjanakāryaḥ sūtrādīn dharmān vyavasthāpya yugapaccittaparitoṣaṇe samarthā bhavantīti
# chos la dbang bas ni ci rigs par ji tsam du sems can thams cad la ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs gzhan dang gzhan dag gis mdo la sogs pa'i chos rnam par bzhag nas cig car du sems yongs su tshim par byed nus par 'gyur ro /
buddhānāṃ buddhakṛtyānuṣṭhānakarmācintyam / katham
# sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bsgrub pa'i 'phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab pa ji lta bu zhe na /
anābhogapratigatā dharmadhātvekarasatāprāptā sarve buddhā bhagavantaḥ sattvānāṃ yathā yadā yāvatkṛtyamanuṣṭhātavyaṃ tatsarvamanutiṣṭhanti evaṃ buddhānāṃ buddhaviṣayo 'cintyaḥ
# sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad lhun gyis grub par gtogs par thugs su chud cing chos kyi dbyings rog cig pa nyid du gyur nas sems can rnams la gang gi tshe dang ji lta bu dang ji srid du mdzad pa bsgrub par bya ba de thams cad rjes su gnas te / / de ltar sangs rgyas rnams kyi yul bsam gyis mi khyab bo /
punarbhavasya vāsanāyā āhārakaṃ kāraṇamiti hetuḥ
# yang srid pa'i bag chags 'jog pa'i byed rgyu zhes bya ba ni rgyu'o /
upacitavāsanānāṃ sattvanāṃ devādisatvanikāye tadākṛtiprakṛtisādṛśyena samasyodayasya kāraṇamiti samudayam / pratyātmaṃsaṃtānanaiyabhyena gatiyonyādisarvaprakāraiḥ prakarṣeṇa yāvadbhavāgragatasyodbhavasya kāraṇamiti prabhavaḥ
# sems can bag chags bsags pa rnam pa lha la sogs pa'i sems can gyi ris su de'i cha byad dang rang bzhin dang 'dra bar mthun par 'byung ba'i byed rgyu zhes bya ba ni kun 'byung ba'o / / so so rang gi rgyud nges pa dang 'gro ba dang skye gnas la sogs pa rnams dang mchog tu 'byung bas srid pa'i rtse mo'i 'gro ba'i bar du 'byung ba'i byed rgyu zhes bya ba ni rab tu skye ba'o /
apūrvasyānyasyātmabhāvasya prāptau pūrvātmabhāvātyayena kāraṇamiti pratyayaḥ / saṃskārāṇāmuparamātsa nirodho 'nyaḥ syāttadasaṃvadhyamāno 'rthāntarabhūtaḥ syāt
# sngon ma byung ba'i lus gzhan dang gzhan 'thob pa dang sngon 'thob pa'i lus 'da' ba'i byed rgyu zhes bya ba ni rkyen to / / 'du byed de dag gi 'jig pa las 'gog pa de dag gzhan zhig yin na ni 'brel ba med de don gzhan du 'gyur ro /
athānanyaḥ syātsaṃkleśalakṣaṇaḥ syāt
# ji ste gzhan ma yin na ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i mtshan nyid du 'gyur te /
ata eva nobhayo nānubhayaśca / prapañcaḥ punarasminnarthe 'yoniśaścintyetyamārgeṇānyāyenānayena cintyetyarthaḥ anyathā cintayitavye 'nyathācintanāt
# de'i phyir gnyi ga yang ma yin / / gnyi ga yin pa yang ma yin no / / spros pa ni skabs 'dir tshul bzhin ma yin par sems pa yin te zhes bya ba ni lam ma yin pa dang / / rigs ma yin pa dang thabs ma yin par sems pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / sems pa yang gzhan las sems par bya ba yang gzhan pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ punaścintyaḥ
# sems pa ji lta bu zhe na /
śāntaḥ praṇīta ityevamādibhiḥ prakāraiḥ
# zhi ba dang gya nom pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis so; /
niralaṃkāraḥ prajñāviktānāṃ vidyādivaiśeṣikaguṇālaṃkārābhāvāt / paryāyato 'śeṣaprahāṇamityuddeśaḥ śeṣo nirdeśaḥ
# rgyan med pa ni shes rab kyi cha las rnam par grol ba rnams kyi yon tan khyad par can rigs pa la sogs pa'i rgyan med pa'i rgyan med pa'i phyir ro / / rnam grangs kyi sa ni ma lus par spangs pa zhes bya ba ni bstan pa'o /
ata eva tatpariśiṣṭāni padānyupādāyetyucyate taistasya nirdeśāt / kathaṃ kṛtvāśeṣa prahāṇam
# lhag ma ni bshad pa'o / / de'i phyir de'i tshig lhag ma rnams kyis phyir ro zhes brjod de; de dag gi de bshad pa'i phyir ro / / ji ltar byas na ma lus par spangs she na /
paryavasthānānuśayaprahāṇāt
# kun nas dkris pa dang bag la nyal spangs pa'i phyir ro /
tatra pratiniḥsargaḥ paryavasthānaprahāṇamadhikṛtya utpannasya parivarjanāt
# de la nges par spangs pa ni kun nas dkris pa'i dbang du byas pa ste / / 'byung ba yongs su spangs pa'i phyir ro /
vyantībhāvo 'nuśayaprahāṇam mūlābhāve 'tyantamanutpādāt
# byang bar gyur pa ni bag la nyal spangs pa ste / / rtsa ba med na gtan mi skye ba'i phyir ro /
tatpunardarśanabhāvanāmārgapratipakṣabhedāddvidhā vyavasthāpyate kṣayo virāga iti
# de ni gnyen po mthong ba dang bsgom pa'i lam gyi bye brag gis rnam pa gnyis su rnam par gzhag ste / / zad pa dang 'dod chags dang bral zhes bya ba'o /
tatra darśanamārgeṇa virāgatāmadhikṛtya kṣayaḥ alpamātrāvaśiṣṭatvāt kleśarāśeḥ
# de la zad pa ni mthong ba'i lam gyis bral ba nyid kyi dbang du byas pa ste / / nyon mongs pa'i tshogs cung zad tsam zhig lus pa'i phyir ro /
bhāvanāmārgeṇa virāgaḥ tasya bhūmivairāgyagamanapravibhāvitatvāt
# 'dod chags dang bral ba ni bsgom pa'i lam gyis bral ba nyid kyi dbang du byas pa ste /
tadubhayavisaṃyoge punaḥ satyāyatyāṃ ca duḥkhaṃ nirudhyate anutpattidharmatāpādanāt / dṛṣṭe ca dharme daurmanasyaṃ vyupaśāmyati asamudācārāt
# de ni sa la 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid du 'gyur bas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro / / de gnyis kyis bral bar gyur na mi skye ba'i chos nyid du byas pas phyi ma la sdug bsngal 'gog pa dang kun du mi 'byung bas mthong ba'i chos la yid mi bde ba rnam par zhi bar 'gyur te /
atastatphalabhūtasya duḥkhasya prahāṇamadhikṛtyāha nirodho vyupaśama iti
# de'i phyir de'i 'bras bur gyur ba sdug bsngal rnam pa gnyis spong pa'i dbang du byas nas 'gog pa dang rnam par zhi bzhes bya ba smos so /
pūrvakarma kleśasamudāgatānāṃ tu sattvānāṃ svarasenaivoparamamadhikṛtyāha astaṃgama iti / evaṃ kṛtvāśeṣaprahāṇaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ veditavyam
# sngon gyi las dang nyon mongs pas yang dag par bsgrub pa'i phung po rnams ni rang gi ngang gis 'jig pa'i dbang du byas nas nub pa zhes bya'o / / de ltar byas na ma lus par spangs pa bstan par rig par bya'o /
asaṃskṛtamutpādavyayasthityanyathātvābhāvātsaṃskṛtaviparyayeṇa
# 'dus ma byas ni 'dus byas las bzlog pa ste / / skye ba dang 'jig pa dang gnas pa gzhan du 'gyur ba med pa'i phyir ro /
durdṛśamāryasyaivaikasya prajñā cakṣuṣo gocaratvāt
# blta dka' ba ni 'phags pa gcig pu'i shes rab kyi spyan gyi spyod yul yin pa'i phyir ro /
acalaṃ narakādigatyasaṃcāreṇa sthiratvāt
# g yo ba med pa ni sems can dmyal ba la sogs pa'i 'gro bar mi 'pho bas bstan pa'i phyir ro /
anataṃ kāmarūpārūpyatṛṣṇābhāvena bhaveṣvanamanāt
# mi 'dud pa ni 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i sred pa med pas srid par mi 'dud pa'i phyir ro /
amṛtaṃ maraṇāśrayaskandhābhāvāt
# 'chi ba med pa ni 'chi ba'i rten phung po med pa'i phyir ro /
anāsravamāsravābhāvāt / layanaṃ vimukti prītisukhasaṃniśrayatvāt
# zag pa med pa ni zag pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / gnas ni rnam par grol ba'i bde ba'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro /
dvīpaṃ saṃsāramahārṇave sthalabhūtatvāt / trāṇaṃ tatprāptau jātyādisarvopadravāpagamanāt
# gling ni 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho chen po la thang lta bur gyur pa'i phyir ro / / skyob pa ni de thob na skye ba la sogs pa'i gnod pa thams cad las bzlog pa'i phyir ro /
śaraṇaṃ tatkṛtāśayaprayogayoravandhatvasya padasthānatayāśrayaṇīyatvāt
# mgon ni de'i bsam pa dang sbyor ba byas pa 'bras bu yod pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin pas rten yin pa'i phyir ro /
parāyaṇaṃ paramasyāryatvasyāgamanāya padasthānatvādārhatyatvaprāptyupāyālaṃbanatvādityarthaḥ
# dpung gnyen ni 'phags pa'i mchog nyid du 'gro ba'i gzhi'i gnas yin pa'i phyir to / / dgra bcom pa nyid 'thob pa'i thabs la dmigs pa'i phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
acyutamajātatvena bhraṃsāsaṃbhavāt
# 'chi 'pho med pa ni ma skyes pas nyams pa med pa'i phyir ro /
nirjvaraṃ sarvecchāvighātasaṃtāpābhāvāt
# rims nad med pa ni 'dod pas phongs pa'i gdung ba thams cad med pa'i phyir ro /
niṣparidāhaṃ śokādisarvaparidāhapratiprasrabdhyā śītalatvāt / kṣemaṃ vyādhijarāmaraṇabhayarahitārya vihārāśrayatvāt
# yongs su gdung ba med pa ni mya ngan la sogs pa'i yongs su gdung ba thams cad rgyun chad pas bsil ba'i phyir ro / / bde ba ni na ba dang rga ba dang 'chi ba'i 'jigs sba dang bral bas 'phags pa'i gnas pa'i rten yin pa'i phyir ro /
śivaṃ sarvakuśaladharmāśrayatvāt
# zhi ba ni dge ba'i chos thams cad kyi gnas yin pa'i phyir ro /
sauvarṇakaṃ lokottarasukhavastutvāt
# bde gzhi ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bde ba'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro /
svastyayanaṃ sukhena prayogeṇa tatpprāptaye ālaṃbanabhavāt
# bde bar 'gyur ba ni sbyor ba bde bas de thob par 'gyur ba'i dmigs pa yod pa'i phyir ro /
ārogyaṃ kleśādyāvaraṇarogarahitatvāt
# nad med pa ni nyon mongs pa la sogs pa'i sgrib pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
āniñjyaṃ sarvaviṣayaprapañcavikṣeparahitatvāt / nirvāṇaṃ rūpādisaṃjñāpagamasya śāntasukhavihārasyālaṃbanatvāt
# mi g yo ba ni yul gyi spros pa'i rnam par g yeng ba thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / mya ngan las 'das pa ni gzugs la sogs pa'i 'du shes thams cad dang bral te zhi zhing bde bar gnas pa'i dmigs pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
punarnirodhasatyamārabhyājātādayaḥ paryāyāḥ duḥkhalakṣaṇaviparyayārthena veditavyāḥ / dukhaṃ hi tatra tatra sattvanikāye pratisaṃdhibandhena jāyate
# yang 'gog pa'i bden pa la brtsams nas / / ma skyes pa la sogs pa rnam grangs su gtogs pa rnams te / / sdug bsngal gyi mtshan nyid las bzlog par rig par bya'o /
tata uttarakālamātmabhāvaparipūryā vardhate
# sdug bsngal ni sems can gyi ris de dang der nyid mtshams sbyor bar byed pas skye ba'o /
tacca duḥkhaṃ pūrvakarmakleśāvedhena kṛtam
# de'i 'og tu lus yongs su rdzogs par 'phel lo /
tacca vartamānaṃ duḥkhaṃ karmakleśānāṃ cānyabhavasaṃskaraṇe padasthānaṃ bhavati
# sdug bsngal de yang sngon gyi las dang nyon mongs pas 'phangs te byas pa ni da ltar gyi las dang nyon mongs pa rnams kyis srid pa gzhan du byed pa'i gzhi'i gnas yin te /
tato 'vyucchedayogena punarbhavasya saṃtatyutpādo bhavati
# de'i rgyun mi 'chad pa'i tshul gyis yang srid pa'i rgyun skye bar 'gyur ro /
atastadviparyayeṇa duḥkhanirodha āryasatyaṃ yathākramamajātamabhūtamakṛtamasamutpannaṃ veditavyam
# de las bzlog pa ni sdug bsngal 'gog pa 'phags pa'i bden pa ste / / ma skyes pa dang ma byung ba dang ma byas pa dang 'dus ma byas pa dang skyes pa med pa dang go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o /
api khalu nirodhasatyamadhikṛtya / śāntalakṣaṇaṃ saṃskāraduḥkhatayāpraśāntalakṣaṇānāmupādānaskandhānāṃ visaṃyogamadhikṛtya / praṇītalakṣaṇaṃ kleśaduḥkhavisaṃyogāt svayaṃ śucisukhasvabhāvatāmadhikṛtya / niḥsaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ nityahitasvabhāvatāmadhikṛtya apunarāvartanāt kṣematvācca yathākramaṃ hitaṃ kuśalamiti śakyatvāt
# yang 'gog pa'i bden pa mtshan nyid rnam pa bzhir rig par bya ste / / 'gog pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'byung ba'i rgyu nyon mongs pa rnams dang bral ba'i dbang du byas pa'o / / zhi ba'i mtshan nyid ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal nyid kyis ma zhi ba'i mtshan nyid nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga rnams dang bral ba'i dbang du byas pa'o / / gya nom pa'i mtshan nyid ni nyon mongs pa dang sdug bsngal dang bral ba'i phyir / / bdag nyid gtsang ba dang bde ba'i ngo bo nyid kyi dbang du byas pa'o / / nges par 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid ni rtag pa dang phan pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi dbang du byas pa ste / / yang phyir mi ldog pa dang bde ba'i phyir phan pa dang bde ba dang go rims bzhin no /
mārgasatyaṃ yena dukhaṃ parijānīta ityevamādi satyeṣvasya kṛtyādhikāreṇa lakṣaṇanirdeśo veditavyaḥ
# lam gyi bden pa ni gang gis sdug bsngal gyi bden pa yongs su shes pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste / / bden pa rnams la 'di'i bya ba'i skabs kyis mtshan nyid bstan par rig par bya'o /
pañcavidho mārga iti prabhedādhikāreṇa / pañcaprabhedaḥ saparivāramārgasatyādhikārādveditavyam
# lam rnam pa lnga zhes bya ba ni rab tu dbye ba lnga'i skabs kyi'o / / rab tu dbye ba 'di yang lam gyi bden pa 'khor dang bcas pa'i skabs kyis rig par bya'o /
tatra saṃbhāramārgaḥ śīlādiko yasya paripūrṇatvāduṣmagatādyānupūrvyā satyadarśanāya tadāvaraṇaprahāṇāya ca saṃtānasya yogyatāṃ pratilabhata iti
# de la tshogs kyi lam ni tshul khrims la sogs pa ste / / de yongs su rdzogs pas dro bar gyur pa la sogs pa'i go rims kyis bden pa mthong bar bya ba dang de la sgrib pa spangs bar bya ba'i phyir sems kyi rgyud 'os su gyur pa 'thob bo /
yadvā punaranyadaupaniṣadaṃ kuśalamityavipratisārādikaṃ veditavyam
# gang yang rgyur gyur pa'i dge ba gzhan zhes bya ba ni 'gyod pa med pa la sogs par rig par bya'o /
uṣmagataṃ pratyātmaṃ satyeṣvālokalabdhaḥ samādhiḥ prajñā sasaṃyoga iti samāhitena cittena satyādhipateyasya sūtrādikasya dharmasya manojalpasya mukhairarthasaṃprakhyāne sati śamathaśca vipaśyanā coṣmagatamiti veditavyam
# dro bar gyur pa ni so so rang gis bden pa rnams la snang ba thob pa'i ting nge 'dzin shes rab dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'o zhes bya ba ni mnyam par gzhag pa'i sems kyis bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos mdo sde la sogs pa yid kyis brjod pa'i sgo nas don snang bar gyur pa'i zhi gnas dang lhag mthong ni dro bar gyur par rig par bya'o /
tadvṛddhirmūrdhānastadupari vyavasthāpanārthena
# de 'phel pa ni rtse mo ste / / de'i gang na rnam par gnas pa'i phyir ro /
kṣāntirekadeśapraviṣṭānusṛtaḥ samādhiriti
# bzod pa ni phyogs gcig la zhugs pa dang rjes su song ba'i ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba la /
kathamekadeśapraviṣṭo bhavati
# ji ltar na phyogs gcig la zhugs pa yin zhe na /
ekāntena grāhyabhāvalakṣaṇāt
# gcig tu gzung ba med par bzod pa'i phyir ro /
kathamekadeśānumṛtaḥ grāhakābhāvaprativedhānukūlyāvasthānāt
# ji ltar na phyogs gcig gi rjes su song ba yin zhe na / / 'dzin pa med par rtog pa'i rjes su mthun par gnas pa'i phyir ro /
laukiko 'gradharmo yadantaramādito lokottaro mārgaḥ / darśanamārgo laukikāgradharmānantaraṃ nirvikalpaśamathavipaśyanālakṣaṇo veditavyaḥ
# 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog ni gang gi 'og tu thog mar 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam mo / / mthong ba'i lam ni 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog gi 'og gi rnam par mi rtog pa'i zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gi mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o /
samasamālaṃbyālaṃbanajñānamapi taditi tena grāhya grāhakābhāvatathatāprativeghāt / pratyātmamapanīta sattvasaṃketadharmasaṃketa sarvato 'panītobhayasaṃketālaṃbanadharmajñānamapi taditi
# dmigs par bya ba dang dmigs par byed pa mnyam pas mnyam par shes pa'ang de bzhin te zhes bya ba ni des gzungs ba dang 'dzin pa med pa'i de bzhin nyid rtogs pa'i phyir ro / / so so rang la sems can gyi brda dang chos kyi brda gsal ba dang thams cad du gnyi ga'i brda gsal pa dmigs pa'i chos shes pa 'ang de yin no zhes bya ba la /
kathaṃ pratyātmamapanītasattvasaṃketālaṃbanadharmajñānam
# sems can gyi brda so so rang gis gsal ba la dmigs pa'i chos shes pa ji lta bu zhe na /
tena svasantāne ātmanimittāvikalpanāt
# des rang gi rgyud la bdag gi mtshan mar rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ pratyātmamapanītadharmasaṃketālaṃbanadharmajñānam / tena svasaṃtāna eva rūpādidharmanimittāvikalpanāt
# so so rang la chos kyi brda gsal ba la dmigs pa'i chos shes pa ji lta bu zhe na / / des rang gi rgyud nyid la gzugs la sogs pa'i mtshan mar rnam par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ sarvato 'panītobhayasaṃketālaṃbanadharmajñānam
# thams cad du gnyi ga'i brda gsal ba la dmigs pa'i chos shes pa ji lta bu zhe na /
sarvatrāviśeṣeṇātma dharmanimittāvikalpanāditi
# thams cad du bye brag med par bdag dang chos kyi mtshan ma la rnams par mi rtog pa'i phyir ro /
prabhedaśaḥ punardarśanamārgaḥ satyeṣu ṣoḍaśadharmānvayakṣāntijñānāni / tatra duḥkhe dharmajñānakṣāntiḥ prayogamārge duḥkhasatyādhikārikasūtrādidharmavicāraṇājñānaṃ yoniśo manaskārasaṃgṛhītamadhipati kṛtvā svasaṃtānikaduḥkhasatye tattathatāpratyakṣānubhāvino lokottarā prajñā samyagdṛṣṭisvabhāvotpadyate yayā duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyāṃstraidhātukānaṣṭāviṃśatimanuśayān prajahāti
# yang mthong ba'i lam la rab tu dbye ba na bden pa rnams pa bcu drug ste / / chos dang rjes su rtog pa la bzod pa dang shes pa rnams so / / de la sdug bsngal la chos shes pa'i bzod pa ni sbyor ba'i lam la / / sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i mdo la sogs pa'i chos la rnam par dpyod pa'i shes pa ste / / tshul bzhin yid la byed pas bsdus pa'i dbang du byas nas rang gi rgyud la yod pa'i sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la de'i de bzhin nyid mngon sum du 'gyur pa'i 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab yang dag par lta ba'i rang bzhin 'byung ste / / des sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba khams gsum pa'i bag la nyal nye shu rtsa brgyad rab tu spang ngo /
tasmāducyate duḥkhe dharmajñānakṣāntiriti / tayā kṣāntyā duḥkhadarśanaprahātavyakleśaprahāṇāt parivartita āśraye tadanantaraṃ yena jñānena tāmāśrayaparivṛtti pratyanubhavati tadduḥkhe dharmajñānamityucyate
# de bas na sdug bsngal la chos shes pa'i bzod pa zhes bya'o; / / bzod pa des sdug bsngal mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa spang ba'i phyir gnas gyur nas de ma thag tu shes pa gang gi gnas gyur ba de myong ba de ni sdug bsngal la chos shes pa zhe bya'o /
etaccobhayamādyaṃ kṣāntijñānamanvayaḥ sarveṣāṃ śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāmāryadharmāṇām tatasteṣāṃ samudāgamāt
# dang po'i bzod pa dang shes pa 'di gnyis ni slong ba dang slob pa'i 'phags pa'i chos thams cad kyi rgyu yin te / / de las de dag yang dag par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
atastadālaṃbyānvaya eṣa āryadharmāṇāmiti pratyātmaṃ pratyakṣānubhāvinyanāsravā prajñā duḥkhe anvayajñānakṣānti
# de'i phyir 'di gnyis ni 'phags pa'i chos thams cad kyi rgyu'o zhes de la dmigs nas so so rang la mngon sum du 'gyur ba'i zag pa med pa'i shes rab ni sdug bsngal la rjes su rtog par shes pa'i bzod pa'o /
tāmanvayajñānakṣāntiṃ yena jñānena pratyanubhavati tadanvayajñānamityucyate
# rjes su rtog par shes pa'i bzod pa dang de shes pa gang gis myong ba de ni rjes su rtog pa'i shes pa zhes bya'o /
lokottarasya hi mārgasya dvayaṃ viṣayaḥ tathatā samyagjñānaṃ ca
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi yul ni gnyis te / / de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i ye shes so /
tatra dharmajñānapakṣasya mārgasya tathatā viṣayaḥ
# de la chos shes pa'i phyogs kyi lam gyi yul ni de bzhin nyid do /
anvayajñānapakṣasya samyagjñānam
# rjes su rtog pa'i shes pa'i phyogs kyi yul ni yang dag pa'i ye shes so /
ata idamucyate dharmajñānakṣāntijñānairgrāhyāvabodhaḥ anvayakṣāntijñānairgrāhakāvabodha iti
# de'i phyir 'di skad ces bya ste chos shes pa'i bzod pa dang shes pa rnams kyis ni gzung ba rtogs so / / rjes su rtog pa'i bzod pa dang shes pa rnams kyis ni 'dzin so [?] rtogs so zhes bya'o /
yo bhagavatā ṣaṣṭho 'nimittavihārī pudgala ākhyātaḥ sa eteṣu kṣāntijñāneṣu vartamāno veditavyaḥ sarvanimittānupalaṃbhāt
# bcom ldan 'das kyis gang mtshan ma med pa la gnas pa'i gang zag drug bka' stsal pa / / de ni bzod pa dang shes pa de dag la gnas par rig par bya ste / / mtshan ma thams cad mi dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
ta ete kṣāntijñānasaṃgṛhītāḥ ṣoḍaśa cittakṣaṇā darśanamārgaḥ tairadṛṣṭapūrvāṇāmāryasa tyānāṃ pratyekaṃ caturbhirdarśanāt
# bzod pa dang shes pas bsdus pa sems kyi skad cig bcu drug po 'di dag ni mthong ba'i lam ste / / de dag gis sngon ma mthong ba'i 'phags pa'i bden pa re re la yang rnam pa bzhi bzhir mthong ba'i phyir ro /
na cātra bhāvasyābhatvā prādurbhāvamātraṃ cittakṣaṇo veditavyaḥ
# 'dir dngos po ma byung ba byung ba tsam la sems kyi skad cig tu rig par bya ba ni ma yin gyi /
kiṃ tarhi yāvatā jñeye jñānātpatteḥ parisamāptirbhavati / tadyathā duḥkhaṃ parijñeyamityekaścittalakṣaṇaḥ
# ji tsam du shes bya la shes pa 'byung ba yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba la bya ste / / 'di lta ste / / sdug bsngal ni yongs su shes par bya'o zhes bya ba ni sems kyi skad cig gcig go /
evaṃ samudayaḥ prahātavya ityevamādiḥ / yaccaitaddarśanamārgamārabhya vistareṇa vipaṃcittaṃ vyavasthānamātraṃ tatsarvaṃ veditavyam pratyātmameva vedanīyatvāt lokottarāyā avasthāyāḥ
# kun 'byung ni spang bar bya'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa yang de bzhin no / / gang mthong ba'i lam las brtsams te / / rgya cher rnam par spros pa de thams cad ni rnam par gzhag pa tsam du rig par bya ste / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i gnas skabs ni so so rang gis rig par bya ba'i phyir ro /
sarvaṃ hi mārgasatyaṃ caturbhiḥ prakārairanugantavyam vyavasthānato vikalpanato 'nubhavataḥ paripūritaśca
# lam gyi bden pa thams cad ni rnam pa bzhir rig par bya ste / / rnam par gzhag pa dang rnam par rtog pa dang myong ba dang yongs su rdzogs pa'o / / de la rnam par gzhag pa ni nyan thos la sogs pas ji ltar rang gi khong du chud pa mthar phyin nas /
tatra vyavasthānata yathāsvamadhigamaniṣṭhāprāptā śrāvakādayastatpṛṣṭhalabdhena jñānena pareṣāṃ prāpaṇanimittaṃ nāmapadavyañjanakāyaiḥ mārgasatyaṃ vyavasthāpayanti ityapi satyeṣu kṣāntayo jñānānī tyevamādi
# de'i rjes la thob pa'i shes pas gzhan dag la go bar bya ba'i phyir ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs rnams kyis lam gyi bden pa rnam par 'jog ste / / bden pa rnams la bzod pa dang shes pa ni 'di lta bu'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
vikalpanataḥ abhisamayaprayuktā laukikena yathāvyavasthānaṃ vikalpayato yadabhyasya nti
# rnam par rtog pa ni mngon par rtogs pa la zhugs pa'i 'jig rten pa'i shes pas ji ltar rnam par bzhag pa bzhin du rnam par rtog cing goms par byed pa'o /
anubhavataḥ tathābhyasyanto yāmādito darśanamārgākhyāṃ lokottarāṃ niṣprapañcāvasthāṃ pratyātmamanubhavanti paripūritaḥ tadūrdhva yāmāśrayaparivṛttiṃ paripūrya yāvadadhigamaniṣṭhāṃ prāpnuvanti
# myong ba ni de ltar goms par byed pa na mthong ba'i lam zhes brjod pa'i 'jig rten las 'das pa spros pa med pa'i gnas skabs gang yin pas dang po so sor rang gis myong ba'o / / yongs su rdzogs pa ni de'i 'og tu gnas gyur pa yongs su rdzogs nas thob pa mthar phyin pa'i bar du 'thob pa'o /
te punaradhigamaniṣṭhāprāptāstatpṛṣṭhalabdhena jñānena mārgasatyaṃ vyavasthāpayanti
# thob pa mthar phyin pa de dag ni de'i rjes la thob pa'i shes pas lam gyi bden pa rnam par 'jog go /
ityevamādi taccaturākāraṃ mārgacakraṃ punaḥ punaranyonyāśrayeṇa pravartata iti veditavyam
# de ltar na rnam pa 'di bzhi ni lam gyi 'khor lo ste / / yang dang yang gzhan dang gzhan la brten nas 'jug par rig par bya'o /
yaduktaṃ virajo vigatamalaṃ dharmeṣu dharmacakṣurutpadyata iti taddarśanamārgamadhikṛtyoktam tatprathamataḥ satyeṣvāryaprajñācakṣuḥsvabhāvatvāt
# chos rnams la chos kyi mig rdul med cing dri ma dang bral ba skyes so zhes bya ba gang gsungs pa de ni mthong ba'i lam gyi dbang du mdzad nas gsungs pa ste zhes bya ba de ni thog ma kho nar bden pa rnams la 'phags pa'i shes rab kyi spyan gyi rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra dharmakṣāntibhirvirajaḥ tābhiḥ kleśarajaḥprahāṇāt
# de la chos la bzod pa rnams kyis ni rdul med de / / de dag gis nyon mongs pa'i rdul spong ba'i phyir ro /
dharmajñānairvigatamalam teṣāṃ prahāṇatadāvaraṇamalāśrayotpādāt
# chos shes pa rnam ba ni dri ma dang bral ste / / de dag ni de'i sgrib pa'i dri ma spangs pa'i gnas su skyes pa'i phyir ro /
punaranayoreva kṣāntijñānāvasthayoryathākramaṃ parijñayā prahāṇena ca mārgasya viśuddhatāmadhikṛtya virajo vigatamalaṃ veditavyam
# yang bzod pa dang shes pa'i gnas skabs 'di gnyis ni go rims bzhin du yongs su shes pa dang spangs pa'i lam gyi rnam par dag pa'i dbang du byas ba ste / / rdul med pa dang dri ma dang bral bar rig par bya'o /
dṛṣṭetyevamādyāpi darśanamārgamevādhikṛtya veditavyam vineyānāṃ satyābhisamayānantaraṃ vacanāt
# chos mthong ba zhes pa la sogs pa yang mthong pa'i lam nyid kyi dbang du byas par rig par bya ste / / 'dul ba rnams bden pa mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i 'og tu gsungs pa'i phyir ro /
tatra dharmakṣāntibhirdṛṣṭadharmāḥ tābhistattvaprativedhāt
# de la chos la bzod pa rnams kyis ni chos mthong ste de dag gis de kho na rtogs pa'i phyir ro /
dharmajñānaiḥ prāptadharmāḥ tairāśrayaparivṛttisākṣātkaraṇāt
# chos shes pa rnams kyis chos thob ste / / chos shes pa rnams kyi gnas gyur pa mngon sum du thob par byed pa'i phyir ro /
anvayakṣāntibhirviditadharmāḥ tābhirāryadharmānvaya eṣa iti tadubhayasaṃvedanāt
# rjes su rtog pa'i bzod pa rnams kyis chos rig ste / / de dag gis 'di ni 'phags pa'i chos kyi rgyu'o zhes de gnyis rig pa'i phyir ro /
anvayajñānaiḥ paryavagāḍhadharmāḥ tairyāvajjñeyaṃ parisamāpanāt
# rjes su rtog pa'i shes pa rnams kyis chos rtogs te / / de dag gis shes bya ji snyed pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir ro /
sarvaistīrṇakāṃkṣaḥ sarvaiḥ kṣāntijñānaiḥ lokottareṇa mārgeṇa phalādhigame sati dīrgharātramabhikāṃkṣite svādhigame 'saṃdehāt
# bzod pa dang shes pa thams cad kyis som nyi las brgal te / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi 'bras bu thob pas yun ring po nas 'dod pa rang gis thob pa la the tshom med pa'i phyir ro /
tīrṇavicikitsaḥ paridhigame sarvairiti vartate parādhigame tadavasthasyānyeṣāmapi viśeṣādhigamaṃ prati vimatyabhāvāt / aparapratyayo mārgabhāvanāyāṃ paropadeśamantareṇāpi svayaṃkuśalatvāt
# thams cad kyi gzhan gyis thob pa la the tshom las brgal te / / de'i dus na gzhan dag gis kyang khyad par thob pa la yid gnyis za ba med pa'i phyir ro / / lam bsgom pa la gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa ni gzhan la lung mnos pa med par yang bdag nyid kyis mkhas pa'i phyir ro /
ananyaneyo 'vetya prasādapratilabhena śāstuḥ śāsane 'nyatīrthyairjanmāntare 'pyahāryatvāt
# gzhan gyis mi bkri pa ni shes nas dang pa thob pas gzhan mu stegs can rnams kyis tshe rabs gzhan la yang ston pa'i bstan pa las mi 'phrogs pa'i phyir ro /
dharmeṣu vaiśāradyaprāpto 'dhigamamārabhya paripraśnadharmeṣu pāpecchābhimānikavadavalīnacittatābhāvāt / bhāvanāmārgo laukiko mārgaḥ / tatra laukiko mārgo dhyānānyārūpyāśca / te punardhyānārūpyāḥ saṃkleśato vyavadānato vyavasthānato viśuddhitaśca veditavyāḥ / kathaṃ saṃkleśataḥ / catvāryavyākṛtamūlāni tṛṣṇā dṛṣṭirmāno 'vidyā ca taiḥ saṃkliṣṭacittānāṃ kliṣṭadhyānamukhena rūpārūpyāvacarasarvanivṛtāvyākṛtakleśopakleśāvartanāt / tatra tṛṣṇayāsvādasaṃkleśena saṃkliśyate prasrabdhisukhāsvādāt / dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭyuttaradhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate dhyānaṃ niścitya pūrvāntakalpādidṛṣṭisamutthāpanāt
# chos rnams la 'jigs pa thob pa ni thob pa las brtsams nas yongs su dri ba'i chos rnams dang lung bstan pa'i chos rnams la sdig pa 'dod pa mngon pa'i nga rgyal can bzhin du sems zhum pa med pa'i phyir ro / / bam po drug pa / / bsgom pa'i lam ni 'phags pa nyan thos bden pa rnams mngon par rtogs pa dang ldan pa'i'o / / de'i gong du gyur pa ni kun tu sbyor ba lhag ma spangs pa'i phyir zhugs pa ste / / gang 'jig rten pa la sogs pa'i lam mo / / de la 'jig rten pa'i lam ni bsam gtan rnams dang gzugs med pa rnams so / / bsam gtan dang gzugs med pa de dag kyang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba dang rnam par gzhag pa dang rnam par dag pas rig par bya'o / / kun nas nyon mongs pas ji lta bu zhe na / / lung du ma bstan pa'i rtsa ba bzhi po sred pa dang lta ba dang nga rgyal dang ma rig pa ste / / de dag gis sems kun nas nyon mongs pa can du gyur ba rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i bsam gtan gyi sgo nas gzugs dang gzugs med na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad bsgribs pa'i lung du mi ston par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / de la sred pas ni ro myang ba'i kun nas nyon mongs pas kun nas nyon mongs te / / shin tu sbyangs ba'i bde ba'i ro myong bar byed pa'i phyir ro / / lta bas ni lta ba shas che ba'i bsam gtan pa nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs te / / bsam gtan la brten nas sngon gyi mtha' la rtog pa la sogs pa'i lta ba kun nas slong ba'i phyir ro /
mānena mānottara dhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate tena viśeṣādhigamenonnatigamanāt
# nga rgyal gyis ni nga rgyal gyi shas che ba'i bsam gtan pa nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs te / / des khyad par du thob na khengs par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
avidyayā vicikitsottaradhyāyitayā saṃkliśyate tattvā prativedhena mokṣakāmasya tasminviśeṣādhigame mokṣo na mokṣa iti vicikitsotpādanāt
# ma rig pa ni the tshom gyi shas che ba'i bsam gtan pa nyid kyis kun nas nyon mongs pa ste / / de kho na ma gtogs pas thar pa 'dod pa khyad par de thob pa la thar pa yin nam ma yin snyam du the tshom skye ba'i phyir ro /
kathaṃ vyavadānataḥ / śuddhakā dhyānārūpyā laukikā api kuśalatvātparyavasthānamalāpagatatvena vyavadātā ityucyante
# rnam par byang ba ji lta bu zhe na dag pa'i bsam gtan dang gzugs med pa 'jig rten pa rnams kyang dge ba'i phyir kun nas dkris pa'i dri ma dang bral bas na rnam par byang ba zhes bya'o /
kathaṃ vyavasthānataḥ / dhyānānāṃ tāvaccaturdhā vyavasthānam aṅgasamāpattimātrāsaṃjñākaraṇabhedāt
# rnam par gzhag pas ji lta bu zhe na bsam gtan rnams ni yan lag dang snyoms par 'jug pa dang tshad dang ming du gdags pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa bzhir rnam par gzhag go /
ārūpyāṇāṃ tridhāṅgavarjaiḥ
# gzugs med pa rnams ni yan lag ma gtogs pa rnam pa gsum mo /
kiṃ punaradhikṛtya dhyāneṣu / vitarkādaya evāṅgatvena vyavasthāpitāḥ satsvanyeṣu dharmeṣu
# gang gi dbang du byas nas chos gzhan dag kyang yod bzhin du rtog pa la sogs pa kho na bsam gtan rnams la yan lag nyid du rnam par gzhag ce na /
tāvadbhiḥ pratipakṣānuśaṃsatadubhayāśrayāṅgaparisamāpteḥ / prathame tāvaddhyāne vitarko vicāraśca pratipakṣāṅgam tābhyāṃ kāmavyāpādavihiṃsāvitarkādiprahāṇāt
# de tsam gyis gnyen po dang phan yon dang de gnyi ga'i gnas kyi yan lag yongs su rdzogs pa'i phyir ro / / bsam gtan dang po la rtog pa dang dpyod pa ni gnyen po'i yan lag ste / / de gnyis kyis 'dod pa dang gnod sems dang 'tshe ba'i rnam par rtog pa la sogs pa spong ba'i phyir ro /
prītiḥ sukhaṃ cānuśaṃsāṅgam vitarkavicārābhyāṃ pratipakṣite vipakṣe tadvivekajaprītisukhalābhāt
# dga' ba dang bde ba ni phan yon gyi yan lag ste / / rtog pa dang dpyod pa gnyis kyis gnyen po byas pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs de las dben pa las skyes pa'i dga' ba dang bde ba thob pa'i phyir ro /
cittaikāgratā tadubhayaniśrayāṅgam samādhisaṃniśrayabalena vitarkādipravṛtteriti
# sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni de gnyi ga'i gnas kyi yan lag ste / / ting nge 'dzin la brten pa'i stobs kyis rtog pa la sogs pa 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
tathā dvitīye dhyāne 'dhyātmasaṃprasādaḥ pratipakṣāṅgam tena vitarkavicārapratipakṣaṇāt
# de bzhin du bsam gtan gnyis pa la nang rab tu dang ba ni gnyen po'i yan lag ste / / de rtog pa dang dpyod pa'i gnyen po byed pa'i phyir ro /
prītisukhe cittaikāgratā ca śeṣe aṅge pūrvavat
# dga' ba dang bde ba dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni yan lag lhag ma gnyis la snga ma bzhin no /
tṛtīye dhyāne upekṣā smṛtiḥ saṃprajanyaśca pratipakṣāṅgam taiḥ prītipratipakṣaṇāt
# bsam gtan gsum pa la btang snyoms dang ngan pa dang shes bzhin ni gnyen po'i yan lag ste / / de dag dga' ba'i gnyen po byed pa'i phyir ro /
sukhaṃ cittaikāgratā ca śeṣe aṅge yathākramam / caturthe dhyāne upekṣāpariśuddhiḥ smṛtipariśuddhiśca pratipakṣāṅgam tābhyāṃ sukhapratipakṣaṇāt
# bde ba dang sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni yan lag lhag ma gnyis dang go rims bzhin no / / bsam gtan bzhi pa la btang snyoms yongs su dag pa dang dran pa yongs su dag pa ni gnyen po'i yan lag ste / / de gnyis bde ba'i gnyen po byed pa'i phyir ro /
aduḥkhāsukhā vedanānuśaṃsāṅgam / cittaikāgratā tadubhayāṅgamiti
# sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa ni phan yon gyi yan lag go / / sems rtse gcig pa nyid ni de gnyi ga'i gnas kyi yan lag go; /
kathaṃ punaḥ prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ samāpadyamānasya sapta manaskārā bhavanti
# ji ltar na bsam gtan dang po la snyoms par 'jug pa'i yid la byed pa bdun du 'gyur zhe na /
yena samāhitabhūmikena manaskāreṇa kameṣvādīnavādidarśanenaudārikalakṣaṇaṃ pratisavedayate
# mnyam par gzhag pa'i sa pa'i yid la byed pa gang gi 'dod pa rnams la nyes dmigs la sogs par lta bas rags pa'i mtshan nyid rab tu rig pa ste /
tadabhāvācca prathamadhyāne śāntalakṣaṇam
# de med pa'i phyir bsam gtan dang po la zhi ba'i mtshan nyid do /
ayamucyate lakṣaṇapratisaṃvedanīya manaskāraḥ sa ca śrutacintāvyavakīrṇo veditavyaḥ
# 'di ni mtshan nyid rab tu rig pa'i yid la byed pa zhes bya ste / / de ni thos pa dang sems pa dang 'dres par rig par bya'o /
tadūrdhva śrutaṃ cintāṃ cātikramyaikāntena bhāvanākāreṇa tadaudārikaśāntalakṣaṇanimittālaṃbanāṃ śamathavipaśyanāṃ bhāvayan punaḥ punaryathāparyeṣitāmaudārikaśāntatāmadhimucyate ityayamadhimokṣikaḥ / tadabhyāsāttatprathamataḥ prahāṇamārgasahagato manaskāraḥ prāvivekyaḥ tenādhimātrakleśaprakāraprahāṇāttatpakṣadauṣṭhulyāpagamācca
# de'i 'og tu thos pa dang sems pa las 'das nas gcig tu bsgom pa'i rnam pas de'i rags pa dang zhi ba'i mtshan nyid kyis mtshan ma la dmigs pa'i zhi gnas dang lhag mthong bsgom zhing yang ji ltar yongs su bsal ba rags pa dang zhi ba nyid du mos te / / 'di ni mos pa las byung ba zhes ba'o / / de goms pas thog ma kho nar spong ba'i lam dang ldan pa'i yid la byed pa ni rab tu dben pa las byung ba ste; des nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa chen po spangs pa dang de'i phyogs kyi gnas ngan len dang bral ba'i phyir ro / / rnal 'byor ba de de'i 'og tu spong ba la dga' bar 'gyur zhing /
sa yogī tadūrdhva prahāṇārāmo bhavati prahāṇe 'nuśaṃsadarśī parīttapravivekaprītisukhasaṃspṛṣṭaḥ kālena kālaṃ prasadanīyena manaskāreṇa saṃpraharṣayati yāvadeva styānamiddhauddhatyopaśamāya / ayaṃ ratisaṃgrāhakaḥ
# spong ba la phan yon du lta ste / / rab tu dben pa'i dga' ba dang bde ba chung du reg nas dus dus su dang bar 'gyur ba'i yid la byed pa ji tsam du rmugs pa dang gnyid dang rgod pa dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir rab tu dga' bar byed par 'di ni dga' ba sdud pa zhes bya'o /
tasyaivaṃ samyakprayuktasya kuśalapakṣaprayogopastabdhatvāt kāmāvacarakleśaparyavasthānāsamudācāre sati tatprahīṇāprahīṇatāvagamārtha tadutpattyanukūlaśubhanimittamanaskāreṇa pratyavekṣaṇaṃ mīmāṃsāmanaskāraḥ
# de ltar legs par zhugs pa de dge ba'i phyogs la sbyor bas brten pa'i phyir 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa'i kun nas dkris pa kun nas mi 'byung bas / / de spangs sam ma spangs pa khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir /
tasyaivaṃ mīmāṃsāpratipakṣaṃ bhāvayataḥ tāvatkālikayogena sarvakāmāvacarakleśavisaṃyogāya prathamadhyānaprayogaparyavasānagataḥ pratipakṣamanaskāraḥ prayoganiṣṭhaḥ
# de 'byung ba dang mthun pa'i sdug pa'i mchan ma yid la byed pas so sor rtog pa ni dpyod pa'i yid la byed pa'o / / des de ltar dpyad nas gnyen po bsgoms pas dus de srid cig pa'i tshul gyis 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa thams cad spang bar bya ba'i phyir bsam gtan dang po la sbyor ba'i mthar thug pa'i gnyen po yid la byed pa ni sbyor ba'i mtha'o /
tadanantaraṃ maulaprathamadhyānasahagataḥ prayoganiṣṭhāphala iti / tatra lakṣaṇapratisavedinā prahātavyaṃ prāptavyaṃ ca samyakparijñāya prahāṇāya prāptaye ca cittaṃ praṇighatte
# de'i 'og tu dngos gzhi'i bsam gtan dang por gyur ba ni sbyor ba'i mtha'i 'bras bu yid la byed pa zhes bya'o / / de la mtshan nyid rab tu rig pas ni spang bar bya ba dang thob par bya ba legs par yongs su shes nas spang ba dang thob par bya ba'i phyir sems 'jog go /
ādhimokṣikena tadartha samyakprayogamārabhate
# mos pa las byung ba ni de'i 'og tu yang dag par sbyor ba tsam mo /
prāvivekyenādhimātrān kleśān jahāti / ratisaṃgrāhakeṇa madhyaṃ kleśaprakāraṃ jahāti
# rab tu dben pa las byung bas ni kun nas nyon mongs pa chen po rnams rab tu spong ngo / / dga' ba sdud pas ni nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa 'bring du spong ngo /
mīmāṃsakena prāptinirabhimānatāyāṃ cittamavasthāpayati
# dpyod pas ni thob par mngon pa'i nga rgyal med pa la sems 'jog par byed do /
prayoganiṣṭhena mṛduṃ kleśaprakāraṃ jahāti
# sbyor ba'i mthas ni nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa chung ngu rab tu spong ngo /
prayoganiṣṭhāphalena eṣāṃ manaskārāṇāṃ subhāvitānāṃ bhāvanāphalaṃ pratyanubhavati
# sbyor ba'i mtha'i 'bras bus ni yid la byed pa legs par bsgoms pa 'di dag gis bsgoms pa'i 'bras bu myong bar byed do /
yathā prathamadhyānasamāpattaye sapta manaskārā evaṃ yāvannaivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanasamāpattaye yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyāḥ / audārikalakṣaṇaṃ punaḥ sarvāsvadhobhūmiṣu yāvadākiṃcanyāyatanāt samāsena dvividhaṃ veditavyam duḥkhataravihāritāpraśāntavihāritayā alpāyuskataratā ca tadviparyayeṇordhvabhūmeḥ śāntalakṣaṇaṃ veditavyam
# bsam gtan dang po la snyoms par 'jug pa'i phyir yid la byed pa rnam pa bdun ji lta ba bzhin du 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched kyi bar la snyoms par 'jug pa'i phyir yang ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o / / rags pa'i mtshan nyid ni sa 'og ma thams cad de / / ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi bar du'o / / mdor bsdu na rnam pa gnyis su rig par bya ste / / rab tu ma zhi bar gnas pas shin tu sdug bsngal bar gnas pa dang shin tu tshe thung ba'o / / de las bzlog ste sa gong ma ni zhi ba'i mtshan nyid du rig par bya'o /
mātrāvyavasthānaṃ dhyānānāṃ tāvanmṛdumadhyādhimātraparibhāvitatvāt
# tshad rnam par gzhag pa zhes bya ba la / / bsam gtan rnams ni chung ngu dang 'bring dang cher yongs su bsgom pa'i phyir ro /
pratyekaṃ tridhā dhyānopapattiḥ phalaṃ bhavati
# re re la yang bsam gtan gyi skye ba gsum gsum ni 'bras bu yin te /
tadyathā brahmakāyikā brahmapurohitā mahābrahmāṇaṃ ityevamādi yathāpūrvamuktam / ārūpyeṣu tu vimānasthānāntarasaṃniveśāsaṃbhavādevamupapatti bhedo na vyavasthāpyate
# 'di lta ste tshangs ris dang tshangs pa mdun na 'don dang tshangs pa chen po zhes bya ba la sogs pa ji ltar gong du bshad pa'o / / gzugs med pa rnams na ni gzhal med khang gi gnas gzhan gnas pa med pa'i phyir de ltar skye ba'i bye brag rnam par gzhag pa med de /
api tu teṣāmapyasti mṛdvādiparibhāvitānāmupapattāvuccanīcatā āyurādiviśeṣeṇa hīnapraṇītatā ca kliṣṭākliṣṭatābāhulyaviśeṣeṇeti
# 'on kyang de dag chung du la sogs pa yongs su bsgoms pa rnams kyis skye ba la tshe la sogs pa'i khyad par gyis mthon po dang dma' ba dang nyon mongs pa can dang nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa mang ba'i khyad par gyis ngan pa dang bzang po ni yod do /
saṃjñākaraṇavyavasthānaṃ caturthadhyānaprabhedānāṃ samādhīnāmasaṃkhyeyānyacintyāni ca nāmāni / tathāhi yāvataḥ prathamadhyānasaṃgṛhītān samādhīn buddhā bhagavanto bodhisattvāśca mahāprabhāvaprāptāḥ samāpadyante teṣāṃ samādhīnāṃ śrāvakāḥ pratyekabuddhāśca nāmānyapi na jānanti
# ming du gdags pa rnam par gzhag pa ni bsam gtan bzhi'i rab tu dbye ba'i ting nge 'dzin rnams kyi ming grangs med pa dang bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te / / 'di ltar bsam gtan dang pos bsdus pa ji snyed la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' mthu chen po thob pa rnams snyoms par 'jug pa'i ting nge 'dzin de dag gi ming yang nyan thos rnams dang rang sangs rgyas rnams kyis mi shes na /
kutaścaiṣāṃ saṃkhyāṃ jñāsyanti samāpatsyante vā
# de dag gi grangs shes par 'gyur ba'am snyoms par 'jug par lta ga la 'gyur te /
yathā nirdiṣṭaṃ prajñāpāramitāyām "sādhitaṃ samādhiśatam" / evamanyeṣvapi teṣu teṣu mahāyānasūtreṣviti
# ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las ting nge 'dzin brgya lha gcig bstan pa dang de bzhin du theg pa chen po'i mdo sde gzhan de dang de dag nas 'byung ba'o /
kathaṃ viśuddhitaḥ
# rnam par dag pas ji lta bu zhe na /
prāntakoṭikā dhyānārūpyā viśuddhirityucyate vaiśeṣikaguṇābhinirhārāya nikāmalābhādibhiḥ karmaṇyatāprakarṣanayanāt
# rab kyi mtha'i cha las byung ba'i bsam gtan dang gzugs med pa rnams ni rnam par dag pa zhes bya ste / / yon tan khyad par can mngon par bsgrub ba'i phyir 'dod pa bzhin du 'thob pa la sogs pas las su rung ba mchog tu phyin par khrid pa'i phyir ro /
lokottaramārgo bhāvanāmārge 'ṣṭau duḥkhādidharmānvayajñānāni yathā darśanamārge nirdiṣṭāni / tatsaṃprayuktaśca samādhiranāgamyasaṃgṛhītaḥ prathamaṃ dhyānaṃ yāvadākiṃcanyāyatanam / naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanamaparisphuṭaṃ saṃjñāpracāratayā paramapaṭupracārasyāryamārgasyāsaṃniḥśrayatvādekāntena laukikaṃ veditavyam / ata eva ca tatsaṃjñāmāndyādālambanānimittīkaraṇārthenānimittamityucyate / kutaḥ punaretat jñāyate naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatane āryamārgo nāstīti
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi bsgom pa'i lam la brgyad de / / sdug bsngal la sogs pa la chos dang rjes su rtog pa'i shes pa rnams te / / ji ltar mthong ba'i lam la bstan pa rnams te / / ji ltar mthong ba'i lam la bstan pa rnams so / / de dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni mi lcogs pa med pas bsdus pa'am / / bsam gtan dang po nas ci yang med pa'i skye mchod kyi bar du'o / / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched ni 'du shes kyi rgyu ba yongs su mi gsal bas 'phags pa'i lam mchog tu gsal ba'i gnas ma yin pa'i phyir gcig tu 'jig rten par rig par bya'o / / de'i phyir de'i 'du shes dman pas dmigs pa la mtshan mar mi byed pa'i phyir mtshan ma med pa zhes bya'o / / 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched la 'phags pa'i lam med pa de ji ltar shes she na /
yasmāduktaṃ bhagavatā "yāvadeva saṃjñāsamāpattistāvadājñāprativedha" iti
# 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis ji tsam du 'du shes kyi snyoms par 'jug pa de tsam du kun shes pas rtogs so zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro /
nirodhasamāpattirlokottarā āryamārgapṛṣṭhalabhyatvāt / manuṣyeṣvabhinirhriyate utpādyata ādita ityarthaḥ pūrvotpāditāyāḥ paścātsaṃmukhobhāvo manuṣyeṣu vā tasminneva janmani rūpadhātau vā upapadya
# 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ste / / 'phags pa'i lam gyi rjes la thob pa'i phyir ro / / mi rnams kyi nang du mngon bar sgrub po zhes bya ba ni / / thog ma nyid du skyed ces bya ba'i tha tshig ste / / sngar skye na mi rnams kyi nang du tshe de nyid dam gzugs kyi khams su skyes nas mngon du 'gyur ro /
kathamārūpyalābhino rūpadhātuvītarāgasyāryaśrāvakasya rūpadhātāvupapatiḥ / nāvaśyaṃ rūpadhātuvītarāga evārūpyaṃ samāpadyate
# 'phags pa nyan thos gzugs kyi khams las 'dod chags dang bral ste / / gzugs med pa thob pa gzugs kyi khams su ji ltar skye zhe na / / gzugs kyi khams kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba nyid gzugs med pa la snyoms par 'jug pa nges pa med do /
ata evātra catuṣkoṭikaṃ bhavati yo rūpavītarāgaḥ sarvaḥ sa ārūpyaśāntavimokṣasamāpattā yo vā ārūpyaśāntavimokṣasamāpattā sarvaḥ sa rūpavītarāga iti
# de'i phyir gang gzugs la 'dod chags dang bral ba de thams cad gzugs med pa zhi ba rnam par thar pa la snyoms par 'jug par byed la / / gang yang gzugs med pa zhi ba rnam par thar pa la snyoms par 'jug par byed pa de thams cad gzugs las 'dod chags dang bral ba yin nam zhe na /
prathamā koṭiḥ anāgamyaṃ niśritya rūpavītarāgaḥ
# mu bzhir 'gyur te mi lcogs pa med pa la brten nas gzugs la 'dod chags dang bral ba ni mu dang po'o /
dvitīyā koṭiḥ caturthadhyānalābhī ārya āryopapattyānarthī prahāṇamārgaṃ nirākṛtya viśeṣamārgaṃ niśrityārūpyaśāntavimokṣasamāpattā
# bsam gtan bzhi pa thob pa'i 'phags pa gzugs med par skye ba don du mi gnyer ba la spong ba'i lam bsal nas khyad par can gyi lam la gnas te gzugs med pa zhi ba rnams par thar pa la snyoms par 'jug par byed pa ni mu gnyis pa'o /
tṛtīyā koṭiḥ sa eva vairāgyārthī prahāṇamārgaṃ niśrityārūpyaśāntavimokṣasamāpattā
# de nyid 'dod chags dang bral ba don du gnyer zhing spong ba'i lam la gnas te gzugs med pa zhi ba rnam par thar pa la snyoms par 'jug par byed pa ni mu gsum pa'o /
caturthī etānākārān sthāpayitvā
# rnam pa de dag ma gtogs pa ni mu bzhi pa'o /
ārūpye ṣūpapannānāṃ kasmānna saṃmukhībhavati
# gzugs med par skyes pa rnams la ci'i phyir mngon sum du mi 'gyur zhe na /
śāntena vihāreṇa vihartukāmā āryā manuṣyeṣvenāmabhinirhṛtya saṃmukhīkurvanti
# zhi bar gnas pas gnas par 'dod pa'i 'phags pa rnams mi'i nang du de mngon par bsgrubs nas mngon sum du byed do /
ārūpyeṣu tūpapannāste 'prayatnenaiva vaipākikaiḥ paramaśāntaiḥ vimokṣavihārairviharantītyatastatsaṃmukhīkaraṇārthaṃ na punaḥ prayatnamārabhanta iti
# gzugs med par skyes pa de dag ni bsgrim mi dgos par rnam par smin pa las byung ba mchog tu zhi ba rnam par thar pa la gnas pas gnas pa ste / / de'i phyir de mngon sum du bya ba'i don du yang 'bad pa mi rtsom mo /
mṛdumadhyādhimātro mārgaḥ pratyekaṃ punaḥ mṛdvādibhistribhiḥ prakārairbhittvā navaprakāro vyavasthāpyate bhāvanā heyānāṃ krameṇa prahāṇajñāpanārtham
# lam chung du dang 'bring dang chen po re re la yang chung du la sogs pas rnam pa gsum du phye nas rnam pa dgur rnam par gzhag ste / / bsgoms pas spang bar bya ba rnam pa rim gyis spang ba bstan pa'i phyir ro /
kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ mṛdumṛdunā mārgeṇādhimātraḥ kleśaḥ prahīyate
# ci'i phyir lam chung ngu'i chung dus nyon mongs pa chen po'i chen po spang zhe na /
sa hyatyarthaḥ vipannahrīvyapannāpyālajjinaḥ saṃtāne samudācarati sūpalakṣaścāsau suparicchedastasmādasau sthūlamalavadalpenāpi pratipakṣeṇāpanīyate
# de ni ngo tsha shes pa dang khrel yod pa dang shin tu bral zhing 'dzem pa med pa'i sems kyi rgyud la kun du 'byung bas de rtogs par sla zhing yongs su gcad par sla ba ste / / de'i phyir de ni dri ma che long bzhin du gnyen po chung ngus sel to /
yastvayaṃ duṣparicchedasamudācāraḥ sūkṣmalīnaḥ saṃtāne mṛdumṛdukleśaḥ sūkṣmamalavanmahatā pratipakṣabalenāpanīyata ityado vipakṣaprakāraviparyayeṇa pratipakṣaprakāravyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# gang yongs su gcad par dka' bar kun tu 'byung zhing phra la rgyud la zhen pa'i nyon mongs pa chung ngu'i chung ngu de ni dri ma chung ngu bzhin du gnyen po chen po'i stobs kyis sel te / / de'i phyir mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi rnam pa las bzlog nas gnyen po'i phyogs kyi rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
prayogamārgo yena mārgeṇa bhāvyamānena pratyekamadhimātrādhimātrādikleśaprakārādijātipakṣasya dauṣṭhulyāṅgasyāpagamātkrameṇāśrayaḥ parivartate sa bhāvanāmārge prayogamārge ityucyate / yasya tvanantaraṃ tatprakārakleśajātitatpakṣadauṣṭhulyāvaśeṣāpagamāttena dauṣṭhulyena nirdauṭhulya āśrayaḥ parivartate sa ānantaryamārgaḥ
# sbyor ba'i lam ni lam gang bsgoms pas chen po'i yang chen po la sogs pa nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa'i bye brag dang phyogs kyi gnas ngan len gyi cha shas re re dang bral ba'i phyir rim gyis gnas gyur pa de ni bsgom pa'i lam la sbyor ba'i lam zhes bya'o / / gang gi 'og tu de nyon mongs pa'i bye brag gi rnam pa dang phyogs kyi gnas ngan len ma lus pa dang bral ba'i phyir des gnas ngan len med par gnas gyur pa de ni bar chad med pa'i lam lo /
vimuktimārgo yena nāmāśrayaparivṛtti pratyātmamanubhavati
# rnam par grol ba'i lam ni gang gis gnas gyur pa de so sor rang gis myong ba'o /
viśeṣamārgastadūrdhvāvaśeṣakleśaprahāṇaṃ kurvato ye prayogānantaryavimuktimārgāḥ / aparaḥ paryāya 'viśeṣamārgastasya kleśaprahāṇaprayogamadhyupekṣya sūtrādīn dharmāścintayataḥ pūrvacintitādhigatadharmapratyavekṣaṇāvihāreṇa vā viharataḥ samāpattyantaraṃ vā samāpadyamānasya yo mārgaḥ
# khyad par gyi lam ni de'i 'og tu nyon mongs pa lhag ma spong par byed pa'i sbyor ba dang bar chad med pa dang rnam par grol ba'i lam gang yin pa'o / / rnam grangs gzhan du na khyad par gyi lam ni nyon mongs pa spong bar sbyor ba btang ste / / mdo la sogs pa'i chos sems pa'am sdar bsam pa dang khong du chud pa'i chos la so sor rtog pa'i gnas pas gnas pa'am / / snyoms par 'jug pa gzhan la snyoms par 'jug pa gzhan pa snyoms par 'jug pa'i lam gang yin pa'o /
punarabhijñādīn vaiśeṣikān guṇānabhinirharatastairvā viharato yo mārgaḥ / ityevaṃ bhāvanāmārga vistareṇa nirdiśya tadanuṣaṃgeṇa mārgabhāvanā varṇyate / caturvidhā mārgabhāvanā samyak prahāṇānadhikṛtya yathāyogam
# yang mngon par shes pa la sogs pa yon tan khyad par can mngon par sgrub pa'am de dag gi gnas pa'i lam gang yin pa'o / / de ltar bsgom pa'i lam rgya cher bshad nas de'i zhar la byung ba'i lam bsgom pa brjod par bya'o / / lam bsgom pa rnam pa bzhi ni yang dag par spong pa'i dbang du byas pa ste / / ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar ro /
tatra pratilambhāya bhāvanā pratilambhabhāvanā tayālabdhakuśaladharmapratilambhāt
# de la thob par bya ba'i phyir bsgom pa ni thob par bya ba'i don du bsgom pa ste / / des dge ba'i chos ma thob pa rnams thob pa'i phyir ro /
niṣevaṇameva bhāvanā niṣevaṇabhāvanā labdhakuśaladharmābhyasanāt
# brten pa bsgom pa ni brten pa nyid bsgom pa ste / / dge ba'i chos thob pa goms par byed pa'i phyir ro /
nirdhāvanāya bhāvanā nirdhāvanabhāvanā samudācārāvasthākuśaladharmanirvāsanāt
# bsal ba'i phyir bsgom pa ni bsal ba'i don du bsgom pa ste / / kun 'byung ba'i gnas skabs su mi dge ba'i chos sel ba'i phyir ro /
pratipakṣasya bhāvanā pratipakṣabhāvanā anāgatākuśaladharmānutpattidharmatāpādanāt
# gnyen po bsgom pa ni gnyen po la bsgom pa ste / / ma 'ongs pa'i mi dge ba'i chos mi skye ba'i chos can du byed pa'i phyir ro /
aparaḥ paryāyaḥ mārga utpadyamānaḥ svāṃ vāsanāṃ sthāpayatisādhāsanā pratilambhabhāvanā tatastadanvayānāmuttaptatarāpatteḥ / asyaiva mārgasya saṃmukhībhāvo 'bhiniṣevaṇabhāvanā
# rnam grang gzhan du na 'phags pa'i lam skye ba na rang gi bag chags 'jog pa de ni bag chags thob par bya ba'i phyir bsgom pa ste / / de las de'i rgyu las byung ba rnams cher 'bar bar 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / lam de nyid mngon du byed pa ni brten pa'i bsgom pa'o /
tena svavipakṣadauṣṭhulyanirodhanānnirdhāvanabhāvanā
# des rang gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi gnas ngan len 'gog par byed pa ni bsal ba'i phyir bsgom pa'o /
āśrayasya parivṛttatvādāyatyāmanutpattidharmatāyāmavasthāpanaṃ pratipakṣabhāvanā / punaḥ pratipakṣasya vidūṣaṇādikaḥ caturvidhaḥ prabhedo veditavyaḥ
# gnas 'gyur ba'i phyir phyi ma la mi skye ba'i chos can du 'jog pa de ni gnyen po bsgom pa'o / / yang gnyen po ni rnam par sun 'byin pa la sogs pa rnam pa bzhir rab tu dbye bar rig par bya ste / / de la rnam par sun 'byin pa'i gnyen po ni /
tatra vidūṣaṇāpratipakṣaḥ sāsraveṣu saṃskāreṣvādīnavadarśanam tena rogagaṇḍādibhirākārairupādānaskandhadūṣaṇāt
# zag pa dang bcas pa'i 'du byed rnams la nyes dmigs su lta ba ste / / des nad dang 'bras la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis nye bar len pa'i phung po sun 'byin pa'i phyir ro /
prahāṇapratipakṣaḥ prayogānantaryamārgāḥ taiḥ kleśaprahāṇāt
# spong ba'i gnyen po ni sbyor ba dang bar chad med pa'i lam rnams te / / de dag gi nyon mongs pa spong ba'i phyir ro /
ādhārapratipakṣo vimuktimārgāḥ taiḥ prahāṇaprāptisaṃdhāraṇāt / dūrībhāvapratipakṣastaduparimo mārgaḥ tena pūrvaprahīṇakleśadūrīkaraṇāt
# rten gnyis po ni rnam par grol ba'i lam rnams te / / de dag gis spong ba'i thob pa kun tu 'dzin pa'i phyir ro; / / thag bsring ba'i gnyen po ni de'i gong ma'i lam ste / / des sngon spangs pa'i nyon mongs pa thag bsring ba'i phyir ro /
punarbodhipakṣyādibhedenaikādaśavidho mārgo vyavasthāpyate
# yang byang chub kyi phyogs la sogs ba'i bye brag gis lam rnam pa bcu gcig tu rnam par gzhag ste / / 'di lta ste /
tadyathā vastuparīkṣāmārgaḥ smṛtyupasthānāni āditastenāśubhādibhirākāraiḥ kāyavedanācittadharmavastuparīkṣaṇāt
# dngos po la yongs su rtog pa'i lam ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams te / / des thog ma nyid du mi gtsang ba la sogs pa'i rnam gyi lus dang tshor ba dang sems dang chos kyi dngos po la yongs su rtog pa'i phyir ro /
vyāvasāyiko mārgaḥ samyakprahāṇāni tathā sarvāṇi vastūni parīkṣyānenāvaraṇaprahāṇāya vīryārambhāt
# rtsol ba las byung ba'i lam ni yang dag par spong ba rnams te / / de ltar dngos po rnams la yongs su brtags nas des sgrib pa spangs pa'i don du brtson 'grus rtsom pa'i phyir ro /
samādhiparikarmamārga ṛddhipādāḥ tathāpariśodhitāvaraṇasyānena chandavīryacittamīmāṃsāmukhaiḥ samādheḥ karmaṇyatāpādanāt
# ting nge 'dzin yongs su sbyong bar byed pa'i lam ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams te / / de ltar sgrib pa yongs su sbyangs pa ni 'dis 'dun pa dang brtson 'grus dang sems dang dpyod pa'i sgo nas ting nge 'dzin rnams kyis las su rung bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
abhisamayaprayogiko mārga indriyāṇi tathākṛtasamādhiparikarmaṇo 'nenāryamārgasamudāgamāyādhipatibhūtoṣmagatordhvaprayogāt
# mngon par rtogs par bya ba'i sbyor ba'i lam ni dbang po rnams te / / de ltar ting nge 'dzin yongs su sbyang ba byas pa ni des 'phags pa'i lam yang dag par sgrub pa'i phyir dbang byed par gyur pa dro bar gyur pa dang rtse mo la sbyor ba'i phyir ro /
abhisamayaśliṣṭo mārgo balāni tathādhipatyaprāptasyānenānantaraṃ satyaprativedhāyāśraddhādivipakṣānabhibhūtakṣāntyagradharmaprayogāt
# mngon par rtogs pa dang 'dres pa'i lam ni stobs rnams te / / de ltar dbang byed pa thob pa ni lnga po 'dis de ma thag tu bden pa rtogs par bya ba'i phyir ma dang pa la sogs pa mi mthun pa'i phyogs zil gyis mi non pa bzod pa dang 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog la sbyor ba'i phyir ro /
abhisamayamārgo bodhyaṅgāni tenāditaḥ pratyātmaṃ tattvābhisaṃbodhāt
# mngon par rtogs pa'i lam ni byang chub kyi yan lag rnams te / / des thog ma kho nar so so rang gis de kho nar mngon du yang dag par rtogs pa'i phyir ro /
viśuddhinairyāṇiko mārga āryāṣṭāṅgo mārgaḥ tadūrdhvaṃ tena bhāvanāprahātavyakleśaprahāṇāya viśuddhaye niryāṇāditi
# rnam par dag pa nges par 'byin pa'i lam ni 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ste / / de'i 'og tu des bsgoms pas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams rnam par dag par bya bar nges par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
ata evaiṣāṃ bodhipakṣāṇāmevānupūrvī veditavyā / niśrayendriyabhinno mārgaḥ catasraḥ pratipadaḥ
# de'i phyir de ltar byang chub kyi phyogs 'di dag gi go rims ni 'di lta bu yin par rig par bya'o / / gnas dang dbang po tha dad pa'i lam ni lam bzhi ste /
tatra duḥkhā pratipadanāgamyārūpyaniśritā yathākramaṃ śamathavipaśyanāmāndyāt / sukhā dhyānaniśritā yuganaddhavāhitvāt
# de la dka' ba'i lam ni mi lcogs pa med pa dang gzugs med pa la brten pa ste / / go rims bzhin du zhi gnas dang lhag mthong zhan pa'i phyir ro / / sla ba ni bsam gtan la brten pa ste / / zung ngu 'brel par 'jug pa'i phyir ro; /
dhandhābhijñā dvayorapyanayorduḥkhasukhaniśrayayormṛdvindriyāṇām
# mngon par shes pa bul ba ni dka' ba dang sla ba'i gnas 'di gnyis la ste / / dbang po rtul po rnams kyi'o /
kṣiprābhijñā tayoreva tīkṣṇendriyāṇāmiti / śikṣā trayapariśodhano mārgaḥ catvāri dharmapadāni / tatrānabhidhyāvyāpādamadhiśīlaṃ śikṣāyāḥ pariśodhanam ananunayāpratighamukhena śikṣāpadākhaṇḍanāt
# mngon par shes pa myur ba ni 'di gnyis nyid la ste / / dbang po rnon po rnams kyi'o / / bslab pa gsum yongs su sbyong ba'i lam ni chos kyi gnas bzhi ste / / de la brnab sems med pa dang gnod sems med pa gnyis kyis ni lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyi bslab pa yongs su sbyong ba ste / / rjes su chags pa dang khang khro ba spangs pa'i bslab pa'i gnas mi nyams par byed pa'i phyir ro /
samyaksmṛtyādhicittaṃ śikṣāyāḥ pariśodhanam ālaṃbanāsaṃmoṣe sati cittasamādhānāt
# yang dag pa'i dran pas ni lhag pa'i sems kyi bslab pa yongs su spyod pa ste / / dmigs pa ma brjed pa ni sems mnyam par 'jog pa'i phyir ro /
samyaksamādhinādhiprajñaṃ śikṣāyāḥ pariśodhanam samāhitacittasya yathābhūtajñānāditi
# yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis ni lhag pa'i shes rab kyi bslab pa yongs su sbyong ste / / sems mnyam par gzhag pa las yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes pa'i phyir ro /
sarvaguṇābhinirhārako yo mārgaḥ śamathavipaśyanā tataḥ sarvalaukikalokottaraguṇābhiniṣpatteḥ
# yon tan thams cad sgrub par byed pa'i rnal 'byor gyi lam ni zhi gnas dang lhag mthong ste / / de las 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i yon tan thams cad mngon par 'grub pa'i phyir ro /
mārgasaṃgrahamārgastrīṇīndriyāṇī tatrānājñātamājñāsyāmīndriyeṇa prayogadarśanamārgayoḥ saṃgrahaḥ ājñendriyeṇa bhāvanāmārgasya ājñātāvīndriyeṇa niṣṭhāmārgasyeti / punarbodhipakṣyāṇāṃ dharmāṇāṃ pañcabhiḥ prakāraiḥ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam ālambanataḥ svabhāvataḥ sahāyato bhāvanāto bhāvanāphalataśca / tatra smṛtyupasthānānāmālaṃbanaṃ yathākramaṃ kāyo vedanā cittaṃ dharmāḥ / kimartha punaretadevamālaṃbanaṃ vyavasthāpyate
# lam sdud pa'i lam ni dbang po gsum po dag ste / / de la mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang pos ni sbyor ba dang mthong ba'i lam sdud do / / kun shes pa'i dbang pos ni bsgom pa'i lam sdud do / / kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang pos ni mthar phyin pa'i lam sdud do / / yang byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos rnams ni rnam par lngas rnam par gzhag par rig par bya ste / / dmigs pa dang ngo bo nyid dang grogs dang bsgom pa dang bsgoms pa'i 'bras bus so / / de la dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyi dmigs pa ni lus dang tshor ba dang sems dang chos rnams te / / go rims bzhin no / / ci'i phyir 'di dag dmigs par rnam par gzhag ce na /
yasmādviparyastabuddhayo bālāḥ prāyeṇa sendriyaṃ kāyamāśritya sukhādimupabhuñjānā upalabdhalakṣaṇā ātmarāgādibhiḥ śraddhādibhiśca saṃkliśyante vyavadāyante ceti vikalpayantyata āditaḥ samyaktadvastulakṣaṇaparīkṣārthamevaṃ caturdhālambanavyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# 'di ltar byis pa phyin ci log gi blo can rnams ni phal cher dbang po dang bcas pa'i lus la brten nas bde ba la sogs pa la spyod pa na dmigs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi bdag 'dod chags la sogs pa dang dad pa la sogs pas kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ba dang rnam par byang bar 'gyur bar rtogs te / / de'i phyir thog ma nyid du dngos po'i mtshan nyid de / / legs par yongs su brtags pa'i phyir dmigs pa rnam pa bzhi rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
svabhāvataḥ prajñā smṛtiśca kāyādyanupaśyanāvacanāt smṛtyupasthānavacanācca yathākramam
# ngo bo nyid ni shes rab dang dran pa ste / / lus la sogs pa la rjes su lta ba zhes 'byung ba dang; dran pa nye bar gzhag pa zhes 'byung ba'i phyir go rims bzhin no /
sahāyatastābhyāṃ saṃprayuktāścitacaitasikāḥ / bhāvanādhyātmaṃ bahirdhādhyātmabahirdhā ca kāyādiṣu kāyādyanupaśyanā / tatrādhyātmaṃ kāyaścakṣuśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyendriyāṇi ādhyātmikāyatanasaṃgṛhītatvātsattvasaṃkhyātatvācca / bahirdhā kāyo bahirdhārūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyāni bāhyāyatanasaṃgṛhītatvādasattvasaṃkhyātatvācca
# grogs ni de gnyi ga dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams so / / bsgom pa ni nang dang phyi'i lus la sogs pa la lus la sogs pa'i rjes su lta ba'o / / de la nang gi lus ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi dbang po rnams te / / nang gi skye mched kyis bsdus pa dang sems can gyi grangs su gtogs pa'i phyir ro / / phyi'i lus ni phyi rol gyi gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya rnams te / / phyi'i skye mched kyis bsdus pa dang sems can gyi grangs sum gtogs pa'i phyir ro /
adhyātmabahirdhā kāyaścakṣurādyāyatanasaṃbaddhāni rūpādīnyāyatanānīndriyādhiṣṭhānabhūtāni sattvasaṃkhyātatvādvāhyāyatanasaṃgṛhītatvācca
# nang dang phyi'i lus ni mig la sogs pa'i skye mched dang 'brel ba'i gzugs la sogs pa'i skye mched dbang po'i gnas su gyur pa rnams te / / sems can gyi grangs su gtogs pa dang phyi'i skye mched kyis sdud pa'i phyir ro /
pārasaṃtānikāni cādhyātmikāni rūpīṇyāyatanānyadhyātmabahirdhā kāyaḥ āyatanavyavasthāṃ saṃtānavyavasthāṃ ca pramāṇayitvā
# gzhan gyi rgyud la yod pa'i nang gi skye mched gzugs can rnams kyang nang dang phyi'i lus te / / skye mched rnam par gzhag pa dang rgyud rnam par gzhag pa brtson par byas pa'i phyir ro /
kāye kāyasya sādṛśyena paśyanā kāye kāyānupaśyanā vikalpapratibimbakāyadarśanānusāreṇa prakṛtibimbakāyāvadhāraṇāt
# lus la lus kyi rjes su lta ba ni lus la lus dang 'dra bar lta ba ste / / rnam par rtog pa'i gzugs brnyan gyi gzugs mthong ba dang mthun par rang gzhin gyi gzugs kyi lus nges par 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
adhyātmaṃ vedanādayo 'dhyātmaṃ kāyamupādāyotpannāḥ cakṣurādyālaṃbanatayā svāśrayotpannanatayā vā
# nang gi tshor ba la sogs pa ni nang gi lus la brten nas 'byung ba rnams te / / mig la sogs pa la dmigs pa dang rang gi gnas las byung ba'i phyir ro /
bahirdhā vedanādayo bahirdhā kāyamupādāyotpannāḥ rūpādyālambanatayā parāśrayotpannatayā vā
# phyi'i tshor ba la sogs pa ni phyi rol gyi lus la brten nas 'byung ba rnams te / / gzugs la sogs pa la dmigs pa dang gzhan gyi gnas las byung ba'i phyir ro /
adhyātmabahirdhā vedanādayo dhyātmabahirdhākāyamupādāyotpannāḥ svasantānikabāhyāyatanālambanatayā pārasaṃtānikādhyātmikāyatanālaṃbanatayā vā / cetaso līnatvaṃ viśeṣādhigamapratyātmaparibhavamukhaiḥ viṣādaḥ / parisravaparikhedo daṃśamaśakādyupadravotpīḍanāsahanam / alpamātrasaṃtuṣṭiḥ alaṃ me tāvatā kuśalapakṣeṇeti prativāraṇam
# nang dang phyi'i tshor ba la sogs pa ni nang dang phyi'i lus la brten nas 'byung ba rnams te / / rang gi rgyud la yod pa'i phyi'i skye mched la dmigs pa dang gzhan gyi rgyud la yod pa'i nang gi skye mched la dmigs pa'i phyir ro / / tshor ba la sogs pa'i rjes su lta ba yang de bzhin te / / ci rigs su sbyar ro zhes ba ni blo la snang ba dang khyad par med pa bsgom pa zhes bya'o / / 'dun pa la sogs pa dgu po 'di dag ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa'i yan lag go / / sems zhum pa ni khyad par thob par bya ba la bdag dman par sems pa'i sgo nas sgyid lug pa'o / / gnod pas yongs su skyo ba ni sha sbrang dang sbrang bu la sogs pa'i gnod pas nyen pa mi bzod pa'o / / cung zad tsam gyis chog par 'dzin pa ni dge ba'i phyogs 'di tsam gyis chog go zhes phyir bzlog pa'o /
āpattivipratisāro 'bhikramapratikramādiṣvasaṃprajñānacāriṇaḥ śikṣāvyatikramapūrvaḥ paścāttāpaḥ / nikṣiptadhuratā pramādadoṣeṇa yathārambhaṃ kuśalapakṣaprayogāntānirvāha iti / phalaṃ yathākramaṃ smṛtyupasthānānāṃ śucisukhanityātmaviparyāsapraharaṇam aśubhabhāvanātaḥ yatkiṃcit veditamidamatra duḥkhasyeti jñānāt āśrayālaṃbanādibhedaiḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ vijñānasyānyathāvagamāt nirvyāpārasaṃkleśabyavadānadharmamātraparīkṣaṇācceti / punareṣāṃ yathākramaṃ catuḥsatyāvatāraḥ phalam
# ltung bas yid la gcags pas ni 'gro ba dang ldog pa la sogs pa la shes bzhin med par spyod pa ste / / sngar bslab pa dang 'gal nas phyis 'gyod pa'o / / brtson pa 'dor ba ni bag med pa'i nyes pas dge ba'i phyogs ji ltar brtsams pa la sbyor ba mthar mi 'byin pa'o / / 'bras bu ni go rims bzhin du dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la gtsang ba dang bde ba dang rtag pa dang bdag tu phyin ci log spang ba ste / / mi sdug pa bsgom pa'i phyir ro / / gang ci tshor yang rung ste / / de ni 'di ltar sdug bsngal bar shes pa'i phyir ro / / gnas dang dmigs pa la sogs pa'i bye brag gis rnam par shes pa skad cig re re la gzhan du 'gyur bar rtogs pa'i phyir ro / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba chos tsam du zad de byed pa med par yongs su rtogs pa'i phyir ro / / yang 'di dag gi 'bras bu ni go rims bzhin du bden pa bzhi la 'jug ste /
kāyasmṛtyupasthānena duḥkhasatyamavatarati saṃskāraduḥkhatālakṣaṇena dauṣṭhulyena prabhāvitatvāt kāyasya / tathāhi tatpratipakṣabhūtā prasrabdhiḥ kāya eva viśeṣeṇotpadyata iti
# lus dran pa nye bar gzhag pas ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa la 'jug ste / / lus ni 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal gyi mtshan nyid gnas ngan len gyis rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro / / 'di ltar de'i gnyen por gyur pa shin tu sbyangs pa ni lus nyid la khyad par can du 'byung ngo /
vedanāsmṛtyupasthānena samudayasatyamavatarati sukhādivedanādhiṣṭhānatvāt saṃyogāditṛṣṇāyāḥ / cittasmṛtyupasthānena nirodhasatyamavatarati nirātmakaṃ vijñānamātraṃ na bhaviṣyatīti paśyata ātmocchedāśaṅkāmukhena nirvāṇottrāsābhāvāt
# tshor ba dran pa nye bar gzhag pas ni kun 'byung gi bden pa la 'jug ste / / phrad pa la sogs par srid pa ni bde ba la sogs pa'i tshor ba'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / sems dran pa nye bar gzhag bas ni 'gog pa'i bden pa la 'jug ste / / bdag med cing rnam par shes pa tsam med par 'gyur ba lta bas na / / bdag chad par 'dogs pa'i sgo nas mya ngan las 'das pa la skrag pa med pa'i phyir ro /
dharmasmṛtyupasthānena mārgasatyamavatarati vipakṣadharmaprahāṇāya pratipakṣadharmabhāvanāditi / punareṣāṃ kāyavedanācittadharmavisaṃyogaḥ phalaṃ yathākramaṃ veditavyam tadbhāvanayā kāyādipakṣadauṣṭhulyāpagamāditi
# chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pas ni lam gyi bden pa la 'jug ste / / mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi chos spong ba dang gnyen po'i chos la brten pa'i phyir ro / / yang 'di dag gi 'bras bu ni lus dang tshor ba dang sems dang chos dang bral bar go rims bzhin du rig par bya ste / / de dag bsgoms pas lus la sogs pa'i phyogs kyi gnas ngan len dang bral ba'i phyir ro /
samyakprahāṇānāṃ prathamasyānutpanno vipakṣa ālaṃbanam tenānutpannapāpakākuśaladharmānutpādāya chandajananāt
# yang dag par spong ba rnams kyi dang po'i dmigs pa ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs skyes pa ste / / des sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams spang ba'i phyir 'dun pa skyed pa'i phyir ro /
dvitīyasyotpanno vipakṣaḥ / tṛtīyasyānutpannaḥ pratipakṣaḥ / caturthasyotpanna ālaṃbanamiti yathāsūtraṃ yojayitavyam
# gnyis pa'i dmigs pas ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma skyes pa dang gsum pa'i dmigs pa ni gnyen po ma skyes pa dang bzhi pa'i dmigs pa ni gnyen po skyes pa ste / / ji ltar mdo sde las 'byung ba bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o /
chandaṃ janayatītyevamādibhiḥ sāśrayā vīryabhāvanā paridīpitā
# 'dun pa skyed do zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i tshig rnams kyis ni brtson 'grus bsgom pa gnas dang bcas pa yongs su bstan to /
atrāśrayaśchandaḥ tatpūrvakatvādudyogasya / yadā śamathādinimittamanaskāreṇa nirapekṣālaṃbanaṃ kevalaṃ pratipakṣaṃ bhāvayati tadā vyāyaccjhata ityucyate
# de la gnas ni 'dun pa ste / / de ni brtson 'grus rtsom pa'i sngon du 'gro ba'i phyir ro / / gang gi tshe zhi gnas kyi mtshan ma yid la byed pas gnyen po skyon med pa 'ba' zhig sgom pa de'i tshe 'bad pa zhes bya'o /
yadā tulayopakleśe utpanne tadapakarṣaṇārtha prasadanīyādimanaskāraiḥ cittamunnāmayati auddhatyopakleśe cotpanne pratyāsaṃkṣepamukhena cittaṃ dhārayati tadā vīryamārabhata ityucyate / ata eva layauddhatyāpakarṣaṇopāyasaṃdarśanārthamanantaramāha cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti pradadhātīti
# gang gi tshe nye ba'i nyon mongs pa bying ba 'byung ba de bsal ba'i phyir dga' bar gyur pa la sogs pa'i yid la byed pa rnams kyis sems 'bar bar byed pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rgod pa byung ba na nang du sdud pa'i sgo nas sems 'dzin pa de'i tshe brtson 'grus rtsom pa zhes bya'o / / de'i phyir bying ba dang rgod pa bsal ba'i thabs bstan pa'i phyir de'i 'og tu sems rab tu 'dzin pa dang rab tu 'jog pa smos so /
phalaṃ prathamadvitīyayoḥ samyakprahāṇayoraśeṣavipakṣahāniḥ tābhyāṃ yathāyogamutpannānutpannapāpakākuśaladharmaprahāṇāt
# 'bras bu ni yang dag pa'i spong ba dang po dang gnyis pa'i ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma lus par nyams pa ste / / de gnyis kyis ji ltar mthun mthun du sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa dang ma skyes pa'i chos rnams nyams par byed pa'i phyir ro /
tṛtīyasya pratipakṣapratilambhaḥ tenānutpannakuśaladharmotpādanāt
# gsum pa'i ni gnyen po thob pa ste / / des dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa skyed pa'i phyir ro /
caturthasya pratipakṣavṛddhiḥ tenotpannakuśaladharmavipulatāpādanāditi
# bzhi pa'i ni gnyen po thob bas 'phel ba ste / / des dge ba'i chos skyes pa spong bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
ṛddhipādālaṃbanaṃ niṣpannena samādhinā yatkaraṇīyamṛddhayādikaṃ kṛtyam
# rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang ba rnams kyi dmigs pa ni ting nge 'dzin gyis grub pa'i bya ba rdzu 'phrul la sogs pa'i bye brag gang yin pa'o /
chandasamādhiryat satkṛtyaprayogamāgamya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratāṃ tīvreṇa chandena tīvreṇādareṇa prayogaḥ satkṛtyaprayoga iti kṛtvā
# 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni gang gus par sbyor ba la brten nas sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa ste / / gus par sbyor ba ni 'dun pa drag po dang rim gro cher byas te sbyor ba'o /
vīryasamādhiryatsātatyaprayogamāgamya spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām / tadvīryamityucyate yannityaṃ prayujyata eva na kadācinna prayujyate / cittasamādhiryatpūrvajanmāntare samādhibhāvanāmāgamyatatparipuṣṭabījatvāccittasya svarasena samādhyanukūlapariṇāme sati spṛśati cittasyaikāgratām
# brtson 'grus kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang rgyun du sbyor ba la brten nas sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa ste / / gang rtag tu sbyor zhing nam yang mi sbyor ba ma yin pa de ni brtson 'grus zhes bya'o / / sems kyi ting nge 'dzin ni sngon gang gi tshe rabs gzhan na ting nge 'dzin bsgoms pa la brten nas des sems kyi sa bon yongs su brtas pa'i phyir rang gi ngang gis ting nge 'dzin gyi rjes su mthun par gyur na sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o /
api khalu ṛddhipādābhinirhārayornidarśanārthameva samyakprahāṇabhāvanāyāṃ chandaṃ janayatītyevamādinirdeśo veditavyaḥ / cittaṃ pradadhāti pragṛhṇātītyeṣā cātra pāṭhānupūrvī veditavyā
# rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa mngon par sgrub pa'i rgyu yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir yang dag par spong ba bsgom pa la 'dun pa skyed do zhes bya ba la sogs pas bstan par rig par bya'o / / sems rab tu 'jog pa dang rab tu 'dzin zhes bya ba de ni 'dir brjod pa'i lugs kyi go rims su rig par bya'o /
tatra cittasamādhiryaccitaṃ pradadhat spṛśatīti pratyātmaṃ cittameva cittaṃ dhārayan śamayannabhisaṃkṣipannadhigacchatītyarthaḥ
# de la sems kyi ting nge 'dzin ni gang sems rab tu 'jog pa ni sems rtse gcig pa nyid la reg pa'o zhes bya ba ni sems nyid kyis sems nang du 'dzin zhing zhi bar byed / / sdud par byed / / 'thob par byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
mīmāṃsāsamādhiryaccitaṃ pragṛhṇanniti dharmavipaśyanāmukhena cittamuttāpayatītyarthaḥ / bhāvanā chandādīnāmaṣṭānāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāmabhyāsaḥ
# dpyod pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni sems rab tu 'dzin pa na zhes bya ba ni chos la lhag mthong gi sgo nas sems 'bar bar byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / bsgom pa ni 'dun pa la sogs pa spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad goms par byed pa'o /
te punaraṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārāścaturdhā kriyante
# spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad po de dag ni rnam pa bzhir rig par bya ste /
tadyathā vyāvasāyikaśchandavyāyāmaśraddhāḥ / tatra chando vyāyāmasyāśrayaḥ
# 'di lta ste / / 'bad pa ni 'dun pa dang rtsol ba dang dad pa'o / / de la 'dun pa ni rtsol ba'i gnas so /
chandasya punaḥ śraddhā nimittam / tathāhi yo yenārthī bhavati tatprāptyartha vyāyacchate
# 'dun pa'i rgyu ni dad pa ste / / 'di ltar gang zag gang zhig don du gnyer bar 'gyur ba de ni de thob par bya ba'i phyir rtsol lo /
arthitvaṃ ca nāntareṇa tadasti tvādyabhisaṃpratyamiti
# de yod pa nyid la sogs pa yid ches pa med na don du gnyer bar mi 'gyur ro /
anugrāhikaḥ prasrabdhiḥ tayā kāyacittānugrahakaraṇāt / aupanibandhikaḥ smṛtisaṃprajanye ālaṃbanāsaṃpramoṣeṇa cittasyaikāgrāvasthānāt tatpramāde ca sati paricchedāt yathākramam
# phan 'dogs pa ni shin tu sbyangs pa ste / / des lus dang sems la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir ro / / nye bar 'dogs pa ni dran pa dang shes bzhin te / / dmigs pa ma brjed pas sems rtse gcig pa nyid la 'jug pa dang de la bag med par gyur na yongs su gcod pa'i phyir te / / go rims bzhin no /
prātipakṣikaścetanopekṣe cittapragrahapradhānābhisaṃskārābhyāmutpannalayauddhatyaparivarjanānnirupakleśaśamathādinimittānukaraṇācceti
# gnyen po ni sems pa dang btang snyoms te / / sems rab tu 'dzin pa dang rab tu 'jog pa mngon bar 'du byed pas bying ba dang rgod pa 'byung ba yongs su spong ba dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa med pa ni zhi gnas la sogs pa'i mtshan ma rjes su 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
saṃkṣepanidānaṃ vipaśyanārahitasya kausīdyamukhena layaḥ / vikṣepanidānamaśubhasaṃjñārahitasyauddhatyamukhena saṃpragrahaḥ
# yang 'dun pa la sogs pa'i sdud pa dang g yeng ba bzhi dang bcas par yongs su spangs pa la sogs pa sgom pa de la sdud pa'i gzhi ni lhag mthong dang bral ba ste / / le lo'i sgo nas bying bar 'gyur ro / / g yeng ba'i gzhi ni mi sdug pa'i 'du shes dang bral ba ste /
saṃkṣepaḥ styānanimittamukhe nāntaḥsaṃkocaḥ
# rgod pa'i sgo nas yang dag par rab tu mi 'dzin to /
vikṣepaḥ śubhanimittānusāramukhena viṣayeṣu visāraḥ / ālīnatvānukūlā bhāvanā pratyavekṣaṇānimittaṃ niśritya dharmavipaśyanā / avikṣepānukūlāśubhataḥ keśādidravyapratyavekṣā
# sdud pa ni rmugs pa dang gnyid kyi sgo nas nang du zhum pa'o / / g yeng ba ni sdug pa'i mtshan ma'i rjes su 'brang ba'i sgo nas yul rnams la rnam par 'phro ba'o / / zhum pa med pa dang mthun pa'i sgom pa ni so sor rtog pa'i mtshan ma la brten nas chos la rnam par blta ba'o / / g yeng ba med pa dang mthun pa ni skra la sogs pa'i rdzas la mi gtsang bar so sor rtog pa'o /
tadubhayānukūlālokasaṃjñā
# de gnyi ga dang mthun pa ni snang ba'i 'du shes so /
etacca yathā kramamadhikṛtyoktaṃ bhagavatā naca me chando 'tilīno bhaviṣyati nātipragṛhītaḥ nādhyātmaṃ saṃkṣiptaḥ na bahirdhā vikṣiptaḥ paścātpūrvasaṃjñī bhaviṣyati ūrdhvamadhaḥsaṃjñī ca vivṛtena cetasāparyavanaddhena saprabhāsasahagataṃ cittaṃ bhāvayiṣyāmi na ca me 'ndhakārāyattatvaṃ bhaviṣyati cetasa iti
# de yang bdag gi 'dun pa ha cang yang zhum par yang me 'gyur ba dang ha cang rab tu gzung bar yang ma yin pa dang nang du bsdus pa yang ma yin pa dang phyi rol tu g yeng ba yang ma yin pa dang phyi ma dang snga ma'i 'du shes dang steng dang 'og gi 'du shes su bya'o snyam pa dang de ltar rnam par phye ba'i sems kun nas dkris pa med pas snang ba dang ldan pa'i sems bsgom par bya'i bdag gi sems mun pa can gyi tshul du ni mi 'gyur bar bya'o zhes bya ba'i dbang du mdzad nas / / bcom ldan 'das kyis go rims bzhin du gsungs so /
phalaṃ yatheṣṭamṛddhayādiguṇaniṣpādanāt / indriyāṇāṃ catvāryāryasatyānyālaṃbanam satyābhisamayaprayogasaṃgṛhītatvena tadākāratvāt
# 'bras bu ni ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du rdzu 'phrul la sogs pa'i yon tan bsgrub pa'i phyir ro / / dbang po rnams kyi dmigs pa ni 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po rnams te / / bden ba mngon par rtogs pa la sbyor bas bsdus pas de'i rnam par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
phalaṃ tadādhipatyādacireṇa kālena darśanamārgasyotpādaḥ tasminneva ca kāle nirvedhabhāgīyabhajanaṃ ca saṃtānasya
# 'bras bu ni de'i dbang gis ring por mi thogs par mthong ba'i lam skye ba dang de nyid kyi dus na nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa la brten pa'i sems kyi rgyud do /
balānāmālaṃbanādikamindriyaiḥ samānam
# stobs rnams kyis dmigs pa la sogs pa ni dbang po rnams dang mthun no /
phale tu viśeṣaḥ / tathāhyeṣāṃ tacca yathoktam āśradvyādivipakṣanirlekhaścādhika ityata evaiṣāṃ tulyānāmālaṃbanasvabhāvādikānāmapyanavamṛdyatārthaviśeṣeṇa bodhipakṣāntaratvam
# 'bras bu la ni bye brag yod de / / 'di ltar de dag gi 'bras bu de ni ji skad du / / ma dad pa la sogs pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs bsrabs pas lhag par bstan pa ste / / de'i phyir 'di dag gis dmigs pa dang ngo bo nyid la sogs pa mthun du zin yang mi brdzi ba'i don gyi bye brag gis byang chub kyi phyogs gzhan nyid do /
bodhyaṅgānāmālaṃbanaṃ caturṇāmāryasatyānāṃ yathābhūtateti paramārtho viśuddhayālaṃbanamityarthaḥ / svabhāvaḥ smṛtyādayaḥ sapta dharmāḥ
# byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyi dmigs pa ni 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag gi yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba'o zhes bya ba ni don dam pa rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / ngo bo nyid ni dran pa la sogs pa'i chos bdun no /
tatra smṛtiḥ saṃniśrayāṅgam upasthitasmṛteḥ sarvakuśaladharmābhilapanāt
# de la dran pa ni gnas kyi yan lag ste / / dran pa nye bar gnas pa ni dge ba'i chos thams cad mngon bar brjod pa'i phyir ro /
dharmavicayaḥ svabhāvāṅgam saṃbodhilakṣaṇatvāt
# chos rnam par 'byed pa ni ngo bo nyid kyi yan lag ste / / byang chub kyi mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
vīryaṃ niryāṇāṅgam tena yāvadgamyaṃ gamanāt
# brtson 'grus ni nges par 'byung ba'i yan lag ste / / des bgrod pa ji srid par 'gro ba'i phyir ro /
prītiranuśaṃsāṅgam tayā saṃtānaprīṇanāt
# dga' ba ni phan yon gyi yan lag ste / / des sems kyi rgyud tshim par byed pa'i phyir ro /
prasrabdhiḥ samādhirupekṣā cāsaṃkleśāṅgam / tatra prasrabdhyā na saṃkliśyate tayā dauṣṭhulyasrāvaṇāt
# shin tu sbyangs pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang btang snyoms ni kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i yan lag ste / / de la shin tu sbyangs pas ni kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur te / / des gnas ngan len 'jig pa'i phyir ro /
samādhau na saṃkliśyate tatra sthitasyāśrayaparivartanāt
# ting nge 'dzin ni kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur te / / de la gnas 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
upekṣāsaṃkleśaḥ abhidhyādaurmanasyāpagatākliṣṭāvasthāsvabhāvatvāt / bhāvanā smṛtisaṃbodhyaṅgaṃ bhāvayati vivekaniśritamityevamādirebhiḥ caturbhiḥ padairyathākramaṃ catuḥsatyālaṃbanā bodhyaṅgabhāvanā paridīpitā
# btang snyoms ni kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa ste / / brnab sems dang yid mi bde ba dang bral ba nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i gnas skabs kyi ngo bo nyid yin pa'i phyir ro / / bsgom pa ni dran pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag dben pa la gnas pa bsgom pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste / / tshig 'di dag dang go rims bzhin du 'phags pa'i bden pa la dmigs pa ni byang chub kyi yan lag bsgom pa yongs su bstan pa yin te /
tathāhi duḥkhaṃ duḥkhata ālaṃbamānasya tadvivekānveṣaṇādduḥkhālaṃbanaṃ vivekaniśritamityucyate / tṛṣṇālakṣaṇaṃ duḥkhasamudayaṃ duḥkhasamudayata ālaṃbamānasya tadvirāgānveṣaṇāttadālaṃbanaṃ virāganiśritam / duḥkhanirodhaṃ duḥkhanirodhata ālaṃbamānasya tatsākṣātkaraṇānveṣaṇāttadālaṃbanaṃ nirodhaniśritam
# 'di ltar sdug bsngal la sdug bsngal nyid du dmigs pa ni de las dben ba tshol bas sdug bsngal la dmigs pa ni dben pa la gnas pa zhes bya'o / / srid pa'i mtshan nyid ni sdug bsngal kun 'byung ba ste / / sdug bsngal kun 'byung bar dmigs pa ni de dang bral ba tshol bas de la dmigs pa ni 'dod chags dang bral ba la gnas pa'o / / sdug bsngal 'gog pa la sdug bsngal 'gog par dmigs pa ni de mngon sum du byed par 'dod pas de la dmigs pa ni 'gog pa la gnas pa'o /
duḥkhanirodhagāminī pratipad vyavasarga ityucyate tayā duḥkhavisarjanāt / tāṃ tathālaṃbamānasya tadbhāvanānveṣaṇāttadālaṃbanaṃ vyavasargapariṇatamityucyate
# sdug bsngal 'gog par 'gro ba'i lam ni des sdug bsngal rnams spong ba'i phyir rnam par spong ba zhes bya'o / / de la de ltar dmigs pa ni bsgom pa tshol bas de la dmigs pa ni rnam par spong bas yongs su bsgyur ba zhes bya'o /
