phalaṃ darśanaheyānāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇam bodhyaṅgānāṃ darśanamārgasvabhāvatvāt / mārgāṅgānāmālaṃbanaṃ darśanamārgāduttarakālaṃ saiva yathādṛṣṭānāṃ satyānāṃ yathābhūtatā
# 'bras bu ni mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams spangs pa ste / / byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyi mthong ba'i lam gyi ngo bo nyid yin pa'i phyir ro / / lam gyi yan lag rnams kyi dmigs pa ni de'i 'og tu bden pa ji ltar mthong ba rnams kyi yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba de nyid do /
svabhāvaḥ samyagdṛṣṭayādayo 'ṣṭau dharmāḥ
# ngo bo nyid ni yang dag pa'i lta ba la sogs pa chos brgyad po rnams so /
tatra samyagdṛṣṭiḥ paricchedāṅgam tayā yathānubhavaṃ tattvāvadhāraṇāt
# de la yang dag pa'i lta ba ni yongs su gcod pa'i yan lag ste / / des ji ltar myong ba'i de kho na nges par 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
samyaksaṃkalpaḥ parasaṃprāpaṇāṅgam tena yathādhigamaṃ vyavasthāpya vāksamutthāpanāt
# yang dag pa'i rtog pa ni gzhan go bar byed pa'i yan lag ste / / des ji ltar rtog pa rnam par bzhag nas ngag kun nas slong ba'i phyir ro /
samyagvākkarmāntājīvāḥ parasaṃpratyayāṅgam tairyathākramamadhigantuḥ paraidṛṣṭayādiviśuddhiniścayanāt
# yang dag pa'i ngag dang las kyi mtha' dang 'tsho ba ni gzhan yid ches par byed pa'i yan lag ste / / de dag gi rtogs pa dang lnga na ba'i lta ba la sogs pa rnam par dag pa'i go rims bzhin du gzhan dag gis gtan la 'bebs pa'i phyir ro /
tatra samyagvācādhigamānurūpapraśnavyākaraṇasāṃkathyaviniścayenāsya darśanaviśuddhirvijñāyate
# de la yang dag pa'i ngag gis ni rtogs pa dang mthun par 'dri ba dang lung ston pa 'bel ba'i gtam gtan la 'bebs pas de'i lta ba rnam par dag par rnam par shes so /
samyakkarmāntenābhikramapratikramādiṣu saṃpannacāritratayā śīlaviśuddhiḥ samyagājīvena yathānujñaṃ dharmeṇa cīvarādiparyeṣaṇādājīvaviśuddhiriti
# yang dag pa'i lam gyi mthas ni 'gro ba dang ldog pa la sogs pa la spyod pa phun su ma tshogs pas tshul khrims rnam par dag par rnam par shes so / / yang dag pa'i 'tsho bas ni ji ltar gnang ba bzhin du chos dang mthun pas gos la sogs pa tshol bas yang dag pa'i 'tsho ba rnam par dag par rnam par shes so / / yang dag pa'i rtsol bas ni /
samyagvyāyāmaḥ kleśāvaraṇaviśodhanāṅgam tenāśeṣa saṃyojanaprahāṇāt
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par sbyor ba'i yan lag ste / / des kun tu sbyor ba lhag ma spong ba'i phyir ro /
samyaksmṛtirupakleśāvaraṇaviśodhanāṅgam tayā samyakśamathādinimittāsaṃpramoṣeṇa layādyupakleśānavakāśāt / samyaksamādhirvaiśeṣikaguṇāvaraṇaviśodhanāṅgam tenābhijñādiguṇābhinirharaṇāt / bhāvanā bodhyaṅgavat tadyathā samyagdṛṣṭiṃ bhāvayati vivekaniśritāmiti vistaraḥ
# yang dag pa'i dran pas ni nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i yan lag ste / / des yang dag pa'i zhi gnas la sogs pa'i mtshan ma ma brjed pas nye ba'i nyon mongs pa bya ba la sogs pa'i skabs med pa'i phyir ro / / yang dag pa'i ting nge 'dzin ni yon tan khyad par can la sgrib pa rnam par sbyong pa'i yan lag ste / / des mngon par shes pa la sogs pa'i yon tan mngon par sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
teṣāṃ ca padānāmarthaḥ yathānirdiṣṭaṃ purastāttathānugantavyaḥ / pratipadāṃ dharmapadānāṃ ca pūrvavadarthanirdeśo veditavyaḥ dukhā pratipadanāgamyārūpyaniśritā yathākramaṃ śamathavipaśyanāmāndhāt / sukhā dhyānaniśritā yuganaddhavāhitvāt dhandhābhijñā dvayorapyanayorduḥkhasukhaniśrayayormṛdvindriyāṇām / kṣiprābhijñā tayoreva tīkṣṇendriyāṇāmiti / śamathaḥ navakāracittasthitiḥ / tatra bāhyālaṃbanebhyaḥ pratisaṃhṛtyā dhyātmamavikṣepāpāditaścittasyopanibandhaḥ sthāpanā / tasya cittasyaivamādita upanibaddhasya calasyaudārikasya tasminnevālaṃbane saṃtatiyogena sūkṣmīkaraṇena cābhisaṃkṣepaḥ saṃsthāpanā / tasya smṛtisaṃpramoṣādvahirdhā vikṣiptasya punaḥ pratisaṃharaṇamavasthāpanā / ādita eva tasya cittasya bahiravisārāyopasthitasmṛtitopasthāpanā
# bsgom pa ni byang chub kyi yan lag bzhin te / / 'di lta ste / / yang dag pa'i lta ba dben pa la gnas pa bsgom pa zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o / / lam dang chos kyi gnas rnams kyi don ni snga ma bzhin du bshad par rig par bya'o / / zhi gnas ni sems gnas pa rnam pa dgu ste / / de la phyi rol gyi dmigs pa rnams las phyir blan nas nang du mi g yeng bar gang dang po nyid du sems nye bar 'dogs pa ni 'jog pa'o / / de ltar sems g yo ba rags pa thog ma nyid du nye bar brtags pa de dmigs pa de nyid la rgyun gyi tshul dang phra bar byed pas mngon par bsdus pa ni rgyun du 'jog pa'o / / brjed nas phyi rol tu g yengs par gyur pa de yang phyir bkug pa ste / / brlan te 'jog pa'o / / sems phyi rol tu mi 'phro bar bya ba'i phyir thog ma nyid du dran ba nye bar gnas pa ni nye bar 'jog pa'o /
pūrvameva vikṣepanimitteṣu rūpādiṣvādīnavasaṃjñāmadhipati kṛtvā cittasya prasarādānaṃ damanam
# rnam par g yeng ba'i rgyu gzugs la sogs pa la nyes dmigs kyi 'du shes kyi dbang du byas nas thog ma nyid du sems rab tu 'phror mi ster ba ni dul bar byed pa'o /
cetaḥsaṃkṣobhakareṣu vitarkopakleśeṣvādīnavadarśanena prasarādānaṃ śamanam
# sems 'khrug par byed pa nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnam par rtog par byed pa la nyes dmigs su lta bas 'phror mi ster ba ni zhi bar byed pa'o /
smṛtisaṃpramoṣādvitarkādisamudācāre sati tadanadhivāsanā vyupaśamanam
# brjed nas rnam par rtog pa la sogs pa kun tu 'byung ba na de dang du mi len ba ni rnam par zhi bar byed pa'o /
abhisaṃskāreṇa niśchidranirantarasamādhipravāhāvasthāpanā ekotīkaraṇam
# mngon par 'du byed pas skabs med cing bar chad med par ting nge 'dzin rgyun du brlan te 'jog pa ni rtse gcig tu byed pa'o /
svabhyastatvādanabhisaṃskāreṇānābhogena cittasamādhipravāhasyāvikṣepeṇa pravṛttiḥ samādhānamiti
# shin tu goms pa'i phyir mngon par 'du byed pa med cing lhun gyis grub par sems kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyun g yeng ba med par 'byung ba ni mnyam par 'jog pa'o /
vipaśyanā yathāpi taddharmānvicinotītyevamādiḥ / tatra caritaviśodhanamālaṃbanaṃ kauśalyālaṃbanaṃ vā kleśaviśodhanaṃ vā yāvadbhāvikatayā vicinoti yathāvadbhāvikatayā pravicinoti savikalpenamanaskāreṇa prajñāsahagatena nimittīkurvan parivitarkayati saṃntīrayan parimīmāṃsāmāpadyata iti / api khalu śamathavipaśyanāmāgamya catvāro mārgā iti catvāro mārgopadeśanāmadhikṛtya
# lhag mthong ni 'di lta ste; chos rnams la rnam par 'byed pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste / / de la dpyod pa rnam par sbyong ba la dmigs pa'am / / mkhas pa la dmigs pa'am / / nyon mongs pa rnam par sbyong ba'ang rung ste / / ji snyed yod pas rnam par 'byed pa'o / / ji lta ba bzhin du yod pas rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'o / / rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i yid la byed pa shes rab dang bcas pas mtshan mar byed pa ni yongs su rnam par rtog pa'o / / kun tu rtog pa ni yongs su dpyod par byed pa'o / / yang zhi gnas dang lhag mthong la brten nas lam bzhir 'gyur te zhes bya ba ni lam bzhi bsten pa'i dbang du byas pa ste /
tatra prathamaḥ śamathasya lābhitvādabhiniṣīdanneva cittaṃ sthāpayati yāvatsamādhatte vipaśyānāyā alābhitvāttu samādhiṃ niśritya paścāttathāniṣaṇṇastān dharmānvicinoti yāvatparimīmāṃsāmāpadyate
# de la dang po ni zhi gnas thob pa'i phyir 'dug bzhin du sems 'jog pa nas mnyam par 'jog pa'i bar dang lhag mthong ma thob pa'i phyir ting nge 'dzin de la brten nas phyis de bzhin du 'dug ste / / chos de dag la rnam par 'byed pa nas yongs su dpyod par byed pa'i bar ngu'o; /
dvitīyo viparyayeṇa veditavyaḥ
# gnyis pa ni de las zlog par byed par rig par bya'o /
tṛtīyā ubhayasyālābhyubhayatra yogaṃ karoti
# gsum pa ni gnyi ga ma thob pa ste gnyi ga la brtson par byed do /
kathaṃ kṛtvā śrutodgrahaṇamukhena vivaśyanāyāṃ yogaṃ karoti tatpūrvakaṃ ca śamathe
# ji ltar zhe na thos pa 'dzin pa'i sgo nas lhag mthong la brtson par byed do / / de sngon du 'gro bas zhi gnas la brtson par byed do /
caturtha ubhayasya lābhāt / ajñātamājñāsyāmīndriyaṃ prayogamārge nirvedhabhāgīyasaṃgṛhīte pañcadaśasu ca darśanamārgacittakṣaṇeṣu yadindriyam tadyathā manaindriyam pañca śraddhādīni anāgamyādiniśrayabhedena yathāsaṃbhavaṃ sukhasaumanasya daurmanasyopekṣendriyāṇāṃ cānyatamam / daurmanasyendriyaṃ punaḥ prayogakāle nirvedhabhāgīyapṛṣṭhenottaravimokṣaspṛhāsaṃgṛhītaṃ veditavyam
# bzhi ba ni gnyi ga thob pa'o / / mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po ni sbyor ba'i lam nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pas bsdus pa dang mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bco lnga po dag la dbang po gang yin pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / yid kyi dbang po dang dad pa la sogs pa lnga dang mi lcogs pa med pa la sogs pa gnas kyi bye brag gis ji ltar mthun mthun du bde ba dang yid mi bde ba dang btang snyoms kyi dbang po rnams las gang yang rung ba'o / / yid mi bde ba'i dbang po ni sbyor ba'i dus na nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i rjes la rnam par thar pa mchog 'dod pas bsdus par rig par bya'o /
tadetatsaṃbhavato daśavidhamindriyamanājñātapūrvasya tattvasyājñāyai pravṛttatvādanājñātamājñāsyāmīndriyamityucyate
# de dag ni srid pas dbang po rnam pa bcu ste / / de kho na sngon mi shes pa kun shes par bya ba'i phyir zhugs pas mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po zhes bya'o /
etadeva daśavidhamindriyaṃ ṣoḍaśāddarśanamārgacittakṣaṇādyāvadvajropamaḥ samādhirityetasminśaikṣamārge ājñendriyamityucyate apūrvajñeyābhāvāt
# dbang po rnam pa bcu po 'di dag nyid mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bcu drug pa nas rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin ces bya ba'i bar du slob pa'i lam de la kun shes pa'i dbang po zhes bya ste / / sngon ma mthong ba'i shes bya med pa'i phyir ro /
etadeva punarnavavidhamindriyaṃ daurmanasyendriyavarjamaśaikṣamārge ājñātāvīndriyamityucyate ājñātāvino 'rhat indriyamiti kṛtvā / bhāvanā mārgādhikāreṇedamapi vakṣyate
# yid mi bde ba'i dbang po ma rtogs par dbang po rnam pa dgu po de dag nyid mi slob pa'i lam la kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang po zhes bya ste / / kun shes pa dang ldan pa ni dgra bcom pa'i dbang po yin pa'i phyir ro; / / bsgom pa'i lam gyi skabs su 'di yang brjod par bya ste /
ūrdhvabhūmike mārge saṃmukhībhāvena bhāvyamāne 'saṃmukhībhūtānyapyadhobhūmikāni kuśalamūlakāni bhāvanāṃ gacchanti teṣu vibhutvalābhāt
# gong ma'i sa pa'i lam la mngon du byed pa bsgom pa na sa 'og ma'i dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon sum du ma gyur pa rnams kyang bsgom par 'gyur te / / de dag la dbang 'byor ba thob pa'i phyir ro /
vibhutvaṃ punaruttaptasaṃmukhībhāvena taśitā veditavyā
# dbang 'byor ba ni mchog tu sbyangs pa thob pa ste / / mngon sum du byed pa ni dbang du rig par bya'o /
niṣṭhāmārgaḥ sarvadauṣṭhulyānāṃ pratiprasrabdheriti vistaraḥ / tatra sarvadauṣṭhulyāni caturvitirbhavanti
# mthar phyin pa'i lam ni gnas ngan len thams cad rgyun chad pa zhes rgya cher 'byung ba de la gnas ngan len thams cad ni nyi shu rtsa bzhi yin te / / 'di lta ste /
tadyathā sarvatragamabhilāpadauṣṭhulyaṃ yā cakṣurādisarvadharmanāmābhiniveśavāsanālayavijñāne saṃniviṣṭānādikālānusṛtā yāsāvucyate prapañcavāsaneti yataścakṣurādayo dharmāḥ sanāmābhiniveśāḥ punaḥ punaḥ pravartanta iti
# mngon par brjod pa'i gnas ngan len ni kun tu 'gro ba ni mig la sogs pa chos thams cad kyi ming la mngon bar zhen pa'i bag chags kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa thog ma med pa'i dus nas rjes su zhugs pa gang yin pa ste / / de las mig la sogs pa'i chos ming la mngon par zhen pa dang bcas pa rnams yang dang yang 'byung ba'i phyir te de ni spros pa'i bag chags zhes bya'o /
veditadauṣṭhulyaṃ sāsravāṇāṃ vedanānāṃ vāsanā
# tshor ba'i gnas ngan len ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i tshor ba rnams kyi bag chags so /
kleśadauṣṭhulyaṃ kleśānāmanuśayaḥ
# nyon mongs pa'i gnas ngan len ni nyon mongs pa rnams kyi bag la nyal lo /
karmadauṣṭhulyaṃ sāsravāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ vāsanā
# las kyi gnas ngan len ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i las rnams kyi bag chags so /
vipākadauṣṭhulyaṃ vipākasyā karmaṇyatā
# rnam par smin pa'i gnas ngan len ni rnam par smin pa'i lus las su mi rung ba nyid do /
kleśāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ tīvrāyatakleśatā
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len ni nyon mongs pa mi bzad cing rgyun ring ba'o /
karmāvaraṇadauṣṭhalyaṃ mārgāntarāyikānantaryādikakarmāvṛtatā
# las kyi sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len ni lam gyi bar chad byed pa mtshams med pa la sogs pa'i las kyi sgrib pa nyid do /
vipākāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ satyābhisamayavidhuranārakādyātma bhāvapratilambhaḥ
# rnam par smin pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len ni bden pa mngon par rtogs pa dang mi mthun pa sems can dmyal ba la sogs pa'i lus thob pa'o /
nivaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ kuśalapakṣaprayogāntarāyikakāmachandādyabhibhūtatā
# sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len ni dge ba'i phyogs la sbyor ba'i bar chad byed pa 'dod pa la 'dun pa la sogs pas zil gyis gnon pa nyid do /
vitarkadauṣṭhulyaṃ pravrajyābhirati vibandhakāmavitarkādyabhibhūtatā
# rtog pa'i gnas ngan len ni rab tu 'byung ba la gags byed pa 'dod pa la rnam par rtog pa la sogs pas zil byis gnon pa nyid do /
āhāradauṣṭhulyamatyalpabahubhojananena prayogāyogyatā / maithunadauṣṭhulyaṃ dvayadvayasamāpattikṛtā kāyacittavyathā
# zas kyi gnas ngan len ni za ha cang nyung ba dang mang du zos pas sbyor ba'i 'os sum gyur ba nyid do / / 'khrig pa'i gnas ngan len ni gnyis kyis gnyis phrad pa las gyur pa dang lus dang sems la gnod pa'o /
svapnadauṣṭhulyaṃ middhakṛtamāśrayajāḍyam
# rmi lam gyi gnas ngan len ni gnyid las gyur ba'i lus sems po nyid do /
vyādhidauṣṭhulyaṃ dhātuvaiṣamyakṛtāsvasthatā
# nad kyi gnas ngan len ni khams ma snyoms pa las gyur ba'i nyams rab tu mi bde ba nyid do /
jarādauṣṭhulyaṃ bhūtavipariṇāmakṛtāvidheyatā
# rga ba'i gnas ngan len ni 'byung bar 'gyur ba las gyur ba'i dbang med pa nyid do /
maraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ mriyamāṇasya sarvendriyākulatā
# 'chi ba'i gnas ngan len ni 'chi ba na dbang po thams cad 'khrug pa'o /
pariśramadauṣṭhulyamatigamanādikṛto 'ṅgamardaḥ
# yongs su ngal ba'i gnas ngan len ni ha cang 'gro ba las gyur ba'i lus dub pa'o /
dṛḍhadauṣṭhulyaṃ yathāsaṃbhavameta devābhilāpadauṣṭhulyādikamaparinirvāṇavatām
# gnas ngan len bstan pa ni mngon par brjod pa'i gnas ngan len la sogs pa 'di dag dang ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar te / / yongs su mya ngan las mi 'da' ba'i chos can no /
audārikamadhyasūkṣmadauṣṭhulyāni yathākramaṃ kāmarūpārūpyāvacarāṇi veditavyāni
# gnas ngan len chen po dang 'bring dang chung du ni go rims bzhin du 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa rnams su rig par bya'o /
kleśāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhabodhivipakṣaḥ
# nyon mongs pa'i sgrib ba'i gnas ngan len ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs so /
samāpattyāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ navānupūrvasamāpattyabhinirhāravipakṣaḥ
# snyoms par 'jug pa'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len ni / / mthar gyi gnas ba'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu mngon bar bsgrub pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs so /
jñeyāvaraṇadauṣṭhulyaṃ sarvajñatāvipakṣaḥ
# shes bya'i sgrib pa'i gnas ngan len ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs so /
ityevameṣāṃ yathāyogaṃ sarvadauṣṭhulyānāṃ pratiprasravdheniṣṭhāmārgaḥ / yathoktaṃ "tasya cetovimukteḥ pāripūryā prajñāvimukteḥ pāripūryā kāyadauṣṭhulyānāṃ pratiprasrabdheḥ
# de ltar gnas ngan len 'di dag thams cad ji ltar mthun mthun du rgyun bcad pa ni mthar phyin pa'i lam ste / / ji skad du sems rnam par grol ba yongs su rdzogs pa dang shes rab rnam par grol ba yongs su rdzogs nas lus kyi gnas ngan len rnams rgyun bcad de / / dran pa dang ldan pa'i rgyus 'di ltar de'i sgo dang po 'di lta ste /
smṛtyā samanvāgamahetorevamasya prathamaṃ dvāraṃ sudāntaṃ bhavati suguptaṃ surakṣitaṃ susaṃvṛtaṃ subhāṣitam yaduta cakṣurvijñeyeṣu rūpeṣvevaṃ yāvanmano vijñeyeṣu dharmeṣvi"ti / vajropamaḥ samādhirbhāvanāmārgasyāntyā prahāṇamārgāvasthā veditavyā
# mig gis rnam par shes par bya ba'i gzugs rnams la shin tu dul ba dang shin tu spas pa dang shin tu bsrungs pa dang shin tu bsdams pa dang shin tu bsgoms pa yin te / / yid kyis rnam par shes par bya ba'i chos rnams kyi bar la zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o; / / rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin ni bsgom pa'i lam gyi mtha'i spong ba'i lam gyi gnas skabs su rig par bya'o /
sa ca samādhirnirantarastatpravāharaya laukikena mārge ṇāntarākhaṇḍanāt
# ting nge 'dzin de yang bar chad med pa ste / / de'i rkyen gyis 'jig rten pa'i spyod pas rab tu phan mi phyed pa'i phyir ro /
dṛḍhaḥ sarvāvaraṇairacchidraṇāt sarvāvaraṇabheditayā ca sāratvāt / ekarasa iti nirvikalpaikarasatvāt
# brtan pa ni sgrib pa thams cad kyis mi phigs pa dang sgrib pa thams cad ni phigs pas sra ba'i phyir ro / / ro gcig pa ni rnam par mi rtog pa ro gcig pa'i phyir ro /
vyāpī sarvajñeyasāmānyatathatālaṃbanatvāt
# khyab pa ni shes bya thams cad kyi spyi'i de bzhin nyid la dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
etadarthapratibimbanārtha bhagavatoktam tadyathā mahāśailaḥ parvato 'khaṇḍo 'cchidro 'śuṣira ekadhanaḥ susaṃvṛta iti
# de'i don dang 'dra bar bya ba'i don du bcom ldan 'das kyis dper na brag chen po ma grum pa ser ka med pa khong stong ma yin pa gcig tu bsdus pa shin tu mkhregs pa zhes gsungs so /
nirantarāśrayaparivṛttividhārśakṣamārgalābhinaḥ / cittāśrayaparivṛttirdharmatā cittasya prakṛtiprabhāsvarasyāśeṣāgantukopakleśāpagamādyā parivṛttiḥ tathatāparivṛttirityarthaḥ
# gnas ma lus par gyur pa ni rnam pa gsum ste / / mi slob pa'i lam thob pa'i sems kyi gnas gyur ba ni chos nyid kyi sems rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa ma lus pa dang bral bas gnas gyur pa gang yin pa ste / / de bzhin nyid du gyur zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
mārgāśrayaparivṛtiḥ pūrvaṃ laukiko mārgo 'bhisamayakāle lokottaratvena parivṛtaḥ śaikṣaścocyate sāvaśeṣakaraṇīyatvāt / yadā tu nirhatāśeṣavipakṣo bhavati traidhātukavairāgyāttadāsya mārgasvabhāvasyāśrayasya paripūrṇā parivṛttirvyavasthāpyate
# lam gyi gnas gyur pa ni 'jig rten pa'i lam snga ma mngon par rtogs pa'i dus na 'jig rten las 'das pa nyid du gyur pa ste / / bya ba'i lhag ma yod pa'i phyir slob pa zhes kyang bya'o / / gang gi tshe khams gsum pa la 'dod chags dang bral ba mi mthun pa'i phyogs ma lus par gyur bar bsal ba de'i tshe lam gyi ngo bo nyid kyi gnas gyur pa yongs su rdzogs par rnam par gzhag go /
dauṣṭhulyāśrayaparivṛttirālayavijñānasya sarvakleśānuśayāpagamena parivṛttirveditavyā
# gnas ngan len gyi gnas gyur pa ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi bag la nyal gyi bag chags dang bral bar gyur bar rig par bya'o /
kṣaye sati viṣaye vā tasmin yajjñānaṃ kṣayajñānametaduktaṃ bhavati
# zad par gyur nas shes pa'am / / yul de la shes pa gang yin pa de ni zad pa shes pa ste /
niravaśeṣaṃ prakṣīṇe samudaye yajjñānaṃ tadavasthasya hetunirodhālaṃbanaṃ vā kṣayajñānamiti
# de ni 'di skad du kun nas 'byung ba ma lus par spangs nas shes pa gang yin pa dang de'i gnas skabs na rgyu 'gog pa la dmigs pa ni zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o / / de bzhin du mi skye bar gyur nas shes pa'am /
tathānutpāde sati viṣaye vā tasmin yajjñānamanutpādajñānam āyatyāṃ sarvasya duḥkhasyātyantamanutpattidharmatāyāṃ satyāṃ yajjñānamanyasatyālaṃbanamiti
# yul de la shes pa gang yin pa de ni mi skye ba shes pa ste / / phyi ma la sdug bsngal thams cad gtan du mi skye ba'i chos nyid du gyur nas shes pa gang yin pa de ni bden pa gzhan la dmigs pa yang yin pa'o /
yadvā duḥkhasatyānutpādālaṃbanaṃ tadanutpādajñānamityarthaḥ
# yang na gang sdug bsngal gyi bden ba la mi skye bar dmigs pa de mi skye bar shes pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
daśāśaikṣā dharmā aśaikṣāñchīlādīn pañca skandhānadhikṛtya
# mi slob pa'i chos bcu ni mi slob pa'i tshul khrims la sogs pa'i phung po lnga'i dbang du byas pa ste /
tatra aśaikṣā samyagvākkarmāntājīvā aśaikṣaśīlaskandhaḥ
# de la mi slob pa'i yang dag pa'i ngag dang las kyi mtha' dang 'tsho ba rnams ni mi slob pa'i tshul khrims kyi phung po'o /
samyaksmṛtisamādhiḥ samādhiskandhaḥ
# yang dag pa'i dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin ni ting nge 'dzin gyi phung po'o /
samyagdṛṣṭisaṃkalpavyāyāmāḥ prajñāskandhaḥ
# yang dag pa'i lta ba dang rtog pa dang rtsol ba rnams ni shes rab kyi phung po'o /
samyagvimuktirvimuktiskandhaḥ
# yang dag pa'i rnam par grol ba ni rnam par grol ba'i phung po'o /
samyagjñānaṃ vimuktirjñānadarśanaskandha iti
# yang dag pa'i shes pa ni rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba'i phung po'o /
punarmārgasatyasya catvāra ākārāścatvāri lakṣaṇāni / tatra tattvārtha mārgayatyaneti mārgaḥ
# yang lam gyi bden pa'i rnam pa bzhi dang mtshan nyid bzhi'o / / de la 'dis de kho na'i lam tshol bas lam mo /
ayathābhūtānāṃ kleśānāṃ pratipakṣatvāt nyāyaḥ
# rigs pa ma yin par gyur pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyi gnyen por gyur pa sa rigs pa'o /
tattvānavabodhadoṣeṇānityādiviparyāsairviparyastasya cittasyāviparyāse tattvāvabodhe pratipādanātpratipat
# de kho na khong du ma chud pa'i nyes pas mi rtag pa la rtag pa la sogs par phyin ci log pa rnams kyis phyin ci log tu gyur pa'i sems phyin ci log med pa de kho na khong du ma chud pa la 'jog pas sgrub pa'o /
nitya ātyantike niḥsaraṇapade yānānnairyāṇika iti
# nges par 'byung ba'i gnas rtag pa brtan du bar 'gro bas nges par 'byin ba zhes bya'o /
duḥkhādisatyeṣvanityādayaḥ ṣoḍaśākārā laukikā lokottarāśca santi
# sdug bsngal la sogs pa'i bden pa rnams la mi rtag pa la sogs pa rnam pa bcu drug ni 'jig rten pa yang yod 'jig rten las 'das pa yang yod de /
tatra laukikā jñeye 'praviṣṭāḥ sāvaraṇāḥ savikalpāśca tathatāyā aprativedhāt kleśānuśayitvādabhilāpamukhena prapañcanācca yathākramam
# de la 'jig rten pa rnams ni shes bya la legs par ma zhugs pa dang sgrub pa dang bcas pa dang rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa ste / / de bzhin nyid ma rtogs pa dang nyon mongs pa'i bag la nyal yod pa dang mngon par brjod pa'i sgo nas spros pa'i phyir te / / go rims bzhin no /
viparyayeṇa lokottarāḥ supraviṣṭā nirāvaraṇāśca santo nirvikalpatayā laukikebhyo viśiṣyante
# bzlog pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ste / / rgas par zhugs pa dang sgrib pa med par gyur nas rnam par mi rtog pas 'jig rten pa rnams las khyad par du 'gyur ro /
kathaṃ punarete 'vikalpayanto jñeyeṣu praviṣṭā bhavanti
# de dag rnam par mi rtog na ji ltar shes bya la legs par zhugs par gyur zhe na /
yasmādeteṣu vartamāno 'nityārtha paśyati sākṣādanubhavati na tvanityamiti paśyatyabhilāpaprapañcamukheneti
# 'di ltar 'di dag la gnas pa ni mi rtag pa'i don mthong zhing mngon du myong gi / / mi rtag go zhes mngon par brjod pa dang spros pa'i sgo nas mthong ba ni ma yin no /
evaṃ duḥkhādiṣvākāreṣu yojayitavyam
# de bzhin du sdug bsngal la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams la yang sbyar bar bya'o /
dharmaviniścayo nāma tṛtīyaḥ samuccayaḥ / dharmaviniścaye dharmo dvādaśāṅgaṃ vacogatam
# bden pa rnam par nges pa'o / / chos rnam par nges pa la chos ni gsung rab tu gtogs pa yan lag bcu gnyis te / / de la mdo'i sde ni gang bzhed pa'i don smos pa'i tshul gyis rkyang bar gsungs pa'o /
tatra sūtraṃ yadabhipretārthasūcanākāreṇa gadyabhāṣitam
# ci'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pas bzhed pa'i don rnam par phye ste / / ma gsungs she na / / smas pa /
kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ tathāgatastamabhipretamartha vivṛtyaiva na deśayatītyāha daśānuśaṃsān saṃpaśyaṃstathāgataḥ sūcanākāreṇa dharmaṃ deśayati
# phan yon bcu gzigs nas de bzhin gshegs pa smos pa'i tshul gyis chos ston te / / rnam par gzhag par sla ba ni ston pas go bar bya ba'i don rnam pa mang du rnam par gzhag pa mdor bsdus te /
sukhaṃ vyavasthāpayati daiśikairhi bahudhā vyavasthāpya prāpaṇīyasyārthasya saṃkṣipyākṛcchreṇa vyavasthāpanāt
# tshegs chung ngus rnam par 'jog pa'i phyir ro / / bshad sla ba ni tshig nyung ngus don chen po rgyas par go bar byed pa'i phyir te /
sukhaṃ deśayati alpena mahato 'rthavistarasya pratyāyanāt tadyathā sthāpayati saṃsthāpayatītyevamādi / śrotāpi sukhamudgṛhṇāti / dharmagauravatayā kṣipraṃ saṃbhārān paripūrayati bhāvagamyo 'yaṃ dharma ityavagamya jātāsthasya tasmin dharme ādaramukhena śraddhādisaṃbhāraparipūraṇāt
# 'di lta ste / / 'jog pa dang rgyun du 'jog pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / nyen pas kyang gzung sla ba'o / / chos la gus pas myur du tshogs yongs su rdzogs par byed pa ni chos 'di dag bsgoms pas shes par bya ba yin par rtogs nas gus pa skyes pa chos de la gces spras su bya ba'i sgo nas dad pa la sogs pa'i tshogs yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro /
āśu dharmatāṃ pratividhyati tathādaraprayogiṇaḥ prajñāyāḥ taikṣṇībhāvāt
# myur du chos nyid rtogs par 'gyur ba ni de ltar gces spras su bya ba sbyor ba'i shes rab rno bar gyur pa'i phyir ro /
ratneṣvavetya prasādaṃ pratilabhate deśanāyāḥ suvyavasthitabhāvagamena daiśikādiṣvabhiprasādotpādāt / paramadṛṣṭadharmasukhavihāraṃ spṛśati abhiprāyārtha tīvreṇa yogena cintayitvā labdhavataḥ prāmodyaviśeṣādhigamāt
# dkon mchog rnams la shes nas dad pa thob pa ni bstan pa la legs par rnam par gnas par khong du chud nas ston pa la sogs pa la dad pa skye ba'i phyir ro / / mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa'i mchog la reg pa ni dgongs pa'i don rtsol ba chen pos bsams nas rtogs pas rab tu dga' ba'i khyad par thob pa'i phyir ro /
sāṃkathyaviniścayena satāṃ cittamārādhayati gūḍhārthavivaraṇāt ata eva paṇḍitaḥ paṇḍita iti saṃkhyāṃ gacchati yaśo 'sya samantānniścaratītyarthaḥ
# 'phel ba'i gtam gyis gtan la 'bebs pas dam pa rnams kyi sems mgu bar byed pa ni don zab pa rnam par 'byed pas de'i phyir mkhas pa mkhas pa zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro ste / / 'di'i snyan pa kun tu 'byung zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ubhayaṃ caitatpaścimasabhisamayaiko 'nuśaṃso draṣṭavyaḥ
# tha ma 'di gnyi ga bsdus te phan yon gcig tu blta bar bya'o /
nītārtha sūtraṃ vyākaraṇam tena vivṛtyābhisaṃdhivyākaraṇāt / udānaṃ yadāttamanaskenodāhṛtam tadyathā yadā ime prādurbhavanti dharmā ityevamādi / nidānaṃ yatkiṃcideva pudgalamuddiśya bhāṣitaṃ sotpattikaśikṣā prajñaptikabhāṣitaṃ vā tadyathāsminnidāne 'smin prakaraṇa iti vistaraḥ
# nges pa'i don gyi mdo sde ni lung du bstan pa'i sde ste / / des rnam par phye nas dgongs pa lung ston pa'i phyir ro / / ched du brjod pa'i sde ni gang yi rangs nas brjod pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / gang gi tshe chos de dag 'byung ngo zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / gleng gzhi'i sde ni gang zag 'ga' zhig gi ched du gsungs pa dang byung ba dang bcas pa'i bslab pa bcas pa gsungs pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / gzhi 'di dang skabs 'di zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o / / rtogs pa brjod pa'i sde ni dpe dang bcas par gsungs pa ste /
avadānaṃ sadṛṣṭāntakaṃ bhāṣitam tenārthavyavadānādabhivyañjanādityarthaḥ
# des don gsal bar byed pa'i phyir te / / mngon du gsal bar byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
vaipulyaṃ vaidalyaṃ vaitulyamityete mahāyānasya paryāyāḥ tadetatsaptavidhamahattvayogānmahattvayānamityucyate
# shin tu rgyas pa'i sde zhes bya ba la rnam par 'thag ba dang mtshungs bral zhes bya ba ni theg pa chen po'i rnam grangs su gtogs pa ste / / de ni chen po rnam pa bdun dang ldan pa'i phyir theg pa chen po zhes bya'o /
saptavidhaṃ mahatvam ālaṃbanamahattvaṃ śatasāhasrikādisūtrāparimitadeśanādharmā laṃbanādbodhisattvamārgasya / pratipattimahattvaṃ sakalasvaparārthapratipatteḥ
# chen po rnam pa bdun la dmigs pa chen po ni byang chub sems dpa'i lam stong phrag brgya pa la sogs pa'i mdo sde bskyang du med pa'i bstan pa'i chos la dmigs pa'i phyir ro / / sgrub pa chen po ni bdag dang gzhan gyi don mtha' dag sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
jñānamahatvaṃ pudgaladharmanairātmyajñānāt / vīryamahattvaṃ triṣu mahākalpāsaṃkhyeyeṣvanekaduṣkaraśatasahasraprayogāt
# ye shes chen po ni gang zag dang chos la bdag med par shes pa'i phyir ro / / brtson 'grus chen po ni bskal pa grangs med pa chen po gsum du dka' ba brgya stong la sbyor ba'i phyir ro /
upāyakauśalyamahattvaṃ saṃsāranirvāṇāpratiṣṭhānāt
# thabs la mkhas pa chen po ni 'khor ba dang mya ngan las 'das pa la mi gnas pa'i phyir ro /
prāptimahattvaṃ valavaiśāradyāveṇikabuddhadharmādyaprameyāsaṃkhyeyaguṇādhigamāt
# 'thob pa chen po ni stobs dang mi 'jigs pa dang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa la sogs pa yon tan dpag tu med cing grangs med pa thob pa'i phyir ro /
karmamahattvaṃ yāvatsaṃsārabodhyādisandarśanena buddhakāryānuṣṭhānāditi
# las chen po ni 'khor ba ji srid par byang chub la sogs pa yang dag par ston pas sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
upadeśo yatrāviparītena dharmalakṣaṇena sūtrādīnāmarthanirdeśaḥ
# gtan la phab bar bstan pa'i sde ni gang du phyin ci ma log pa'i mtshan nyid du mdo sde la sogs pa'i don bshad pa'o /
nidānaṃ sotpattikaśikṣāprajñaptibhāṣitasaṃgṛhītaṃ vinayapiṭakam avadānādikaṃ tasya parivāro veditavyaḥ
# gleng gzhi'i sde ni byung ba dang bcas pa'i bslab pa bcas pa gsungs pa bsdus pa ni 'dul ba'i sde snod do / / rtogs pa brjod pa la sogs pa ni de'i 'khor du rigs par bya'o /
adbhutadharmāṇāṃ bodhisattvasūtrapiṭake saṃgrahaṇam teṣāṃ viśeṣeṇācintyodāraprabhāvaviśeṣayogāt
# rmad du byung ba'i chos rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i mdo sde'i sde snod du bsdus ba ste / / de dag gi khyad par gyi mthu bsam gyis mi khyab cing rgya cha ba'i khyad par dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
upadeśa ubhayatra śrāvakayāne mahāyāne cābhidharmapiṭakam / sūtrapiṭakavyavasthānaṃ vicikitsopakleśapratipakṣeṇa vineyānāmutpannānutpannasaṃśayacchedādhikāreṇa sūtrageyādi deśanāt / vinayapiṭakavyavasthānamantadvayānuyogopakleśapratipakṣeṇa saṃnidhikāraparibhogādipratikṣepāt śatasāhasrakavastrānujñānācca / antadvayaṃ punaḥ kāmasukhallikānta ātmaklemathāntaśca
# gtan la phab par bstan pa'i sde ni nyan thos kyi theg pa dang theg pa chen po gnyi ga'i chos mngon pa'i sde snod do / / nye ba'i nyon mongs pa the tshom gyi gnyen por ni mdo sde'i sde snod rnam par gzhag ste / / gdul bya rnams kyi som nyi byung ba bcad pa'i ched du mdo'i sde dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde la sogs pa bshad pa'i phyir ro / / nye ba'i nyon mongs pa mtha' gnyis dang ldan pa'i gnyen por 'dul ba'i sde snod / / rnam par gzhag ste / / sog 'jog byed pas yongs su spyod pa la sogs pa spong ba dang brgya stong ri ba'i gos la sogs pa gnas ba'i phyir ro / / mtha' gnyis ni 'dod pa bsod snyoms kyi mtha' dang bdag dub pa'i mtha'o /
abhidharmavyavasthānaṃ svayaṃdṛṣṭiparāmarśopakleśapratipakṣeṇa tatra vistareṇa dharmalakṣaṇasthāpanāt
# rang gi lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por chos mngon pa'i sde snod rnam par gzhag ste / / der chos kyi mtshan nyid rgya cher bstan pa'i phyir ro /
punaḥ sūtrapiṭakaṃ niśritya vineyāḥ śikṣātraye vyutpadyante tatra tasya vistareṇodbhāvitatvāt / vinayaṃ niśrityādhiśīlamadhicittaṃ śikṣāṃ niṣpādayanti tatra prātimokṣasaṃvaraśikṣāmārgopadeśaniśrayeṇa śīlapariśodhanāttatpariśuddhikṛtāvipratisārādyānupūrvyā ca cittasamādhānāt / abhidharmaniśrityādhiprajñaṃ śikṣāṃ niṣpādayanti tatra vistareṇa dharmapravicayopāyopadeśāditi ato 'pi piṭakatrayavyavasthānam / punaḥ sūtrapiṭakaṃ niśritya granthārthavyutpattiḥ / vinayaṃ niśritya tadubhayasākṣātkriyā śikṣāpratipattiprabhāvitatvādvinayasya
# yang mdo sde'i sde snod la brten nas gdul bya rnams bslab pa gsum la byang bar byed do / / de las de rgyas par brjod pa'i phyir ro / / 'dul ba la brten nas lhag pa'i tshul khrims dang lhag pa'i sems kyi bslab pa bsgrub ste / / der so sor thar pa'i sngom pa'i bslab pa'i lam nye bar bstan pa la brten pa la brten nas tshul khrims yongs su sbyong ba dang de yongs su dag par 'gyur te / / 'gyod pa med pa la sogs pa'i rim gyis sems mnyam par 'jog pa'i phyir ro / / chos mngon pa la brten nas lhag pa'i shes rab kyi bslab pa 'grub ste / / der chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'i thabs rgya cher bstan pa'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir yang sde snod gsum rnam par gzhag go / / yang mdo sde'i sde snod la brten nas tshig dang don la byang bar byed do / / 'dus ba la brten nas gnyi ga mngon sum du byed do / / 'dul ba'i sde snod ni bslab pa sgrub pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
tato dharmārthayoḥ sākṣātkriyāyāḥ padasthānamityucyate āśrayārthena
# de'i phyir chos dang don mngon sum du bya ba'i gnas yin pas gzhi'i gnas zhes bya'o /
abhidharmaṃ niśritya parasparaṃ sāṃkathyaviniścayakṛtena dharmasaṃbhogena sparśavihāro bhavati tatra bahuprakāraṃ dharmāṇāṃ svalakṣaṇādidharmatāyā vyutpādanāt
# chos mngon pa la brten nas phan tshun 'bel ba'i gtam gtan la 'bebs pa las gyur ba'i chos la rdzogs par longs spyod pas bde ba la reg par gnas par 'gyur te / / der chos rnam par mang po rnams kyi rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid la sogs pa'i chos nyid la byang bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
etānyeva trīṇi piṭakāni caturaśītidharmaskandhasahasrāṇi bhavanti śrāvakayānādhikāreṇa yāni sthavirānandenodgṛhītāni
# nyan thos kyi theg pa'i skabs su gnas brtan kun dga' bos chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong gang dag gzung ba rnams ni sde snod gsum po 'di dag nyid yin no /
kiṃ punarekasya dharmaskandhasya parimāṇam
# chos kyi phung po gcig gi tshad ji tsam zhe na /
daśaśatasaṃkhyo dharmaskandhaḥ sahasrasaṃkhya ityarthaḥ / yadyevaṃ sahasrasaṃkhya ityevaṃ ki nocyate
# grangs brgya phrag bcu ni chos kyi phung po ste / / grangs stong zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / gal te de lta yin na grangs stong zhes de skad du ci'i phyir mi brjod ce na /
sāhasrikaikaskandhavyavasthāne prayojanajñāpanārtham / tathāhyekādivṛddhayā daśasaṃkhyā śatasaṃkhyā sahasrādisaṃkhyāḥ
# phung po re re la yang stong stong rnam par gzhag pa'i dgongs pa brtan pa'i phyir te / / 'di ltar gcig la sogs pa bskyed na grangs bcur 'gyur ro / / bcur bskyed na grangs bcur 'gyur ro / / grangs stong la sogs pa'i gzhi ni grangs brgya phrag bcu yin par blta'o /
taddaśaśatasaṃkhyā upaniṣado draṣṭavyāḥ / tadyathā daśa śatāni sahasram śataṃ sahasrāṇāṃ śatasahasram śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ koṭirityevaṃ sarvāsūttarāsu saṃkhyāsvavaśyamanayoḥ daśaśatasaṃkhyayoranyataropaniṣadbhavati
# 'di lta ste brgya phrag bcu ni stong ngo / / stong phrag brgya ni 'bum mo / / 'bum phrag brgya ni bye ba'o / / de bzhin du grangs gong ma thams cad la yang brgya dang bcu po 'di gnyis las gang yang rung ba zhig gdon mi za bar gzhir 'gyur te /
ata ete eva samasya daśaśatānyeko dharmaskandho vyavasthāpyate
# de'i phyir de dag bsdus na brgya phrag bcu po de dag la chos kyi phung po gcig rnam par gzhag go /
anayā ca gaṇanayā caturaśītidharmaskandhasahasrāṇyaṣṭau koṭyaḥ catvāriśacca lakṣā bhavanti
# bgrad pa'i tshul 'dis na chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong gi tshig le 'ur byas pa bye ba phrag brgyad dang 'bum phrag bzhi bcur 'gyur ro / / bam po bdun pa /
sa eṣa piṭakatrayasaṃgṛhīto dharmaḥ kasya gocaraḥ
# sde snod gsum gyis bsdus pa'i chos 'di dag gang gi spyod yul yin zhe na /
śrutamayādīnāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ gocara ālaṃbanamityarthaḥ
# thos pa las byung ba la sogs pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi spyod yul te / / dmigs pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
etatprasaṃgena sālaṃbanādilakṣaṇānāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ dharmamārabhyālaṃbanādikaṃ vyavasthāpyate
# de'i zhar la dmigs pa dang bcas pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi chos las brtsams te dmigs pa la sogs pa rnam par gzhag go /
tatra dharme teṣāṃ kimālaṃbanam
# de la chos kyi nang nas de dag gi dmigs pa gang zhe na /
sūtrādi nāmapadavyañjanakāyasaṃgṛhītā sūtrādideśanetyarthaḥ / ākāraḥ yān skandhādīnartha prakārānārabhya sā deśanā tadākārāste cittacaitasikā veditavyāḥ
# mdo'i sde la sogs pa ste / / ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs kyis bsdus pa'i mdo'i sde la sogs pa bshad pa'o zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / rnam pa ni gang phung po la sogs pa'i don gyi rnam pa rnams las brtsams te bstan pa gang yin pa de ni rnam pa rnams te / / de dag ni sems dang sems las byung ba rnams su rig par bya'o /
āśrayaḥ paravijñaptismṛtirvāsanā ca / tatra deśanākāle paravijñaptirāśrayo yo 'sāvucyate parato ghoṣata iti tata uttarakālaṃ smṛtirāśrayo yathāśrutamanusmṛtyābhyasanāt / tata uttarakālaṃ vāsanāśrayastadanusmṛtimantareṇāpi paścādabhyāsabhāvanābalena pratibhāsanāditi
# gnas ni gzhan las rnam par rig pa dang dran pa dang bag chags so / / de la bshad pa'i dus na gzhan las rnam par rig pa gnas te / / de ni gzhan gyi sgra las shes pa 'byung ngo / / de'i 'og tu dran pa gnas te ji ltar thos pa bzhin du rjes su dran pas goms par byed pa'i phyir ro / / de'i 'og tu bag chags gnas te / / de'i rjes su dran pa med kyang goms pa'i bag chags kyi dbang gis phyis snang bar 'gyur pa'i phyir ro /
saṃprayogaḥ cittacaitasikānāmanyonyasahāyabhāvena sūtrādyālaṃbane skandhādipratisaṃyuktārthākāraiḥ saṃpratipattiḥ
# mtshungs par ldan pa ni sems dang sems las byung ba rnams gcig gi grogs gcig yin pa'i tshul gyis phung po la sogs pa dang rab tu ldan pa'i don gyi rnam pa rnams kyi mdo sde la sogs pa'i dmigs pa yang dag par rtogs pa'o /
qharme ālaṃbana prabhedo vyāpyālaṃbanādikaścaturvidhaḥ
# chos la dmigs pa rab tu dbye ba ni khyab pa'i dmigs pa la sogs pa rnam pa bzhi'o /
vyāpyālaṃbanaṃ punaḥ savikalpapratibimbādibhedena caturbidham / tatra adhimuktimanaskāra ekāntalaukiko yo manaskāraḥ
# khyab pa'i dmigs pa ni rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs brnyan la sogs pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa bzhi'o / / de la mos pa yid la byed pa ni gang gcig tu 'jig rten pa'i yid la byed pa'o /
tattvamanaskāro lokottarastatpṛṣṭhalabdhaśca
# de kho na yid la byed pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa dang de kho na'i rjes las thob pa'o /
yāvadbhāvikatayā dharmāṇāmetāvanti sarvadharmavastuni yajjñeyavyavasthānam tadyathā skandhadhātvāyatanāni
# chos rnams kyi ji snyed yod pa ni chos thams cad kyi dngos po 'di dag tu zad do zhes gang zhes bya rnam par gzhag pa ste / / 'di ltar phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams so /
yathāvadbhāvikatayā ebhiḥ prakāraiḥ sujñeyamiti
# ji lta ba bzhin du yod pa ni rnam par 'di dag tu de shes par bya ba ste /
tadyathā satyamukhena tānyeva skandhadhātvāyatanāni yathāsaṃbhavaṃ duḥkhatojñeyāni yāvanmārgataḥ
# 'di ltar bden pa'i sgo nas phung po dang khams dang skye mched de dag nyid ji ltar mthun mthun du sdug bsngal nyid du shes par bya ba nas lam gyi bar du'o /
ākāramukhenaikaikaṃ satyaṃ caturbhirākārairjñeyam aviśeṣataśca sarvāṇi tathatākāreṇa
# rnam pa'i sgo nas bden pa re re la yang rnam pa bzhi bzhis shes par bya'o / / bye brag med par na thams cad kyang de bzhin nyid kyis rnam par shes par bya'o /
dharmoddānādhikāreṇa vānityataḥ sarvasaṃskārā jñeyā yāvacchāntato nirvāṇam
# chos kyi sdom gyi skabs kyis na 'du byed thams cad mi rtag pa nyid du shes par bya ba nas / / mya ngan las 'das bzhi ba nyid kyi bar du'o /
vimokṣādhikāreṇa vā śūnyato yāvadanimittata iti
# rnam par thar pa'i rnam pa'i skabs kyis na stong ba nyid nas mtshan ma med pa'i bar du'i /
kāryapariniṣpattirāśrayapariniṣpattiḥ parinivṛttāśrayasyāviparītālaṃbanasaṃprakhyānāt
# dgos pa yongs su grub pa ni gnas gyur pa grub pa ste / / gnas gyur pa la dmigs pa phyin ci ma log par snang ba nyid do /
yathāvadbhāvikatāyā nirdaśe ṣoḍaśaprakārā uktāstrayaśca vimokṣākārāḥ teṣāṃ cānyonyasaṃgrahaḥ
# ji lta ba bzhin du yod par bstan pa rnam pa bcu drug dang rnam par thar pa rnam pa gsum bstan pa de dag ni gcig gis gcig sdud do /
katha kṛtvā
# ji lta zhe na /
ṣoḍaśānāmākārāṇāṃ dvau śūnyatākārau śūnyākārānātmākāraśca / ṣaḍapraṇihitākārāḥ anityākārā duḥkhākāro hetusamudayaprabhavapratyayākārāśca taistraidhātuke 'praṇidhānāt
# rnam pa bcu drug gi nang nas gnyis ni stong pa nyid kyi rnam pa ste / / stong pa'i rnam pa dang bdag med pa'i rnam pa'o / / drug ni smon pa med pa'i rnam pa ste / / mi rtag pa'i rnam pa dang sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa dang rgyu dang kun 'byung ba dang rab tu skye ba dang rkyen gyi rnam pa ste / / de dag gis khams gsum pa la smon pa med pa'i phyir ro /
aṣṭāvinimittākārāḥ śeṣāḥ nirodhamārgayornimittīkartumaśakyatvāt
# lhag ma brgyad ni mtshan ma med pa'i rnam pa ste / / 'gog pa dang lam la mtshan mar byed mi nus pa'i phyir ro /
caritaviśodhanamālaṃbanaṃ rāgacaritādīnāmaśubhādi tenotsadarāgādyupaśamanāt / avidyādayo dharmāḥ saṃskārādīndharmānabhiṣyandayanti na hyeṣāṃ nirhetuka utpādo nāpīśvarādiviṣamahetuka iti yajjñānamidaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam
# spyod pa rnam par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa ni 'dod chags la spyod pa la sogs pa'i mi sdug pa la sogs pa ste / / des 'dod chags la sogs pa'i shas che ba nye bar zhi bar byed pa'i phyir ro / / ma rig pa la sogs pa'i chos rnams ni 'du byed la sogs pa'i chos rnams mngon du 'byin te / / 'di dag rgyu med pa las byung par ma yin zhing dbang phyug la sogs pa mi mthun pa'i rgyu las byung ba yang ma yin par shes pa gang yin pa de ni / / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba la mkhas pa'o /
dharmamātrahetukatve 'pi satyanurūpāddhetoranurūpasyaiva phalasyotpattiḥ tadyathā sucaritasyeṣṭo vipāko duścaritasyāniṣṭa ityevamādi yajjñānamidaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyaṃ veditavyam
# chos tsam gyi rgyu las byung ba yin du zin kyang mthun pa'i rgyu las mthun pa'i 'bras bu nyid 'byung ste / / 'di lta ste legs par spyod pa'i rnam par smin pa sdug pa dang nyes par spyod pa'i rnam par smin pa mi sdug pa zhes bya ba la sogs par shes pa gang yin pa de ni gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas par rig par bya'o /
kleśaviśodhanamālaṃbanaṃ laukikamārgādhikāreṇādhaūrdhvabhūmīnāmaudārikaśāntatā tena paryavasthānaviṣkambhaṇāt
# nyon mongs pa rnam par sbyong ba'i dmigs pa ni 'jig rten pa'i lam gyi gnas skabs su sa 'og ma dang gong ma rnams kyis rags pa dang zhi ba nyid des kun nas dkris pa rnam par gnon pa'i phyir ro /
lokottaramārgādhikāreṇa samāsatastathatā vyāsena catvāryāryasatyāni tenānuśayasamudghātāt
# 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyi skabs su ni bsdu na de bzhin nyid do / / spros na 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi ste /
sūtrādidharmavicārāṇāṃ saṃbnadhena catasro yuktayo varṇyante tābhistadvicāraṇāt / tatra apekṣāyuktiryā saṃskārāṇāmutpattau pratyayāpekṣā tadyathāṅkurasyotpattau bījodakakṣetrāṇyapekṣyante vijñānasyendriyārthamanaskārā ityevamādi / kāryakāraṇayuktistadyathā cakṣurādīnāṃ cakṣurvijñānādyāśrayabhāvaḥ rūpādīnāmālaṃbanabhāvaḥ cakṣurvijñānādīnāṃ rūpādiprativijñāpanam suvarṇakārādīnāṃ ca śilpināṃ suvarṇādighaṭanamityevamādi / upapattisādhanayuktisvabhāvaviśeṣasaṃgṛhītasya sādhyasyārthasya pratyakṣādipramāṇāviruddhaḥ pratijñādyupadeśaḥ
# des bag la nyal legs par bcom pa'i phyir ro / / mdo'i sde la sogs pa'i chos dpyad pa dang 'brel bas rig pa bzhir brjod par bya ste / / de dag gis de dpyad pa'i phyir ro / / de la ltos pa'i rigs pa ni gang 'du byed rnams 'byung ba na rkyen la ltos pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / myu gu 'byung ba nas sa bon dang dus dang chu dang; zhing rnams la ltos pa dang rnam par shes pa'i dbang po dang don dang yid la byed pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / bya ba byed pa'i rigs la ni 'di lta ste mig la sogs pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa'i gnas kyi dngos po'o / / gzugs la sogs pa ni dmigs pa'i dngos po'o / / mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa ni gzugs la sogs pa so sor rnam par rig par byed do / / gser mgar la sogs pa'i lag bzo ba rnams ni gser la sogs pa byed ces bya ba la sogs pa'o / / gtan tshigs sgrub pa'i rigs pa ni sgrub pa'i don ngo bo nyid dang khyad par gyis bsdus pa mngon sum la sogs pa'i tshad ma dang mi 'gal bar dam bcas pa la sogs par bstan pa'o /
dharmatāyuktistadyathāgninā dāhaḥ udakena kleda ityevamādikā prasiddhā dharmāṇāṃ dharmatā / yathoktaṃ cakṣuḥ samṛddhaṃ śūnyaṃ nityena yāvadātmīyena
# chos nyid kyi rigs pa ni 'di lta ste / / mes ni tshig chus ni 'drul zhes bya ba la sogs par grags pa'i chos rnams kyi chos nyid de / / ji skad du 'byor ldan mig ni rtag pa nas bdag gi pa'i bar gyis stong ngo /
tatkasya hetoḥ
# de ci'i phyir zhe na /
prakṛtirasyaiṣeti / nāmaparyeṣaṇā nāmakāyādīnāṃ prajñaptisattvādapariniṣpannameṣāṃ svalakṣaṇamiti yā vicāraṇā
# 'di'i rang bzhin ni 'di'o zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o / / ming kun tu tshol ba ni ming gi tshogs la sogs pa btags pa'i yod pa yin pa'i phyir 'di dag gi rang gi mtshan nyid yongs su grub pa med par dpyod pa'o /
vastuparyeṣaṇā skandhādīnāṃ tathāpariniṣpattiryathā nāmakāyādibhirabhilapyanta iti yā saṃtīraṇā parīkṣaṇetyarthaḥ
# dngos po kun tu tshol ba ni ji ltar ming gi tshogs la sogs pa brjod pa de bzhin du phung po la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su grub pa med par gang rtog pa ste / / yongs su rtog ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā yābhidhānābhidheyasaṃbandhe svabhāvaprajñaptimātrasya vyavahāranimittatvena saṃtīraṇā / abhidhānābhidheyasaṃbandhaḥ
# ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba ni brjod pa dang brjod par bya ba 'brel pa la ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa tsam gyi tha snyad kyi rgyu nyid du rtog pa'o zhes bya ba la brjod pa dang brjod par bya ba 'brel ba ni rtogs pa'i rgyu nyid do /
punaranyonyasaṃpratyayanimittatvam / tathāhi vyutpannavyavahārasyābhidhānamātraṃ śrutvā tadabhidheye saṃpratyaya utpadyate smṛtimukhena abhidheyaṃ vā punarupalabhya tadabhidhāne
# 'di ltar tha snyad la bya ba ni brjod pa tsam du thos pas de'i brjod par bya ba la dran pa'i sgo nas rtogs pa 'byung ngo / / brjod par bya ba dmigs na yang de brjod pa la rtogs pa 'byung ste /
ityevaṃvidhe saṃbandhe prasiddhe cakṣurityevamādisvalakṣaṇaprajñaptimātraṃ tadākhyāmāsapiṇḍādivyavahārasya nimittaṃ bhavatīti yā parīkṣeyamucyate svabhāvaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā / viśeṣaprajñaptiparyeṣaṇā yā tathaivābhidhānābhidheyasaṃbandhe nityānityottarānuttararūpyasanidarśanānidarśanatādiviśeṣalakṣaṇaprajñaptimātrasya vyavahāranimittatā saṃtīraṇā / catvāri yathābhūtaparijñānāni yathāparyeṣitāni nāmādyanupalabdhijñānāni
# rnam pa de lta bur 'brel bar grags pa la mig la sogs pa'i rang gi mtshan nyid du btags pa tsam ni de brjod pa sha sna gu la sogs pa'i tha snyad kyi rgyur gyur par gang kun tu rtog pa de ni ngo bo nyid du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba zhes bya'o / / khyad par du 'dogs pa kun tu tshol ba ni gang de bzhin du brjod pa dang brjod par bya ba 'brel ba rtag pa dang mi rtag pa dang bla na yod pa dang bla na med pa dang gzugs can dang gzugs can ma yin pa dang bstan du yod pa dang bstan du med pa khyad par gyi mtshan nyid du 'dogs pa tsam gyi tha snyad kyi rgyu nyid du rtogs pa'o / / yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa gzhi ni ji ltar kun du brtsal ba rnams kyis ming la sogs pa mi dmigs par shes pa rnams so /
samādhiprayuktasya yogabhūmiḥ pañcākārādhārādiḥ
# chos la ting nge 'dzin bar brtson pa'i rnal 'byor gyi sa ni rnam pa lnga ste / / gzhi la sogs pa'o /
tatra ādhāro yādṛśaṃ bāhuśrutyaṃ śamathavipaśyanayoḥ pratiṣṭhā bhavatyālaṃbanayogena tadādhāra ityucyate
# de la gzhi ni mang du thos pa ci 'dra bar dmigs pa'i tshul gyis zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gi gnas su 'gyur te / / de ni gzhi zhes bya'o /
tatpunaḥ saṃbhṛtasaṃbhārasya satyābhisamayamadhikṛtyodgṛhītaṃ yatsūtrādikaṃ śrutam
# de yang tshogs bsags pa'i bden pa mngon par rtogs pa'i dbang du byas pa ste / / gang mdo sde la sogs pa thos pas bzung ba'o /
ādhānaṃ tadālaṃbano yoniśomanaskāraḥ tena tasmin bāhuśrutye 'viparītārthacittākāreṇa cittākaraṇāt
# bskyed pa ni de la dmigs pa'i tshul bzhin yid la byed pa ste / / nges mang du thos pa de la phyi ci ma log par don sems pa'i tshul gyis sems 'dzin pa'o /
ādarśastadbāhuśrutyālaṃbanaḥ sahanimittena samādhiḥ jñeyavastusabhāgapratibimbākāra ityarthaḥ
# me long lta bu ni mang du thos pa de nyid la dmigs pa'i ting nge 'dzin mtshan ma dang bcas pa ste / / shes bya'o dngos po dang mthun pa gzugs brnyan lta bu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ādarśatvaṃ punarasya tena jñeyabimbaparīkṣaṇādveditavyam
# 'di'i mi long lta bu nyid ni des shes bya'i gzugs brnyan la yongs su rtog par rig par bya'o /
āloko grāhyagrāhakānupalabdhijñānaṃ darśanamārgasaṃgṛhītaṃ pratyakṣavṛttitvāditi
# snang ba ni gzung ba dang 'dzin pa mi dmigs par shes pa ste / / mngon sum du 'byung ba'i phyir mthong ba'i lam gyis bsdus pa'o /
kathaṃ ca punaḥ bodhisattva ekasyāṃ yaugabhūmau prayukto nopalambhaṃ spṛśati saṃbhṛtapuṇyajñāna saṃbhāro bodhisattvaḥ kalpāsaṃkhyeyaniryātastathāprativedhānukūlaṃ śrutaṃ yoniśomanasikurvan samādhiṃ niṣpādayati / sa evaṃ samāhite citte yajjñeyapratibimbaṃ niśritya dhyāyati tattasmātsamāhitāccittādananyaditi saṃpaśyaṃstasmin pratibimbe viṣayasaṃjñāṃ vyāvartya tadākāraṃ svasaṃjñāmātramavadhārayati
# ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rnal 'byor gyis 'di la brtson pa mi dmigs pa la reg ce na / / bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs bsags pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni bskal pa grangs med pa tshar phyin nas de bzhin nyid rtogs pa dang mthun pa'i chos thos pa tshul bzhin yid la byed cing ting nge 'dzin sgrub ste / / de de ltar mnyam par gzhag pa'i sems kyis shes bya'i gzugs brnyan gang yin pa la brten nas bsam gtan du byed do / / mnyam par gzhag pa'i sems de las de gzhan ma yin par mthong nas gzugs brnyan de la yul gyi 'du shes bzlog ste /
tadā cāsau svacittamātrāvasthānādadhyātma sthitacitto bhavan sarvathā grāhyabhāvaṃ prativedayate / tataśca grāhyābhāvādgrāhakamapi na pariniṣpannamiti tasyāpyabhāvaṃ parivedayate
# de'i rnam pa rang gi 'du shes tsam du 'dzin to / / de'i tshe rang gi sems tsam la gnas ba'i phyir sems nang du gnas par gyur pas gzung ba rnam pa thams cad du med par rab tu rtogs so / / de'i 'og tu gzung ba med pas 'dzin pa yang yongs su ma grub bo zhes de yang med par rab tu rtogs so /
tataḥ pratyātmaṃ tadubhayasvabhāvopalambhāpagatamanupalambhamadhigacchati / etadeva cādhikṛtyoktaṃ bhagavatā pratibimbaṃ manaḥ paśyanniti vistaraḥ
# de'i 'og tu so so rang la de gnyi ga'i rang bzhin du dmigs pa dang bral nas dmigs pa med par khong du chud do / / de nyid kyi dbang du mdzad nas bcom ldan 'das kyis / / byang chub sems dpa' mnyam gzhag pa / / yid kyi gzugs brnyan mthong bas na / / zhes rgya cher gsungs so /
āśrayaḥ āśrayaparivṛttiḥ dauṣṭhulyāpagamātpariśuddha āśraya ityarthaḥ / sā ceyaṃ yogabhūmirhetutaḥ phalataśca nirdiṣṭā veditavyā
# gnas ni gnas gyur pa ste / / gnas ngan len dang bral ba'i phyir gnas yongs su dag zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / rnal 'byor gyi sa 'di ni rgyu dang 'bras bus bstan par rig par bya ste /
tatrādhārādibhiścaturbhirhetunirdeśaḥ paścimenaikena phalanirdeśa iti / yaduktaṃ sthavirānandena pañcabhirāyuṣmañchāriputradharmaiḥ samanvāgato bhikṣurlaghu ca gṛhṇātītyatra sūtre taireva pañcabhirdharmairlaghugrahaṇādīni catvāri yathāyogaṃ veditavyāni
# de la gzhi la sogs pa bzhis ni rgyu bstan to / / tha ma gcig gis ni 'bras bu bstan to / / gnas brtan kun dga' bos tshe dang ldan pa sh'a ri'i bu chos lnga dang ldan pa'i dge slong myur du 'dzin to zhes gang smras pa'i mdo de la chos lnga po 'di dag gis myur du 'dzin pa la sogs pa bzhin du ci rigs su rig par bya'o /
catvāri kathaṃ kṛtvā / dharmakuśalo laghu gṛhṇāti bāhuśrutyātprāyeṇa bhinnapadavyañjanatayā / arthakuśalo bahu gṛhṇāti abhidharmādilakṣaṇajñatvāt skandhadhātvādikathāvastvadhikāreṇa prabhūtagranthasaṃkalanataḥ / vyañjanakuśalo niruktikulaśca sūdgṛhītaṃ gṛhṇāti suniruktavyañjanajñatvādātmātmeti janapadaniruktimanabhiniviśyānuvyavahārajñatvācca granthārthayoraviparotagrahaṇataḥ
# ji ltar na chos la mkhas pas myur du 'dzin zhe na / / mang du thos pas tshig dang yi ge phal cher lcigs pa'i phyir ro / / don la mkhas pas mang du 'dzin te / / chos mngon pa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid shes pa'i phyir te; phung po dang khams la sogs pa'i gtam gyi gzhi'i skabs su tshig le'u mang du bzlums pa'i phyir ro / / yi ge la mkhas pa dang nges pa'i tshig la mkhas pas ni tshig dang don ma nor bar 'dzin pas legs par zin par 'dzin te / / nges pa'i tshig bzang po'i yi ge shes pa dang; bdag go zhes yul gyi mi'i nges pa'i tshig la mngon par zhen pa rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa shes pa nyid kyi phyir ro /
pūrvāntāparāntānusaṃdhikuśala udgṛhītaṃ na nāśayati pūrvamudgahītāndharmānniśritya paścānniḥsartavyamiti buddhābhisaṃdhijñatvādadhigamena tatsārādānataḥ
# sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' la dgongs pa la mkhas pa ni ril gyis byed na chos la gnas pa yin gyi / / sbyor ba gang brten nas phyis 'byung bar bya bar shes te / / dgongs pa shes pa'i phyir khong du chud pas de'i snying po len pa'i phyir ro /
dharmavihārī bhikṣurdharmavihāri bhikṣuriti bhadantocyata ityatra sūtre bhagavatā samastena śrutacintābhāvanāvihāreṇa dharmavihāro bhavati nānyataraprayogamātreṇeti saṃdarśitam / tatra paryāptisvādhyāyadeśanābahulā vitarkaṇā bahulāścetyanena kevalaṃ śrutacintāprayuktā na bhāvanāprayuktā yogādiriñcanādato na dharmavihāriṇo vyavasthāpyante
# btsun pa chos la gnas pa'i dge slong zhes bya ba'i do der ni bcom ldan 'das kyis thos pa dang bsam pa dang bsgom pa ni ril gyis byed na chos la gnas pa yin gyi / / sbyor ba gang yang rung ba tsam gyis ni ma yin par bstan to / / de la kun chub par byed pa dang kha ton du byed pa dang bshad pa mang ba dang rtog pa mang ba de 'ba' zhig ni thos pa dang sems pa la zhugs pa yin gyi / / bsgom pa la zhugs pa ma yin te / / rnal 'byor la sogs pa bor ba'i phyir ro /
yo 'pi kaścicchrutacintāmanāgamya kevalaṃ bhāvanāprayuktaḥ syātso 'pi na dharmavihārī vyavasthāpyate
# de'i phyir chos la gnas pa ma yin par rnam par gzhag go / / gang la la zhig gis thos pa dang sems pa la ma brten par bsgom pa 'ba' zhig la zhugs pa de yang chos la gnas pa ma yin par rnam par gzhag go /
tata eva tāvaddharmavihāriṇaṃ bhikṣumārabhya iha tu bhikṣurddharmaṃ paryāpnoti sūtraṃ geyamiti vistareṇoktvā paścādāha na riñcati yogamityevamādi yathā vijñāyeta śrutaṃ cintāṃ bhāvanāṃ cāgamya tadubhayavihāreṇa dharmavihārīti
# de'i phyir bcom ldan 'das kyis chos la gnas pa'i dge slong las brtsams te / / ci nas thos pa dang bsam pa dang bsgom pa la brten nas de gnyi ga la gnas pas chos la gnas pa yin par shes par bya ba'i phyir 'di la dge slong mdo'i sde dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde'i chos kun chub bar byed pa zhes rgya cher bka' stsal nas de'i 'og tu rnal 'byor mi 'dor ro zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so /
na riñcati yogamityevamādinā samādhiprayogāsaṃtuṣṭibhyāṃ bhāvanāmayaṃ saṃdarśitam / samādhiprayogaḥ punardvividhaḥ saṃdarśitaḥ sātatyasatkṛtyaprayogasaṃgṛhītaśca na riñcati yogamityanena aviparītaprayogasaṃgṛhītaśca na riñcati manaskāramityanena
# rnal 'byor mi 'dor ro zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni / / ting nge 'dzin la sbyor ba dang chog par mi 'dzin pas bsgom pa las 'byung ba bstan to / / ting nge 'dzin la sbyor ba ni rnam pa gnyis te / / rgyun du chud pa dang gus par sbyor bas bsdus pa ni rnal 'byor mi 'dor ba zhes bya ba 'dis bstan to / / ma log par sbyor bas bsdus pa ni yid la byed pa mi 'dor ba zhes bya ba 'dis bstan to /
asaṃtuṣṭirna riñcatyadhyātmacetaḥ śamathamityanena saṃdarśitā tadanāsvādanāduttaraśamathaprayogāccāsyāriñcanaṃ veditavyam
# chog par mi 'dzin pa ni nang du sems zhi gnas su byed pa mi 'dor ba zhes bya ba 'dis bstan te de'i ro mi myang ba dang gang du zhi gnas la sbyor bas mi 'dor bar blta'o /
kena kāraṇena vaipulyaṃ sūtrāntare bodhisattvapāramitāpiṭakamityucyate
# ci'i phyir mdo sde gzhan las shin tu rgyas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i sde snod ces bya zhe na /
tatra pāramitānāṃ saṃkhyānirdeśādyāvadanyonyaviniścayanācca
# der pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyi grangs bstan pa nas gcig la gcig rnam par nges pa'i bar du bstan pa'i phyir ro /
tatra saṃkhyā dvividhā gaṇanāsaṃkhyā tanmātrasaṃkhyā ca / ṣaṭpāramitā iti gaṇanāsaṃkhyā
# de la grangs ni rnam pa gnyis te / / bgrangs ba'i grangs dang de tsam gyi grangs so / / pha rol tu phyin pa drug ces bya ba ni bgrang ba'i grangs so /
sarvākārayorvodhisattvābhyudayaniḥśreyasamārgayostisṛbhistisṛbhiśca saṃgrahāt ṣaḍevapāramitā na bhūyasyo nālpoyasya itīyaṃ tanmātrasaṃkhyā
# byang chub sems dpa'i lam mngon par mtho ba dang nges par legs pa rnam pa thams cad dang ldan pa gnyis gsum gsum gyis bsdus pa'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa drug nyid de / / mi mang mi nyung ba ni de tsam gyi grangs so /
trividho 'bhyudayo mahābhogatā mahātmatā mahāpakṣatā ca
# mngon par mtho ba ni rnam pa gsum ste / / longs spyod chen po nyid dang; bdag nyid chen po nyid dang phyogs chen po nyid do /
tatra dānapāramitāyā mahābhogatā phalam / śīlapāramitāyā mahātmatā phalam śīlena sugatātmabhāvasaṃpattipratilambhāt / kṣāntipāramitāyā mahāpakṣatā phalam kṣāntyā sarvajanābhigamanoyatāpratilambhāditi / trividho niḥśreyasamārgaḥ kleśamabhibhūya kuśalapakṣaprayogopāyaḥ sattvaparipācanopāyaḥ buddhadharmasamudānayanopāyaśca eṣāmanyatareṇāpi vinā bodhisattvasya niḥśreyasānupapatteḥ
# de la sbyin pas longs spyod chen po thob pa'i phyir sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni longs spyod chen po nyid do / / de la tshul khrims kyis bde 'gro'i lus phun sum tshogs pa 'thob pa'i phyir tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni bdag nyid chen po nyid do / / bzod pas skye bo thams cad kyi mngon du 'gro bar 'gyur ba thob pa'i phyir bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i 'bras bu ni phyogs chen po nyid do / / nges par legs pa'i lam yang rnam pa gsum ste / / nyon mongs pa zil gyis mnan nas dge ba'i phyogs la sbyor ba'i thabs dang; sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i thabs dang sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par sgrub pa'i thabs te / / 'di dag las gang yang rung ba zhig med na byang chub sems dpa'i nges par legs pa mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
tatra sattvaparipācanopāyo dhyānapāramitā tatsaṃniśrayeṇābhijñābhiḥ sattvaparipācanāt
# de la sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i thabs ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste / / de la brten nas mngon par shes pa rnams kyis sems can yongs su smin par byed pa'i phyir ro /
punarapratiṣṭhitanirvāṇopāyataḥ ṣaḍeva pāramitāḥ
# yang mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i thabs su pha rol tu phyin pa drug nyid de /
bodhisattvena hi nirvāṇapratiṣṭhāviparyayeṇa saṃsāre 'bhyudayaḥ parigrahītavyaḥ
# byang chub sems dpa' mya ngan las 'das pa la gnas pa las bzlog ste / / 'khor ba na mngon bar mtho ba yongs su gzung bar bya'o /
saṃsārapratiṣṭhāviparyayeṇa tasminnasaṃkleṣṭavyam / atastisro 'bhyudayalābhopāyāstisrastadasaṃkleśopāyā yathāyogaṃ pūrvānusāreṇaiva veditavyāḥ
# 'khor ba na gnas pa las bzlog ste / / der nyon mongs pa med par bya'o / / de'i phyir gsum ni mngon par mtho ba thob pa'i thabs so / / gsum ni de na nyon mongs pa med pa'i thabs te / / snga ma'i tshul du go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o /
asaṃkleśopāye tu vīryeṇa pratipakṣabhāvanā dhyānena kleśaviṣkambhaṇam prajñayā kleśānuśayasamudghāta iti
# kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i thabs la brtson 'grus kyis ni gnyen po bsgom mo / / bsam gtan gyis ni nyon mongs pa rnam par gnon to / / shes rab kyis ni bag la nyal legs par 'joms so /
sarvānugrahatāṃ kleśapratipakṣatāṃ copādāyetyaparaḥ paryāyaḥ
# sems can rjes su 'dzin pa dang nyon mongs pa'i gnyen pa'i phyir yang rnam grangs gzhan te /
tatra dānena bodhisattvaḥ sattvānupakaraṇopasaṃhārānugraheṇānugṛhṇāti
# de la sbyin pas ni byang chung sems dpa' sems can rnams la yo byad nye bar sgrub pa'i phan 'dogs pas rjes su 'dzin to /
śīlena vighātotpīḍāviheṭhākaraṇenānugṛhṇāti yathākramaṃ bhogakāyacittopaghātānupasaṃhārāt
# tshul khrims kyis ni phongs pa dang gnod pa dang rnam par 'tshe ba mi byed pa'i tshul gyis rjes su 'dzin te / / go rims bzhin du logs spyod dang lus dang sems la gnod pa mi sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
kṣāntyā vighātotpīḍāviheṭhāmarṣaṇenānugṛhṇāti parebhya ātmano bhogādyupaghātasahanāt
# bzod pas ni phongs pa dang gnod pa la ji mi snyam par rjes su 'dzin to / / gzhan dag gis bdag gi longs spyod la sogs pa la gnod pa la mi mjed pa'i phyir te /
ābhistisṛbhiranugṛhṇāti
# de gsum gyis rjes su 'dzin to /
vīryeṇāviṣkambhitakleśo 'pi kuśalapakṣe prayujyate
# brtson 'grus kyis ni nyon mongs pa rnam par ma mnan yang dge ba'i phyogs la sbyor ro /
dhyānena kleśaṃ viṣkambhayati
# bsam gtan gyis ni nyon mongs pa rnam par gnon to /
prajñayānuśayaṃ samudghātayati / imāstisraḥ kleśapratipakṣā veditavyā / tatra pāramitālakṣaṇam / bodhisattvasya dānapāramitā katamā / yadbodhisattvasya bodhisattvadharmatāyāṃ vyavasthitasya bodhicittaṃ niśritya karuṇāpuraḥsareṇa cetasā sarvāstiparityāge kāyavāṅmanaskarma / evaṃ ca kṛtvā dānapāramitāyāḥ lakṣaṇaṃ gotrataḥ praṇidhānata āśayato vastutaḥ svabhāvataśca nirdiṣṭaṃ veditavyam / tadyathā bodhisattvadharmatā gotram bodhicittaṃ praṇidhānam karuṇāpuraḥsaraṃ ceta āśayaḥ sarvāstiparityāgo vastu kāyavāṅmanaskarmasvabhāva ityevaṃ yāvat prajñāpāramitā vistareṇa veditavyāḥ / ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ / śīlakṣāntivīryapāramitāsu yathākramaṃ sarvasaṃvarasamādānānurakṣāyāṃ sarvāpakāraduḥkhamarṣaṇādhivāsanāyāṃ sarvakuśaladharmasamudānayanatāyāṃ yatkāyavāṅmanaskarmeti veditavyam
# shes rab kyis ni bag la nyal legs par 'joms par byed do / / 'di gsum ni nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por rig par bya'o / / de la byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mtshan nyid ni gang zhe na / / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni gang byang chub sems dpa'i chos nyid la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i byang chub kyi sems la brten nas snying rje sngon du btang ba'i sems kyis bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong ba la lus dang dag dang yid kyi las te / / de ltar byas na sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mtshan nyid rigs dang; smon lam dang bsam pa dang dngos po dang ngo bo nyid kyis bstan par rig par bya'o / / 'di lta ste byang chub sems dpa'i chos nyid ni rigs so / / byang chub kyi sems ni smon lam mo / / snying rje sngon du gtong ba'i sems ni bsam pa'o / / bdog pa thams cad yongs su gtong ba ni dngos po'o / / lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las ni ngo bo nyid do / / de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar la yang rgya cher rig par bya'o / / 'di ni bye brag yin te / / tshul khrims dang bzod pa dang brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la ni sdom pa thams cad yang dag par len pa dang; rjes su bsrung ba dang gnod par byed pa dang sdug bsngal la ji mi snyam pa dang dang du len pa dang dge ba'i chos thams cad yang dag par bsgrub pa la lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las so zhes go rims bzhin du brjod par bya'o /
dhyānapāramitāyāṃ sarvākārakāyavāṅmanaskarmavibhutve sarvākārā cetasaḥ sthitiriti
# bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las kyi rnam pa thams cad dang dbang 'byor ba la sems kyi gnas pa rnam pa thams cad dang ldan pa'o /
prajñāpāramitāyāṃ sarvākārakāyavāṅmanaskarmavibhutve yaḥ sarvākāro dharmapravicaya iti vaktavyam
# shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las kyi rnam pa thams cad dang dbang 'byor pa la gang rnam pa thams cad du chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'o zhes brjod par bya'o /
śeṣaṃ dānavadeva sarvaṃ veditavyam
# lhag ma thams cad ni sbyin pa bzhin du rig par bya'o /
punaryaddānaṃ sarvajñatāmārabhya sarvajñatāyai saṃvartate sarvajñatāṃ parigṛhṇāti sarvajñatākṛtyaṃ ca karoti taddānapārimitetyucyate
# yang sbyin pa ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la brtsams pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'gyur ba dang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su 'dzin pa dang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bya ba byed pa ste / / de ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o /
etāni punaścatvāri padāni yathākramamārambhato vāsanātaḥ kāyato nisyandataśca veditavyāni
# tshig bzhi po de dag ni go rims bzhin du rtsom pa dang bag chags dang sku dang rgyu mthun par rig par bya'o /
tatrārambhataḥ sarvajñatāmārabhyotpannotpannasya tatra pariṇāmanāt
# de la rtsom pa ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid las brtsams te / / 'byung ba dang byung ba der yongs su bsngo ba'i phyir ro /
tadeva punardānaṃ saṃtati vāsayate yata āyatyāṃ sarvajñatāyai saṃvartate
# sbyin pa de nyid rgyud la bag chags su bsgos te / / de las phi ma la thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du 'gyur ro /
tadeva yadā paripūrṇaṃ bhavati tadā dharmakāyapariniṣpādanayogena sarvajñatāṃ parigṛhṇāti
# gang gi tshe de nyid yongs su rdzogs par gyur pa de'i tshe / / chos kyi sku yongs su grub pa'i tshul gyis thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su 'dzin to /
tata uttarakālaṃ sāṃbhogikarnarmāṇikakāyanisyandamukhena sarvajñatākṛtyaṃ karoti
# de'i 'og tu longs spyod rdzogs pa dang sprul pa'i skus rgyu mthun pa'i sgo nas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bya ba byed do /
evaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitā veditavyāḥ
# shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du yang de bzhin du rig par bya'o /
anukramaḥ / uttarottarasaṃniśrayatāmupādāya dānapāramitayādhyātmikabāhyasarvavastuparityāgābhyāsātkāyajīvitanirapekṣo bodhisattvo mahāntamapi bhogaskandhaṃ prahāya śīlasamādānaṃ karoti
# go rims ni 'og ma 'og ma la brten pa'i phyir te / / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pas ni nang dang phyi'i dngos po thams cad yongs su gtong bar goms pas / / lus dang srog la mi lta ba'i byang chub sems dpa' longs spyod kyi phung po chen po yang spangs nas tshul khrims la yang dag par 'dzin par byed do /
śīlānurakṣī ākruṣṭena mayā na pratyākroṣṭavyam ityevamādibhiḥ prakāraiḥ kṣamo bhavati
# tshul khrims rjes su bsrung ba ni gshe yang bdag gis slar gshe bar mi bya'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis bzod par 'gyur ro /
kṣamaḥ śītādīnām tannidānaṃ prayogāsrasanādārabdhavīryā bhavati
# grang ba la sogs pa bzod pa ni de'i gzhi las sbyor ba mi nyams pas brtson 'grus brtsams pa yin no /
ārabdhavīryaḥ prayoganiṣṭhāphalādhigamādadhyānaṃ saṃpādayati
# brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni sbyor ba'i mtha'i 'bras bu thob pas bsam gtan bsgrub bo /
saṃpannadhyānaśca samāhitacitto yathābhūtajñānāllokottarāṃ prajñāṃ pratilabhata iti
# bsam gtan phun sum tshogs te sems mnyam par gzhag pa ni yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab thob po / / yang gong ma gong ma ni gzhi yin pa'i phyir ro /
punaruttarottarādhārataḥ śīlaṃ dānasyādhāra evaṃ yāvatprajñā dhyānasya
# tshul khrims ni sbyin pa'i gzhi yin no / / de bzhin du shes rab ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i gzhi yin pa'i bar du'o /
tathāhi śīlavato dānaṃ viśuddhaṃ bhavati dānenānugṛhītasya śīlena paghātākaraṇataḥ / evamasya pratigrāhakasya bodhisattvena viheṭhāvirahitopakaraṇasukhopasaṃhārācchīlabalena dānapāramitā viśuddhirveditavyā
# 'di ltar tshul khrims dang ldan pa ni sbyin pas phan btags pa la tshul khrims kyis gnod pa'i byed pa'i phyir sbyin pa rnam par dag par 'gyur ro / / de ltar byang chub sems dpa' len pa po de la rnam par 'tshe ba dang bral bar yo byad kyis bde bar sbyor bas tshul khrims kyi stobs kyis sbyin pa rnam par dag par rig par bya'o /
evaṃ kṣamiṇaḥ śīlaviśuddhiḥ parāpakāraiḥ śikṣāpadākhaṇḍanāt
# de ltar bzod pa dang ldan pa ni gzhan gnod par byed pa dag gis bslab pa'i gzhi mi 'dral bas tshul khrims rnam par dag go /
ārabdhavīryasya kṣāntiviśuddhiḥ utsāhabalenotpatya saṃsāramabhyupagatavato 'kṛcchreṇa sattvavipratipattiduḥkhasahanāt
# brtson 'grus brtsams pas spro ba'i stobs kyi ched du 'khor ba khas blangs pa ni sems can log par sgrub pa'i sdug bsngal bde blag tu bzod pas bzod pa rnam par dag go /
dhyāyinī vīryaviśuddhiḥ saha sukhena saumanasyena sarvakuśaladharmaprayogāt
# bsam gtan pa ni bde ba dang bcas pa dang yid bde pa dang bcas par dge ba'i chos thams cad la sbyor bas brtson 'grus rnam par dag go /
prajñāvato dhyānaviśuddhiḥ bahuprakārāndharmānvipaśyatyadhyātmaṃ śamathataḥ samādhyabhivṛddheḥ nāsti dhyānamaprajñasyeti gāthāyāṃ vacanāditi
# brtson 'grus brtsams pas shes rab dang ldan pa ni chos rnam pa mang po la rnam par bltas nas nang du zhi bar byed pa ni ting nge 'dzin rnam par 'phel bas bsam gtan rnam par dag ste / / shes rab med la bsam gtan med / / ces tshig su bcad pa las gsungs pa'i phyir ro /
yathaudārikaścāparo 'nukramo veditavyaḥ
# ji ltar rags pa'i rim gyis yang go rims kyis yang go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o /
sarvaudārikaṃ hi dānamataḥ prathamato vyavasthāpyate
# sbyin pa ni thams cad kyi nang nas rags ste [*te] / / de'i phyir sbyin pa thog mar rnam par gzhag go /
tadanantaraṃ kṣāntyādibhyaḥ śīlamaudārikamevaṃ yāvatprajñāyā dhyānamaudārikam
# de'i 'og tu bzod pa la sogs pas tshul khrims rags so / / de bzhin du shes rab pas bsam gtan rags pa'i bar du'o /
sarvasūkṣmā tu prajñā ataḥ sarvapaścādvyavasthāpyata iti / nirvacanam
# shes rab ni thams cad kyi nang na phra ste / / de'i phyir thams cad kyi tha mar rnam par gzhag go /
kena kāraṇena dānaṃ dānapāramitetyucyate
# nges tshig ni ci'i phyir sbyin pa la sbyin pa'i pha rol du phyin pa zhes bya zhe na /
mahaddānaṃ nirdoṣaṃ nirmalaṃ dānapāramitetyucyate / tatra mahaddānaṃ sarvaprakārādhyātmikabāhyavastu dānato dīrghakāladānataśca
# sbyin pa chen po dang skyon med pa dang dri ma med pa ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o / / de la sbyin pa chen po ni nang dang phyi'i dngos po'i rnam pa thams cad sbyin pa dang yun ring du sbyin pa'i phyir ro /
nirdoṣaṃ viṣamaparyeṣṭayādivivarjitatvāt nirmalaṃ mātsaryavipakṣaprahāṇāt
# skyon med pa ni gnod pas kun tu tshol ba la sogs pa rnam par spangs pa'i phyir ro /
yathoktaṃ dānapāramitāmārabhyāryākṣayamatinirdeśasūtre nirmalaṃ savāsanavipakṣaprahāṇāt / tadanayā trividhayā paramatayā dānapāramitetyabhidyotitaṃ bhavati / trividhā paramatā svabhāvaparamatā sahaparicayena upāyaparamatā phalaparamatā ca / paricayaḥ punardīrghakāladānato veditavyaḥ / evaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitā veditavyā / śīlādīnāṃ punarnirdoṣatvamā tmasamāropavarjitatvādibhiryathāyogam tadakṣayamatisūtreṣu draṣṭavyam / punardvādaśavidhena paramatvena yogātpāramitetyucyate / dvādaśavidhaṃ punaḥ paramatvam audāryaparamatvaṃ sarvalokasampattyanarthitvādutkṛṣṭatvācca / āyatatvaparamatvaṃ trikalpāsaṃkhyeyaparibhāvanāt / adhikāraparamatvaṃ sarvasattvārthakriyādhikārapravṛttatvāt / akṣayatvaparamatvaṃ mahābodhipariṇāmanayātyantamaparyādānāt / nairantaryaparamatvamātmaparasamatādhimokṣātsarvasattvadānādibhiḥ pāramitāparipūraṇāt / akṛcchratvaparamatvamanumodanāmātreṇa paradānādīnāṃ pāramitāparipūraṇāt / vibhutvaparamatvaṃ gaganagañjasamādhyādibhirdānādiparipūraṇāt / parigrahaparamatvaṃ nirvikalpajñātaparigṛhītatvāt / ārambhaparamatvamadhimukticaryābhūmāvadhimātrāyāṃ kṣāntau / pratilambhaparamatvaṃ prathamāyāṃ bhūmau / nisyandaparamatvaṃ tadanyāsvaṣṭāsu / niṣpattiparamatvaṃ daśamyāṃ bhūmau tāthāgatyāṃ ca bodhisattvapariniṣpattyā buddhapariniṣpattyā ceti / punaḥ paramairīhitā itāśceti pāramitāḥ buddhabodhisattvaiśceṣṭitā gatāścetyarthaḥ / punarjñeyapāraṃgatāḥ pāramitāḥ buddhatve pratiṣṭhitā ityarthaḥ / punaḥ parānātmānaṃ ca paramāmīti tārayantoti pāramitāḥ parānātmānaṃ ca duḥkhārṇavamatikrāmantītyarthaḥ / idaṃ tāvatsādhāraṇaṃ nirvacanam / pratyekaṃ punardāyakadāridrayāpanayatāddānam dāhāpanayanādvā pratigrāhakānām / śāntendriyālambhanācchubhagatilīyanācchaityālayācca śīlaṃ yathākramamindriyeṣu guptadvāratāvāhanāt sugatigamanahetubhāvanādavipratisārādyānupūrvyā yāvannirvāṇāśrayatvāditi / krodhakṣāratiraskaraṇāt kṣaticittāgatitiraskaraṇāt kṣemāviṣkaraṇācca kṣatināṃ kṣāntiḥ / kṣaticittaṃ punaryenāpa kāriṇāṃ pratyapakāraḥ kriyate tasyāgatasyānayā vilopanaṃ tiraskaraṇaṃ veditavyam / kṣatameṣāṃ vairaṃ vidyata iti kṣatinasteṣāmabhayaprakāśanaṃ kṣemasyāviṣkaraṇaṃ veditavyam / vadhavṛddhohāyogādvoryam / tatra vadhāyehākuśaladharmavigamāya dvābhyāṃ samyakprahāṇābhyām vṛddhaye īhā kuśaladharmasamudāgamāya dvābhyāṃ samyakprahāṇābhyāṃ ca / dhāraṇayamanasaṃyamanavinayananayanāddhyānam / tatra dhāraṇāmālaṃbane cittasya yamanaṃ vikṣepataḥ saṃyamanaṃ cittasya vinayanaṃ paryavasthānānāṃ viṣkambhaṇam nayanaṃ vibhutvasya prāpaṇaṃ veditavyam / parapraṇītajñānāt pratyātmajñānāt prakārajñānāt śamaprāptiguṇaprakarṣajñānācca prajñā / tatra parapraṇītajñānaṃ parato ghoṣānvayā yoniśomanaskārasaṃprayuktā prajñā pratyātmajñānaṃ lokottarā prakārajñānaṃ lokottarapṛṣṭhalabdhā śamaprāptaye jñānaṃ bhāvanāmārge kleśapratipakṣabhūtā guṇaprakarṣāya jñānaṃ vaiśeṣikaguṇābhinirhārāya prajñā veditavyā / bhāvanā pañcavidhā upadhisaṃniśritā yāvadvibhutvasaṃniśritā / tatropadhisaṃniśritā caturākārā / hetusaṃniśritā yo gotrabalena pāramitāsu pratipattyabhyāsaḥ vipākasaṃniśritā ya ātmabhāvasaṃpattibalena / prāṇidhānasaṃniśritā yaḥ pūrvapraṇidhānabalena / pratisaṃkhyānabalasaṃniśritā yaḥ prajñābalena pāramitāsu pratipattyabhyāsaḥ / manaskārasaṃniśritā pāramitābhāvanā caturākārā / adhimuktimanaskāreṇa sarvapāramitāpratisaṃyukta sūtrāntamadhimucyamānasya / āsvādanāmanaskāreṇa labdhāḥ pāramitāḥ āsvādayato guṇadarśanayogena / anumodanāmanaskāreṇa sarvalokadhātuṣu sarvasattvānāṃ dānādikamanumodamānasya / abhinandanāmanaskāreṇātmanaḥ sattvānāṃ cānāgataṃ pāramitāviśeṣamabhinandamānasya / āśayasaṃniśritā pāramitābhāvanā ṣaḍākārā atṛptāśayena vaipulyāśayena muditāśayenopakarāśayena nirlepāśayena kalyāṇāśayena ca / tatra bodhisattvasya dāne 'tṛptāśayo yadbodhisattvasyaikakṣaṇe gaṅgānadīvālikāsamānlokadhātūn saptaratnaparipūrṇān pratipādayato gaṅgānadīvālikāsamāṃścātmabhāvanevaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ gaṅgānadīvālikāsamān kalpān pratipādayataḥ
# ji skad du 'phags pa blo gros mi zad pas bstan pa'i mdo las sbyin pa'i zad pa las brtsams te bstan pa / / btsun pa shar dva ti'i bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyin pa yang mi zad pa ste / / de ci'i phyir zhe na / / tshad med pa'i phyir ro / / btsun pa sha ra dva ti'i bu byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sbyin pa yongs su sbyang ba yang tshad med pa ste / / tshe dang spobs pa dang bde ba dang stobs dang kha dog nye bar brtan pa'i phyir zas 'dod pa rnams la zas sbyin pa'o / / nyon mongs pa'i sred pa bsal ba'i phyir btung ba 'dod pa rnams la btung ba sbyin pa'o / / bde ba dang 'byor ba'i dngos po thams cad bsdu ba'i phyir / / bzhon pa 'dod pa rnams la bzhon pa sbyin pa'o / / ngo tsha shes pa dang khrel yod pa dang mdog gser gyi kha dog yongs su sbyang ba'i phyir gos 'dod pa rnams la gos sbyin pa'o / / de bzhin gshegs pa'i lha'i sbyan yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir mar me 'dod pa rnams la mar me sbyin pa'o / / de bzhin gshegs pa'i lha'i snyan yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir sil snyan 'dod pa rnams la sil snyan sbyin pa'o / / tshul khrims dang thos pa dang ting nge 'dzin gyi dris byug pa'i phyir spos dang byug pa 'dod pa rnams la spos dang byug pa sbyin pa'o / / gzugs dang spobs pa dang byang chub kyi yan lag gi me tog thob par bya ba'i phyir phreng ba 'dod pa rnams la phreng ba sbyin pa'i / / lus kyi dri yid du 'ong ba thob par bya ba'i phyir / / phye ma 'dod pa rnams la phye ma sbyin pa'o / / skyes bu chen po'i mtshan ro bro ba'i mchog yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir ro bro ba thams cad 'dod pa la ro bro ba thas cad sbyin pa'o / / sems can thams cad kyi gnas dang skyabs dang gon dang dpung gnyen bya ba'i phyir gnas 'dod pa rnams la gnas sbyin pa'o / / sgrib pa thams cad rab tu spangs pa dang lha dang tshangs pa'i gnas pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzims cha thob par bya ba'i phyir / / mal cha 'dod pa rnams la mal cha sbyin pa'o / / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi sa thams cad kyi byang chub kyi snying rdo rdo rje'i gdan thob par bya ba'i phyir stan 'dod pa rnams la stan sbyin pa'o / / byang chub kyi yo byad thams cad yongs su bskang bar bya ba'i phyir yo byad 'dod pa rnams la yo byad sbyin pa'o / / mi rga mi 'chi ba'i bdud rtsi'i bde bas yongs su bskang ba'i phyir na ba dang sman 'dod pa rnams la sman sbyin pa'o / / rang dbang dang rang nyams dang rang byung gi ye shes yongs su bskang ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis bran po dang bran mo yongs su gtong ba'i sbyin pa'o zhes rgya cher 'byung ba lta bu'o / / dri ma med pa ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs bag chags dang bcas pa spangs pa'i phyir ro; / / dam pa rnam pa 'di gsum gyis sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa zhes brjod pa yin te / / dam pa rnam pa gsum ni 'dris pa dang bcas pa'i ngo bo nyid dam pa dang thabs dam pa dang 'bras bu dam pa'o / / 'dris pa ni yun ring po nas sbyin par rig par bya'o / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du yang de bzhin du rig par bya'o / / tshul khrims la sogs pa'i skyon med pa ni bdag tu sgro 'dogs pa rnam par spangs pa la sogs pa'i phyir te / / ci rigs su blo gros mi zad pas bstan pa las blta bar bya'o / / yang dam pa rnam pa bcu gnyis dang ldan pa'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o / / dam pa rnam pa bcu gnyis la / / rgya che ba dam pa ni 'jig rten gyi phun sum tshogs pa thams cad mi 'dod pa dang mchog tu gyur ba'i phyir ro / / yun ring ba dam pa ni bskal ba grangs med pa gsum du yongs su bsgom pa'i phyir ro / / ched du bya ba dam pa ni sems can thams cad kyi don bya ba'i ched kyi phyir ro / / zad mi shes pa dam pa ni byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pas gtan du yongs su gtugs par mi 'gyur pa'i phyir ro / / rgyun mi 'chad pa dam pa ni bdag dang gzhan mnyam pa nyid du mos pa'i phyir sems can thams cad kyi sbyin pa la sogs pas pha rol tu phyin pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro / / chogs med pa dam pa ni gzhan gyi sbyin pa la sogs pa la rjes su yi rang ba tsam gyis pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro / / dbang 'byor pa dam pa ni nam mkha' mdzod kyi ting nge 'dzin la sogs pas sbyin pa la sogs pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro / / yongs su bzung ba dam pa ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis yongs su bzung ba'i phyir ro / / rtsom pa dam pa ni mos pas spyod pa'i sa la bzod pa chen por gyur pa la'o / / thob pa dam pa ni sa dang po la'o / / rgyu mthun pa dam pa ni de ma yin pa gzhan brgyad po dag la'o / / 'grub pa dam pa ni sa bcu pa dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la byang chub sems dpa' 'grub pa dang sangs rgyas 'grub pa'i phyir ro / / yang dam pa rnams kyis spyad pa dang bgrod pa'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa ste / / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis spyad pa dang bgrod ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / yang shes bya'i pha rol tu son pas pha rol tu phyin pa ste / / sangs rgyas nyid la gnas zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / yang gzhan dang bdag mchog tu gnod pa las sgrol bar byed pa'i phyir pha rol tu phyin pa rnams te / / gzhan dang bdag sdug bsngal gyi rgya mtsho las 'da' bar byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / 'di ni re zhig thun mong gi nges pa'i tshig go / / so so'i nges pa'i tshig ni sbyin bdag gi dbul ba sel ba dang len pa po rnams kyi gdung ba sel ba'i phyir sbyin pa'o / / dbang po zhi ba thob pa dang 'gro ba bzang por sbyor ba dang bsil pa'i gnas yin pas tshul khrims te / / go rims bzhin du dbang po rnams kyi sgo sdom par byed pa dang bde 'gror 'gro ba'i rgyur gyur pa dang 'gyod pa med pa la sogs pa'i rim gyis mya ngan las 'das pa la sogs pa'i bar gyi gnas yin pa'i phyir ro / / khro ba'i tsha ba sel ba dang rma 'byin pa'i sems 'ongs pa sel ba dang zhi bar brjod pa'i phyir bzod pa'o / / rma 'byin pa'i sems zhes bya ba ni gang gis gnod pa byed pa rnams la lan du gnod pa byed pa ste / / de 'ongs pa 'dis 'bral bar byed pa ni sel bar rig par bya'o / / rma 'byin pa ni 'di dag la shar gnyer ba yod pas rma 'byin pa can te / / de dag la mi 'jigs pa sgrogs pa ni bde bar brjod par rig par bya'o / / sel ba dang 'phel bar byed pa dang ldan pas brtson 'grus te / / de la sel ba'i phyir spyod pa ni yang dag par spong ba gnyis kyis mi dge ba'i chos dang bral bar byed pa'o / / 'phel ba'i phyir spyod pa ni yang dag par spong ba gnyis kyis dge ba'i chos yang dag par sgrub pa'o / / 'dzin pa dang sdom pa dang 'dul ba dang 'thob par byed pas bsam gtan te / / de la 'dzin pa ni dmigs pa la sems 'dzin pa'o / / sdom pa ni rnam par g yeng ba las sems yang dag par sdom pa'o / / 'dul ba ni kun nas dkris pa rnams rnam par gnod pa'o / / thob par byed pa ni dbang 'byor pa thob par byed par rig par bya'o / / gzhan gyis smras pa shes pa dang so so rang gis shes pa dang rnam par shes pa dang rab tu zhi ba thob pa dang; / / yon tan mchog tu phyin par shes pas shes rab ste / / de la gzhan gyis smras pa shes pa ni gzhan gyi sgra'i rgyu las byung ba'i tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i shes rab bo / / so so rang gis shes pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'o / / rnam par shes pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i rjes las thob ba'o / / zhi ba thob par bya ba'i phyir shes pa ni bsgom pa'i lam la nyon mongs pa'i gnyen por gyur pa'o / / yon tan mchog tu phyin par bya ba'i phyir shes pa ni yon tan khyad par can mngon par sgrub pa'i shes rab tu rig par bya'o / / bsgom pa ni rnam lnga ste / / phung po la gnas pa nas dbang 'byor pa la gnas pa'i bar du'o / / 'dir tshigs su bcad pa / / phung por brten nas bsgom pa ste / / yid la byed dang bsams pa dang / / thabs dang dbang 'byor de bzhin te / / de dag thams cad brjod pa yin / / ji skad du / / rgyu dang smin dang smon lam dang / / so sor brtags pas phung por dran / / zhes bshad pa lta bu'o / / de la phung po la gnas pa rnam pa bzhi ste / / de la rgyu la gnas pa ni gang rigs kyi stobs kyis pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la nan tan gyis goms par byed pa'o / / rnam par smin pa la gnas pa ni gang lus phun sum tshogs pa'i stobs kyis so / / smon lam la gnas pa ni gang sngon gyi smon lam gyi stobs so / / so sor brtags pa'i stobs la gnas pa ni shes rab kyi stobs kyis pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la nan tan gyis goms par byed pa'o / / yid la byed pa la gnas pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa rnam pa bzhi ste / / mos pa yid la byed pas bsgom pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad dang ldan pa'i mdo sde la mos pa bsgom pa'o / / ro myang ba'i yid la byed pas bsgom pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa rnams la phan yon mthong ba'i tshul gyis ro myong bar byed pa'o / / rjes su yi rang ba yid la byed pas bsgom pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi sbyin pa la sogs pa la rjes su yi rang ba'o / / mngon bar dga' ba yid la byed pas bsgom pa ni bdag dang sems can rnams kyi ma 'ongs pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i khyad par la mngon par dga' ba'o / / bsam pa la gnas pa ni pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa rnam drug ste / / mi ngoms pa'i bsam pa dang yangs pa'i bsam pa dang dga' ba'i bsam pa dang phan gdags pa'i bsam pa dang gos pa med pa'i bsam pa dang dge ba'i bsam pa'o / / de la byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa la mi ngoms pa'i bsam pa ni gang byang chub sems dpa' skad cig gcig la gang g'a'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che sna bdun gyis yongs su bkang ba dang lus gang g'a'i klung gi bye ma snyed sems can gcig la sbyin par byed ce'o /
yathā caikasattvasyaivaṃ yāvān sattvadhāturanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau paripācitavyaḥ / tamanena paryāyeṇa pratipādayedatṛpta eva bodhisattvasya dānāśaya iti
# de bzhin du skad cig re re la gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi bskal par sbyin par byed cing sems can gcig la ji lta ba bzhin du sems can gyi khams ji snyed pa bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la yongs su smin par byed la rnam grang 'dis de la sbyin yang mi ngoms pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa'i bsam pa ste /
ya evaṃrūpaṃ āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya dāne 'tṛptāśayaḥ
# rnam pa 'di lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa 'di ni sbyin pa la byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa mi ngoms pa yin no /
na ca bodhisattva evaṃrūpāṃ dānaparaṃparāṃ kṣaṇamātramapi hāpayati vicchinattyābodhimaṇḍaniṣadanāditi
