# byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug gi bar du byang chub sems dpa' rnam pa de lta bur sbyin pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa skad cig tsam yang nyams par mi byed cing rgyun mi gcod de /
ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya dāne vipulāśayaḥ
# rnam pa 'di lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa 'di ni sbyin pa la byang chub sems dpa'i yangs pa'i bsam pa'o /
muditataraśca bodhisattvo bhavati tānsattvāṃstathā dānenānugṛhṇan na ca te sattvāstena dānenānugṛhyamāṇā iti
# de ltar sbyin pas sems can de dag rjes su 'dzin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni shin tu dga' ba yin gyi sbyin pa des rjes su gzung ba'i sems can de dag ni de lta ma yin te /
ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya dāne muditāśayaḥ
# rnam pa de lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin ba de ni sbyin pa la byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba'i bsam pa'o /
upakaratarāṃśca bodhisattvastān sattvānātmanaḥ samanupaśyati yeṣāṃ tathā dānenopakaroti nātmānam teṣāmanuttarasamyaksaṃbodhyupastambhatāmuṣādāya iti
# gang dag la de ltar sbyin pas phan 'dogs pa'i sems can de dag ni bdag la shin tu phan 'dogs par byang chub sems dpas mthong gi / / bdag gis ni ma yin te / / de dag ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ston pa'i phyir ro /
ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya dāne upakarāśayaḥ
# rnam pa 'di lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa de ni sbyin pa la byang chub sems dpa'i phan 'dogs pa'i bsam pa'o /
na ca bodhisattvaḥ sattveṣu tathā vipulamapi dānamayaṃ puṇyamabhisaṃskṛtya pratikāreṇa vārthī bhavati vipākena veti
# byang chub sems dpa' ni sems can rnams la de ltar sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams yangs pa mngon par 'du byas kyang len du phan 'dogs pa'am / / rnam par smin pa 'dod pa med de /
ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya dānapāramitābhāvanāyāṃ nirlepāśayaḥ / yadbodhisattvastathā vipulasyāpi dānaskandhasya vipākaṃ sattveṣvevābhinandati nātmanaḥ sarvasattvasādhāraṇaṃ ca kṛtvānuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau pariṇāmayatīti / ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya dānapāramitābhāvanāyāṃ kalyāṇāśayaḥ / tatra bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitābhāvanāyāṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāyāmatṛptāśayaḥ yadbodhisattvo gaṅgānadīvālikāsameṣvātmabhāveṣu gaṅgānadīvālikāsamakalpāyuḥpramāṇeṣu sarvopakaraṇanirantaravighātī trisāhasramahāsāhasre lokadhātāvāgniparipūrṇe caturvidhamīryāpathaṃ kalpayannekaṃ śīlapāramitākṣaṇaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitākṣaṇaṃ bhāvayet etena paryāyeṇa yāvacchīlaskandho yāvatprajñāskandho yenānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyate śīlaskandhaṃ yāvatprajñāskandhaṃ bhāvayet atṛpta evaṃ bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitābhāvanāyāmāśayo yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāyāmāśaya iti
# rnam pa 'di lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa la byang chub sems dpa'i gos pa med pa'i bsam pa'o / / byang chub sems dpa' sbyin pa'i phung po yangs pa'i rnam par smin pa de lta bu yang sems can rnams kyi yin bar mngon par dga' bar byed kyi / / bdag la ni ma yin te / / sems can thams cad dang thun mong du byas nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo'o / / rnam pa 'di lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa la byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i bsam pa'o / / de la tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa nas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa'i bar la byang chub sems dpa'i mi ngoms pa'i bsam pa ni / / gang byang chub sems dpa' lus gang gla'i klung gi bye ma snyed du gyur cing tshe'i tshad bskal ba gang gla'i klung gi bye ma snyed du gyur la rgyun du yo byad thams cad kyis phongs par gyur cing / / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams mes rab tu gang ba na spyod lam bzhi byed cing skad cig gcig la tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa nas / / skad cig gcig la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom zhing rnam grangs 'dis tshul khrims kyi phung po ji snyed pa dang shes rab kyi bar gyi phung po ji snyed pa gang gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'i tshul khrims kyi phung po nas shes rab kyi bar gyi phung po de bsgom yang byang chub sems dpa'i mi ngoms pa nyid ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa la mi ngoms pa'i bsam pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa la mi ngoms pa'i bsam pa ste /
ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitābhāvanāyāmatṛptāśayo yāvatprajñāpāramitāyāṃ bhāvanāyām
# byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa rnam pa 'di lta bu gang yin pa 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa la mi ngoms pa'i bsam pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa la mi ngoms pa'i bsam ba'o /
yadbodhisattvastāṃ śīlapāramitābhāvanāparaṃparāṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāparaṃparamā bodhimaṇḍaniṣadanānna bhraṃśayati na vicchinattīti / ya evaṃrūpa āśāyo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitābhāvanāyāṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāyāṃ vipulāśayaḥ / muditataraśca bodhisattvo bhavati tayā śīlapāramitābhāvanayā yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanayā sattvānanugṛhṇan na tveva te sattvā anugṛhyamāṇā iti
# byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug gi bar du tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa nas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa nyams par mi byed cing / / rgyun mi gcod pa'i bsam pa rnam pa 'di lta bu gang yin pa 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa nas; shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa la byang chub sems dpa' yangs pa'i bsam pa'o / / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa des sems can rjes su 'dzin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni rab tu dga' ba yin gyi / / rjes su bzung ba'i sems can de dag ni de lta ma yin te / / rnam pa de lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa de ni /
ya evaṃrūpaāśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitābhāvanāyāṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāyāṃ muditāśayaḥ
# tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa la byang chub sems dpa'i dga' ba'i bsam pa'o / / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa nas /
upakaratarāṃśca sa bodhisattvastān sattvānātmanaḥ samanupaśyati yeṣāṃ tathā śīlapāramitābhāvanayā yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanayā upakarāti nātmānam teṣāmanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhyupastambhatāsu pādāyeti / ya evarūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitābhāvanāyāṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāyāmupakarāśayaḥ
# shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pas / / gang dag la phan 'dogs pa'i sems can de dag ni bdag la shin tu phan 'dogs par byang chub sems dpas mthong gi bdag gis ni ma yin no / / de dag ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ston pa'i phyir ro / / rnam pa 'di lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa la / / byang chub sems dpa'i phan 'dogs pa'i bsam pa'o /
na ca bodhisattvastathā vipulamapi śīlapāramitāmayaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitāmayaṃ puṇyamabhisaṃskṛtya tasya pratikāreṇa vārthī bhavati vipākena veti / ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitāyāṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitāyāṃ nirlepāśayaḥ / tatra yadbodhisattva evaṃ śīlapāramitābhāvanāmayasya yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāmayasya puṇyaskandhasya vipākaṃ sattveṣvevābhinandati nātmanaḥ sarvasattvasādhāraṇaṃ ca kṛtvānuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhau pariṇāmayatīti
# byang chub sems dpa' ni 'di ltar tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las byung ba nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar las byung ba'i bsod nams yangs pa mngon par 'dus byas kyang / / de la lan du phan 'dogs pa'am rnam par smin pa las 'dod pa med de / / rnam pa 'di lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa de ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin ba bsgom pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa la byang chub sems dpa'i gos pa med pa'i bsam pa'o / / de la byang chub sems dpa' tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgoms pa las byung ba nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgoms pa las byung ba'i bsod nams kyi phung po rnam par smin pa de lta bu yang sems can rnams kyi yin par mngon par dga' bar byed kyi bdag la ni ma yin te / / sems can thams cad dang thun mong du byas nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo'o /
ya evaṃrūpa āśayo 'yaṃ bodhisattvasya śīlapāramitāyāṃ bhāvanāyāṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitābhāvanāyāṃ kalyāṇāśayaḥ / upāyasaṃniśritā pāramitābhāvanā trayākārā nirvikalpena jñānena trimaṇḍalapariśuddhipratyavekṣaṇatāmupādāya / tathāhi sa upāyaḥ sarvamanaskārāṇāmabhiniṣpattaye
# rnam pa de lta bu'i bsam pa gang yin pa de ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du bsgom pa la byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i bsam pa'o / / thabs la gnas te pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa gang zhe na / / rnam pa gsum ste / / so sor rtog pa'i phyir rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis 'khor gsum yongs su dag pa ste / / thabs de ni yid la byed pa thams cad mngon par 'grub pa'i phyir ro /
vibhutvasaṃniśritā pāramitābhāvanā trayākārā kāyavibhutvataḥ caryāvibhutvataḥ deśanāvibhutvaśca
# dbang 'byor ba la gnas te pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa ni rnam pa gsum ste / / lus la dbang 'byor pa dang spyod pa la dbang 'byor pa dang bshad ba la dbang 'byor ba'o /
tatra kāyavibhutvaṃ tāthāgatau dvau kāyau draṣṭavyau svābhāvikaḥ sāṃbhogikaśca
# lus la dbang 'byor pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gnyis su blta bar bya ste / / rang bzhin dang longs spyod rdzogs pa'o /
tatra caryāvibhutvaṃ nairmāṇikaḥ kāyo draṣṭavyo yena sarvākārāṃ sarvasattvānāṃ sahadhārmikacaryāṃ darśayati
# de la spyod pa la dbang 'byor ba ni sprul pa'i skur blta bar bya ste / / des sems can thams cad la spyod pa rnam pa thams cad kun tu ston to /
deśanā vibhutvaṃ ṣaṭpāramitāsarvākāradeśanāyāmavyāghātataḥ
# bshad pa la dbang 'byor ba ni pha rol tu phyin pa drug rnam pa thams cad du bshad pa la thogs pa med pa'o /
prabhedato 'ṣṭādaśabhirupastambhaiḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ pāramitānāṃ prabhedo veditavyaḥ
# rab tu dbye ba ni ston pa bco brgyad kyis pha rol tu phyin pa drug rab tu dbye bar blta bar bya'o /
aṣṭādaśopastambhāḥ kāyopastambhaḥ cittopastambhaḥ kuśalopastambhaḥ sugatyupastambhaḥ bodhyupastambhaḥ karuṇopastambhaḥ sattvāparityāgopastambhaḥ hīnacittaparityāgopastambhaḥ / anutpattikadharmakṣāntyupastambhaḥ kuśalamūlaprayogopastambhaḥ kuśalamūlasamudāgamopastambhaḥ kuśalamūlākṣayatopastambhaḥ aparikhedopastambhaḥ sarvacintitārthasamṛddhayupastambhaḥ gaṇaparikarṣaṇopastambhaḥ bhūmipraveśopastambhaḥ buddhadharmasamudānayanopastambhaḥ buddhakṛtyānuṣṭhānopastambhaśca
# rtog pa bco brgyad ni lus rton pa dang; sems rton pa dang dge ba rton pa dang bde 'gro rton pa dang byang chub rton pa dang snying rje rton pa dang sems can yongs su mi gtong pa rton pa dang dman pa'i sems yongs su dor ba rton pa dang mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa rton pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba la sbyor ba rton pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba yang dag par sgrub pa rton pa dang / / dge ba'i rtsa ba mi zad pa rton pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba la yongs su mi skyo ba rton pa dang bsam pa'i don thams cad 'byor ba rton pa dang tshogs sdud pa rton pa dang sa la 'jug pa rton pa dang sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par sgrub pa rton pa dang sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa sgrub pa rton pa ste /
pratyekaṃ dānādīnāṃ traivighyāt tribhistribhirupastambhairyathākramaṃ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ
# sbyin pa la sogs pa rnam pa gsum gsum du tha dad pas / / gsum gsum gyi go rims bzhin du bsdus par rig par bya'o /
tatra trividhaṃ dānam abhayadānaṃ dharmadānamāmiṣadānaṃ ca
# de la sbyin pa rnam pa gsum ni zang zing gi sbyin pa dang mi 'jigs pa'i sbyin pa dang chos kyi sbyin pa'o /
trividhaṃ śīlam saṃvaraśīlaṃ kuśaladharmasaṃgrāhakaṃ śīlaṃ sattvārthakriyāśīlaṃ ca / trividhā kṣāntiḥ apakāramarṣaṇakṣāntirduḥkhādhivāsanākṣāntirdharmanidhyānakṣāntiśca
# tshul khrims rnam pa gsum ni sngom pa'i tshul khrims dang dge ba'i chos sdud pa'i tshul khrims dang sems can gyi don bya ba'i tshul khrims so / / bzod pa rnam pa gsum ni / / gnod pa byed pa la ji mi snyam pa'i bzod pa dang sdug bsngal dang du len pa'i bzod pa dang chos la nges par sems pa'i bzod pa'o /
trividhaṃ vīryam saṃnāhavīryaṃ prayogavīryaṃ sattvārthakriyāvīryaṃ ca / trividhaṃ dhyānam dṛṣṭadharmasukhāvihārāya dhyānamabhijñānirhārāya dhyānaṃ sattvārthakriyāyai ca dhyānam / trividhā prajñā saṃvṛtyālaṃbanā paramārthālaṃbanā sattvārthālambanā ca
# brtson 'grus rnam pa gsum ni / / go cha'i brtson 'grus dang sbyor ba'i brtson 'grus dang sems can gyi don bya ba'i brtson 'grus so / / bsam gtan rnam pa gsum ni mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas par bya ba'i bsam gtan dang mngon par shes pa mngon bar sgrub ba'i bsam gtan dang sems can gyi don bya ba'i bsam gtan no / / shes rab rnam pa gsum ni kun rdzob la dmigs pa dang don dam pa la dmigs pa dang sems can gyi don la dmigs pa'o /
tatrāmiṣadānaṃ kāyopastambhaḥ annapānādyupakaraṇaiḥ pratigrāhakāśrayānugrahaṇāt
# de la zang zing gi sbyin pa ni lus rton pa ste / / bza' ba dang btung ba la la sogs pa'i yo byad rnams kyis len pa'i lus la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
abhayadānaṃ cittopastambhaḥ daurmanasyaviśeṣāpagamāya cetasa āśvāsāya saṃhārāt
# mi 'jigs pa'i sbyin pa ni sems rton pa ste / / yid mi bde ba'i bye brag dang bral bar bya ba'i phyir sems kyi dbugs 'byin pa nye bar bsgrub pa'i phyir ro /
ityevamanyadapi yojyam / hīnacittaṃ punarbodhisattvasya saṃsāraduḥkhaparikheditayā śrāvakapratyekabuddhacittam tatparityāgopastambho duḥkhādhivāsanakṣāntirveditavyā
# gzhan la yang de bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o / / dman pa'i sems ni byang chub sems dpa' 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyis yongs su skyo bas nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sems te / / de yongs su 'dor ba rton pa ni sdug bsngal dang du len pa'i bzod par rig par bya'o /
kuśalamūlākṣayatā sarvasattveṣu kriyārthādhikāritayā yāvatsāraṃ nirupadhiśeṣe 'pi nirvāṇadhātāvaparityāgaḥ tadupastambhaḥ sattvārthakriyāyaṃ vīryaṃ veditavyam
# dge ba'i rtsa ba mi zad pa ni sems can thams cad kyi don du bya ba lhag par byed pas 'khor ba ji srid pa dang phung po lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su yongs su mi gtong ba ste / / de rton pa ni sems can gyi don bya ba'i brtson 'grus su rig par bya'o /
gaṇaparikarṣaṇaṃ karmaṃ adhigamaṃ niśritya vineyānāmasamāhitasya cittasya samādhānāya samāhitasya vā cittasya vimokṣāyāvavādānuśāsanopradānam tadupastambhaḥ sattvārthakriyāyai dhyānam
# tshogs sdud pa ni thob pa la brten nas 'dus pa rnams sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa mnyam par gzhag par bya ba dang sems mnyam par bzhag pa rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir gdams pa dang rjes su bstan pa rab tu sbyin pa ste / / de rton pa ni sems can gyi don bya ba'i bsam gtan no /
bhūmipraveśo yayā deśanayā dharmādhimuktipūrvikayāsaṃbhāraparipūryāpramuditāṃ bhūmiṃ praviśati tadupastambhaḥ saṃvṛtisatyālaṃbanā prajñā
# sa la 'jug pa ni chos la mos pa sngon du btang ba'i bshad pa gang gis tshogs yongs su rdzogs par byas nas / / rab tu dga' ba'i sa la 'jug pa ste / / de rton pa ni kun rdzob kyi bden pa la dmigs pa'o / / lhag ma ni legs par sbyor ba'i phyir sbyar bar ma byas so /
śeṣaṃ suyojyatvānna yojitam / punaḥ prabhedaḥ sapta dānāmi mūladānaṃ gotrāvasthasya bodhisattvasya dānapāramitā gotramātraṃ niśritya dānāt
# yang rab tu dbye ba ni sbyin pa bdun te / / rtsa ba'i sbyin pa ni rigs kyi gnas skabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ste / / rigs tsam la brten nas sbyin pa'i phyir ro /
ādhānadānaṃ cittotpādāvasthasya praṇidhānasamādānaṃ niśritya dānāt
# blangs pa'i sbyin pa ni sems bskyed pa'i gnas skabs pa'i ste / / smon lam yang dag par blangs pa la brten nas sbyin pa'i phyir ro /
anugrahadānaṃ svaparārthapratyavasthasya
# rjes su 'dzin pa'i sbyin pa ni bdag dang gzhan gyi don sgrub pa'i gnas skabs pa'o /
anavagrahadānaṃ tattvārthaparīkṣāvasthasya dāyakādivikalpābhiniveśāvagrāhābhāvāt / niṣparigrahadānaṃ prabhāvāvasthasya vinā vāhyenopakaraṇaparigraheṇa gaganagañjādisamādhibhirākāśe pāṇiṃ saṃcārya yatheṣṭaṃ ratnādivarṣaṇāt
# 'dzin pa ngan pa med pa'i sbyin pa ni de kho na'i don la yongs su rtogs pa'i gnas skabs pa ste / / sbyin bdag la sogs par rnam par rtog pa la mngon par zhen pa'i 'dzin pa ngan pa med pa'i phyir ro / / yongs su 'dzin pa med pa'i sbyin pa ni mthu'i gnas skabs pa ste / / phyi rol gyi yo byad yongs su 'dzin pa med par yang nam mkha' mdzod la sogs pa'i ting nge 'dzin rnams kyis nam mkha' la lag pa brkyang nas ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du rin po che la sogs pa'i char 'bebs pa'o /
pratyarhadānaṃ paripākāvasthasya yathāvineyānurūpaṃ dānāt / mahādānaṃ paramabodhyavasthasya niruttaratvāt / evaṃ yāvatprajñā yathāyogaṃ veditavyam
# so sor rig pa'i sbyin pa ni yongs su smin pa'i gnas skabs pa'i ste / / sbyin pa 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du mthun par sbyin pa'i phyir ro / / sbyin pa chen po ni byang chub mchog gi gnas skabs pa ste / / bla na med pa'i phyir ro / / de bzhin du shes rab kyi bar du ci rigs su sbyar bar rig par bya'o /
saṃgrahaḥ dānādabhirbodhisattvabhūmisaṃgrahārthena tatredamudāharaṇamātraṃ pāramitādibhiḥ / gotrasaṃgraho dānapāramitādigotraṃ liṅgato 'nugantavyam
# bsdus pa ni sbyin pa la sogs pas byang chub sems dpa'i sa bsdus pa'i phyir te / / de la pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyis rigs bsdus pa 'di ni dpe tsam mo / / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa la sogs pa ni rigs kyi rtags kyis bsdus par shes par bya'o /
cittotpādasaṃgraho viśiṣṭacittotpādasaṃgrahaṇāt / dvividho hi cittotpādaḥ aviśiṣṭo viśiṣṭaśca
# sems bskyed pas bsdus pa ni khyad par du 'phags pa'i sems bskyed pas bsdus pa'i phyir ro / / sems bskyed pa ni rnam pa gnyis te / / khyad par can ma yin pa dang khyad par du 'phags pa'o /
tatrāviśiṣṭo 'ho vatāhamanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyeyeti / viśiṣṭa evaṃ dānapāramitāṃ paripūrayeyaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitāmiti / tadanena viśiṣṭena cittotpādena pāramitānāṃ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ tāsāṃ kāraṇabhāvāt
# de la khyad par can ma yin pa ni kye ma'o bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar shog shig snyam pa'o / / khyad par du 'phags pa de ni de ltar sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par shog shig snyam pa nas / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du'o / / khyad par du 'phags pa'i sems bskyed pa 'dis ni pha rol tu phyin pa rnams bsdus par rig par bya ste / / de dag gi rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
svaparārthasaṃgraho yaddānenaiśvarya parigṛhaṇātyayaṃ svārthaḥ yatpunaḥ parānupakaraṇopasaṃhāreṇānugṛhṇātyayaṃ svārthaḥ evamavaśiṣṭābhiḥ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ / paramārthasaṃgrahaḥ dharmadhātumārabhya tathatāyā dānādisāmānyalakṣaṇatvāt
# bdag dang gzhan gyi don bsdus pa las gang sbyin pas phyug po yongs su 'dzin pa 'di ni bdag gi don to / / gang gzhan la yo byad nye bar sgrub pas rjes su 'dzin pa 'di ni gzhan gyi don to / / lhag ma rnams kyis bsdus pa yang de bzhin du rig par bya'o / / don dam pas bsdus pa chos kyi dbyings las brtsams pa ni de bzhin nyid sbyin pa la sogs pa spyi'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
jñānasaṃbhāramārabhya sarvajñatābhājanatāpādanāt
# ye shes kyi tshogs las brtsams pa ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi snod du sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
jñānaparigrahamārabhya sarvajñatāpariniṣpādanāt
# ye shes yongs su 'dzin pa las brtsams pa ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
jñānānuparivartatāmārabhya pañcānāṃ prajñāpāramitānuparivartanāt / jñānalakṣaṇamārabhya prajñāpāramitāḥ samyagjñānasvabhāvatvāt / ityevaṃ tathatāsamyajjñānasvabhāvataḥ paramārtho dānādibhiḥ saṃgṛhīto veditavyaḥ
# ye shes kyi rjes su 'jug pa las brtsams pa ni lnga po dag shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i rjes su mthun pa'i phyir ro / / ye shes kyi mtshan nyid las brtsams pa ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang dag pa'i ye shes kyi ngo bo nyid yin pa'i phyir te / / de ltar na de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i ye shes kyi ngo bo nyid don dam pa ni sbyin pa la sogs pas bsdus par rig par bya'o /
etenodāharaṇamātreṇa śeṣaḥ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ
# dpe brjod pa 'dis bsdus pa la lhag ma rnams brtag par bya'o /
vipakṣo dānādīnāṃ yathākramaṃ mātsaryadauḥśīlye krodhakauśīdye vikṣepadauḥprajñe
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs ni ser sna dang 'chal ba'i tshul khrims dang khro ba dang le lo dang rnam par g yeng ba dang 'chal ba'i shes rab ste sbyin pa la sogs pa dang go rims bzhin no /
api khalu yāvantaḥ kuśalā dharmāḥ pāramitābhiḥ saṃgṛhītāsteṣāṃ yo vipakṣo jñeyāvaraṇaṃ ca sa tāsāṃ vipakṣo veditavyaḥ / anuśaṃsaḥ pañcavidhaphalādhikāreṇāprameyo veditavyaḥ
# yang pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyis bsdus pa'i dge ba'i chos ji snyed pa de dag gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs gang yin pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa gang yin pa de yang de dag gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs su rig par bya'o /
tadyathā yathāsvamāsāṃ vipakṣaprahāṇaṃ visaṃyogaphalam / dṛṣṭe dharme svaparānugrahaṇaṃ puruṣakāraphalam / āyatyāmuttarāttaraviśiṣṭattaratamotpattirniṣyandaphalam / mahābodhiradhipatiphalam / mahābhogatā sugatigamanamavarābhedasukhasaumanasya bahulatā sattvādhipapatyamavyābādhyātmabhāvatā maheśākhyatā ca yathākramaṃ dānādīnāṃ vipākaphalaṃ veditavyam
# phan yon ni 'bras bu rnam pa lnga'i gnas skabs su dpag tu med par rig par bya'o / / 'di lta ste / / ji ltar 'di dag gi rang gi mi mthun pa'i phyogs spong ba bral ba'i 'bras bu dang mthong ba'i chos la bdag dang gzhan rjes su 'dzin pa skyes bu byed pa'i 'bras bu dang phyi ma la gong nas gong du khyad par du 'phags pa mchog dam pa 'byung ba rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu dang byang chub chen po dbang gi 'bras bu dang longs spyod chen po dang bde 'gror 'gro ba dang khon med pa dang dbye ba med pa dang bde ba dang yid bde ba mang ba dang sems la dbang ba dang lus la gnod pa med pa dang dbang che bar grags pa ni go rims bzhin du sbyin pa la sogs pa'i rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bur rig par bya'o /
anyonyaviniścayastrividhaḥ prāyogikaḥ prābhedikaḥ prabhidyasāṃdarśikaśca
# gcig la gcig rnam par nges pa ni rnam pa gsum ste / / sbyor ba las gyur pa dang rab tu dbye ba las gyur pa dang rab tu phye nas bstan pa las gyur ba'o /
tatra prāyogikaḥ dānaprayoge sarvāsāṃ vṛttirūpalabhyate
# de la sbyor ba las gyur pa ni sbyin pa la sbyor bar thams cad 'dus par dmigs te /
tadyathādhyātmikaṃ bāhyaṃ vastuparityajanataḥ dānaprayogaḥ
# 'di lta ste / / nang dang phyi'i dngos po yongs su gtong ba'i sbyin pa la sbyor ba'o /
tatra yaḥ parityāgaḥ sa dānapāramitā
# de la gang yongs su btang ba de ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o /
tatraiva yā maitracittasya paratravighātotpīḍāviheṭhasaṃvaraṇatā sā śīlapāramitā / tatraiva yoparodhavighātakhedamarṣaṇatā sā kṣāntipāramitā / tatraiva yā bhūyo bhūyaścittasyotsahanatā sā vīryapāramitā / tatraiva yā cittasyaikāgratā kuśalādbahiravisaraṇatā sā dhyānapāramitā
# de la byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i phyir gang gzhan la kun nas ma nar sems pa dang gnod pa dang rnam par 'tshe ba sdom pa de ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o / / de nyid la gang nye bar skor ba dang phongs pa dang skyo ba la ji mi snyam pa de ni bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o / / de nyid la gang phyir zhing sems spro ba de ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o / / de nyid la gang sems rtse gcig pa nyid de dge ba las sems phyi rol tu mi 'phro ba de ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o /
tatraiva yā yathāvaddhetu phalasugṛhītatā dṛṣṭyaparāmarṣaṇatā sā prajñāpāramitā
# de nyid la rgyu dang 'bras bu ji lta ba bzhin du legs par bzung ba dang lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa med pa de ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o /
evaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitāyāṃ yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyamubhayadānaṃ sarvajñajñānamiti kṛtvā
# de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar la yang ci rigs su sbyar bar bya ste / / mi 'jigs pa'i sbyin pa ni thams cad du yang sbyin pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra prābhedikaḥ svabhāvaprabhedena anukāraprabhedena ca / tatra dānādīnāṃ svabhāvo yathākramaṃ visargaḥ saṃvaro marṣaṇābhyutsāhaścitasthitiḥ pravicayaśca / tatra dānādiprayogeṣu tadanyapāramitānāmanuvṛttiḥ pūrvavat / tatra dānādīnāmupayogaḥ samādāpanā varṇavāditā sumanojñatā ca
# de yang rab tu dbye ba las gyur pa ni ngo bo nyid kyis rab dbye ba dang rjes su byed pas rab tu dbye ba dang rjes su sbyor bas rab tu dbye ba dang skyed pas rab tu dbye ba'o / / de la sbyin pa la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid ni rnam par gtong ba dang sdom pa dang ji mi snyam pa dang mngon par spro ba dang sems gnas pa dang rab tu rnam par 'byed pa ste / / go rims bzhin no / / de la sbyin pa la sogs pa'i rjes su byed pa ni sbyin pa la sogs pa la sbyor ba na / / de las gzhan pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa rnams rjes su 'jug ba ste snga ma bzhin no / / de la sbyin pa la sogs pa'i rjes su sbyor ba ni 'dzin du 'jug pa dang bsngags pa brjod pa dang rab tu dga' ba'o /
tatra dānādīnāṃ ropaṇā yā parasaṃtāne pratiṣṭhāpanā
# de la sbyin pa la sogs pa skyed pa ni gzhan gyi sems kyi rgyud la 'jog pa'o /
tadatra dānapāramitāmiṣadānam tadanyāḥ pañcābhayadānam sarvāḥ saddharmadānaṃ parasaṃtāne ropaṇāt
# de la sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa ni zang zing gi sbyin pa'o / / de ma yin pa gzhan lnga ni mi 'jigs pa'i sbyin pa'o / / thams cad ni dam pa'i chos kyi sbyin pa ste / / gzhan gyi sems kyi rgyud la skyes pa'i phyir ro /
tatra prabhidyasāṃdarśika ekāvacārakādibhiḥ / tadyathā yā dānapāramitā śīlapāramitāpi sā yā vā śīlapāramitā dānapāramitāpi sā paścātpādakaḥ yā yāvacchīlapāramitā dānapāramitāpi sā syāddānapāramitā na śīlapāramitā śīlapāramitayāsaṃgṛhītā yā dānapāramitā / evaṃ yāvatyajñāpāramitayāsaṃgṛhītā dānapāramitā paścātpādakairyojayitavyā
# de la rab tu phye nas bstan pa las gyur pa ni gcig nas rtogs pa la sogs pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa gang yin pa tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang de yin nam / / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang yin pa sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang de yin nam zhe na / / tshig 'og ma dang sbyar ba ste / / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang yin pa de sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'ang de'o / / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yin la / / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin pa yang yod de / / tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pas ma zin pa'i sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o / / de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar du sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa tshig 'og ma dang sbyor ba rnams dang sbyar bar bya'o /
yaddānaṃ sarvā sā pāramitā yā dānapāramitā sarvaṃ taddānamiti catuṣkoṭikam
# sbyin pa gang yin pa de thams cad sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yin nam; pha rol tu phyin pa gang yin pa de thams cad sbyin pa yin nam zhe na /
syāddānaṃ na pāramitā yanna mahobodhipariṇāmitam
# mu gsum du 'gyur te / / sbyin pa yin la pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin pa ni /
syāt pāramitā na dānaṃ śīlādayo mahābodhipariṇāmitāḥ
# gang byang chub chen por yongs su ma bsngos pa'i sbyin pa'o /
syāddānaṃ ca pāramitā ca bodhipariṇāmitāni dānādīni
# sbyin pa'ang yin la pha rol tu phyin pa'ang yin pa yod de; byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pa'i sbyin pa rnams so /
syānna dānaṃ na pāramitā uktavinirmuktā dharmāḥ / evaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitāmārabhya catuṣkoṭikaṃ pratyekaṃ yojayitavyam
# sbyin pa yang ma yin la pha rol tu phyin pa yang ma yin pa yod de / / sngar bshad pa ma gtogs pa'i chos rnams so / / de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar las brtsams te / / re re la yang mu gsum gsum du sbyar bar bya'o /
yo dānaṃ samācarati sarvo 'sau dānapāramitānvayaṃ puṇyaṃ prasavatīti catuṣkoṭikam
# sbyin pa la kun tu spyod pa gang yin pa de thams cad sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i rgyu las byung ba'i bsod nams skyed dam zhe na / / mu bzhir 'gyur te /
prathamā koṭiḥ mahābodhyapariṇāmitaṃ dānaṃ samācarati
# mu dang po ni byang chub chen por yongs su ma bsngos pa'i sbyin pa spyod pa'o /
dvitīyā koṭiḥ dānapāramitāṃ yāṃ samādāpanavarṇabhāṣaṇasumanojñatābhiḥ
# mu gnyis pa ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang bsngags pa brjod pa dang yid rab tu dga' ba'o /
tṛtīyā koṭiḥ mahābodhipariṇāmitena dānena
# mu gsum pa ni byang chub chen por yongs su bsngos pa'i sbyin pa'o /
caturthī koṭiḥ etānākārān sthāpayitvā
# mu bzhi pa ni rnam pa 'di dag ma gtogs pas so /
evaṃ yāvatprajñāpāramitāmārabhya pratyekaṃ catuṣkoṭikaṃ yojayitavyam / viśeṣato vaipulye audāryagāmbhīryadeśanā tatphalasya sarvajñatvasya paramodāragambhīratvātphalānurūpyeṇa hetunirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ
# de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i bar las brtsams te / / re re la yang mu bzhi bzhir sbyar bar bya'o / / shin tu rgyas pa la rgya che ba dang zab par yang bstan pa ni de'i 'bras bu thams cad mkhyen pa nyid mchog tu rgya che ba dang zab pa'i phyir 'bras bu dang mthun par rgyu bsten par blta'o /
ekatyānāṃ tadanadhimokṣe trāsaḥ bodhisattvagotravaikalyaṃ prakṛtyā hīnacittatayā gāmbhīryaudāryadeśanāṃ nādhimoktuṃ śaknuvanti / satyapi tadgotratve mahābodhimārabhya praṇidhānādīnāṃ kuśalamūlādīnāmanavaropaṇāt satyapi tadavaropaṇe mahāyānapratikṣepakasattvaparigṛhītatvāditi
# kha cig de la mi mos pa dang skrag pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i rigs dang mi ldan pa dang rang bzhin gyis sems dman pa'i phyir ro / / de'i rigs su gyur du zin kyang byang chub chen po las brtsams te / / smon lam la sogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba ma bskyed pa'i phyir ro / / dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed du zin kyang theg pa chen po spong ba'i sems can gyis yongs su zin pa'i phyir ro /
adhimucyamānānāmapyekatyānāmaniryāṇaṃ nītārtha sūtramananviṣya svayaṃ dṛṣṭiparāmarṣasthāyitayā yathārutamarthābhiniveśāta
# kha cig mos kyang nges par 'byung bar mi 'gyur ba ni nges pa'i don gyi mdo sde ma brtsal te / / bdag nyid lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa la gnas pa dang don la sgra ji bzhin du mngon par zhen pa'i phyir te /
tadyathā sarvadharmaniḥsvabhāvatāvacanāt sarvalakṣaṇena sarvabhāvāpavādinaḥ
# 'di lta ste / / chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pa'o zhes bya ba'i tshig gis mtshan nyid thams cad kyis dngos po thams cad la skur ba 'debs pa'o /
evamanye 'pi yathārutārthābhiniveśino mahāyāne na niryāntotiveditavyaṃ nānābhiprāyabhāṣitatvāt mahāyānasyeti
# de bzhin du gzhan la yang don la sgra ji bzhin du mngon par zhen pa ni theg pa chen po las nges par mi 'byung bar rig par bya ste / / theg pa chen po la ni dgongs pa sna tshogs kyis gsungs pa'i phyir ro /
idaṃ ca saṃdhāyoktaṃ bhagavatā mahādharmādarśe dharmaparyāye bodhisattvasya yathārutamayoniśo dharmān vicinvato 'ṣṭāviṃśatirasaddṛṣṭaya utpadyante
# 'di la dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi me long chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs las gsungs pa / / byang chub sems dpa' sgra ji bzhin du tshul bzhin ma yin par chos rnams rnam par 'byed pa la lta ba ngan pa nyi shu rtsa brgyad 'byung ste /
aṣṭāviṃśatirasaddṛṣṭayaḥ katamāḥ / nimittadṛṣṭiryāvadabhimānadṛṣṭiśca
# lta ba ngan pa nyi shu rtsa brgyad po dag gang zhe na / / mtshan mar lta ba nas mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyi bar du lta ba'o /
tatra nisvabhāvāḥ sarvadharmā anutpannā ityevamādikaṃ mahāyāne rutamupalabhya tadabhisaṃdhyakuśalāḥ yathārutamevāsyārthamadhimucyamānā abhāva evāyaṃ bhagavatā deśitaḥ sarvadharmāṇāmanutpāda evetyabhāvādinimittamabhiniviśante saiṣāṃ bhavati nimittadṛṣṭiḥ
# de la theg pa chen po la chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pa dang ma skyes pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i sgrar dmigs shing thos nas / / dgongs pa de la mi mkhas pa dag 'di'i don la sgra ji bzhin du mos nas 'di ni dngos po med pa nyid du bstan to zhes chos thams cad ma skyes pa nyid du med pa la sogs pa'i mtshan mar mngon par zhen pa ni de dag gi mtshan mar lta ba yin no /
ta evamabhāvādinimittamabhiniviśamānāstrīnsvabhāvānavadante parikalpitaṃ svabhāvaṃ paratantraṃ pariniṣpannaṃ ca / tatrāyaṃ parikalpitaḥ svabhāvo yadrūpamiti vā yāvannirvāṇāmiti vābhilāpaprajñaptimātrabhabhūto niḥśarīrārtho yadbālā rūpādilakṣaṇaṃ samāropattaḥ parikalpayanti
# de dag nyid med pa la sogs pa'i mtshan mar mngon par zhen nas kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid gsum la skur pa 'debs pa'o / / de la 'di ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid de gang gzugs zhes bya ba nas / / mya ngan las 'das pa zhes bya ba'i bar du brjod pas brtags pa tsam du zad nas yang dag pa ma yin pa lus med pa'i don gang la byis pa rnams kyis gzugs la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid du sgro btags nas yongs su rtog pa'o /
tatrāyaṃ paratantraḥ svabhāvā yattadevābhūtaparikalpamātram / tatrāyaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvo yatsarvadharmāṇāṃ tattvaṃ tathatā
# de la 'di ni gzhan gyi dbang gi ngo bo nyid de / / gang yang dag pa ma yin pa kun tu rtog pa tsam de nyid do / / de la 'di ni yongs su grub pa'i ngo bo nyid de / / gang zhe na / / chos thams cad kyi de kho na de bzhin nyid do /
tadapavādākārāstisro dṛṣṭayo bhavanti prajñaptyapavādadṛṣṭiḥ parikalpāpavādadṛṣṭistattvāpavādadṛṣṭiśca
# de la skur pa 'debs pa'i rnam pa 'dis lta ba gsum du 'gyur te / / btags pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba dang kun du rtog pa la skur ba 'debs pa'i lta ba dang de kho na la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba'o /
ta evaṃ sarvathā sarvadharmānapavadamānāstasyā apavādadṛṣṭeḥ pratiṣṭhāpanārthaṃ kāṃcideva yuktiṃ parigṛhṇanti ye 'pi nītārthāḥ sūtrāntā nirabhilāpadharmatādyotakāstānapi sarvān svadṛṣṭayānulomyena pariṇāmayanti
# de ltar de dag rnam pa thams cad du chos thams cad la skur pa 'debs pas na / / skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba de gzhag pa'i phyir rigs pa 'ga' zhig yongs su 'dzin pa dang nges pa'i don gyi mdo sde gang dag brjod du med pa'i chos nyid ston pa de dag thams cad kyang rang gi lta ba dang mthun par yongs su grub pa de dag ni lta ba gnyis su 'gyur te /
te eva dve dṛṣṭo bhavataḥ parigrahadṛṣṭiḥ pariṇatidṛṣṭiśca / te punarevaṃdṛṣṭayo bhavanti ya etāmīdṛśīṃ dṛṣṭiṃ niśritya kuśalamakuśalaṃ vā samācarati sa niravadya eva bhavati nirdoṣaḥ sarvamevāsya tatkalyāṇatāṃ yāti pūrvopacitāccāvaraṇātsa niḥsaratotyevameṣāṃ dve dṛṣṭī anavadyatādṛṣṭirniḥsaraṇadṛṣṭiśca
# yongs su 'dzin pa'i lta ba dang sgyur ba'i lta ba'o / / de dag yang lta ba 'di 'dra bar 'gyur te / / lta ba 'di lta bu la brten nas dge ba'am mi dge ba yang rung spyad na kha na ma tho ba med pa dang skyon med par 'gyur zhing de thams cad dge bar 'gyur ba dang sngon bsags pa'i sgrib pa las de 'byung bar 'gyur bar 'dzin pa de lta bu de dag gi lta ba gnyis te / / kha na ma tho ba med par lta ba dang nges par 'byung bar lta ba'o /
te caivaṃ svadṛṣṭāvabhiniviṣṭāstad dṛṣṭiviparyayeṇa skandhādidharmavyavasthāpakaṃ śrāvakapiṭakamavajānanti ye ca tāmapavādadṛṣṭimanadhimuktāḥ śrāvakayānīyāstān pradviṣanti / te ete dve dṛṣṭī bhavato 'vajñādṛṣṭiḥ prakopadṛṣṭiśca / svadṛṣṭyanusāreṇa caite yathāvacchūnyatānimittāpraṇihitāni vyavasthāpayamānā atallakṣaṇe tallakṣaṇasaṃjñino viparītameṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vyavasthāpayanti evaṃcittāśca bhavanti yasyāmīdṛśyāṃ dharmatāyāmavatarantyavatārayanti vā sarve te 'prameyaṃ puṇyaṃ prasavantītyevamete dṛṣṭī viparītadṛṣṭiḥ prasavadṛṣṭiśca
# de dag lta ba de lta bu la mngon par zhen pas lta ba de las bzlog pa'i phung po la sogs pa'i chos rnam par 'jog pa nyan thos kyi sde snod khyad du gsod pa dang gang dag skur ba 'debs par lta ba de la mi mos pa nyan thos kyi theg pa pa de dag la rab tu sdang ba'i lta ba 'di gnyis te / / dbang za ba'i lta ba dang rab tu 'khrug pa'i lta ba'o / / rang gi lta ba'i tshul du na stong pa nyid dang mtshan ma med pa dang smon pa med pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par gzhag pa yin no snyam nas / / de'i mtshan nyid ma yin pa la de'i mtshan nyid du 'du shes pa ni de dag gi mtshan nyid phyin ci log tu rnam par 'jog cing 'di snyam du yang sems te / / gang dag chos nyid 'di lta bu la 'jug pa dang 'dzud pa de dag thams cad bsod nams kyi phung po dpag tu med pa skyed do snyam pa la de lta bu'i lta ba 'di gnyis te /
yadā punaste tāṃ dṛṣṭimārabhya paraṃranuyujyante tadā na kiṃcitsvayamicchantyabhyupagantum chalajātibhyāṃ ca parānanuyuñjante / te ete anabhyupagamadṛṣṭiḥ kusṛtidṛṣṭiśca
# phyin ci log tu lta ba dang 'phel ba'i lta ba'o / / gang gi tshe de dag lta ba de las brtsams te gzhan dag gis dris pa de'i tshe bdag ni ci yang khas len par mi 'dod kyi / / tshig dor dang ltag chod kyis gzhan la 'dri ba'i lta ba 'di gnyis te / / khas mi len pa'i lta ba dang ngan g yo'i lta ba'o /
te caivamabhimānino bhavanti ya evaṃ pratipadyante te samyagbuddhān bhagavataḥ pūjayanti satkurvantītyeṣāṃ satkāradṛṣṭiḥ
# de dag yang 'di lta bu'i nga rgyal can du 'gyur ro / / gang dag de ltar sgrub pa de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la mchod pa byed pa dang rim gro byed par 'dzin pa de dag gi lta ba ni bkur sti'i lta ba'o /
aviparītadharmatākuśalaiśca tatā dṛṣṭervivecyamānāḥ sūpapannayā prasiddhayā yuktayā pratyāyamānā api tāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ na kathaṃcit parityajanti etadeva tathyaṃ mithyānyadityeṣā dṛḍhamūḍhatādṛṣṭiḥ
# phyin ci log ma yin pa'i chos nyid la mkhas pa dag gis lta ba de dang 'byed cing legs par 'thad pa dang rab tu grags pa'i rigs pas yid ches par byed pa na yang lta ba de ji ltar yang yongs su mi 'dor te 'di nyid bden gyi gzhan ni log pa'o snyam pa de dag ni rmongs pa brtan pa'i lta ba'o /
etāsāṃ ca yathānirdiṣṭānāṃ dṛṣṭīnāṃ yadvāsanādauṣṭhulyaṃ sā mūladṛṣṭiḥ
# lta ba ji skad du bstan pa de dag gi bag chags kyi gnas ngan len gang yin pa de ni rtsa ba'i lta ba'o /
eta eva ca saptadaśadṛṣṭayo doṣodbhāvanāmukhenāvaśiṣṭābhiḥ dṛṣṭibhiḥ punarnidiśyante
# lta ba bcu bdun po de dag nyid kyi skyon brjod pa'i sgo nas yang bshad par bya ste / / 'di lta ste /
tadyathā dṛṣṭāvadṛṣṭadṛṣṭi nimittadṛṣṭirityucyate abhāvādinimittābhiniveśina eva sataḥ sarvanimittānabhiniveśasajñitvāt
# mtshan mar lta ba ni lta ba la lta ba ma yin par lta ba zhes bya ste / / med pa la sogs pa'i mtshan ma la mngon par zhen pa nyid du gyur kyang /
prajñaptyapavādadṛṣṭiḥ parikalpāpavādadṛṣṭistattvāpavādadṛṣṭiśca prayoganirākaraṇadṛṣṭiḥ sarvāpavādino vyāyāmaniḥ sāmarthyasaṃjñitvāt / parigrahadṛṣṭiḥ pariṇatidṛṣṭiścānairyāṇikadṛṣṭiḥ anupāyaprayuktasya tatphalānavāpteḥ / anavadyatādṛṣṭiniḥsaraṇadṛṣṭiścāvaraṇopacayadṛṣṭiḥ mithyāpratipadyamānasyāvaraṇakṣayāsaṃbhavāt / avajñādṛṣṭiḥ prakopadṛṣṭiścāpuṇyaprasavadṛṣṭiḥ saddharmasabrahmacārivipratipattimukhena mahākṣatisamāsādanāt / viparītadṛṣṭiḥ prasavadṛṣṭiśca vaiphalyadṛṣṭiḥ asamyagdharmatāvyavasthāpanagrahaṇagrāhaṇairviśeṣā nadhigamāt anabhyupagamadṛṣṭiḥ kusṛtidṛṣṭiśca nigrāhyadṛṣṭiḥ anyāyena vādaṃ kurvato jayāsaṃbhavāt
# mtshan ma thams cad la mngon par zhen pa med do snyam pa'i 'du shes can du gyur pa'i phyir ro / / brtags pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba dang kun du rtog pa la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba dang de kho na la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba ni sbyor ba sel ba'i lta ba ste / / thams cad la skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba ni 'bad pa mthu med pa'i 'du shes can du 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / yongs su 'dzin pa'i lta ba dang sgyur ba'i lta ba ni nges par 'byin pa ma yin pa'i lta ba ste / / thabs ma yin pa la sbyor ba ni de'i 'bras bu mi 'thob pa'i phyir ro / / kha na ma tho ba med par lta ba dang nges par 'byung ba'i lta ba ni sgrib pa sogs pa'i lta ba ste / / log par sgrub pa'i sgrub pa zad mi srid pa'i phyir ro / / dbang za ba'i lta ba dang rab tu 'khrug pa'i lta ba ni bsod nams ma yin pa 'phel ba'i lta ba ste / / dam pa'i chos dang tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa la log par sgrub pa'i sgo nas smas pa chen po 'thob pa'i phyir ro / / phyin ci log tu lta ba dang 'phel ba'i lta ba ni 'bras bu med pa'i lta ba ste / / yang dag pa ma yin pa'i chos nyid rnam par 'jog pa 'dzin pa dang 'dzin du 'jug pa la khyad par mi 'thob pa'i phyir ro / / khas mi len pa'i lta ba dang ngan g yo'i lta ba ni chad pas bcad pa'i lta ba ste / / rigs pa ma yin pas rgol na rgyal mi srid pa'i phyir ro /
satkāradṛṣṭirabhyākhyānadṛṣṭiḥ atadākhyāyini tatsamārāpaṇāt
# bkur sti'i lta ba ni skur pa 'debs pa'i lta ba ste / / de mi gsung ba la de sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
dṛḍhamūḍhatādṛṣṭirakathyadṛṣṭiḥ mithyābhiniveśinā saha sāṃ kathyapratiṣedhānnirathakatāmupādāya
# rmongs pa brtan pa'i lta ba ni bsnyad pa ma yin pa'i lta ba ste / / log pa la mngon par zhen pa dang 'bel ba'i gtam bya ba bkag pa'i phyir te / / don med pa'i phyir ro /
mūladṛṣṭirmahādṛṣṭiḥ tata āyatyāṃ puṣṭatarasarvadṛṣṭigatapratāpanāt
# rtsa ba'i lta ba ni lta ba chen po ste / / de las phyi ma la lta bar gyur pa thams cad shin tu brtas pa rgyas par 'gyur pa'i phyir ro /
sarvā etāḥ saptaviṃśatidṛṣṭayo 'bhimānadṛṣṭiḥ abhūtābhimānasamutthitatvāt
# lta ba nyi shu rtsa bdun po thams cad ni mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyi lta ba ste /
ata evānantaraṃ tatraiva sūtra uktamitīmāḥ saptadaśa samānāḥ daśa bhavanti daśa samānāḥ saptadaśa bhavanti saptaviṃśatiḥ samānā ekā bhavati ekā samānā saptaviṃśatirbhavantīti
# yang dag pa ma yin pa'i mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyis slong ba'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir mdo sde de nyid las de'i 'og tu 'di dag gi bcu bdun yin yang bcur 'gyur ro / / bcu yin yang bcu bdun du 'gyur ro / / nyi shu rtsa bdun yin yang gcig tu 'gyur ro / / gcig yin yang nyi shu rtsa bdun du 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so / / bam po brgyad pa /
niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarvadharmāḥ yasmātsvayameṣāṃ bhāvo nāsti pratyayāṃstvapekṣya bhāvo na pratiṣidhyate
# chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pa ste / / 'di ltar 'di dag ni bdag nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyi / / rkyen la ltos nas 'byung ba bkag pa ni ma yin no /
yena vā svabhāvenaite pūrvamabhūvanna tena svena bhāvena bhūyaḥ śakyamebhirbhavitumiti niḥsvabhāvāḥ
# ngo bo nyid gang du de dag sngar byung ba'i ngo bo nyid der yang de dag gis bskyed mi nus pas ngo bo nyid med pa'o /
prāptābhraṣṭalakṣaṇānāmapi pratyutpannānāṃ sve bhāve 'vasthānābhāvānniḥsvabhāvāḥ
# thob la ma nyams pa dang da ltar byung ba rnams kyang rang gi ngo bo la mi gnas pas ngo bo nyid med pa'o /
yādṛśo vādṛṣṭasatyairdharmāṇāṃ svabhāvo lakṣaṇamabhilāpaprapañcavāsanāmukhena gṛhyate tena bālagrāhānurūpeṇa svabhāvena virahitatvānniḥ svabhāvāḥ
# bden pa ma mthong ba rnams kyis chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid de mtshan nyid mngon par brjod pa spros pa'i bag chags kyi sgo nas ji ltar bzung ba bzhin du byis pas bzung ba dang mthun pa'i ngo bo nyid de dang bral ba'i phyir ngo bo nyid med pa'o /
api khalu sarvadharmā ucyante trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ
# yang chos thams cad ces bya ba ni ngo bo nyid gsum ste /
tatra parikalpitasya svalakṣaṇameva nāstyataḥ svalakṣaṇaniḥsvabhāvatayā niḥsvabhāvaḥ
# de la kun brtags kyi ngo bo nyid ni rang gi mtshan nyid kyis med pa ste / / de'i phyir rang gi mtshan nyid ngo bo nyid med pas ngo bo nyid med pa'o /
paratantrasya svayamutpattirnāsti pratyayāpekṣaṇādato nāsya svena bhāvena bhāva ityutpattiniḥ svabhāvatayā niḥsvabhāvaḥ / pariniṣpanno viśuddhyālaṃbanatvāt paratantraparikalpitalakṣaṇābhāvasvabhāvatvācca paramārthaścaiṣa niḥsvabhāvatāprabhāvitaśceti paramārthaniḥsvabhāvatayā niḥsvabhāvaḥ
# gzhan gyi dbang ni rkyen la ltos pa'i phyir bdag nyid kyis 'byung ba med pa ste / / de'i phyir rang gis 'byung ba med pas na skye ba ngo bo nyid med pas ngo bo nyid med pa'o / / yongs su grub pa ni rnam par dag pa'i dmigs pa yin pa dang gzhan gyi dbang dang kun rtags pa'i mtshan nyid med pa'i ngo bo nyid yin pa'i phyir te / / don dam pa yin la ngo bo nyid med pas rab tu phe ba ste / / don dam pa ngo bo nyid med pas ngo bo nyid med pa'o /
ityevaṃ ca kṛtvā niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarvadharmā draṣṭavyāḥ na tu sarvathālakṣaṇābhāvamadhikṛtyeti
# de ltar chos thams cad la ngo bo nyid med par lta'i / / rnam pa thams cad du mtshan nyid med pa'i dbang du byas pa ni ma yin no /
api khalu mahāyāne tathāgatasya sarve 'bhiprāyāḥ saṃkṣepeṇa catvāro bhavanti
# yang theg pa chen po la de bzhin gshegs pa'i dgongs pa thams cad ni mdor na bzhir 'gyur te / / 'di lta ste /
tadyathā samatābhiprāyo yadāha ahameva tasmin samaye vipaśyī samyaksaṃbuddho 'bhūvamiti avaśiṣṭadharmakāyatvāt
# mnyam pa nyid la dgongs pa ni nga nyid de'i tshe yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par gzigs su gyur to zhes gang gsungs pa ste / / chos kyi sku la bye brag med pa'i phyir ro /
kālāntarābhiprāyoyadāha ye sukhāvatyāṃ lokadhātau praṇidhānaṃ kariṣyanti te tatropa patsyanta iti vimalacandraprabhavasya ca nāmadheyagrahaṇamātreṇa niyato bhavatyanuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāviti kālāntareṇetyabhiprāyaḥ
# dus gzhan la dgongs pa ni gang dag bde ba can gyi 'jig rten gyi khams su smon lam 'debs pa ste / / de dag der skye bar 'gyur zhes bya ba dang de bzhin gshegs pa dri med zla 'od kyi mtshan bzung ba tsam gyis nges par bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'thob bo zhes gang gsungs pa ste / / dus gzhan na'o zhes dgongs pa'o /
arthāntarābhiprāyo yadāha niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarvadharmā anutpannā ityevamādi ayathārutārthatvāt
# don gzhan la dgongs pa ni chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pa'o / / ma skyes pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa gang gsungs pa ste /
pudgalāśayābhiprāyo yattadeva kuśalamūlaṃ kasyacitpraśaṃsanti kasyacidvigarha te 'lpamātrasaṃtuṣṭasya
# sgra ji bzhin ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / gang zag gi bsam pa la dgongs pa ni gang la la nas bsngags pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de nyid cung zad tsam gyis chog par 'dzin pa la la la smod do /
tathā rāgacaritasya buddhakṣetravibhūti darśayati mānacaritasya keṣāṃcideva buddhānāmadhikāṃ saṃpattiṃ varṇayanti
# de bzhin du 'dod chags pa spyod pa la ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rnam par 'byor ba bsngags so / / nga rgyal la spyod pa ni sangs rgyas kha cig gis phun sum tshogs pa lhag par bsngags so /
kaukṛtyenāvṛtasya ye buddhabodhisattveṣvapakāramapi kariṣyanti te sarve svargopagā bhaviṣyantītyāha / aniyatagotrasya mahāśrāvakān buddhatve vyākaroti ekaṃ ca yānaṃ na dvitīyamastīti deśayati śrāvakatvāśayatyājanārtham
# 'gyod pas bsgribs pa la ni gang dag sngas rgyas dang byang chu ba sems dpa' rnams la gnod par byed pa de dag thams cad kyang mtho ris su nye bar 'gro bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so / / ma nges pa'i rigs can la ni nyan thos nyid kyi bsam pa dor ba'i phyir nyan thos chen po rnams sangs rgyas nyid du lung ston cing theg pa ni gcig ste gnyis su med do zhes ston to /
punaḥ sarve 'bhisaṃghayo 'bhisamasya catvāro bhavantya vatāraṇābhisaṃdhyādayaḥ
# yang ldem por dgongs pa thams cad ni mdor na gzhug pa la ldem por dgongs pa la sogs pa bzhir 'gyur ro /
tatra avatāraṇābhisaṃdhiḥ śrāvakeṣu draṣṭavyaḥ śāsanā vatāraṇārthamanutrāsāya rūpādyastitvadeśanāt
# de la gzhug pa la ldem por dgongs pa ni nyan thos rnams la blta bar bya ste / / bstan pa la gzhug pa'i don du mi skag par bya ba'i phyir gzugs la sogs pa yod pa skad du bstan pa'i phyir ro /
lakṣaṇābhisaṃdhistriṣu parikalpitādisvabhāveṣu draṣṭavyaḥ niḥsvabhāvānutpannādisarvadharmadeśanāt
# mtshan nyid la ldem por dgongs pa ni kun brtags la sogs pa ngo bo nyid gsum la blta ste / / chos thams cad ngo bo nyid med pa dang ma skyes pa la sogs pa bstan pa'i phyir ro /
pratipakṣābhisaṃdhiḥ doṣāṇāṃ vinaye draṣṭavyo yathāṣṭāvaraṇapratipakṣatāgrayānasaṃbhāṣā
# gnyen po la ldem por dgongs pa ni nyes pa rnams 'dul bar blta ste / / dper na sgrib pa brgyad kyi gnyen por theg pa mchog yang dag par bshad pa lta bu'o /
aṣṭāvaraṇāni buddhadharmāvajñeti vistaraḥ
# sgrib pa brgyad ni / / sangs rgyas dang ni chos la brnyas pa dang /
tadudāharaṇāni ca yathāyogaṃ caturabhiprāryānirdeśāni draṣṭavyāni
# zhes rgya cher 'byung ba ste / / de'i dper brjod pa ni ci rigs su dgongs pa gzhi bstan par blta'o /
pariṇāmanābhisaṃdhirabhidhānagāmbhīrye draṣṭavyaḥ yadāha
# bsgyur ba la ldem por dgongs pa ni brjod pa zab pa la blta bar bya ste /
asāre sāramatayo viparyāse ca susthitāḥ
# ji skad du snyong po med la snying por shes / / phyin ci log la shin tu gnas /
kleśena ca susaṃkliṣṭā labhante bodhimuttamām / iti / atrāyamabhisaṃdhiḥ avikṣepe yeṣāṃ sārabuddhiḥ pradhānabuddhiḥ vikṣepo hi visāraścetasaḥ viparyāse ca susthitāḥ iti nityasukhaśucyātmaviparyayeṇānityādike viparyāse ca susthitā aparihāṇitaḥ kleśena ca susaṃkliṣṭāḥ iti dīrghaduṣkara vyāyāmaśrameṇātyartha parikliṣṭāḥ / vaipulye dharmasamādhikuśalabodhisattvanirdeśaḥ śamathānuśaṃsaṃ vipaśyanānuśaṃsaṃ tadubhayānuśaṃsaṃ cādhikṛtya veditavyaḥ
# nyon mongs kun nas rab nyin mongs / / byang chub dam pa thob par 'gyur / / zhes bya ba 'di la ldem por dgongs pa ni 'di yin te / / rnam par mi g yeng ba la gang dag snying por blo 'byung ba dang mchog tu blo 'byung ba'o / / rnam par g yeng ba ni sems rnam par 'phro ba'o / / phyin ci log la shin tu gnas zhes bya ba ni / / rtag pa dang; bde ba dang gtsang ba dang bdag las bzlog pa ste / / mi rtag pa la sogs pa'i phyin ci log la shin tu gnas pa yongs su mi nyams pa'i phyir ro / / nyon mongs kun nas rab nyon mongs / / zhes bya ba ni yun ring por dka' ba byed pa'i rtsol bas shin tu yongs su nyon mongs par gyur pa'o / / shin tu rgyas pa la byang chub sems dpa' chos la ting nge 'dzin du mkhas par bstan pa ni zhi gnas kyi phan yon dang lhag mthong gi phan yon dang de gnyi ga'i phan yon gyi dbang du byas par rig par bya'o /
tatra śamathānuśaṃso dvividhaḥ
# de la zhi gnas kyi phan yon ni rnam pa gnyis te /
kṣaṇe kṣaṇe prakarṣagāminyā prasrabdhyā nirantaramāśrayaspharaṇāt pratikṣaṇaṃ sarvadauṣṭhulyāśraya drāvaṇam aviśeṣeṇa sarvadeśanādharme karasatādhimokṣasamādhānādvividhaskandhādyarthākārasaṃjñāvigatāyāḥ sūtrādidharmārāmarateḥ pratilambhaśca / vipaśyanānuśaṃso 'pi dvividhaḥ
# skad cig skad cig la khyad par du 'gro ba'i shin tu sbyangs pas rgyun mi 'chad par lus la khyab pa'i phyir skad cig re re la gnas ngan len gyi gnas thams cad 'jig par byed pa dang bstan pa'i chos thams cad khyad par med pas so gcig par mos te / / mnyam par 'jog pas phung po la sogs pa'i don gyi rnam pa tha dad pa'i 'du shes dang bral bas mdo la sogs pa'i chos kyi dga' ba las dga' ba thob pa'o / / lhag mthong gi phan yon yang rnam pa gnyis te /
yathāpravicittadharmanirantarāsaṃpramoṣātpratismṛtimātramukhenāparicchinnākāro 'pramāṇaḥ sūtrādidharmeṣu prajñāvabhāsaḥ āśrayaparivṛttipūrvarūpabhūtānāṃ cāvikalpitānāmanabhisaṃskṛtānāṃ nimittānāṃ samudācāraśca / tadubhayānuśaṃso dharmakāyasya jñeyāvaraṇa prahāṇāśrayaparivṛttisaṃgṛhītasya paripūraye daśamyāṃ bhūmau pariniṣpattaye vā tāthāgatyāṃ bhūmāvuttarāduttaratara niṣyandavāsanādhānayogena hetuparigraha iti / tadetatpañcavidhāyā bhāvanāyāḥ phalaṃ pañcavidhaṃ nirvartata iti saṃdarśitam
# ji ltar rab tu rnam par phyir ba'i chos rgyun mi 'chad par mi brjed pas so sor dran pa tsam gyi sgo nas mdo la sogs pa'i chos rnams la shes rab kyi snang ba'i rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa tshad med pa dang gnas 'gyur ba'i snga rtags su gyur pa rnam par mi rtog pa mngan par 'dus ma byas pa'i mtshan ma rnams kun du 'byung ba'o / / de gnyi ga'i phan yon ni chos kyi sku shes bya'i sgrub pa spangs pa gnas gyur pas bsdus pas sa bcu pa la yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang; de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la yongs su bsgrub pa'i phyir gong ma bas kyang ches gong ma'i rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags bskyed pa'i tshul gyis rgyu yongs su 'dzin par byed pa'o /
pañcavidhā bhāvanā katamā / prasrabdhinimittabhāvanāsaṃbhinnabhāvanānimittabhāvanānābhogabhāvanā parinirvṛtinimittabhāvanā ca
# chos kyi sku'i rgyu mthun par 'dra ba la ci'i phyir shin tu rgyas pa'i chos la bdug pa dang phye ma la sogs pas mchod par 'os kyi /
kena kāraṇena tulye dharmakāyaniṣyandatve vaipulyadharmo dhūpamālyādibhiḥ pūjyo na tathā śrāvakayānadharmaḥ
# nyan thos kyi theg pa'i chos la ni de lta ma yin zhe na / / shin tu rgyas pa'i chos ni sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde ba'i gzhir gyur pa'i phyir te /
vaipulyadharmasya sarvasattvahitasukhādhiṣṭhānatāmupādāya mahārthatayā niruttarāprameyapuṇyaprasavāyatanatvāt / prāptiviniścayo nāma caturthaḥ samuccayaḥ / prāptiviniścayo 'dhigantṛpudgalavyavasthānato 'dhigamavyavasthānataśca draṣṭavyaḥ / asatyapi pudgaladravye pudgalavyavasthānaṃ caturbhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ
# don che bas bsod nams bla na med cing dpag tu med pa skyed pa'i gnas su gyur pa'i phyir ro / / thob pa rnam par nges pa ni thob par byed pa'i gang zag rnam par gzhag pa dang mngon par rtogs par rnam par gzhag par lta ba'o / / gang zag rdzas su med kyang rnam pa bzhis gang zag rnam par gzhag ste / / 'di lta ste /
tadyathā sukhasaṃvyavahārārtham rūpādīnāṃ bahūnāṃ bahudhābhinnalakṣaṇasaṃjñānāmekayā sāmudāyikyā sattvaprajñaptyākṛcchreṇa ehi yāhi ityevamādisaṃvyavaharaṇāt
# sla bar tha snyad gdags pa'i phyir ni gzugs la sogs pa rnam par mang po mtshan nyid dang ming tha dad pa mang po rnams gcig tu bsdus te / / sems can zhes brtags nas so zhes bya ba la sogs pa tshegs med pa nyid du tha snyad 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
lokānuvṛttyartham na hi loke dharmamātrasaṃjñābhiḥ sarvaḥ saṃvyavahāro nirūḍhaḥ kiṃtarhi prāyeṇa sattvasaṃjñayā
# 'jig rten pa dang mthun par bya ba'i phyir ni 'jig rten na chos tsam gyi ming rnams kyi tha snyad thams cad ma grags kyi phal cher sems can gyi ming gis so /
tasmāllokena saha saṃvyavaharadbhirāryairavaśyaṃ so 'nuvartitavya iti
# de bas na 'phags pa rnams kyis kyang gdon mi za bar 'jig rten dang mthun pa'i tha snyad rnams kyis de dang mthun par bya'o /
anutrāsārtham pratītyasamutpādadharmatāyāma kovidāḥ sahasāditaḥ sarvathā sattvābhāvaṃ śrutvottrasyeyuriti
# ji skrag par bya ba'i phyir ni rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i chos nyid la mi mkhas pa glo bur du thog mar rnam pa thams cad du sems can med pa thos pa na skrag par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
ātmanaḥ pareṣāṃ ca doṣavattvaguṇavattvodbhāvanārthaṃ ca itarathā hi sattvaprajñaptimantareṇa saṃkleśavyavadānalakṣaṇamātradeśanāyāṃ satyāmamuṣmin saṃtāne 'mī doṣāḥ prahīṇā amī vā guṇā utpannā iti na śakyate vijñātumiti
# bdag dang gzhan dag gi nyes pa dang ldan pa dang yon tan dang ldan pa brjod pa'i phyir na gzhan du sems can du btags pa med par kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid tsam bstan na che ge mo zhig gi sems kyi rgyud la nyes pa 'di rnams spangs so / / yon tan 'di rnams skyes so zhes shes par mi nus pa'i phyir ro /
pudgalavyavasthānaṃ punaścaritādiprabhedena saptavidham
# gang zag rnam par gzhag pa ni spyod pa la sogs pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa bdun te / / de la 'dod chags la spyod pa ni /
tatra rāgādicaritastīvrāyatarāgaḥ hīne 'pi rañjanīye vastunyadhimātrarāgotpādādutpannasya ca ciramanubandhāt
# 'dod chags kyi shas che zhing rgyun ring ba ste / / chags par 'gyur ba'i dngos po ngan pa la yang 'dod chags cher 'byung ba dang byung nas kyang yun ring du rjes su 'brel pa'i phyir ro /
ityevaṃ yāvadvitarkacarito yathāsvaṃ vastuni yojayitavyaḥ / samabhāgacaritaḥprakṛtisthaḥ saṃkleśaḥ autkaṭayamāndyavivarjitasamāvasthe kleśa ityarthaḥ yathāvastvanurūpaṃ kleśasamudācārāt / mandarajaskaḥ prakṛtisthaḥ tanutarakleśaḥ prakṛtisthebhya uktalakṣaṇebhyastanutarāḥ kleśā asya so 'yaṃ prakṛtisthaḥ utkaṭe 'pi vastuni pūrvapratipakṣābhyāsavaśena prakṛtyā mṛdukleśasamudācārāditi / śrāvakayāniko gotrendriyapraṇidhānāśayālaṃbanapratipattiphalaprabhedairnidiṣṭo veditavyaḥ
# rnam par rtog pa la spyod pa'i bar du yang de bzhin te / / rang gi dngos po ji lta ba bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o / / cha mnyam pa la spyod pa ni / / nyon mongs pa rang bzhin du gnas pa ste / / nyon mongs pa shas che ba dang shas chung ba rnam par spangs nas mnyam pa'i gnas skabs zhes bya ba'i tha tshig ste / / dngos po ji lta ba dang mthun par nyon mongs pa kun du 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / nyon mongs pa chung du ni nyon mongs pa shin tu srab pa'i rang bzhin du gnas pa ste; nyon mongs pa rang bzhin du gnas pa'i mtshan nyid bstan pa dag nas / / nyon mongs pa ches srab pa yod pa de ni nyon mongs pa'i rang bzhin du gnas pas srab pa ste / / sngon gnyen po chen po goms par bya ba'i dbang gis dngos po shas che ba la yang rang bzhin gyis nyon mongs pa chung dus kun du 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / nyan thos rnams kyi theg pa ni rigs dang dbang po dang smon lam dang bsam pa dang dmigs pa dang sgrub pa dang 'bras bu'i rab tu dbye ba'i dbang gis bstan par rig par bya'o /
prakṛtyā mṛdvindriyatvaṃ punarasya pratyekabuddhabodhisattvendriyā pekṣayā itarathā hi dharmānusāryādayastīkṣṇendriyā ityetadvirudhyeta / tatrānutpāditapūrvanirvedhabhāgīyo 'prāptapūrvakaphalaśca khaḍgaviṣāṇakalpo bhavatyeka vihārī tadanyaḥ pratyekajino vargacārī draṣṭavyaḥ
# 'di'i dbang po rtul po nyid ni rang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i dbang po las ltos pa'o / / gzhan du ni chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba la sogs pa dbang po rnon po yin no zhes bya ba dang 'gal bar 'gyur ro / / de la nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa sngon ma bskyed pa dang sngon 'bras bu ma thob pa ni bse ru lta bur gyur te gcig pur gnas pa'o /
vyākaraṇaṃ ca pratyalabhata ityaṣṭābhyāṃ bhūmāvanutpattikeṣu dharmeṣu kṣāntiṃ pratilabhata ityarthaḥ
# de las gzhan pa'i rang rgyal ba ni tshogs dang spyod pa'o / / lung bstan pa yang thob ces bya ba ni sa brgyad pa la mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
asaṃbhṛtasaṃbhārādayo mokṣabhāgīyānāṃ ca mṛdumadhyādhi mātratayā nirvedhabhāgīyotpādanaṃ satyābhisamayaṃ ca pratiniyatāniyatatajjanmakālikatvādyathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ / tatra satyādhipateye dharme 'dhimuktiprasādalakṣaṇāni mokṣabhāgīyāni tatraiva dharmanidhyānakṣāntilakṣaṇāni nirvedhabhāgīyāni śraddhāpradhānatvātprajñāpradhānatvācca yathākramam
# tshogs ma bsags pa la sogs pa ni thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams dang nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen po rnams kyi nges par 'byed pa'i phyogs dang bden pa mngon par rtogs pa skyed pa'o / / de yang nges pa dang ma nges pa dang tshe rabs de nyid kyi dus dang ldan pa'i phyir go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o / / 'di la bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos la mos pa dang dad pa'i mtshan nyid kyi thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams te / / de nyid la chos la nges par sems pa'i bzod pa'i mtshan nyid kyis nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa rnams ni dad pa mchog yin pa dang shes rab mchog yin pa'i phyir te / / go rims bzhin no /
laukikā gradharmaprakṛtyaiva kṣaṇika ityaprāvandhika ityarthaḥ
# 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog ni rang bzhin gyis skad cig pa ste zhes bya ba ni rgyun ma yin pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
no tu vāsanāparihāṇita iti nirvāṇādhikārikasya kuśalamūlasyotpāditapūrvasyāpunarutpādyatvāt
# bag chags yongs su nyams pas yongs su nyams pa ni ma yin no zhes bya ba ni mya ngan las 'das par byed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba sngar bskyed pa'ang skyed mi dgos pa'i phyir ro /
mṛdu mokṣabhāgī yamadhikṛtyoktaṃ bhagavatā
# thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa chung ngu'i dbang du mdzad nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa /
samyagdṛṣṭiradhimātraṃ laukikī yasya vidyate
# 'jig rten pa yi yang dag lta / / chen po su la yod gyur pa /
api jātisahasrāṇi nāsau gacchati durgatim
# de ni tshe rabs stong du yang / / ngan 'gror 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro /
iti / api khalu caturvidhaṃ mokṣabhāgīyam ādhikārikamādhimokṣikamādhikāmikamābhigāmikaṃ ca
# zhe'o / / yang thar pa'i cha dang mthun pa bzhi ste / / skabs su gtogs pa dang mos pa las gyur pa dang lhag par 'dod pa las gyur pa dang; thob pa las gyur pa'o /
kuśaladharmacchandamupādāya yāvanmokṣārthaṃ kriyate tadādhikārikam / tatpratisaṃyuktadeśanādhimokṣasahagataṃ yattadādhimokṣikam
# dge ba'i phyogs la 'dun pa nas nye bar bzung ste / / thar pa'i cha mthun du bya ba ji snyed pa de ni skabs su gtogs pa'o / / de dang rab tu ldan pa'i bstan pa la mos pa dang ldan pa gang yin pa de ni mos pa las gyur pa'o /
prītiprasādasahagatamokṣālaṃbanamanaskārabahulaṃ yattadādhikāmikam
# dga' ba dang dad pa dang ldan pa thar pa la dmigs pa'i yid la byed pa mang ba gang yin pa de ni lhag par 'dod pa las gyur pa'o /
nirvedhabhāyīyotpāda niyataṃ tatraiva janmani yattadābhigāmikam
# tshe 'di nyid la nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa skyed par nges pa gang yin pa de ni thob pa las gyur pa'o /
nirvedhamāgīyaṃ ṣaḍvidham ānulomikaṃ prākarṣikaṃ prātivedhikamanyapāriṇāmikamaikajanmikamekāsanikaṃ ca
# nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa ni rnam pa drug ste / / rjes su mthun pa dang khyad par ba dang rab tu rtogs pa dang gzhan du yongs su sgyur ba dang skye ba gcig pa dang stan gcig pa'o /
tatra yatsatyālambanakāramādito mṛdukaṃ kuśalamūlamutpadyate tadānulomikam
# de la gang bden pa la dmigs pa'i rnam pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang po nyid du chung du 'byung ba de ni rjes su mthun pa pa'o /
yanmadhyaṃ tatprākarṣikam tataḥ tatprakṛṣṭataratvāt / yadadhimātraṃ satyaprativedhāya tatraiva janmani saṃvartate tatprātivedhikam
# gang 'bring du gyur pa de ni khyad par ba ste / / de bas chos mchog tu gyur pa'i phyir ro / / gang tshe 'di nyid la bden pa rtogs pa shas chen por gyur pa de ni rab tu rtogs pa pa'o /
tatpunaryadaniyatagotrāṇāṃ bodhiviśeṣāya pariṇāmyate tacca pratyekabuddhānāmanācāryakābhisaṃbodhāya janmāntare pariṇamati tadanyapāriṇāmikam / yattatraiva janmani satyaprativedhāya saṃvartate tadaikajanmikam
# de yang gang ma nges pa'i rigs can rnams byang chub khyad par du gyur par yongs su bsgyur ba dang gang yang rang sangs rgyas rnams tshe rabs gzhan la slob dpon med par mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par yongs su bsgyur ba de ni gzhan du yongs su bsgyur pa'o / / gang gi tshe de nyid la rab tu rtogs par 'gyur ba de ni tshe gcig pa'o /
yattatraivāsane tadekāsanikamiti
# gang stan de nyid la rab tu rtogs par 'gyur ba de ni stan gcig pa'o /
kāyasākṣī vimokṣalābhyanāgāmī aṣṭau vimokṣān kāyena sākṣātkṛtvopasaṃpadya viharaṇāt / aṣṭau vimokṣā rūpī rūpāṇi paśyatītyevamādayaḥ paścānnirdekṣyante
# lus kyis mngon du byed pa zhes bya ba ni phyir mi 'ong ba rnam par thar pa brgyad thob pa'o / / rnam par thar pa brgyad po de dag lus kyis mngon sum du byas nas rdzogs par byas te gnas pa'i phyir ro / / rnam par thar pa brgyad ni gzugs can gzugs rnams la lta ba zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste / / 'og nas 'chad do /
prajñāvimuktaḥ prajñāvipakṣakleśāvaraṇamātrāśeṣaprahāṇāt / ubhayato bhāgavimuktaḥ sarvakleśasamāpattyāvaraṇābhyāṃ yo vimuktaḥ
# shes rab kyis rnam par grol ba zhes bya ba ni shes rab kyis mi mthun pa'i phyogs nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa tsam ma lus par spangs pa'i phyir ro / / gnyi ga'i cha las rnam par grol ba ni nyon mongs pa dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i sgrib pa thams cad las gang rnam par grol ba'o /
srotāpattiphalapratipannaka ekāsanikaṃ nirvedhabhāgīyamārabhya yāvadādyaṃ phalaṃ na prāpnoti
# rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa ni nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa stan gcig pa nas bzung ste / / dang po'i 'bras bu ma thob kyi bar du'o /
kaḥ punardarśanamārgāvasāne ādyaṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti
# mthong ba'i lam gyi tha ma la dang po'i 'bras bu thob pa gang zhe na /
yaḥ pradeśavairāgyeṇāpi kāmebhyo 'vītarāgaḥ samyaktvaṃ niyāmamavakrāmati
# gang phyogs las 'dod chags dang bral yang 'dod pa dag las 'dod chags dang ma bral zhing yang dag pa nyid du nges par 'gyur ba la 'jug pa'o /
yastu pūrvaṃ laukikena mārgeṇa kāmāvacarān bhāvanāprahātavyān ṣaṭprakārān prahāya yatra yo vītarāgo bhavan paścātsamyaktvaṃ niyāmamavakrāmati sa ṣoḍaśe cittakṣaṇe sakṛdāgāmyeva bhavati
# gang sdar 'jig rten pa'i lam gyis bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i 'dod pa na spyod pa rnam pa drug spangs nas phal cher las 'dod chags dang bral bar gyur te / / phyis yang dag pa nyid la nges par 'jug pa de ni sems kyi skad cig bcu drug pa la lan cig phyir 'ong ba nyid du 'gyur ba'o /
navāpi prakārān prahāya kāmavītarāgo bhavan yo niyāmamavakrāmati so 'nāgāmyeva bhavati
# gang rnam pa dgu char spangs nas 'dod pa las 'dod chags dang bral bar 'gyur te / / nges par gyur pa la 'jug pa de ni phyir mi 'ong ba nyid du 'gyur ba'o /
sarvadarśanaprahātavyaprahāṇe 'pi trayāṇāmeva saṃyojanānāṃ prahāṇāt srotāpannavacanam eṣāṃ mokṣaprāptibibandhanatvena prādhānyāt / tathāhi satkāyadṛṣṭayā pañcopādānaskandhānātmata ātmīyataścābhiniveśyālayārāmatayā duḥkhānnoccalati
# mthong bas spang par bya ba thams cad spangs kyang kun du sbyor ba gsum spangs nas rgyun du zhugs pa zhes brjod pa ni / / 'di dag thar pa thob pa'i gegs su gyur pas gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te / / 'di ltar 'jig tshogs la lta bas nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po dag la bdag dang bdag gir mngon par zhen nas bdag la dga' ba sdug bsngal las mi 'phags so /
uccalito 'pi kathaṃcinmokṣaṃ prati śīlavrataparāmarśena vicikitsayā cāsanmārgābhiniveśātsanmārgasaṃśayanācca mithyā niryāti samyaktvamaniryāti
# ji snyed 'phags kyang thar par bya ba'i phyir tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa dang the tshom gyi lam ngan pa la mngon bar zhen pa dang lam bzang po la the tshom za ba'i phyir / / log pas nges par 'byung gi yang dag par nges par mi 'byung ngo /
punaḥ satkāyadṛṣṭayā jñeye vipratipadyate duḥkhamātra ātmātmīyalakṣaṇa samāropaṇāt
# yang 'jig tshogs la lta bas zhes bya ba la log par rtogs pa ste / / sdug bsngal tsam la bdag dang bdag gi ba'i mtshan nyid du sgro 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
śīlavrataparāmarśena dṛṣṭau tayā śuddhipratyayanāt
# tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pas lta ba la log par rtogs te / / des dag par yid ches pa'i phyir ro /
vicikitsayā pratipakṣe ratnatrayāniścayanāditi / sakṛdāgāmiphalapratipannakaḥ darśanamārgādūrdhvaṃ kāmāvacarasya yāvanmadhyamadhyasya kleśaprakārasya prahāṇamārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# the tshom gyis ni gnyen po la log par rtogs te / / dkon mchog gsum la nges par mi byed pa'i phyir ro / / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa ni mthong ba'i lam gyi gong du 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa 'bring po'i 'bring gi bar du spong ba'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag gang yin pa'o /
sakṛdāgāmī madhyamṛdoḥ kleśaprakārasya prahāṇa mārga parisamāptau yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# lan cig phyir 'ong ba ni nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa 'bring po'i chung du spong ba'i lam yongs su rdzogs pa la gnas pa'i gang zag gang yin pa'o /
anāgāmiphalapratipannakaḥ sakṛdāgāmiphalādūrdhvaṃ kāmāvacarāṇāṃ mṛdvadhimātramṛdumadhyayoḥ kleśaprakārayoḥ prahāṇamārge yaḥ pudgalaḥ
# phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa ni / / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i gong du 'dod pa na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa chung du'i chen po dang chung du'i 'bring po spangs pa'i lam la gnas pa'i gang zag gang yin pa'o /
anāgāmī navamasya mṛdumṛdoḥ kleśaprakārasya prahāṇāya mārgaparisamāptau yaḥ pudgalaḥ / sarvakāmāvacarabhāvanāprahātavyaprahāṇe 'pi pañcānāmavarabhāgīyānāṃ saṃyojanānāṃ prahāṇādanāgāmivacanaṃ sūtre eṣāṃ gatidhātvavarakāraṇatvena prādhānyāt
# phyir mi 'ong ba ni dgu pa nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa chung ngu'i chung du spong ba'i lam yongs su rdzogs pa la gnas pa'i gang zag gang yin pa'o / / 'dod pa na spyod pa gang bsgom pas spang bar bya ba thams cad spangs kyang tha ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun du sbyor ba lnga spangs pas phyir mi 'ong ba zhes mdo las 'byung ba ni 'di dag 'gro ba dang khams tha ma'i rgyur gyur pas gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te /
gatyavaraṃ punaḥ narakatiryakpretagatayaḥ / dhātvavaraṃ kāmadhātuḥ
# 'gro ba tha ma ni sems can dmyal ba dang yid gas dang dud 'gro'o / / khams tha ma ni 'dod pa'i khams so /
tatra satkāyadṛṣṭiśīlavrataparāmarśavicikitsābhiḥ gatya varāsamatikrāntatvātkāraṇatvam
# de la 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa dang the tshom rnams kyis ni 'gro ba tha ma las mi 'da' bas de'i rgyu nyid do /
kāmacchandavyāpādābhyāṃ dhātvavarāsamatikramāditi / traidhātukasarvakleśaprahāṇe 'pi pañcānāmūrdhvabhāgīyānāṃ prahāṇādarhadvacanam ūrdhvopādānāparityāgakāraṇatvena prādhānyam
# 'dod pa la 'dun pa dang gnod sems gnyis kyis ni khams tha ma la mi 'da' bas de'i rgyu nyid do / / khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs kyang gong ma'i cha dang mthun pa lnga spangs pas dgra bcom pa zhes brjod pa ni gong ma nye bar len pa dang yongs su mi gtong ba'i rgyur gyur pas gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te /
tatra rūpārūpyarāgābhyāṃ kāmadhātau ūrdhvopādānaṃ rūpārūpyadhātūpapattirityarthaḥ
# de la gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i 'dod chags gnyis kyis ni 'dod pa'i khams nas gong ma nye bar len te / / gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams su skye zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go; /
auddhatyamānāvidyābhirurdhvāparityāgaḥ tṛṣṇāmānavicikitsottaradhyāyitvena satra saṃkleśāditi
# rgod pa dang nga rgyal dang ma rig pa rnams kyis ni gong ma yongs su mi gtong ste / / sred pa dang nga rgyal dang the tshom gyi shas che ba'i bsam gtan pa nyid du der kun nas nyon mongs pa'i phyir ro /
kulaṃ kulaḥ kulaḥ srotāpanna eva sakṛdāgāmiphalapratipannako deveṣu vā manuṣyeṣu vā niyamena dvau bhavau saṃsṛtya parinirvāti
# rigs nas rigs su skye ba ni rgyun du zhugs pa nyid de / / lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa lha'am mi rnams kyi nang du nges par srid pa gnyis 'khor bar byas nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'o /
ekavīcikaḥ sakṛdāgāmyevānāgāmiphalapratipannako deveṣvevaikaṃ bhavaṃ saṃsṛtyaṃ parinirvāti
# bar chad gcig pa ni lan cig phyir 'ong ba nyid de / / phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la 'jug pa lha nyid kyi nang du srid pa gcig 'khor ba byas nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'o /
ekā vīcirantaraṃ janmāvakāśo 'sya so 'yamekavīcikaḥ
# bar chad gcig pa ni bar skabs te skye ba'i skabs yod pa de'i phyir de ni bar chad gcig pa'o /
antarāparinirvāyī yena kleśāvedhenopapattideśaṃ gatvā pratisandadhyāttatparikṣaye sati yenānuśayamātreṇa maraṇādūrdhva skandhānabhinirvartayan tadavaśeṣe satyantarābhavamabhinirvartya pūrvābhyastamārgasaṃmukhībhāvādeva sa viśiṣṭānuśayaprahāṇe parinirvāti
# bar ma dor yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba ni nyon mongs pa'i shugs gang gis skye ba'i yul du song na nying mtshams sbyor ba de zad nas bag la nyal tsam gang gis shi ba'i 'og tu phung po mngon par 'grub pa de'i lhag ma lus pas bar de'i srid pa mngon par 'grub ste / / sngon goms par byas pa'i lam mngon du gyur pas bag la nyal lhag ma spangs ste / / de nyid du yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'o /
sa punarupapattideśaṃ pratyanuccalitoccalitamātradūragabhāvasthatayā trividho veditavyaḥ satpuruṣagatisūtrānusāreṇa
# de yang skye ba'i yul las mi 'phags pa dang 'phags pa tsam dang ring du song ba'i gnas skabs kyi rnam pa gsum ste / / skyes bu dam pa'i 'gro ba'i mdo'i tshul du rig par bya'o /
anabhisaṃskāreṇa yo mārgaṃ saṃmukhīkṛtyeti pūrvaṃ svabhyastatvātsvarasavāhitayāprayatnenetyarthaḥ
# mngon par 'du byed pa med par lam mngon du byas nas zhes bya ba ni sngon shin tu goms par 'jug pa'i phyir te / / bsgrim mi dgos zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
viparyayādabhisaṃskāraparinirvāyī / ūrdhvasrotā dvividhaḥ akaniṣṭhago bhavāgragaśca
# de las bzlog pa ni mngon par 'du byed pa dang bcas pas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'o / / gong du 'pho ba ni rnam pa gnyis te / / 'og min du 'gro ba dang srid pa'i rtse mor 'gro ba'o /
tatra akaniṣṭhaga āsvādanābahulatayotpannotpannamṛdvādidhyānaprakārāsvādanāt brahmakāyikānārabhya nirantaraṃ sarveṣu sthānāntareṣu sakṛtsakṛdupapadyamāno yāvadakaniṣṭhānpraviśya parinirvāti
# de la 'og min du 'gro ba ni ro myang ba mang bas bsam gtan gyi rnam pa chung du la sogs pa skyes shing skyes pa'i ro myong bar byed pa'i phyir tshangs ris nas bzung ste / / rgyun mi 'chad par gnas gzhan thams cad du lan re re skyes nas 'og min gyi bar du zhugs te / / yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'o /
bhavāgragaścaturthasya dhyānasyāvyavakīrṇabhāvitvāt kevalaṃ śuddhāvāsān parihṛtya tathaiva yāvadbhavāgraṃ gatvā parinirvāti / vyavakīrṇabhāvitasya caturthasya dhyānasya mṛdvādipañcaprakārabhāvitatvādyathākramaṃ pañcasu śuddhāvāseṣūpapattirveditavyā
# srid pa'i rtse mor 'gro ba ni bsam gtan bzhin pa la spel mar ma bsgoms pas gnas gtsang ma 'ba' zhig bkol te / / de bzhin du srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du song nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'o / / spel mar bsgom pa ni bsam gtan bzhi pa'i rnam pa chung du la sogs pa lnga bsgoms pas go rims bzhin du gnas gtsang ma lnga po rnams su skye bar rig par bya'o /
cetayitvācetayitveti svayamātmānamupakramamāṇo 'nupakramamāṇo vetyarthaḥ / dṛṣṭadharmasukhavihārātparihāṇameti laukikebhyo dhyānebhya ityarthaḥ
# gsod kyang rung mi gsod kyang rung zhes bya ba ni bdag gis bdag gi srog gcod pa'am / / mi gcod ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa las yongs su nyams pa zhes bya ba ni / / 'jig rten pa'i bsam gtan rnams las zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
indriyottāpanaṃ punaradhimātratānayanaṃ tīkṣṇakaraṇamityarthaḥ
# dbang po rnams sbyong ba zhes bya ba ni chen po thob par byed pa ste / / rno bar byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ata evākopyadharmā bhavyaścendriyāṇyuttāpayitumiti noktam prakṛtyā tīkṣṇendriyatvāt
# de'i phyir mi 'khrugs pa'i chos can la dbang po rnams yongs su sbyong ba'i skal ba can zhes ma bshad de / / rang bzhin gyis dbang po rno ba'i phyir ro /
kāmāvacararūpāvacara eva bodhisattvo nārūpyāvacaraḥ prabhāvaprāptasya sattvaparipācanānāyatanatāmupādāya tatrānupapattitaḥ
# byang chub sems dpa' ni 'dod pa na spyod pa dang gzugs na spyod pa nyid yin gyi gzugs med pa na spyod pa ni ma yin te / / sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i gnas ma yin pa'i phyir mthu'i khyad par thob pa der mi skye'o /
ārūpyadhātuvyavakarṣitena dhyāneneti paryudastārūpyopapattikena samādhinetyarthaḥ
# gzugs med pa'i khams rnams par spangs pa'i bsam gtan zhes bya ba ni gzugs med par skyes bor ba'i ting nge 'dzin zhing bya ba'i tha tshig go /
dhyānasukhaviharatyaparihīṇa eva dhyānebhyaḥ dhyānavyāvartanakuśalatvāt / sattvaparipācanārthaṃ kāmadhātāvapi bodhisattva upapadyata iti veditavyam
# bsam gtan gyi bden pas gnas pa ni yongs su ma nyams pa nyid de / / bsam gtan las rnam par bzlog pa la mkhas pas sems can yongs su smin par bya ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' ni 'dod pa'i khams su yang skye bar rig par bya'o /
sarvāṃ bodhisattvacaryāmiti tuṣitabhavanavāsamupādāya yāvanmāraparājayam
# byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad ces bya ba ni dga' ldan gyi gnas na gnas pa nas bzung ste / / bdud las rgyal ba'i bar du'o /
buddhacaryāṃ ca darśayatītyabhisaṃbodhimupādāya yāvanmahāparinirvāṇam
# sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa zhes bya ba ni mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa nas bzung ste / / yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i bar du'o /
adhimukticārī bodhisattvagotre vyavasthita ādito mahābodhiprasthānamupādāya yāvatpramuditāṃ bhūmiṃ na praviśati pratyātmaṃ lokottarābhigamābhāvāt
# mos pas spyod pa can gyi byang chub sems dpa' ni rigs las gnas pa thog mar smon lam chen po btab pa nas bzung nas rab tu dga' ba'i sa la ma zhugs kyi bar du ste / / so sor rang gis 'jig rten las 'das pa thob pa med pa'i phyir ro /
adhyāśayacāro daśasu bhūmiṣu lokottareṇādhigamena viśuddhāśayatvāt
# lhag pa'i bsam pas spyod pa can ni sa bcu rnams su 'jig rten las 'das pa thob pas bsam pa dag pa'i phyir ro /
nimittacārī ṣaṭsu bhūmiṣu anicchato 'pi nimittavyavakiraṇāt
# mtshan ma la spyod pa can ni sa drug po dag la mi 'dod bzhin du mtshan ma dang 'dre ba'i phyir ro /
animittacārī saptamyām yatnaṃ kurvato yāvadicchaṃ nimittāsamudācārāt
# mtshan ma med par spyod pa can ni sa bdun po dag la bsgrims nas ji srid 'dod par mtshan ma kun du mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
anabhisaṃskāracārī śeṣāsu bhūmiṣu vaipākikanirvikalpajñānapratilambhāditi / sakṛnnairyāṇikaḥ sakṛttraidhātukāvacarānkleśān prajahāti / prakāraśa ityadhimātrādhimātrānkāmarūpārūpyāvacarānbhāvanāprahātavyānanuśayān prajahāti evaṃ yāvan mṛdumṛdūn darśanaprahātavyān na tu laukikamārgavadbhūmiprakārabhedena pṛthakpṛthagityarthaḥ / tatredaṃ jñāpakaṃ yathoktamaṃgulyagrasūtre "yatkiṃcidrūpaṃ yāvadvijñānamatītānāgatapratyutpannamiti vistareṇa yāvaddūre yadvāntike tatsarvamekadhyamasaṃkṣipyaikaṃ bhāgaṃ karotyekaṃ piṇḍamekaṃ puñjamekaṃ rāśiṃ karotyekaṃ kṛtvātaḥ pratisaṃśikṣate sarvametadanityaṃ sarvaṃ duḥkhamiti vistaraḥ
# mngon par 'du byed pa med par spyod pa can ni sa lhag ma rnams su rnam par smin pa las byung ba'i rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes rnams thob pa'i phyir ro / / cig car nges par 'byin pa ni khams gsum na spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa'i rnam pa cig car spong ba'o / / rnam pas zhes bya ba ni bsgom pas spang bar bya bar 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa na spyod pa chen po'i chen po cig car spong ba dang de bzhin du chung ngu'i chung ngu'i bar du ste / / mthong bas spang bar bya ba bzhin no / / 'jig rten pa'i lam bzhin du sa'i rnam pa'i bye brag gis so so ba ni ma yin pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / 'dir khungs ni sor mo'i rtse mo'i mdo las gzugs gang ci yang rung ste zhes bya ba nas / / rnam par shes pa'i bar du 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba zhes rgya cher 'byung ba nas / / rgyang ring po dang thag nye ba zhes bya ba'i bar du de thams cad gcig tu bsdus te cha gcig tu byed do / / gcig tu bzlum mo / / gcig tu sdom mo / / phung po gcig tu byed do / / cha gcig tu byas shing phung po gcig gi bar du byas nas 'di ltar yang dag par slob ste / / 'di thams cad ni mi rtag pa / / 'di thams cad ni sdug bsngal ba zhes rgya cher gsungs pa lta bu'o /
dvayorevādyantayoḥ phalayoḥ prajñāpyate / tayostraidhātukasarvadarśanabhāvanāprahātavyāśeṣaprahāṇaprabhāvitatvādyathākramam / madhyayostu na prajñāpyate tayordṛṣṭasatyasya kāmavacarāṇāmeva bhāvanāprahātavyānāṃ sāvaśeṣaniravaśeṣaprahāṇaprabhāvitatvāt
# de ni 'bras bu dang po'o / / tha ma gnyis kho na la gdags te / / de gnyis ni khams gsum pa'i mthong ba dang bsgom pas spong bar bya ba thams cad ma lus pa spangs pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir go rims bzhin no / / bar ma dag la mi gdags te / / de dag ni bden pa mthong ba'i bsgom pas spang bar bya ba 'dod pa na spyod pa nyid la lhag ma dang bcas pa dang lhag ma med par spangs pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
sakṛnnairyāṇikaṃ cādhikṛtya vibhaṅgasūtre srotāpannānantaramarhadvyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# cig car nges par 'byin pa'i dbang du byas nas rnam par 'byed pa'i mdo las rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'i 'og tu dgra bcom pa rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
sa dṛṣṭe dharme yadyājñāṃ tārāgayati sarvato niḥśeṣamavītarāgatvātpraṇidhānavaśena kāmadhātāvupapadyate kṣipraparinirvāṇārtham
# thams cad la ma lus par 'dod chags dang bral ba ma yin pas de gal te mthong ba'i chos la kun shes pa thob par mi byed na myur du yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar bya ba'i phyir smon lam gyi dbang gis 'dod pa'i khams nyid du skye'o /
abhisamayavyavasthānaṃ daśavidham
# mngon par rtogs pa rnam par gzhag pa ni rnam pa bcu ste /
tatra dharmābhisamayaḥ satyādhipateyeṣu sūtrādiṣu dharmeṣu paratoghoṣamadhipatiṃ kṛtvā dhimātrasyādhimuktiprasādasya paścimamokṣabhāgīyasaṃgṛhītasya pratilambhaḥ
# de la chos mngon bar rtogs pa ni gzhan gyi sgra'i dbang du byas pa ste / / bden pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos rnams la thar pa'i cha dang mthun ba tha mas bsdus pa'i mos pa dang dad pa chen po thob pa ste /
tathāhi tadadhimuktiprasādapratilambhāttāni satyāni dharmābhisamayenābhisamitānītyucyante
# 'di ltar de la mos pa dang dad pa thob pas bden pa de dag la chos mngon par rtogs pas mngon par rtogs par gyur zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
arthābhisamayasteṣveva dharmeṣu yoniśomanaskāramadhipatikṛtvādhimātrāyāḥ satyeṣu dharmanidhyānakṣānte: paścimanirvedhabhāgīya saṃgṛhītāyāḥ pratilambhaḥ
# don mngon par rtogs pa ni chos de dag nyid la gang tshul bzhin du yid la byed pa'i dbang du byas nas bden pa rnams la nges par 'byed pa'i cha dang mthun pa tha mas bsdus pa'i chos nges par sems pa'i bzod pa chen po thob pa'o /
sā punardharmanidhyānakṣāntistrividhena yoniśomanaskāreṇa prabhāvitā adhimātramṛdunā tajjanmakāleṣūṣmagateṣu adhimātramadhyena mūrdhvasu kṣāntiṣu ca adhimātrādhimātreṇa laukikeṣvagradharmeṣviti
# chos nges par sems pa'i bzod pa de yang tshul bzhin yid la byed pa rnam pa gsum gyis rab tu phye ba ste / / chen po'i chung ngus ni tshe de'i dro bar gyur pa rnams su'o / / chen po'i 'bring pos ni rtse mo dang bzod pa rnams su'o / / chen po'i chen pos ni 'jig rten pa'i chos kyi mchog rnams su'o /
tattvābhisamayo darśanamārgaḥ / tatra punaḥ satyavyavasthāpanānyabhisamayāntikāni saṃvṛtijñānāni pratilambhato lokottarajñānādhipatyena tadabījapoṣaṇānna tu sammukhīkaroti ṣoḍaśānāṃ darśanamārgacittakṣaṇānāṃ nirantaratvena laukikacittānavakāśāt
# de kho na mngon par rtogs pa ni mthong ba'i lam ste / / der ni bden pa rnam par 'jog pa mngon par rtogs pa'i mtha' las byung ba kun rdzob shes pa rnams thob ste / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes kyi dbang gis de'i sa bon gsos pa'i phyir gyi mngon sum du byed pa ni ma yin te / / mthong ba'i lam gyi sems kyi skad cig bcu drug po dag rgyun mi 'chad pas 'jig rten pa'i sems kyi skabs med pa'i phyir ro /
pṛṣṭhābhisamayo darśanamārgādūrdhvasarvabhāvanāmārgo laukiko lokottaro vā / ratnābhisamayaḥ samyaksaṃbuddho vata bhagavān svākhyāto 'sya dharmavinayaḥ supratipannaḥ śrāvakasaṃgha ityevamavetya niścityāryaśrāvakasya buddhādiṣu prasādaḥ
# rjes la mngon par rtogs pa ni mthong ba'i lam gyi gong du 'jig rten pa yang rung / / 'jig rten las 'das pa yang rung ste / / bsgom pa'i lam thams cad do / / dkon mchog mngon par rtogs pa ni / / kye ma bcom ldan 'das ni yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams so / / de'i chos 'dul ba ni legs par gsungs pa'o / / nyan thos kyi dge 'dun ni legs par zhugs pa'o zhes de ltar shes te / / nges nas sangs rgyas la sogs pa la 'phags pa nyan thos dad pa'o /
asamudācārābhisamayo yasyākaraṇasaṃvarasyāyaṃkāntaśīla saṃgṛhītasya lābhāttadvipakṣanarakādyasamudācāraṃ pratyevaṃ niścayaḥ pravarttate kṣoṇā me narakāḥ ityevamādiḥ so 'samudācārābhisamayaḥ
# kun du mi 'byung bar mngon par rtogs pa ni mi bya ba'i sdom pa 'phags pa dgyes pa'i tshul khrims kyis bsdus pa thob pas de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs byed pa la sogs pa kun du mi 'byung ste / / bdag gi sems can dmyal ba zad do zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste / / bdag gi sems can dmyal ba zad do zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste /
niṣṭhābhisamayaḥ sarvadauṣṭhulyānāṃ pratiprasrabdhirityevamādiryathā mārgasatye niṣṭhāmārgo nirdiṣṭaḥ / eta eva saptābhisamayāḥ śrāvakāṇāṃ paratoghoṣamāgamya pratilambhataḥ śrāvakābhisamaya ityucyate
# de ltar nges par 'byung ba de ni kun du mi 'byung ba mngon par rtogs pa'o / / mthar thug pa mngon par rtogs pa ni gnas ngan len thams cad shin tu sbyangs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pas ji ltar lam gyi bden pa las mthar phyin pa'i lam bstan pa lta bu'o / / mngon par rtogs pa bdun po de dag ni nyan thos rnams kyis gzhan gyi sga la brten nas thob pas nyan thos kyi mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya'o /
paratoghoṣamanāgamya pratilambhataḥ pratyekabuddhabhisamaya iti / bodhisattvābhisamaya eṣu saptasvabhisamayeṣu bodhisattvasya yā samudāgamakṣāntiḥ śrāvakapratyekabuddhavinayopāyakauśalyārthaṃ no tu sākṣātkriyā sattvāpekṣayā hīnayānāniryāṇāt / api khalu tatprathamato bodhisattvasya bhūmipraveśābhisamaya ityucyate
