# gzhan gyi sgra la ma brten par thob pas rang sangs rgyas kyi mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya'o / / byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas 'dul ba'i thabs la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir / / mngon par rtogs pa bdun po de dag la byang chub sems dpa'i yang dag par 'grub pa'i bzod pa gang yin pa ste / / sems can la lta bas theg pa chung dus nges par mi 'byung ba'i phyir mngon du byed pa ni ma yin no / / yang thog ma nyid du sa la 'jug pa yang byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa zhes bya'o /
etaṃ cābhisamaya niśrityocyate śrāvakābhisamayādbodhisattvābhisamasya kaḥ prativiśeṣaḥ ālaṃbanaviśeṣato vaipulyālaṃbanatvāt
# mngon par rtogs pa de la brten nas nyan thos kyi mngon par rtogs pa las byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par rtogs pa khyad par ci yod pa brjod par bya ste / / dmigs pa'i khyad par na shin tu rgyas pa la dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
upastambhaviśeṣataḥ paripūrṇamahākalpāsakhyeyamahāpuṇyajñānasaṃbhāraparipūraṇāt
# nye bar rtog pa'i khyad par ni bskal pa chen po grangs med par bsod rnams dang ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir ro /
prativedhaviśeṣataḥ pudgaladharmanairātmyādhipateyadharmaprayogavedhato lokottareṇa jñānena tadubhayaprativedhāt abhyupagamaviśeṣataḥ svātmasamatayā sarvasattvābhyupagamāt
# rab tu rtogs pa'i khyad par ni gang zag dang chos la bdag med pa'i dbang du byas pa'i chos la sbyor ba'i 'phen pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes kyis de gnyi ga rab tu rtogs pa'i phyir ro / / khas len pa'i khyad par ni bdag dang sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid du khas len pa'i phyir ro /
niryāṇaviśeṣato daśabhirbhūmibhirniryāṇāt
# nges par 'byung ba'i khyad par ni sa bcu po dag gis nges par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
parigrahaviśeṣato 'pratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaparigrahaṇāt
# yongs su 'dzin pa'i khyad par ni mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i phyir ro /
pratiṣṭhāparivāraviśeṣato buddhakṣatrapariśīdhanādvineyajanopagrahaṇācca
# gnas dang g yog 'khor gyi khyad par ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su sbyong ba dang gdul ba'i skye bo nye bar sdud pa'i phyir ro /
abhijanmaviśeṣataḥ pitṛvaṃśasaṃdhārakaurasaputralakṣaṇatvāt
# btsun par skye ba'i khyad par ni pha bzhin du rang gi rigs yang dag par 'dzin pa'i bu gtso bo'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
janmaviśeṣataḥ pariṣanmaṇḍaleṣūpapannaḥ
# skye ba'i khyad par ni 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnams su skye ba'i phyir ro /
phalaviśeṣaśca punaḥ āśrayaparivṛttiviśeṣataḥ kliṣṭākliṣṭasarvaprakāradauṣṭhulyaprahāṇātsarvaniruttaraguṇāśrayatvenāśrayaparivartanāt
# 'bras bu'i khyad par de yang gnas gyur pa'i khyad par ni nyon mongs pa can dang nyon mongs pa can ma yin pa'i gnas ngan len gyi rnam pa thams cad spangs pa'i phyir yon tan bla na med pa thams cad kyi gnas nyid du gyur pas gnas gyur pa'i phyir ro /
guṇasamṛddhiviśeṣato balavaṃśāradyāveṇikabuddhadharmādyaparimitaguṇaniṣpatteḥ
# yon tan phun sum tshogs pa'i khyad par ni stobs dang mi 'jigs pa dang sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa la sogs pa yon tan dpag tu med pa 'grub pa'i phyir ro /
pañcākāraviśeṣato viśuddhyādiviśeṣāt / tatra viśuddhiviśeṣaḥ savāsanakleśaprahāṇāt / pariśuddhiviśeṣo buddhakṣetrapariśodhanāt / kāyaviśeṣo dharmakāyapariniṣpādanāt / bhogaviśeṣaḥ sadā bodhisattveḥ saha parṣanmaṇḍaleṣu vicitradharmasaṃbhogāt / kamaviśeṣo yathārhaṃ nirmāṇeḥ samantādanantāparyanteṣu lokadhātuṣu buddhakṛtyānuṣṭhānāditi / kāyatrayaviśeṣataḥ svabhāvikasāmbhāgikanairmāṇikāyapariniṣpattilābhāt
# rnam pa lnga'i khyad par ni rnam par dag pa la sogs pa'i khyad par gyi phyir te / / rnam par dag dang yongs dag dang / / lus dang longs spyod rdzogs pa dang / / las kyi sangs rgyas chos rnams kyi / / khyad par yongs su brjod pa yin / / de la rnam par dag pa'i khyad par ni bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa spong ba'i phyir ro / / yongs su dag pa'i khyad par ni / / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su sbyong ba'i phyir ro / / lus kyi khyad par ni chos kyi sku yongs su sgrub pa'i phyir ro / / longs spyod kyi khyad par ni rtag tu byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang lhan cig 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnams su chos sna tshogs brjod par longs spyod pa'i phyir ro / / las kyi khyad par ni ci rigs par sprul pa rnams kyis kun du 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas mu med pa rnams su sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa sgrub pa'i phyir ro / / sku gsum gyi khyad par ni rang bzhin dang longs spyod rdzogs pa dang sprul pa'i sku 'grub pa thob pa'i phyir ro /
nirvāṇaviśeṣato nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau sarvasattvahitāya sarvaguṇāsamucchedāt
# mya ngan las 'das pa'i khyad par ni phung po lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings su yang sems can thams cad la phan par yon tan thams cad rgyun mi gcod pa'i phyir ro /
miśropamiśrajñānaśaktilābhaviśeṣataḥ suviśuddhadharmadhātvekarasatayā tadāśritāsu sarvākāravarajñatāsu pratyekaṃ sarvabuddhānāṃ sāmarthyāt
# 'dres shing nye bar 'dres pa'i ye shes kyi nus pa thob pa'i khyad par ni chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag par ro gcig pa nyid dang de la brten pa rnams rnam pa thams cad kyi mchog shes pa nyid rnams la sangs rgyas thams cad so sor mthu dang ldan pa'i phyir ro /
āvaraṇaviśuddhiviśeṣataḥ sarvakleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇāt
# sgrib pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'i khyad par ni nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa thams cad spong ba'i phyir ro /
miśropamiśrakarmakriyāviśeṣata ekaikasattvavinayanaṃ prati sarvabuddhādhipatyāt
# 'dres pa dang nye bar 'dres pa'i las byed pa'i khyad par ni / / sems can re re 'dul ba'i phyir yang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dbang gis byed pa'i phyir ro /
abhisaṃbodhinirvāṇasaṃdarśanopāyaviśeṣato daśasu dikṣu yathāyogaṃ sarvalokadhātuṣu yāvadaparāntaṃ punaḥpunarbuddhotpādādi saṃdarśanena sarvavineyajanaparipācanavimocanāt
# mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa dang mya ngan las 'das pa ston pa'i thabs kyi khyad par ni phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du ci rigs par phyi ma'i mtha'i bar du yang dang yang sangs rgyas 'byung ba la sogs pa ston pas 'dul ba thams cad yongs su smin par byed pa dang rnam par thar par byed pa'i phyir ro /
pañcākāraparitrāṇaviśeṣataśca veditavya upadravādiparitrāṇāt / tatra upadravaparitrāṇaṃ nagarapraveśādibhi randhādīnāṃ cakṣurādipratilambhāt
# yongs su skyob pa rnam pa lnga'i khyad par gyis kyang rig par bya'o zhes bya ba ni gnod pa la sos pa las yongs su skyob pa'i phyir ro / / de la gnod pa las yongs su skyob pa ni grong khyer du 'jug pa la sogs pas long ba la sogs pas mig la sogs pa thob pa'i phyir ro /
anupāyaparitrāṇaṃ laukika samyagdṛṣṭipratilambhena sarvakudṛṣṭivivecanāt
# thabs ma yin pa las yongs su skyob pa ni 'jig rten pa'i yang dag pa'i lta ba thob pas lta ba ngan pa thams cad dang bral bar byed pa'i phyir ro /
apāyaparitrāṇaṃ darśanamārgotpādanena durgatisamatikramaṇāt satkāyaparitrāṇamarhattvasākṣātkaraṇena traidhātukavi mokṣāṇāt
# ngan song las yongs su skyob pa ni mthong ba'i lam skyed pas ngan 'gro las shin tu bzlog pa'i phyir ro / / 'jig tshogs las yongs su skyob pa ni dgra bcom pa nyid mngon du byed pas khams gsum pa las rnam par thar par byed pa'i phyir ro /
yānaparitrāṇaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ hīnayānavicchandanāditi / vaiśaṃṣikaguṇā āryaśrāvakairbhāvanāmārge vābhinirhriyante 'śaikṣamārge vetyata eṣāṃ pṛṣṭhaniṣṭhābhisamayābhyāṃ saṃgraho veditavyaḥ / te punarmaitryādayo yathāsūtrāntareṣu nirdiṣṭāḥ śrāvakayāne mahāyāne ca tathaiva veditavyāḥ
# theg pa dman pa las yongs su skyob pa ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams theg pa dman pa las 'dun pa bzlog pa'i phyir ro / / gnod pa dag ni thams cad dang / / thabs ma yin dang ngan song dang / / thag pa dman las skyob pas na / / de phyir mgon po dam pa'o / / yon tan khyad par can rnams ni 'phags pa nyan thos rnams kyis bsgom pa'i lam dang mi slob pa'i lam la mngon par sgrub ste / / de'i phyir 'di dag rjes la mngon par rtogs pa dang thar thug pa'i mngon par rtogs pas bsdus par rig par bya'o / / byams pa la sogs pa mdo sde gzhan dag las ji skad bstan pa de dag ni nyan thos kyi theg pa dang theg pa chen por yang de bzhin du rig par bya'o /
teṣāṃ cāya samāsena pañcabhirākārairyathāyogaṃ lakṣaṇanirdeśo veditavyaḥ niśrayata ālaṃbanata ākārataḥ svabhāvataḥ sahāyataśca / tatra tāvat maitryā dhyānaṃ niśrayaḥ sattvā ālaṃbanam sukhena saṃprayujyerannityākāraḥ samādhiḥ prajñā ca svabhāvaḥ śamathavipaśyanāsaṃgṛhītatvātsarvaguṇānām cittacaitasikāḥ sahāyā ityevaṃ karuṇādiṣu yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyam
# de dag kyang mdor bsdus na rnam pa lngas ci rigs su mtshan nyid bshad par blta ste / / gnas dang dmigs pa dang rnam pa dang rang bzhin dang grogs kyis so / / de la byams pa'i gnas ni bsam gtan no / / dmigs pa ni sems can no / / rnam pa ni bde ba dang ldan par gyur cig snyam pa'o / / rang bzhin ni ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab ste / / zhi gnas dang lhag mthong gis bsdus pa'i phyir ro / / yon tan thams cad kyi grogs ni sems dang sems las byung ba rnams so / / snying rje la sogs pa la yang de bzhin du ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o /
upekṣayā sukhādiṣu sattveṣvanunayādyabhyupekṣaṇamaho vata saṃkleśādvimucyerannityayamākāro veditavyaḥ
# sems can bde bar gyur pa la sogs pa la yang rjes su chags pa la sogs pa btang snyoms su byed cing kye ma nyon mongs pa las rnam par grol bar gyur cig snyam pa 'di ni btang snyoms kyi rnam par rig par bya ste /
sa ca hitāśayavihāra ityucyate
# de yang phan pa'i bsam pas gnas pa zhes bya'o /
aṣṭau vimokṣāḥ / rūpī rūpāṇi paśyatyayaṃ prathamo vimokṣa iti vistaraḥ / tatra kathaṃ rūpītyucyate
# rnam par thar pa brgyad ni gzugs can gzugs rnams la lta ba 'di ni rnam par thar pa dang po'o zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o / / de la ji ltar na gzugs can zhes bya zhe na /
svātmanyā rūpyasamāpattisaṃniśrayeṇa rūpasaṃjñāyā abhibhāvanādrūpasaṃjñāsaṃniveśanādvā draṣṭavyāni rūpasaṃjñāsaṃmukhī karaṇādityarthaḥ
# gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la brten nas bdag la gzugs kyi 'du shes rnam par mi 'jog pa'i phyir ram / / gzugs kyi 'du shes 'jog pa'i phyir te / / lta ba po bdag la gzugs kyi 'du shes mngon du byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
kathaṃ rūpāṇi paśyatītyucyate
# ji ltar na gzugs rnams la lta ba zhes bya zhe na /
suvarṇadurvarṇādīni rūpāṇyadhimucyadarśanāt / kathaṃ vimokṣa ityucyate
# kha dog mdzes pa dang kha dog mi sdug pa la sogs pa'i gzugs rnams su mos nas lta ba'i phyir ro / / ji ltar rnam par thar pa zhes bya zhe na /
vimucyate 'nena nirmāṇāvaraṇāditi kṛtvā
# 'dis sprul ba'i sgrib pa las rnam par grol ba'i phyir ro /
adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñārūpyasamāpattisaṃniśrayeṇa draṣṭari svātmani rūpasaṃjñāvibhāvanādarūpasaṃjñāsaṃniveśanādvādraṣṭari nāmasaṃjñāsaṃmukhīkaraṇādityarthaḥ
# nang gzugs med par 'du shes pa zhes bya ba ni gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la brten nas gzugs kyi 'du shes rnam par 'jig pa'i phyir ram / / gzugs med pa'i 'du shes 'jog pa'i phyir te / / lta ba po la ming du 'du shes pa mngon du byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
śeṣaṃ pūrvavat
# lhag ma ni snga ma bzhin no /
śubhaṃ vimokṣaṃ kāyena sākṣātkṛtvopasaṃpadya viharata śubhāśubheṣu rūpeṣvanyonyāpekṣāsaṃjñāmanyonyānugamasaṃjñāṃ ca niśrityānyonyaikarasasaṃjñālābhāt / tathāhi śubhāni rūpāṇyapekṣya tadanyeṣvaśubhānīti bhavatyaśubhāni vāpekṣya śubhānīti nānapekṣyaikajātīyānāmeva darśane śubhāśubhatābuddhyabhāvāt / tathāhi śubheṣvapyaśūbhatānugatāśubheṣvapi śubhatā śubhasaṃmatasyāpi tvaṅmātrasya keśādiṣaṭtriśadaśucidravyāntarabhāvādityevamanyonyaṃ sarvarūpāṇi miśrayitvā śubhataikarasākārayā saṃjñayā vimucyate
# sdug pa'i rnam par thar pa lus kyis mngon sum du byas te / / rdzogs par byas nas gnas pa ni sdug pa dang mi sdug pa'i gzugs rnams la phan tshun ltos pa'i 'du shes dang phan tshun rjes su 'brel ba'i 'du shes la brten nas phan tshun ro gcig pa'i 'du shes thob pa'i phyir ro / / 'di ltar sdug pa'i gzugs rnams la ltos nas de las gzhan pa rnams la mi sdug go zhes bya bar 'gyur la mi sdug pa la ltos nas sdug ces bya bar 'gyur gyi / / ma ltos par ni ma yin no / / rigs gcig pa rnams nyid mthong na sdug pa dang mi sdug pa gnyis kyi blo mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / de bzhin du sdug pa rnams la yang mi sdug pa nyid rjes su 'brel to / / mi sdug pa rnams la yang sdug pa nyid rjes su 'brel to / / sdug par grags pa yang brtags pa tsam du zad de / / skra la sogs pa mi gtsang ba'i rdzas sum cu rtsa drug gi nang du 'dus pa'i phyir ro / / de ltar gzugs thams cad phan tshun bsres te sdug pa nyid du ro gcig pa'i rnam pa'i 'du shes kyis mos par byed do /
tasyaivaṃ rūpādivimokṣavibhutvalābhinaḥ śubhāśubhanirmāṇāvaraṇaṃ ca prahīyate tatra ca saṃkleśotpattyāvaraṇam
# de ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du gzugs la sogs par mos pa la dbang 'byor pa thob pa de sdug pa dang mi sdug pa la sprul pa la sgrib pa spong ste / / der ni kun nas nyon mongs pa 'byung ba'i sgrib pa spong ngo /
kaḥ punarnirmāṇe saṃkleśaḥ
# sprul pa la kun nas nyon mongs pa gang yin zhe na /
śubharūpanirmāṇe ābhogaḥ aśubharūpanirmāṇe prātikūlyamiti
# sdug pa'i gzugs sprul pa la ni chags pa'o / / mi sdug pa'i gzugs sprul pa la ni mi mthun pa'o /
ākāśānantyāyatanādīni catvāryāryaśrāvakasya yānyanāśravānukūlāni śuddhāni tāni vimokṣakākhyāṃ labhante tadāsvādanavimokṣaṇāt
# nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la sogs pa bzhi ni 'phags pa nyan thos kyi zag pa med pa'i rjes su mthun pa dag pa gang yin pa de dag rnam par thar pa zhes bya ba thob ste / / de'i ro myang ba las rnam par thar par bya ba'i phyir ro /
ye te śāntā vimokṣā atikramya rūpāṇyārūpyāsteṣvasaktiḥ pariśuddhiḥ
# zhi ba'i rnam par thar ba ni gzugs rnams las shin tu 'das nas gzugs med pa gang yin pa dag ste / / de dag la mi chags pa ni yongs su dag pa'o /
tasyā āvaraṇamārūpyāsvādanamiti
# de'i sgrib pa ni gzugs med pa'i ro myang ba'o /
saṃjñāvedayitanirodhasya niśrayo naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatanam ālaṃbanākārasahāyā na santi cittacaitasikānāmabhāvāt
# 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa'i gnas ni 'du shes med 'du shes med min skye mched do / / sems dang sems las byung ba rnams med pa'i phyir dmigs pa dang rnam pa dang grogs ni med do /
svabhāvastasya cittacaitasikānāṃ nirodhaḥ / sa ca mokṣānusadṛśo vihāraḥ lokottareṇa mārgeṇa parivṛtyāśrayasyāryaśrāvakasya punaścitacaitasikānāmapyapravṛttyavasthāyāḥ paramaśāntatvāt kliṣṭamano 'samudācārācca
# de'i rang bzhin ni sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos rnams 'gog pa'o / / de yang thar pa dang mthun par gnas pa ste / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyis gnas gyur pa'i nyan thos rnams kyi sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyang mi 'byung ba'i gnas skabs na / / mchog tu zhi ba dang nyon mongs pa can gyi yid kyang kun du mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
ete cāṣṭau vimokṣā vihārā ityucyante ebhirāryāṇāṃ viharaṇāt / tatrāpi bahulamābhyāṃ vimokṣābhyāṃ viharanti tṛtīyenāṣṭamena ca pradhānatvāt
# 'phags pa rnams ni 'di dag gis gnas pa'i phyir 'di dag ni 'phags pa gnas pa'i rnam par thar pa brgyad ces bya'o / / de la 'phags pa dag ni gnas pa gnyis kyis lan mang du gnas te / / gsum pa dang brgyad pa ste / / mchog yin pa'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir de gnyis lus kyis mngon sum du byas te /
ata eva cānayoḥ kāyena sākṣātkṛtyopasaṃpadya viharatīti vacanaṃ nānyeṣu rūpyarūpivimokṣāvaraṇāśeṣaprahāṇādyathākramam
# rdzogs par byas nas gnas so zhes gsungs kyi gzhan rnams la ni ma yin te / / gzugs can dang gzugs med pa'i rnam par thar pa la sgrib pa ma lus par spangs pa'i phyir go rims bzhin no /
tayoḥ saṃpūrṇāśrayaparivṛttisākṣātkaraṇamupādāyetyaparaḥ paryāyaḥ
# rnam grangs gzhan du na de gnyis kyi gnas gyur pa rdzogs pa mngon du byed pa'i phyir ro /
aṣṭāvabhibhvāyatanāni tatra adhyātmaṃ rūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyati parīttāni suvarṇadurvarṇāni hīnapraṇī tāni tāni khalu rūpāṇyabhibhūya jānātyabhibhūya paśyati tathā ca saṃjñī bhavati
# zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched brgyad po de la nang gzugs su 'du shes pa'i phyi rol gyi gzugs chung du kha dog mdzes pa dang kha dog mi sdug pa dang ngan pa dang bzang po rnams la lta zhing gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zil gyis mnan nas mthong ste /
idaṃ prathamamabhibhvāyatanam / adhyātmaṃ rūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyatyadhimātrāṇi suvarṇadurvarṇāni vistareṇa yāvattayā ca saṃjñī bhavati
# de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur ba 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched dang po'o / / nang gzugs su 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs chen po kha dog mdzes pa dang kha dog mi sdug pa dang ngan pa dang bzang po rnams la lta zhing gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zin gyis mnan nas mthong ste /
idaṃ dvitīyamabhibhvāyatanam / ityete dve abhibhvāyatane rūpī rūpāṇi paśyatītyetasmādvimokṣādabhinirhriyete
# de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur ba 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched gnyis pa'o zhes bya ba zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched 'di gnyis ni gzugs can gzugs rnams la lta pa'o zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa de las 'byung ngo /
adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyati parīttāni vistareṇa yāvattathāsaṃjñī ca bhavati
# nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs chung ngu kha dog mdzes pa dang kha dog mi sdug pa dang ngan pa dang bzang po rnams la lta zhing gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zil gyis mnan nas mthong ste /
idaṃ tṛtīyamabhibhvāyatanam / adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyatyadhimātrāṇi yathā tathāsaṃjñī ca bhavati / idaṃ caturthamabhibhvāyatanam / ityete dve abhibhvāyatane adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyatītyeta smādvimokṣādabhinirhriyete
# de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur ba 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched gsum pa'o / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs chen po kha dog mdzes pa dang kha dog mi sdug pa dang ngan pa dang bzang po rnams la lta zhing gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zil gyis mnan nas mthong ste / / de lta bur 'du shes par gyur pa 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched bzhi pa'o zhes bya ba zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched 'di gnyis ni nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs rnams la lta zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa de las 'byung ngo /
evaṃ kṛtvā dvābhyāṃ vimokṣābhyāṃ catvāryabhibhvāyatanāni veditavyāni / adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyati nīlāni nīlavarṇāni nīlanidarśanāni nīlanirbhāsāni / tadyathā umakāpuṣpaṃ saṃpannaṃ vā vārāṇasīyakaṃ vastraṃ nīlaṃ nīlavarṇa nīlanidarśanaṃ nīlanirbhāsamevamevādhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyati nīlāni yāvannīlanirbhāsāni tāni khalu rūpāṇyabhibhūya jānātyābhibhūya paśyati tathāsaṃjñī ca bhavati
# de ltar na zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched bzhi ni rnam par thar pa gnyis kyis rig par bya'o / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs sngon po / / kha dog sngon po / / sngon po lta bur ston pa / / 'od sngon po 'byung ba rnams la lta ste / / dper na zar ma'i me tog gam yul w'a r'a na s'ir byas pa'i ras phun sum tshogs pa sngon po / / kha dog sngon po / / sngon po lta bur ston pa / / 'od sngon po 'byung ba de bzhin du nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs sngon po / / kha dog sngon po / / sngon po lta bur ston pa / / 'od sngon po 'byung ba rnams la lta zhing gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zil gyi sa mnan nas mthong ste / / de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur ba 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched lnga pa'o / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs ser pa'o /
idaṃ pañcamamabhibhvāyatanam / adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyati pītāni yāvatpītanirbhāsāni / tadyathā karṇikārapuṣpaṃ saṃpannaṃ vā vārāṇasīyakaṃ vastraṃ pītaṃ pītavarṇamiti vistaraḥ / idaṃ ṣaṣṭhamabhibhvāyatanam / adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyati lohitāni yāvallohitanirbhāsāni / tadyathā bandhujīvakapuṣpaṃ saṃpannaṃ vā vārāṇasīyaṃ vastraṃ lohitaṃ lohitavarṇamiti vistaraḥ / idaṃ saptamamabhibhvāyatanam / adhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyatyavadātānyavadātavarṇānyavadātanidarśanānyavadātanirbhāsāni / tadyathā uṣasi tārakāyā varṇaṃ saṃpannaṃ vā vārāṇasīyakaṃ vastramavadātamavadātavarṇamavadātanidarśanamavadātanirbhāsamevamevādhyātmamarūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyatya vadātānyavadātavarṇānyavadātanidarśanānyavadātanirbhāsāni tāni khalu rūpāṇyabhibhūya jānātyabhibhūya paśyati tathāsaṃjñī ca bhavati / idamaṣṭamamabhibhvāyatanam
# kha dog ser po / / ser po lta bur ston pa / / 'od ser po 'byung ba rnams la lta ste / / dper na dong ka'i me tog gam / / yul w'a r'a na s'i'i ras phun sum tshogs pa ser po / / kha dog ser po / / ser po lta bur ston pa / / 'od ser po 'byung ba de bzhin du nang gi gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs ser po / / kha dog ser po / / ser po lta bur ston pa / / 'od ser po 'byung ba rnams la lta zhing / / gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zil gyis mnan nas mthong ste / / de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur ba 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched drug pa'o / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs dmar po / / kha dog dmar po / / dmar po lta bur ston pa / / 'od dmar po 'byung ba rnams la lta ste / / dper na ban du dzi ba ka'i me tog gam / / yul w'a r'a na s'i'i ras phun sum tshogs pa dmar po / / kha dog dmar po / / dmar po lta bur ston pa / / 'od dmar po 'byung ba de bzhin du / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs dmar po kha dog dmar po / / dmar po lta bur ston pa / / 'od dmar po 'byung ba rnams la lta zhing / / gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zil gyis mnan nas mthong ste / / de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur pa 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched bdun pa'o / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs dkar po / / kha dog dkar po / / dkar po lta bur ston pa / / 'od dkar po 'byung ba rnams la lta ste / / dper na skar ma pa wa sangs kyi mdog gam / / yul w'a r'a na s'i'i ras phun sum tshogs pa dkar po / / kha dog dkar po / / dkar po lta bur ston pa / / 'od dkar po 'byung ba de bzhin du / / nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs dkar po / / kha dog dkar po / / dkar po lta bur ston pa / / 'od dkar po 'byung ba rnams la lta zhing gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zil gyis mnan nas mthong ste / / de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur pa 'di ni zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched brgyad pa'o zhes bya ba 'di bzhi ni sdug ba'i rnam par thar pa lus kyis mngon sum du byas te /
etāni catvāri śubhaṃ vimokṣaṃ kāyena sākṣātkṛtvopasaṃpadya viharatītyetasmādvimokṣādabhinirhriyate / tatra vimokṣairālaṃbanamadhimucyate parīttādikam abhibhvāyatanaistvabhibhavati tadantardhānādyatheṣṭaṃ vā karaṇādvaśavartamānatāmupādāya
# rdzogs par byas nas gnas so zhes bya ba'i rnam par thar pa de las 'byung ngo / / de la rnam par thar pa rnams kyis ni dmigs pa chung du la sogs pa la mos par byed do / / zil gyis gnon pa rnams kyis ni dbang byed pa'i phyir zil gyis gnon te / / de'i nang du 'dus par byed pa dang ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du byed pa'i phyir ro /
tatra parīttāni rūpāṇi sattvasaṃkhyātānyalpapramāṇatvāt
# de la gzugs chung du rnams ni sems can du gtogs pa ste / / chung ba'i phyir ro /
adhimātrāṇyasattvasaṃkhyātāni gṛhavimānaparvatādīni mahāpramāṇatvāt
# chen po ni sems can ma yin par gtogs pa ste / / khang pa dang gzhal med khang dang ri la sogs pa rgya che ba'i phyir ro /
suvarṇadurvarṇāni śubhāśubhavarṇasaṃgṛhītāni / hīnapraṇītāni mānuṣyakadivyāni yathākramam
# kha dog mdzes pa dang kha dog mi sdug pa ni kha dog sdug pa dang kha dog mi sdug pa las bsdus pa rnams so / / mi'i dang lha rnams ni bzang po dang ngan pa rnams te / / go rims bzhin no /
tāni khalu rūpāṇyabhibhūyeti vaśe vartayitvā / jānātīti śamathamārgeṇa
# gzugs de dag zil gyis mnan nas shes zhes bya ba ni dbang bsgyur nas so zhes bya ba ni zhi gnas kyi lam gyis so /
paśyatīti vipaśyanāmārgeṇa
# mthong zhes bya ba ni lhag mthong gi lam gyis so /
tathāsaṃjñī ca bhavatītyabhibhūte nābhibhūte vā tannirabhimānasaṃjñitāmupādāya
# de lta bur 'du shes par 'gyur ba zhes bya ba ni zil gyis mnan tam / / zil gyis ma mnan kyang rung ste / / de la mngon pa'i nga rgyal med pa'i 'du shes can gyi phyir ro /
nīlānītyuddeśapadam / nīlavarṇāni sahajāṃ nīlatāmupādāya
# sngon po zhes bya ba ni bstan pa'i tshig go / / kha dog sngon po zhes bya ba ni lhan cig skyes ba'i sngo ba nyid kyi phyir ro /
nīlanidarśanāni saṃyoganīlatāmupādāya / nīlanirbhāsāni tadubhayoḥ prabhānirmokṣabhāsvaratāmupādāya
# sngon po lta bur ston pa zhes bya ba ni sbyar ba las gyur pa'i sngo ba nyid kyi phyir ro / / 'od sngon po 'byung ba rnams zhes bya ba 'di ni de gnyi ga las 'od 'byung ba rnams 'od gsal ba nyid kyi phyir ro /
yathā nīlānyevaṃ pītalohitāvadātāni vistareṇa veditavyāni
# sngon po la ji lta ba de bzhin du ser po dang dmar po dang dkar po rnams la yang rgya cher rig par bya'o /
dṛṣṭāntadvayaṃ caikaikasmin sahajasāṃyogikavarṇodbhāvanatāmupādāya / aparaḥ paryāyastadyathā nīlamiti puṣpavastrayoḥ samānamuddeśapadam / nīlavarṇamiti puṣpamevādhikṛtya tasya sāṃyogikanīlatvasaṃbhavāt
# dpe gnyis po re re la yang lhan cig skyes pa dang sbyar ba las byung ba'i kha dog brjod pa'i phyir ro / / 'di lta ste / / sngon po zhes bya ba ni me tog dang ras gnyi ga la mtshungs par bstan pa'i tshig go / / kha dog sngon po zhes bya ba ni me tog nyid kyi dbang du byas pa ste / / de lhan cig skyes pa'i sngon po yin pa'i phyir ro / / sngon po lta bur ston pa zhes bya ba ni ras kyi dbang du byas pa ste / / de la sbyor ba las gyur pa'i sngon po nyid yod pa'i phyir ro /
nīlanirbhāsamityucyate puṣpavastre adhikṛtya dvayorapi bhāsvaratvasaṃbhavāt
# 'od sngon po 'byung bzhes bya ba ni me tog dang ras gnyi ga'i dbang du byas pa ste / / gnyi ga la yang 'od gsal ba nyid yod pa'i phyir ro /
ityevaṃ kṛtvā dṛṣṭānte 'pi tadyathomakāpuṣpaṃ saṃpannaṃ vā vārāṇasīyakaṃ vastraṃ nīlaṃ nīlavarṇamityevamādinirdeśa upapanno bhavati
# de ltar byas na dper na zar ma'i me tog dang yul w'a r'a na s'i'i ras phun sum tshogs pa sngon po kha dog sngon po zhes bya ba la sogs pa bstan pa'i dpe yang 'thad par 'gyur ro /
evaṃ pītādikaṃ yojayitavyam
# de bzhin du ser po la sogs pa la yang sbyar bar bya'o /
śiṣṭaṃ yathādhimokṣeṣu / kiṃ śiṣṭam / adhyātmaṃ rūpasaṃjñī bahirdhā rūpāṇi paśyatītyevamādi
# lhag ma ni rnam par thar pa las byung ba ji lta ba bzhin no zhes bya ba la lhag ma gang zhe na / / nang gzugs su 'du shes pas phyi rol gyi gzugs rnams mthong ba zhes bya ba la sogs pa ste /
tatpunaryathā rūpī rūpāṇi paśyatītyevamādi nirdeśānusāreṇa draṣṭavyam
# de ni gzugs can gzugs rnams la lta ba zhes ji skad bstan pa'i tshul bzhin du blta bar bya'o /
evamabhibhvāyatanairālaṃbanaṃ vaśe vartayitvā kṛtsnāyatanaiḥ kṛtsnaṃ spharati samantānantā paryantaṃ vistārayatītyarthaḥ
# ji ltar zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched rnams kyis dmigs pa la dbang bsgyur nas zad par gyi skye mched rnams kyis zad par rgyas par byed de / / kun du mtha' yas pa khyab par byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tāni punaḥ kṛtsnāyatanāni daśa bhavanti / tadyathā pṛthivīkṛtsnamapkṛtsnaṃ tejaḥkṛtsnaṃ vāyukṛtsnaṃ pītakṛtsnaṃ lohitakṛtsnamavadātakṛtsnamākāśānantyāyatanakṛtsnaṃ vijñānānantyāyatanakṛtsnaṃ ca
# zad par gyi skye mched de dag ni bcu yin te / / zad par sa dang zad par chu dang zad par med dang zad par rlung dang zad par sngon po dang zad par ser po dang zad par dmar po dang zad par dkar po dang zad par nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched dang zad par rnam shes mtha' yas skye mched do /
kṛtsnāyataneṣu pṛthivyādīni yadi na vyavasthāpyeran tenāśrayamahābhūtairvinā tadupādāyarūpaṃ nīlādiakaṃ spharituṃ na śakyeta
# zad par gyi skye mched rnams la sa la sogs pa rnam par mi gzhag na ni des na gnas 'byung ba chen po rnams la rgyur byas ba'i gzugs sngon po la sogs pa des khyab par byed mi nus pa ste /
tasyāśrayasya rūpasya spharaṇasamṛddhimupādāyaiṣāṃ kṛtsneṣu vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# de bas na gnas dang bcas ba'i gzugs la khyab par bya ba 'byor pa nyid kyi phyir / / de dag ni zad par la rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
śeṣaṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vimokṣavadākāśānantyāyatanakṛtsnādi / tatra vimokṣairārambhaḥ abhibhvāyataneḥ prayogaḥ kṛtsnāyatanaiḥ pariniṣpattirvimokṣāṇāṃ veditavyāḥ
# lhag ma ni rnam par thar pa bzhin du ji ltar mthun mthun du sbyar bar bya'o zhes bya ba ni zad par nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched la sogs pa'o / / de la rnam par thar pa rnams kyis ni rnam par thar pa rnams rtsom mo / / zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched rnams kyis ni sbyor ro / / zad par gyi skye mched rnams kyis ni yongs su grub par rig par bya'o / / bam po dgu pa /
araṇā vihārī yeṣāṃ sattvānāmābhāsaṃ gantukāmo bhavati teṣāmātmani kleśasamudācāramadhikṛtyānāgatavṛttāntaṃ vihāragata eva praṇidhijñāna balenāvalokya tathā tatsamīpamupasaṃkrāmati na vā yathā te tatrānunayapratidherṣyāmātsaryādikaṃ kleśopakleśasaraṇaṃ notpādayanti
# nyon mongs pa med par gnas pa ni sems can gang dag gi mig lam du snang bar 'dod pa de dag bdag la nyon mongs pa kun du mi 'byung ba'i rnam pa'i dbang du byas nas 'dug bzhin du bsams nas shes pa'i dbang gis ma 'ongs pa na 'byung ba la lta ste / / de ltar de'i drung du 'gro yang rung mi 'gro yang rung ci nas der de dag la rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba dang phrag dog dang ser sna la sogs pa'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dang 'thab rtsod mi skyed do /
ata idamucyate 'raṇā dhyānaṃ niśritya kleśotpattyanurakṣāvihārasamṛddhāviti vistaraḥ
# de'i phyir nyon mongs pa med pa ni bsam gtan la brten nas gzhan gyi nyon mongs pa 'byung ba rjes su srung bar gnas pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes rgya cher 'byung ba de skad ces bya ba'o /
praṇidhijñānaṃ tallābhī yadyadeva traiyadhvikādikajñeyavṛttāntaṃ jñātukāmobhavati tatra tatra mānasaṃ praṇidhāyedaṃ jānīyāmiti dhyānaṃ samāpadyate tato vyutthitasya tatpraṇidhānaṃ samṛdhyati tajjñeyaṃ jānātītyarthaḥ
# bsams nas zhes bya ba ni de thob pa gal te dus gsum pa la sogs pa'i shes bya'i rnam pa de nyid shes par 'dod par gyur na de dang der 'di shes par 'gyur bar bya'o zhes bsams nas bsam gtan la snyoms par 'jug cing de las langs nas de'i smon pa 'grub par 'gyur te / / shes bya de ni shes so zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
dharmapratisaṃvit paryāyeṣu tadyathāvidyādīnārabhyājñānamadarśanamanabhisamaya ityevamādiṣvavyāghātasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiriti vistaraḥ
# chos so so yang dag par rig pa ni rnam grangs su gtogs pa rnams la 'di lta ste / / ma rig pa la sogs pa la brtsams nas mi shes pa dang mi mthong ba dang mngon par mi rtogs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa la thogs pa med par yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin zhes bya ba la sogs pa rgya cher 'byung ba'o /
arthapratisaṃvitsvasāmānyalakṣaṇe dharmāṇām arthāntarādyabhiprāye cāvyāghātasamṛddhāviti vistaraḥ
# don so so yang dag par rig pa ni / / chos rnams kyi rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid dang don gzhan la sogs pa la dgongs pa la thogs pa med par yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes rgya cher 'byung ba'o /
niruktipratisaṃvijjanapadabhāṣāyāmiti prativiṣayaṃ yathāsvamanyonyasaṃjñāntarānuvyavahāre dharmanirvacane ceti tadyathā lujyate pralujyate tasmāllokaḥ rūpyate tasmādrūpa ityevamādike
# nges pa'i tshig so so yang dag par rig pa la yul mi'i skad ces bya ba ni yul so so bas ji ltar rang rang gis gzhan dang gzhan ming gzhan gyi tha snyad 'dogs pa'o / / chos kyi nges pa'i tshig la zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste /
pratibhānapratisaṃviddharmaprabhedeṣviti dravyasantaḥ prajñaptisantaḥ saṃvṛtisantaḥ paramārthasanta ityevamādiṣu / ṛddhayabhijñā vicitraddhivikuvitasamṛddhāviti tadyathā eko bhūtvā bahudhā bhavatītyevamādau / vicitrāṇāṃ śabdānāmanuśravasamṛddhāviti divyamānuṣyakādīnām
# 'jig pa dang rab tu 'jig pas de'i phyir 'jig rten zhes bya ba dang gzugs su rung bas de'i phyir gzugs zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / spobs pa so so yang dag par rig pa ni rdzas su yod pa'o / / btags pa'i yod pa'o / / kun rdzob tu yod pa'o / / don dam par yod pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa chos rab tu 'byed pa'o / / rdzu 'phrul gyi mngon par shes pa la rdzu 'phrul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes bya ba ni 'di lta ste gcig tu gyur nas mang por gyur zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / sgra sna tshogs nyan pa yang dag par 'byor pa zhes bya ba ni lha dang mi'i la sogs pa'o /
parasattveṣu cittacaritapraveśasamṛddhāviti sarāgādicittapracārayathābhūtajñānasamṛddhāvityarthaḥ / pūrvāntacaryāyā anusmaraṇasamṛddhāvityatītaṃ janmaparaṃparāmārabhya nāmajātigotrādiprakāravṛttāyā ityarthaḥ
# sems can gzhan dag gi sems can gyi spyod pa la 'jug pa yang dag par 'byor pa zhes bya ba ni 'dod chags dang bcas pa la sogs pa'i sems kyi rgyu ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / sngon gyi mtha'i spyod pa rjes su dran pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes bya ba ni 'das pa'i tshe rabs gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa las brtsams te / / ming dang rigs dang rus la sogs pa'i rnam pa'i lo drung shes zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
cyutyutpādābhijñā divyena cakṣuṣā sattvānāṃ cyavamānānāmupapadyamānānāṃ suvarṇānāṃ durvarṇānāṃ sugatimapi gacchatāṃ durgatimapyaparāntamārabhya cyutyupapādasaṃdarśanasamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ / āsravakṣayajñāna samṛddhāviti yenopāyenāsravāḥ parikṣoyante yaścaiṣāṃ parikṣayastajjñānaniṣpattinimittamityarthaḥ
# 'chi 'pho dang skye ba mngon par shes pa ni lha'i mig gis sems can 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba dang kha dog bzang po dang kha dog ngan pa dang bde 'gror 'gro ba dang ngan 'gror 'gro ba dang phyi ma'i mtha' las brtsams te / / 'chi 'pho dang skye ba mthong ba yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o / / zag pa zad pa shes pa yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba ni thabs gang gis zag pa rnams yongs su zad pa dang de dag yongs su zad pa gang yin pa de shes pa 'grub pa'i rgyu zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
lakṣaṇānuvyañjanāni yatsamādhiprajñādhipatyena buddhā bhagavanto dvātriṃśatā lakṣaṇairaśītyānuvyañjanaiḥ vibhrājamānaṃ rūpakāyaṃ saṃdarśayanti vineyānām
# mtshan dang dpe byang bzang po rnams ni gang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi dbang gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis dang dpe byad bzang po brgyad cus rnam par mdzes pa'i gzugs kyi skus 'dul ba rnams la kun du ston to /
tatsvabhāvāni tāni teṣāṃ veditavyāni dharmakāyaprabhāvitatvādbuddhānāṃ bhagavatāmiti
# de dag gi de dag ni de'i rang bzhin du rig par bya ste / / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi skus rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
bodhisattvānāṃ tu tathāsaṃdarśanasamarthānāṃ samādhiprajñāsvabhāvāni
# byang chub sems dpa' de ltar ston nus pa rnams kyang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi rang bzhin no /
tadanyeṣāṃ parṣanmaṇḍaleṣūpapannānāṃ tatsamutthitavipākasvabhāvāni veditavyāni
# nga la gzhan pa 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dag tu skyes pa rnams ni de las byung ba'i rnam par smin pa'i rang bzhin du rig par bya'o /
catasraḥ sarvakārāḥ pariśuddhayo buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ mahābhijñāprāptānāṃ ca bodhisattvānām / tatra yathākāmamāśrayasyopādānasthānaparityāgānāṃ samṛddhāviti yatrecchati tatropapattigrahaṇataḥ tasyāṃ copapattāvāyuḥsaṃskārānadhiṣṭhāya yāvadicchamavasthānataḥ yadecchati tadāyuḥsaṃskārotsarjanataśca yathākramam
# sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' mngon par shes pa chen po thob pa rnams kyi rnam pa thams cad yongs su dag pa ni bzhi ste / / de la ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du gnas len ba dang bzhugs pa dang yongs su gtong ba yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes bya ba ni gang du bzhed pa der skye ba 'dzin pa dang der skyes nas kyang tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs te ji srid bzhed par bzhugs pa dang gang gi tshe bzhed pa de'i dus na tshe de'i 'du byed 'der ba ste / / go rims bzhin no /
yathākāmamālaṃbanamadhikṛtya nirmāṇapariṇāmanajñānānāṃ samṛddhāvityapūrvarūpādinirmāṇataḥ pūrvotpannānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ suvarṇāditvena pariṇāmataḥ sarvaprakārāvagamanataśca yathākramam
# ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du dmigs pa'i dbang du mdzad pa'i sprul pa dang sgyur ba dang mkhyen pa yang dag par 'byor pa dang zhes bya ba ni sngon ma byung ba'i gzugs la sogs pa sprul pa dang sngon byung ba'i gzugs la sogs pa gser la sogs par bsgyur ba dang rnam pa thams cad du thugs su chud pa'i phyir de go rims bzhin no /
yathākāmaṃ samādhimukhavaśavartisamṛddhāviti pratikṣaṇaṃ yatheṣṭamaparimitasamādhyantarasamāpattaye
# ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo la dbang sgyur ba yang dag par 'byor ba'i zhes bya ba ni skad cig re re la ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du ting nge 'dzin gzhan dpag tu med pa la snyoms par 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
yathākāmaṃ dhāraṇīmukhasaṃdhāraṇasamṛddhāviti dvācatvāriṃśato 'kṣarāṇāmanyatamākṣaramanasikāre tadādisarvadharmaparyāyābhilapanasāmarthyapratilambhāyetyarthaḥ
# ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du gzungs kyi sgo kun du 'dzin pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes bya ba ni yi ge bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis las yi ge gang yang rung ba yid la byed pa na des thog ma kho nar chos kyi rnam grangs thams cad brjod nus pa thob pa'i phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / stobs ni bcu ste /
daśa balāni sthānāsthānajñānabalaṃ karmasvakajñānabalaṃ dhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpattijñānabalamindriyaparāparajñānabalaṃ nānādhimuktijñānabalaṃ nānādhātujñānabalaṃ sarvatragāminīpratipajjñānabalaṃ pūrvanivāsānusmṛtijñānabalaṃ cyutyupapādajñānabalamāsravakṣayajñānabalaṃ ca / tatra sthānāsthānajñānabalaṃ dhyānaṃ niśritya sarvaprakārahetvahetujñānāsaṃgāpratihatasaṃmukhībhāve samādhyādayaḥ / evaṃ karmasvakajñānabalādiṣu sarvākārakarmasvakatājñānāsaṃgāpratihatasaṃmukhībhāva iti yojayitavyam
# gnas dang gnas ma yin pa mkhyen pa'i stobs dang las bdag gir bya ba mkhyen pa'i stobs dang / / bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa mkhyen pa'i stobs dang dbang po mchog dang mchog ma yin pa mkhyen pa'i stobs dang mos pa sna tshogs mkhyen pa'i stobs dang khams sna tshogs mkhyen pa'i stobs dang thams cad du 'gro ba'i lam mkhyen pa'i stobs dang sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa'i mkhyen pa'i stobs dang shi 'pho ba dang skye ba mkhyen pa'i stobs dang zag pa zad pa mkhyen pa'i stobs so / / gnas dang gnas ma yin pa mkhyen pa'i stobs ni bsam gtan la brten nas rgyu dang rgyu ma yin pa rnam pa thams cad du mkhyen pa chags pa med cing thogs pa med pa mngon du gyur pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o /
catvāri vaiśāradyāni samyaksaṃbuddhasya vata me sata ime te dharmā anabhisaṃbuddhā ityatra māṃ kaścicchramaṇo vā devo vā māro vā brahmā vā sahadharmeṇa codayedvā smārayedvā nimittamapi na samanupaśyāmyetacca nimittamasamanupaśyan kṣemaprāptaśca vaiśāradyaprāptaścodāramārṣabhaṃ sthānaṃ prajānāmi brahmacaryaṃ pravartayāmi pariṣadi samyak siṃhanādaṃ nadāmi / kṣīṇāsravasya vata me sata ime āsravā aparikṣīṇā iti / ye vā punarme śrāvakāṇāmantarāyikā dharmā ākhyātāḥ tān pratiṣevamānasya nālamantarāyāteti yo vā punarme śrāvakāṇāṃ niryāṇāya mārga ākhyāta āryonairyāṇiko nairvedhikaḥ sa vata na samyaṅniryāti tatkarasya samyagduḥkhakṣayāya duḥkhasyāntakriyāyai ityatra māṃ kaścit śramaṇo vā brāhmaṇo vā yāvatsiṃhanādaṃ nadāmīti vistareṇaikaikasmin vaktavyam
# de bzhin du las bdag gir bya ba mkhyen pa'i stobs la sogs pa la yang rnam pa thams cad du de mkhyen pa chags pa med cing thogs pa med pa mngon du gyur pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa zhes bya bar sbyar bar bya'o / / mi 'jigs pa ni bzhi ste / / nga mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so zhes bya ba 'di la chos 'di dag mngon par rdzogs par sangs ma rgyas so zhes dge sbyong dang bra ma ze 'am / / lha 'am / / bdud dam / / tshangs pa'am / / sus kyang chos dang mthun par nga la rgol ba'am / / drod bar byed pa'i mtshan ma mi mthong ste / / mtshan ma de mi mthong bas bde ba thob mi 'jigs pa thob bag tsha ba med pa thob nas gnas so / / khyu mchog gi gnas rgya chen por zhal gyis 'che'o / / tshangs pa'i 'khor lo bskor ro / / 'khor gyi nang du seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrog go / / nga zag pa zad do zhes bya ba la zag ba 'di dag yongs su ma zad do / / zhes bya ba dang ngas nyan thos rnams la bar du gcod pa'i chos gang dag bstan pa de dag bsten kyang bar du gcad par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya ba dang yang ngas nyan thos rnams la nges bar 'byung bar bya ba'i phyir / / 'phags pa nges par 'byin pa des par 'byung pa'i lam gang bshad pa de nges par 'byung ba ma yin no zhe'am / / de byed pa'i sdug bsngal yang dag par zad par 'gyur ba dang sdug bsngal gyi tha ma byed par mi 'gyur ro zhes 'di la dge sbyong ngam sus kyang nga la zhes bya ba nas seng ge'i sgra yang dag par sgrog ces bya ba'i bar du rgya cher re re la yang brjod par bya'o /
tānyetāni vaiśāradyāni svārthaṃ parārthaṃ cārabhya veditavyāni
# mi 'jigs pa bzhi po 'di dag ni rang gi don dang gzhan gyi don las brtsam par rig par bya'o /
tatra dvividhaḥ svārthaḥ jñānaviśeṣaḥ prahāṇaviśeṣaśca
# de la rang gi don ni rnam pa gnyis te / / ye shes kyi khyad par dang spangs pa'i khyad par ro /
dvividhaḥ parārthaḥ vipakṣadharmavivarjanaṃ pratipakṣadharmaniṣevaṇaṃ ca
# gzhan gyi don yang rnam pa gnyis te / / mi mthun pa'i chos yongs su spang ba dang gnyen po'i chos la brten pa'o /
tatrābhisaṃbodhivaiśāradyaṃ jñānātmakaṃ svārthamevārabhya sarvākāraṃ mayā saprabhedaparyantaṃ jñeyamabhisaṃbuddhamityetasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ samyaṅniranuyojyatvena sarvasmin loke pratiṣṭhāpanasamṛddhau yaḥ samādhiriti pūrvavat
# de la mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa la mi 'jigs pa ni ye shes kyi bdag nyid de rang gi don la brtsams nas rnam pa thams cad du ngas rab tu dbye ba'i mtha' dang bcas par shes par bya ba mngon par sangs rgyas so zhes zhal gyis 'che ba ste / / yang dag par rgol ba med par 'jig rten thams cad du 'jog pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin gang yin pa zhes bya ba snga ma bzhin no /
evaṃ śeṣāṇyapi vaiśāradyāni yojayitavyāni
# mi 'jigs pa lhag ma rnams kyang de bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o /
sarvākārāḥ punarāsravāḥ savāsanāḥ kleśā draṣṭavyāḥ
# zag pa'i rnam pa thams cad ces bya ba ni bag chags dang bcas pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams su rig par bya'o /
sarvākārā antarāyikā dharmāḥ sarve sāṃkleśikāḥ vipakṣadharmā draṣṭavyāḥ
# bar du gcod pa'i chos rnam pa thams cad ces bya ba ni mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi chos kun nas nyon mongs pa thams cad du rig par bya'o /
sarvākāro nairyāṇiko mārgaḥ prayogamārgamārabhya yāvanniṣṭhāmārgo draṣṭavyaḥ
# nges par 'byin pa'i lam gyi rnam pa thams cad ces bya ba ni sbyor ba nas bzung ste / / mthar phyin pa'i lam gyi bar du rig par bya'o /
trīṇyāveṇikāni smṛtyupasthānāni / iha śāstā śrāvakāṇāṃ dharmaṃ deśayatyanukampakaḥ kāruṇiko 'rthakāmo hitaiṣī karuṇāyamānaḥ idaṃ vo bhikṣavo hitāya idaṃ sukhāya idaṃ hitasukhāyeti / tasya te śrāvakāḥ śuśrūṣante śrotramavadadhatyājñācittamupasthāpayanti pratipadyante dharmasyānudharmam
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa gsum ni 'di la ston pa thugs brtse ba can thugs rje dang ldan pa / / don bzhed pa / / phan par bzhed pa / / thugs rje can nyan thos rnams la dge slong dag 'di ni phan par 'gyur ba'o / / 'di ni bde bar 'gyur ba'o / / 'di ni phan pa dang bde bar 'gyur ba'o zhes chos ston pa 'di la nyan thos de dag gus par nyan pa dang rna ba gtod pa dang kun shes pa'i sems nye bar 'jog pa dang chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa de la de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes par mi 'gyur /
tatra tathāgatasya na nāndī bhavati na saumanasyaṃ na cetasa utplāvitatvamupekṣakastatra tathāgato viharati smṛtaḥ saṃprajānan / idaṃ prathamāveṇikaṃ smṛtyupasthānam
# yid bde bar mi 'gyur / / thugs dga' ba ya ya por mi 'gyur gyi btang snyoms can du de bzhin gshes pa de la gnas te / / dran pa dang shes bzhin dang ldan pa 'di ni ma 'dres pa'i dran pa nye bar gzhag pa dang po ste /
yadāryaḥ sevate yadāryaḥ sevamāno 'rhati gaṇamanuśāsitum
# gang 'phags pa bsten nas kyang 'khor la rjes su bstan par 'os pa'o /
punaraparaṃ śāstā śrāvakāṇāṃ dharmaṃ deśayati yāvadidaṃ hitasukhāya
# gzhan yang ston pa 'di ni phan pa dang bde bar 'gyur ba'o zhes bya ba'i bar du chos ston pa de la nyon thos de dag gus par mi nyan pa nas /
tasya te śrāvakā na śuśrūṣante yāvanna pratipadyante dharmasyānudharmam
# chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos mi sgrub ba'i bar de la de bzhin gshegs pa kun nas mnar sems su mi 'gyur / / mi bzod par mi 'gyur /
tatra tathāgatasya nāghāto bhavati nākṣāntirnāpratyayo na cetaso 'nabhirāddhirupekṣakastatreti vistaraḥ / idaṃ dvitīyam
# thugs mi ches par mi 'gyur / / thugs mi mnyes par mi 'gyur gyi btang snyoms can du de la zhes bya ba rgya cher sbyar te 'di ni gnyis pa'o /
tṛtīye 'yaṃ viśeṣaḥ asyaike śrāvakāḥ śuśrūṣante yāvatpratipadyante dharmasyānudharmameke na śuśrūṣante yāvanna pratipadyante dharmasyānudharmam / tatra tathāgatasya na nāndo bhavati yāvaccetaso nābhirāddhiriti
# gsum pa'i bye brag ni 'di yin te / / de la nyan thos kha cig gus par nyan pa nas chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub par byed pa dang kha cig gus par mi nyan pa nas chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos mi sgrub pa'i bar de la de bzhin gshegs par dgyes par mi 'gyur ba nas thugs mi mnyen par mi 'gyur ba'i bar du'o /
etāni trīṇi smṛtyupasthānāni śāsturgaṇaparikarṣaṇe yathākramaṃ sarvākārānunayapratighatadubhayasaṃkleśavāsanāyā asamudācārasamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa gsum po 'di dag ni ston pa'i tshogs yongs su sdud pa la go rims bzhin du rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba dang de gnyi ga'i kun nas nyon mongs pa dang bag chags kyi rnam pa thams cad kun du mi 'byung ba yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o /
trīṇyarakṣāṇi / pariśuddhakāyasamudācārastathāgataḥ
# bsrung ba med ba gsum ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i phrin las kyi spyod pa yongs su dag pa ste /
nāsti tathāgatasyāpariśuddhakāyasamudācāratā yāṃ tathāgataḥ praticchādayitavyāṃ manyeta kaccinme pare vijānīyuriti
# de bzhin gshegs pa la sku'i phrin las yongs su ma dag pa med de / / bdag la gzhan gyis shes su 'ong ngo zhes bcab par dgongs pa med pa dang de bzhin du gsung dang thugs kyi phrin las la yang rig par bya'o /
evaṃ vāṅmanaḥsamudācārate veditavye
# de dag gi tha snyad gdags su med par dogs pa mi mda' ba'i phyir /
ebhirnirvaktavyatayā nirāśaṅkatvātsvayaṃ śāstuvineyajanaparikarṣaṇamārabhya yatheṣṭaṃ nigṛhya prasajyāvavādānuśāsanīprayogaḥ samṛddhayatīti veditavyam
# ston pa nyid kyis gdul ba'i skye bo sdug pa las brtsams te / / ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du tshar bcad de spa bkod nas gdams pa dang rjes su bstan pa la sbyor ba yang dag par 'byor par rig par bya'o /
asaṃmoṣadharmatā sarvavineyakāryamārabhya yathāvatkṛtasya bhāṣitasya cābhilapanasamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ
# bsnyel ba med pa'i chos nyid ni gdul ba'i bya ba thams cad las brtsams te / / ji lta ba bzhin du mdzad pa dang gsungs pa'i rnam pa thams cad mngon par brjod pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o /
vāsanāsamudghātaḥ sarvajñasya sataḥ kleśajñeyāvaraṇaśeṣasūcakānāṃ kāyavākceṣṭitānāmasamudācārasamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ
# bag chags yang dag par bcom pa ni thams cad mkhyen par gyur nas nyon mongs pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa'i lhag ma yod pa ston pa'i sku dang gsung gi g yo ba kun du mi 'byung ba yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o /
mahākaruṇā traidhātukāvacareṣu sarvasattveṣu nirantarasarvaprakāraduḥkhālaṃbana karuṇāvihārasamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ
# thugs rje chen po ni khams gsum na spyod pa'i sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa thams cad la dmigs pa'i thugs rje la gnas pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o /
aṣṭādaśāveṇikā buddhadharmāstadyathā nāsti tathāgatasya skhalitam nāsti ravitam nāsti muṣitā smṛtiḥ nāstyasamāhitaṃ cittam nāsti nānātvasaṃjñā nāstya pratisaṃkhyāyopekṣā nāsti chandaparihāṇiḥ nāsti vīryaparihāṇiḥ nāsti smṛtiparihāṇiḥ nāsti samādhiparihāṇiḥ nāsti prajñārihāṇiḥ nāsti vimuktiparihāṇiḥ sarvaṃ tathāgatasya kāyakarma jñānapūrvagamaṃ jñānānuparivarti sarvaṃ vākkarma jñānapūrvagamaṃ jñānānuparivarti sarvaṃ manaskarma jñānapūrvagamaṃ jñānānuparivarti atīte 'dhvanyasaṅgamapratihataṃ jñānam anāgate 'dhvanyasaṅgamapratihataṃ jñānam pratyutpanne 'dhvanyasaṅgamapratihataṃ jñānamiti / eṣāṃ punarvyavasthānam tadyathā arhan bhikṣuḥ kṣīṇāsravaḥ grāmaṃ piṇḍāya carannekadā caṇḍena hastinā sārgha samāgacchati
# sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa ni bco brgyad de / / 'di lta ste de bzhin gshegs pa la 'khrul pa med pa dang ca co med pa dang bsnyel ba med pa dang sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa med pa dang tha dad pa'i 'du shes med pa dang so sor ma brtags pa'i btang snyoms med pa dang 'dun pa nyams pa med pa dang brtson 'grus nyams pa med pa dang dran pa nyams pa med pa dang ting nge 'dzin nyams pa med pa dang shes rab nyams pa med pa dang rnam par grol ba nyams pa med pa dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i lus kyi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang ngag gi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang yid kyi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba dang 'das pa'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes dang ma 'ongs pa'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes dang da ltar byung ba'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes so /
yathā caṇḍena hastinevaṃ caṇḍanāśvena caṇḍayā gavā caṇḍena kukkureṇa / gahanaṃ vā kaṇṭakabāṭaṃ vā mṛdnāti / alagardaṃ vā padābhyāṃ samākrāmati / tadrūpaṃ vāgāraṃ praviśati yatrainaṃ mātṛgrāmo 'yogavihitenopanimantrayati / araṇye vā punamārgaṃ hitvā kumārgeṇa gacchati / corairvā taskarairvā sārdhaṃ samāgacchati siṃhairvyāghrairvāparavṛkairvā ityevaṃbhāgīyaṃ skhalitamarhatastathāgatasya sarveṇa sarva nāsti / punarayamarhannekadāraṇye pravaṇe 'nvāhiṇḍanmārgādapanaśya śūnyāgāraṃ praviśya śabdamudīrayati ghoṣamanuśrāvayati mahārutaṃ ravati
# de dag gi rnam par gzhag pa ni 'di lta ste / / dge slong dgra bcom pa zag pa zad pa bsod snyoms kyi phyir grong du rgyu ba na res 'ga' glang po che gtum po dang lhan cig 'gro ba dang / / glang po che gtum po ji lta ba de bzhin du rta gtum po dang ba rdung khus ma dang khyi za ba dang tshang tshing tsher mas 'dzings pa dang sprul la rkang pa gnyis kas rdzi ba dang gang du bud med mi rigs pa skyes pas bos pa'i khyim de lta bur 'jug pa dang dgon par lam nor nas lam log par 'gro ba dang chom rkun rnams dang rkun po rnams dang seng ge dang stag dang spyang ki dang lhan cig 'gro ba dang de lta bu dang mthun pa la sogs pa dgra bcom pa'i 'khrul pa de ni de bzhin gshegs pa la thams cad kyi thams cad du mi mnga'o / / gzhan yang dgra bcom pa res 'ga' dgon pa na nags khrod chen por rgyu ba na lam nor te / / grong stong du phyin nas sgra 'byin pa dang sgra sgrogs pa dang ku co cher 'don pa dang bag chags kyi nyes pa la brten nas nyon mongs pa can gyi gad mo rta gad so snang bar dgod pa dang 'phya ba nye bar ston pa dang de lta bu dang mthun pa dgra bcom pa'i ca co de bzhin gshegs pa la thams cad kyi thams cad du mi mnga' ba'o / / de bzhin gshegs pa la bsnyel ba med de nyon mongs pa med par yun ring po nas mdzad pa dang gsungs pa rjes su dran pa'i phyir ro /
vāsanādoṣaṃ vāgamya kliṣṭaṃ mahāhāsaṃ hasati dantavidarśakaṃ saṃcagdhitamupadarśayati / ityevaṃbhāgīyamarhato ravitaṃ tathāgatasya sarveṇa sarvaṃ nāsti / nāsti tathāgatasya muṣitā smṛtirakliṣṭacirakṛtacirabhāṣitānusmaraṇatāmuṣādāya / punaraparamarhan samāpannaḥ samāhito bhavati vyutthito 'samāhitaḥ / tathāgatasya tu sarvāvasthaṃ nāstyasamāhitaṃ cittam
# gzhan yang dgra bcom pa ni snyoms par zhugs nas mnyam par bzhag par 'gyur gyi langs nas mnyam par bzhag pa ni ma yin no / / de bzhin gshegs pa la ni gnas skabs thams cad du sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa med do / / gzhan yang dgra bcom pa ni phung po la shin tu mi mthun pa'i 'du shes su lta zhing phung po med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa la zhi ba'i 'du shes su 'gyur ro /
punaraparamarhannekāntenopadhā ca pratikramaṇasaṃjñī bhavati nirupadhike ca nirvāṇe śāntasaṃjñī
# de bzhin gshegs pa la ni phung po dang mya ngan las 'das pa la tha dad pa'i 'du shes mi mda'o /
tathāgatasya upadhau nirvāṇe ca nānātvasaṃjñā nāsti paramopekṣāvihāritāmupādāya
# gzhan yang dgra bcom pa ni so sor ma brtags par sems can gyi don yal bar 'dor ro /
punaraparamarhannapratisaṃkhyāya sattvārthakriyāmadhyupekṣate
# de bzhin gshegs pa la ni de lta bu dang mthun pa so sor ma brtags pa'i btang snyoms mi mda'o /
tathāgatasya tviyamevaṃbhāgīyāpratisaṃkhyāyopekṣā nāsti / punaraparamarhan jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhimārabhyāprāptaparihāṇyā chandenāpi parihīyate vīrye ṇāpismṛtyā samādhinā prajñayā vimuktyā vimuktijñānadarśanenāpi parihīyate / itīyaṃ saptākārā parihāṇistathāgatasya nāsti
# gzhan yang dgra bcom pa ni shes bya'i sgrib pa rnam par dag pa las brtsams te / / 'dun pa las kyang ma thob pa'i yongs su nyams pas yongs su nyams so / / brtson 'grus dang dran ba dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab dang rnam par grol ba las kyang yongs su nyams so / / de bzhin gshegs pa la ni yongs su nyams pa rnam pa 'di drug med do /
punaraparamarhannekadā kuśale kāyakarmaṇi pravartate ekadāvyākṛte
# gzhan yang dgra bcom pa ni res 'ga' lus kyi las dge ba la 'jug / / res 'ga' lung du ma bstan pa la 'jug go /
yathā kāyakarmaṇyevaṃ vākkarmaṇi manaskarmaṇi ca / tathāgatasya trayāṇāmapi karmaṇāṃ jñānapūrvagamatvājjñānānuparivartitvācca nāstyavyākṛtaṃ karma tatra jñānasamutthāpanatāmupādāya jñānapūrvagamam / jñānasahacaratāmupādāya jñānānuparivarti
# lus kyi las ji lta bar dag gi las dang yid kyi las kyang de bzhin no / / de bzhin gshegs pa'i phrin las gsum po ni ye shes sngon du 'gro ba dang ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i phyir lung du ma bstan pa'i las med do / / de la ye shes kun nas slong ba'i phyir ye shes sngon du 'gro ba'o / / ye shes dang lhan cig rgyu ba'i phyir ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba'o /
punaraparamarhan traiyadhvikaṃ jñeyavastu na cābhogamātrātpratipadyate yenāsya saktaṃ jñānadarśanaṃ bhavati
# gzhan yang dgra bcom pa ni rtsol btsam gyis dus gsum gyi shes bya'i dngos po rtogs par mi 'gyur te / / des na de'i ye shes mthong ba chags par 'gyur ro /
na ca sarvaṃ pratipadyate yenāsya pratihataṃ jñānadarśanaṃ bhavati
# thams cad rtogs par yang mi 'gyur te / / des na de'i ye shes mthong ba thogs par 'gyur ro /
tathāgatastraiyadhvikamābhogamātrāt sarvaṃ vastu pratipadyate / tasmādete aṣṭādaśāveṇikā buddhadharmā ityucyante
# de bzhin gshegs pa ni rtsol ba tsam gyis dus gsum gyi shes bya'i dngos po thams cad rtogs te / / de lta bas na de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad ces bya'o /
tatraiṣāmādyāḥ ṣaṭ asādhāraṇakāyavāṅmanaskarmapariśuddhisamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ / tatra nāsti skhalitamityayaṃ kāyakarmapariśuddhimārabhya / nāsti ravitamityayaṃ vākkarmaparaśuddhimārabhya
# de la 'di dag las dang po drug ni sku dang gsungs dang thugs kyi phrin las thun mong ma yin pa yongs su dag pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o / / de la 'khrul pa med ces bya ba 'di ni sku'i phrin las yongs su dag pa las brtsams pa'o / / ca co med ces bya ba 'di ni gsung gi phrin las yongs su dag pa las brtsams pa'o /
tatra nāsti muṣitasmṛtiḥ nāstyasamānitaṃ cittaṃ nāsti nānātvasaṃjñā nāstyapratisaṃkhyāyopekṣetyetaccatuṣṭayaṃ manaskarmapariśuddhimadhikṛtya veditavyam
# bsnyel ba med pa dang tha dad pa'i 'du shes med pa dang sems mnyam par ma bzhag pa med pa dang so sor ma brtags pa'i btang snyoms med ces bya ba 'di bzhis ni thugs kyi phrin las yongs su dag pa'i dbang du byas par rig par bya'o / / 'dun pa nyams pa med ces bya ba nas /
nāsti chandaparihāṇiryāvannāsti vimuktijñānadarśanaparihāṇiriti sāśrayāṇāṃ saphalānāṃ tathāgatendriyāṇāmaprāptyaparihāṇisamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ / tatrāśrayaśchandaḥ / phalaṃ vimuktirvimuktijñānadarśanaṃ ca
# rnam par grol ba nyams pa med ces bya ba'i bar du drug ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbang po gnas dang bcas pa dang 'bras bu dang bcas pa rnams ma thob pa'i yongs su nyams pa med pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o / / de la gnas ni 'dun pa'o / / 'bras bu ni rnam par grol ba'o /
indriyāṇi vīryādīni veditavyāni
# dbang po ni brtson 'grus la sogs par rig par bya'o /
sarvaṃ kāyakarma vākkarma manaskarma jñānapūrvagamaṃ jñānānuvartītyete trayo 'sādhāraṇakarmacārasamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ
# lus kyi las dang dag gi las dang yid kyi las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro zhing ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ba zhes bya pa 'di gsum ni thun mong ma yin pa'i phrin las mdzad pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o /
atīte 'dhvanyasaṅgamapratihataṃ jñānaṃ yāvatpratyutpanne 'dhvanītyete trayo 'sādhāraṇajñānavihārasamṛddhau samādhyādayaḥ
# 'das pa'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes zhes bya ba nas / / da ltar byung ba'i dus la zhes bya ba 'di gsum ni ye shes la gnas pa thun mong ma yin pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'o /
skandhadhātvāyataneṣu sarvākārajñatāsamṛddhāviti skandhādīnāṃ svabhāvaviśeṣalakṣaṇaprabhedaparyantajñānaniṣpattāvityarthaḥ / teṣāṃ punarabhinirhāro niśrayato 'bhinirhārakapudgalato 'bhinirhāropāyataśca paridīpitaḥ
# phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams la rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yang dag par 'byor pa zhes bya ba ni phung po la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid dang khyad par gyi mtshan nyid dang rab tu dbye ba'i mthar thug pa mkhyen pa grub ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de dag ni mngon par sgrub pa'i gnas dang mngon par sgrub pa po gang zag dang mngon par sgrub pa'i thabs kyis yongs su bstan to /
abhinirhāropāyaḥ punaryathāvyavasthānaṃ manaskārabahulīkāratā yathādeśanaṃ samāhitasya cittasya punaḥpunastatra dhāraṇamityarthaḥ
# mngon par sgrub pa'i thabs ni ji ltar rnam par gzhag pa bzhin du lan mang du yid la byed pa ste / / ji ltar bstan pa bzhin du sems mnyam par gzhag nas yang dang yang de la 'jog ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tadyathāpramāṇānyabhinirhartukāmo maṃtrīsahagatena cittenāvaireṇāsapatnenetyevamādikāṃ deśanāṃ dhyānasaṃniśrayeṇa bhāvayan manasikurvan bahulīkaroti evamabhijñādīnabhi nirhartukāma eko bhūtvā bahudhā bhavatītyevamādikaṃ vyavasthānaṃ manasikurvan bahulīkarotīti yojayitavyam
# 'di lta ste tshad med pa mngon par bsgrub par 'dod pa byams pa dang ldan pa'i sems kho na med pa 'gran zla med pa zhes bya ba la sogs pas bstan ba bsam gtan la brten nas bsams pas yid la byed pas mang du byed do / / de bzhin du mngon par shes pa la sogs pa mngon par bsgrub par 'dod pas gcig tu gyur nas mang por 'gyur zhes bya ba la sogs pa rnam par gzhag pa yid la byed pas mang du byed do zhes sbyar bar bya'o /
ta ete 'pramāṇādayo guṇā dviprakārāḥ
# tshad med pa la sogs pa yon tan 'di dag ni rnam pa gnyis te /
svakāritrapratyupasthānāśca yairāryo yathāyogaṃ vipakṣaprahāṇādikaṃ karma karoti vaihārikāśca yaiḥ paramapraśāntanirvikalpajñānasaṃgṛhītairanālaṃbanāpramāṇādibhirdṛṣṭe dharme sukhaṃ viharati / tatrāpramāṇaivipakṣaṃ prajahātīti yathākramaṃ vyāpādaṃ vihiṃsāmaratimanunayapratighau ca
# rang gi bya ba la nye bar gnas pa ni gang dag gis 'phags pa ci rigs su mi mthun pa'i phyogs spong ba la sogs pa'i las byed pa'o / / gnas pa las gyur pa ni mchog tu zhi ba rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyis bsdus pa dmigs pa med pa'i tshad med pa la sogs pa gang dag gis mthong ba'i chos la bde bar gnas pa'o / / de la tshad med pa rnams kyis mi mthun pa'i phyogs spong ngo zhes bya ba ni gnod sems dang rnam par 'tshe ba dang mi dga' ba dang rjes su chags pa dang khong khro ba dang go rims bzhin no /
etāni ca catvāryapramāṇānyanukampetyucyate ebhiḥ sattvārthaṃ pratyanuguṇaṃ pravartanāt
# tshad med pa bzhi po 'di dag ni snying brtse ba zhes bya ste / / 'di dag gis sems can gyi don gyi rjes su mthun par 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
atastairviharamāṇaḥ sarvasattveṣvanukampāvihāritayā puṇyasaṃbhāraṃ paripūrayati
# de'i phyir de dag gi gnas na sems can thams cad la thugs brtse bar gnas pas bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs par mdzad do /
ata eva sattvaparipāke ca na parikhidyate sarvasattvānukampitvena svātmanirapekṣatvāt
# de nyid kyi phyir sems can yongs su smin par mdzad pa la yongs su mi skyo ste / / sems can thams cad la thugs brtse bas bdag la mi lta ba'i phyir ro /
vimokṣeṣu dvābhyāṃ vimokṣābhyāṃ nirmāṇakarmābhinirharati
# rnam par thar pa rnams las gnyis kyis ni sprul pa'i lam mngon par sgrub bo /
tṛtīyena śubhe nirmāṇe na saṃkliśyate
# gsum pas ni dge ba sprul pa la kun nas nyon mongs par mi 'gyur ro /
catubhirāryavimokṣaiḥ śānteṣu mokṣeṣu na sajjate
# gzugs med pa'i rnam par thar pa bzhi ni zhi ba'i rnam par thar pa rnams la mi chags so /
praścimena paramapraśāntenāryavihāreṇa viharati / tathā tathādhimokṣārthaśca vimokṣo veditavyaḥ / abhibhvāyatanādīnāṃ karma pūrvavat tannirdeśānusāreṇaiva yojayitavyam
# tha mas ni 'phags pa'i gnas pa mchog tu rab tu zhi ba'i gnas pas nas te / / de la de ltar mos pa'i don ni rnam par thar pa'i don du rig par bya'o / / zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched la sogs pa'i las kyang snga ma bzhin du de bstan pa'i tshul du sbyar bar bya'o /
araṇāyā ādeyavacano bhavati paracittānurakṣaṇapradhānatayā yathānurūpaṃ vacanāt
# nyon mongs pa med pas ni gzhan gyi sems rjes su bsrung ba gces su byed pas ji ltar mthun pa bzhin du smra ba'i phyir gzung ba'i tshig tu 'gyur ro /
praṇidhijñānena bahumataśca bhavati lokasya sarvaṃ jānātīti gauravitatvāt
# bsams nas shes pas ni thams cad shes so zhes gus par bya ba'i phyir 'jig rten na mang pos bkur bar 'gyur ro /
pratisaṃvidbhirdeśanayā sattvacittāni saṃtoṣayati bahuvicitraiḥ prakāraiḥ saṃśayacchedanāt
# so so yang dag par rig pa rnams kyis ni rnam pa sna tshogs mang pos the tshom gcod pa'i phyir bshad pas sems can rnams kyi sems tshim par mdzad do /
ṛddhidivyaśrotraparacittajñānapūrvenivāsacyutyupapādāsravakṣayābhijñābhiryathākramaṃ kāyakarmādinā śāsane āvarjayati
# rdzu 'phrul dang lha'i rna ba dang gzhan gyi sems shes pa dang sngon gyi gnas dang 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba dang zag pa zad pa'i mngon par shes pa rnams kyis ni go rims bzhin du lus kyi las la sogs pas bstan pa la 'dun par mdzad do /
divyaśrotrābhijñayā sarvarutaprakārābhyupapattito vākkarmaṇāvarjanaṃ veditavyam / āśrayapariśuddhayā yathākāmamāśrayasyopādānasthānaparityāgānadhikṛtya saṃcintya bhavopapattiparigrahaṇādīni trīṇi veditavyāni
# lha'i rna ba'i mngon par shes pas ni sgra'i rnam pa thams cad rtogs nas ngag gi las kyis 'dun par mdzad par rig par bya'o / / gnas yongs su dag pas ni ji ltar bzhed pa bzhin du gnas len pa dang bzhugs pa dang yongs su gtong pa'i dbang du byas nas srid par skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa la sogs pa gsum du rig par bya'o /
ālaṃbanapariśuddhayā dharmavaśavartī bhavati cittapariśuddhayā samādhivaśavartī jñānapariśuddhyā saddharmaṃ dhārayati
# dmigs pa yongs su dag pas ni chos la dbang sgyur ro / / sems yongs su dag pas ni ting nge 'dzin la dbang sgyur ro / / ye shes yongs su dag pas ni dam pa'i chos yang dag par 'dzin to /
baleṣu dvābhyāṃ balābhyāmabhyudayamārga deśayati śeṣairniḥśreyasamārgame tāvacca buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ karaṇīyam / tatra sthānāsthānajñānabalena bhagavannirhetuko 'bhyudayaḥ prakṛtīśvarādihetuko vetyevamahetuviṣamahetuvādaṃ pratikṣipati / karmasvakatājñānabalena svayamakṛtamapi karmāgacchatītyevamakṛtābhyāgamavādaṃ pratikṣipati yataḥ samyagaviparītaṃ sugatimārga deśayati
# stobs rnams kyi nang nas stobs gnyis kyis ni mngon bar mtho ba'i lam ston to / / lhag ma rnams kyis ni nges par legs pa'i lam ston te / / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa ni 'di dag go / / de la bcom ldan 'das kyis gnas dang gnas ma yin pa mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni mngon par mtho ba rgyu med pa las byung ba dang rang bzhin dang dbang phyug la sogs pa'i rgyu las byung ngo zhes rgyu med pa dang mi mthun pa rgyur smra ba de spong ngo / / las bdag gir bya ba mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni las bdag gis ma byas kyang las 'ong ngo zhes ma byas pa dang phrad par smra ba de spong ngo / / 'di ltar yang dag par ma nor bar bde 'gro'i lam ston to /
dhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpattijñānabalena sattvānāṃ cittacaritāni cetaḥ pracarānanupraviśati
# bsam gtan dang rnam par thar pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni sems can gyi sems kyi spyod pa rnams te; sems kyi rgyu ba rnams rjes su rtogs so /
indriyaparāparajñānabalena deśanābhājanatāṃ śraddhādīndriyaparipākamanupraviśati
# dbang po mchog dang mchog ma yin pa mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni bshad pa'i snod dad pa la sogs pa'i dbang po yongs su smin pa rjes su rtogs so /
nānādhimuktijñānabalenāśayaṃ hīnapraṇītādhimuktikatāmanupraviśati
# mos pa sna tshogs mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni bsam pa ste / / ngan pa dang bzang po la mos pa rjes su rtogs so /
nānādhātujñānabalenānuśayasamudghātanaśakyakleśatāmanupraviśati
# khams sna tshogs mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni bag la nyal skyed nus pa'i nyon mongs pa rjes su rtogs so /
sarvatragāminīpratipajjñānabalenālaṃbanaṃ śrāvakayānaṃ mahāyānaṃ vā deśanādharmasaṃgṛhītadharmamanupraviśati
# thams cad du 'gro ba'i lam mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni dmigs pa nyan thos kyi theg pa'am / / theg pa chen po bstan pa'i chos kyis bsdus pa rjes su rtogs so; /
pūrvenivāsānusmṛtijñānabalena saṃbhāraṃ pūrvajanmasamudāyagatamāryamārgahetumanupraviśati
# sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni tshe rabs snga ma dag na tshogs yang dag par sgrub pa 'phags pa'i lam gyi rgyu rjes su rtogs so /
cyutyupapādajñānabalena bhavyatā māyatyāmanupraviśati
# 'chi 'pho dang skye ba mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni phyi ma la 'os su 'gyur ba rjes su rtogs so /
āsravakṣayajñānabalena niḥsaraṇaṃ ca sarvasmāttraidhātukādanupraviśati yato yathāvanmokṣamārga deśayati
# zag pa zad pa mkhyen pa'i stobs kyis ni 'jig rten thams cad nas nges par 'byung ba rjes su rtogs te / / gang las ji lta ba bzhin du thar pa'i lam ston to /
balatvaṃ punareṣāmebhiḥ skandhakleśadevaputramaraṇamāranigrahaṇaviśeṣāt / viśeṣaḥ punarjñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇe 'pyanantarāyakṛtatvāt sthānāsthāne yāvadāsravakṣaya iti sarvatra praśnaṃ pṛṣṭasya praśnavyākaraṇavyāghātācca / vaiśāradyaiḥ pariṣadi samyagātmanaḥ śāstṛtvamātmaparahitapratipannatvaṃ vyavasthāpayati
# stobs nyid ni 'di dag gi phung po dang nyon mongs pa dang lha'i bu dang 'chi bdag gi bdud tshar gcod pa'i khyad par gyi phyir ro / / khyad par ni shes bya'i sgrib pa spangs nas bar chad mi byed pa dang gnas dang gnas ma yin pa nas zag pa zad pa mkhyen pa'i stobs kyi bar thams cad du dri ba dris na dri ba lung ston pa la thogs pa med pa'i phyir ro / / mi 'jigs pa rnams kyis ni 'khor gyi nang du bdag ston pa yang dag pa bdag dang gzhan la phan par zhugs pa nyid du yang dag par 'jog pa'o /
codakāṃścābhisaṃbodhau yāvanmārge tīrthyān sahadharmeṇa nigṛhṇāti
# mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa nas lam gyi bar la rgol ba'i mu stegs can rnams chos dang mthun pas tshar gcod do /
smṛtyupasthānairasaṃkliṣṭo gaṇaṃ parikarṣati śūśrūṣamāṇādiṣvanunayādisaṃkleśābhāvāt / arakṣyairnirantaraṃ gaṇamavavadati samanuśāsti svadoṣāvirbhāvanā śaṃkayānurakṣyābhāvāt
# dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyis ni gus par nyan pa la sogs pa la rjes su chags pa la sogs pa'i kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i phyir / / kun nas nyon mongs pa can ma yin pas tshogs yongs su sdud do / / bsrung ba med pa rnams kyis ni rang gi nyes pa brjod du dogs nas bsrung ba med pa'i phyir rgyun mi 'chad par tshogs la 'doms so /
asaṃmoṣadharmatayā buddhakṛtyaṃ na hāpayati upasthite sattvārthakṛtye pramādena kṣaṇamapyalaṃghanāt
# bsnyel ba med pa'i chos nyid kyis ni sems can gyi don bya ba nye bar gnas pa la skad cig tsam yang bag med pas 'gal bar mi mdzad pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mi 'dor ro /
vāsanāsamudghātena niḥkleśaḥ kleśapratirūpāṃ ceṣṭāṃ na darśayati yathārhan bhikṣuḥ skhalitādikaṃ darśayati
# bag chags legs par bcom pas ni de ltar dgra bcom pa las 'khrul pa la sogs pa ston pa lta bu ma yin te / / nyon mongs pa med pas /
mahākaruṇayā ṣaṭkṛtvā rātriṃdivasena lokaṃ vyavalokayati ko hīyate kaḥ parihīyata ityevamādibhiḥ prakāraiḥ pratyavekṣaṇāt
# nyon mongs pa lta bu'i spyod pa mi ston to / / thugs rje chen pos ni su nyams par 'gyur su 'phel bar 'gyur zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis so sor rtog pa'i phyir nyin mtshan lan drug du 'jig rten rnam par gzigs so /
āveṇikānāṃ buddhadharmāṇāṃ karmāsādhāraṇakāyavāṅmanaskarmapariśuddhisamṛddhāvityevamādilakṣaṇanirdeśādhikāreṇayojayitavyam
# sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams ni sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi phrin las thun mong ma yin pa yongs su dag pa yang dag par 'byor pa'i zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid bstan pa'i skabs bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o /
sarvakārajñatayā sarvasattvānāṃ sarvasaṃśayān chinatti sarvatrāvyāhatajñānatvāt
# rnam pa thams mkhyen pa nyid kyis ni thams cad du ye shes thogs pa med pas sems can thams cad kyi the tshom gcod do /
dharmanetrīṃ ca dīrghakālamavasthāpayati tatra tatra vineyasaṃśayacchedanārtha deśitānāṃ dharmaparyāyāṇāṃ saṃgītikārairanukrameṇa saṃjñāpanāt
# the tshom bcad pa'i phyir de dang der bstan pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs rnams yang dag par bsdus pa'i rim gyis yang dag par bsdus nas chos kyi tshul yang yun ring du 'jog go /
dharmanetrīṃ nisrityāparipakvāḥ sattvāḥ paripacyante paripakvāśca vimucyante / viśiṣṭamārgalābhe hīnamārgavihānistadyathā phalasaṃgṛhītamārgalābhe pratipannakamārgo vihīna ityucyate punarasaṃmukhīkaraṇāt / sakalaprahāṇaṃ ca sākṣātkaroti phalaprāptikāle tu tadvipakṣajātīyakleśapratipakṣadauṣṭhulyāśeṣaprahāṇādāśrayaparivṛttiviśeṣalābhataḥ samavasargavihānyā vijahātītyatyantāsamudācāraṃ vijahātītyarthaḥ
# chos kyi tshul de la brten nas sems can yongs su ma smin pa rnams ni yongs su smin par mdzad / / yongs su smin pa rnams ni rnam par grol bar mdzad do / / khyad par du 'phags pa'i lam thob nas lam dman pa 'dor ba ni 'di lta ste / / 'bras bus bsdus pa'i lam thob par gyur na 'jug pa'i lam rnam par 'dor zhes bya ste / / yang mngon du mi byed pa'i phyir ro; / / bsdoms te spong ba yang mngon sum du byed do zhes bya ba ni 'bras bu thob pa'i dus te / / de'i mi mthun pa'i rigs kyi nyon mongs pa'i phyogs kyi gnas ngan len ma lus par spangs pas gnas gyur pa'i khyad par thob pa'i phyir ro / / rgyun yang dag par gcod pa'i rnam par 'dor bas rnam par spong zhes bya ba ni gtan du kun du mi spyod pas rnam par 'dor zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
no tu bodhisattvastathā vijahāti sarvasattvaparinirvāṇābhiprāyapūrvakatvāttanmārgasya
# byang chub sems dpa' ni de ltar rnam bar spong ba ma yin te / / de'i lam ni sems can thams cad yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i bsam pa sngon du btang ba'i phyir ro /
ata eva bodhisattvā akṣayakuśalamūlā akṣayaguṇā ityucyante tadyathākṣamiti sūtre 'kṣayatānirdiṣṭeti
# de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba mi zad pa dang yon tan mi zad pa zhes bya ste / / 'di ltar blo gros mi zad pas bstan pa'i mdo las mi zad pa bstan pa rnams yin no /
śāśvato loka aśāśvata ityevamādiṣu praśneṣvavyākṛtavastuvyavasthānamanarthopasaṃhitatvenāyoniśatvāt
# 'jig rten rtag pa'o mi rtag pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa 'dri ba la lung mi ston pa'i dngos po rnam par gzhag pa ni don dang mi ldan pas tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
teṣāṃ teṣāṃ praśnānāṃ kīdṛśaḥ punaḥ praśno 'rthopasaṃhitaḥ
# 'dri ba de dag gi 'dri ba'i don dang ldan pa ji lta bu zhe na /
tadyathā catvāryāryasatyānyārabhya yaḥ praśnaḥ
# 'di lta ste 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi las brtsams nas gang 'dri ba ste /
tathāhi sahetuphalasaṃkleśavyavadānacintāntarbhūta iti
# 'di ltar de rgyu dang 'bras bu dang kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba'i sems pa'i nang du gtogs pa'i phyir ro /
bodhisattvasya nyāmāvakrāntāvapi śrotāpannatvāvyavasthānam apratiṣṭhitamārgapratilambhāt pratiśrotaḥ pratipattyapariniṣpannatāmupādāya
# byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa la zhugs kyang rgyun du zhugs pa la sogs par rnam par mi gzhag pa ni mi gnas pa'i lam thob pas rgyun la 'jug pa yongs su ma grub pa'i phyir ro / / shes bya ni rnam pa drug ste /
jñeyaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ bhrāntiryāvadabhrāntiniṣyandaśca
# 'khrul ba nas ma 'khrul pa'i rgyu mthun pa'i bar du'o /
tatra bhrāntirgrāhyagrāhakābhiniveśaḥ
# de la 'khrul pa ni gzung ba dang 'dzin par mngon par zhen pa'o /
bhrāntyāśrayo yasminnāryajñā nagocare saṃskāranimittamātre 'bhūtaparikalpātmake sati bālānāṃ so 'bhiniveśaḥ pravartate
# 'khrul pa'i gnas ni 'phags pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul 'du byed kyi rgyu tsam yang dag pa ma yin par kun du rtog pa'i bdag nyid du gyur ba gang la byis pa rnams gang mngon par zhen pas 'jug go /
abhrāntyāśrayastathatā nirvikalpasya jñānasya tadadhiṣṭhānatvāt
# ma 'khrul pa'i gnas ni de bzhin nyid de / / de rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes kyi rten yin pa'i phyir ro /
bhrāntyabhrāntilokottarajñānānukūlāḥ śrutamayyādayaḥ kuśalā dharmāḥ jñeyavikalpanānnirvikalpajñānānukūlyācca
# 'khrul pa yang yin la ma 'khrul ba yang yin pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes dang mthun pa thos pa las byung ba la sogs pa dge ba'i chos rnams te / / shes bya ba rnam par rtog pa dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes dang mthun pa'i phyir ro /
abhrāntirnirvikalpajñānam
# ma 'khrul pa ni rnam par mi rtog pa'i ye shes so /
abhrāntiniṣyanda āryamārgapṛṣṭhalabdhāḥ kuśalā dharmāḥ
# ma 'khrul pa'i rgyu mthun pa ni 'phags pa'i lam gyi rjes la thob pa'i dge ba'i chos rnams so /
upāyakauśalyaṃ punaścaturvidham
# thabs la mkhas pa ni rnam pa bzhi ste /
sattvaparipākakauśalyaṃ catvāri saṃgrahavastūni taiḥ saṃgṛhya kuśaleṣu dharmeṣu niyojanāt / buddhadharmaparipūraṇakauśalyaṃ prajñāpāramitā dānapāramitāṃ yāvat sarvākāravarajñatāṃ paripūrayitukāmena bodhisattvena mahāsattvenāsyāmeva prajñāpāramitāyāṃ śikṣitavyamiti vacanāt
# sems can yongs su smin par bya ba la mkhas pa ni bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi ste / / de dag gis bsdus nas dge ba rnams la 'dzud pa'i phyir ro / / sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs par bya ba la mkhas pa ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste / / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa nas / / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi bar du yongs su rdzogs par byed par 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di nyid la bslab par bya'o zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro /
kṣiprābhijñatākauśalyaṃ ṣaṭkṛtvā rātridivasaṃ pāpapratideśanā puṇyānumodanā buddhādhyeṣaṇā kuśalamūlapariṇāmanā ca yathākramamāryamaitreyaparipṛcchāyām
# mngon par shes pa myur ba la mkhas pas ni nyid mtshan lan drug tu sdig pa bshags pa dang bsod nams la rjes su yi rang ba dang; sangs rgyas la gsol ba btab pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngo ba ste / / 'phags pa byams pas zhus pa las ji skad gsungs pa lta bu'o /
dharmānupacchedakauśalyaṃ cāpratiṣṭhitanirvāṇatayā punaḥpanaranuparatamatyantaṃ ca samantāllokadhātuṣu yathāvineyaṃ buddhabodhisattvacaryāsaṃdarśanāditi
# lam rgyun mi 'chad pa'i mkhas pa ni mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pas phyir zhing rgyun mi 'chad par gtan du 'jig rten gyi khams kun du 'dul pa ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa kun du ston pa'i phyir ro /
abhūtaparikalpo daśavidhaḥ
# yang dag pa ma yin pa'i kun du rtog pa ni rnam pa bcu ste /
tatra mūlavikalpa ālayavijñānam sarvavikalpānāṃ bījabhūtatvāt
# rtsa ba'i rnam par rtog pa ni kun gzhi'i rnam par shes pa ste / / rnam par rtog pa thams cad kyi sa bon du gyur pa'i phyir ro /
nimittavikalpo dehapratiṣṭhābhogapratibhāsā vijñaptayaḥ grāhyanimittabhūtatvāt
# mtshan ma'i rnam par rtog pa ni lus dang gnas dang longs spyod kyi rnam par rig pa ste / / gzung ba dang mtshan mar gyur pa'i phyir ro /
tāḥ punaryathākramaṃ rūpīndriya bhājanalokarūpādiviṣayalakṣaṇā draṣṭavyāḥ / nimittapratibhāsasya vikalpaḥ ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥ manaśca yathoktagrāhyanimittākāratvāt
# de dag ni dbang po gzugs can dang snod kyi 'jig rten dang gzugs la sogs pa'i yul gyi mtshan nyid dang go rims bzhin du blta bar bya'o / / mtshan mar snang ba'i rnam par rtog pa ni rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug dang yid de gzung ba'i mtshan ma ji skad du bshad pa'i rnam par gyur pa'i phyir ro /
nimittavikāravikalpo yathoktadehādinimittasyānyathātvenotpādaḥ
# mtshan mar gyur pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni ji skad bshad pa'i lus la sogs ba'i mtshan ma'i rnam pa gzhan du bskyed pa'o /
nimittapratibhāsavikāra vikalpo yathoktasya cakṣarvijñānādinimittapratibhāsasya sukhādyavasthāntareṇotpādaḥ
# mtshan mar snang bar 'gyur ba'i rnam par rtog pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa mtshan mar snang ba ji skad du bstan pa dag bde ba la sogs pa'i gnas skabs gzhan du bskyed pa'o /
paropanīto vikalpo deśanāsaṃgṛhītanāmapadavyañjanakāyalakṣaṇaḥ
# gzhan gyis bstan pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni bstan par bsdus pa'i ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs kyi mtshan nyid do /
sa punardvividhaḥ durākhyātadharmavinayātmakaḥ svākhyādharmavinayātmakaśca / atastadadhipateyamanaskārasaṃgṛhītau yathākramaṃ yoniśovikalpo 'yoniśovikalpaśca veditavyaḥ
# de la yang rnam pa gnyis te / / nyes par bshad pa'i chos kyi tshul gyi bdag nyid dang legs par bshad pa'i chos kyi tshul gyi bdag nyid do / / de'i phyir de'i dbang du byas pa yid la byed pas bsdus pa tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i rnam par rtog pa dang tshul bzhin gyi rnam par rtog pa dang go rims bzhin du rig par bya'o /
abhiniveśavikalpo 'yoniśovikalpādvāṣaṣṭidṛṣṭigatasaṃgṛhīto yo vikalpaḥ / vikṣepavikalpaḥ yoniśo vikalpādabhāvādigrāhalakṣaṇo yo vikalpaḥ / sa punardaśavidhaḥ abhāvavikalpaḥ yāvadyathārthanāmavikalpaśca / sa eṣa daśavidho vikalpaḥ prajñāpāramitādinirdeśamadhikṛtya veditavyaḥ
# mngon par zhen pa'i rnam par rtog pa ni tshul bzhin ma yin pa'i rnam par rtog pa las lta bar song ba drug cu rtsa gnyis su bsdus pa'i rnam par rtog pa gang yin pa'o / / rnam par g yeng ba'i rnam par rtog pa ni tshul bzhin dang tshul bzhin gyi rnam par rtog pa las dngos po med pa la sogs pa 'dzin pa'i mtshan nyid kyi rnam par rtog pa gang yin pa'o / / de yang rnam pa bcu ste / / dngos po med par rnam par rtog pa nas don ji lta ba bzhin du ming du rnam par rtog pa'i bar du'o / / rnam par rtog pa 'di bcu ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las thog mar bstan pa'i dbang du byas par rig par bya ste /
yathoktam iha śāriputra bodhisattvo bodhisattva eva san bodhisattvaṃ na samanupaśyati
# ji skad du sh'a ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' ni byang chub sems dpa' nyid yod bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang dag par rjes su mi mthong /
bodhisattvanāma na samanupaśyati
# byang chub sems dpa'i ming yang dag par rjes su mi mthong /
prajñāpāramitāṃ na samanupaśyati
# shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yang dag par rjes su mi mthong /
bodhiṃ na samanupaśyati
# byang chub yang dag par rjes su mi mthong /
caratīti na samanupaśyati
# spyod ces bya bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong /
na caratīti na samanupaśyati / tathāhi nāma svabhāvena śūnyaṃ na śūnyatayā rūpaṃ svabhāvena śūnyaṃ na śūnyatayā yāvadvijñānaṃ svabhāvena śūnyaṃ na śūnyatayā
# mi spyod ces bya bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ste / / 'di ltar ming ni ming gi ngo bo nyid kyis stong ste / / stong pa nyid kyis ni stong pa ma yin no / / gzugs ni ngo bo nyid kyis stong ste / / stong pa nyid kyis ni stong pa ma yin no / / rnam par shes pa'i bar du ngo bo nyid kyis ni stong ste / / stong pa nyid kyis ni stong pa ma yin no /
tatkasya hetoḥ
# de ci'i phyir zhe na /
yā rūpasya śūnyatā na tadrūpam nāpyanyatra rūpācchanyatā rūpameva śūnyatāḥ śūnyataiva rūpam evaṃ yāvadvijñānam
# gzugs kyi stong pa nyid gang yin pa de gzugs ma yin no / / stong pa nyid las gzugs gzhan ma yin no / / gzugs nyid stong pa nyid do / / stong pa nyid gzugs so / / de bzhin du rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o / / de ci'i phyir zhe na /
tatkasya hetoḥ / nāmamātramidaṃ yaduta bodhisattvanāmeti bodhisattva iti prajñāpāramiteti bodhiriti rūpamiti yāvadvijñānamiti
# 'di lta ste / / byang chub sems dpa'i ming zhes bya ba dang byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba dang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ba dang byang chub ces bya ba dang gzugs zhes bya ba nas rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i bar 'di ni ming tsam ste / / ngo bo nyid kyis mi skye mi 'gag /
svabhāvasya hi notpādo na nirodho na saṃkleśo na vyavadānam
# kun nas nyon mongs pa ma yin / / rnam par byang ba ma yin no /
prajñāpāramitāyāṃ caran bodhisattva utpādamapi na samanupaśyati yāvadvayavadānamapi na samanupaśyati
# shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni skye ba yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ba nas / / rnam par byang ba'i bar du yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ngo /
tatkasya hetoḥ
# de ci'i phyir zhe na /
kṛtrimaṃ nāma prati prati te dharmāḥ kalpitā āgantukena nāmnānuvyavahriyante
# ming bcos ma la chos de dag so sor brtags nas / / glo bur gyi ming gis rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
yathā yathānuvyavahriyante tathā tathābhiniviśanti
# ji lta ji ltar rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa de lta de ltar mngon par zhen to /
tāni bodhisattvaḥ sarvanāmāni na samanupaśyati asamanupaśyannābhiniviśate / tatra abhāvavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha bodhisattvo bodhisattva eva sannityevamādi sacchabdasya bhāvārthatvāt
# byang chub sems dpa' ni ming thams cad yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ngo / / yang dag par rjes su mi mthong bas mngon par zhen pa med do / / de la dngos po med pa rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por byang chub sems dpa' nyid du yod do zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te / / yod pa'i sgra ni dngos po'i don yin pa'i phyir ro /
bhāvavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha bodhisattvaṃ na samanupaśyati yāvadvayavadānamapi na samanupaśyati yāvanna caratīti na samanupaśyati pudgaladharmabhāvapratiṣedhāt
# dngos por rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por byang chub sems dpa' yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ba nas / / mi spyod do zhes bya bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ngo zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te /
samāropavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha tathāhi nāma svabhāvena śūnyamiti abhūtaparikalpasya svabhāvapratiṣedhāt
# gang zag dang chos kyi dngos po bkag pa'i phyir ro / / sgro 'dogs pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por 'di ltar ming ni ngo bo nyid kyis stong ngo zhes bya ba gsungs te /
apavādavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha na śūnyatayeti tasminnāmni tena parikalpitena parikalpita svabhāvena virahitatāyāḥ sarvadāstitvāt
# yang dag pa ma yin pa'i kun du brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid bkag pa'i phyir ro / / skur pa 'debs pa'i rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por stong pa nyid kyis ma yin no zhes bya ba gsungs te /
ekatvavikalpaprati pakṣaiṇāha yā rūpasya śūnyatā na tadrūpaṃ yāvadvijñānamiti bhāvāntaratvāt / rūpādayo hi parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ śūnyatā pariniṣpanna iti / pṛthakatvavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha nāpyanyatra rūpācchūnyatāyā rūpam yāvacchanyataiva vijñānamiti parikalpitasvabhāvasyā lakṣaṇatvāttadvyatirekeṇa tadbhā vāsaṃbhavataḥ / svabhāvavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha nāmamātramidaṃ yaduta rūpamiti yāvadvijñānamiti abhilāpavyatirekeṇābhilāpyasvabhāvābhāvāt
