# ming de kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid de dang bral ba nyid du thams cad du yod pa'i phyir ro / / gcig pa nyid du rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por gzugs kyi stong pa nyid gang yin pa de gzugs ma yin no zhes bya ba nas rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid gang yin pa de rnam par shes pa ma yin no zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te / / ngo bo nyid gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir gzugs la sogs pa ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid do / / stong pa nyid ni yongs su grub pa'o / / tha dad pa nyid du rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por stong pa nyid las gzugs gzhan pa yang ma yin no / / gzugs nyid stong pa nyid do / / stong pa nyid gzugs so zhes bya ba nas rnam par shes pa'i bar du gsungs te / / kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi mtshan nyid yin pas / / de las ma gtogs par de med pa'i phyir ro / / ngo bo nyid du rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por 'di lta ste / / gzugs zhes bya ba nas rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i bar 'di ni ming tsam mo zhes bya ba gsungs te / / brjod pa las ma gtogs par brjod pa'i ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir ro /
viśeṣavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha svabhāvasya notpādo yāvadvayavadānamapi na samanupaśyatīti utpādādiviśeṣalakṣaṇapratiṣedhāt
# khyad par du rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por ngo bo nyid kyis mi skye zhes bya ba nas / / rnam par byang ba yang yang dag par rjes su ma mthong ngo zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs te /
yathānāmārthavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha kṛtrimaṃ nāma prati prati te dharmāḥ kalpitā āgantukena nāmnā vyavahriyante ityevamādi
# skye ba la sogs pa'i khyad par gyi mtshan nyid bkag pa'i phyir ro / / ming ji lta ba bzhin du don du rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por ming bcos ma la chos de dag so sor brtags nas glo bur gyi ming gis rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs so /
yathārthanāmavikalpapratipakṣeṇāha tāni bodhisattvaḥ sarvanāmāni na samanu paśyannābhiniviśata iti yathārthaṃ nāmnāmadarśanānabhiniveśāt / nirvikalpanāt tridhā saṃtuṣṭinirvikalpanādibhiḥ
# don ji lta ba bzhin du ming du rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen por byang chub sems dpa'i ming de dag thams cad yang dag par rjes su mi mthong do / / yang dag par rjes su ma mthong bas mngon par zhen pa med do zhes bya ba gsungs te; don ji lta ba bzhin du ming du mi mthong na mngon par zhen pa med pa'i phyir ro / / rnam par mi rtog pa nyid ni rnam pa gsum ste / / chog par 'dzin pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa la sogs pa'o /
tatra pṛthagjanā yadi anityatādikāṃ kāṃcidevadharmatāmārabhya cittaparyavasānaṃ nītvā labdhaparitoṣā bhavantyevametaditi niścinvantaḥ sā teṣāṃ saṃtuṣṭinirvikalpatetyucyate tatra sarvatarkākhyavikalpoparateḥ
# de la so so'i skye bo rnams ni gang mi rtag pa nyid la sogs pa chos nyid 'ga' zhig las brtsams nas sems pa mthar khrid de / / 'di ni de bzhin no zhes nges par 'byed cing yongs su tshim pa thob par byed par 'gyur te / / de dag gi de ni chog par 'dzin pa'i rnam par rtog pa nyid ces bya ste / / de la mi rtog pa zhes bya ba ni rnam par rtog pa thams cad rgyun bcad pa'i phyir ro /
śrāvakāḥ skandheṣu nityādiviparyāsapratipakṣeṇa yathāvadrūpādikaṃ dharmadhātuṃ parīkṣamāṇā lokottareṇa jñānena nairātmyaṃ pratividhyantyataḥ sā teṣāmaviparyāsanirvikalpatetyucyate / bodhisattvāstadapi rūpādidharmamātraṃ prapañca iti viditvā sarvadharmanimittāni vibhāvayantaḥ paramaśāntena lokottareṇa jñānena sarvatragāṃ tathatāṃ pratividhyantyataḥ sā teṣāṃ niṣprapañcanirvikalpatetyucyate
# nyan thos rnams ni phung po rnams la rtag pa la sogs pa phyin ci log gi gnyen por ji lta ba bzhin du gzugs la sogs pa la chos tsam du yongs su brtags pas 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes pas bdag med par rtogs te / / de'i phyir de dag gi ni de phyin ci ma log pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa nyid ces bya'o / / byang chub sems dpa' ni gzugs la sogs pa chos tsam de yang spros par rig nas chos thams cad kyi mtshan ma rnam par bshig ste / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes mchog tu zhi bas de bzhin nyid thams cad du 'gro ba rtogs te /
kathaṃ punarasau niṣprapañcanirvikalpatetyucyate / yadyamanaskāratastena suptamattādīnāṃ nirvikalpatāprasaṅgaḥ teṣāṃ dharmanimittāmanaskārāt / atha samatikramatastena dvitīyadhyānāt prabhṛti sarvatra nirvikalpatā prāpnoti vitarkavicāravikalpānāṃ samatikramāt tataśca vikalpasya śarīraṃ hi cittacaittāḥ traidhātukā ityasya virodhaḥ
# de'i phyir de dag gi de ni spros pa med pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa nyid ces bya'o / / ji ltar na de spros pa med pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa zhes bya zhe na gal te yid la byed pa med pas de skad bya ba ni / / des na gnyid kyis log pa dang ra ro pha la sogs pa yang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du 'gyur te / / de dag la chos kyi mtshan ma yid la byed pa med pa'i phyir ro / / ji ste yang dag par 'das pas de skad bya na ni des na bsam gtan gnyis pa la sogs pa thams cad kyang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du 'gyur te / / rtog pa dang dpyod pa'i rnam par rtog pa rnams las yang dag par 'das pa'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir na rnam par rtog pa'i lus ni khams gsum pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'o zhes bya ba ni 'di dang 'gal lo / / ji ste rnam par zhi bas de skad bya na ni /
atha vyupaśamatastena saṃjñāveditanirodhasamāpattirnivikalpatā prāpnoti tatra cittacaitavikalpavyupaśamāt tataśca jñānābhāvaḥ prasajyate
# des na 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa yang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du 'gyur te / / der sems dang sems las byung ba'i rnam par rtog pa rnam par zhi ba'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir shes pa med par 'gyur ro /
atha svabhāvatastena rūpaṃ nirvikalpatā prāpnoti tasyāvikalpasvabhāvatvāt / athālaṃbane 'bhisaṃskārastena savikalpataiva nirvikalpatā prāpnoti nirvikalpametadityetasyābhisaṃskārasya nimittavikalpalakṣaṇatvāt
# ji ste ngo bo nyid kyis de skad bya na ni / / des na gzugs kyang rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du 'gyur te / / de rnam par mi rtog pa'i ngo bo nyid yin pa'i phyir ro / / ji ste dmigs pa la mngon bar 'du byed pa med pas de skad bya na ni / / des rnam par rtog pa dang bcas pa nyid rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du 'gyur te / / 'di ni rnam par mi rtog pa'o zhes mngon par 'du byed pa 'di ni mtshan ma la rnam par rtog pa'i mtshan nyid yin pa'i phyir ro /
tasmānnaibhiḥ prakāraiḥ nirvikalpatā draṣṭavyā
# de lta bas na rnam pa de dag gis rnam par mi rtog pa nyid du mi blta ste /
api tvālaṃbane 'nabhisaṃskāratādraṣṭavyā
# 'on kyang dmigs pa la mngon par 'du byed pa med pa nyid du blta'o /
kathaṃ kṛtvā / yadā hyasya bodhisattvasyānulomikamavavādamāgamya prakṛtyā sarvadharmanimittānyapariniṣpannānīti vicārayatastadvicāraṇābhyāsabalādhānāt pratyātmamanabhisaṃskāreṇaiva yathāvanniṣprapañcadhātau sarvadharmatathatāyāṃ cittaṃ samādhīyate sāsāvucyate niṣprapañcanirvikalpateti
# ji ltar zhe na gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' rjes su mthun pa nyid kyi gdams pa la brten nas / / chos thams cad kyi mtshan ma ni rang bzhin gyis yongs su ma grub par rnam par rtog pa ste / / rnam par rtog pa de la goms pa'i stobs bskyed pas so so rang gis mngon bar 'du byed pa med pa nyid kyis ji lta ba bzhin du spros pa med pa'i chos kyi dbyings chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid la sems mnyam par 'jog ste / / de ni de'i spros pa med pa'i rnam par mi rtog pa nyid ces bya'o /
prakṛtyā tīkṣṇendriyo bodhisattva ityuktaṃ prākkathaṃ tena kālena kālamindriyāṇyutāpayitavyānītyucyate
# byang chub sems dpa' ni rang bzhin gyis dbang po rnon po zhes sngar bshad na / / de ji ltar dus dus su dbang po rnams sbyang bar bya zhe na /
svajātīyānāṃ mṛdvāditraividhyāduttarottarābhinirhāratastaduttāpanaṃ veditavyam
# rang gi rigs kyi dbang po rtul po la sogs pa rnam pa gsum gyis gong nas gong du mngon par bsgrubs pas de sbyar bar rig par bya'o /
anyathā tīkṣṇendriyagotrāṇāmindriyāṇāmaikavidhye sati bodhisattvānāmindriyakṛto viśeṣo naivopalabhyate
# gzhan du na dbang po rnon po'i rigs rnams kyi dbang po rnams rnam pa gcig tu gyur na ni / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang por gyur pa'i khyad par mi dmigs par 'gyur na /
sa copalabhyata iti / sāṃkathyaviniścayo nāma pañcamaḥ samuccayaḥ / saptavidhasāṃkathyaviniścaye 'rthaviniścayaḥ svabhāvārthādīn ṣaḍarthānārabhya veditavyaḥ
# de yang dmigs pa de'i phyir ji skad bshad pa de grub bo / / bo ma po bcu pa ste tha ma'o / / 'bel ba'i gtam gyi rnam par nges pa bdun la don rnam par nges pa ni ngo bo nyid kyi don la sogs pa don drug las brtsams par rig par bya'o /
tatra / svabhāvastrayaḥ svabhāvāḥ parikalpitaḥ paratantraḥ pariniṣpannaśca / hetvarthastrayo hetavaḥ
# de la ngo bo nyid kyi don ni ngo bo nyid gsum ste / / kun brtags pa dang gzhan gyi dbang dang yongs su grub pa'o / / rgyu'i don ni rgyu gsum ste / / skye ba'i rgyu ni 'di lta ste /
utpattihetustathā hetusamanantarālaṃbanādhipatipratyayāḥ tataḥ sarvasaṃskṛtanirvartanāt / pravṛttihetustadyathāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā yāvatsamudayo nirodhaśca bhavatītyetayānupūrvyā saṃkleśavyavadānapravṛtteḥ
# rgyu dang de ma thag pa dang dmigs pa dang bdag po'i rkyen rnams te / / de la 'dus byas thams cad grub pa'i phyir ro / / 'byung ba'i rgyu ni 'di lta ste / / ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ba nas kun 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang 'gag par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar 'dis mthar gyis kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
siddhihetuḥ pratyakṣopalambhānupalambhasamākhyānasaṃgṛhītaḥ tena sādhyasyāpratītasyārthasya sādhanāt / phalārthaḥ pañca phalāni
# 'grub pa'i rgyu ni mngon sum du dmigs pa dang mi dmigs pa mtshungs pa sro bsnyad pas bsdus pas te / / des bsgrub par ma grags pa'i don sgrub pa'i phyir ro / / 'bras bu'i don ni 'bras bu lnga ste /
vipākaphalaṃ tadyathālayavijñānam
# rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ni 'di lta ste / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'o /
niṣpandaphalaṃ tadyathā pūrvotpannānāṃ kuśalādīnāṃ dharmāṇāṃ tatsāntānikā uttara kuśalādayo dharmāḥ
# rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu ni 'di lta ste / / sdar skyes pa'i dge ba la sogs pa'i chos rnams kyi de'i rgyu las byung ba dge ba la sogs pa chos phyi ma rnams so / / bdag po'i 'bras bu ni 'di lta ste /
adhipatiphalaṃ tadyathā sarvasattvasādhāraṇaṃ karmādhipatyena bhājanalokaḥ
# sems can thams cad kyi thun mong gi las kyi dbang gis snod kyi 'jig rten no / / skyes bu byed pa'i 'bras bu ni 'di lta ste /
puruṣakāraphalaṃ tadyathā sasyādayaḥ visaṃyogaphalaṃ tadyathāryamārgeṇānuśayasamudghātaḥ
# lo tog la sogs pa'o / / bral ba'i 'bras bu ni 'phags pa'i lam gyi bag la nyal legs par bcom pa'o /
karmārthaḥ pūrvavaddraṣṭavyastadyathā karmasaṃkleśanirdeśe
# las kyi don ni 'di lta ste / / las kyi kun nas nyon mongs pa bstan pa'o /
yogārthaḥ pañca yogāḥ sāmūhiko yogastadyathā gṛhakāṣṭheṣṭakādīnām / ānubandhiko yogastadyathānuśayādihetuḥ tathāhi tasmin satyasamudācaradbhirapi kleśādibhiryukta ityucyate
# ldan pa'i don ni rnam pa lnga ste / / mang po las gyur pa'i ldan pa ni 'di lta ste / / khang pa'i shing dang pha gu la sogs pa'o / / rjes su 'ching ba las gyur pa'i ldan pa ni 'di lta ste / / bag la nyal ba la sogs pa'i rgyu ste / / 'di ltar de yod na kun du mi spyod kyang nyon mongs pa sogs pa dang ldan pa zhes bya'o /
sāmbandhiko yogastadyathā svajanmanāṃ parasparam / āvasthiko yogastadyathānugrahādyāḥ saṃtānavyavasthāḥ tathāhi tāsu vartamānaḥ sukhena yukto yāvadduḥkhāsukhena yukta ityucyate / vaikāriko yoga āgantukopakleśādika saṃmukhībhāvaḥ tathāhi tasmin sati rāgādibhiḥ śraddhādibhiśca yukta ityucyate
# 'brel par gyur pa'i ldan pa ni 'di lta ste / / rang gi skye bo rnams phan tshun 'brel pa'o / / gnas skabs las gyur pa'i ldan pa ni 'di lta ste / / phan 'dogs pa la sogs pa'i sems kyi rgyud kyi gnas skabs te; / / 'di ltar de'i 'phral du bde ba dang ldan pa nas / / sdug bsngal yang ma yin bde ba yang ma yin pa'i bar du ldan pa zhes bya'o / / 'gyur ba las gyur pa'i ldan pa ni 'di lta ste / / glo bur gyi nye ba'i nyon mongs pa la sogs pa mngon du gyur pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / de yod na 'dod chags la sogs pa dang dad pa la sogs pa dang ldan pa zhes bya'o /
vṛttyarthaḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ
# 'jug pa'i don ni 'jug pa lnga ste /
lakṣaṇavṛttiḥ saṃskṛtasya trīṇi lakṣaṇānyutpādādīni taiḥ prakārairvartanāt
# mtshan nyid la 'jug pa ni skye ba la sogs pa 'dus byas kyi mtshan nyid gsum ste / / de dag gi rnam par 'byung ba'i phyir ro /
avasthānavṛttirādheyasyādhāre vyavasthānam
# rten la 'jug pa ni rten la gnas par bya ba gnas pa ste /
viparyāsavṛttiḥ sāṃkleśikānāṃ dharmāṇāmayathābhūtaṃ vartanāt / aviparyāsavṛttirvyāvadānikānāṃ dharmāṇām / prabhedavṛttiḥ sarvasaṃskārāṇāmatītānāgatapratyutpannādhyātmikabāhyādiprakārairvartanāt / vyākhyāviniścayo yena sūtrāntānāmarthaṃ nirdiśati
# 'di ltar sa la sems can rnams so / / phyin ci log gi 'jug pa ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos rnams te / / yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin ma yin par 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / phyin ci log ma yin pa'i 'jug pa ni 'phags pa'i lam ste / / de phyin ci ma log par 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / rab tu dbye ba'i 'jug pa ni chos rnams kyi rnam pa tha dad pa gang yin pa ste / / 'di ltar 'du byed thams cad 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba dang nang dang phyi la sogs pa'i rnam par 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / rnam par bshad pa rnam par des pa ni gang gis mdo sde rnams kyi don ston pa ste /
sa punaḥ parijñeyavastvādīnāṃ ṣaṣṇāmarthānāṃ pratisūtraṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pratipādanāt / tatra parijñeyaṃ vastu skandhādi
# de yang yongs su shes par bya ba'i dngos po la sogs pa don drug po dag mdo sde so sor ji ltar mthun mthun du ston pa'i phyir ro / / de la yongs su shes par bya ba'i dngos po ni phung po la sogs pa'o /
parijñeyo 'rtho 'nityatādi / parijñopaniṣacchīlendriyaguptadvāratādi
# yongs su shes par bya ba'i don ni mi rtag pa nyid la sogs pa'o / / yongs su shes par bya ba'i rgyu ni tshul khrims dang dbang po'i sgo bsdams pa la sogs pa'o /
parijñā bodhipakṣyā dharmāḥ
# yongs su shes pa ni byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos rnams so /
parijñāphalaṃ vimuktiḥ / tatpravedanā vimuktijñānadarśanamiti / api khalu caturdaśa mukhāni vyākhyāyāḥ
# yongs su shes pa'i 'bras bu ni rnam par grol ba'o / / de rab tu shes pa ni rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba'o / / yang rnam par bshad pa'i sgo bcu bzhi ste /
vyākhyāsaṃgrahamukhaṃ yatra sūtrasyotpattiprayojanaṃ padārtho 'nusandhirabhiprāyaścodyaparihāraśca varṇyate
# rnam par bshad pa bsdu ba'i sgo ni gang na mdo sde 'byung ba'i dgos pa dang tshig gi don dang mtshams sbyar ba dang dgongs pa dang brgal ba dang lan brjod pa'o /
vastusaṃgrahamukhaṃ yatra sūtramukhaṃ śikṣāryasatyavastvādiṣu pratipādyate / tadyathā sarvapāpasyākaraṇamiti gāthā tisraḥ śikṣāmadhikṛtyetyevamādi / aṅgopāṅgamukhaṃ yatraikena padenoddeśaḥ śeṣairnirdeśa iti pradarśyate
# dngos po bsdu ba'i sgo ni gang na mdo sde bslab pa dang 'phags pa'i bden pa dang dngos po la sogs par ston pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / sdig pa thams cad mi bya ste / / dge ba phun sum tshogs par bya / / rang gi sems ni yongs su 'dul / / 'di ni sangs rgyas bstan pa'o / / zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa bslab pa gsum gyi dbang du byas pa la sogs pa'o / / yan lag dang nye ba'i yan lag gi sgo ni gang du tshig gcig gis bstan pa la lhag ma rnams kyis bshad do zhes rab tu ston pa ste /
tadyathā dvādaśakṣaraṇasaṃnipātadeśanāyāmātmasampatparasampadityanayordvayoryathākramaṃ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiruttaraiḥ padairnideśa iti / uttarottaranirhāramukhaṃ yatrottarasyottarasyābhinirharaṇāśrayatvādette dharmā evaṃ deśitā iti pradarśyate / tadyathā pañcendriyāṇi / tathāhi śraddadhāno vīryamārabhate ārabdhavīryasya smṛtirupatiṣṭhate upasthitasmṛteścitaṃ samādhīyate samāhitacitto yathābhūtaṃ prajānātīti / pratikṣepamukhaṃ yatredamārabhyedaṃ pratikṣipyata iti pradarśyate / tadyathā vāsyaupamyasūtre āsravakṣayamārabhya catvāraḥ pudgalāḥ pratikṣipyante / ito bāhyaka ihadhārmikaḥ śrutacintāmātrasaṃtuṣṭaḥ bhāvanāyāṃ paritasyamāno 'paripūrṇasaṃbhāraśca
# dper na dal 'byor phun sum tshogs pa bcu gnyis bstan pa las bdag phun sum tshogs pa dang gzhan phun sum tshogs pa zhes bya ba'i tshig 'di gnyis go rims bzhin du tshig 'og ma lnga lngas bshad pa lta bu ste / / 'di lta ste mi nyid dang yul dbus su skyes pa dang dbang po rnams ma tshang ba med pa dang las kyi mtha' smin par ma gyur pa dag gnas su gyur pa la dad pa dang sangs rgyas rnams 'byung ba dang dam pa'i chos ston pa dang bstan pa'i chos rnams gnas pa dang gnas pa'i chos rnams kyi rjes su 'jug pa dang gzhan la snying brtse ba'o / / gong nas gong du mngon par bsgrub pa'i sgo ni gong du 'og ma ni gong ma la mngon bar bsgrub pa'i gnas yin pa'i phyir chos de dag ni de ltar bstan to zhes ston pa'o / / dper na dbang po lnga po rnams te 'di ltar dang na brtson 'grus brtsom mo / / brtson 'grus brtsams na dran pa nye bar gnas so / / dran ba nye bar gnas na sems mnyam par 'jog go / / sems mnyam par bzhag na yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so zhes bya'o / / spong ba'i sgo ni 'di las brtsams nas 'di spong bar ston pa ste / / 'di lta ste / / ste'u yu lta bu'i mdo las zag pa zad pa las brtsams nas 'di las phyi rol pa dang chos 'di ba thos pa dang sems pa tsam gyis chog par 'dzin pa dang bsgom pas yongs su yi chad pa dang tshogs yongs su ma rdzogs pa'o /
jānataścāhaṃ bhikṣavaḥ paśyataścāsravāṇāṃ kṣayaṃ vadāmītyevamādinā sūtrakhaṇḍenādyaḥ pudgalaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ
# dge slong dag nga ni shes bzhin mthong bzhin du zag pa rnams zad par smra'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i mdo'i tshig gi dum bus dang po'i gang zag spangs so /
bhāvanāyogamanuyuktasyetyevamādinā dvitīyaḥ
# sgom par sbyor ba la brtson pa zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni gnyis pa spangs so /
vāsyaupamyadṛṣṭāntena tṛtīyaḥ
# ste yu'i dpes ni gsum pa spangs so /
naudṛṣṭāntena caturtha iti
# gru'i dpas ni bzhi pa spangs so /
akṣarapaṇimamukhaṃ yatrānyasminnarthe prasiddhānyakṣarāṇyanyasmin pariṇāmyante
# yi ge yongs su sgyur ba'i sgo ni gang du don gzhan la rab tu grub pa'i yi ge rnams gzhan du yongs su bsgyur ba ste / / dper na mi gang ma dad byas mig za /
tadyathāśraddhaścākṛtajñaśceti gāthāyām
# zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i tshigs su bcad pa lta bu'o /
nāśānāśamukhaṃ tatra praṇāho 'praṇāśastadubhayopāyastadubhayaprabhedaśca pradarśyate
# chud za ba dang chud mi za ba'i sgo ni gang du rab tu chud za ba dang rab tu chud mi za ba dang de gnyi ga'i thabs dang de gnyi ga'i rab tu dbye ba ston pa ste /
tadyathā sujātasūtre praṇāśo bāhyādhyātmikopadhyavasānam
# dper na legs par skyes kyi mdo las rab tu chud za ba ni phyi dang nang gi rdzas la lhag par chags pa'o /
tatra bāhya upadhirgṛhakalatrādilakṣaṇaḥ ādhyātmikaḥ pañcopādānaskandhalakṣaṇaḥ
# de la phyi'i rdzas ni khyim dang chung ma la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid do / / nang gi rdzas ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga'i mtshan nyid do /
apraṇāśastadubhayādhyavasānavigamaḥ
# rab tu chud mi za ba ni de gnyi gal lhag par chags pa dang bral ba'o /
praṇāśopāyo 'pravrajanaṃ pravrajitasya cāsravakṣayaṃ prati pramādaḥ
# rab tu chud za ba'i thabs ni rab tu mi 'byung ba dang rab tu byung nas kyang zag pa zad par bya ba la bag mi byed pa'o /
viparyayādapraṇāśopāyo draṣṭavyaḥ / tatrobhayato vatāyaṃ sujātaḥ kulaputraḥ śobhate yacca keśaśmaśrūṇyavahārya yāvat pravrajito yaccāsravāṇāṃ kṣayādyāvatprajānāmītyanenāpraṇāśatadupāyāpadeśena tadviparītalakṣaṇapraṇāśatadupāyau sūcitau bhavataḥ
# de las bzlog pa ni chud mi za ba'i thabs su blta bar bya'o / / de la kye ma rigs kyi bu legs par skyes 'di ni gnyis kyis mdzes te / / gang skra dang kha sphu bregs nas rab tu byung ba'i bar dang gang zag pa zad nas rab tu shes so zhes bya ba'i bar 'dis chud mi za ba dang de'i thabs nye bar bstan pas de las bzlog pa'i mtshan nyid chud za ba dang de'i thabs bstan par 'gyur ro /
apraṇāśaprabhedo gāthānugītena darśitaḥ "śobhate vata bhikṣurayamupaśānto nirāśrava" iti
# chud mi za bar rab tu dbye ba'i tshigs su bcad pa'i dbyangs kyis rab tu bstan pa / / dge slong 'di ni mdzes pa ste / / nye bar zhi zhing zag pa zad /
tadevaṃ pravrajanamāsravakṣayaśca paridīpitaḥ / sa punarāsravakṣayaḥ
# ces bya ba'o / / de ltar rab tu byung ba dang zag pa zad pa yongs su bstan to / / zag pa zad pa de yang /
vītarāgo visaṃyukto hyanupādāya nirvṛtaḥ
# 'dod chags bral zhing bral ba ste / / nyer len med pas mya ngan 'das /
dhārayatyanti maṃ dehaṃ jitvā mārasya vāhinīm
# bdud kyi sde ni pham byas nas / / lus kyi tha ma 'dzin pa yin /
ityanena laukikamārgavairāgyataḥ lokottareṇa mārgeṇāvarabhāgīyasaṃyojanaprahāṇataḥ ūrdhvabhāgīyasaṃyojanaprahāṇataḥ ādhyātmikopadhiprahāṇataśca paridīpitaḥ / hetuphalakṣayādhikārāccāyaṃ nirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ
# zhes bya ba ste / / 'dis ni 'jig rten pa'i lam la 'dod chags dang bral nas 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gyis tha ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun du sbyor ba spangs pa dang gong ma'i cha dang mthun pa'i kun du sbyor ba yang spangs pa dang nang gi rdzas yongs su spangs par yang bstan pa'o / / rgyu dang 'bras bu zad pa'i skabs yin pas kyang 'di ba stan par blta'o /
etadviparyayeṇa praṇāśaprabhedaḥ sūcito draṣṭavyaḥ iti / pudgalavyavasthānamukhaṃ yatreyataḥ pudgalānadhikṛtyedaṃ bhāṣitamiti pradarśyate
# 'di las bzlog pa ni rab tu chud za ba'i bar du dbye ba bsnyad par blta bar bya'o / / gang zag rnam par gzhag pa'i sgo ni gang du gang zag 'di snyed kyi dbang du byas nas 'di gsungs so zhes bya bar ston pa ste /
tadyathā audakopame sūtre dvividhau pudgalau tricatuḥprabhedānadhikṛtya bhāṣitam pṛthagjanaṃ dṛṣṭasatyaṃ ca
# dper na chu las gyur pa lta bu'i mdo las byung ba lta bu ste / / de ni gang zag gnyis dang gsum dang bzhir rab tu dbye ba'i dbang du mdzad nas gsungs te /
pṛthagjanastribhedaḥ aśuklo 'lpaśuklaḥ bahuśuklaśca
# so so'i skye bo dang bden pa mthong ba'o / / so so'i skye bo ni gsum du rab tu phye nas bsnyad par blta bar bya ste /
dṛṣṭasatyaścatuḥprabhedaḥ catvāraḥ pratipannakāḥ catvāraḥ phalasthāḥ trayaḥ śekṣāḥ eko 'śaikṣaḥ
# dkar po ma yin pa dang cung zad dkar ba dang cher dkar ba'o / / bden pa mthong ba ni bzhir rab tu dbye ste / / 'bras bu la gnas pa bzhi ste / / gsum ni slob pa'o /
prabhedavyavasthānamukhaṃ yatra catuṣkoṭikadibhiḥ praśnairartho varṇyate
# gcig ni mi slob pa'o / / rab tu dbye ba rnam par gzhag pa'i sgo ni gang du mu bzhi la sogs pa dri ba rnams kyi don brjod pa ste /
tadyathānityasūtre yaḥ sadidaṃ samanupaśyati sarvo 'sau rūpaṃ samanupaśyati yo vā rūpaṃ samanupaśyati sarvaḥ sa sadidaṃ samanupaśyatīti catuṣkoṭikaḥ / prathamā koṭirvedanārdīścaturaḥ skandhānnityaśucisukhātmaviparyāsairasamāropya parijñeyaprahātavyāṃśca samanupaśyataḥ
# dper ni mi rtag pa'i mdo las gang gis 'di legs par mthong ba des gzugs thams cad mthong ngam / / gang gis gzugs thams cad mthong ba des thams cad legs par mthong ngam zhes bya ba mu bzhi'o / / mu dang po ni tshor ba la sogs pa phung po bzhi la rtag pa dang gtsang ba dang bde ba dang bdag tu phyin ci log tu sgro ma btags par yongs su shes par bya ba dang spang bar bya ba yang dag par rjes su blta ba'o /
dvitīyā koṭī rūpaṃ nityaśucisukhātmaviparyāsaiḥ samāropyāparijñeyāprahātavyaṃ ca samanupaśyataḥ
# mu gnyis pa ni gzugs la rtag pa dang gtsang ba dang bde ba dang bdag tu phyin ci log tu sgro btags nas yongs su shes par bya ba ma yin pa dang yongs su spang bar bya ba ma yin par yang dag par rjes su blta ba'o /
tṛtīyā koṭī rūpaṃ nityaśucisukhātmaviparyāsairasamāropya parijñeyaprahātavyāṃśca samanupaśyataḥ caturthīkoṭirvedanādīṃścaturaḥ skandhānnityaśucisukhātmaviparyāsaiḥ samāropyāparijñeyāprahātavyaṃ ca samanupaśyataḥ / yathā rūpe catuṣkoṭika evaṃ vedanādau sarvatra vistareṇa draṣṭavyam
# mu gsum pa ni gzugs la rtag pa dang gtsang ba dang bde ba dang bdag tu phyin ci log tu sgro ma btags par yongs su shes par bya ba dang yongs su spang bar bya ba yang dag par rdzes su blta ba'o / / mu bzhi pa ni tshor ba la sogs pa phung po bzhi la rtag pa dang gtsang ba dang bde ba dang bdag tu phyin ci log tu sgro btags nas yongs su shes par bya ba ma yin pa dang spang bar bya ba ma yin par yang dag par rjes su blta ba'o / / gzugs la mu bzhi ji lta ba de bzhin du tshor ba la sogs pa thams cad la yang rgya cher sbyar bar bya'o /
yāvadyasya kṛtaṃ karaṇīyaṃ sarvaḥ sa nāparamasmādbhavaṃ prajānāti yāvannāparamasmādbhavaṃ prajānāti sarvasya tasya kṛtaṃ karaṇīyam
# gang bya ba byas pa de thams cad 'di las srid pa gzhan mi shes so zhes bya ba yin nam / / gang 'di las srid pa gzhan mi shes pa de thams cad bya ba byas pa yin nam zhes bya ba'i bar du'o /
āha catuṣkoṭikam
# smras pa / / mu bzhi ste /
prathamā koṭiryāvajjīvaṃ sucaritacāriṇaḥ pṛthagjanasya
# mu dang po ni ji srid 'tsho'i bar du legs par spyad pa spyod pa'i so so'i skye bo'i'o /
dvitīyocchedadṛṣṭayādīnām / tṛtīyā aśaikṣasya
# gnyis pa ni chad par lta ba la sogs pa'o / / gsum pa ni mi slob pa'i'o /
caturthī tānākārān sthāpayitvā
# bzhi pa ni rnam pa de dag ma gtogs pa'i'o zhes 'byung ba lta bu'o /
nayamukhaṃ yatra ṣaḍbhirnayairartho varṇyate tattvārthanayena prāptinayena deśanānayenāntadvayavivarjanānayenācintyanayenābhiprāyanayena ca
# tshul gyi sgo ni gang du tshul drug gi sa bon brjod pa ste / / de kho na'i don gyi tshul dang 'thob pa'i tshul dang bshad pa'i tshul dang mtha' gnyis spangs pa'i tshul dang bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i tshul dang dgongs pa'i tshul gyis so /
eṣāṃ ca ṣaṇṇāṃ nayānāṃ pūrvakāstrayo nayā uttaraistribhirnayairyathākramamanugantavyāḥ
# tshul drug po 'di dag las tshul gong ma gsum ni tshul 'og ma gsum gyis go rims bzhin du rig par bya ste /
tadyathāsvādanasūtre asti bhikṣavaḥ rūpe āsvāda ityevamādināpavādāntaṃ samāropāntaṃ ca varjayitvā tattvārthanayo 'bhidyotitaḥ / astyāsvāda ādīnavo niḥsaraṇamityanenāpavādānto varjitaḥ rūpe yāvadvijñāna ityanena samāropāntaḥ skandhamātre saṃkleśo vyavadānaṃ cānātmanīti pradarśayatā yāvaccāhaṃ bhikṣavaḥ yāvadanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddho 'smītyadhyajñāsiṣamityanena prāptinayo 'cintyanayena paridīpitaḥ pratyātmavedanīyādhigamasūcanāt / sarvamevedaṃ sūtraṃ deśanānayaḥ
# dper na ro myang ba'i mdo las dge slong dag gzugs la ro myong ba yod do zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni skur pa 'debs pa'i mtha' dang sgro 'dogs pa'i mtha' spangs nas de kho na'i don gyi tshul ston to / / ro myang ba dang nyes dmigs dang nges par 'byung ba yod do zhes bya ba 'dis ni skur ba 'debs pa'i mtha' spangs so / / gzugs nas rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i bar 'dis ni sgro 'dogs pa'i mtha' spangs te / / phung po tsam la kun nas nyon mongs pa'am / / rnam par byang bar zad kyi bdag ni med do zhes rab tu bstan to / / dge slong dag ngas ji tsam tu bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi bar du mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas so zhes bya bar nang du 'du shes so zhes bya ba 'dis ni 'thob pa'i tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i tshul gyis yongs su bstan te / / so so rang gis rig par bya ba thob par ston pa'i phyir ro / / mdo 'di thams cad ni bshad pa'i tshul gyis so /
sa cābhiprāyeṇānugantavyaḥ / sa parijñeyaṃ vastu parijñeyamartham parijñām parijñāphalam tatpravedanāṃ cābhipretyedaṃ sūtraṃ bhāṣitamiti
# de yang dgongs pa'i tshul gyis khong du chud par bya ste / / yongs su shes par bya ba'i dngos po dang yongs su shes par bya ba'i don dang yongs su shes pa dang yongs su shes par bya ba'i 'bras bu dang de rab tu shes pa la dgongs nas mdo de dag bshad do /
tatra parijñeyaṃ vastu rūpādikam
# de la yongs su shes par bya ba'i dngos po ni gzugs la sogs pa'o /
parijñeyo 'rtha āsvādādikaḥ tena prakāreṇa tasya rūpādikasya vastunaḥ parijñānāt
# yongs su shes bar bya ba'i don ni ro myang ba la sogs pa ste / / rnam pa des gzugs la sogs pa'i dngos po de yongs su shes pa'i phyir ro /
parijñaiṣāṃ pañcānāmupādānaskandhānāmevaṃ triparivartena yathābhūtaparijñānam
# yongs su shes pa ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po dag nga ltar gsum du bsgyur bas yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs pa'i shes pa'o /
parijñāphalamasmāt sadevakāllokādyāvat sadevamānuṣāyāḥ prajñāyā vimuktiryāvadvipramuktiḥ
# yongs su shes pa'i 'bras bu ni lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten 'di las zhes bya ba nas / / lha dang mi dang bcas pa zhes bya ba'i bar las grol ba nas rnam par rab tu grol zhes bya ba'i bar du'o /
tatpravedanānuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbuddho 'smītyadhyajñāsiṣamiti
# de rab tu shes pa ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par nang du shes so zhes bya ba'o /
parijñādimukhaṃ yatra tattvalakṣaṇamāramya parijñālakṣaṇena prahāṇalakṣaṇena sākṣātkriyālakṣaṇena eṣāmeva tattvalakṣaṇādīnāṃ prakārabhedalakṣaṇena āśrayāśritasaṃvandhalakṣaṇena parijñādīnāmāntarāyikadharmalakṣaṇena āmulomikadharmalakṣaṇena aparijñādiṣu cādīnavānuśaṃsālakṣaṇena cārtho nirdiśyate
# yongs su shes pa la sogs pa'i sgo ni gang du de kho na'i mtshan nyid las brtsams nas yongs su shes pa'i mtshan nyid dang spong ba'i mtshan nyad dang mngon sum du byed pa'i mtshan nyid dang bsgom pa'i mtshan nyid dang de kho na'i mchan nyid la sogs pa 'di dag gi rnam pa'i rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid dang; gnas dang gnas par 'brel ba'i mtshan nyid dang yongs su shes pa la sogs pa'i bar du gcod pa'i chos kyi mtshan nyid dang rjes su mthun pa'i chos kyi mtshan nyid dang yongs su ma shes pa la sogs pa dang yongs su shes pa la sogs pa la nyes dmigs dang phan yon gyi mtshan nyid kyis don ston pa ste /
tadyathātraivāsvādanasūtre
# dper na ro myang ba'i mdo de nyid las 'byung ba /
tatra tattvalakṣaṇamupādānaskandhasaṃgṛhītaduḥkhasatyam
# de la de kho na'i mtshan nyid ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lngas bsdus pa sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'o /
parijñālakṣaṇaṃ tasyaivāsvādādinā yathābhūtaṃ parijñānam / prahāṇalakṣaṇaṃ sākṣātkriyālakṣaṇaṃ ca sarvasmāllokādvimuktiḥ āvaraṇaprahāṇe nāśrayaparivṛttisākṣātkaraṇāt bhāvanālakṣaṇaṃ viparyāsāpagatena cetasā bahulavihāraḥ
# yongs su shes pa'i mtshan nyid ni ro myang ba la sogs pas de nyid yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so; ;spang ba'i mtshan nyid dang mngon sum du byed pa'i mtshan nyid ni 'jig rten thams cad las rnam par grol ba ste / / sgrib pa spong ba dang gnas gyur pa mngon sum du byed pa'i phyir ro / / bsgom pa'i mtshan nyid ni phyin ci log dang bral ba'i sems kyis len mang du gnas pa'o /
prakārabhedalakṣaṇam tattvalakṣaṇasya pañcadhā bhedo rūpaṃ yāvadvijñānamiti
# rnam par rab tu dbye ba'i mtshan nyid ni de kho na'i mtshan nyid rnam pa lnga'i dbye ba ste / / gzugs nas rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o /
parijñālakṣaṇasya tridhā bheda āsvādaṃ cāsvādayato yāvanniḥsaraṇaṃ ca niḥsarato yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti
# yongs su shes pa'i mtshan nyid ni rnam par gsum du rab tu dbye ste / / ro myang ba la ro myang ba dang nyes dmigs la nyes dmigs dang nges par 'byung ba'i bar la nges par 'byung bar yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so /
prahāṇalakṣaṇasya sākṣātkriyālakṣaṇasya dvidhā bhedaḥ kleśavimuktirduḥkhavimuktiśca
# spong ba'i mtshan nyid dang mngon sum du byed pa'i mtshan nyid ni rnam pa gnyis su dbye ste / / nyon mongs pa las rnam par grol ba dang sdug bsngal las rnam par grol ba'o /
tatra sadevakāllokādyāvatsadevamānuṣāyāḥ prajāyā vimuktiḥ kleśebhyo vimokṣādata eva tadviśeṣaṇārthamāha niḥsṛta iti
# de la lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten zhes bya ba nas / / lha dang mir bcas pa'i skye dgu'i bar las grol ba ni nyon mongs pa rnams las rnam par thar pa'i phyir ro / / de bas na de bye brag tu bya ba'i phyir nges par 'byung ba zhes gsungs te /
tadyathā hyanyatra sūtre niḥsaraṇaṃ katamadbhayaḥ
# 'di ltar mdo gzhan las nges par 'byung ba gang zhe na /
chandarāgavinayaḥ chandarāgaprahāṇaṃ chandarāgasamatikrama ityuktam / evamanāgataduḥkhābhinirvartaka kleśavisaṃyoge sati duḥkhādapi vipramukto bhavatīti viśeṣaṇārthamāha visaṃyukto vipramukta iti
# gang 'dir 'dun pa dang 'dod chags 'dul ba dang 'dun pa dang 'dod chags spang ba dang 'dun pa dang 'dod chags las yang dag par 'da' ba'o zhes gsungs so / / de ltar ma 'ongs pa'i sdug bsngal mngon bar 'grub par byed pa'i nyon mongs pa dang bral na sdug bsngal las kyang rnam par grol bar 'gyur ro zhes bye brag tu bya ba'i phyir bral ba dang rnam par grol ba zhes bya ba gsungs so /
bhāvanālakṣaṇasya dvidhā bhedo darśanamārgo bhāvanāmārgaśca / tatra viparyāsāpagatena cetaseti darśanamārgaṃ darśayati bahulaṃ vyahārṣamityanena bhāvanāmārgam
# bsgom pa'i mtshan nyid ni rnam pa gnyis su rab tu dbye ste / / mthong ba'i lam dang bsgom pa'i lam mo / / de la phyin ci log dang bral ba'i sems kyis zhes bya ba ni / / mthong ba'i lam ston to / / len mang du gnas par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba 'di ni bsgom pa'i lam ston to /
āśrayāśritasaṃbandhalakṣaṇaṃ tatvalakṣaṇādīnāmuttarottarāṇāmāśrayatvasūcanāt
# gnas dang gnas par 'brel ba'i mtshan nyid ni / / de kho na'i mtshan nyid la sogs pa 'og ma gong ma'i gnas yin par ston pa'i phyir ro /
parijñādīnāmāntarāyikalakṣaṇamevaṃ triparivartena yathābhūtamaparijñānam
# yongs su shes pa la sogs pa'i bar du gcod pa'i mtshan nyid ni de ltar gsum du bsgyur ba yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par mi shes pa'o /
anulomikalakṣaṇaṃ yathāvyavasthānameṣāmeva rūpādīnāmāsvādādito vicāraṇā
# rjes su mthun pa'i mtshan nyid ni gzugs la sogs pa 'di dag ji ltar gnas pa bzhin du nyes dmigs la sogs par rnam par dpyod pa'o /
aparijñānādīnavalakṣaṇamavimuktiryāvadanuttarāyāḥ samyaksaṃbodherasaṃbodhaḥ / viparyayādanuśaṃsalakṣaṇaṃ veditavyamiti
# yongs su mi shes pa la sogs pa la nyes dmigs kyi mtshan nyid ni mi grol ba nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang mi rgya pa'i bar du'o / / de las bzlog pa ni phan yon gyi mchan nyid du rig par bya'o /
balābalamukhaṃ yatraikena padenānucyamānenāyamartho na gamitaḥ syāditi pratyekaṃ sarveṣāṃ padānāṃ sāmarthya pradarśyate
# stobs dang stobs ma yin pa'i sgo ni gang du tshig gcig ma brjod na don 'di go bar mi 'gyur bas tshig so so thams cad kyis nus pa ston pa ste / / dper na rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i mdo las 'di yod pas 'di 'byung / / 'di skyes pa'i phyir 'di skye ba ste /
tadyathā pratītyotpādasūtre 'smin satīdaṃ bhavatyasyotpādādidamutpadyate yadutāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ityevamādi eṣāṃ ca padānāṃ pratyekaṃ sāmarthya pūrvavadveditavya yathā pratītyasamutpādasya lakṣaṇanirdeśe
# 'di ltar ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa lta bu'o / / tshig 'di dag gi so so'i nus pa ni ji ltar gang du rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid du bshad pa bzhin du rig par bya'o /
pratyāhāramukhaṃ yatra sūtrasyaikaṃ padaṃ gṛhītvā vistareṇārthaḥ pratinirdiśyate
# bzlas te brjod pa'i sgo ni gang du mdo'i tshig gcig bzung bas rgya cher don yang dag par ston pa ste /
tadyathā ṣaḍbhirdharmaiḥ samanvāgato bhikṣurhimavantamapi parvatarājaṃ mukhavāyunā cālayet kaḥ punarvādaḥ savāsanāyā avidyāyāḥ
# dper na chos drug dang ldan pa'i dge slong ni kha'i dbugs kyis ri'i rgyal po gangs ri yang 'thor na ro lta bu'i ma rig pa lta smos kyang ci dgos /
katamaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ / iha bhikṣavo bhikṣuścittasyotpādakuśalo bhavati iha bhikṣurviviktaṃ kāmairyāvaccaturthadhyānamupasaṃpadya viharati / evaṃ hi bhikṣuścittasyotpādakuśalo bhavati
# drug gang zhe na / / 'di la dge slong dag 'di la dge slong sems bskyed pa la mkhas pa yin pa nas / / thabs la mkhas pa yin no zhes bya ba'i bar du gsungs pa lta bu'o / / mdo 'di las ji ltar na dge slong sems bskyed pa la mkhas pa yin zhe na / / 'di la dge slong ni 'dod pa dag las dben pa nas bsam gtan bzhi pa'i bar du rdzogs par byas nas gnas te / / de ltar na dge slong sems bskyed pa la mkhas pa yin no /
kathaṃ ca bhikṣuścittasya sthitikuśalo bhavati
# ji ltar na dge slong sems gnas pa la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
iha bhikṣurāsevanānvayādyaddhānabhāgīyaṃ dhyānaṃ tat sthitibhāgīyaṃ karoti
# 'di la dge slong ni kun du bsten pa'i rgyu'i bar gyis gang nyams pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i bsam gtan de gnas pa'i cha dang mthun par byed de /
evaṃ bhikṣuḥ sthitikuśalo bhavati
# de ltar na dge slong de sems gnas pa la mkhas pa yin no /
kathaṃ ca bhikṣurvyutthānakuśalo bhavati
# ji ltar na dge slong de sems ldang bar byed pa la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
iha bhikṣurāsevanānvayādyatsthitibhāgīyaṃ dhyānaṃ tadviśeṣabhāgīyaṃ karoti
# 'di la dge slong ni kun du bsten pa'i rgyus gnas pa'i cha dang mthun pa'i bsam gtan de khyad par du gyur pa'i cha dang mthun par byed de /
evaṃ hi bhikṣurvyutthānakuśalo bhavati
# de ltar na dge slong ldang bar byed pa la mkhas pa yin no /
kathaṃ ca bhikṣurāyakuśalo bhavati
# ji ltar na dge slong 'phel bar byed pa la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
iha bhikṣuranutpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāmiti vistareṇa dve samyakprahāṇe
# 'di la dge slong ni dge ba'i chos ma skyes pa rnams zhes bya ba yang dag par spang ba nyid rgya cher bya ste /
evaṃ hi bhikṣurāyakuśalo bhavati
# de ltar na dge slong 'phel ba la mkhas pa yin no /
kathaṃ ca bhikṣurapāyakuśalo bhavati
# ji ltar na de slong 'bri ba la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
iha hi bhikṣurutpannānāṃ pāpakā nāmakuśalānāmiti vistareṇa dve samyakprahāṇe
# sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos skyes pa rnams zhes bya ba yang dag par spong ba gnyis kyis rgya cher bya ste /
evaṃ hi bhikṣurapāyakuśalo bhavati
# de ltar na dge slong 'bri ba la mkhas pa yin no /
kathaṃ hi bhikṣurupāyakuśalo bhavati
# ji ltar na dge slong thabs la mkhas pa yin zhe na /
iha hi bhikṣuśchandasamādhipradhānasaṃskārasamanvāgatamṛddhipādaṃ bhāvayatīti vistareṇa catvāra ṛddhipādāḥ / evaṃ hi bhikṣurupāyakuśalo bhavatīti
# 'di la dge slong ni 'dun pa'i ting nge 'dzin spong ba'i 'du byed dang ldan pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bsgom mo zhes bya ba la sogs pa rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi rgya cher sbyar te / / de ltar na dge slong thabs la mkhas pa yin no zhes 'byung ngo /
abhinirhāramukhaṃ yatra pratipadaṃ catuṣkādibhirnirdiśyate
# mngon par sgrub pa'i sgo ni gang du tshig re re la yang mu bzhi la sogs pa ston pa ste /
teṣvapi catuṣkādiṣvekaikaṃ padamaparaiścatuṣkādibhiraparyanto hi nirhāro veditavyaḥ
# mu bzhi pa la sogs pa la de dag gi tshig re re la yang gzhan bzhi la sogs pas thug pa med par mngon bar bsgrub par rig par bya'o / / dper na sangs rgyas rtsom pa'i mdo las /
tadyathā buddhākṣepasūtre catvāra ime bodhisattvānāṃ bodhipariśodhakā dharmāḥ śūnyatābhāvanā sarvasattveṣvapratihatacittatā bodhisattvānāṃ nityaṃ hitopasaṃharaṇatā nirāmiṣeṇa cittena dharmadānasaṃprakāśanatā ceti / catuṣkaḥ svārtha paramārtha cārabhya bodhipariśodhanāya caturvipakṣapratipakṣeṇa veditavyaḥ
# bzhi po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub yongs su sbyong bar byed pa'i chos rnams te / / stong pa nyid sgom pa dang sems can thams cad la zhe 'gras pa med pa'i sems dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams la rtag tu phan pa nye bar sgrub pa'i sems dang zang zing med pa'i sems kyis chos kyi sbyin pa yang dag par rab tu ston pa'o zhes bya ba bzhi ni bdag dang gzhan gyi don las brtsams te / / byang chub yongs su sbyong ba'i phyir mi mthun pa'i phyogs bzhi'i gnyen por rig par bya'o /
catvāro vipakṣāḥ samāpattyāsvādanā vyāpādaḥ mānaḥ tṛṣṇā ca lābhasatkāre
# mi mthun pa'i phyogs bzhi ni snyoms par 'jug pa'i ro myang ba dang gnod sems dang nga rgyal dang rnyed pa dang bkur sti la sred pa'o /
aparaḥ paryāyaḥ prathamena dharmeṇa kleśaprahāṇapratipakṣaḥ / śeṣairhīnayānaparivarjanā paridīpitāstribhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ bodhicittena sarvasattvopādānataḥ avatīrṇaparipācanataḥ anavatīrṇāvatāraṇataśca
# rnams grangs gzhan du na chos dang pos ni nyon mongs pa spong ba'i gnyen po bstan to / / lhag ma rnams kyis ni rgyu gsum gyis theg pa dman pa yongs su spang bar bsten te / / byang chub kyi sems kyis sems can thams cad nye bar 'dzin pa dang zhugs pa yongs su smin par byed pa dang ma zhugs pa 'jug par byed pas so / / rnam grangs gzhan du na dang pos ni ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su bstan to /
aparaḥ paryāyaḥ prathamena jñānasaṃbhārastribhiḥ puṇyasaṃbhāraḥ paridīpitaḥ upādānaparipācanāvatāraṇaiḥ pratyekaṃ puṇyaviśeṣaprasavanataḥ
# gsum gyis ni bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs su bstan te / / nye bar 'dzin pa dang yongs su smin par byed pa dang 'jug pa rnam pa re res kyang bsod nams kyi khyad par skyed pa'i phyir ro / / yang rgyu gnyis kyis rig par bya ste /
punardvābhyāṃ kāraṇābhyāmāśayataśca maitracittatayā pratipattitaścādhigamāgamopadeśābhyām / caturbhirdharmaiḥ samanvāgatā bodhisattvāḥ śūnyatāṃ bhāvayanti adhyātmaṃ cittāvikaṃpanatayādhimuktipravicayabalādhānatayā sarvadharmāṇāṃ yathātmyaprativedhataḥ sarvāvaraṇavimokṣataśca / yadāśritya yathā ca bhāvayanti tadetena paridīpitam
# bsam pas ni byams pa'i sems su'o / / bsgrub bas ni thob pa dang lung nye bar ston par rig par bya'o / / chos bzhi dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' stong pa nyid bsgom ste / / nang du sems su rnam par mi rtog pa dang mos pa la rab tu rnam par 'byed pa'i stobs skyed pa dang chos thams cad ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs par byed pa dang sgrib pa thams cad las rnam par thar pa ste / / 'di dag gis ni gang la brten nas ji ltar bsgom pa de yongs su bsten to /
kimāśritya / dhyānapāramitām / kathaṃ bhāvayanti
# gang la brten nas she na / / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'o / / ji ltar bsgom zhe na /
pṛthagjanamārgeṇa śrutacintābalādhānataḥ śaikṣamārgeṇāśaikṣamārgeṇa ca / caturbhirdharmaiḥ samanvāgatā bodhisattvāḥ sarvasattveṣvapratihatacittā bhavanti maitrībhāvanayā pratipatyavikopanatayā nimittāvikalpanatayā khedasahiṣṇutayā ca / atrāpi yadāśritya yathā cāpratihatacittā bhavanti tatparidīpitaṃ bhavati
# so so'i skye bo'i lam gyis thos pa dang bsam pa'i stobs skyed pa dang slob pa'i lam dang mi slob pa'i lam gyis so / / byang chub sems dpa' chos bzhi dang ldan na / / sems can thams cad la zhe 'gras ba med pa'i sems dang ldan pa yin te / / byams pa bsgom pa dang sgrub pa rnam par mi 'khrugs pa dang mtshan ma la rnam par mi rtog pa dang skyo ba bzod pa'o / / 'dir yang gang la brten nas ji ltar zhe 'gras pa med pa'i sems dang ldan pa yin pa de yongs su bstan to /
kimāśritya / paurvajanmikīṃ maitrībhāvanām
# gang la brten nas she na / / tshe rabs snga ma'i byams pa bsgoms pa las so /
kathamapratihatacittā bhavanti
# ji ltar zhe 'gras pa med pa'i sems dang ldan pa yin zhe na /
mithyāpratipattisthiteṣu svacitāvikopanataḥ apakāriṣvapakāranimittāvikalpanataḥ parahitārthaṃ vyāyāmāparikhedataśca / caturbhirdharmaiḥ samanvāgatā bodhisattvā bodhisattvānāṃ nityaṃ hitamupasaṃharanti ātmanaḥ paritulanatayā samyagavavādapravartanatayā saurabhyasukhasaṃvāsanatayā pūjālābhasatkāraparicaryopasaṃharaṇatayā ca / atrāpi yadāśritya yathā copasaṃharati tatparidīpitam
# log par sgrub pa la gnas pa rnams la sems rnam par mi 'khrugs pa dang gnod par byed pa rnams la gnod par byed pa'i mtshan mar rnam par mi rtog pa dang gzhan la phan pa'i don du rtsol ba la yongs su mi skyo ba'o / / byang chub sems dpa' chos bzhi dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' rnams la rtag tu phan pa nye bar bsgrub pa yin te / / bdag yongs su 'jal ba dang yang dag pa'i gdams pa la 'jug pa dang des shing 'grogs na bde ba dang mchod pa dang rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang bsnyen bkur bya ba nye bar sgrub pa'o / / 'dir yang gang la brten nas ji ltar nye bar ba sgrub pa de yongs su bsten to /
kimāśritya / nihatamānatām
# gang la brten nas she na / / nga rgyal bcag pa la'o /
kathamupasaṃharati
# ji ltar nye bar bsgrub ce na /
yathoktaṃ tribhiḥ prakārairhīnasamaśiṣṭānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ yathākramam
# ji skad bstan pa rnam pa gsum gyis dma' ba dang mtshungs pa dang khyad par du 'phags pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la go rims bzhin no /
caturbhirdharmaiḥ samanvāgatā bodhisattvā nirāmiṣeṇa cittena dharmadānaṃ saṃprakāśayanti antarāyasukhaprativedhatayā mohalayāpanayanakauśalyatayā nāthakaradharmārāmatayā ca
# byang chub sems dpa' chos bzhi dang ldan na zang zing med pa'i sems kyis chos kyi sbyin pa yang dag par rab tu ston te / / bar du gcod pa legs par rab tu rtogs pa dang rmongs pa dang bying ba sel ba la rab tu mkhas pa dang yid bde ba nye bar sgrub pa dang mgon byed pa'i chos las dga' ba'o /
atrāpi yadāśritya / yathā ca saṃprakāśayanti tatparidīpitam
# 'dir yang gang la brten nas ji ltar yang dag par rab tu ston pa de yongs su bstan to /
kimāśritya / lābhasatkārasyāntarāyakaratvaprativeghatām
# gang la brten nas she na / / rnyed pa dang bkur sti bar du gcod par byed pa nyid du legs par rtogs pa la'o /
kathaṃ saṃprakāśayanti
# ji ltar yang dag par rab tu ston ce na /
saṃdarśanato mūḍhānām samādāpanataḥ samuttejanataśca pramādasaṅgānātmaparibhavena vā līnānām saṃpraharṣaṇataḥ samyakpratipannānām prakṛtyaiva ca dharmārāmatayā
# rmongs pa rnams la yang dag par ston pa dang bag med pa la chags pa dang bdag dman par 'dzin pas zhum pa rnams la yang dag par 'dzin du 'jug pa dang yang dag par gzengs bstod pa dang yang dag bar zhugs pa rnams la yang dag par rab tu dga' bar byed ba dang rang bzhin gyis chos la dga' bas so /
prathamasyānyacatuṣkaḥ padaprabhedādibhirnirhāro veditavyaḥ
# de ltar bzhi pa gzhan ni bzhi pa dang po'i tshig rab tu dbye ba mngon par sgrub par rig par bya'o /
prabhidyasaṃdarśanaviniścayo yathānirdiṣṭeṣu skandhādiṣu dharmeṣu yathāyogamekāvacārakādīni / tatra / ekāvacārako nāma praśno yenaikaṃ dharmaṃ pariśiṣṭaiḥ saha pratyekaṃ praśnayitvā tamapahāya dvitīyaṃ tenānyaiśca saha praśnayatyevamekaikasyaiva sarvān praśnayati
# rab tu phye nas kun tu bstan pa rnam par nges pa ni ji skad du bstan pa'i phung po la sogs pa'i chos rnams la gcig nas rtogs pa la sogs par ci rigs par sbyar ro / / de la gcig nas rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i dri ba ni gang gis chos gcig chos lhag ma gzhan rnams dang lhan cig tu re re nas dris nas de bor te / / des gnyis ba yang gzhan rnams dang lhan cig tu 'dri ba'o / / de bzhin du re re nas thams cad 'dri ba ste /
tadyathā yaścakṣurāyatanena samanvāgato rūpāyatanenāpi saḥ yo vā rūpāyatanena cakṣurāyatanenāpi sa iti pūrvapādakaḥ
# dper na gang mig gi skye mched dang ldan pa de gzugs kyi skye mched dang yang ldan nam / / gang gzugs kyi skye mched dang ldan pa de mig gi skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes bya ba ni tshig gong ma dang sbyar ba'o /
yaścakṣurāyatanena samanvāgataḥ śrotrāyatanenāpi sa ityatra catuṣkoṭikam
# gang mig gi skye mched dang ldan pa de rnam ba'i skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes bya ba 'di la mu bzhi'o /
evaṃ yāvanmanaāyatanenāpi sa ityatra yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyam
# de bzhin du de yid kyi skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes bya ba'i bar du 'di la mu ci rigs su sbyar bar bya'o /
dharmāyatanenāpi sa ityatra pūrvapādakaḥ / yo rūpāyatanena samanvāgataścakṣurāyatanenāpi saḥ yo vā cakṣurāyatanena rūpāyatanenāpi sa iti paścātpādakaḥ / yo rūpāyatanena samanvāgataḥ śrotrāyatanenāpi sa ityatra cāpi paścātpādakaḥ
# de la chos kyi skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes bya ba 'di ni tshig gong ma dang sbyar bar bya'o / / gzugs kyi skye mched dang ldan pa gang yin pa de mig gi skye mched dang yang ldan nam / / gang mig gi skye mched dang ldan pa de gzugs kyi skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes bya ba 'di ni tshig 'og ma dang yang sbyar ba'o / / gang gzugs kyi skye mched dang ldan pa de rna ba'i skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes bya ba 'di yang tshig 'og ma dang sbyar bar bya'o /
evaṃ yāvaddharmāyatanena yathāyogaṃ yojayitavyam / yaḥ śrotrāyatanena samanvāgataścakṣurāyatanenāpi sa ityatra catuṣkoṭikam
# de bzhin du chos kyi skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes ci rigs su sbyar bar bya'o / / gang rna ba'i skye mched dang ldan pa de ni mig gi skye mched dang yang ldan nam zhes bya ba 'di la mu bzhi'o /
evaṃ yāvaddharmāyatanenāpi yojyam
# de bzhin du chos kyi skye mched kyi bar du yang sbyar bar bya'o /
evamekaṃkāmarṣeṇānukramaśaḥ sarvāṇyāyatanāni parasparaṃ yojayitavyāni
# de ltar re re nas gsal ba'i tshul gyis skye mched thams cad phan tshun du sbyar bar bya'o /
pūrvapādakaṃ dvayordharmayoḥ kathaṃcideva dharmamārabhya parasparaṃ pṛṣṭayoḥ pūrvadharmamadhiṣṭhāya yadvayākriyate
# tshig gong ma dang sbyor ba gnyis gnyis po ni chos 'ga' zhig la brtsams nas phan tshun dris na chos gong ma la brten nas gang lung ston pa ste / / dper na shes pa gang yin pa de shes bya yang de'am /
tadyathā yajjñānaṃ jñeyamapi tadyadvā jñeyaṃ jñānamapi taditi / pūrvapādakam yattāvajjñānaṃ jñeyamapi taditi / syājjñeyaṃ na jñānam tadanye dharmā iti
# shes bya gang yin pa shes pa yang de 'am zhes bya ba'i ni tshig gong ma dang sbyor ba ste / / shes pa gang yin pa de shes bya yang de yin no / / shes bya yin la shes pa ma yin pa'ang yod de / / de las gzhan pa'i chos rnams so /
paścātpādakaṃ tathaiva dvayordharmayoḥ parasparaṃ pṛṣṭayoryatpaścimamadhiṣṭhāya vyākriyate
# tshig 'og ma dang sbyor ba ni / / de bzhin du gnyis gnyis dris pa la gang phyi ma la brten nas lung ston pa ste /
tadyathā yadgrāhyaṃ grāhakamapi tadyadvā grāhakaṃ grāhyamapi taditi / paścātpādakam yattāvadgrāhakaṃ grāhyamapi tat
# dper na gzung ba gang yin pa de 'dzin pa'ang de 'am / / 'dzin pa gang yin pa de gzung ba'ang de'am zhes bya ba ni tshig 'og ma dang sbyor ba ste / / 'dzin pa gang yin pa gzung ba yang de'o /
syādgrāhyaṃ na grāhakam rūpādayaḥ pañca viṣayā dharmāyatanaṃ ca saṃprayuktakavarjyam / dvikoṭikaṃ yatra dve koṭī vyākriyete tadanyāsaṃbhavāt tadyathā skandhasya vyavasthānaṃ dhātuvyavasthānaṃ ca nigamayyocyate yā skandhasaṃkhyā dhātusaṃkhyāpi sā yā vā dhātusaṃkhyā skandhasaṃkhyāpi seti
# gzung ba yin la 'dzin pa ma yin pa'ang yod de / / gzugs la sogs pa yul lnga po dag dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma gtogs pa'i chos kyi skye mched do / / mu gnyis pa ni gang du mu gnyis ston pa ste / / de las gzhan med pa'i phyir ro / / dper na phung po rnam par gzhag pa dang khams rnam par gzhag pa la brten nas brjod pa ste / / phung po'i grangs gang yin pa khams kyi grangs kyang de'am / / khams kyi grangs gang yin pa phung po'i grangs kyang de'am zhes bya ba ni mu gnyis pa ste /
dvikoṭikam syāt skandhasaṃkhyā na dhātusaṃkhyā rūpaskandho vijñānaskandhaścaḥ
# phung po'i grangs yin la khams kyi grangs ma yin pa'ang yod de gzugs kyi phung po dang rnam par shes pa'i phung po'o /
tathāhi naiko dhāturasti yaḥ sakalarūpaskandhalakṣaṇo vā syāt sakalavijñānaskandhalakṣaṇo vā
# 'di ltar gzugs kyi phung po'i mtshan nyid mtha' dag gam rnam par shes pa'i phung po'i mtshan nyid mtha' dag khams gcig tu gyur pa med do /
dhātusaṃkhyā na skandhasaṃkhyāḥ dharmadhāturiti
# khams kyi grang yin la phung po'i grangs ma yin pa'ang yod de / / chos kyi khams so /
trikoṭikaṃ yatra tisra eva koṭayo vyākriyante / tadyathā yā skandhasaṃkhyāyatanasaṃkhyāpi sā yā vāyatanasaṃkhyā skandhasaṃkhyāpi seti
# mu gsum pa ni gang du mu gsum pa kho na ston pa ste / / dper na phung po'i grangs gang yin pa skye mched kyi grangs kyang de 'am / / skye mched kyi grangs gang yin pa phung po'i grangs kyang de'am zhes bya ba ni mu gsum pa ste /
trikoṭikam syāt skandhasaṃkhyā nāyatanasaṃkhyā rūpaskandhaḥ
# phung po'i grangs yin la skye mched kyi grangs ma yin pa'ang yod de / / gzugs kyi phung po'o /
syādāyatanasaṃkhyā na skandhasaṃkhyā dharmāyatanam
# skye mched ni grangs yin la phung po'i grangs ma yin pa 'ang yod de / / chos kyi skye mched do /
syāt skandhasaṃkhyāyatanasaṃkhyā ca vijñānaskandho manaāyatanaṃ ca
# phung po'i grangs kyang yin la skye mched kyi grangs kyang yin pa'ang yod de / / rnam par shes pa'i phung po dang yid kyi skye mched do /
anubhayasaṃkhyāyāḥ skandhāyataneṣvasaṃbhava eveti
# gnyi ga ma yin pa'i grangs ni phung po dang skye mched la med do /
catuṣkoṭikaṃ yatra catasro 'pi koṭayo vyākriyante / tadyathā yaścakṣurindriyeṇa samanvāgataḥ śrotrendriyeṇāpi saḥ yo vā śrotrendriyeṇa samanvāgataścakṣurindriyeṇāpi sa iti / catuṣkoṭikam prathamā koṭirutpannāvihīnacakṣurbadhiraḥ
# mu bzhi pa ni gang du mu bzhi ston pa ste / / dper na mig gi dbang po dang ldan pa gang yin pa rna ba'i dbang po dang ldan pa'ang de'am / / rna ba'i dbang po dang ldan pa gang yin pa mig gi dbang po dang ldan pa'ang de'am zhes bya ba ni mu bzhi pa ste / / mu dang po ni mig skyes shing ma nyams la 'on pa'o /
dvitīyotpannāvihīnaśrotro 'ndhaḥ / tṛtīyotpannāvihīnacakṣuḥśrotraḥ
# mu gnyis pa ni rna ba skyes shing ma nyams la long ba'o / / mu gsum pa ni mig dang rna ba skyes la ma nyams pa'o /
caturthī tānākārān sthāpayitvā
# mu bzhi pa ni rnam pa de dag ma gtogs pa'o /
oṃkāritaṃ yatra praśne vyākaraṇamomiti kriyate evametadityabhyupagamyata ityarthaḥ
# de de bzhin no zhes bya ba ni gang dris pa lung du bstan pa la de bzhin no zhes brjod pa ste / / de de bzhin no zhes khas len ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tadyathā ye 'nityāḥ sarve te saṃskārāḥ ye vā saṃskārāḥ sarve te 'nityā iti pṛṣṭena omiti vyākartavyam / prātikṣepikaṃ yatra neti pratikṣipyate
# dper na gang mi rtag pa de dag thams cad 'dus byas yin nam / / 'dus byas gang yin pa de dag thams cad mi rtag pa'am zhes dris pa la de bzhin no zhes bstan par bya'o / / spang ba ni gang du ma yin no zhes spong ba ste /
tadyathā skandhavinirmuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ katibhiḥ satyaiḥ saṃgṛhītā iti / prātikṣepikam na santi skandhavinirmuktāḥ saṃskārā iti
# dper na phung po lnga las ma gtogs pa'i 'du byed rnams bden pa gang dag gis bsdus zhes zer ba la phung po lnga las ma gtogs pa'i 'du byed dag med do zhes spong ba'o /
saṃpraśnaviniścayaḥ aṣṭākāraḥ kāpadeśastadyathā ko nopalabhate
# yang dag par dri ba rnam par nges pa ni rnam pa brgyad de / / ci zhes bstan pa ni 'di lta ste /
prajñāpāramitālābhī bodhisattvaḥ / kiṃ nopalabhate / grāhyalakṣaṇaṃ grāhakalakṣaṇaṃ ca / kena nopalabhate
# su zhig mi dmigs she na / / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa'o / / ci mi dmigs she na gzung ba'i mtshan nyid dang 'dzin pa'i mtshan nyid do / / gang gis mi dmigs she na /
prajñāpāramitayā / kasmai nopalabhate
# shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas so / / ci'i phyir mi dmigs she na /
sarvasattvaparitrāṇārthamanuttarāyai samyaksaṃbodhaye
# sems can thams cad yongs su bskyab pa dang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub par bya ba'i phyir ro /
kuto nopalabhate
# gang las mi dmigs she na /
buddhotpādārāgaṇataḥ saddharmaśravaṇato yoniśomanaskārato dharmānudharmapratipattitaśca
# sangs rgyas 'byung ba mnyes par byed pa dang dam pa'i chos nyan pa dang tshul bzhin yid la byed pa dang chos kyi rjes su mthun pa'i chos sgrub pa las so /
kasya nopalabhate
# gang dag gi mi dmigs she na /
sarvadharmāṇām
# chos thams cad kyi'o /
kutra nopalabhate / adhimukticaryābhūmau yāvaddaśamyāṃ bodhisattvabhūmau
# gang du mi dmigs she na mos pas spyod pa'i sa nas sa bcu pa'i bar du'o /
kativighaścānupalambhaḥ
# rnam pa du zhig mi dmigs she na /
ekādaśavidhaḥ utpannaviruddhaḥ anutpannaḥ saṃmukhībhūtaḥ hetuvalotpannaḥ mitrabalotpannaḥ sarvadharmānupalambhaḥ śūnyatānupalambhaḥ sāsmimānaḥ nirasmimānaḥ asaṃbhṛtasaṃbhārasya saṃbhṛtasaṃbhārasya ca
# rnam pa bcu gcig ste / / skyes nas 'gags pa dang ma skyes pa dang mngon du gyur pa dang rgyu'i stobs las byung ba dang mdza' bo'i stobs las byung ba dang chos thams cad mi dmigs pa dang stong pa nyid mi dmigs pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal dang bcas pa dang nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal med pa dang tshogs ma bsags pa dang tshogs bsags pa ste /
ete cānupalambhā yat kiṃcidatītānāgatapratyutpannaṃ yāvadyadvā dūre yadvāntika ityetadanukramānusāreṇa draṣṭavyāḥ / yathā kāpadeśa evaṃ yāpadeśaḥ / yo nopalabhate yadyena yasmai yato yasya yatra nopalabhate yāvadvividhaścānupalambha iti
# mi dmigs pa 'di dag ni gang ci yang rung ste / / 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba dang nang dang phyi dang rags pa dang phra ba dang ngan pa dang bzang po dang rgyang ring ba dang thag nye ba zhes bya ba 'di dag gi go rims kyi tshul gyis blta bar bya'o / / ci zhes bstan pa la ji lta bar gang zhes bstan pa la yang de bzhin no zhes bya ba 'di la gang zhig mi dmigs pa dang gang dang gang gis dang gang gi phyir dang gang las dang gang gi dang gang du mi dmigs pa dang ji snyed cig mi dmigs pa'o /
api khalu catvāro viniścayamārgā dūṣakādayaḥ
# yang rnam par nges pa'i lam bzhi ste / / sun 'byin par byed pa la sogs pa'o /
tatra dūṣakaḥ durākhyātasya parapakṣasyāsādhurayamiti pratiṣedhakaḥ
# de la sun 'byin par byed pa ni gzhan gyi phyogs nyes par smras pa la / / 'di legs pa ma yin no zhes sel par byed pa'o /
sādhakaḥ svākhyātasya svapakṣasya sādhurayamiti pratiṣṭhāpakaḥ
# sgrub par byed pa ni rang gi phyogs legs par smras pa la 'di ni legs pa'o zhes 'jog par byed pa'o /
chedakaḥ pareṣāmutpannotpanneṣu saṃśayeṣu niścayadāyakaḥ
# gcod par byed pa ni gzhan dag gi the tshom skyed pa'am / / ma skyes pa la rnam par nges par sbyin par byed pa'o /
bodhakasteṣvartheṣu samūḍhānāṃ tadarthavyutpādakaḥ
# khong du chud par byed pa ni don de dang de dag la rmongs pa rnams la don de ston par byed pa'o /
kṛtyānuṣṭhānaviniścayo laukikānāmanyonyaṃ jīvikopāyādisamarthanaprayojanam
# bya ba sgrub pa rnam par nges pa ni 'jig rten phan tshun du 'tsho ba'i thabs la sogs pa'i dgos pa sgrub pa'o /
avatāraviniścayastrayāṇāṃ yānānāṃ katamasminyāne 'vatareyamavatārayeyaṃ ceti vicāraṇā
# 'jug pa rnam par nges pa ni theg pa gsum po dag las theg pa gang la 'jug par bya zhing zhugs par bya zhes rnam par spyod pa'o /
adhimuktiviniścayaḥ śrutamayyā prajñayā yathādeśanaṃ saṃpratyayaḥ
# mos par rnam par rnam par nges pa ni thos pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyis ji ltar thos pa bzhin du yid ches pa'o /
yuktiviniścayaḥ cintāmayyā prajñayā paurvāparyeṇābhiprāyaparitulanam
# rigs pas rnam par nges pa ni bsam pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyis snga phyi'i dgongs pa yongs su 'jal ba'o /
sāṃkathyaviniścayo yathāśrutacintitānāṃ praśnapratipraśnakriyāyogenānyonyaṃ dharmasaṃbhogaḥ
# 'bel pa'i gtam gyis rnam par nges pa ni ji ltar thos pa dang bsam pa rnams dri ba dang phyir zhing dri bar bya ba'i tshul gyis phan tshun chos la rdzogs par longs spyod pa'o /
prativedhaviniścayo darśanamārgastena satyaprativedhāt
# rab tu rtogs pas rnam par nges pa ni mthong ba'i lam ste / / des bden pa rab tu rtogs pa'i phyir ro /
viśuddhiviniścayo bhāvanāmārgastenāvaśeṣa kleśa viśoghanāt
# rnam par dag pas rnam par nges pa ni bsgom pa'i lam ste / / nges nyon mong pa ma lus par rnam par spong ba'i phyir ro /
abhinirhāraviniścayo viśeṣamārgastena vaiśeṣikaguṇābhinirhārāt
# mngon par bsgrub pas rnam par nges pa ni khyad par can gyi lam ste / / des yon tan khyad par can mngon par sgrub pa'i phyir ro /
padaprabhedaviniścayo dvikatrikacatuṣkādiprakārābhinirhāramukhenāparyantā dharmadeśanā
# tshig rab tu dbye ba rnam par nges pa ni gnyis pa dang gsum pa dang bzhi ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa mngon par sgrub pa'i sgo nas chos ston pa la mtha' yas so /
anābhogābhogamātrasarvārthasiddhiviniścayastathāgataṃ jñānam vinā pūrvābhogena sarveṣvartheṣvābhogasahakālamasaṃgāpratihatajñānadarśanapravṛtteḥ / vādaviniścayo vādavādādhikaraṇādiṣu kauśalyam / tatra sarvaṃ vacanaṃ vādaḥ
# lhun gyis grub pa dang rtsol ba tsam gyi don thams cad 'grub pa rnam par nges pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes te / / sngon gyi rtsol ba med par yang don thams cad la rtsol ba'i mdo las chags pa med pa dang thogs pa med pa'i ye shes kyi mthong ba 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / smra ba rnam par nges pa ni smra ba dang smra ba'i zhal ce ba la sogs pa la mkhas pa ste / / de la smra ba ni tshig thams cad do /
prakāraśo loke vādaḥ pravādaḥ
# rmad khyer bar smra ba ni 'jig rten na rnam par smra ba'o /
viruddhayorvādo vivādaḥ
# rtsod par smra ba ni mi mthun par smra ba'o /
apavādo garhito vādaḥ
# tshig ngan par smra ba ni smad par smra ba'o /
anukūlo vādo 'nuvādaḥ sāṃkathyaviniścayaḥ
# mthun par smra ba ni rjes su mthun par smra ba'o /
avagamāya vādo 'vavādaḥ / vādādhikaraṇam atra vādaḥ kriyata iti kṛtvā
# gdams par smra ba ni khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir smra ba'o / / smra ba'i zhal ce ba ni gang du smra bar bya ba ste / / 'di lta ste /
rājakulaṃ yatra rājā svayaṃ saṃnihitaḥ yuktakulaṃ yatra rājñādhiyuktāḥ sabhā vaṇik sabhādi
# rgyal po'i pho brang ni gang na rgyal po nyid bzhugs pa'o / / bskos pa 'du ba'i sa ni gang du rgyal pos bskos pa rnams 'du ba'o / / 'dus pa ni tshong ba la 'dus pa la sogs pa'o /
prāmāṇikāḥ sahāyakāḥ yeṣāṃ vacanaṃ vādiprativādinau na saṃśayataḥ / dharmārthakuśalāśca śramaṇabrāhmaṇā ye teṣu śāstreṣu granthataścārthataśca vyutpannabuddhayaḥ
# tshad mar rung ba'i zla grogs ni gang dag gi tshig smra ba dang phyir rgol ba gnyi gas mi gcod pa'o / / dge sbyong dang bram ze chos dang don la mkhas pa rnams ni gang dag bstan bcos de dang de dag gi tshig dang don la blo byang ba'o /
vādādhiṣṭhānaṃ yadadhiṣṭhāya vādaḥ kriyate tadyathā sādhyaṃ sādhanaṃ ca / tatra svabhāvaḥ sādhya ātmasvabhāvo dharmasvabhāvaśca nāstīti vāstīti vā / viśeṣaḥ sādhya ātmaviśeṣo dharmaviśeṣaśca sarvagato na sarvagato nityānityo rūpyarūpītyevamādibhiḥ prakāraiḥ
# smra ba'i gzhi ni gang la brten nas smra bar bya ba ste / / 'di lta ste sgrub pa dang grub pa'o / / de la ngo bo nyid sgrub pa ni bdag gi ngo bo nyid dang chos kyi ngo bo nyid de yod de zhe'am / / med do zhes bya ba'o / / khyad par sgrub pa ni bdag gi khyad par dang chos kyi khyad par te / / thams cad du song ba'am / / thams cad du song ba ma yin pa'am / / rtag pa'am mi rtag pa'i gzugs can nam gzugs can ma yin pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa su'o /
pratijñā sādhyasya svarucitārthasya parasaṃprāpaṇavijñāpanā / sādhyagrahaṇaṃ yadi na kriyeta siddhasyāpi svapakṣasya pareṣāṃ deśanā pratijñā prasajyeta / svarucitārthagrahaṇaṃ na kriyeta parapakṣasyāpi sādhyasya vacanaṃ pratijñā prasajyeta / paragrahaṇaṃ na kriyeta ekākino 'pi tadvacanaṃ pratijñā prasajyeta / saṃprāpaṇagrahaṇaṃ na kriyeta kāyenāpi tadarthābhinayanaṃ pratijñā prasajyeta
# dam bca' ba ni bdag 'dod pa sgrub pa'i don gzhan la go bar ston pa zhes bya ba la / / gal te sgrub pa ma smos na bdag gi phyogs grub zin pa yang gzhan dag la bstan par dam bca' bar 'gyur ro / / bdag 'dod pa'i don ma smos na ni gzhan gyi phyogs bsgrub pa'i tshig kyang dam bca' bar 'gyur ro / / gzhan ma smos na ni gcig pu yang tshig de dam bca' bar 'gyur ro / / gal te go bar ma smos na ni lus kyi don de brda spyod pa yang dam bca' bar 'gyur ro /
vijñāpanāgrahaṇaṃ na kriyetāvijñāte 'pi tadarthe śrotṛbhiḥ pratijñā prasajyeta
# gal te ston pa ma smos na ni nyan pa rnams kyis don de ma shes na yang dam bca' bar 'gyur ro /
yathokte tu vyavasthāne sarva ete doṣā na bhavanti tasmādevamasyā vyavasthānaṃ veditavyam
# ji ltar bstan pa bzhin du rnam par gzhag pa la nyes pa 'di dag thams cad med par 'gyur te / / de lta bas na 'di rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
hetustasminneva sādhye 'pratītasyārthasya saṃpratyayanimittaṃ pratyakṣopalaṃbhānupalaṃbhasamākhyānama / saṃpratyayanimittārtha iha hetvartha iti darśayati
# gtan tshigs ni sgrub pa nyid la ma grags pa'i don yid ches par byed pa'i rgyu mngon sum du dmigs pa dang mi dmigs par bsnyad pa'o zhes bya ba la / / yid ches par byed pa'i rgyu'i don 'dir gtan tshigs kyi don zhes bya bar ston te /
tathāhi pratyakṣānupalaṃbhādupalaṃbhādvetyanena samākhyānena tasmin sādhye 'pratītasyārthasya saṃpratyaya utpadyate
# 'di ltar mngon sum du dmigs pa dang ma dmigs pa zhes bstan pa 'dis sgrub pa de nyid la ma grags pa'i don la yid ches pa skye ba ste /
tena tatsamākhyātaṃ tannimittatvāddheturityucyate / pratyakṣopalaṃbhānupalaṃbhau punaḥ svabhāvaṃ liṅgaṃ cādhikṛtya veditavyau
# des na de bsnyad pa'i rgyur gyur pa'i phyir gtan tshigs zhes bya'o / / mngon sum du dmigs pa dang ma dmigs pa ni ngo bo nyid kyi tshul dang rtags kyi dbang du byas par rig par bya'o /
dṛṣṭānto dṛṣṭenāntenādṛṣṭasyāntasya samīkaraṇasamākhyānam pratītena bhāgenāpratītasya bhāgasya pratyāyanāya samākhyānamityarthaḥ
# dpe ni mtha' mthong ba dang mtha' ma mthong ba mtshungs par sbyar zhing bsnyad pa'o zhes bya ba ni grags pa'i cha dang ma grags pa'i cha rtogs par bya ba'i phyir / / bsnyad ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
upanayaḥ śiṣṭatajjātīyataddharmopagamāya nayatvasamākhyānam / yathā sādhyo 'rthastribhiravayavaiḥ sādhitastathā śiṣṭānāmapi tajjātīyānāṃ sādhyānāṃ sādhitārthadharmopagamāya nayatvena samākhyānaṃ yuktyātideśa upanayaḥ
# nye bar sbyor ba ni de'i rigs kyi chos lhag ma de dang 'dra ba la de'i chos sbyar ba'i phyir tshul gyis mthun par bsnyad pa'o zhes bya ba ni ji ltar bsgrub pa'i don yan lag gsum gyis bsgrubs pa de bzhin du / / lhag ma de dang 'dra ba sgrub pa grub pa rnams la yang sgrub pa'i don gyis chos sbyar ba'i phyir ro /
nigamanaṃ niṣṭhāgamanasamākhyānam / yasmādevaṃ yuktyā sūpapannaṃ tasmāditthamevedamityetannigamanaṃ veditavyam / eṣāṃ pratijñādīnāmidamudāharaṇamātraṃ pradarśyate
# tshul gyis mthun par bsnyad cing rigs pa 'dra bar ston pa ni nye bar sbyar bar bya'o / / mjug sdud pas ni mthar phyin par bsnyad pa'o zhes bya ba ni gang gi phyir de ltar rigs pas legs par 'thad pa de'i phyir de ni de bzhin no zhes bya ba de ni mjug sdud du rig par bya'o / / dam bca' ba la sogs pa 'di dag gi dper brjod pa tsam 'di rab tu bstan par bya ste /
tadyathā / nairātmyavādinastadrūpe 'dhikaraṇe saprativādike nāstyātmeti vacanaṃ pratijñā
# dper na rtsod pa'i phyir rgol ba dang bcas pa de la bdag med par smra bas bdag med do zhes bya ba'i tshig 'di dam bca' ba'o /
skandhavijñaptau caturvidhadoṣopalaṃbhāditi hetuḥ / sa hyātmā prajñapyamānaḥ skandhalakṣaṇo vā prajñapyeta skandheṣu vā anyatra vā skandhebhyaḥ askandhako vā
# phung po la bdag tu 'dogs pa la nyes pa rnam pa bzhi dmigs pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni gtan tshig te / / bdag de la 'dogs na phung po'i mtshan nyid du'am / / phung po rnams la'am / / phung po rnams las gzhan pa'am / / phung po med pa zhig tu gdags grang na /
tadyadi skandhalakṣaṇastenāsvatantrāḥ skandhāḥ pratītyasamutpannā udagavyayadharmāṇastallakṣaṇa ātmānopapadyata iti doṣaḥ
# de gal te phung po'i mtshan nyid ces byar ni phung po de dag rang dbang med par rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba dang 'jig pa'i chos can te / / bdag de'i mtshan nyid du mi 'thad pas nyes par 'gyur ro /
atha skandheṣu tenānityaskandhāśrita ātmānityaḥ prāpnotīti doṣaḥ
# ji ste phung po rnams la 'dogs na ni nges na phung po mi rtag pa la brten pas bdag mi rtag par 'gyur pa'i phyir nyes par 'gyur ro /
athānyatra skandhebhyastena nirdehaka ātmā niṣprayojana iti doṣaḥ
# ji ste phung po dag las gzhan du 'dogs na ni des na bdag lus med cing sgrim ma mi dgos pa'i phyir nyes par 'gyur ro /
athāskandhakastena prakṛtyaiva muktasya kevalino mokṣārthaprayatnavaiyarthyamiti doṣaḥ / vartamāne 'tītaprajñaptivaditi dṛṣṭāntaḥ
# gal te phung po med par 'dogs na ni / / rang bzhin gyis grol ba ma 'dres pa yin pas thar par bya ba'i phyir 'bad pa don med pa'i nyes par 'gyur ro / / da ltar la 'das pa 'dogs pa bzhin no zhes bya ba ni dpe'o /
taddhayatītaṃ vidyamānalakṣaṇatvena prajñapyamānaṃ vartamānalakṣaṇaṃ vā prajñapyeta vartamāne vā anyatra vā vartamānāt vartamānanirapekṣaṃ vā
# 'das pa de yod pa'i mtshan nyid kho nar 'dogs pa na de ltar gyi mtshan nyid du'am / / da ltar byung ba'am / / de ltar byung ngam sa gzhan du'am / / da ltar byung ba la mi ltos pa zhig tu gdags grang na /
tadyadi vartamānalakṣaṇaṃ tena vartamānamutpannāniruddhatallakṣaṇamatītamutpannā niruddhātmakamiti doṣaḥ
# de gal te da ltar gyi mtshan nyid du 'dogs na ni des na da ltar ni byung la ma 'gags pa yin pas de'i mtshan nyid 'das pa yang byung la ma 'gags pa'i mtshan nyid kyis nyes par 'gyur ro /
atha vartamāne tenāniruddhe niruddhātmakasya saṃbandho na yujyata iti doṣaḥ
# ji ste da ltar la 'dogs na des na ma 'gags pa ni 'gags pa'i bdag nyid dang 'brel bar mi rung bas nyes par 'gyur ro /
athānyatra vartamānāttena vartamānaṃ hitvā na kiṃcittadvastūpalabhyate yatra tatprajñapyata iti doṣaḥ
# ji ste da ltar las gzhan du 'dogs na ni des na da ltar bor na dngos po de ci yang mi dmigs te / / de la de 'dogs pa nyes par 'gyur ro /
atha vartamānanirapekṣaṃ tenāsaṃskṛtamapyatītaṃ prāpnotīti doṣaḥ
# ji ste da ltar la mi ltos na ni des na 'dus ma byas kyang 'das par 'gyur bas nyes par 'gyur ro /
taccātītaṃ bhraṣṭalakṣaṇatvāllakṣaṇato nāstīti siddham / ato 'nena vartamānaprajñaptau caturdoṣeṇa siddhenāsiddha ātmā nāstīti skandhaprajñaptau caturvidhadoṣopalaṃbhāt prasādhyate nāstīti / evamātmaviparyāsaṃ pratiṣidhyaitayaiva yuktyā nityādayo 'pi na santītyatideśa upanayaḥ
# 'das pa de ni mtshan nyid nyams pa'i phyir mtshan nyid kyis med par grub bo / / de'i phyir da ltar la 'dogs pa la nyes pa bzhi grub pa 'dis / / bdag med pa ma grub pa yang phung po la 'dogs pa la nyes pa rnam pa bzhi dmigs pa'i phyir med par rab tu grub bo / / de ltar bdag tu phyin ci log pa bkag nas rig pa 'dis rtag pa la sogs pa yang med do zhes 'dra bar ston pa ni nye bar sbyar ro /
yasmādetadevaṃ tasmādanityāḥ pañca skandhāḥ yāvadanātmāna iti nigamanamiti
# gang gi phyir de de ltar yin pa de'i phyir phung po lnga ni mi rtag pa nas bdag gi ba med pa'o zhes bya ba ni mjug sdud do /
pratyakṣaṃ svasatprakāśābhrānto 'rthaḥ / tatra svo 'rthastadyathā cakṣuṣo rūpam
# mngon sum ni rang gi don yod cing snang la ma nor ba'o zhes bya ba de la rang gi don ni 'di lta ste / / mig gi gzugs so /
sadgrahaṇaṃ ghaṭādidravyāṇāṃ loke pratyakṣasaṃmatānāṃ pratyakṣatvavyudāsārtha prajñaptimātratvāt
# yod pa smos pa ni bum pa la sogs pa'i rdzas 'jig rten na mngon sum du grags pa rnams mngon sum ma yin pa gsal ba'i phyir te / / brtags pa tsam gyi phyir ro /
prakāśagrahaṇamāvṛtatvādibhiranupalabdhikāraṇairanābhāsagataviṣayavyudāsārtham
# snang ba smos pa ni bsgrib pa la sogs pa mi dmigs pa'i rgyu rnams kyis mi snang bar 'gyur ba'i yul bsal ba'i phyir ro /
abhrāntagrahaṇamalātacakramāyāmarīcikādivyudāsārthamiti
# ma nor ba smos pa ni mgal me bskor ba dang sgyu ma dang smig rgyu la sogs pa bstsal ba'i phyir ro /
anumānaṃ pratyakṣaśiṣṭasaṃpratyayaḥ / pratyakṣādyadanyacchiṣṭamapratyakṣaṃ niyamena tatsahavarti prasiddhaṃ draṣṭuḥ pūrvaṃ tasya tatpratyakṣamīkṣamāṇasya tadanyasmin śiṣṭasaṃpratyaya utpadyate tenāpyatra bhavitavyametat sahavartineti tatpratyakṣapūrvakamanumānam
# rjes su dpag pa ni mngon sum gyi lhag ma la yid ches pa'o zhes bya ba la / / mngon sum las gzhan pa gang yin pa ni lhag mthong mngon sum ma yin pa ste / / nges par de dang lhan cig gnas par mthong ba la sngar rab tu grub pa'o / / mngon sum de la de lta bas na de las gzhan la lhag ma la 'dir ni 'di de dang lhan cig gnas pa yin no zhes yid ches par 'gyur ba de mngon sum sngon du song ba'i rjes su dpag pa ste /
tadyathā dhūmaṃ paśyato 'gnāviti
# dper na du ba mthong ba la me lta bu'o /
āptāgamastadubhayāviruddhopadeśaḥ
# yid ches pa'i lung ni de gnyi ga dang mi 'gal bar ston pa ste /
yatropadeśe tatpratyakṣamanumānaṃ ca sarvathā na virudhyete na vyabhicarataḥ sa āptāgamaḥ saṃpratyayitvāt
# nye bar bstan pa gang la mngon sum dang rjes su dpag pa de rnam pa thams cad du 'gal ba med cing 'khrul pa med pa ste / / yid ches pa'i lung ni yid ches par byed pa'i phyir ro /
vādālaṃkāro yena yukto vādī vādaṃ kurvāṇo 'tyarthaṃ śobhate
# smra ba'i rgyan ni gang dang ldan na smra ba smra bar byed pa'i tshe shin tu mdzes pa'o /
sa punaḥ svaparasamayajñatādiḥ
# de yang bdag dang gzhan gyi gzhung lugs shes pa la sogs pa ste /
tatra svaparasamayajñatā svasiddhāntaṃ parasiddhāntaṃ cārabhya granthataścārthataśca paurvāparyeṇa nirantaraṃ vyutpattiparipākaḥ
# de la bdag dang gzhan gyi gzhung lugs shes pa ni rang gi grub pa'i mtha' dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' las brtsams te / / tshig dang don snga phyi rgyun chags par rnam par ston par lcogs pa'o /
vākkaraṇasaṃpat śabdavādino vakṣyamāṇakathādoṣaviparyayeṇānākulādivāditā
# tshig zur phyin pa phun sum tshogs pa ni sgra smra ba 'og nas 'byung ba'i gtam gyis nyes pa las bzlog pa ste / / cal col la sogs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
vaiśāradyamanekodāhārābhiniviṣṭavidvajjanasamāvarte 'pi bruvato nirāsthatā gatavyathatā
# mi 'jigs pa ni du ma btsun pa dang mngon bar zhen pa can mkhas pa dag 'dus par smra zhing / / bag tsha ba med pa la 'dzem pa med pa'o /
sthairyaṃ prativādino vacanāvasānamāgamayyātvaramāṇabhāṣitā
# brtan pa ni phyir rgol ba'i tshig mjug tu phyin par bsdad nas yid dal du smra ba'o /
dākṣiṇyaṃ prakṛtibhadratā prāśnikaprativādicittānuvartitā
# mthun par byed pa ni rang bzhin gyis bzang bas gzu bo dang phyir rgol ba'i sems dang mthun pa'o /
vādanigraho yena vādī nigṛhīta ityucyate
# smra ba chad pas bcad pa ni gang gis smra ba chad pas bcad ces bya ba ste /
sa punaḥ kathātyāgādibhiḥ
# de yang gtam rjes bcad pa la sogs pa'o /
tatra kathātyāgo 'sādhu mama sādhu tavetyevamādibhiḥ prakāraiḥ svaparavādadoṣaguṇābhyupagamaḥ
# de la gtam rjes bcad pa la ni bdag gi ni ma legs so / / khyod kyi ni legs so zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa rnams kyis rang dang gzhan gyi smra ba'i skyon dang yon tan khas blang ba'o /
kathāsādo 'nyenānyapratisaraṇādibhiḥ vikṣepa ityarthaḥ / yathoktaṃ sūtre āyuṣmāṃścundikastīrthikaiḥ saha vādaṃ kurvannavajānitvā pratijānāti pratijānitvāvajānātīti
# gtam 'phro lus pa ni gzhan nas gzhan du brgyud pa la sogs pas bskal ba'o / / gtam gyi nyes pa ni cal col la sogs pa'i tshig go / / de la cal col ni gang skabs bor te / / gtam sna tshogs rgyas par byed pa'o / / 'khrugs pa ni gang khros pas g yeng ba dang dga' bas g yeng ba'o /
kathādoṣa ākulā divacanam / tatra ākulaṃ yadadhikāramutsṛjya vicitrakathāpratānanam
# brda phrad du mi rung ba ni gang chos dang don 'khor dang phyir rgol ba rnams kyis ma zin pa'o / / ran pa ma yin pa ni gang tshig lhag ma dang zlos pa dang nyungs pa'o /
saṃrabdhaṃ yatkopoddhavaṃ dravoddhavam
# don dang ldan pa ma yin pa ni de rnam pa lngar ba lta bar bya ste /
agamakaṃ yaddharmato 'rthataśca parṣadvādibhyāmagṛhītam
# don med pa dang don dang bral ba dang rigs pa dang bral ba dang sgrub par mtshungs pa dang ltag chod dang ldan pa ste /
amitaṃ yadadhikaṃ punaruktārthaṃ jñātārthaṃ ca
# don mi dmigs pa'i phyir ri / / don dang ma 'brel ba'i phyir ro /
anarthamanarthayuktam tatpañcākāraṃ draṣṭavyam / nirarthakam apārthakam yuktibhinnam sādhyasamam jāticchalopasaṃhitam arthānupalabdhito 'saṃbaddhārthato 'naikāntikataḥ sādhanasyāpi sādhyato 'yoniśo 'sabhyasarvavādānugamataśca / akālayuktavacanaṃ yatpūrvakaṃ vaktavyaṃpaścādabhihitam paścādvaktavyaṃ pūrvamabhihitam / asthiraṃ yatpratijñāyāvajñātamavajñāya pratijñātamatitvaramāṇayā vācā hi tūrṇaparāmṛṣṭaḥ
# ma nges pa'i phyir ro / / grub pa yang bsgrub dgos pa'i phyir ro / / tshul bzhin ma yin pa dang tshogs par 'byung ba ma yin pa dang smra ba thams cad dang ldan pa'i phyir ro / / dus tshigs ma yin par smra ba ni gang sngar smra bar bya ba de phyis smra ba dang phyis smra bar bya ba de sngar smra bar bya'o / / mi rtag pa ni gang dam bcas nas smod pa dang smad nas yang dam 'cha' ba dang myur ches pas ha cang rtab rtab por gyur te mi gsal ba'o /
apradīptavacanaṃ yacchandalakṣaṇasamatikrāntamapratyanubhāṣyottaravihittam saṃskṛtenārabhya prākṛtenāvasitam prākṛtenārabhya saṃskṛtena paryavasitaṃ ca
# tshig mi gsal ba ni gang sgra'i mtshan nyid dang 'gal ba dang phyir ma bzlas par len smras pa dang legs par sbyar ba las brtsams te / / tha mal bas mthar phyung ba dang tha mal pa las brtsams te legs par sbyar bas mthar phyung ba'o /
aprabaddhaṃ yadantarādhiṣṭhitavicchinnaṃ vākpratibhānamiti
# tshig rgyun chags pa ma yin pa ni / / gang bar skabs su tshig dang spobs pa thogs pa dang rgyun chad pa'o /
vādaniḥsaraṇaṃ yena vādānniḥsarati akaraṇena vā guṇadoṣau vicārya vādasya nigrahasthānānāsādanāt karaṇena vā nirvahanāditi
# smra ba las byung ba ni gang gis smras pa las byung ba ste / / smra ba'i yon tan dang nyes pa brtags nas mi byed pas 'byung ba ni chad pa'i gnas su mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / byed pas 'byung ba ni lcogs pa'i phyir ro /
tatra prativādinyabhājanatākuśalātsthānādvyutthāpya kuśale sthāne pratiṣṭhāpayitumaśakyatā
# de la phyir rgol ba snod ma yin pa ni mi dge ba'i gnas nas bslang ste / / dge ba'i gnas su gzhag par mi nus pa'o /
parṣado vaiguṇyamasabhyābhiniviṣṭapakṣapātitādinā / ātmano 'kauśalyaṃ vāde yāvadvādālaṅkāre 'vyutpattiḥ viparyayātprativādibhājanatādīni veditavyāni
# 'khor yon tan med pa ni tshogs pa rung ba ma yin pa dang mngon par zhen pa can dang phyogs su lhung ba la sogs pa'o / / bdag kyang mi mkhas pa ni smra ba nas smra ba'i rgyan gyi bar la ma byang ba'o / / de las bzlog pa ni 'khor snod du gyur pa la sogs par rig par bya'o /
vāde bahukarā dharmā ye vāde 'vaśyamupayujyante
# smra ba la gces spras byed pa'i chos rnams ni gang dag smra ba rnams la gdon mi za bar dgos pa ste /
tadyathā svaparasamayajñatā vāde bahukaro dharmo yena sarvatra kathāvastuni vādaṃ karoti
# 'di ltar gzhan gyi gzhung lugs la mkhas pa ni smra ba la gces spras byed pa'i chos te / / des gtam gyi gzhi thams cad du smra bar byed do /
śeṣaṃ sugamam / kuśalapakṣaprayuktenetyuktvā pratipattisārakeṇeti vacanamāśayaviśuddhijñāpanārthaṃ na lābhasatkārādinimittaṃ śrutādikuśalapakṣe prayuktenetyarthaḥ
# lhag ma rnams ni go sla bsam bshad do / / dge ba'i phyogs la brtson pa zhes bya ba gsungs nas nan tan snying por byed pa zhes bka' stsal pa ni bsam pa rnam par dag pa bstan pa'i phyir te / / rnyed pa dang bkur sti la sogs pa'i rgyur thos pa la sogs pa dge ba'i phyogs la brtson pa ma yin zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
sattvasaṃgrāhakeṇeti śrāvakādiviśeṣaṇārthaṃ parahitapratipattipradhānenetyarthaḥ / evaṃ ca svahitaparahitapratipannaḥ kṣipramanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhimabhisaṃbudhyata ityayameṣāṃ padānāmanusaṃdhirveditavyaḥ / avigṛhyāpi tāvadvāde kriyamāṇe prakṛtigambhīratvānmahāyānadharmasya durlabhājñā prāgeva vigṛhya
# sems can bsdus pa ni nyan thos la sogs pa las bye brag tu bya ba'i phyir te / / gzhan la phan par sgrub pa lhur len ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / de ltar bdag la phan ba dang gzhan la phan par zhugs pa ni myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba zhes bya ba 'di ni tshig 'di dag gi mtshams sbyar bar rig par bya'o / / mi rtsod par smra bar byed du zin kyang theg pa chen po'i chos ni rang bzhin gyis zab pa'i phyir kun shes pa dkon na rtsod pas lta smos kyang ci dgos /
yaiśca saha vigṛhya vādaḥ kriyate te 'pi pratipattāro nājñābhiprāyāḥ pratibruvanti kiṃtarhyupālambhābhiprāyāḥ
# gang dag dang lhan cig tu rtsod pas smra bar bya ba'i phyir / / smra ba de dag kun shes par bya ba'i bsam pas phyir smra ba ma yin gyi skyon gdags pa'i bsam pas so /
yeṣvapi prāśnikeṣu sa vādaḥ kriyate te vāsabhyā avyutpannā vā bhavantyabhiniviṣṭā vā
# gzu bo gang dag gi mdun du de smra bar bya ba'i tshogs de dag kyang rung ba ma yin zhing bya ba ma yin pa'am / / mngon bar zhen pa can dag go /
sarvo 'pi ca vādā prāyeṇa ṣaḍbhirdoṣairyukto bhavati
# smra bar bya ba thams cad kyang phal cher nyes pa drug dang ldan pa yin te /
tathāhi vādaṃ kurvāṇaḥ kadācidatirabhasenāsatpakṣamapi parigṛhyābhiniveśena chalajātinigrahasthānānyapi prayukte / vacanaparyavasānamanigamayyāpyakālena vaktumārabhate
# 'di ltar smra bar byed pa na yang res 'ga' byung rgyal du phyogs ngan pa yang yongs su bzung nas mngon bar zhen pa dang tshig dor dang ltag chod dang chad pa'i gnas rnams la yang sbyor ba dang tshig mjug tu phyin phyin du mi sdong par dus ma yin par smra bar rtsom pa dang phyir rgol bas legs par smras kyang khyad du gsod de smod ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
samyagapyuktāṃ prativādinaḥ kathāmapapātayati paṃsayatītyarthaḥ / paruṣamapi bruvate yena prativādyādayaḥ cittaṃ pradūṣayanti / svayaṃ ca teṣu cittaṃ pradūṣayatītyebhiḥ ṣaḍbhirdoṣairyukto bhavati / upaśāntasya ca durlabho vādaḥ / sati cānupaśame durlabhaṃ paracittānurakṣaṇaṃ svacittānurakṣaṇaṃ ca yena pare prasādaṃ labheran vimuktyāyatanayogena svacittaṃ samādhīyate
# tshig brlang po yang smra ba ste / / des phyir rgol ba la sogs pa'i sems 'khrugs par byed pa dang bdag kyang de dag la sems 'khrugs pa zhes bya ba'i nyes pa 'di drug dang ldan pa yin no / / nye bar zhi ba ni smra ba dkon no / / nye bar ma zhi ba la ni gang gis gzhan dad pa thob par 'gyur ba dang rnam par grol ba'i gnas dang ldan pa dang rang gi sems mnyam par 'jog par 'gyur ba dang gzhan gyi sems bsrung ba dang rang gi sems bsrung ba gnyi ga dkon no /
prāyeṇa vāde kathamahaṃ jayeyaṃ pare parājīyerannityevaṃ cittaṃ samudācarati
# smra ba phal cher ni ji ltar na bdag rgyal bar 'gyur zhing pha rol pham par 'gyur snyam pa'i sems de kun du 'byung ngo /
sati ca tasmin paridāhaduḥkhasaṃkleśaḥ
# de yod na yongs su gdung pa'i sdug bsngal gyis kun nas nyon mongs par 'gyur ro /
tasminsatyasparśavihāraḥ
# de yod na bde ba la gnas par mi 'gyur ro /
tato nirantarakuśalapakṣaprayogāsāmarthyāttato viśeṣādhigamaṃ pratyaprāptiparihāṇiriti
# de'i phyir rgyun mi chad par dge ba'i phyogs la sbyor bar mi nus so / / de'i phyir khyad par thob par bya ba la ma thob pas yongs su nyams par 'gyur ro /
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ hatvā ityasyāṃ gāthāyāṃ loke yadatyarthamavadyaṃ pātakaṃ tadabhidhāyīnyakṣarāṇyetāni viśuddhau pariṇāmitāni
# pha dang ma ni bsad byas shing / / zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di ni 'jig rten na gang shin tu kha na ma thob sdig tor rtsi ba da brjod pa'i yi ge rnams rnam par dag par yongs su bsgyur ba'o /
kiṃ ca loke 'tyarthamavadyaṃ saṃmatam / gurujanaghāto mahājanaghātaśca
# 'jig rten na shin tu kha na ma tho bar grags pa ni skye bo bla ma bsad pa dang skye bo chen po bsad pa'o /
sa punargurujano dvividhaḥ pratiniyato lokasādhāraṇaśca
# skye bo bla ma de yang rnam pa gnyis te / / so sor nges pa dang 'jig rten dang thun mong ba'o /
lokasādhāraṇo 'pi punardvividhaḥ paripālako dakṣiṇīyaśca / tatra pratiniyato gurujano mātā pitā ca pālako rājā dakṣiṇīyaḥ śrotriyabrāhmaṇāḥ teṣāṃ śuddhatarasamatatvāt
# 'jig rten dang thun mong ba la yang rnam pa gnyis te / / yongs su skyong bar byed pa dang sbyin gnas so / / de la so sor nges pa'i skye bo bla ma ni pha dang ma'o / / skyong bar byed pa ni rgyal po'o / / sbyin gnas ni bram ze gtsang sbra can rnams te / / de dag ni shin tu dag par grags pa'i phyir ro /
tadeṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ ghāto gurujanaghāta ityucyate
# de dag thams cad bsad na ni skye bo bla ma bsad pa zhes bya'o /
mahājanaghāto rāṣṭrasya sānucarasya ghātaḥ
# skye bo chen po bsad pa ni yul 'khor 'khor dang bcas bcom nas zhes bya ba'o /
anucarāḥ punaḥ gavāśvamahiṣoṣṭrādayo veditavyāḥ / kathaṃ punaretānyakṣarāṇi viśuddhau pariṇāmyante
# 'khor ni ba lang dang rta dang rnga mo dang ma he la sogs par rig par bya'o / / ji ltar yi ge 'di dag dag par yongs su bsgyur zhen /
mātrādighātavacanasya tṛṣṇādiprahāṇapariṇāmanādyathākramaṃ tṛṣṇām karmabhavam sopādānaṃ vijñānam dṛṣṭiśīlavrataparāmarśadvayam ṣaḍāyatanaṃ ca sagocaramadhikṛtya mātrādayo draṣṭavyāḥ tatsādharmyāt / tatra tṛṣṇā nirvṛttihetuḥ
