# ma la sogs pa bsad pa'i tshig ni sred pa la sogs pa spong bar yongs su bsgyur ba'i phyir te / / go rims bzhin du sred pa dang las kyi sred pa dang nye bar len pa dang bcas pa'i rnam par shes pa dang lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa gnyis dang skye mched drug spyod yul dang bcas pa'i dbang du byas nas / / ma la sogs par blta bar bya ste / / de dang 'dra ba'i phyir ro / / de la sred pa ni mngon par grub pa'i rgyu'o /
karmabhava utpattihetuḥ
# las kyi srid pa ni skye ba'i rgyu ste /
sa ca bhāvanābījāghānayogena pitṛbhūto draṣṭavyaḥ
# de ni bsgom pa'i bag chags skyed pa'i tshul gyis pha lta bur blta bar bya'o /
ābhyāṃ hetubhyāṃ sopādānaṃ vijñānaṃ pravartate / tasyaivaṃ pravartamānasya satyapi mokṣābhilāṣe mokṣaprāptivighnakarāvanupāyāgraśuddhipratyāyakau parāmarśau
# rgyu 'di gnyis las ni nye bar len pa dang bcas pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ngo / / de de ltar byung na thar pa 'dod du zin kyang mchog tu dag par yid ches par byed pa'i mchog tu 'dzin pa gnyis thar pa thob pa la gegs byed do /
śrotriyasādharmyamanayoretadeva veditavyaṃ yadutāgraśuddhayabhiniveśaḥ
# 'di gnyis gtsang sbra can dang 'dra ba ni 'di lta bur rig par bya ste / / 'di ltar mchog dang 'dag par mngon bar zhen pa'o /
tasyaiva punarvijñānasyāśrayālaṃbanabhāvena ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sagocaraṃ veditavyamiti
# rnam par shes pa de'i gnas dang dmigs pa'i dngos pos skye mched drug spyod yul dang bcas par rig par bya'o / / yid mi ches dang byas mi gzo /
aśrāddhaścākṛtajñaścetyasyāṃ gāthāyāṃ hīnārthābhidhāyīnyakṣarāṇyuttamārthe paridīpitāni
# zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di ni / / don ngan pa brjod pa'i yi ge rnams mchog gi don du yongs su bsgyur ba'o /
hīno loke caturvidhaḥ manaskarmahīnaḥ kāyakarmahīno vākkarmahīna upabhogahīnaśca
# 'jig rten na ngan pa rnam pa bzhi ste / / yid kyi las ngan pa dang lus kyi las ngan pa dang ngag gi las ngan pa dang longs spyod ngan pa'o / / yid kyi las ngan pa yang rnam pa gnyis te /
manaskarmahīnaḥ punardvividhaḥ kuśalapravṛttivailomyena cāśrāddhaḥ paralokādyasaṃpratyayena dānādiṣvaprayogāt
# dge ba la 'jug pa dang mi mthun pas yid mi ches pa ste / / 'jig rten pa rol la sogs pa la yid mi ches pas / / sbyin pa la sogs pa la mi sbyor ba'i phyir ro /
akuśalapravṛttyānukūlyena cākṛtajñaḥ yatropakārānapekṣitvena mātṛvadhādiduścarite nirmaryādatvāt
# mi dge ba la 'jug pa dang mthun pas byas pa mi gzo ba ste / / sngon phan btags pa la mi lta bar ma gsod pa la sogs pas nyes par spyod pa la yang mi 'dogs pa'i phyir ro /
kāyakarmahīnaścauraḥ saṃdhicchedakaḥ atyarthaṃ garhitajīvitatvāt
# lus kyi las ngan pa ni khyim 'bigs pa'i rkun po ste / / 'tsho ba shin tu smad pa'i phyir ro /
vākkarmahīno mṛṣāvādādipradhānaḥ tadrūpasya sabhādiṣu praveśābhāvāt / upabhogahī naḥ śvā kā kaḥ preto vetyevamādikaḥ charditabhakṣaṇāditi
# ngag gi las ngan pa ni brdzun du smra ba la sogs pa lhur len pa ste / / de lta bu dang ldan pa ni tshogs pa la sogs pa'i nang du 'jug tu mi rung ba'i phyir ro / / longs spyod ngan pa ni / / khyi dang bya rog dang yi nga gas la sogs pa ste /
kathaṃ punaretānyakṣarāṇyuttamārthe pariṇāmyante
# skyugs pa za ba'i phyir ro / / ji ltar yi ge 'di dag mchog gi don du yongs su bsgyur zhe na /
aśrāddhādivacanānāmarhati pariṇāmanāt / tatrāśrāddho vimuktijñānadarśanayogena svapratyayatvāt
# yid mi ches pa la sogs pa'i tshig rnams ni dgra bcom par yongs su bsgyur ba'i phyir ro / / de la yid mi ches pa ni rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba dang ldan pas rang gi yid ches pa'i phyir ro /
akṛtajño 'saṃskṛtanirmāṇajñānāt / saṃdhicchettā punarbhavapratisaṃdhihetukleśaprahāṇāt
# byas pa mi gzo ba ni 'dus ma byas pa mya ngan las 'das pa shes pa'i phyir ro / / khyim 'bigs par byed pa ni yang srid par nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rgyu nyon mongs pa spangs pa'i phyir ro /
hatāvakāśa āyatyāṃ sarvagatiṣu duḥkhānabhinirvartanāt
# go skabs bcom zhes bya ba ni / / phyi ma la 'gro pa thams cad du sdug bsngal mngon par mi 'grub pa'i phyir ro /
vāntāśo dṛṣṭe dharme upakaraṇabalena kāyaṃ saṃdhā rayato 'pi bhogajīvitāśābhāvāditi
# skyugs pa za ba ni mthong ba'i chos la yo byad kyi stobs kyis lus 'dzin kyang longs spyod dang srog la re ba med pa'i phyir ro /
yathā coktam asāre sāramataya iti
# snying po med la snying por shes /
asyā gāthāyāḥ pūrvavadarthanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ
# zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di'i don snga ma bzhin du bshad par bya'o /
śarīraṃ punarasyāḥ samādhiṃ niśritya bodhisattvā darśanabhāvanāmārgābhyāṃ mahābodhiṃ spṛśantīti
# 'di'i lus ni byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin la brten nas mthong ba dang bsgom pa'i lam gnyis kyis byang chub chen po la reg pa'o /
mātsaryadharmatāmanuvṛṃhayatīti savāsanamātsaryānuśayaprahāṇena tattathatāśrayaparivṛttisākṣātkaraṇāt / dānena ca parikhidyate dīrghakālaṃ dānanimittaṃ paramaduṣkaraśramābhyupagamāt
# ser sna'i chos nyid 'phel bar byed pa ni bag chags dang bcas pa'i sems ser sna'i bag la nyal spangs pas de'i de bzhin nyid gnas gyur pa mngon du byed pa'i phyir ro / / sbyin pas yongs su skyo ba ni yun ring por sbyin pa'i rgyu mchog tu bya dka' bas ngal bar bya ba khas blangs pa'i phyir ro /
yācanakaṃ ca dveṣṭi svayaṃ grāhābhirucitatayā yācanakaprātikūlyāt
# slong ba la tshig pa za ba ni rang gis len par 'dod pas slong ba dang mi mthun pa'i phyir ro /
na kiṃcit kadāciddadāti sarvasya vastunaḥ sarvadā dānāt
# res 'ga' ni ci yang sbyin par mi byed pa ni dngos po thams cad rtag tu sbyin pa'i phyir ro /
dūre ca bhavati dānasya āsādyadānādiparivarjanāt
# sbyin pa las ring du gyur pa ni nye ba la sbyin pa la sogs pa yongs su spangs pa'i phyir ro /
tatra parameṇa brahmacaryeṇa samanvāgata iti lokottareṇa mārgeṇetyarthaḥ / nānyatra maithunānmaithunasya niḥsaraṇaṃ paryeṣata iti tasyaiva yathābhūta parijñānena tatprahāṇāt
# tshangs par spyod pa dang ldan pa zhes bya ba ni / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam dang ldan zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / 'khrig pa las gzhan du 'khrig pas nges par 'byung ba mi 'tshol ba ni de nyid yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes nas spong ba'i phyir ro /
yathābhūtaparijñānaṃ punarasya tathatāpratibedhādveditavyam
# de la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa ni / / de'i de bzhin nyid rab tu rtogs par rig par bya'o /
maithunaprahāṇenopekṣako bhavati abrahmacaryaprahāṇopekṣaṇāt
# 'khrig pa spong ba la g yeng ba ni mi tshangs par spyod pa spong ba'i thabs la rtog pa'i phyir ro /
utpannaṃ ca maithunarāgamadhivāsayati kāmarāgasyādhyātmamutpannasya bahiḥpravāsanāt
# 'khrig pa'i 'dod chags skyes pa dang du len pa ni / / 'dod pa la 'dod chags nang du skyes pa phyi rol du spong ba'i phyir ro /
maithunapratipakṣeṇa ca dharmeṇottrasyati tatpratipakṣeṇa mārgeṇa sarvasattvottaraṇāya vyavasyatīti kṛtvā
# 'khrig pa'i gnyen po'i chos kyis skrag pa ni de'i gnyen po'i chos kyis sems can thams cad bsgral ba'i don du rtsol ba'i phyir ro / / rgyun mi 'chad par gnyis kyis gnyis sbyor ba ni /
abhīkṣṇaṃ ca dvayadvayaṃ samāpadyate saṃkleśavyavada nadvayena phalahetubhedena catuḥsatyātmakena śamathavipaśyanādvayena / punaḥpunarlaukikalokottaramārgadvayaṃ samāpadyata iti kṛtvā / kimupādāyedaṃ śāstramabhidharmasamuccaya iti nāma labhate
# zhi gnas dang lhag mthong ba gnyis kyis 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa gnyis la snyoms par 'jug pa ste / / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba gnyis kyis 'bras bu dang rgyu'i bye brag gis bden pa bzhi'i bdag nyid du gyur pa'i don du 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam gnyis la snyoms par 'jug pa'i phyir ro / / bstan bcos 'di ci'i phyir chos mngon par kun las btus pa zhes bya bar ming btags she na /
niruktinyāyena / sametyoccayatāmupādāya tattvamabhisametyādhigamya bodhisattvaṃḥ saṃkalanādityarthaḥ
# nges pa'i tshig gi tshul gyis rtogs nas bsdus pa'i phyir te / / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis de kho na nyid mngon par rtogs shing khong du chud nas mdor bsdus zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
samantāduccayatāmupādāyābhidharmasūtrataḥ sarvacintāsthānasaṃgrahādityarthaḥ / samyaguccayatvāyāyatanatāṃ copādāyetyaviparītenopāyena yāvadbuddhatvaprāpaṇādityarthaḥ
# kun las btus pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni chos mngon pa'i mdo rnams las te / / bsam pa'i gnas thams cad bsdus pa'i phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / yang dag par mtho ba'i gnas yin pa'i phyir zhes bya ba ni phyin ci ma log pa'i thabs kyis sangs rgyas nyid kyi bar du thob par byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ityabhidharmasamuccaye bhāṣyataḥ sāṃkathyaviniścayo nāma pañcamaḥ samuccayaḥ samāptaḥ
# chos mngon pa kun las btus pa'i bshad pa / / slob dpon chen po rgyal ba'i sras kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so /

#
